Bɔ̌ma dɨŋɨ́ yɛ ká bɛ́ chí ɛ̌ti Yesu kɛ Mandɛm áfòŋori bɛbʉ́ mbɔ ɛnyu sɛ́ghàti bhe.
Kɛ ɛchi wɨkɨrɨk bɛ mfay ámfʉ́ɛ́t, mmɨk amfʉɛt, ɛcha bɛ mandú ɛnyɨŋ ndǔ basɨŋ amɛn Moses nɛ amɛn barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ ánɛ́m.
Chɔŋ ntɔ́ŋ be ɛnyǔ mmǔ anɛ átwɔ́ ntá ya, aghók ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ndɛ́mɛ́, ankʉ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi ághókó achi.
Mpú rɛm nɔ chí ɛ̌ti ntɨ mmu ywɛká. Nchí rɛm chí ɛ̌ti ntɨ mmu achák wu. Mmu ǎkwáy bɛ́rɛ́m bɛ, “Ndaká yí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chɔ̀ŋti ntɨ mmu achák amɛm ɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́kaŋ mɛ bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ mbɔŋ ngǎngaŋ ndǔ mmʉɛ́t ɛya?”
Bě kɛ̌ Moses ásɔ́rɛ́ ɛbhé Mandɛm ntá bɔángɛl achyɛ ntá yɛka, yɛ̌ nɔ, bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ bhʉɛrɛ yɔ́.’” 
Mbák akʉ mbɔ ɛnyu ɔ́ghátí yi ɔpú kwáy bɛkaka yi bɛ, ‘Ɔkʉ a’ mbɔnyunɛ akʉ chí bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ.
Pɔ̌l abhɨŋɨ mǔnti batɛmɛ́ nɛnu amɔt aghati yí bɛ, “Sɔt ɛsakámu anɛ́ dɔ́k ntá mǔngo nɛ yí. Abhɔŋ ɛnyɨŋ bɛ́gháti yi.”
Páílet achyɛ yɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ mánsɔ́t Yesu mandɛn nɛ ɛ́kpá.
Bǎghɔ yɛ bɛ mbák mmu abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm, ɛ́pú kway bɛfakari bɛ Mandɛm ambɔŋ maŋák nɛ yi. Yɛ̌ agha anɛ árɔ̀ŋ kɛkwɔt nɛ Mandɛm abhɔŋ mɛ́nóko bɛ Mandɛm achi, nɛ bɛ ǎchyɛ̀ ǎkap yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ áyàŋ yi nɛ ntɨ ɛni nɛnkɛm.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka ánkʉ́ yɛ nɛ batɨ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi ákway bɛyaŋ bɛ bo mankʉ ntá yi. Mbák mǎnkʉ́ nɔ, ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ bǎkʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Moses nɛ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ bághàti bhɛsɛ amɛm basɨŋɨ́ amap.
Mpɛmɛ anɛ ɔ́tɔ̀ŋti bɛ bǒ mankɛm mángɔ.
Yesu akʉ nyaka bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay bɛ́chák bɛsí bakoŋo bhi, ɛbhɛ́n bábhɨ́kɨ́ sɨŋ amɛm ɛkáti ɛnɛ.
Kɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ achi nyaka nɛ Stífin tontó. Ayoŋ amɨ́k ayɨŋɨ mfay, aghɔ́ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ Mandɛm, nɛ Yesu téé ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt kɛnókó Mandɛm,
Yesu afa ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí yɔ, arɔk, ndǔ ɛkɛt Símun. Nnɔ ngɔrɛ́ Símun abhɔ̌ŋ mbʉ́ɛ́p ataŋataŋ. Baghɔk Yesu manɨk yi mmʉɛt bɛ ambu yi.
Chi afʉɛ́t arɔk ntá mmɔ̌ anɛ mɔ́nkwɛn, aghati yi nkwɔ bɛ, “Mɔ́wa, dɔ́k amɛm nkɨ kʉ bɛtɨk ɛchɔŋ. Mɔ́wu akɛmɛ yi bɛ ‘Ɛta, chɔŋ ndɔk.’ Kɛ akɛrɔ́ŋ.
Bǎrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ yɛ̌ agha anɛ ábhʉ̀ɛrɛ bɛbhé Mandɛm mɛnkɛm kɛ ankwɛ́n bɛ́bhʉrɛ ɛbhé ɛ́mɔ́t, bɛsí Mandɛm, achí ɛnyumɔ́t mbɔ mmu anɛ ákwɛ́nɛ́ bɛbhé mɛnkɛm.
Ató yɛ bakwak abhi batí ápay, Tímɔti nɛ Ɛrástɔs, bɛ́ mándɔ́k ambɨ atú Masidónia. Yímbɔŋ arɔp ansɛm atú Esia ndu mɔ́mbɨŋɨ́ mpok.
Yesu Kristo achí ɛnyumɔt ɛyu, nɛ ɛchɔŋ, nɛ mpoknkɛm.
Bɛyǎ bo Israɛl bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́ Yesu achi Bɛ́tani, bárɔ́k arɛ, puyɛ̌ ndiɛrɛ ndu bɛ́ghɔ Yesu kɛ ndu bɛghɔ Lásárɔs nkwɔ mmǔ yi akʉ apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.
Mbák chi ɛnyɨŋ bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ ɛnɛ ɛyɨŋɨ mambe tándrámɔt anɛ ɔ́ghɔ́ ndǔ awɔ́nɛm awa nɛ mɛnyɨŋ gol tándrámɔt ɛbhɛn bɛ́pɔ̀kɔ bɛrɔ́ŋɔ́, dɨŋɨ́ bɛ́ mambe tándrámɔt chí bɔángɛl tándrámɔt abhɛn bábhàbhɛri bɛka bǒnkwɔ tándrámɔt. Nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́pɔ̀kɔ bɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ tándrámɔt chí bɛká bǒnkwɔ tándrámɔt bhɔ.
Kɛ bájwɛ́ yi, barɛm bɛ, “Bʉrɛ́ nɛ bhɛsɛ. Nywɔp nɛ́rɔŋ nɛ mbaŋ anaŋ ǎgiri.” Arɔk yɛ bɛbhʉrɛ nɛ bhɔ.
Básɔt mfɔ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́ mmu árwɔ̀ nyaka bo mámɛ́sɛ amɛm nɛpǐngó anɛ ádù nɛ ɛkɛ́m sɔ́lfɔ. Mámɛ́sɛ yi ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ mámɛ́sɛ́ nnya mbʉ́mbʉ nɛ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ nsé. Arɛ́, bǎbhak ndǔ bɛbě ngó anɛ ásɔ̀ŋ bhɔ bɛtǐ nɛ ngósí. 
Nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́, bakɛmɛ́ ɛtɔk nɛ bǒ batí bo Israɛl, nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm bákɛ́m ɛchɛmɛ amɛm ɛtɔk Yerúsalɛm.
Sɛptí nɔ́kɔ́ ka mmʉɛt ntá batɨ. Ɛpɨŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́mfú ndǔ kɛnókó ɛkɛn bǎchyɛ̀ Kristo.
Ɛyɔŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́re rɛm ntá ángɛl anɛ ajwi bátándát mmu ákɛ́mɛ́ mbá awɔ bɛ, “Dɔ̌ bɔángɛl manwi abhɛn bágwɔ́rɛ́ awu nɛpak nyɛ́n-nɛgho ɛnɛ́n bábhɨŋɨ bɛ Yúfretis mámfú mándɔ́k!”
Yesu aghati yi bɛ ándɔk ɛkɛt ɛyi, nɛ bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ, “Kɛ́pɛtnsɛm ɛtɔk.” 
Mandɛm Ɛta yɛsɛ́ nɛ Yesu Kristo Acha mántɔ́ŋ bé bɛrɨ̌ndu, mánchyɛ bhe kpák. 
Bǒ-bhɔ bati apay bárɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ Yesu, bǒfu basɔt mbók bárɔ́k ntá Yesu nɛ yi. Ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ kɛ ɛ́kʉ́ nyaka yi ákwɛ́nɛ́ kɛbhok.
Ɛchi nɔ mbɔnyunɛ yi kɛ Mandɛm árɛ́mɛ́ bɛ ángókó yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ, ɛbhɛn bɛchi amfay nɛ ɛbhɛn bɛchi fá amɨk, ɛbhɛn bo bághɔ̀ nɛ ɛbhɛn bo bápú kway bɛghɔ, bɛtaŋtí bɛfóŋó, ɛbhɛn bɛbhɔŋɔ bɛtaŋ bɛcha bafɔ bachak nɛ bɛfóŋó ɛbhɛn nɛŋɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ ɛkap nɛcha ɛkɛn bachak, nɛ yɛ̌ chí ɛbhɛn bɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ amfay bho mbɔ bafɔ. Bɛ́fʉɛt ntá yi, nɛ ntá yi, kɛ bághókó mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm.
Chɔŋ ɔ́mpɛt bhɔ́ ɔ́mfɛrɛ mbɔ bɛsɨ́ ndɛn ɛbhɛn mmu áwùpsi, kɛ wɔ ɔchí ɛnyumɔt mpoknkɛm, nɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛ nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.”
Ɛso ɛ́twɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́, manyiɛp akwɛn tontó, ajwi, ataka ɛbhɨ, babhʉɛ́p ataŋataŋ ánú, ɛkɛt ɛyɔ ɛ́báy mmʉɛt amɨk juu! 
“Kɛ mpok mfɔ áchwé anywɔ́p bɛghɔ bǒ abhɛn yi ánáká, aghɔ́ bɛ́ mmu amɔt abhɨkɨ bhɔŋ nkú-nɛbhay amʉɛt.
Yesu asɛmti bho bɛ bákɛ́ ghati yɛ̌ mmu ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fákári. Yɛ̌ nɔ, ásɛ́mtí nɔ́kɔ́ bhɔ, mángati nɔkɔ ghati bho.
Nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́, sɛrɔ, sɛrɔk Seséria. Ngati Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm amɔt abhak arɛ́ anɛ aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Fílip. Abhak mmu amɔt ndǔ nkwɔ́ bo batí tándrámɔt abhɛn báyábhɛ́ nyaka Yerúsalɛm bɛ mánkwak nɔkɔ bǒnto. Sɛ́rɔ́k sɛchɔkɔ ɛkɛt ɛyi.
Símun Píta amak yi nɛ awɔ arɛm bɛ, “Ghatí bhɛ́sɛ́ mmu anɛ ɔ́rɛ̀m nɔ ɛ̌ti yi.”
Bákɛ́m nɔ́kɔ́ Yesu, mmu amɔt anɛ áchí nɛ yi, agwɔp akparɛnja ywi akpɔ́t atú nsɛm Mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm chwát agʉɛp amɨk.
Kɛ mpok mmu árɛ̀m bɛ, “Nsé ɛnɛ mɛ̌sè ɛ́kwak bo mángɔ kpoŋoroŋ bɛ Mandɛm achi mmu tɛtɛp, nɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ mánchyɛ yi kɛnókó. Mbák ɛchi nɔ, ná Mandɛm akway bɛtaŋ mɛ andɛm bɛ nchí mmu bɛbʉ́ ndu nchí sense.”
mámfyɛ́ amɛm nɛpǐngo. Arɛ́, bábhak ndǔ nɛdǐ kɛbhɔ nɛ nɛnyiɛ ámɛ́n.” 
Ndǔ bǎchɛ́mɛ́ nkáp nɛ bǎchyɛ́ bo bhɔ, bǎtɔŋ bɛ bǎkoŋo tɛtɛp anɛ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ bǎrɛm bɛ mǎnókó. Ndǔ bǎchyɛ ɛnyu yɔ nɛ awɔ fuu ndu bɛkwak bhɔ nɛ bo bachak, bo bághɔ nɛ báchyɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ aghati bhɔ́ bɛ, “Bǎbhɔŋ ɛrɨ́tí mbi bɛ́rɔ bɛbhé Mandɛm ndu bɛ́koŋo chí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bachǐmbɨ bhɛka bátɔ́ŋɔ́!
Ɛtayi arɛm bɛ, nɛ́nɛ ‘Fú, dɔ́k, ɛtɔk ndǔ babhǐ agho nɛ ndǔ babhǐ bɛbhɨ. Fíɛ́ bɛtaŋ bɛ́ bo mántwɔ́ bɛ́ ɛkɛt ɛpa ɛ́njwi.
Ɛ́chá bhɔ ɛnyu bákʉ. Tɛ́mté wu, babhakanɛm bati apay nɛ ndɛn amʉɛt ɛnɛ́ ɛ́kɔ̀t ŋwaŋwǎŋwaŋ báté kɛkwɔt nɛ bhɔ.
Dɔ̌ ká Ɛyɔŋ Kristo ɛ́mbɔŋ bɛtaŋ amɛm batɨ ayɛka. Tɔ́ŋ nɔ́kɔ́ ká batɨ ɛkɔŋ ɛyɔ, mǎnchyɛ nɔkɔ bhɔ maniɛ́, nɛ bɛyǎ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak. Kwáy nɔ́kɔ́ ka bakwáy anɛ áfù ndu Ɛkáti Bakway ɛnɛ ɛchi amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm, nɛ bakwáy Mandɛm achak, nɛ bakwáy anɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ afyɛ́ be antɨ. Kwáy nɔ́kɔ́ ka yɔ nɛ bakak ntá Mandɛm amɛm batɨ yɛka.
Bɔ̌ma, ndak anɛ chí ɛrɛmɛ́ ndak. Mbák ɔrɛm ɛnyɨŋ, ɔ́kɛ́ yɨkɨ. Ɔ́kɛ́ yɨkɨ ɔ́mbɨŋɨ nnyɛ́n Mandɛm mmu áchí amfay. Kɛ́yɨkɨ ɔ́mbɨ́ŋɨ́ mmɨk, nɛ ɔ́kɛ́ yɨkɨ ndǔ nnyɛ́n yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛ́chák. Mbák ɔká ɛnyɨŋ, dɛm bɛ, “Ɛɛ”, nɛ “Ɛ̌” ámbák chí Ɛɛ. Mbák ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ ká, dɛm bɛ, “Cháo” nɛ “Cháo” ambak chí Cháo. Mbák ɔká ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mɔt, ɔ́nkʉ chí ɛ́chák nɔ ɔ́kwɛ̌n ɛbhé Mandɛm.
Kɛnókó ɛkɛn báchyɛ̀ mɛ kɛchi chi ndɛ́ndɛm, mbɔnyunɛ bɛbhé ɛbhɛn bakwǎŋwaŋ báfyɛ́, kɛ bɔ bátɔ̀ŋ bho mbɔ bɛ bɛchi Ɛyɔŋ ɛya.’” 
Nɛ bo abhɛn bákòŋo chi nɛpɛ́m bakwǎŋwaŋ, bápú kway bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chyɛ Mandɛm maŋák.
Akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Mmu anɛ ábú mɛ kɛ ághátí mɛ bɛ, ‘Pɛ́t ɛ̌sák ɛyɛ, faté kɔ.’”
Ɛ̌ti ɛyɔ kɛ nsɨ́ŋɨ́ bhe ɛkáti ɛnɛ. Nsɨŋ yɔ́ ɛnyu ɛyɔ bɛ nnáŋ ntwɔ́ awu, be bho bǎbhɔŋɔ bɛchyɛ mɛ maŋák, bǎkɛ́ kʉ ntɨ nɛnchɔŋɔ́ mɛ amɛm. Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ sayri bɛ mbák nchí maŋák, be nkwɔ bǎbhak maŋák.
Nɛ mpok Mandɛm áyɨ́kɨ́ arɛm bɛ, “Bápú kway bɛchwe ndǔ nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt ɛna wáwák”, ntɨkɨ bho yi árɛ́mɛ́ nyaka nɔ ɛ̌ti yap? Pú bǒ abhɛn bápú ghok nyaka yi?
Debhít ǎbhɨ̀ŋɨ nyaka Mpɛmɛ ɛrɛ bɛ Acha. Ná Achǎ áyibhiri ambak ɛbhárɛ́mɔ ywi?” 
Mmɛ nɛ ɛtayɛ sɛ́kɔ, sɛ́yàŋ wɔ nɛ bɛyǎ bɛcháy antɨ. Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Báyàŋ mbʉ mɛ ndaká yí? Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛ mbɔ̌ŋ bɛbhak amɛm ɛkɛt Ɛtaya?”
Bɔ̌ Sɛva bati tándrámɔt bare kʉ nɔ. Sɛva achi nyaka mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm amɔt.
Nɛka Ábraham kɛ nɛ́kʉ́ bɛ mpok Mandɛm áchyɛ́ yi nɛmɔ ndu aghati yi bɛ ándɔ́k ánchyɛ́ mɔ́ywi Áisek mbɔ akap, Ábraham mmu Mandɛm afyɛ́ yi bariɛp, aka bɛchyɛ njaŋa mɔ́ywi mbɔ akap.
Kɛ mbák bǎbhɔŋ batɨ anɛ ájwí nɛ bɛyǎ mpabhamɨ́k nɛ ɛpɨŋ ɛnɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ánù chí ndǔ aywi ntí, bǎkɛ́ pányu ndɛ́ndɛm bɛ bǎchi barɨŋɨ́ndak mbɔnyunɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́bhak chi nsé.
Báchwé amɛm nnɛm, kɛ bákɛ ghɔ mmʉɛt yi.
Ɛyɔ ɛkʉ bakwɔ Yesu bárɔk ambɨ bɛ́sɨkɨ ntɨ nɛ Yesu, nɛ mpǎy yap anjá andɔkɔ nɔkɔ chi ambɨ. 
Ngufú, ɛ́fákárí nyaka bɛ Onɛ́simɔs ándɔ́ wɔ ndu mɔ́mbɨŋɨ́ mpok chi bɛ ámpɛ́tnsɛm ntá yɛ ndu nté anɛ yi ákway bɛbhak nɛ wɔ mpoknkɛm.
Nchí ghati bhe bɛ, bɛ́bhó ɛchɔŋ, mpú pɛrɛ nyú mmɛ́mɛn kpátɛ mpok anɛ Mandɛm abhak Mfɔ bo mankɛm.”
Ngók yɛ́ ɛyɔŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fú amfay ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Sɨ́ŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn amɨk: Bɛbho ɛchɔŋ, ɛrɨ ɛcha ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ágú ɛnɛ́ yi ábhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Acha nɛ ntɨ nɛmɔt.” Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ árɛ̀m bɛ, “Ɛchi tɛtɛp, chɔŋ yi ambɔŋ nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt ndǔ bɛtɨk ɛbhi mbɔnyunɛ nsáy bɛtɨk ɛbhi ǎkoŋo yi.” 
Mpú rɛm chi ɛ̌ti bǒ abhɛn bápú bakoŋo Yesu, yɛ̌ bachi chi bo ɛpusí, yɛ̌ chí bǒ abhɛn báfyɛ̀ amɨ́k ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ bo báchák, yɛ̌ bághɛ̀p, yɛ̌ chí bo abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɔmandɛm bɛ́chák. Mpú rɛm ɛ̌ti bǒ mmɨk mbɔnyunɛ mbák mmu ándɛ́m bɛ́ apú chɛm mmʉɛt nɛ bhɔ́, abhɔŋ bɛ́rɔ́ mmɨkɨ nɛ.
Mandɛm afʉɛt nyaka ntá Moses achyɛ bho bɛbhé. Kɛ afʉɛt chi ntá Yesu Kristo kɛ ǎtɔŋ bhɛsɛ bɛrɨ̌ndu bhi nɛ tɛtɛp.
Bǎkɛ rɔ mɛnɨkmʉɛt, mbɔnyunɛ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ́ bo bábhɔ̀ŋ mpok yɔ chi ɛnyǔ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ re ghɔ wáwák tɛ nɛbhǒmɨk. Nɛ mpok yɔ ánáŋ ámfʉɛ́t, ɛnyǔ ɛsɔŋɔri yɔ ɛpu pɛrɛ bhák wáwák.
Ɛta Mandɛm akɔŋ Mɔ́ywi nɛ afyɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm yi awɔ. Mandɛm achyɛ́ yi Ɛfóŋó ɛyi njɛnti ti.
Mmɛ kɛ̌ nchí mmu anɛ achi nɛpɛ́m. Ngǔ nyaka, kɛ ghɔ́, nchí nɛpɛ́m mpoknkɛm. Nɛ mbɔ̌ŋ bɛtaŋ ndu bɛkʉ bawú mambak nɛpɛ́m, nɛ mbɔ̌ŋ ɛfɨŋɨ́ ndu mɛ́nɛ́nɛ ɛtɔkɔ́ bawú.
Sɛ́kɛ́ pɔp yɛ bɛkʉ bɛrɨ mbɔnyunɛ, mbák sɛbhɨkɨ fɛrɛ amɔ́, mpok ánkwáy, chɔŋ sɛ́ngɛm ɛrɨ́tí mbwɔt.
Kɛ mbák mmu anɛ átáŋ acha yi atwɔ ǎnu nɛ yí, andɛ́n yi, ansɔt mɛnyɨŋɨ́ nɛnu ɛbhi ɛbhɛn yi asɨkɨ ntɨ arɛ, ampɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhi andɔk ankɔrɛ nɛ bo bachak.
Bě bakoŋo Yesu bǎrɨ́ŋɨ́ sayri bɛ́ bǎchí mbɔ ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm nɛ bɛ́ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm achí nɛ bhe.
Kɛ mbák ndɔ́k ambɨ bɛbhak nɛpɛ́m fá amɨk, ɛyɔ ɛ́chyɛ̀ mɛ mbi bɛkʉ bɛtɨk Kristo ndu bɛkwak bo. Chɔŋ nsɔt yɛ chí nɛpɛ́m kɛ nɛwú-e? Ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́páy, ɛ́chá mɛ ɛnɛ́ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛsɔt.
Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bhɛsɛ bɛ Mandɛm Acha arɨ́ŋɨ́ ndu áfɛrɛ bo abhɛn bákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ mbɔ ɛnyǔ bo Mandɛm bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ, nɛ ndu átɛ̀msi bo abhɛn bápù chak, bɛ ntɛmsi yap ambak nɛ bhɔ tɛ ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɛn manyé.
Ghatí bo abhɛn báchí basɛm bɛ ɛ́rɨ mángók nɔkɔ bachi bhap ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ. Ɛrɨ bɛ mámbɔŋ ntɨ bɛkʉ bachi bhap mámbɔŋ maŋák nɛ bhɔ mpoknkɛm nɛ bɛ bákɛ́ kɛmɛ bhɔ ɛyɔŋ anyu.
Kaká ká Apɛ́lis mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛ̌ti Kristo nɛ atɔ́ŋ bɛ achi mmu ywi tɛtɛp. Kaká ka bo ɛfo ɛnɛ Aristobulɔs mankɛm.
Kɛ Pɔ̌l akɛmɛ bɛ, “Ɛta, wo mmu kɛnókó ɛkɛ kɛya kɛcha, mpú bhokori! Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n mɛ́rɛ̀m bɛchi tɛtɛp.
Bɛsɛ́ mankɛm sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ bɛbhé Mandɛm áchyɛ́ nyaka ntá Moses bɛ́rɨ mbák bo bábhʉ̀rɛ bhɔ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɛ́yàŋ.
Bɔ bábhɛ́p yɛ Yesu bɛ, “Bɛtɨk Mandɛm ɛbhɛn sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ nɔ́kɔ́ chi yi?”
Ɛ́chí ɛnyu yɔ mbɔnyunɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ bo bábhɔ̀ŋ mpabhamɨ́k nɛ batɨ nɛ ɛpɨŋ ɛnɛ́ mmu ánù chí ndiɛrɛ ndǔ ayi mmʉɛt, ɛbyɔk ɛ́bhàk arɛ, nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbɛ́ptí ɛpɨŋ ɛ́bhàk arɛ́ nkwɔ́.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ́yàŋ mǎnjwimɛm chi bɛ Mandɛm anaŋ anyu nyaka nku nɛ Ábraham, kɛ ɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ mamiɛ́ bɛsa ɛsa nsɛm amɔt nsɛm byo, achyɛ bo Israɛl ɛbhé. Bɛbhé bhɔ bɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ yɛ̌ bɛtaŋ ndu bɛway nku anɛ Mandɛm anyu nɛ Ábraham, bɛ bariɛp amɛn yi afyɛ́ nyaka akɛ pɛrɛ téé.
Bɔ́ mankɛm bábhák maknkay, batí átáká bhɔ́, bábhó bɛbhɛp batɨ bɛ, “Anɛ́ ndak-aa?”
Ǎbhʉ̀rɛ nyaka bariɛp ami bɛsí Mandɛm mmu áyábhɛ́ yi bɛ ambak mǔngo bachiǎkap nɛ mǔnto nkúbhɛ́ mbɔnyu Moses nkwɔ achi nyaka mmu anɛ ábhʉ̀rɛ bariɛp ndǔ bɛtɨk ɛbhi amɛm ɛkɛrɛ Mandɛm.
“Wɔ kɛ ɔ́chí Mpɛmɛ anɛ Jɔ̌n árɛ́mɛ́ bɛ ǎtwɔ, kɛ chi bɛ sɛ́bhɔŋ mɛnoŋ mmu achak?”
Nu ɛrɨ́tí nɛnu ɛ̌ti Yesu nɛ́ bɔ́ŋ nɛka nɛ yi, ɔ́ngɔ́ bɛ́ ɔbhɔŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti. Mandɛm abhɨ́ŋɨ́ wɔ chí ɛ̌ti nɛpɛ́m ɛnɔ mpok ɔ́rɛ́mɛ́ kpoŋoroŋ bɛsí bɛyǎ batísiɛ bɛ́ ɔnókó Yesu.
Ansɛm mpok, ɛnɛ́ bakoŋo bhi batí byo nɛ amɔt mányìɛ nɛnyíɛ́, Yesu afú bhɔ bɛsí. Are bé nɛ bhɔ nɛ ntí bɛ bágwɔt batɨ yap nɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ noko bɛ yi apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m mbɔ ɛnyǔ bo abhɛn báyámbɨ baghɔ yi bágháti bhɔ́.
Tě ka kákátí ndǔ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt, mǎmbak pě, nɛ mǎnkaka nɔkɔ Mandɛm.
Nchí sɨŋ be mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ maŋák amɛsɛ anjwi pɔɔt. 
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Mandɛm akʉ mǎndɨŋɨ tɛtɛp anɛ áchí bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́, nɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́kwak bǎrɨŋɨ ɛnyǔ yi ábhák nɛ bho mbɔ Mfɔ wap. Kɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ kʉ nɔ nɛ bo bachak.
Sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ́ Mandɛm ayámbɨ aghókó Adam kɛ ǎghoko Ifa,
Yɛ̌ndu bɔ bárɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka bɛ Mandɛm achi, babhɨkɨ chyɛ yi kɛnókó mbɔ Mandɛm, nɛ yɛ̌ chi bakak bábhɨkɨ chyɛ yi. Kɛ bárɔ́bhɛ́ kaysi chi bɛchǒŋ mɛnyɨŋ nɛ bɔ kɛkway bɛjwimɛn ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm áyàŋ bɔ mandɨŋɨ.
Akʉ nɔ nɛ mɛ yɛ̌ndu nchí rɛm nyaka ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti yi nchyɛ́ nɔkɔ yi ɛsɔŋɔri, nsɔkɔti nɔkɔ yi. Kɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ nyaka ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ mɛ̌kʉ̀ nɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ re noko nyaka yi. Ɛ́kʉ́ aghɔ mɛ ntínso.
Yesu afaté asáy mbʉ́ɛ́p arɛm bɛ, “Mbaŋ ánkwɛn!” Aghati nnyɛ́n bɛ, “Kwɛn tɨ̌!” Mbʉ́ɛ́p ámáy, mbǎŋ akwɛn chák.
Mbák ntó bhɔ mámpɛtnsɛm kɛnyiɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́, bákway bɛgu nsay ambi, nɛ bɛyǎ bhap báfú bakɔ asiɛ.”
Tɛtɛ̌tɛp, sɛ́rɛ̀m mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́, nɛ sɛ́ghàti bho chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn sɛ́ghɔ́ nɛ amɨ́k, yɛ̌ nɔ bǎpú noko mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn sɛ́ghàti bhe.
Ɛ́fákari bɛ nchiakap Mandɛm amɔt ǎsɛ̀p ndǔ nkúbhɛ́ mbi wu. Ágháká nɔ́kɔ́ arɛ, aghɔ́ yi, apé ɛbhěmbi, arɔk ɛbhak ɛyi.
Mbɔk bho bárɛ̀m bɛ, “Bɛkati Pɔ̌l ásɨ̀ŋ bɛtaŋ bɛcha nɛ bɛyɔŋ ɛbhi bɛ́tɔ̀k mmu tɛ antɨ, kɛ mpok yi achi nɛ bhɛsɛ, apú bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ nɛ apú rɛm yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chwè bo antɨ.”
Akʉ mmʉɛt yi mmɔ̌bɛtok bɛ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl mánchyɛ nɔkɔ Mandɛm kɛnókó mbɔnyunɛ yi ághɔ́ bhɔ ntínso. Ɛchi mbɔ ɛnyu Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Ndu ɛ́chí nɔ, chɔŋ ndɛm yɛ nɛ́ntɨ́ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl bɛ, wɔ ɔchí Mandɛm. Chɔŋ nkway nɔkɔ bakwáy ndu bɛ́bɨ́ti wɔ.”
Náshɔn mmɔ̌ Amínadap, Amínadap mmɔ̌ Rám, Rám mmɔ̌ Hɛ́rɔn, Hɛ́srɔn mmɔ̌ Pɛ́res, Pɛ́res mmɔ̌ Júda,
Kɛ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ yɛ̌ chí nɛ́nɛ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́bhɛ́bhɛ́ Mandɛm ǎchyɛ.”
Ɛ̌ti yɔ, Mandɛm afɛ́rɛ́ amɔ nɛ bhɔ bɛ mámkpɨk mánkʉ bɛpɔ̌ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn batɨ yap áŋwaka bɛ mánkʉ, ɛnyu ɛnɛ básɔ̀t mmʉɛt ɛyap bɛkʉ nɛ batɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chyɛ̀ bhɔ ntíánwɔ́p.
Ntí anɛ nchí ghati bhɔ mɛnyɨŋ ndǔ bakay achi bɛ, báyɨ̀ŋɨ kɛ bápú ghɔ, nɛ bághok mɛnyɨŋ mbɔ bɛ bápú ghok, nɛ bápú jwimɛm.
Nɛ ndu amɔt ndǔ barǔ nnya ɛnɛ ɛchi anyɛ́n arat ɛ́gú ɛnkɛm. Nɛ bɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ bachwi anɛ áchí anyɛ́n, ndu amɔt ndǔ baru arat áchɔ́ŋɔ.
Puyɛ̌ mmʉɛt anɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm áchyɛ̀ kɛ ayambɨ. Anɛ bǒ mmɨk kɛ áyámbɨ, kɛ anɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm áchyɛ̀ antwɔ chɔŋ ansɛm mpok.
Bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bhɔ bɛ́kʉ bafɔ mánchɛm ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt wu nɔ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ ndǔ ɛyɔŋ bo Israɛl bɛ Amágɛdɔn.
Anɛ ájwí bati arat nkwɔ asɔt yí kɛ agú kɛbhɔ́ŋ mmɔ́ nɛ yi. Ɛ́fákári ɛnyumɔt nɛ bɔ mankɛm bati tándrámɔt.
Kɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm ákʉ́ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ bhi bághátí bo tɛsáy bɛ, Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò, abhɔŋ bɛghɔ ɛsɔŋɔri, Mandɛm akʉ yɔ ɛfu tɛtɛp.” Tɨ́k yɛ́ ka nsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛka, mámpɛtnsɛm ntá Mandɛm, bɛ yi amfoŋori bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛka.
Ɛnyu yɔ kɛ ɛ́chí nɛ bhe. Mandɛm arɨ́ŋɨ́ yɛ̌ chí mpǎy bɛkaká ɛmɛnɛ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chí yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka anti.
Yesu arɛm nɔkɔ nɔ, abhɛ́p ntɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm bɛ, “Ɔkáysí bɛ ndǔ nkwɔ wu bati arat, agha átɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́ achi nkokosi ntá anɛ akwɛnɛ amɔ bághɛ́p?”
Bǒ abhɛn bákʉ̀ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛtaya mmu achi amfay áyàŋ bɔ́ mankʉ, kɛ báchí maya, nɛ bɔ̌maya.”
Bákɛ́m nnya mbʉ́mbʉ yɔ nɛ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ nsé mmu ákʉ̀ nyaka mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay bɛsí nnya mbʉ́mbʉ. Ɛnyu yɔ̌ kɛ̌ yi árwɔ bho, báká bɛ mámfyɛ́ bhɔ ɛrɨ̌ŋ ɛnɛ́ nnya mbʉ́mbʉ amʉɛt nɛ báchyɛ́ ntí ako yi kɛnókó. Bakɛm nɔkɔ nnya mbʉ́mbʉ nɛ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ nsé bágʉ́ɛp bhɔ, amík anti fúú, amɛm nɛpǐngo anɛ ádù nɛ sɔ́lfɔ.
Bo mankɛm abhɛn bachi amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí, bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, batɨ ábé bhɔ amɛm tontó.
Páílet ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn, asɔt Yesu afú nɛ yi, achɔkɔ ndǔ ɛnɔk ntaŋá manyé, nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ ndu ɛyɔŋ bo Israɛl bɛ́ Gabáta. Nɔ́ chi, nɛbhʉɛt batǎy batay.
Josɛ́f nɛ Nikɔdɛ́mɔs báfɛ́rɛ Yesu ndǔ ɛkotákátí, básɔ́t bɛ́syɛ́ndɛn nɛ babhé amɔ arɛ́, mánɛ́p yi bɛkoŋo ɛpɨŋ bo Israɛl.
Bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ Píta arɛmɛ, ɛ́kwɛ́n bɔ́ tɛ antɨ. Babhɛp Píta nɛ bǒnto bachak bɛ, “Bɔ̌ma, chɔŋ sɛ́nkʉ yɛ ná?”
Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ beku, baghɔkɔ́ bhi bárɔ́k ntá yi barɛm bɛ, “Nywɔp nɛ́naŋ nɛrɔŋ, nɛ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ chi ɛbhɨ. Ghatí bǒbhɛn bɛ mándɔ́k ndǔ bɔ̌bɛtɔk abhɛn báchí fá kɛkwɔt manku ɛnyɨŋ mɛ́nyiɛ.”
Ndɔŋ anɛ ákʉ́ ɛ́rát ɛnɛ nchí twɔ bɛghɔ bɛ bǎkɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk bɛ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ mbák bo mándɛm bɛ mmǔ ákʉ́ ndak, bábhɔŋ bɛ́twɔ nɛ batísiɛ bapay, mbák apu nɔ, barat.
Kɛ ndu Yesu áyíbhírí mmʉɛt aghɔ baghɔkɔ́ bhi, aji Píta bɛ, “Satan, fá mɛ́ bɛsí! Nkaysi yɛ chi anɛ nkwǎŋwaŋ, abhɨ́kɨ́ fu ntá Mandɛm!” 
Bǒ bhɛsɛ chi bǒ Mandɛm nɛ bábhɔŋ bɛ́fyɛ ntí ndu bɛkʉ bɛrɨ, bɛ́ ɛ́kɛ́ be bhɔ mmʉɛt bɛ́kwak bo abhɛn ɛyap ɛ́pú. Bákɛ́ bhák mbɔ mmu anɛ ápú kʉ bɛrɨ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛni.
Ɛyɔ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ mbɔ̌ŋ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm ǎchɛm nɛ batɨ yɛsɛ nɛ ǎkʉ sɛndɨŋɨ bɛ sɛchi bɔ Mandɛm.
Kɛ bákɛ bhɔŋ yɛ̌ mbi. Bɛyǎ bho báfú báré sénse amʉɛt Yesu, kɛ yɛ̌ mmú kɛrɛm ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kway bɛkʉ bɛ mángwáy yi. Ɛ́tárɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, bo bati apay báfú báté bɛsí bataŋá manyé,
Ɛchi kpoŋoroŋ bɛ Acha ywɛsɛ Yesu afu nyaka ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt Júda, nɛ Moses ábhɨ́kɨ́ rɛm yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛ̌ti nnɛrɛ́kɛt wu mpok yi árɛ̀m ɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti bachiǎkap. 
Baghɔkɔ́ bhi bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, mmʉɛt agú bhɔ. Kɛ Yesu apɛt arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Bɔ̌bha, ɛ́be mmʉɛt tontó bɛ mmu anka Mandɛm ambak Mfɔ ywi!
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, nɛ ndǔ mbát mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Kristo nchí kwáy bɛdɛp awɔ́ antɨ ɛ̌ti bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn mɛ̌kʉ̀ ntá Mandɛm.
Nɛ bɛ́rɔ́ŋ ndu ngwɛ́nti, mǔnti bo Mandɛm abhɔŋ bɛ́kɛ́m Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu nɛ bɛtaŋ mbɔ ndu sɛ́tɔ́ŋ. Mbok yɔ́ achí tɛtɛp nɛ ɛnyumɔt mpoknkɛm. Ɛyɔ ɛ́kwàk mǔnti ámfyɛ́ bo ntɨ ndu átɔ̀ŋ bhɔ, ɛ́mpɛt ɛ́nkwak yi ányúrɛ́ bo abhɛn bátɔ̀ŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́pú ndɔ́ŋ ámɔ́t nɛ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm.
Nɛ mbák aghɔ wu, ǎpɔkɔ anyaŋa mankɨ nɛ maŋák,
Bǎghok mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi árɛ́mɛ́ ndu bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ́ ǎyɛnti mmʉɛt nɛ Mandɛm. Bǎkaysi bɛ yi? Báká ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt bɛ mángwáy yi.”
Sɛptí yɛ̌ ka mmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm. Bǎkɛ́ chyɛ Satan mbi, nɛ chɔŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́nkʉ yi ambʉ́ɛ́ andɔ bhe.
‘Nɛ ɔbhɔŋ bɛkɔŋ Mandɛm Acha ywɛ nɛ ntɨ ɛnɛ nɛnkɛm, nɛ ɛfóŋó ɛyɛ ɛnkɛm, nɛ nkaysi yɛ nkɛm, nɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛ mɛnkɛm.’
Tɛtɛp, ndǔ ndak anɛ, nku nsɨ́ abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ mbɔnyunɛ sɛ́rɔbhɛ koŋo chi Nku Nkɔ anɛ áchá nku nsɨ́ ndǔ átɔ̀ŋ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ Mandɛm tontó.
Nchí kaka Yesu Kristo Acha ywɛsɛ tontó. Yi kɛ áchyɛ́ mɛ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn. Nchí chyɛ yí bakak mbɔnyunɛ aghɔ bɛ́ nkway bɛ́bhak mǔbɛtok yi, ayap yɛ mɛ bɛ́ nkʉ bɛtɨk ɛbhi.
mbɔnyunɛ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ kɛ bɛ́kʉ̀ mángɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ. Ndu ɛchi nɔ kɛ bárɛ̀m bɛ, “Mbʉɛrɛ kɛnɔ́, ŋɛmɛ́! Fú ndǔ nɛwú, nɛ chɔŋ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ Kristo mɛ́ngɔ wɔ amʉɛt.”
Kʉ ka yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ kɛnywinti ansɛm nɛ batɨ, nɛ bǎkɛ bhak bɛyɔŋ bɛyɔŋ.
Mbák mmu ǎmàkati nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn yi áyàŋ mɛnyiɛ, yɛ̌ nɔ, andɔk ambɨ anyíɛ́ nɔ́, nɔ abhɔ̌ŋ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bɛsí Mandɛm nɛ ntí bɛ ǎnyiɛ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn yi ábhɨ́kɨ́ noko bɛ ɛchi chak bɛ yi ányíɛ́. Mbák mmu ǎkʉ̀ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi anoko bɛ ɛpu chak, nɔ ákʉ́ bɛbʉ́.
Bǒ abhɛn báchí amɛm ɛjuri, bághɔ bɛyǎ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́. Bǒ abhɛn báchí ndǔ mmɨk ndɨ́kándǐ nɛwu, mbaŋ ǎghɔ ɛtɔk ɛyap nɛ́nɛ.”
Ɛ́kʉ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Jeremáya árɛ́mɛ́ bɛ́ chɔŋ ɛ́mfakari, ɛmfu tɛtɛp.
María achɔkɔ nɛ Ɛlísabɛt ndǔ bataŋ árát, kɛ ǎpɛtnsɛm ɛkɛt ɛyi. 
Ɛnɛ́ bo bághòk mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Yesu árɛ̀m, arɔk ambɨ bɛtɛm nɛkay nɛchak. Ntí abhak bɛ, anáŋ agháká nyaka kɛkwɔt nɛ Yerúsalɛm, nɛ bo bákàysi nyaka bɛ Kɛfɔ Mandɛm kɛ́twɔ̀ fá amɨk mandú mpok.
Bǎchí bǒ abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ kɛboŋ. Bě bábhɔŋ mǎnjɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛghɔ mbák ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́nɛ́ mɛ́rɛ̀m ɛ́pú tɛtɛp.
Mpǎy babhakanɛm abhɛn manyíɛ́ brɛt wu nɛ nsi ɛyɔ ábhák mbɔ nka ɛtay, kɛfyɛ́ baghɔrɛ́ nɛ bhɔ. 
Ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ Mandɛm Acha ághátí bhɛsɛ sɛnkʉ, mpok árɛ́mɛ́ bɛ, ‘Nkʉ wɔ ɔ́mbák ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ ntá bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl, bɛ́ ndǔ bɛtaŋ Mandɛm, ɔ́nkwak mmɨk nkɛm ambɔŋ nɛpɛ́m.’”
Yesu achwe amɛm ɛkɛrákap, abho bɛtɔŋ bho Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm. Ndǔ yí ákʉ̀ nɔ, bǒbati bachiǎkap nɛ bǒbati ɛtɔk báchák bárɔ́k ntá yi bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ntɨkɨ bɛtaŋ ɔ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nɛ ɔ́kʉ̀? Agha áchyɛ́ wɔ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɔ?”
Mɛ Pɔ̌l mǔnto Yesu Kristo bɛkoŋo nkaysi Mandɛm, kɛ nchí sɨŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ. Nchí fá nɛ ntɨ mǔnkwɔ ywɛsɛ Tímɔti.
Jɔ̌n Njwiti atwɔ nyaka antarɛ nɔkɔ nsay ndu mɛnɨkmʉɛt, nɛ mmɛ́m yi kɛnyu. Bě bǎre rɛm bɛ, ‘Ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛchi nɛ yi!’
Nɨk nɔ́kɔ́ ká mmʉɛt ɛ̌ti ya nkwɔ bɛ Mandɛm anchyɛ mɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛghati bo ɛ̌ti Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ achi nyaka bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ nkɛbhɔŋ bɛcháy.
Awu áfʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, ngɔ́ ángɛl ndǔ áfú amfay ásɛ̀p amɨk. Akɛ́m ɛfɨŋɨ́ nɛpi ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.
Mpok ɛyɔ, bǎbhɔŋ nyaka ntɨkɨ nsáy ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bákʉ̀, ɛbhɛn-nɛ bǎbhɔŋ ntíánwɔ́p bɛkʉ nɛ́nɛ? Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ bɛ́twɔ̀ chi nɛ nɛwú.
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, chɔŋ bɛsɛ mankɛm sɛndɔk ambɨ mɛnoko Mmɔ Mandɛm, nɛ ndu bɛrɨŋɨ yi ɛnyu ɛ́mɔt. Mbák sɛ́chí ɛnyu ɛyɔ, chɔŋ sɛ́ngo sɛ́nsɛnɛ, nɛ sɛ́naŋa bɛbhak mbɔ Kristo.
Baghɔk Yesu báchák bati byo bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Jems nɛ Jɔ̌n bárɛ́mɛ́, bábhó bɛběntɨ nɛ bhɔ.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Fá amɨk, baghɔrɛ́ nɛ babhakanɛm bábháy batɨ,
Mandɛm Mmu achí Chi ntá Yesu Acha arɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ mpú sénse. Bakak ámbak nɛ yi ngwɛnti ti.
Mbák bawú bápú pɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, ntí anɛ sɛ́kà nɛwú mpoknkɛm achi bɛ yi?
Nchí ghati yɛ be bɛ, mbák mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎkʉ̀ bɛbhɨkɨ cha ɛbhɛ́n batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm nɛ ɛbhɛn bǒnkwɔ Fárisi, bǎpú bhák bo abhɛn Mandɛm achi Mfɔ wap.” 
Mmu wu ǎbhɔ́ŋ yɛ chí batɨ ápáy. Mɔ́nkwɛn ngɔrɛ́ nɛ baghɔrɛ́ bachak abhɛn bábhɨkɨ bhɔ́ŋ manɛm bafyɛ́ ntí chí ndǔ bɛtɨk Acha Yesu. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap ǎyaŋ bɛ́chyɛ ntɨ nɛ mmʉɛt nkɛm chí ntá Mandɛm. Kɛ nkaysi ngɔrɛ́ anɛ ábháy nnɛ́m, ǎbhák chí ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ mmɨk, nɛ ǎyáŋ bɛkʉ chí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́kʉ nnɛ́m aywi ambɔŋ maŋák nɛ yi.
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu nɛ bakoŋo bhi bápɛtnsɛm anywɔ́p, bo abhɛn báchɛ́mɛ́ arɛ́, bápɛt baya bacha, ɛkʉ yí nɛ bakoŋo bhi kɛbhɔ́ŋ yɛ̌ ɛpok ndu mɛ́nyiɛ nɛnyíɛ́.
Yɛ̌ mmu apu bhɔŋ chɔŋ bɛtɔŋ ntɨ, nɛ yɛ̌ chi ntɨ manɔ bɛ, ‘Dɨŋɨ́ Mandɛm’, mbɔnyunɛ bo mankɛm bárɨ̀ŋɨ chɔŋ mɛ, bɛbho amʉɛt ndɛ́ndɛmɛ bho bɛghaka amʉɛt manɛ́m bho.
Kɛ mǔnkwɔ Fárisi amɔt, anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ Gamáliɛl, abhak arɛ́. Abhak mmu ɛchɛmɛ́ bǒ batí amɔt nkwɔ́ nɛ ntɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm. Bǒ mankɛm báchyɛ̀ nyaka yi kɛnókó. Afate achyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ mántɛn kpɨk bǒnto Yesu nɛfí.
Mánaŋ bátɔŋ nyaka yí mbi Yesu Acha nɛ ághàti nyaka bo mɛnyɨŋ abhɛn bɛ́dù yi antɨ bɛghati bo ɛ̌ti Yesu nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyu bɔ bɛchi. Kɛ arɨŋɨ chí nɛjwiti ɛnɛn Jɔ̌n atɔŋɔ bo.
Kɛnɔ́ ɛkɛn Yesu árɛ́mɛ́ nyaka bɛ Lásárɔs ǎbhʉrɛ kɛbhak chi nɛwú kɛ bákáysi bɛ Yesu arɛm chi bɛ Lásárɔs ábhʉ̀rɛ kɛnɔ́ mbɔ́ŋ.
Sɛ́mbɨ́tí Mandɛm nɛ Chi Yesu Kristo Acha ywɛsɛ. Achí Mandɛm ntínso nɛ ǎchyɛ bhɛsɛ nɛpɔptǐntɨ́.
“Mpok mmu ywɛka ánɨ̀kmʉɛt, ákɛ́ rɛm bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ntí nɛ nnɛt, mbɔ bǒ abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl bákʉ̀. Bákʉ̀ nɔ mbɔnyunɛ bákaysi bɛ bɛyǎ kɛpɨ kɛ kɛ́kʉ̀ Mandɛm angok nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt ɛnap.
Yɛ̌ ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛ́pú pɛrɛ ghɔɔ amɛm ɛtɔk ɛyɔ. Maŋák amɛn ábhàk mpok mmu abhay ngɔrɛ́ apú pɛrɛ bhák arɛ́. Chɔŋ ɛ́mfakari ɛnyu ɛyɔ nɛ Bábilɔn mbɔnyunɛ bakɔ̌siɛ́ bhi abhɛn báchá báchák mankɛm bátwɔ nta bǒ mmɨk mankɛm nɛ bapu.
Kɛ dɔ́k ká ambɨ bɛgo ndǔ nɛrɨŋɨ anɛ bǎrɨ̀ŋɨ Yesu Kristo mmu achi Acha nɛ Mpɛmɛ ywɛsɛ, mǎndɔk ambɨ bɛ́go ndu bɛ́bhak ɛnyunɛ́ bɛrɨ̌ndu bhi bɛ́bhák nɛ bhe. Kɛnókó kɛ́mbak nɛ yi nɛ́nɛ, nɛ mpoknkɛm.
Ndu bɛrɔŋ ambɨ, bǎrɨŋɨ mpok anɛ sɛchi arɛ́ nɛ́nɛ. Mpok mɛ́ŋɛ́mɛ ndǔ kɛnɔ́ akway mbɔnyunɛ mpok anɛ Mandɛm ánaŋa bɛpɛmɛ bhɛsɛ achí kɛkwɔt nɛ́nɛ achá mpok anɛ sɛ́bho nyaka mɛnoko Yesu Kristo.
Ndu manywɔp ɛyɔ, chɔŋ nkʉ Ɛfóŋó ya ɛ́ntwɔ́ ntá bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk abha, abhɛ́n baghɔrɛ́, nɛ abhɛn babhakanɛm, nkʉ bɔ́ mángati barak anɛ́ mfyɛ́ bɔ́ antɨ.
“Mɛ Klaudiɔs Lísias kɛ nchí sɨŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ ntá Ɛta yɛsɛ gɔ́bhanɔ Fɛ́liks. Ɛta, nchí to wɔ bakak.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mɔt kɛ baghati bɛsɛ, nɔ chi bɛ, sɛkɛ ghɔkɔntɨk bɛchyɛ nɔkɔ nɛkwak ntá bachɛ́bhɛ́bho abhɛn Yerúsalɛm, nkúbhɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi nyaka mɛ antɨ bɛ́kʉ. 
Yɛ̌ ndu ɛchi nɔ, nchí ghati bhe ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi tɛtɛp. Ɛ́rɨ ntá yɛka bɛ́ ndɔ́k mbɔnyunɛ mbák mbɨ́kɨ́ rɔŋ, Nkwak apú twɔ́ ntá yɛka. Kɛ mbák ndɔ́k, chɔŋ ntó yi ntá yɛka.
Páílet abhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Wɔ kɛ ɔ́chí nɛ́ Mfɔ bo Israɛl?” Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Ɛ́chí mbɔ ɛnyu ɔ́rɛ́mɛ́.”
Yesu aghati yí bɛ, “Faté, pɔkɔ́ ɛ̌sák ɛyɛ kɔ.”
Kɛ Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ́ bɛ, “Sayri sayri, máyá chi agha? Nɛ ntɨkɨ bho bachi bɔ̌maya?”
Bábhɔ́ŋ maŋák tontó nɛ babhak maknkay bɛ yi achi nɛpɛ́m. Ɛkʉ bɔ́ kɛnókó bɛ ɛchi tɛtɛp. Yesu abhɛ́p bɔ́ bɛ, “Bǎbhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ mɛnyiɛ fá?”
Mbák mpú kʉ chi bɛtɨk Ɛtaya, bǎkɛ́ noko mɛ.
Bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn sɛ́kʉ̀, sɛ́kʉ̀ bhɔ chi mbɔnyunɛ ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ́ Kristo ɛ́pùri bhɛsɛ. Sɛ́noko bɛ ndu Kristo ágú ɛ̌ti yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu, bɛsɛ́ mankɛm sɛ́náŋ sɛgu.
Bárɨŋɨ ɛrɨ́tí ɛnɔk chí ndǔ kɛpɛm ɛki. Bápú rɔŋ ndu támfáŋ mánkɔ́k nɛpɨ.
Kɛ mmu amɔt anɛ aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Banábas asɔt yí arɔk ntá bǒnto Yesu. Aghati bhɔ ɛnyǔ Sɔ̌l aghɔ Yesu Acha ambi mpok yi árɔ̀ŋ Damáskɔs nɛ ɛnyǔ Yesu árɛ́mɛ́ kɛpɨ nɛ yi. Aghati nkwɔ́ bɔ́ ɛnyǔ Sɔ̌l átɔ́ŋ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm kpoŋoroŋ ndu nnyɛ́n Yesu awu Damáskɔs kɛbhɔ́ŋ bɛcháy.
Nɛchwe ɔ́chwé ɔ́káká mɛ, mmɔ́ anɛ achi mɛ mɛniɛ ayoŋ mmʉɛ́t nɛ maŋák.
Anɛnɛ nnyǔ nɛpi ɛnɔ. Mɔ́ngo are fú arɛ tontó mbɔ mɔ́ngo anɛ áfù ndǔ nɛpi ɛnɛn ngó ádù arɛ. Mɔ́ngo wu akútí mmok, mbǎŋ arɔbhɛ giri gíri pyɔɔ.
Mbák Mandɛm afɛ́rɛ́ be bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl ndǔ ɛnɔk ólif ɛnɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ pɨ abhat ndǔ ɛnɛ bápɨ́, mbák yi ǎkway bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ mbɔ ɛyɔ, nɔ ɛchi mandú ɛnyɨŋ ntá yi bɛkɛmɛ bo Israɛl ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ achi nyaka awap, tɛ̌ndu bɔ kɛ bachi mbɔ̌ŋ batap ɛnɔk ólif ɛnɛ bapɨ. 
Bábhé mmɔ́ ngɔrɛ́ nsɛm mbɔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu achak. Mmɔ ngɔrɛ́ anɛ ápú nsɛm, bábhé yi chi bɛkoŋo bariɛp Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka nɛ Ábraham.
Abhɨŋɨ mmɔ̌bɛtok amɔt abhɛ́p yí bɛ ‘Ntɨkɨ ndak áchí fá ɛchɔŋ?’
Arɛ́ ndǔ nɛchyɛ Míra, mǔnti batɛmɛ́ nɛnu aghɔ́ áchwí anɛ áfú Aleksándriya, ɛtɔk Íjip, árɔ̀ŋ Itali. Afɛrɛ bhɛsɛ́ ndǔ ayɛsɛ́ áchwí afyɛ́ amɛm awu.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ mɛ́rɛ̀m puyɛ̌ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Acha aghati mɛ. Nchí rɛm chi mbɔ ɛchɨŋtímu.
Ɛtɔk ɛ́bhɔ́ŋ ɛrɛmɛ nkok anɛ akabhɛ yɔ. Nkók wu asap amfay. Ábhɔ́ŋ manyǔbhá byó nɛ apay. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nyǔ-ɛbhá ábhɔ́ŋ ángɛl anɛ ábhàbhɛri wu. Básɨ́ŋ manyɛ́n manɛrɛ́kɛt Israɛl byo nɛ apay ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nyǔbhá ábhɔ́ŋ ɛni nnyɛ́n.
Kɛ Jɔ̌n kɛyaŋ bɛjwiti Yesu. Are yáŋ bɛkʉ Yesu anjibhiri nkaysi yi. Arɛm bɛ, “Ɔtwɔ bɛ njwítí wɔ, ɛnɛ́ mɛ kɛ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́twɔ ntá yɛ bɛ ɔ́njwítí mɛ́?”
Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi báchwɔp Jɛríko. Ɛnɛ́ bɔ́ bárɔ́ Jɛríko bɛ́rɔŋ, ngɛ́mtay bho bare koŋo bhɔ́ ansɛm. Nnɛ́mámɨk amɔt anɛ aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Batímaɔs, mmɔ́ Timáyɔs, abhak nɛpaká mbi chɔ́kɔ́.
Ndu mbʉ́ɛ́p ataŋataŋ ádɛ̀p áchwí ywɛsɛ, are jaŋari mbɔ bɛ ǎyaŋ bɛbɛt. Nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́, bábhó mɛ́mɛ́sɛ batu ányɛn.
Mbák ɔ́nkʉ́ nɔ, bo bápú rɨŋɨ bɛ ɔchí ndǔ nɛtarɛ́nsay, kɛ Ɛtayɛ mmu bápú ghɔ́ nɛ amɨ́k ǎrɨŋɨ. Nɛ chɔŋ Ɛtayɛ mmu ághɔ̀ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mmu ákʉ̀ bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ ankap wɔ.” 
Bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bhɔ bɛré nɨk Yesu mmʉɛt bɛ́ ákɛ́ tó bhɔ amɛm nɛpi ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.
Abho yɛ bɛghati bhɔ bɛ, “Ɛchɔŋ, ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ basɨŋɨ́ mɛn árɛ̀m ɛ́fákárí mbɔ ɛnyǔ bǎghókó.”
Kaká ká Príska nɛ nnɛ́m ayi Akwíla. Bákʉ̀ nyaka bɛtɨk Yesu Kristo nɛ mɛ.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bǎchí arɛ. Chí nɛbhʉɛt anɛ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ Satan ɛchi! Bǎte kpirí nɛ mɛ nɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔt bɛsɨkɨ ntɨ nɛ mɛ yɛ̌ chí ndǔ mpok anɛ báwày Antipas mmu achi nyaka ntísiɛ wa anɛ ághàti nyaka bǒ tɛtɛp Mandɛm nɛ ntɨ nɛmɔt. Báwáy yi nɛntɨ ɛnɛka ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ Satan áchɔ̀kɔ.
ndu nchí yaŋ bɛ bǒ ɛtɔk ɛya mámbɔ́ŋ mpabhamɨ́k, mánjaŋ bɛbhak mbɔ bhe. Ɛyɔ ɛ́kwáy bɛkʉ bɛ mbɔk ɛyap mántɨ́knsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhap bɛ Mandɛm ámpɛ́mɛ́ bhɔ́.
Chɔŋ nnya mbʉmbʉ nɛ babhaŋ ayi byo anɛ ate ndǔ bafɔ byo mámpap ngɔrɛ́-nɛkɔ. Chɔŋ mánsɔt yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́, mankʉ yi andɔp ɛbho ɛwɔ. Chɔŋ mányiɛ nyamwʉɛ́t ɛyi nɛ mánsɔŋ yi nɛ ngó.
Mandɛm Ɛtayɛsɛ nɛ Yesu Kristo Acha mántɔŋ be bɛrɨ̌ndu, mánchyɛ bhe kpák. 
Ndɔŋ ɛyɔ bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Wɔmbɔ̌ŋ ɔrɛm bɛ ɔchí agha? Ghatí bhɛsɛ mmu wɔ ɔchí bɛ́ sɛ́mpɛ́tnsɛm nɛ ɛyɔŋ ntá bo abhɛn bátó bhɛsɛ. Wɔmbɔ̌ŋ ɔchí agha?”
Bɔ̌bha, bǎkɛ́ rɔ bɛbhak ndǔ nɛbharɛ́mʉɛt nɛ Mmɔ, bɛ mpok anɛ yi ápɛ̀tnsɛm fá amɨk, mǎmbɔ́ŋ maŋák bɛghɔ yi, kɛbhɔŋ bɛcháy nɛ ntíánwɔ́p bɛsí bhi mpok yi átwɔ̀.
Ananías árɔ́ yɛ arɔk áchwé amɛm ɛkɛt ɛnɛ́ Sɔ̌l áchi arɛ. Anyaŋa yí amɔ ántí arɛm bɛ, “Sɔ̌l, manɔ́, mbɔŋ Yesu Acha mmu abhésí ntá yɛ ankɔŋɔmbi mpok ɔ́twɔ̀ fá, kɛ átó mɛ́ nkʉ́ ɔ́mpɛt ɔ́ngɔ́ mbaŋ nɛ bɛ́ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ambak nɛ wɔ.”
Nɛ báchyɛ yɔ mbi bɛ ánu nɛ bo Mandɛm ánsɔt awɔ́nɛm. Nɛ báchyɛ yɔ bɛtaŋ amfay yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nnɛrɛ́kɛt bho ankɛm fá amɨk, nɛ amfǎy bo Mandɛm, nɛ amfǎy bǒ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk nɛ amfǎy bǒ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛtɔk.
kɛ basɛ́mɛ́ ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ mmɨk atwɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ yi antɨ, nɛ ngoŋó nkáp, nɛ ɛkwak bɛbhɔŋ mɛnyǔ mɛnyɨŋ bɛchak mɛnkɛm, angɔkɔntɨk Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ɛnɛ ɛchi arɛ́, yɔ kɛkwak yi ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛni.
Nchí nɨkmʉɛt ntá yɛ ɛ̌ti mɔ́wa Ɔnɛ́simɔs mmu ndɔ́bhɛ́ ɛtayi fá amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ.
Yesu atɛ́m nɛkay ɛnɛ́nɛ́fú bɛ, “Mpok Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm nchí twɔ, mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́bhak mbɔ ɛnyu ɛ́fákárí nyaka nɛ mmu amɔt nɛ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk abhi. Nywɔp nɛ́mɔ́t, achyɛ nkáp bɛ mándɔp mánkɔ nɔkɔ ɛsiɛ́ nɛ wu.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́chí ɛnɛ nnáŋ nchí yaŋ nɔkɔ bɛkʉ, nɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛyɔ chi bɛghati bo Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Kristo mbǎŋ ɛnkɛm ɛnɛ́ bo bábhɨ́kɨ́re ghok yɔ. Kɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ yaŋ bɛkʉ bɛtɨk ndǔ nɛbhʉ́ɛ́rɛ́kɛt ɛnɛn mmu achak.
Bakoŋo Yesu bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, bápɔ́p! Babho bɛbhɛp yi bɛ, “Mbák ɛnyu yɔ kɛ̌ ɛchi, ághá yɛ́ ákway bɛbhak mmu anɛ Mandɛm ápɛmɛ?”
Ghatí baséansi abhɛn babhakanɛm bɛ mándɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛkɛm mmʉɛt nɛ bɛ mámbʉrɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnap ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ bo báchyɛ̀ bhɔ kɛnókó. Ghatí bhɔ bɛ bábhɔŋ bɛtɔŋ bɛ bábhɔ̌ŋ kɛboŋ, mánkɛm baraká Mandɛm ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ ɛ́yàŋ nɛ bɛ bábhɔŋ bɛbhɔŋ ɛkɔŋ nɛ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ.
Batɔŋ-ɛbhé Mandɛm nɛ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi báyá ngɔrɛ́ anɛ bákɛ́mɛ́ ndǔ akwɛn bɛrwɔp, bátwɔ́ nɛ yi, bátɛp bɛsí bǒ mankɛm.
Nɛka ɛnɛn Ɛnɔk kɛ nɛ́kʉ́ Mandɛm asɔrɛ yi amfay ɛnɛ́ yi abhɨkɨ ghɔ́ nɛwú. Ɛ́kʉ yɛ̌ mmu kɛghɔ́ yi ndu Mandɛm anaŋ asɔrɛ nyaka yi. Kɛ Mandɛm ápɛ́rɛ́ sɔt Ɛnɔk, ánáŋ atɔŋ nyaka bɛ abhɔŋ maŋák nɛ yi.
Nɛ ntá bo abhɛn báfyɛ̀ mmɛ́m ndǔ bɛbhǎ nkwɔbhɛ́nya, mmǔ apú kway bɛfyɛ mmɛ́m bakɔ amɛm ɛsɨ́ ɛbhǎ nkwɔbhɛnya, mbɔnyunɛ, mbák ánkʉ ɛnyu yɔ, mmɛ́m bakɔ ǎkʉ ɛsɨ́ ɛbha ɛ́nsɛn, ɛnchɔŋɔ, mmɛ́m andɔk amɨk. Báfyɛ mmɛ́m bakɔ chi amɛm ɛbhǎ nkwɔbhɛ́nya ɛnɛ ɛkɔ.” 
Ngók ndǔ bɛfóŋó ɛbhɔ bɛ́bɨ̀k nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ bɛ, “Mandɛm Acha, wɔ mmu ɔ́chí nyáŋá, ɔbhak tɛtɛp, chɔŋ ɛ́ntat ná kɛ ɔ́ntaŋ bǒ mmɨk abhɛn báwáy bhɛsɛ, ɔ́nkɛmɛ kɛ́mbé?”
Bɔ̌ma, mbɨ́kɨ́ yaŋ mǎngɔ́kɔ́ntɨk ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fákárí nyaka nɛ bachǐmbɨ bhɛsɛ mpok bákɔ̀ nɛ Moses amɛm baso. Mandɛm akʉ ɛkpɔkɔ́ nɛbhaŋ ɛ́kúti bhɔ, Manyu Chu akɔrɛ bɛbhe bɛ́páy bákɔ́ amɨk bápé bárɔ́k ɛbhe ɛ́chák.
Ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ̌ nchí jɛt téé bɛ́rɔŋ ndǔ ngwɛnti. Mpú mbɔ mmu anɛ áté bɛ́dɛ́p ɛ̌kwɔ́t nɛ ntɨ, kɛ andɔ yí, andɛp nɔkɔ chí mbʉ́ɛ́p.
Bo bábhaka nyaka ntɨ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Jɔ̌n árɛ̀m nɛ ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ̀. Ɛ́kʉ bábho bɛbhɛp mmʉɛt mbák Jɔ̌n kɛ achi Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò.
Arɔk ambɨ mɛnɨk Yesu mmʉɛt bɛ ákɛ́ to bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bhɔ atú ɛtɔk achak.
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, nu ká mɛ́máka ɛpɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛrɨ ɛcha ndǔ nɛka ɛnɛka nɛ Yesu, mǎnu nkwɔ bɛrɨŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́chí wɨkɨrɨk chí ɛnɛ́? Bɛrɛm bɛ, ‘Mfóŋórí bɛbʉ́ bhɛ’, kɛ chi bɛrɛm bɛ, ‘Faté kɔ’?
Bábhó yɛ mɛmak nɛ amɔ ndu bɛbhɛp chimɔ nnyɛ́n ɛnɛn yi áyàŋ manchyɛ mɔ.
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bágháká Bɛtsáida, bǒfú básɔ́t nnɛ́mámɨ́k bárɔ́k ntá yi, mánɨkmʉɛt bɛ ántɔk yi.
Bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ bǒ ɛchɛmɛ́ bataŋá manyé bachak mankɛm báré yaŋ bǒ abhɛn bákway bɛbhat Yesu barak amʉɛt ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ bɔ́ bábhɔŋ mbi bɛway yi.
Náhɔ mmɔ̌ Sɛ́rug, Sɛ́rug mmɔ̌ Réu, Réu mmɔ̌ Pɛ́lɛk, Pɛ́lɛk mmɔ̌ Ɛ́ba, Ɛ́ba mmɔ̌ Shɛ́la,
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ́sɨ̀ŋ ntá yɛka ɛchi tɛtɛp. Mandɛm arɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ mpu sénse.
Kɛ Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ re pay amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mfɔ Debhít ákú mpok yi áyàŋ ɛnyɨŋ mɛnyiɛ ndǔ nsay ákɛ́mɛ́ yi nɛ bɔ̌bhi?
Mbák nkwɛn ɛbhé nɛ nkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́yàŋ bɛ mángwáy mɛ nká nɛwú. Kɛ tɛ̌ndu barak anɛ́ bɔ́ bábhàt mɛ amʉɛt apú tɛtɛp, yɛ̌ mmú apú kwáy bɛfyɛ mɛ amɔ́ yap. Nyé ɛna nɛ́bhɔŋ bɛ́rɔ́ŋ ntá Mfɔ Rom.”
Mbák chí bɛsɛ, bɛyǎ batísiɛ bakap bhɛsɛ. Ndu ɛchi nɔ, sɛ́ndɔ́ yɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́nwɔ̀p bhɛsɛ, nɛ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛn bɛ́gwɔ̀t bɛsɛ, sɛ́njɛt ntiɛt anɛ sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́jɛt nɛ ɛkɨ́kɨ́.
Ɛkʉ bǒnto Yesu batí byó nɛ apay bábhɨŋɨ nkwɔ bakoŋo Yesu bárɛm bɛ, “Ɛpú chak bɛ sɛndɔ bɛghati bho Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm, sɛ́ndɔbhɛ taŋ chi baraká nɛnyɛ́.
Kɛ bo Israɛl bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ ngɛ́mtay bo báchɛ̀m arɛ́ ɛnyu ɛyɔ, bábhɔ́ŋ bɛyǎ mpabhamɨ́k nɛ bɔPɔ̌l. Bábhó bɛsɔkɔti Pɔ̌l mánkɛmɛ nɔkɔ ɛpʉ́ítí ndu yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ̀m.
Mpok ǎtwɔ̀ anɛ bǒmpap abhɛka bátwɔ̀ mánkap be, mántɛp nkók ankap ɛtɔk yɛka, mánchɛt bhe bɛbhě mɛnkɛm.
Ntá bo abhɛn bákɔ̀ ndǔ mbi nɛwú, ɛriɛp ɛnɛ ɛchi chi mbɔ ɛbɛ́ptí ɛriɛp ɛnɛ́ ɛ́wày bhɔ way. Kɛ ntá bo abhɛn Mandɛm ápɛ̀mɛ, sɛ́chi ɛrɨ́tí ɛriɛp ɛnɛ ɛ́chyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m. Ntɨkɨ mmu ákway bɛkʉ ɛnɛ́ ɛnyǔ bɛtɨk?
Akʉ mmʉɛt mbɔ bɛ apu yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Asɔt mmʉɛt mbɔ nsɛm, atwɔ́ fá amɨk mbɔ nkwǎŋwaŋ.
Báchɔ́kɔ yɛ amɨk ndǔ barɔ́ŋ, ndǔ bakwɔ́ bɛsa bɛ́tay nɛ bɛsa bɛ́pay nsɛm byo.
Bɛyǎ bo abhɛn bachi arɛ, báfɛ́rɛ ndɛn mfǎmʉɛt yap baghay ambi. Báchák báré kpɔt bɛ́wɔ́kɛ́ndé mángay nɔkɔ ndǔ mbi anɛ yí áfʉɛ̀t arɛ́.
Nde ya batú bo Israɛl nɛ abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl bɛ́ mántɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhap mánkóŋó Mandɛm nɛ bɛ́ mámbɔ́ŋ nɛka nɛ Acha ywɛsɛ Yesu Kristo.
“Twɔ́ ká ghɔ mmǔ anɛ ághátí mɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ nkʉ́ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛna. Chí Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò kɛ?”
Yɛ̌ nɔ́, bárɔ́ŋ nɔ́kɔ́, mángati nɔkɔ bho ndǔ atú ɛtɔk wu ankɛm ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu ákʉ́ ntá yap. 
Nɛrɛm anɛ mbɔk bho bárɛ̀m bɛ bárɨŋɨ ǎkʉ́ bábhɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ noko nɛtɔ́ŋ ɛnɛn tɛtɛp. Bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm mɛ́mbák nɛ bhe mankɛm.
Ɛ̌ti ɛyɔ kɛ̌ bó bábhʉɛ́t bɛ́bhɨ́ŋɨ nɛbhʉ́ɛ́rɛ́mɨk wu bɛ́ Mmɨkɨ́ Manoŋ kpátɛ̌ ɛchɔŋ.
Mandɛm ayap mɛ bɛ mbák mǔnto Yesu, ayap mɛ bɛ́ mbák mmú nchí ghati bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́, nɛ ayap mɛ mbák mmú anɛ nchí tɔ́ŋ bo Ɛyɔŋ ɛyi.
Ángɛl ayɛnti nkók nkwɔ́. Ábhak bɔmɛta bɛsa bɛrat nsɛm batandat. Ayɛnti mbɔ ɛnyǔ bakwǎŋwaŋ báyɛ̀nti mɛnyɨŋ.
Akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Kɛ chí mmǔ bɛbʉ́ kɛ puyɛ̌ mmǔ bɛbʉ̌-a, mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ. Ɛnɛ́ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ chi bɛ nchí nyaka nnɛ́mámɨk, kɛ nɛ́nɛ nchí ghɔ mbaŋ.”
Yɛ̌ndu mpú awu nɛ bhe bɛsí nɛ bɛsi, nchí nɛ bhe mbɔnyunɛ ntɨ ɛna nɛ́chí awu nɛ bhe. Nɛ nnáŋ mkpɔt nnyé mmu anɛ ákʉ́ awu ndak,
Kɛ mbák ɔpú foŋori bo abhɛn bákʉ̀ wɔ bɛbʉ́, Ɛtayɛ Mandɛm Mmu achi amfay apú foŋori wɔ.” 
Mandɛm akʉ nyaka barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ bhi abhɛn bachi nyáŋá mandɛm ɛnyu ɛyɔ tɛntɛp,
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ngátí bhe ansɛm ansɛm, ghatí ká bho kpóŋóróŋ. Ɛnɛ́ bǎghókó ansɛm ansɛm, kó ka amfǎy bɛkɛt mǎndɛm bɛ mmɨk nkɛm ángók.
Nɛ nchí chyɛ yɔ́ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti. Ápú gú ánɛ́m. Mmu apú anɛ ákwày bɛ́fɛrɛ yɔ́ amɔ́ya.
Nɛ nkúbhɛ́ manyiɛp kɛ Mandɛm áchɔ́ŋtí mmɨk.
Bábhɔŋ nyaka bǎrú nsi nkwɔ. Yesu áchyɛ́ nɔkɔ bakak ntá Mandɛm, achyɛ yɔ́ ntá bakoŋo bhi bɛ mánkɔ́rɛ yɔ nkwɔ.
Nókó ká bɛ chɔŋ mǎngɔ bɛ sɛbhɨkɨ kwɛn nɛmɔ.
Bachɛ́bhɛ́bho báchí nɛ bhe mpoknkɛm, kɛ mpú bhak chɔŋ nɛ bhe mpoknkɛm.
Pɔ̌l nɛ Banábas bákɛ́m ɛtaŋtí ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ bhɔ́ ɛ̌ti ndaka wu kɛghɔ́ ntí. Ɛ́kʉ baka ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt bɛ Pɔ̌l nɛ Banábas nɛ mbɔk bakoŋo Yesu abhɛn Antiɔk mándɔ́k Yerúsalɛm, mángɔ́ bǒnto nɛ bǒbati nkwɔ́ Yesu ɛ̌ti ndaka wu.
Bɛtɔk ɛbhɛn bɛchi nɛntɨ nnyɛ́n mɛ́nɛ́msi. Njiɛ ɛnkɛm nkwɔ ɛnɛmsi.
Mbɔk ayap báyàŋ nyaka bɛkɛm yi kɛ yɛ̌ mmu kɛtɔk yi awɔ amʉɛt. 
Bǎkɛ́ rɔ bo mándwɔ bhe. “Ɔ̌kɔ̀ nɛ ngɛ́p, ɔ́ngɛ́p aghɛp.”
Kaká ká bǒnkwɔ abhɛn báchɛmɛ nɔkɔ ɛkɛt ɛyap, nɛ mǎnkaka mʉɛrɛkɔŋ awa Ɛpainɛ́tɔs. Yí achi nyaka mmǔ mbɨ bɛbhak nkoŋo Kristo atú Esia.
Bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ mpok anɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ re bho bɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ baraká Mandɛm, bo bákʉ̀ nyaka mǎnɛ́m ɛbhɨ ndǔ bɛyǎ mɛnyu, mǎnchyɛ nɔkɔ kɛnókó ntá bɔmandɛm abhɛn bápú rɛm kɛpɨ.
Chi-mbɨ ywɛka Ábraham, ǎnòŋ nyaka nɛ maŋák bɛ́ghɔ nywɔp nɛtwɔ ɛna. Aghɔ́ nɔ́, ntɨ nɛ́rɨ yi amɛm.”
Bǒ mmɨk bápú kwáy bɛpap be. Bápap mɛ mbɔnyunɛ nchí rɛm bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ́ bákʉ̀ bɛbɛp.
Bágháti ngɛ́mtay ɛyɔ bɛ ɛkɛ chɔŋti tákɔ, nɛ yɛ̌ chí mɛnɔk, nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́gò amɨk, nɛ bɛ ɛ́nchyɛ́ ɛsɔŋɔri chi ntá bo abhɛn ɛrɨŋ Mandɛm ɛpu bhɔ nɛfó.
Chɔŋ bo mánja bhe gbaka gbaka gbaka ntá bɔgɔ́bhanɔ nɛ bafɔ ɛ̌ti ya. Nɛ chɔŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́nchyɛ bhe mbi bɛghati bhɔ nɛ bǒ abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti ya.
Bɔ́ŋ ká ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ nɛ batɨ, mǎndɔk ambɨ bɛfoŋori batɨ, yɛ̌ ɛ́mbak chi bɛ bákʉ mǎmbentɨ. Bǎbhɔŋ bɛfoŋori batɨ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyu Acha ywɛsɛ áfóŋórí bhe.
Ngók yɛ ndǔ mmu ághàti mɛ mpǎy bhɔ abhɛn báfyɛ́ ɛrɨŋ Mandɛm nɛfó yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap. Bábhak nkwɔ bho bɛsa tándrámɔt nsɛm manwi abhɛn báfù ndǔ manɛrɛ́kɛt Israɛl byo nɛ apay ankɛm.
Awu áfʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, ngɔ́ ngɛ́mtay bo abhɛn yɛ̌ mmu apu kway bɛpay. Báfú ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛtɔk nɛ ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nnɛrɛ́kɛrɛ́ bho. Báfú ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nkwɔ bho, nɛ ndǔ bǒ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk. Bábhak téé bɛsí ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ Mandɛm nɛ bɛsí Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n, nɛ ndɛn pɛ́pɛ́p amʉɛt nɛ bɛwɔ̌amaŋ amɔ.
Pɔ̌l abho yɛ bɛkʉ bɔ́ mánjwímɛm. Arɛm bɛ, “Jɔ̌n ǎjwìti nyaka bo bɛtɔŋ bɛ bátɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhap angati nɔkɔ bo Israɛl bɛ́ bábhɔŋ mɛ́nóko mmu anɛ átwɔ̀ yi ansɛm, nɔ chi Yesu.”
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bati arat bápɛ̀tnsɛm, bátɛ́mɛ́ri bakoŋo bhi báchák. Bághɔ́ bɛyǎ bho nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses ndu bákɛ̀m ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ bhɔ.
Ɛgháká nɔkɔ manywɔp árát, bághɔ́ yi amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm chɔkɔ nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé, ndu ághòk mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ bárɛ̀m, nɛ ambɛbhɛ nɔkɔ bɔ́ bɛbhɛp.
ayap batí byo nɛ apay, áchyɛ bhɔ́ nnyɛ́n bɛ bǒnto. Aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Njap be bɛ́ mǎmbák nɛ mɛ. Chɔŋ ntó bhe nɛfí ndu bɛghati bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ Mandɛm,
Bághɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ mbɔ bárɨ́ngo. Átáka, ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap abhɔ́ŋ nɛmɔt ɛnɛn nɛte yi anti.
Mpok mbʉɛ́t mandu mmɔ, nchí rɛm nyaka kɛpɨ mbɔ mǎmbɔ, nkaysi nɔkɔ barak mbɔ mǎmbɔ, ngɔ nɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋ mbɔ mǎmbɔ. Kɛ mpok nnáŋ nchɨ́kɨ́, ndɔ baraká kɛ̌mbɔ́.
Mpok Yesu áfú amɛm áchwi, aghɔ́ ngɛ́mtay bho. Ntínso nɛ́kɛ́m yi nɛ bhɔ mbɔnyunɛ bachi nyaka ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri, nkwak ti, mbɔ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ mbabhɛri. Abho yɛ bɛ́tɔŋ bhɔ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ.
Mɛ Pɔ̌l, mǔntó Yesu Kristo bɛkoŋo nkaysi Mandɛm, kɛ nchí sɨŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ. Nchí sɨŋ ntá yɛka bo Mandɛm abhɛn bǎbhʉ̀rɛ bariɛp ndǔ Mandɛm áchɛ́mɛ́ bhe nɛ Yesu Kristo.
Ndu Mandɛm ábhárɛ́ bhɛsɛ nɛ Yesu Kristo, yí akʉ sɛ́pɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m nɛ yi. Nɛ akʉ sɛ́chɔ́kɔ́ nɛ Kristo amfay ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ yi achi Mfɔ.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ chi bɛ, ansɔt kɛfɔ̌ nkáp ɛki nɛ kɛfɔ̌ mɛnyɨŋ bɛchak ambʉrɛ amfay ntá Mandɛm. Arɛ́, kɛngɔk nɛ mfárɛ́káŋ bápú kway bɛchɔŋti bhɔ nɛ baghɛ́p bápú kway bɛdak ɛkɛt mángɛ́p wú.
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Bě mkpáká bho anɛ abhɨkɨ bhɔŋ nɛka nɛ mɛ, bě bhó bǎyìbhiri tɛtɛp ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛchak, chɔŋ mpɛt ntat nɛ bhe ná? Chɔŋ nkɛ́pntɨ nɛ bhe ngaka fá?” Kɛ arɛm ntá chimɔ bɛ, “Twɔ́ nɛ mɔ́ywɛ fá.”
Bo abhɛn baghoko bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɔ bábhɛ́p Yesu bɛ, “Agha ákwày yɛ bɛbhɔŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti?”
Nɛ́nɛ, akʉ bǒ bɛtɔk mɛnkɛm mándɨ́ŋɨ́ yɔ kpoŋoroŋ mbɔ ɛnyǔ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ básɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm mmu achi nɛpɛ́m mpoknkɛm ághátí bhɔ. Aghati bhɔ mánsɨ́ŋ bɔ amɨk bɛ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl mánkoŋo ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ̀m bɛ mánoko yi nɛ mangók nɔkɔ yi.
Mmɔ̌káti apu kway bɛrɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ancha ntɔ̌ŋ aywi. Kɛ mpok anɛ bátɔ́ŋ yi kpát ánaŋa nɛghɔ́k ɛni, ǎbhák mbɔ ntɔ̌ŋ aywi.
Bǒ mankɛm abhɛn bárɨ́ŋɨ́ Yesu, nɛ baghɔrɛ́ abhɛn bábhó bɛkoŋo yi tɛ Gálili, báté nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ mángɔ nɔkɔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ. 
Chiɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ka bo mankɛm kɛnókó. Bɔ́ŋ ká ɛkɔŋ nɛ batɨ bǒnkwɔ, Bɔ́ŋ ká bɛcháy Mandɛm, chyɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ká mfɔ-ngo kɛnókó. 
Ágháti nɔ́kɔ́ bhɔ bɛ, “Mǎnkɔ sayri”, arɔ akó amfay njiɛ ndu mɛnɨkmʉɛt.
Kɛ mbɔk ɛyap báré rɛm chi bɛ, “Yi mmu ákʉ́ nnɛ́mámɨ́k ǎghɔ mbaŋ, apú kwáy nyaka bɛkʉ bɛ Lásárɔs ákɛ́ gú?” 
Nkú Jɔ̌n abhak chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ baghoko nɛ babyɔk mpɔŋɔ baso. Mgbat anɛ yi ágwɔ̀t ɛbho abhak nkwɔbhɛ́nya, nɛ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛni nɛ́bhak ngɛ́mtáy nɛ bawɛrɛ́ bɛtu ámɛ́n yi ághɔ̀ amɛm baso.
Mbɨ́kɨ́ kaysi bɛ́ ɛ́chí sayri bɛ́tó mǔkɛnɔŋ ntá Mfɔ Rom nkɛrɛm mbɔ̌ŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ákʉ́.”
Yesu Kristo Mmɔ Mandɛm anɛ Silvánɔs nɛ Tímɔti nɛ mɛ sɛ́ghàti nyaka bhe ɛ̌ti yi ndǔ nkwɔ ayɛka apú mmu bɛyɔŋ bɛyɔŋ. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ́mɛ́, yɔ́ kɛ yi ákʉ̀.
Ɛnyu ɛ́fákárí nyaka kɛ bábhé Yesu Kristo: María achí nyaka nnɔ Yesu. Mpok yɔ Josɛ́f atɨ bɛ́bhay yi. Kɛ bápɛ́rɛ rɨŋɨ batɨ, ɛ́fákari bɛ María achi nɛ mɛniɛ. Apɔkɔ mɛniɛ bhɔ chí ndǔ bɛtaŋ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ.
Kɛ Kristo asɔt nyaka mmʉɛt nkwǎŋwaŋ, agú ndǔ ɛkotákátí ɛ̌ti bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛka. Ɛnyu yɔ kɛ Mandɛm ákʉ́ bɛ mǎmpɛt mǎmbak ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt nɛ yi, bɛ mǎmbak nyáŋá, kɛbhɔŋ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bɛsí bhi.
Bǎbhɔŋ yɛ́ bɛ́té kpirí tɛ ndǔ ngwɛnti bɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́nkʉ mǎngó mǎnjwi pɔɔt, mmǔ ywɛka kɛbhák mbɔk bɛyɨŋɨ bɛpɨŋɨ́ bo Mandɛm.
Bɛsɛ bho sɛchi ndu Nkwɔ Kristo, bo Mandɛm ábhárɛ́ nɛ Yesu Kristo, sɛ́nchíɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó. Ndǔ mkpáká bho ɛnkɛm, mpoknkɛm. Amen.
Ɛ́chí ɛnyu ɛ́mɔ́t mbɔnyu Yesu Acha arɛmɛ bɛ, “Nɛnyiɛ́ mmu anɛ ághàti Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ nɛ́bhɔŋ bɛ́fú ntá bo abhɛn Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ yi aghati bho áyɛ̀t bhɔ.”
Ághátí nɔ́kɔ́ bhɔ́ nkaysi yi, bábhɔ́ŋ maŋák. Báfyɛ́ bariɛp bɛ́chyɛ yi nkáp. Júdas abho bɛyaŋ yɛ mbi ndu bɛti Yesu ntá yap. 
Mbɔ yi achi chi fá amɨk, mbʉ ápú bhak nchiakap wáwák, tɛ̌ndu bachiǎkap bachak bachí fá amɨk abhɛn báchyɛ̀ akap bɛkoŋo ɛnyǔ ɛnɛ́ ɛbhé Moses ɛ́rɛ̀m.
Mandɛm achi Ɛfóŋó, nɛ bǒ abhɛn báchyɛ̀ yi kɛnókó, bábhɔŋ bɛchyɛ yi kɛnókó nɛ ntɨ nɛmɔt ndǔ bɛtaŋ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ.”
Moses asɨŋ nyaka bɛ mmu anɛ áyàŋ bɛbhʉrɛ bɛbhé Mandɛm bɛ ambak chak abhɔŋ bɛbhʉrɛ bɛbhé mɛnkɛm kɛ ambɔ́ŋ nɛpɛ́m.
Kɛ ndǔ nkáysí ya, ɛrɨ ɛcha bɛ ngɔrɛ́ anɛ nnɛ́m ɛ́ywi ágú anchɔkɔ ɛnyu ɛyɔ, yi kɛ bhay nnɛ́m. Nɛ mɛ nnókó bɛ́ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm kɛ̌ áchyɛ́ mɛ́ nkaysi anɛ.
Yesu akɛmɛ bɛ, “Dɔ̌ ká nɛnywíntí ɛnɛká nɔ.
Mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ batú ángók!
Bɔ̌ma, ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ mɛ̌yáŋ mǎndɨ́ŋɨ́ chí bɛ manywɔp anɛ́ Mandɛm áchyɛ́ bhɛsɛ́ ábhɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ yá. Ɛ́yàŋ yɛ bɛ́ bɛ́bhó nɛ́nɛ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ábháy ngɔrɛ́ ámbák mbɔ mmu anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ ngɔrɛ́.
Debhít nkwɔ árɛm nyaka bɛ, “Mɛnyɨŋɨ́nyiɛ bhap mɛ́mbák nta ɛnɛ ɛ́kɛ̀m bɔ, mɛ́mbak ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ̀ mándɨŋɨ nɛkwɛ́n ɛnɛn bákwɛ́nɛ́, bɛ Mandɛm ántɛ́msí bhɔ.
nɛ chɔŋ bǒ mankɛm mángɔ ndu Mandɛm ápɛ̀mɛ bho.’”
Ɛ́chí ɛnyu ɛyɔ mbɔnyunɛ, ngɔrɛ́ afú chí amʉɛt mbakanɛm. Kɛ nɛ́nɛ, ngɔrɛ́ kɛ ábhe mbakanɛm. Nɛ bǎkɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk bɛ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm bɛ́fù chí ntá Mandɛm.
Ɛ́fákárí nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyu yɔ ndɔŋ ɛ́rát, ɛnyɨŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́pɛ́tnsɛm amfay.
“Mmǔ anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ batú ángók ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm árɛ̀m ntá bɛka bo Kristo. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ánú ásɔ́rɛ́ awɔ́nɛm, nchí chyɛ yi mbi bɛ anyiɛ kɛpɛm ɛkɛ́n ɛnɔk ɛnɛ ɛ́chyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m. Yɔ́ ɛchí amɛm *nɛbhʉɛt maŋák Mandɛm.” 
Kɛ bǒ bɛtɨk bhɔ kɛchyɛ. Bákɛ́m yi bádɛ́n, báfɛ́n apɛtnsɛm amɔ́ apay.
Mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu árɛ́mɛ́, akɛ́m nkú yi adak ndu bɛtɔŋ bɛběntɨ bhi. Akók bɛ́, “Akʉ tɛ anáŋá! Ǎyɛnti mmʉɛt nɛ Mandɛm! Sɛ́pɛ́t sɛ́yàŋ batísiɛ́ mántwɔ́ mándɛ́m ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ákʉ́ ndaká yí? Bě mankɛm bǎghok ndǔ yí áyɛ̀nti mmʉɛt nɛ Mandɛm!
Mbɔk bǒ Grik nkwɔ báchí nyaka ndǔ nkwɔ bho abhɛn bárɔ́ŋɔ́ Yerúsalɛm bɛchyɛ bakak ntá Mandɛm ndǔ mpok Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ághókó ɛ́ghati yi kpoŋoroŋ mɛnyɨŋ bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ ɛbhɛn bɛchi yi antɨ, ɛ́nkʉ yi ankwɛn bɛsí Mandɛm anchyɛ yi kɛnókó, andɛm bɛ, “Mandɛm achi nɛ be tɛtɛp!” 
Sɔt yɛ ka mpok nɛ bǎkɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk bɛ nchí ghati nyaka bhe mɛnyɨŋ nɛ babhɛsɛ amɨ́k, njɛp nɔkɔ be batú bɛ̌ti nɛ ngósí ndǔ mamiɛ́ árát.
Mmu wu arɛm bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, nnáŋ nchí bhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm tɛ kɛmbɔ́ ɛka.”
Bábhɛp yi bɛ, “Ɔ̌yàŋ sɛ́ntóŋtí yɔ́ fá?”
Bɛbho yɛ mpok yɔ, achɛm mmʉɛt nɛ bakoŋo Yesu Acha ndu yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bɔ bákʉ̀.
Bě bo bǎpà bɛ bǎrɨ̀ŋɨ ɛbhé Mandɛm, bǎpú chyɛ nɔ Mandɛm ntíánwɔ́p ndǔ bapú bhʉɛrɛ ɛbhé ɛyi?
Bɔ̌ma, kɛ mbák chí bhe, bǎpú amɛm ɛjuri, bɛ́ nywɔp ɛnɔ nɛ́mfɔ́kɔ́rí bhe mbɔ ngɛ́p.
Ndǔ bɛyǎ bakáp kɛ̌ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap áfɛ́rɛ́ mandú achyɛ mbɔ akap, kɛ nchɛ́bhɛ ngɔrɛ́ nɛ achyɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́.”
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ, yɛ̌ ndǔ yi ápú kway bɛfate bɛ anchyɛ yi nɛnyíɛ́, ɛ̌ti yi achi mmʉɛrɛ ywi, abhɔŋ bɛ́fáte anchyɛ yi yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ yi áyaŋ mbɔnyunɛ atóŋórí bɛ́dɛ́p nɛkok kɛbhɔŋ ntíánwɔ́p.
Gɔ́bhanɔ atɔ́ŋ yɛ nɛ awɔ bɛ Pɔ̌l andɛm kɛpɨ. Pɔ̌l abho bɛrɛm bɛ, “Ngɔ bɛ́ ɔnáŋ ɔtaŋ manyé amɛm ɛtɔk ɛnɛ ndǔ bɛyǎ mamiɛ, nɛ mbɔ̌ŋ maŋák bɛ́táŋa mmʉɛ́t bɛsí bhɛ.
“Bǎkɛ́ táŋ batɨ kɛ́ká mántáŋ be nkwɔ.
Apɛtnsɛm anywɔ́p, aghɔ́ mɔ́ bhʉrɛ ndǔ ndu ɛnɛ́ ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ yɔ ɛ́náŋ ɛ́rɔ yi. 
Mmu anɛ árɛ̀m mɛnyɨŋ ndǔ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi, ǎyaŋ kɛnókó ɛki yímbɔŋ. Mmu anɛ áyàŋ bo mánchyɛ́ kɛnókó chi ntá mmu anɛ átó yi, achí mmǔ tɛtɛp, bapu apú nɛ yi.
Bápɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nsɛm, bágháti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛfakari ntá bǒnto Yesu bati byo nɛ amɔt nɛ bakoŋo bhi abhɛ́nɛ́fú mankɛm.
Bě nɛ nkwɔ Ɛchɛmɛ́ bǒ batí ɛtɔk tó yɛ ka ɛyɔŋ ntá mǔngo batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bɛ́ ántó Pɔ̌l ntá yɛka mbɔ bɛ bǎyàŋ bɛghok ɛyɔŋɔ́ manyé ɛyi sayri. Mbák ɛ́mfákárí nɔ́, chɔŋ sɛ́ngway yi ambi.”
Bǒ Grik bhɔ bárɔ́k ntá Fílip anɛ áfú nyaka Bɛtsáida, atú Gálili barɛm bɛ, “Ɛta, sɛ́yàŋ bɛ́ghɔ Yesu.”
Héli mmɔ̌ Mátat, Mátat mmɔ̌ Lɛ́vi, Lɛ́vi mmɔ̌ Mɛ́lki, Mɛ́lki mmɔ̌ Jánai, Jánai mmɔ̌ Josɛ́f,
Ngɛ́mtay bo abhɛn bachi arɛ bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ Pɔ̌l ákʉ́, bábhó bɛ́bɨk ndu ɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛyap, ɛyɔŋ bǒ Likáonia mandɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Bɔmandɛm básɔt mmʉɛt bakwǎŋwaŋ bátwɔ fá amɨk ntá yɛsɛ!”
Bábhɨ́kɨ́ re kɛm nyaka Jɔ̌n mamfyɛ ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ.
Bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm bɛchi chi ndǔ bɛrɨ ɛbhɛka, bɛ ndǔ bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm bɛ́gháká ntá bɛyǎ bho, mɛ́nkʉ́ bo abhɛn báchyɛ̀ Mandɛm bakak mánjá mándɔk nɔkɔ chi ambɨ, bɛ bo mánchyɛ nɔ́kɔ́ Mandɛm kɛnókó. 
Mmǔ anɛ ághɔ́ nyaka ndu ɛ́fákárí kɛ̌ ágháti bhɛsɛ nɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ǎrɛ̀m ɛchí tɛtɛp. Arɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ árɛm chi tɛtɛp bɛ be nkwɔ́ mǎnsɨ́kɨ́ntɨ nɛ Yesu.
Yesu abhɛ́p bo abhɛn bághòk yi bɛ, “Ná bákwày bɛrɛm bɛ Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò achi ɛbhárɛ́mɔ Mfɔ Debhít?
Kɛ Josɛ́f ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́ Akɛlos asɔt ɛpok ɛtayi mbɔ Mfɔ atú ɛtɔk Judɛ́ya, acháy bɛrɔŋ arɛ́. Ndǔ kɛnɔ́ kɛ́chák, ángɛl Mandɛm ayɛp Josɛ́f batú bɛ yi ándɔ́k chí atú Gálili.
Mpok yɔ, bǒ abhɛn bachi ɛbhe awɔghɔ yi bákɛ́mɛ bɛ, ‘Acha, ntɨkɨ mpok sɛ́ghɔ́ ndǔ nsay ánù wɔ, kɛ sɛ́kɛ chyɛ wɔ nɛnyíɛ́? Ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ manyiɛp ákwàk wɔ kɛ sɛ́kɛ chyɛ wɔ manyiɛp? Ntɨkɨ mpok ɔ́twɔ́ mbɔ kɛnkɔ ntá yɛsɛ kɛ sɛ́kɛ sɔt wɔ mbɔ ntɨ manɔ? Ntɨkɨ mpok ndɛn ɛ́chɛ́bhɛ́ wɔ, kɛ sɛ́kɛ chyɛ wɔ ndɛn? Ntɨkɨ mpok ɔ́mè kɛ sɛ́kɛ kokori wɔ? Nɛ ntɨkɨ mpok ɔ́chí ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ kɛ sɛ́kɛ kwak wɔ?’
Ɛnɛ́ bakoŋo Jɔ̌n bárɔ́ bárɔ̀ŋ, Yesu abho bɛrɛm ntá bɛyǎ bo abhɛn bátwɔ̀ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ yi achi ɛ̌ti Jɔ̌n bɛ, “Mpok bǎrɔ̀ŋ nyaka awu amɛm baso, bǎrɔ́k bɛghɔ ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ mmʉ? Bǎrɔk bɛghɔ mmu anɛ achi mbɔ ɛ̌nsɔ́manyiɛp ɛnɛ babhʉɛ́p áfòk ɛ́nkwɛ́n ɛnɛ ɛbhe, ámfok ɛnkwɛn ɛbhe ɛ́chák kɛ?
Yesu abho bɛ́ghati bhɔ bɛ, “Sɔt ka mpok bɛ́ yɛ̌ mmu ákɛ́ rwɔ́ bhe!
Bábhɔŋ bɛ́kɛm nɛ bɛtaŋ mɛnyɨŋ bhɛ́sɛ bhɛ́sɛ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm ákʉ bo mándɨŋɨ nɛ mánóko. Babhɔŋ bɛkɛm bɔ nɛ ntɨ ɛnɛn nɛchi chak.
Mbák mmu ywɛka ángɔ ntɨ mmǔ Mandɛm ndǔ ákʉ̀ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛn bɛpu twɔ nɛ nɛwú, ánɨkmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm nɛ chɔŋ Mandɛm anchyɛ mmǔ wu nɛpɛ́m. Bɛbʉ́ bɛchi ɛbhɛn bɛ́twɔ̀ nɛ nɛwú, kɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ rɛm bɛ mmu ánɨkmʉɛt ɛ̌ti mmu anɛ ákʉ́ ɛnyǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɔ.
nɔ, bǎchɛt bho mbi bɛ bákɛ́ kwak bachi nɛ manɔ bhap.
Mandɛm áyàŋ bɛ mǎnkʉ́ nɔ́kɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi chak bɛ manyu ánchók bɛchɨŋtǐ bho abhɛn babhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ yɛ̌nyɨŋ.
nɛ ntí bɛ, ‘Bákwày bɛ́yɨŋɨ nɛ amɨ́k kɛ bápú ghɔ yɛ̌nyɨŋ; mángók nɛ batú, kɛ kɛjwimɛm, bɛ́ bákɛ́ pɛtnsɛm ntá Mandɛm yi ámfoŋori bhɔ.’” 
Manɛ́mámɨk bati apay babhak nɛpaká mbi chɔkɔ. Bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́ Yesu kɛ̌ áfʉɛ̀t, bábho bɛbɨk mandɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Ɛta, Mmɔ̌ Mfɔ Debhít! Ghɔ́ bhɛsɛ́ ntínso!”
Anyíɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi bɛ́pɛ́tnsɛm. Sɔ̌l abho bɛ́gháti mbok Yesu ɛtɔk Damáskɔs Sɔ̌l abhak Damáskɔs nɛ bakoŋo Yesu ndu mpǎy manywɔp.
Ɛnɛ́ báfú ɛkɛt Páílet bárɔ̀ŋ, bátɛ́mɛri mmu ɛtɔk Sírene fú ambi anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ́ Símun. Bájirɛ yí ápɔ́kɔ́ ɛkotákátí Yesu.
Yesu atɛm nɔkɔ nɛkay ɛnɛn, batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm nɛ bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm bárɨŋɨ bɛ atɛm nɛkay ɛnɔ chi ɛ̌ti yap. Báre yaŋ bɛkɛm yi, kɛ báchày bo abhɛn báchi arɛ.
Kɛ Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́yàŋ nkʉ ntá yɛ. Bǎkwáy bɛka mɛnyu ɛsɔŋɔri anɛ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛ́nyú?” Bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Sɛ́kwày bɛkʉ nɔ.”
Nɛka Nóa kɛ nɛ́kʉ́ bɛ, mpok Mandɛm ásɛ́mtí yi ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yɛ̌ mmu abhɨkɨ re ghɔ́ nyaka nɛ amɨ́k, anoko, aghoko ɛrɛm áchwí, achwe amɛm nɛ ɛfo ɛyi ɛnkɛm, Mandɛm apɛmɛ bhɔ. Nɛkʉ Nóa akʉ nɔ ɛghori ɛ́kwɛ́n amʉɛt bǒ mmɨk nɛ. Mandɛm asɔt bɛ Nóa achi chak ndu abhɔŋ nyaka nɛka.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ̀ sɛ́ndɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ ɛkɔŋ chi nɛchyɛ anɛ Yesu áchyɛ́ nɛpɛ́m ɛni ɛ̌ti yɛsɛ. Nɛ bɛsɛ nkwɔ sɛ́bhɔŋ bɛka, yɛ̌ chi nɛwú, ɛ̌ti batɨ.
Yesu ábɨ́kɨ́ nɔ́kɔ́, asɛbhɛ.
Nɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ Kristo yímbɔŋ afyɛ́ bariɛp bɛchyɛ bhɛsɛ chi nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti?
Mbɔŋ bɛrɔŋ ambɨ bɛdɛp awɔ́ antɨ yɛ̌ndu nsáy ápú arɛ́. Kɛ dɔ̌ ká ngati bhe ɛ̌ti kɛnɔ́ amɨ́k anti fúú, ɛkɛn ngɔ́ nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Yesu Acha ákʉ́ mɛ ndɨŋɨ.
“Nchí ghati bhe bɛ, mbák mmu apú nɛ Mandɛm mbɔ ɛnyǔ mmɔ́ ábhàk nɛ ɛtayi, apú kway bɛbhak ndǔ mpǎy bho abhɛn Mandɛm achi Mfɔ wap wáwák.”
Bábho bɛway Yesu mándɛm nɔkɔ bɛ, “Acha mfɔ bo Israɛl, kɛnókó kɛ́chí ɛkɛ ɛtá!”
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, mbɔŋɔ́nkɨ wu afɛrɛ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk abhi báchák ató. Báyá báchá abhɛn mbɨ. Kɛ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk abhɛn báchí amɛm nkɨ bákɛ́m bhɔ, bákʉ́ ɛnyumɔt nɛ bhɔ́, mbɔ ɛnyǔ bákʉ́ nɛ abhɛn mbɨ.
Nɛ́nɛ, yɛ̌ mbi apu anɛ Mandɛm árɛm bɛ bo abhɛn bábhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Kristo bákwɛn manyé.
mbɔnyunɛ bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ mbák mamɔ ántwɔ́, mǎndɔk nɔkɔ chi ambɨ bɛtɔŋ bɛ bǎbhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm tɛtɛp, ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ mǎnté kpirí nɛ Mandɛm tɛndǔ ngwɛ́nti ɛ́ncha ɛnyu ɛsɨ́.
Ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɛ́n mbɨ ndǔ sɔ́nde, sɛ́chɔ́kɔ nɛ bǒnkwɔ́ nɛbhʉɛt amɔt ndǔ Nɛnyiɛ Ɛta. Pɔ̌l abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɛ́rɔ́ betí. Ɛkʉ́ arɛm kɛpɨ nɛ bhɔ kpátɛ nɛntɨ bɛti.
Ɛyɔŋ ɛ́fú yɛ amfay ɛ́ré rɛm bɛ, “Nɛ́ chí Mɔ́wa. Nkɔŋ yi tontó. Ǎchyɛ̀ mɛ bɛyǎ maŋák.”
Yesu Kristo kɛ̌ áchí nɛbhʉ́ɛ́rɛ́kɛt ɛnɛ́n bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́tée ɛkɛt arɛ́. Nɛ yí kɛ̌ áchí nɛbhʉ́ɛ́rɛ́kɛt ɛnɛ́n bághókó bábhʉ́rɛ́. Yɛ̌ nɛbhʉ́ɛ́rɛ́kɛt nɛ́chák nɛ́pú ɛnɛn mmu ákway bɛ́ghóko.
Amaŋá nɛbu áfú amfay ánkwɛnti nɔkɔ amɨk. Áchɨ́kɨti ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nɛmɔt nɛ́bhak mbɔ bɔkilo bɛsa bɛpay nsɛm byo ndǔ mɛnwɔp ɛbhi. Áre kwɛnti bǒ amʉɛt kpát babho bɛrɛm ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti Mandɛm ɛ̌ti ɛsɔŋɔri ɛyɔ.
Nɛ chɔŋ Mmǔ anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm ambesi ande twɔ́ amɛm nɛbháŋ nɛ bɛyǎ bɛtaŋ nɛ kɛnókó.
Básɔ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bakap ayap, babho mɛnywinti ɛ̌ti mbɔŋɔ́nkɨ,
Kɛ yí aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Mbɔ̌ŋ nɛnyíɛ́ mɛ́nyiɛ ɛnɛ́n bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ.”
Tɨk ka manywɔp anɛ áfʉɛ́rɛ́ ansɛm, mpok bákʉ́ amɨ́k ánɛ́nɛ́ bhe. Mpok yɔ, bǎté kpirí ndǔ bɛyǎ bɛsɔŋɔri ndǔ mǎnù nɛ bhɔ.
Kɛ mbák chí mɛ́, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bǎrɛ̀m ɛ̌ti ya, ɛyɔ ɛ́pú chyɛ mɛ ɛsɔŋɔri antɨ, yɛ̌ chí bɛ́ bo báchák kɛ̌ báyàŋ bɛ́rɛm ɛnyǔ mmʉ̌ bɛtok mɛnchí. Mɛmbɔŋ mpú kwáy bɛ́rɛm bɛ́ nchí ɛsáyrí mǔbɛtok, nɛ mpú kwáy bɛ́rɛm bɛ nchí ɛbɛ́ptí mǔbɛtok.
Yesu ǎkɔ̀ nyaka amɛm bɛtɔk bɛgho nɛ ndǔ bɔ̌bɛtɔk, antɔŋ nɔkɔ bho amɛm bɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt bo Israɛl. Nɛ angati nɔkɔ bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Kɛfɔ Mandɛm. Ǎbù nyaka bo abhɛn bárɔ̀ŋ ntá yi nɛ mame mɛnyu nɛ mɛnyu.
Moses arɛm bɛ, ‘Chiɛ́ ɛ́táyɛ nɛ máyɛ kɛnókó’ nɛ bɛ ‘Yɛ̌ agha anɛ árɛ̀m ɛbɛ́ptí ɛyɔŋ ntá ɛtayi, yɛ̌ máyi, bábhɔŋ bɛway yi.’
Mmǔ wu afa yɛ, arɔk, angati nɔkɔ bho ndǔ bɛtɔk byo mɛnkɛm ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu ákʉ́ ntá yi. Mankɛm abhɛn baghókó bábhák maknkay. 
Kɛ anɛ áyáŋ ntɨ mpay, apuri Moses, abhɛ́p yí bɛ, ‘Agha ákʉ́ wɔ mfɔ nɛ ntaŋá manyé yɛsɛ́?
Ɛ́gháka nɔkɔ beku, Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bárɔ́ ɛtɔk ɛgho báfú. 
Mbák báchi bǒ bɛtok Kristo, mɛ nchá bhɔ́. [Nchí rɛm mbɔ ɛbhokori mmu.] Nkʉ bɛtɨk nchá bɔ́ mankɛm. Nchwe kɛnɔŋ ndɔŋ nɛ ndɔŋ ncha yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu, mǎntɛm áyá acha, nɛ ndɔp kɛ́kwɔ́t bɛgu ndɔŋ nɛ ndɔŋ.
Bɔ̌ma, nɛ́nɛ, sɛ́yàŋ bɛkʉ bɛ bǎkɛ́ rɔp amɛm ɛjuri bɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ bo abhɛn bágú bɛ bǎkɛ́ di bhɔ mbɔ bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhakantɨ bɛ chɔŋ bawú mámpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.
“Mandɛm achyɛ́ bǒbhɛn Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔnyu yí áchyɛ́ nyaka bhɛsɛ bo Israɛl. Agha ákwáy yɛ bɛ́káŋ bɛ́ bákɛ́ jwiti bhɔ́?”
Nɛ bɛbhak ɛchɨŋtímu, nɛ ɛpɨŋ ɛnɛ mmu apu bhʉɛrɛ bariɛp, nɛ bɛbhɔŋ ntɨ ɛnɛn mmu abhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ɛkɔŋ nɛ batɨ, nɛ bɛbhɔŋ ɛpɨŋ ɛnɛ mmu apu ghɔ batɨ ntínso.
“Ntɔŋ, Moses asɨŋ ndǔ ɛbhé ɛyɛsɛ bɛ mbák mmu ángú ándɔ́ ngɔrɛ́ kɛbhɔ́ŋ yɛ̌ mmɔ́, mɔ́mayi abhɔŋ bɛsɔt ngɔrɛ́ wu bɛ́ ámbé bɔ nɛ yi ndǔ nnyɛ́n manɔ anɛ ágú.
Sɛ́nɨ̀kmʉɛt bɛ nɛjwǐmɛm ɛnɔ nɛ́nkwák mǎmbɔŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛ́kwáy ntá nkoŋo Yesu Acha. Ɛnɔ nɛ́kʉ̀ Mandɛm ambɔŋ maŋák, nɛ nɛ́kwàk mǎnkʉ nɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛrɨ ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbi, nɛ nɛ́kʉ̀ mǎndɨŋɨ Mandɛm mǎndɔkɔ nɔkɔ chi ambɨ.
Mandɛm akwak bo Israɛl, bǒ bɛtok bhi. Abhɨ́kɨ́ ghɔkɔntɨk bariɛp ami ntá bachǐmbɨ bhɛsɛ bɛ chɔŋ angɔ bhɔ ntínso.
Ǎtwɔ̀ nɛ nchán myákátí awɔ ndu bɛ́chák nkway bɛ amfáp ɛnɛ ɛrɨ nɛ bɛkpáfu. Ánáŋ ánkʉ́ nɔ, ansɔt mbwɔt antɛn ndu nkpánɛ́, anyɔ mmɨk, ansɔt bɛkpáfu amfyɛ amɛm ngó anɛ apu nɛmɛ.”
Tɛ́mté wu, afaté abho bɛkɔ. [Achí nyaka mamiɛ́ byo nɛ apay.] Manyu áchók bo mankɛm.
Sɛ́mbɨ́tí Mandɛm Mmu achi Chi Yesu Kristo Acha ywɛsɛ. Yi achyɛ́ bhɛsɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ áfɔ́k anɛ́ áfù amfay ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ yi achi Mfɔ arɛ́, mbɔnyunɛ ábhat bhɛsɛ nɛ Kristo.
Nɛ́nɛ, bǎrɨŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn. Chɔŋ ɛndɨ ntá yɛka ɛncha mbák bǎkʉ̀ bhɔ.
Puyɛ̌ nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ kɛ̌ mǔbɛtok Yesu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́tɔŋ bo abhɛn bápú ka nɛ yi. Mandɛm ǎkwáy bɛ́kʉ bɔ́ mántɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhap nɛ mánoko nɛtɔŋ ɛnɛn tɛtɛp.
Mandɛm afʉɛt ndǔ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ sɛ́ghátí bhe abhɨ́ŋɨ́ be. Akʉ nɔ bɛ́ mǎmbɔ́ŋ ákɔ́rɛ́ ndu kɛnɛ́m Yesu Kristo Acha.
Mbɔ̌ŋ bɛyǎ ɛkwak bɛghɔ bhe ndu bɛkʉ mǎmbɔŋ ákɔ́rɛ́ ndu áfɔ́k anɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ áchyɛ chɔŋ be bɛ mǎntáŋ ndǔ mbi Mandɛm.
Mǎmbo yɛ bɛrɛm bɛ, ‘Pú sɛ́chɔkɔ nyaka nɛbhʉɛt amɔt sɛ́nyíɛ́, nɛ sɛnyu nɛ wɔ? Nɛ ɔtɔ́ŋ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm amɛm bɛtɔk ɛbhɛsɛ?’
Yɛ̌ agha anɛ ághàti bho Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm, abhɔŋ bɛkʉ nɔ mbɔ mmu anɛ árɛ̀m nkúbhɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́fú ntá Mandɛm. Yɛ̌ agha anɛ ákʉ̀ bɛtik Mandɛm, abhɔŋ bɛkʉ bhɔ́ chi nɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áchyɛ̀ yi. Ɛ́bhɔŋ bɛbhak nɔ, bɛ ndu yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ, bo mánchyɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ Mandɛm kɛnókó ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo. Mandɛm kɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ kɛnókó kɛnkɛm nɛ bɛtaŋ mɛnkɛm bɛ́chí ɛbhi ngwɛnti tí. Amen. 
Ágháká nɔ́kɔ́ ntá bǒ abhɛn báyámbɨ bábhó bɛtɨk beti beti, bákáysi bɛ chɔŋ anchyɛ awap nkáp anja ancha anɛ bǒ abhɛn babho bɛtɨk chi beku. Kɛ achyɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ntí mmu chi ɛnyumɔt, nɔ chi nkáp bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn nywɔp nɛmɔt.
Kɛ ángɛl wu arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Bǎkɛ́ chay, mbɔnyunɛ ntwɔ bhe nɛ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ áchyɛ̀ chɔŋ bo mankɛm bɛyǎ maŋák.
Ɛtɔk ɛ́rɛ ɛre ghɔɔ ɛ́nkɔt nɔkɔ mbɔ ntay ɛnɛn nɛ́ghɔ̀ ɛnɛn bábhìŋɨ bɛ Jaspa, nɛ ɛ́ŋaŋari nɔkɔ mbɔ glas. Bɛdiɛrɛ́ bhɔ bɛbhak bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ Mandɛm.
Nchí rɛm nɔ mbɔnyunɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ákàka ɛnyǔ mmǔ wu áchɛ̀m mmʉɛt nɛ yí ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhi. 
Mpok anɛ bo Israɛl bárɔ́ Bábilɔn bápɛ̀tnsɛm ɛtɔk ɛyap, Jɛkonáya achí nyaka chi Síltiɛl, Síltiɛl abhak chi Sɛrúbabɛl. Sɛrúbabɛl achí nyaka chi Ábiud, Ábiud abhak chi Ɛliákim, Ɛliákim abhak chi Ásɔ. Ásɔ achí nyaka chi Sádɔk, Sádɔk abhak chi Ákim, Ákim abhak chi Ɛ́liud. Ɛ́liud achí nyaka chi Ɛliása, Ɛliása abhak chi Mátan, Mátan abhak chi Jekɔ́p. Jekɔ́p achí nyaka chi Josɛ́f nnɛ́m María, María anɛ ábhé Yesu mmu achi Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò.
Píta asá ɛyɔŋ arɛm bɛ, “Ná nɛ bhɛsɛ́? Sɛ́rɔ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ sɛ́kòŋo wɔ!”
Yɛ̌ agha anɛ áyòŋ mmʉɛt, Mandɛm ǎsɛpti yi amɨk, nɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ ásɛ̀pti mmʉɛt amɨk, Mandɛm ǎkosi yi amfay.” 
Ɛ́rɔp chi njaŋa-mɔ̌ ywi anɛ yi are kɔŋ. Ndǔ ngwɛnti, mbɔŋɔ́nkɨ arɛm nɛ mmʉɛt yi bɛ, ‘Chɔŋ ntó mbɔ̌ŋ mɔ́wa. Yɛ̌ yí, bábhɔŋ bɛ́chyɛ yi kɛnókó.’ Afɛrɛ yɛ mɔ́ywi ató.
Nkáká Mandɛm bɛ́ mbɨ́kɨ́ jwiti yɛ̌ mmǔ ywɛka ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ fʉɛ́t chí Kríspɔs nɛ Gáyɔs.
Nnáŋ ngɔ́ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́chí ɛbhe ɛya, chɔŋ mbɔŋ nkaysi bɛto yi awu ntá yɛka.
Mɛ̌nɨ̀kmʉɛt ntá Ɛyódia nɛ Sintíke bɛ́ mándɔ́ bɛgwá ɛbhap mámbák ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔ́t, tɛ̌ndu bɔ́ bati apay báchí bǒ Yesu Kristo Acha.
Ɛ̌ti yɛsɛ, Mandɛm akʉ Kristo mmu ábhɨ́kɨ́ kʉ yɛ bɛbʉ́ ámbák mbʉ́mbʉ bɛ sɛ́mfʉ́ɛ́t ntá yi sɛ́mbák chak bɛsí Mandɛm.
Nchí ghati yɛ bhe bɛ mǎmbɔ́ŋ nkaysi amɔt, mǎmbɔ́ŋ ɛkɔŋ nɛ batɨ, mǎmbak ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔ́t ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎkʉ nɛ ntɨ nɛ́mɔ́t. Mbák mǎnkʉ́ nɔ́, maŋák ama ǎyá ancha.
Bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bábhɛ́p Yesu bɛ, “Mbák ɛnyu yɔ kɛ ɛ́chí, ndaká yí Moses árɛ́mɛ́ bɛ́ mmu ǎkway bɛrɔ ngɔrɛ́ ywi mbák achyɛ yi ɛkáti awáy nɛbhay?”
Afɔ̌ kɛ Mfɔ Agripa, nɛ gɔ́bhanɔ Fɛstɔs, nɛ Bɛnis manɔ Mfɔ Agripa, nɛ bǒ mankɛm abhɛn báchí chɔ́kɔ́ nɛ bhɔ́ báfáté.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́re pay ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi amɛm ɛkáti Mandɛm-ɛ? Ɛ́ghàti bhɛsɛ bɛ, tɛ nɛbhǒmɨk, Mandɛm aghókó nyaka mɛnyǔ bo bapay, ngɔrɛ́ nɛ mbakanɛm,
Chɔŋ mángoko yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu nɛ ngó nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyu báfyɛ̀ ngáŋ ndǔ nɛnyíɛ́ bɛ nɛ́ndɨ́ anyu.
Yɛ̌ nɔ́, Píta afate, ajɛt arɔk ndǔ nnɛm. Ákúrí nɔ́kɔ́, agʉɛp amɨ́k, ayɨŋɨ amɛm nnɛm. Aghɔ́ bɛbhɔ́kɔ́ ndɛn ɛbhɛn mánɛ́bhɛ́ nyaka mmʉɛt Yesu nɛ bhɔ bhʉ́rɛ́. Apɛtnsɛm anywɔ́p, amakati nɔkɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́nɛ́ ɛ́fákárí. 
Ángɛl arɛm nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ bɛ, “Cháy ká Mandɛm mǎndɛm bɛ mɛnwɔp ɛbhi bɛya bɛcha mbɔnyunɛ mpok anɛ yi átàŋ bo agháká. Chiɛ́ ká yi kɛnókó! Yi kɛ ághókó mfay nɛ mmɨk, nɛ bɔmanyu, nɛ babhok anɛ́ manyiɛp ányày arɛ.”
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Bo abhɛn bapu me, bápú yaŋ ngaŋ. Bǒ mame kɛ báyàŋ ngaŋ.
Ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ̌ manoŋ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka bɛrɔŋ amɨk ndu bɛkʉ bɛ ɛsɨ́ nku ɛmbɔŋ bɛtaŋ.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka ánkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ bɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛni nɛ́kɛ́ chyɛ bho ɛsɔŋɔri. Mmu ákɛ́ chwe ndǔ ndaká ntɨ. Nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka abhɔŋ bɛkʉ bɛtɨk nɛ amɔ́ yi nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ sɛ́ghátí nyaka bhe.
Bɔ̌ma, nnɛt nsúkúrú ápú kwáy mɛ́nyú bakwa nɛ nnɛt nsɨ́ŋɨ́ ápú kwáy mɛ́nyú nsúkúrú. Ɛ́nyu yɔ kɛ ɛ́chí bɛ nnyɛ́n ngáŋ ngaŋ nɛ́pú kwáy bɛ́chyɛ́ manyiɛp mɛnyu. 
Mpok yɔ, mbák ɛ́fákárí bɛ́ mmu ǎkʉ bɛtɨk amfay ɛkɛt ɛyi, ákɛ́ sɔŋɔri mmʉɛt bɛsɛp kpɨk bɛ andɔk amfɛrɛ mɛnyɨŋ anywɔ́p kɛ ambʉɛ.
Mbɔk yap mánɛ́mɛ ngó anɛ ádù gum gum gum, wu kɛsɔŋ bhɔ. Mbɔk yap bábʉ́ɛ bǒ abhɛn báyàŋ nyaka bɛway bhɔ nɛ akparɛnja. Yɛ̌ndu bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ nyaka bɛtaŋ, bɛtaŋ bɛ́kó bɔ amʉɛt. Mbɔk bábhák bɛtaŋtí batɛmɛ́ nɛnu abhɛ́n mánú básɔt awɔ́nɛm amfǎy nkwɔ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu abhɛn bɛtɔk bɛchak, nɛ bákʉ́ nkwɔ wu bábʉɛ́.
Nchí ghati bhe bɛ, mbák ayaŋ wú aghɔ, maŋák ǎyá yi antɨ ɛ̌ti ághɔ́ŋɔmɛn wu amɔt ɛncha maŋák amɛn yi ábhɔŋ bɛ anɛ́ bɛsa mɛnwi nsɛm nɛku nɛ anwi abhɨkɨ taka ɛbhɨ.
Chɔŋ mfá mpɛtnsɛm ntá Ɛtaya ngati yi bɛ, “Ɛta, nkʉ Mandɛm bɛbʉ́, nɛ nkʉ wɔ bɛbʉ́.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ákáysí bɛ́ atéé sayri, ánsɔ́t yɛ mpok bɛ́ ákɛ́ kwɛ́n.
Kɛ mǔmpap arɔk nɛ bɛti ɛnɛ́ bo bábhʉ̀rɛ kɛnɔ́, aták nchaŋ, arɔk ɛbhak ɛyi.
Ɛyɔ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ Mandɛm achí Mandɛm bo abhɛn bachi nɛpɛ́m. Apú Mandɛm bawú. Ntá Mandɛm, bǒbhɔ mankɛm bachi nɛpɛ́m.”
Nɛ mbák Mandɛm ákʉ́ mmu anɛ achi chɔkɔ andɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ anɛ bárɛ̀m, ánkúsí kpɨ́k.
Mbák mmú ámbɛ́p bhe ntí anɛ bǎkàŋari yɔ́, ghatí ká yí bɛ, ‘Acha kɛ áyàŋ yɔ, nɛ chɔŋ antó mántwɔ mánkɛmɛ yɔ́ tɛ́mté.’”
Tɛ́mté wu, asɔt batɛmɛ́ nɛnu nɛ mbɔk bǒbati bhap básɛ́p barɔk arɛ. Bo bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ yí ndǔ átwɔ̀ nɛ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu, bábhɔ́t bɛdɛn Pɔ̌l.
Nti apu anɛ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛchyɛ akap yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nywɔp mbɔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mǔngo bachiǎkap anɛ mbɨ. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap ǎyambɨ nyaka anchyɛ akap ɛ̌ti ɛbhi bɛbʉ́, kɛ andɔk yɛ ambɨ bɛkʉ nɔ ɛ̌ti bɛbʉ́ bo bachak. Yesu achyɛ́ akap ndɔŋ amɔt ndak ámáy, mpok yi achyɛ mmʉɛt bɛ mango ndu ɛkotákátí.
Chi bɛfʉɛt ntá Yesu Kristo kɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm ákwàk bhɛsɛ nɛ be bɛ sɛ́mbɔ́ŋ mbi bɛrɔŋ ntá Ɛta.
Mbɔk bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, bárɛ́m ntá Yesu bɛ, “Yɨŋɨ́, baghɔkɔ́ bhɛ bákʉ̀ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́pú chak bɛkoŋo ɛbhé yɛsɛ. Bákʉɛ̀p nchwi ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt!”
Bakokosi bhi nɛ bǒnɛrɛ́kɛt, bághók nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyǔ bɛrɨ̌ntɨ ɛbhɛ́n Mandɛm átɔ́ŋɔ́ yí, báré ŋák nɛ yi.
Bárɔ́ŋ nɔ́kɔ́ ntá Páílet nɛ Yesu, ate bɛsí bhi. Páílet abhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Wɔ kɛ ɔ́chí nɛ́ Mfɔ bo Israɛl?” Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Ɛ́chí mbɔ ɛnyu ɔ́rɛ́mɛ́.”
Kɛ sɛbhɔŋ bɛkaka Mandɛm bɛ yɛ̌ndu bǎchi nyaka ndu kɛsɛmɛ́ bɛbʉ́, nɛ́nɛ, bǎkòŋo nɛ batɨ ayɛka ankɛm, mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bátɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka bhe. Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ kɛ bárɔ́ amɔ yɛka.
Kɛ abhɛn kɛ́ŋwáŋ bákɛ́mɛ bɛ, ‘Ngufú bawɛt amɛn sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ apu kway chɔŋ bhɛsɛ nɛ bhe. Dɔ́k ká ntá batǐ bawɛt mǎnku amɛka bawɛt.’
Árɛ́mɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, arɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Dɔ́k ká, mǎnu bɛrɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm árɛ́mɛ́. Arɛm bɛ básɨŋ bɛ, ‘Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ̌yáŋ chi bɛ bo mángɔ́ ntínso nɛ batɨ, puyɛ̌ chi akabhɛ́nya.’ Mbɨ́kɨ́ twɔ bɛbhɨŋɨ bǒ abhɛn bakaysi bɛ bachi chak bɛsí Mandɛm bɛ mámbák bakoŋo bha, ntwɔ bɛ́bhɨ́ŋɨ chi bo babʉ́babʉ́.” 
Nɨk nɔ́kɔ́ ká mmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm nɛ chɔŋ yi anchyɛ bhe kpák. Nɛ ɛnyu kpák anɛ Mandɛm áchyɛ̀, bǒ mmɨk bápú kwáy bɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ wáwák. Nɛ chɔŋ Mandɛm ankʉ kpák ámbák amɛm batɨ yɛka, ankʉ bɛ kpák ámbák nkwɔ́ ndǔ nkaysi yɛká, bɛ yɛ̌yi yɛ̌yi, bǎkɛ bhɔŋ bɛcháy. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́chí tɛtɛp mbɔnyunɛ bǎbhat mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Kristo.
Yesu anyabhɛ awɔ́ atɔk yi arɛm bɛ, “Nkɔŋ bɛkʉ wɔ ɔ́ntáŋ, nɛme ɛnɛ nɛ́máy.” Tɛ́mté wu, ɛbhaŋákwa yi ɛmay.
Abhɛ́p bakoŋo bhi bɛ, “Ntɨkɨ ɛpʉ́ítí nɔ bǎkɛ̀m nɛ bhɔ?”
Bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Sɛ́kwày bɛkʉ nɔ.” Yesu arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Tɛtɛp chɔŋ mǎnka ɛnyǔ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ mɛ̌ghɔ nɛ mǎngu ɛnyǔ nɛwú ɛnɛn mɛ̌gù,
Ɛ́rɨ ɛcha ntá bǒ abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nsay nɛ ɛkwak bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi chak bɛsí Mandɛm, mbɔnyunɛ chɔŋ yi anchyɛ bhɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛkwak bɛbhɔŋ!
Ɛnyumɔt kɛ ɛchi bɛ mbák Satan ǎnù nɛ mmʉɛt ɛyi, ákɔ́rɛ́ ákwɛn ndǔ kɛfɔ ɛki, nɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi mɛ́may.
Mandɛm ǎfoŋori yɛ̌ agha anɛ árɛ̀m ɛbɛ́ptí ɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti nnyɛ́n ɛna, Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm, kɛ apú foŋori mmu anɛ árɛ̀m ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ. Mandɛm apú foŋori yi, yɛ̌ ndǔ mmɨkɨ nɛ, nɛ yɛ̌ ndǔ mmɨk nkɔ.” 
Kɛ mpok ángɛl anɛ ajwi bɔángɛl tándrámɔt áfè chɔŋ ayi mmbá, nkaysi Mandɛm anɛ áchí bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ ǎfu kpoŋoroŋ, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi ághátí nyaka barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ bhi.”
Bǎbhɨkɨ re pay ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ basɨŋɨ ndǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm bɛ́: ‘Nkúbhɛ́ ntay ɛnɛn batɛ̌kɛt bágʉɛ́bhɛ́ bɛ́ nɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ rɨ, nɔ́ kɛ nɛ́rɔ́bhɛ́ ntay ɛnɛn nɛ́kɛ́mɛ́ ɛkɛt nɛchá batay áchák ankɛm?
Ngók ɛyɔŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fù amfay. Ɛ́bhak mɛ batú mbo ɛwarɛ́ tutunyɛ́n nɛ mbɔ nɛfaŋ anɛ ásày nɛ mbɔ ɛyɔŋɔ bakɨŋ anɛ bɔ̌ bákwɛ̀t.
mbɔnyunɛ Mɔ́nkwɔmɛn mmu achi kɛkwɔt nɛ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ ǎbhàbhɛri bhɔ. Ǎrɔŋ nɛ bhɔ ndǔ babhokó nyɛ́n anɛ manyiɛp ami áchyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m. Nɛ chɔŋ Mandɛm antɛsɛ bɔ babhɛsɛ mankɛm amɨk.”
Sɔt basénsí baghɔrɛ́ mbɔ bɔmáyɛ, ɔ́nsɔt baghɔrɛ́ abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ ghaka ɛkaká nɛbhe ɛyɛ mbɔ bɔ̌máyɛ. Nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛ nɛ́kɛ́ bhɔŋ bakwap.
Bě babhɔŋ bǎchí batísiɛ ndǔ ndɛ́mɛ́ bɛ́ puyɛ̌ mɛ kɛ̌ nchí Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò. Nchí chí mpɔkɔntó anɛ Mandɛm átó bɛ njambɨ kɛ yi antwɔ.
Ɛrɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛchak ɛ́bhésí amfay. Ngɔ́ ɛrɛmɛ nnya mbʉ́mbʉ anɛ ápe chuuu nɛ batí tándrámɔt, nɛ babhaŋ byo. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ntí ábhɔ́ŋ aywi mɔ́nta kɛfɔ.
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, Lɛ́vi anak ɛrɛm ɛpa ɛkɛt yi ntá Yesu. Bɛyǎ babhɛbhɛ́ nkábhɛ́nti nɛ bakʉ̌ bɛbʉ́ bachak nkwɔ babhak arɛ́ nɛ Yesu.
“Mmɔ̌ amɔt achi fá, anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkpɔkɔ́ brɛt bɛtay nɛ nsi ɛpay, kɛ ɛyɔ chi yi ntá bɛyǎ bǒbhɛn?”
Ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ yi ndǔ áwàk ngó, ayɨŋɨ yi dǐǐ arɛm bɛ, “Wɔ nkwɔ́ ɔchí mbʉ́ nɛ Yesu mmu Násárɛt-nɛ.”
Manyɛ́n bǒnto Yesu bhɔ bati byo nɛ apay achi bɛ: Anɛ mbɨ abhak Símun. Nnyɛ́n ɛni nɛ́chák nɛ́bhak bɛ Píta. Achák abhak Andru, manɔ́ Píta. Nɛ Jems nɛ mɔ̌máyi Jɔ̌n, bɔ̌ Sɛbɛdi.
Kwak nɔ́kɔ́ ká bo Mandɛm abhɛn ɛyap ɛ́pú, mǎnsyɛpti nɔkɔ mankɔ amɛm bɛkɛt ɛbhɛka sayri.
Mǎnáŋ mǎngɔ ɛsɔŋɔri, nɛ ɛ́pú bhak chɔŋ ndu ɛrɔri mpok, chɔŋ mbɔŋ Mandɛm mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛrɨ̌ndu mɛnkɛm ankʉ mǎnte sɛnɛ́, ɛnyɨŋ kɛchɛp bhe, ambʉrɛ bhe ndu nté anɛ mǎnáŋ bǎchi nyaka arɛ, anchyɛ bhe bɛtaŋ. Yi kɛ ábhɨ́ŋɨ́ be bɛ mǎmbɔŋ ákɔ́rɛ́ ndǔ kɛnɛ́m ɛkɛn kɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti ndǔ bǎchɛ́mɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Kristo.
Chi-bɛtɨk ywi ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́ arwɔ̌ yi ɛnyuyɔ, akaka yí bɛ́ yi abhɔŋ kɛ́ŋwáŋ bɛ́káysi ndak. Ɛchi tɛtɛp bɛ bǒ mmɨkɨ nɛ bákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhap nɛ kɛŋwaŋ bácha ɛnyǔ bo Mandɛm bákʉ̀ ɛbhap.”
antó be Mpɛmɛ yi afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò bɛ ambak Mpɛmɛ yɛka.
Júdas asɔt ɛká batɛmɛ́ nɛnu nɛ mbɔk babhabhɛri abhɛn ɛkɛrákap abhɛn bǒbati bachiǎkap nɛ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bátó. Bɔ́ mankɛm barɔk arɛ nɛ bɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ nɛnu amɔ.
Bǎbhʉɛ́t chí mǎmbɔ mbɔnyunɛ nkaysi yɛká abhʉɛ́t chí ndǔ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ mmɨk. Bǎbhɔŋ mpabhamɨ́k nɛ batɨ. Bǎgwà nɛ batɨ. Ɛyɔ ɛ́pú tɔ́ŋ nɔ́ bɛ́ nkaysi yɛká abhʉɛ́t chí ndǔ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ mmɨkɨ nɛ? Chí ɛnyu ɛyɔ.
Yɛ̌ agha anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ ka bɛpɔkɔ ɛyi ɛko ankoŋo mɛ apú kway bɛbhak nkoŋo wa.
Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm kɛ̌ bǒ abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl básɨ́kɨ́ ntɨ arɛ. Kɛ Ɛtayɛka mmu áchí amfay arɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ bǎbhɔŋ bɛ́bhɔ́ŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm.
Nchwi áchák akwɛnti ndǔ mmɨk ndɨ́ndɨ́, achak, agó, achyɛ bɛyǎ nchwi. Nchwi ayá acha anɛ bápɨ́ ndɔŋ ɛsa nsɛm byo, achák ndɔŋ bɛsa bɛrat, anɛfu ndɔŋ bɛsa bɛtay.”
Kɛ ángɛl arɛm nta baghɔrɛ́ bɛ, “Bǎkɛ́ chay. Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ bǎyàŋ Yesu mmu bágó ndǔ ɛkotákátí.
Ɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ manywɔp átay, mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ́ Ananías asɛp arɔk Siséria nɛ mbɔk bǒbatí ɛtɔk, nɛ ntaŋanyu amɔt anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ́ Tɛtúlɔs. Báchwɔ́bhɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bɛsí gɔ́bhanɔ Fɛ́liks, babho bɛbhat Pɔ̌l barak amʉɛt.
Yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛ́pú bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ bɛsí Mandɛm. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi aghoko ɛchi kpoŋoroŋ bɛsí bhi. Ntá yi kɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛsɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛrɛm ntí anɛ yi ákʉ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ákʉ́. 
Ɛchi mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́ghàti bhɛsɛ bɛ “Nkwǎŋwaŋ nkɛm achi mbɔ tákɔ, bɛrɨ bhi mɛnkɛm mbɔ bɔchuchu abhɛn tákɔ. Tákɔ ǎwɔsi, bɔchuchu mánkuri,
Bǎrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ Mandɛm abhɨ́kɨ́ yap bhɛsɛ chi bɛ sɛ́mbák bo abhɛn yi átàŋ anchyɛ ntɛmsi. Ayap bhɛsɛ chi bɛ ánkʉ Yesu Kristo Acha ámpɛmɛ bhɛsɛ.
Kɛ nchí ghati bhe bɛ, mánkwɛ́sɛ́ bayǎ nyaka amɛm ɛtɔk Israɛl ndǔ mpok ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Ɛláija. Mpok yɔ manyiɛp kɛkwɛ́n ndǔ mamiɛ́ arat nɛ ɛbhɔ́k, nɛ ɛrɛmɛ́ nsay ɛ́kwɛ́n ndǔ ɛtɔk Israɛl ɛnkɛm.
Sɛ́bhɔŋ ɛ́fɛ́mɛ́ akap ɛnɛ bachiǎkap abhɛn bákʉ̀ nyaka bɛtɨk amɛm ɛtɛm bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ngǎngaŋ bɛsɔt ɛnyɨŋ arɛ manyíɛ́.
Nnyɔ́ áré gboko manyiɛp anyu amɛn achi mbɔ nnyɛ́n bɛ́ nɛ́mpɔ́kɔ́ yi mbɔ ɛghori manyiɛp.
Yɨŋɨ́ ká kɛnɛn. Kɛ́pú kwaŋ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ kɛ́pú fɛrɛ mbwɔt ɛbhɨ. Kɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛkɛt nɛ yɛ̌ chi bɛ̌ták ɛbhɛn bɛ́bhʉ̀rɛ nɛnyíɛ́ arɛ́. Mandɛm kɛ áchyɛ̀ kɔ nɛnyíɛ́, nɛ bɛsí Mandɛm, bǎcha kɛnɛn tontó!
Bakoŋo Yesu bhɔ bárɔ́k bakʉ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi aghati bhɔ.
Anɛ mbɨ arɔk aghatí yí bɛ, ‘Acha, mbɔ̌ŋ nsáy bɛbhǎ nkáp byo amfay ɛbha ɛ́mɔt ɛnɛ ɔ́chyɛ́ mɛ.’
Bě bǒ Rom nkwɔ bǎchi ndǔ mpǎy bo abhɛn Mandɛm ábhɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ mǎmbak bǒ Yesu Kristo.
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ bɛ́kóŋó bɛbhé Moses, babhɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɛsɔt manoŋ ndu bɛkʉ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ mɛ́mbak pɛ́pɛ́p. Mbák manoŋ abhɨkɨ rɔŋ amɨk, bápú foŋori bɛbʉ́ bho. 
Ɛnyǔ mǔngo bachiǎkap wu kɛ ákwáy yɛ bɛkwak bɛsɛ, mbɔnyunɛ yi achi nyáŋá, abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛ́kwɛ́nɛ́, abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bakwap, achí kɛkúrí nɛ bǒ bɛbʉ́, nɛ achí ndǔ nɛbhʉɛ́rɛ́ kɛnókó amfay.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛka. Ghók ká, nnɛ́nɛ́ mbǐnywɔp ndɔ́ fúú ntá yɛka anɛ́ yɛ̌ mmu ápú kway bɛtyɛp. Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ bǎbhɔŋ chi mandú bɛtaŋ, Yɛ̌ nɔ́, bǎkòŋo ɛyɔŋ ɛya nɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ bʉɛ mɛ.
Sɔt mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ɔ́ghókó ndǔ mɛ̌tɔ̀ŋ kpoŋoroŋ bɛsí bɛyǎ batísiɛ tɔ́ŋ ntá bǒ tɛtɛp. Sɔt bɔ́ tɔ́ŋ ntá bo tɛtɛp abhɛn bákway bɛtɔ́ŋ bhɔ́ ntá bo báchák nkwɔ́.
Bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Yesu mmu Násárɛt.” Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Ghɔ́ mɛ́ nɛ.” Júdas mmu atí yi abhak arɛ́ téé nɛ bhɔ.
Ɛnɛ́ yi átàk árɔ̀ŋ, mbɔk akwɛnti ndǔ mɔ́mbi anɛ áchí amɛm nkɨ. Kɛnɛn kɛ́twɔ́ kɛ́bwɔ́pti yɔ nkɛm
Bɛ́rɔ́ŋ ambɨ Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Mbák mámbók ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ́ndɔ́ mmu, ɛ́rɔp chí bóŋboŋbóŋ amɛm baso, ɛ́njaŋ nɔkɔ ɛbhak ɛnɛ yɔ ɛ́chwe. Mbák ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ ghɔ́ ɛbhak bɛchɔkɔ,
Mbák be bǒ bɛbʉ́, bǎbhɔŋ ntɨ bɛchyɛ bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ ntá bɔ̌bhɛka, bǎkáysí bɛ Ɛta mmu achi amfay, ǎnɔk bɛchyɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ntá bo abhɛn mánɨ̀kmʉɛt bɛ yi anchyɛ bhɔ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ kɛ?” 
Ɛ́chí ɛnyu ɛyɔ mbɔnyunɛ manoŋ mpɔŋ nɛ manoŋ mmɛ́n ápú kway bɛfɛrɛ mmu bɛbʉ́ anti wáwák.
Kɛ mbák chí bǒ bɛbʉ́ nɛ bǒ bapu bábɛ̀p mándɔk nɔkɔ chi ambɨ, bárwɔ̀ bho, bo mándwɔ nɔkɔ bhɔ́.
Bɔ̌ma, ntí apú bɛsɨŋ be ɛ̌ti mbɔ̌ŋ mpok anɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́fákari.
Ndu mɛ́máka ndǔ nɛrɨŋɨ́mɛnyɨŋ bɔ́ŋ ká nkwɔ nɛkɛmɛ́mʉɛt. Nɛ mɛ́máka ndǔ nɛkɛmɛ́mʉɛt, tě ká kpirí. Nɛ mɛ́máka ndǔ nɛte kpirí, bɔ́ŋ ká ɛpɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bo Mandɛm bábhɔŋɔ bɛbhɔŋ.
Kɛ mbɔŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛcha ɛyɔ chi bɛ sɛbhɔŋ maŋák ndu bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛsɛ mbɔnyunɛ sɛrɨŋɨ bɛ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛkwak bhɛsɛ sɛngɔk bɛte kpirí.
Nkwɔ ywɛka anɛ bákàysi bɛ bɛbhʉrɛ bɛbhé bo Israɛl kɛ ǎkʉ bɔ mambak chak bɛsí Mandɛm babhɔŋ bɛrɨŋɨ bɛ báfap mmʉɛt nɛ Kristo. Báfɛrɛ mmʉɛt ndǔ bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm.
Afate yɛ, apɛtnsɛm ntá baghɔkɔ́ bhi abhɛn bati arat. Aghɔ bhɔ ndu bábhʉrɛ kɛnɔ́. Abhɛ́p Píta bɛ, “Bǎpú kwáy bɛ́chɔ́kɔ pě nɛ mɛ ndǔ nɛŋɔkɔ́ nywɔp nɛ́mɔ́t-ɛ?
Yesu arɛm nɔ, mbɔnyunɛ mbɔk bho bárɛ̀m nyaka bɛ, ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛsɔŋɔri yi. 
Nkoŋo Yesu wu kɛ ághàti bhɛsɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn, nɛ yi kɛ ásɨ́ŋɨ́ bhɔ amɨk. Nɛ sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yí árɛ̀m ɛchi tɛtɛp. 
Arɛm bɛ ɛchi sayri bɛbhɔŋ ɛsɔŋɔri nɛ bo Mandɛm ɛcha mɛ́nyiɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn bɛbʉ́ ndu mɔ́mbɨŋɨ mpok.
Akɛmɛ bhɔ́ bɛ́ “Mandɛm achyɛ́ mbi bɛ mǎndɨ́ŋɨ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛchi bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ ɛ̌ti ɛnyǔ yi ákɛ̀m bǒbhi mbɔ Mfɔ wap. Kɛ mbák chi bo bachak, nchí rɛm kɛpɨ nɛ bhɔ́ chi ndǔ bakay bɛ yɛ̌ndu báyɨ̀ŋɨ bákɛ́ ghɔ, nɛ yɛ̌ndu bághòk bákɛ́ jwimɛm.” 
Yesu aghɔ́ ndu ɛ́bè baghɔkɔ́ bhi mmʉɛt mɛ́nók áchwi ɛ̌ti mbʉ́ɛ́p anɛ áfù bhɔ́ ambɨ. Bɛfʉɛt nkárɛ́nká ɛ́rát bɛghaka nkárɛ́nká ɛtandat betí, abho bɛkɔ amfay manyu ankoŋo nɔkɔ bhɔ. Arɔk kpát ɛrɔp kɛkwɔt bɛfʉɛt bhɔ.
Mbák bǎkɔŋ chi bǒ abhɛn bákɔ́ŋɔ́ bhe, ntɨkɨ nsáy bǎbhɔŋ? Yɛ̌ chí bakʉ̌ bɛbʉ́ mbɔ babhɛbhɛ́ nkábhɛ́nti bakɔŋ bǒ abhɛn bákɔ́ŋɔ́ bhɔ.
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ áchyɛ́ yɛ̌ chí manyiɛp bakwɛn ntá yɛ̌ mmu amɔt ndǔ nkwɔ bɔ̌bha bhɛn mbɔnyunɛ achí nkoŋo wa, dɨŋɨ́ bɛ Mandɛm abhɔŋ bɛchyɛ yi akap.”
Kɛ bǒnkwɔ bákʉ nchwe amɛm ɛkay ɛnɛ básɛ́rɛ́ nnɨk arɛ bátɔ́ ndu mbok anɛ achi ankok, básɛ́bhɛ mɛ amɨk, mbʉɛ.
Bo Israɛl abhɛn Bɛ́roa bábhɔ́ŋ ntɨ bɛghok mbok Yesu anɛ́ Pɔ̌l nɛ Sáilas bághàti bhɔ ɛ́cha abhɛn Tɛsalónika, mbɔnyunɛ básìɛpti nyaka Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm nɛ bɛyǎ ɛkwak. Báre chak Ɛkáti Mandɛm bɛghɔ mbák mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Pɔ̌l átɔ̀ŋ bɛchi tɛtɛp.
“Acha nɛ Mandɛm mmu sɛ́tòk, wɔ kɛ ɔ́kwáy mmu anɛ bo bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛrɛm bɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛ bɛyǎ bɛcha mánchyɛ wɔ kɛnókó nɛ bakak ɛ̌ti bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛ, mbɔnyunɛ wɔ kɛ ɔ́ghókó mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm nɛ chí bɛ́kóŋo nkaysi yɛ kɛ ɔghoko bhɔ nɛ bɛchi.”
Ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ Yesu nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ, ajɛt, arɔk atɛp mánɛ́n bɛsí bhi,
“Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎghɔ̀ nɛ mɛnkɛm, mpok ǎtwɔ̀ anɛ ɛkɛt ɛnɛ ɛ́rɔ̀ŋ amɨk ɛnkɛm yɛ̌nyɨŋ kɛrɔp téé.” 
Yesu aghati yi bɛ, “Dɔ̌ bawú mámbɛ́mɛ́ ngú wap. Kɛ wɔ, dɔ́k ghati bo Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti ɛnyu Mandɛm abhak nɛ bho mbɔ Mfɔ wap.”
achyɛ bakak ntá Mandɛm, abho bɛ́bɔ́kɔ́ti ɛkpɔkɔ́ brɛt ɛyɔ anchyɛ nɔkɔ ntá bakoŋo bhi andɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Nɛ́ chí mmʉɛ́t ɛya anɛ mɛ̌chyɛ̀ ɛ̌ti yɛká. Kʉ nɔ́kɔ́ ká ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ ndu bɛ́tɨk mɛ.”
Ɛkʉ arɔk, abhat mmʉɛt nɛ mmǔ ɛtɔk ɛyɔ amɔt. Ató yi bɛ ándɔ́k, áne nɔ́kɔ́ bakók bhi amɛm nkɨ ywi.
Mányókóti yɛ mbwɔpti anɛ bo mányíɛ́, bárɔ́. Ajwi bɛkay byo nɛ bɛpay.
Achyɛ yɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ́ mánjwiti bhɔ́ ndu nnyɛ́n Yesu Kristo. Bájwítí bhɔ. Bárɛm bɛ Píta anchɔkɔ nɛ bhɔ ndu mpǎy manywɔp.
Faté, sɛp, dɔ́k áyák nɛ bhɔ nɛ ɔ́kɛ́ chɔnti mpok. Mɛ kɛ ntó bɔ.”
Mmǔ anɛ básɔ́rɛ́ ndǔ bɛtɨk bɛ ámbábhɛ́rí nɔ́kɔ́ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n ɛnɛ́ yi ápú mbabhɛri bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n nɛ yɔ apu ayi, ǎghɔ nkwɔ ndu átwɔ̀ andɔ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n ambʉɛ́, nkwɔ ankɛ́m mbɔk, nɛ antak achak.
bɛ́ mbák Mandɛm ánkwák, mɛ nkwɔ́, mpɛ́tnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m mbɔ Yesu. 
Nɔ́ bhɔ! Nchí ghati be bɛ, mbák bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ tɨ́knsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛka, chɔŋ bě mankɛm mǎngu mbɔ bhɔ.” 
Tɛ́mté wu, ɛbhaŋákwa yi ɛ́may, ataŋ.
Bakwɔ́ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu abhɛn mfay báre koŋo yi. Bábhak amfay mpɔŋɔ́ndɨk pɛ́pɛ́p nɛ ndɛn pɛ́pɛ́p amʉɛt ɛnɛ́ ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bakwap.
Bábhʉ́rɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu aghati bhɔ antɨ, bɔ́kɛ ghati yɛ̌ mmu ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bághɔ. Mámbɛbhɛ nɔkɔ chi batɨ bɛ, “Nɛpɛrɛ́nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m chi yi?”
Ɛchi ɛnyumɔt bɛ ndu sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ mɛnɨkmʉɛt mbɔ ɛnyu sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ, Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ǎkwak bhɛsɛ. Yímbɔŋ ǎnɨkmʉɛt ɛ̌ti yɛsɛ ansɔk nɔkɔ nsɔ́k ɛnyu ɛnɛ ɛ́chá ɛnyǔ mmu ánɨkmʉɛt nɛ ɛyɔŋɔ́nyu.
Mɛ Pɔ̌l kɛ nchí sɨŋ nɛ awɔ́ wa ndu bɛkaka bhe. Ɛnyunɛ kɛ nchí sɨŋ ndǔ ngwɛnti bɛkáti bha mɛnkɛm bɛkʉ bo mándɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛkáti ɛnɛ́ ɛ́fú ntá ya.
Yesu ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛtɛm nɛkǎy nkwaŋankɨ, baghɔk abhi bárɔ́k ntá yi bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ndaká yí ɔ́ghàti bho mɛnyɨŋ ndǔ bakay?”
Yesu abú bɛyǎ bo abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ mame mɛnyu nɛ mɛnyu. Abók bɛyǎ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ́rɔ́ bho. Yí kɛka bɛ bɔ́ mɛ́ndɛm yɛ̌nyɨŋ mbɔnyunɛ bɛ́rɨŋɨ nyaka mmǔ yi achi. 
Mandɛm ánchyɛ́ bhe yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛrɨ́tí ɛnyɨŋ, bɛ mǎnkóŋó nɔ́kɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi áyàŋ mǎnkʉ. Mandɛm ankʉ Yesu Kristo ankwak be mǎnkʉ́ nɔ́kɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chyɛ yi maŋák. Sɛ́nchíɛ Yesu Kristo bakak mpoknkɛm ɛ̌ti kɛnɛ́m ɛki. Amen. 
Wáwák! Ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn bɛ́fakari nɛ bhɛsɛ, Kristo mmu ákɔ́ŋɔ́ bhɛsɛ ǎchyɛ bhɛsɛ awɔ́nɛm tontó.
Asɔt yɛ bɔ́ ɛkɛt ɛyi achyɛ bhɔ́ nɛnyíɛ́. Yi nɛ ɛfo ɛyi ɛnkɛm bájwi nɛ maŋák bɛ mánóko Mandɛm.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmíɛ́, chi nɛ nnɔ Yesu bárɔ̀ŋ nyaka Yerúsalɛm ndǔ *Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ.
Sɛ́ré nók sɛ́ndɔkɔ nɔkɔ pɛtii ndǔ mpǎy manywɔp. Sɛ́bhɔ́ŋ bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri kɛ sɛ́chwɔp kɛ́kwɔ́t nɛ Kɨnídɔs. Mbʉ́ɛ́p ataŋataŋ kɛka sɛ́ndɔ́k ámbɨ. Sɛ́mɔ́kɔ́ri sɛ́rɔ́bhɛ́ nók sɛ́mfʉɛrɛ nɔkɔ chi ɛbhě Krɛt ɛnɛ́ nnyɛ́n nɛ́chí tɨ̌í, kɛ́kwɔ́t nɛ njiɛ Salmɔ́nɛ.
Mbʉ́ɛ́p áchí nyaka mpok yɔ. Ɛ́kʉ́ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk abhɛn mǔngo bachiǎkap nɛ babhabhɛrǐ ɛkɛrákap báfyɛ́ ngo ndu nntó bakiri, báté bághábhɛri mángwák nɔkɔ ngó wu. Píta nkwɔ arɔk ate nɛ bhɔ angwaka nɔkɔ ngo. 
Bátwɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɛ yí bo Israɛl abhɛn báfú Yerúsalɛm bákáp yí báfyɛ́ nɛ́ntɨ́ mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ́ Pɔ̌l ákʉ́ bɛyǎ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ. Yɛ̌ nɔ, bɔ́ kɛkwáy bɛtɔŋ kpoŋoroŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ́ bárɛ̀m bɛ́ yí akʉ́.
Yesu abhɨŋɨ bhɔ́ bɛ mantwɔ ntá yi. Bárɔ́ŋɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́, abho bɛghati bhɔ ndǔ bakay bɛ, “Satan ǎkway bɛbok mmʉɛt ná?
Bɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ mmǔ anɛ átɨ́ bɛbhay ngɔrɛ́, mbák aghɔ bɛ abhɔŋ bɛbhay ngɔrɛ́ ndǔ bɛyǎ ɛkwak bɛ́chí yi antɨ nɛ apu kway bɛkɛm mmʉɛt, nɛ mpok ǎfʉɛ̀t, ɛ́rɨ bɛ́ ámbáy ngɔrɛ́. Bɛbʉ́ bɛpu arɛ.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ́ bɛ, “Ndiɛrɛ nɛ nɛnɨkímʉɛt nɛ nɛtarɛ́nsay kɛ bákway bɛkʉ ɛnyǔ ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛnɛ ɛ́mfu mmu amʉɛt.”   
Chɔŋ mandi kɛbhɔ mánto nɔkɔ mfok antí bɛtɔ́ŋ kɛbhɔ ɛkɛn kɛchi bhɔ antɨ. Chɔŋ mandi nɔkɔ bɛ, ‘Ɛrɛm ɛtɔk, ɛbɛp ntá yɛ ɛcha. Ɛtɔk ɛnɛ kɛ ɛ́kʉ́ bǒbhɛn babhɔŋɔ bakáp. Ndǔ mɔ́nɛŋɔkɔ́ nywɔp amɔt, ɛ́rɔŋ ɛnkɛm!
Mpǎy babhakanɛm abhɛn manyíɛ́ brɛt wu nɛ nsi ɛyɔ abhak mbɔ nka ɛtay. 
sɛ́tó mɔ́mayɛsɛ Tímɔti ntá yɛká. Yí achí ntɨ nkʉbɛtɨk Mandɛm ndu bɛ́gháti bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Kristo. Sɛ́tó yi bɛ ámfyɛ bhe ntɨ, ankʉ mǎnté kpirí ndǔ nɛka ɛnɛka,
Mbɔ̌ŋ bɛyǎ maŋák mpok ngókó ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mbɔk bɔ̌mayɛsɛ ndǔ nnyɛ́n Yesu bátwɔ́ fá baghati bɛsɛ. Bághátí bhɛsɛ bɛ wɔ ɔchí mmǔ tɛtɛp ndǔ mbi Mandɛm nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyu, sayri sayri, ɔ́kóŋó tɛtɛp.
Yesu aghati bakoŋo bhi bɛ́ mántóŋtí áchwí anɛ yi áchwè arɛ ndǔ bo baya bacha, bɛ bákɛ́ nyɨrɛ yi.
Ndu bɛ́rɔŋ ambɨ, mpok ɛyɔ bo bápu bhɔŋ ɛkɔŋ nɛ batɨ nɛ yɛ̌ chí amɛm manɛrɛ́kɛt, bápu foŋori batɨ. Bárɛm ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti batɨ ndu bɛchɔŋti manyɛ́n ɛyap. Ndǔ mpok ɛyɔ, bo bápú kway bɛkɛm mmʉɛt, kɛ bádù mbɔ nkwɔ kɛbhɔ́ŋ ntínso nɛ batɨ, nɛ bápú kɔŋ ɛrɨ́tɨ́ ɛnyɨŋ.
Yɛ̌ nɔ, mbɔk yɛka bábhɨ́kɨ́ noko.” Yesu arɨ́ŋɨ́ bo abhɛn bábhɨkɨ noko yi tɛ ndǔ nɛbhǒnɛt, nɛ arɨ́ŋɨ́ mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛti yi.
Tɛ̌ndu sɛ́gú nɛ Kristo, sɛ́noko bɛ chɔŋ sɛ́mbak nkwɔ nɛ yi.
Tɛtɛp, mbák nku nsɨ́ anɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ tat ǎkway nyaka bɛtɔŋ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ Mandɛm, Nku Nkɔ anɛ abhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti abhɔŋ bɛtɔŋ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ ɛbhi ancha anɛ nsɨ́.
Pɔ̌l nɛ Sáilas barɔk baghaka Dɛ́be nɛ bafu nɔkɔ arɛ barɔk Lístra. Nkoŋo Yesu amɔt abhak arɛ́ anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ́ Tímɔti. Máyi abhak mmu Israɛl anɛ ánókó Yesu, kɛ aywi chí abhak mmǔ Grik.
Nkúbhɛ́ Yesu kɛ̌ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m ɛ̌ti yi bɛ́: ‘Ntay ɛnɛ́n bě batě bɛkɛt bǎbyáká, nɔ́ kɛ nɛ́rɔ́bhɛ́ ɛkwap ɛnɛ́ ɛ́kɛ́mɛ́ ɛkɛt.’
Bǒ bhɔ mankɛm bare nu bɛtɔk Yesu, mbɔnyunɛ bɛtaŋ bɛ́fù nyaka yi amʉɛt mɛ́mbu nɔkɔ yɛ̌ ághá anɛ átɔk yi. 
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ányíɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnǐ ɛnɛ́n nɛ́kwáy yi, Yesu aghati bakoŋo bhi bɛ, “Nyokotí ká mbwɔ́ptí anɛ árɔ́bhɛ́ bɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛkɛ chɔŋti ndɛ́ndɛm.”
Nɔ́ kɛ ɛ́fakari nɛ mmu anɛ ábhʉ́rɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ ntá yímbɔŋ, kɛ yi kɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛnwɔp bɛsí Mandɛm.” 
Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ mbɔ nkárɛ́nká ɛyɔ ɛ́rát, Yesu abɨk arɛm bɛ, “Ɛli, Ɛli, lama sabátani?” Nɔ́ chi, “Mandɛm wa, Mandɛm wa, ndaká yí ɔ́fɛ́rɛ́ ntí nɛ mɛ?”
Ɛchi mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Yɛ̌ mmu apu chak bɛsí Mandɛm, yɛ amɔt apu,
Ǎkʉ bɔ mangɔ bɛ bachi bǒ bɛbʉ́ mbɔnyunɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ noko mɛ.
Yɛ̌ chi mpok anɛ sɛ́gháká atú Masidónia sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt. Bɛsɔŋɔri bɛre twɔ bɛbhě mɛnkɛm.
Ɛkʉ, Yesu apɛt aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Tɛtɛ̌tɛp, mɛ kɛ nchí nyǔbhá bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n.
Yesu afa atú ɛtɔk ɛyɔ apɛtnsɛm ɛtɔk ɛyi Násárɛt. Bakoŋo bhi bárɔ́k nɛ yi.
Ntí anɛ ngátí wɔ ɔ́ndɛm bǒbhɔ mándɔ́ bɛ́tɔŋ baraká nsé chí bɛ bo Mandɛm mámbɔŋ ɛkɔŋ nɛ batɨ. Nɛ chi ɛnyǔ ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fù ndǔ ntɨ ɛnɛ́n nɛchí amɛm pɛ́pɛ́p, ntɨ ɛnɛn nɛpú ka mmu ánkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́twɔ̀ yi nɛ áyɔ́mɛ, ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ nɛtɔ́ŋ ɛnɛn tɛtɛp.
Píta arɛm ntá Yesu bɛ, “Ɛta, ghatí bhɛsɛ ntí nɛkay ɛnɛn.”
Ɛbhé ɛ́twɔ̀ nɛ ntɛmsi Mandɛm ntá bo ndu bápú bhʉɛrɛ yɔ, kɛ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ ɛbhé ɛpú, mmu apu kway bɛkwɛn ɛbhé.
Ɛ́tárɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, mpok ɛpǎ bo Israɛl ɛ́chák akwáy. Yesu akó, arɔk Yerúsalɛm.
Bɔ̌ma, bǎchi yɛ bɔ Mandɛm chí mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ chɔŋ mǎmbak bɔ̌bhi. Ɛ́chí nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ chɔŋ Ábraham ambɔ́ŋ Áisek.
Ɛ́kʉ́ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bákpɔ́ti manɨk anɛ ákɛ̀m áchwí bárɔ́ bɛ nnyɛ́n nɛ́ndɔbhɛ wu pɔkɔ́ wú.
Mbok yɔ atwɔ ntá yɛka mbɔ ɛnyǔ átwɔ́ ntá bo mmɨk nkɛm nɛ ǎnyù kɛpɛm nɛ ágò. Nɔ kɛ yɔ achi nyaka ndǔ nkwɔ yɛka bɛbho ndu nywɔp ɛnɛn bǎghókó ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm nɛ bǎjwimɛm ɛnyu bɔ bɛchi tɛtɛp.
Ángɛl anɛ ájwí bárát apɨkɨri ɛyi ɛkwɔbhɛ́ bɛběntɨ amɛm manyɛ́n agho nɛ bɔ̌manyɛ́n nɛ ndǔ bɛbhak ɛbhɛn manyiɛp ányay arɛ. Manyiɛp mankɛm arɔp chi manoŋ.
Ngók yɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fù ndǔ ɛ́fɛ́mɛ́ akap Mandɛm ɛyɔ ɛ́ndɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Acha, Mandɛm Bɛtaŋ Mɛnkɛm, ɔ̌chyɛ̀ bho ntɛ́msi ɛnyu ɛnɛ ɛchi sayri nɛ chak”.
Nɛ sɛ́nɨ̀kmʉɛt bɛ Mandɛm ánsɔt bɛtaŋ ɛbhi ɛbhɛn bɛyǎ bɛcha ánkʉ mǎmbɔŋ nɔkɔ bɛtaŋ, bɛ yɛ̌yí yɛ̌yi, mǎmbɔŋ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ́, mǎnte sɛnɛ́, mǎndɔkɔ nɔkɔ chi ambɨ nɛ maŋák,
“Agha árɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Acha ákàysi? Agha ánáŋ áchí nchyɛ maníɛ́ ntá yi?”
Ngɔ́ ndǔ Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n áfɛ́rɛ́ ɛtabhɛ́ bɛbhanɛ ɛ́mɔt ndǔ bɛtap tándrámɔt ɛbhɛn ɛkáti nɛ́nɛ́p. Ngók ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mɔt ndu ɛbhɛn mɛnwi ɛ́sáy mbɔ nɛfaŋ bɛ, “Twɔ́!”
Ánas mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm, nɛ Káyfas, nɛ Jɔ̌n, nɛ Aleksánda, nɛ bǒnɛrɛ́kɛt mǔngo bachiǎkap báchɛm nɛ bhɔ.
Acha aghati yi bɛ, “Faté dɔ́k ndu nkɔngɔ-ɛtɔk anɛ́ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ́ Téé. Ɔ́náŋ ɔ́nchwɔp ndǔ ɛkɛt Júdas bɛ́p mmu Tásɔs anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ́ Sɔ̌l. Achí arɛ́ ǎnɨ̀kmʉɛt.
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎrɛ́mɛ́ ansɛm ansɛm, chɔŋ bo mangok yɔ kpoŋoroŋ. Nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎghati bǎrǔ bho ansɛm ansɛm chɔŋ bo mánte amfay bɛkɛt mámbɨk bɛ bo mángók. 
Nchí kʉ nɔ nɛ bɛyǎ maŋák mbɔnyunɛ bǎchɛm mmʉɛt nɛ mɛ tɛ nɛbhǒnɛt bɛghaka ɛchɔŋ, ndǔ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn mɛ̌kʉ̀ bɛ́gháti bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu.
Sɛ́yàŋ chí bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi chak, puyɛ̌ chi ndiɛrɛ bɛsí Mandɛm Acha, kɛ bɛsí bho nkwɔ.
Matá ankʉ nɔkɔ chi bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn nywɔp ndu mɛne Yesu. Ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́ bɛtɨk bɛyǎ ntá yi aywǐntí, arɔk ntá Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Acha, ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ ghɔ ndǔ mɔ́maya árɔ́ bɛtɨk mɛnkɛm mɛ awɔ́? Ghatí yi antwɔ ankwak mɛ!”
