Yí wu chi Yesu mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛbhak amfay nɛ Mandɛm kpátɛ mpok anɛ yi ákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm mɛ́njíbhírí mɛ́ndɔp bɛkɔ. Barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm mánáŋ bárɛm tɛntɛp bɛ chɔŋ ɛ́mbak ɛnyu yɔ.
Páílet arɛm yɛ ntá bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ ngɛ́mtay bo abhɛn bachi arɛ bɛ, “Mbɨ́kɨ́ ghɔ yɛ̌ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ nɛ mmǔ-nɛ.”
Ayɨkɨ ndǔ nnyɛ́n mmu anɛ achi nɛpɛ́m mpoknkɛm, mmu anɛ ághɔ́kɔ́ mfǎy nɛ mmɨk nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi amfay nɛ ɛnɛ ɛchi amɨk, aghoko manyu nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨn ɛnɛ ɛchi amɛm. Ayɨkɨ arɛm bɛ, “Mpok bɛpɛt bɛchɔŋti apu!
Nɛ ndu bɛ́rɔŋ ambɨ, ɛ́chí nɛbhʉɛt achák amɛm Ɛkáti Bakway bɛ Debhít arɛm ntá Mandɛm bɛ, ‘Ɔpú rɔ chɔŋ Mmu anɛ áchyɛ́ nɛpɛ́m ɛni ntá yɛ ámpɔ́ amɛm nnɛm.’
Sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ Mandɛm achi chak ndǔ nɛtáŋ anɛ yi átàŋ bo abhɛn bákʉ̀ mɛnyǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ.
Banábas nɛ Sɔ̌l, mánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́pɔ́kɔ́ bhɔ́ Yerúsalɛm, bápɛtnsɛm Antiɔk. Básɔ́t Jɔ̌n Mák, arɔk nɛ bhɔ.
Mmu ákɛ́ pɔkɔ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ nkáp amʉɛt.
Mbák chí mɛ, nɛpɛ́m ɛna nɛ́naŋ nɛ́rɔ̀ŋ mbɔ nnya anɛ bárɔ̀ŋ bɛchyɛ akap ntá Mandɛm nɛ yɔ. Mandú mpok mɛ̌rɔ mmɨk.
“Nɛ́nɛ, Ɛta Mandɛm atɔŋ mɛ bɛrɨ̌ndu. Afɛ́rɛ́ ntíánwɔ́p anɛ́ mɛ̌bhɔ̀ŋ nyaka bɛsí bho.” 
Bábhɔŋ bɛkpaŋ yi amfay ɛnɔk bɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ anoko yi, ámbɔ́ŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.
Abhɛn ɛkɔŋ, mbák batɨ yɛsɛ ápú ji bhɛsɛ sɛ́pu bhɔŋ bɛcháy bɛsí Mandɛm mpok sɛ́nɨkmʉɛt.
Mbɔk bho bátɔ̀ŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi bɛkɔ nɛ kɛkúrí. Bǎkɛ́ rɔ yɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ́ bátɔ̀ŋ mɛ́mpɔ́kɔ́ bhe mǎngúrɛ́ ɛbhɨ. Ɛrɨ bɛ bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm mɛ́nkʉ batɨ yɛsɛ antaŋ, puyɛ̌ chí bɛbhé ɛ̌ti nɛnyíɛ́. Bɛbhé bhɔ bɛ́pú kwak bo abhɛn bákòŋo bhɔ.
Ndak yí ɔ́bhɛ́p mɛ mɛnyɨŋ? Bɛ́p bo abhɛn bághókó mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ndɛ́mɛ́. Bɛ́p bɔ́ mángátí wɔ. Bárɨŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ndɛ́mɛ́.
Yesu árɛ̀m bɛ, “Ghók ká, mɛ́twɔ̀ mandú mpok! Ɛ́rɨ ɛcha ntá mmu anɛ ábhʉ̀rɛ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn bɛchi amɛm ɛkáti ɛnɛ. Yɔ́ ɛ́rɛ̀m ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛbhɔŋɔ bɛfakari.”
Akɔŋ bǒ bhɛsɛ nɛ yímbɔŋ kɛ áté ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí ɛyɛsɛ.”
“Nchí ghati yɛ be bɛ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ árɛ̀m kpoŋoroŋ bɛsí bǒ mmɨk bɛ yi achi mmu wa, chɔŋ Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm ndɛm bɛsí bɔángɛl Mandɛm ndǔ nywɔp manyé bɛ mmu wu achi awa.
Bɔ́ŋ nkaysi anɛ achi chak, mǎndɔ bɛbʉ́. Mbɔk ayɛka bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ Mandɛm wáwák. Nchí rɛm nɔ bɛ ntíánwɔ́p ankɛm be.
Ndu ɛchi yɛ̌ nɔ, yi ɛ́kway bɛkʉ sɛ́mpányu? Yɛ̌nyɨŋ! Nɛ ntí achi bɛ yi? Chi bɛ sɛ́kʉ̀ bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ kɛ? Wáwák! Chi bɛ sɛ́noko.
Mamʉɛrɛ́ abhɛn mǔnti wu átó bápɛtnsɛm ɛkɛt ɛyi, bághɔ́ bɛ mǔbɛtok ywi anáŋ ataŋ. 
Nchí rɛm nɔ mbɔnyunɛ mɛ nkwɔ́ mbɔ̌ŋ bo abhɛn, mbák mángátí mɛ nkʉ ɛnyɨŋ, mbɔ̌ŋ bɛghok bhɔ. Nɛ mbɔ̌ŋ nkwɔ́ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu antɛnɛ ya abhɛn mbák ngátí bhɔ ɛnyɨŋ, bábhɔŋ bɛghok mɛ́. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap anɛ ndɛ́mɛ́ bɛ, ‘Dɔ́k’, ǎrɔŋ, nɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ ndɛ́mɛ́ bɛ, ‘Twɔ́’, ǎtwɔ. Nɛ mbák ngátí mɔ̌bɛtok awa bɛ, ‘Kʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ’, abhɔŋ bɛkʉ yɔ.”
Yesu aghati bho mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm chi ndǔ bakay. Yi kɛ ghati bhɔ́ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi abhɨkɨ tɛ́m nɛkay.
Ɛ́chí yɛ bɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ anoko Mmɔ Mandɛm, ǎrɨŋɨ̀ amɛm ntɨ ɛni bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm arɛmɛ ɛ̌ti Mɔ́ywi ɛchí tɛtɛp. Bǒ abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ noko bárɛ̀m bɛ Mandɛm ǎsè chi nsé mbɔnyunɛ bɔ́ bábhɨ́kɨ́ noko ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ̀m ɛ̌ti Mɔ́ywi.
Ágháká nɔ́kɔ́ ndu nkɔ́k anɛ bɛ́chwe anywɔ́p, batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bápɔ́kɔ yi ndǔ bághɔ́ bɛ́ bɛyǎ bo abhɛn bachi arɛ babho bɛ́twɔ nɛ baraká bɛtaŋ.
Mbɔ ɛnyu yɔ kɛ ɛchi, mbʉ bo abhɛn mánóko Kristo bǎgu mánɛ́m.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Nnáŋ ndɔ́k, mpú rɔ mǎmbák mbɔ bɔ̌bɛrǎ. Chɔŋ mpɛtnsɛm ntá yɛka.
Ngɔrɛ́ abhɔŋ bɛ́chɔ́kɔ kpák ámbɔ́ŋ nɛsɛptǐmʉɛt, antá batu ndu bɛghok mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bátɔ̀ŋ amɛm ɛkɛt Mandɛm.
Ɛnyu ɛyɔ, be nɛ bo Mandɛm báchák mankɛm bǎkwáy bɛjwimɛm bɛ Kristo akɔŋ bhɛsɛ tontó ɛnyu ɛnɛ mmu apu kway bɛyɛnti yɔ.
Chɔŋ bɛtaŋtí nɛnyikisǐ mmɨk nɛ nsay nɛ bɛghorǐ mame mɛ́mbak mbǎŋ nɛ mbaŋ. Nɛ chɔŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ́ntwɔ nɛ bɛyǎ bɛcháy, nɛ bɛrɨŋɨ́ maknkay mɛ́mfu amfǎy.
Sɔt ka mpok bɛghok Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm sayri ɛnyu ɛnɛ bǎjwimɛm mbɔnyunɛ mmǔ anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ, chɔŋ mámaka yi ɛ́chák, kɛ mmǔ anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ, yɛ̌ chí mandú anɛ yi ákáysí bɛ́ abhɔŋ, chɔŋ mánsɔt yɔ ntá yi.” 
Ɛyɔ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛ́chí nɛntɨ bɛbhé Mandɛm nɛ bariɛp Mandɛm kɛ? Wáwák! Mbɔ bachyɛ bo ɛbhé ɛnɛ́ ɛ́kʉ mmu ámbɔ́ŋ nɛpɛ́m mbák ábhʉ̀rɛ yɔ, mbʉ bɛbhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé ákʉ̀ mmu ambak chak bɛsí Mandɛm.
Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ mbɔ nkárɛ́nká ɛyɔ ɛ́rát nɛ ngósí, Yesu abɨk arɛm bɛ, “Ɛli, Ɛli, lama sabatani?” Nɔ́ chi, “Mandɛm wa, Mandɛm wa, ndaká yí ɔ́fɛ́rɛ́ ntí nɛ mɛ?”
aghati yi bɛ anchyɛ yi bɛkáti ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́chyɛ yi bɛtaŋ bɛrɔŋ Damáskɔs ndu bɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt bo Israɛl bɛ́ mbák ángɔ́ bakoŋo Mbi Yesu arɛ́, ankwáy bɛ́kɛ́mti bhɔ́, baghɔrɛ́ nɛ babhakanɛm, angwɔ́t, andɔk Yerúsalɛm nɛ bhɔ́.
Kɛ́ sɛ́chí bo Mandɛm nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ árɨ́ŋɨ́ Mandɛm ǎghòk ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ sɛ́tɔ̀ŋ. Mmu anɛ apu mmǔ Mandɛm apú ghok bhɛsɛ. Ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ sɛ́rɨ̀ŋɨ mbák Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm mmu ákʉ̀ bo mándɨŋɨ tɛtɛp anɛ Mandɛm kɛ achi nɛ mmu, nɛ mbák ɛfóŋó ɛnɛ ɛ́rwɔ̀ bho kɛ ɛchi nɛ mmu.
Ɛnɛ́ bárɔ̀ŋ nɔ, basɔt bakʉ̌ bɛbʉ́ bati apay nkwɔ abhɛn batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bárɔ̀ŋ nyaka bɛway nɛ Yesu.
Píta asá ɛyɔŋ arɛm bɛ, “Yɨŋɨ́, sɛ́rɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm sɛ́kòŋo wɔ.”
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛp ɛncha ntá mmu anɛ ákʉ́ mɔ́wa amɔt anɛ abhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛka nɛ mɛ ánkwɛ́n ndǔ bɛbʉ́. Ɛchi sayri ntá mmu wu, bɛ mánsɔt ntǎy nɛgho mánsɛt ɛmɨ yi, mamɛsɛ amɛm manyu.
Ndǔ nnyɛ́n Yesu Kristo Acha sɛ́ghàti mɛnyǔ bo bhɔ sɛ́njɛp nɔkɔ bhɔ batú bɛ mánkʉ ɛbhap bɛtɨk. Mándɔ́ bɛ́chyɛ ɛsɔŋɔri mánkʉ bɛtɨk ndu bɛbhɔŋ ɛnap nɛnyíɛ́.
Mɛ Jɔ̌n mǔnti bakoŋo Yesu kɛ nchí sɨŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ. Gáyɔs, nchí sɨ́ŋ ntá yɛ, wɔ mmu nkɔ́ŋɔ́ tɛtɛp.
Bǎkɛ́ kaysi bɛ́ chɔŋ ngati Ɛta ɛnyǔ bho bǎchi. Moses kɛ ághati chɔŋ yi, Moses mmu bǎbhaka ntɨ nɛ yi.
Achí nyaka mpoknkɛm nɛ gɔ́bhanɔ ɛtɔk ɛyɔ anɛ aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Sɛjɔs Paólɔs. Sɛjɔs Paólɔs abhak ndɨŋɨndak. Abhɨŋɨ Banábas nɛ Sɔ̌l mbɔnyunɛ áyàŋ nyaka nkwɔ bɛghok Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm.
Tɔmás arɛm ntá Yesu bɛ, “Acha, sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ ɔ́rɔ̀ŋ, ná sɛ́kwày bɛrɨŋɨ mbi?”
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛ́gháti Jɔ̌n bɛ, “Sɨ́ŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ to ntá ángɛl anɛ ábhàbhɛri bǒnkwɔ abhɛn ɛtɔk Smína. Sɨ́ŋ kʉ bɔ́ mándɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fú ntá Mmǔ anɛ achi nɛbhǒnɛt nɛ ngwɛnti, yí mmú ágú nyaka kɛ apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.”
Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ anáŋ akʉ nyaka yi arɨŋɨ bɛ́ apú gu kɛghɔ́ Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò.
Chɔŋ bǒ mmɨk mámbɔŋ bɛyǎ maŋák, mánto batɨ akap nɛ mányiɛ ɛpa mbɔnyunɛ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ bhɔ batí apay báchyɛ̀ nyaka bhɔ bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri.
Ɛkáti ɛnɛ́ báchyɛ́ bhɔ́ mándɔ́k nɛ yɔ ɛ́ré rɛm bɛ, “Bɛsɛ́ bǒnto Yesu nɛ bǒbatí nɛ bǒnkwɔ́ Yesu mankɛm sɛ́kàka be bɔ̌máyɛsɛ abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl awu Antiɔk, nɛ abhɛn Síria nɛ abhɛn Silísha.
Bɛyǎ bǒbhɔ báre koŋo yi mándɛm nɔkɔ bɛ, “Wáy ka yi!” 
Ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ mɛnɨkmʉɛt, afate, apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ yí árɔ́ baghɔkɔ́ bhi. Aghɔ bhɔ ndu bábhʉrɛ kɛnɔ́ ndu mánáŋ bápɔ́bhɛ́ ɛ̌ti bɛyǎ basɛ́mɛ́.
Bɔ̌ma, nnáŋ ntɨ bɛ́twɔ awu bɛyǎ mpok, kɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́chɛ̀t mɛ mbi. Nnáŋ nte bɛ́twɔ awu bɛ bɛtɨk ɛbha mɛnyu kɛpɛm ndǔ nkwɔ ywɛka mbɔ ɛnyu bɛ́kʉ̀ ntá bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl amɛm bɛtɔk bɛchak.
Mbák chi mmu anɛ ághòk Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm anjwimɛm, ɛ́mbak yi antɨ, achí mbɔ mbwɔt anɛ ákwɛ́ntí ndǔ mmɨk ndɨ́ndɨ́, achak, ágó sayri, achyɛ bɛyǎ mbwɔt nkɔ. Nɛ nsáy Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m mmu achi mbɔ mbwɔt nkɔ anɛ áyá áchá anɛ bápɨ́, ndɔŋ ɛsa nsɛm byo, achák ndɔŋ bɛsa bɛrat, nɛ anɛfu ndɔŋ bɛsa bɛtay.” 
Mbɔŋ bɛdɛp awɔ antɨ ɛ̌ti mmu wu, kɛ mpú kʉ nɔ ɛ̌ti mmʉɛ́t ɛya. Nchi dɛp awɔ antɨ chi ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ.
Kɛ bákɛ rɛm yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Yesu asɔt mmu wu abú yí. Arɔ yɛ yí arɔk.
Mmʉɛrɛ wa amɔt anɛ achi ambi ndǔ nɛkɔ atwɔ mɛ anywɔ́p nɛ́nɛ, nɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ nɛnyíɛ́ bɛchyɛ yí anyiɛ!’
Anɛ ɛkɔŋ, ɔ́kɛ́ ŋɔkɔ ɛbɛ́ptí ɛpɨŋ. Ŋɔkɔ́ chí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́rɨ́. Mmǔ anɛ ákʉ̀ bɛrɨ chi mmu Mandɛm, kɛ mmu anɛ ákʉ̀ bɛbʉ́ ábhɨ́kɨ́re ghɔ Mandɛm.
Kɛ ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ noko ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ngati wɔ, ɛnɛ́ ɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛfu tɛtɛp mbák mpok akway. Tɛ̌ndu ɔ́bhɨ́kɨ́ noko, chɔŋ ɔ́nkwɛ́n kɛbhók ɔkɛpɛrɛ kwáy bɛrɛm kɛpɨ kpátɛ nywɔp ɛnɛ́n bariɛp amɛn áfu tɛtɛp.”
Bo ɛchɛmɛ bǒ batí ɛtɔk bághókó nɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Stífin árɛ̀mɛ, batɨ ábé bɔ tontó, amɨ́k apěti anti.
Satan akó anti Júdas anɛ mpɨ́kɨ́rí nnyɛ́n ɛni nɛchi bɛ Iskariɔt. Júdas achi nyaka mmu amɔt ndǔ nkwɔ baghɔk Yesu bati byo nɛ apay.
Sɛ́fɛ́rɛ́ ntí ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́twɔ̀ nɛ ntíánwɔ́p nɛ ndǔ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bo bákʉ̀ ansɛm ansɛm. Sɛ́pú kʉ bɛtábhá nɛ mmu wáwák nɛ sɛpu mɔ bɛyibhiri Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ sɛ́kʉ̀ chi bɛghati bho tɛtɛp Mandɛm ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ákwày bɛrɨŋɨ bɛ sɛchi bǒ tɛtɛp bɛsí Mandɛm.
Píta abho bɛ́koŋo yi. Nɛfú anɛ báfú ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ, yí kɛrɨŋɨ bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ángɛl ákʉ̀ ntá yi chí ndaká tɛtɛp. Are kaysi bɛ́ ághɔ̀ nɔ chi kɛnɔ́ amɨ́k antífú.
Ngɛ́mtay ɛyɔ ɛbhak mbɔ mpɔŋɔ́ndɨk ɛnɛ batoŋti bɛrɔŋ ɛbhɨ̌nɛnu nɛ yɔ. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ngɛ́mtáy abhɔ́ŋ ɛnyɨŋ anti mbɔ nta kɛfɔ anɛ bághókó nɛ pú. Bɛsí ɛbhap bɛbhak mbɔ ɛbhɛn nkwǎŋwaŋ.
Nɛ mbák ngɔrɛ́ anɛ ásɨ́kɨ́ ntɨ nɛ Yesu abhɔŋ nnɛ́m anɛ ápú nkoŋo Yesu, kɛ nnɛ́m akɔŋ bɛ́chɔ́kɔ nɛ yí, ngɔrɛ́ wu ákɛ́ rɔ yí ndǔ nɛbhay.
Mbák bo báchyɛ̀ wɔ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛ̌ti ɔchí nkoŋo Yesu, nɨkmʉɛt bɛ Mandɛm anjɛt bhɔ. Kɛ́ rɛm bɛ ɛyak ɛmbak nɛ bhɔ. Nɨk chí mmʉɛt bɛ Mandɛm anjɛt bhɔ.
Mbák mɛ, Acha nɛ Ntɔŋ aywɛka nsó bɛkak ɛbhɛka, be nkwɔ bǎbhɔŋ bɛso bɛkak batɨ!
Kaká ká batɨ sayri nɛ ɛkɔŋ Mandɛm. Bakwɔ́ bho Kristo mankɛm bátò bhe bakak. 
Nɛka ɛnɛn bo abhɛn tɛ nyaka kɛ nɛ́kʉ́ nyaka Mandɛm arɛm bɛ bɔ bákʉ sayri.
Ɛta Mandɛm árɛ̀m yɛ bɛ, “Fú ká nɛntɨ nap fap ka mmuɛ́t nɛ bhɔ. Bǎkɛ́ nyɔ́p mmʉɛt nɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bakwap, nɛ chɔŋ mpɛt nsɔt be amʉɛt.”
Nɛka ɛnɛn ngɔrɛ́-nɛkɔ anɛ aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Ráhab kɛ nɛ́kʉ́ yi ásɔ́rɛ́ nyaka bǒ abhɛn bárɔ́ŋɔ́ ndu bɛghokoti kɛpɨ abhɛsɛ amɛm ɛkɛt ɛyi, yí kɛgú mpok amɔt nɛ bo abhɛn bapú ghok nyaka Mandɛm.
Nɛchwe áchwè amɛm mɔ́tɔk amɔt, bǒ ɛbhaŋákwa bati byo bághɔ́ yi ndu átwɔ̀, báte, kɛrɔ́ŋ kɛ́kwɔ́t nɛ yí.
Bě bachǐbhɔ, bǎkɛ́ bhɔŋ ɛpɨŋ bɛkʉ batɨ ambe bɔ̌ bhɛka. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ chi mɛ́nyúrɛ nɛ bɛtɔŋ bhɔ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Acha áyàŋ. 
Nɛ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛpɛt ɛ́rɛ̀m ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt áchák bɛ, “Chɔŋ bo mámkpɔk yi anɛ báyɛ́mɛ́.” 
Bɛ́bhó ɛwak ɛyɔ, bǒbati bo Israɛl báré yáŋ mbi bɛ́wáy Yesu.
Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Tɛtɛ̌tɛp, Ábraham ápɛ́rɛ bhák, Mɛ Nchí.”
Bě mankɛm nɛ bo Israɛl mankɛm dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ chí Yesu Kristo mmu Násárɛt kɛ ákʉ́ mmǔ-nɛ ataŋa. Yí mmu bágó ndǔ ɛkotákátí, kɛ̌ Mandɛm akʉ yí apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, ndǔ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi kɛ̌ bǎghɔ́ mmǔ-nɛ áté be bɛsí kpɛrɛp.
Afyɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm amɔ́ yi bɛ ndǔ ákʉ́ yi mmu abhɔŋ bɛtaŋ amfay yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ, ámbák mǔnti ntá bǒnkwɔ.
Sɛ́kwɛn nyaka manyé bɛsí Mandɛm ndu sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ kʉ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi áyàŋ. Kɛ adákátí ɛkati manyé bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛsɛ, nɛ ɛ́bhak mbɔ bɛ ábáy nyaka bhɔ anti Yesu, nɛ bágó yi ndǔ ɛkotákátí nɛ bhɔ.
Páílet ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Josɛ́f árɛ́mɛ́, abhak maknkay bɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ́ Yesu agu. Abhɨŋɨ mǔntí batɛmɛ́ nɛnu anɛ aghɔ ndu Yesu ágù, abhɛ́p yi mbák anáŋ agu tɛtɛp.
nɛ bɛyǎ bo Israɛl bárɔ́k bɛ́wáka nɛ Matá nɛ María ndǔ nɛwú mɔ́mayap.
Kɛ mmu anɛ ataŋa kpoŋoroŋ bɛsí bho bɛ apu mmu wa, chɔŋ mɛnkwɔ ntaŋa bɛsí bɔángɛl Mandɛm bɛ yi apu mmu wa.
Báré su bɛbʉ́ bhap, Jɔ̌n anjwiti nɔkɔ bhɔ amɛm Nnyɛ́n Jɔ́dan.
Bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ bǒ ɛchɛmɛ́ bataŋá manyé bachak mankɛm báré yaŋ bo abhɛn bákway bɛbhat Yesu barak amʉɛt ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ bɔ́ bábhɔŋ mbi bɛway yi, kɛ bákɛ bhɔŋ yɛ̌ mbi.
Bɔ́ŋ ká nɛsɛptímʉɛt nɛnkɛm. Bǎkɛ́ bhak gum gum nɛ bho. Bɔ́ŋ ká ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ. Tɔ́ŋ nɔ́kɔ́ ká batɨ ɛkɔŋ, mǎnsɔt bhɔ mbɔ ɛnyǔ bachi.
Bɛsɛ́ bho sɛ́yámbɨ bɛbhaka ntɨ nɛ Kristo sɛbhɔŋ bɛkʉ bo mámbɨ́tɨ́ yi ɛ̌ti kɛnɛ́m ɛki.
Bák ká ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt nɛ batɨ. Bǎkɛ́ yoŋ mmʉɛt, fyɛ́ ka mmʉɛt nɛ yɛ̌ chí bo abhɛn bápú yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Bǎkɛ́ kaysi bɛ bǎrɨŋɨ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ.
Ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu árɛ́mɛ́, bo Israɛl bápɛ́t báre yaŋ mbi bɛway yi. Ntí abhak bɛ, puyɛ̌ chi ndiɛrɛ bɛ akwɛn ɛbhé nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt, kɛ ndak anɛ́ akpɨk ábɛ́bhɛ́ áchá ábhák bɛ, yí ǎbhɨ̀ŋɨ Mandɛm bɛ ɛtayi, nɛ bɛ bɛ́kʉ nɔ chi bɛyɛnti mmʉɛt nɛ Mandɛm. 
nɛ bǎrɔbhɛ koŋo chi ɛpɨŋ ɛkɔ. Bǎyíbhírí bǎrɔp bǒ bakɔ nɛ bǎyìbhiri mǎndɔkɔ nɔkɔ chi ambɨ mǎndɔbhɛ nɔkɔ mbɔ Mandɛm. Yi kɛ ághókó bhe mbɔ bǒ bakɔ bɛ mǎndɨŋɨ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti yi.
Yesu nɛ Píta bákó nɔ́kɔ́ ndu áchwí, mbʉ́ɛ́p wu ákwɛn.
Ngɛ́mtay bho báré kɔ nɛ Yesu. Ayibhiri mmʉɛ́t arɛm ntá yap bɛ,
Ɛ́kʉ́ barɛm ntá Arɔn bɛ, ‘Ghokó bɔmandɛm ntá yɛsɛ, bɛ mandɔkɔ nɔkɔ bhɛsɛ ambɨ. Mbák chi Moses mmu áfɛ́rɛ́ bhɛsɛ ɛtɔk Íjip, sɛbhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛfakari nɛ yi.’
Sɔt yɛ ka mpok! Nnáŋ ngati nɔ bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ambɨ ambɨ. 
Mbák sɛ́nkɛ́pntɨ ndǔ bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛsɛ, chɔŋ sɛ́mbak bafɔ nɛ yi nkwɔ. Mbák sɛ́ndɛm bɛ́ sɛ́bhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ yi, chɔŋ yí nkwɔ andɛm bɛ́ abhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ bhɛsɛ.
Kɛ Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Puyɛ̌ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu kɛ ǎkway bɛka bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn. Ndiɛrɛ bo abhɛn Mandɛm achyɛ́ bhɔ ntɨ bɛ́chɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, kɛ̌ bákway bɛka bhɔ.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mmu ányíɛ́, ɛ́pú chwe yi antɨ, ɛ́rɔŋ chi mɛniɛ ɛbhi nɛ ǎji yɔ amfɛrɛ.” Yesu arɛm nɔ, ndu áyàŋ bo mándɨŋɨ bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ́kway mɛnyiɛ.
Ghatí bhɔ́ bɛ mmu ákɛ́ rɛm ndak abʉ́abʉ ɛ̌ti ntɨ, nɛ bɛ mánchɔ́kɔ́ sayri nɛ batɨ, mámbak ndu kpak nɛ batɨ. Ɛrɨ mámbɔ́ŋ nɛsɛptímʉɛt bɛsí bo mankɛm.
Mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ bɛtaŋ bɛ́táŋ bǒ abhɛn bápú bakoŋo Yesu. Bǎbhɔŋ bɛ́táŋ chí batɨ̌ bǒ nkwɔ́ abhɛn bákʉ̀ bɛbɛptí mɛnyɨŋ mbɔ ɛbhɛn.
Anɛ ɛkɔŋ, nchí nɨkmʉɛt bɛ ɔ́kɛ́ me, nɛ bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛmbak sayri nɛ wɔ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛ mbɔ mmu Mandɛm nɛchi sayri.
Kɛ ɛ́chí ɛnyu ɛyɔ nɛ bhe nkwɔ. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu abhɔŋ bɛkɔŋ ngɔrɛ́ ywi mbɔnyu ákɔ́ŋɔ́ mmʉɛt ɛyi yímbɔŋ, nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ngɔrɛ́ abhɔŋ bɛchyɛ nnɛ́m ywi kɛnókó.
Mpok básɔ̀kɔti yi, abhɨ́kɨ́ kɛmɛ yɛ̌ nsɔk. Mpok yi ághɔ̀ ɛsɔŋɔri, abhɨ́kɨ́ pa yɛ̌ mmu. Árɔ barak ankɛm ntá Mandɛm mmu átàŋ manyé ɛnyu ɛnɛ ɛchi chak.
Básɨŋ ndǔ ɛkáti bɛbhé ɛyɛka bɛ, batísiɛ bati apay mándɛm ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mɔt, nɔ́ chí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bɔ́ bárɛ́mɛ́ ɛ́chí tɛtɛp.
“Júdas atí nɔ́kɔ́ Yesu, asɔt nkáp manoŋ anɛ́ báchyɛ́ yi aku ɛkpɔkɔ́ mmɨk. Nɛ ndǔ ɛkpɔ́kɔ́ mmɨk ɛyɔ, yímbɔŋ akwɛ́n kɛ́bhɛri mɛniɛ bɛ́sɛ́n, mántɛp árɔ́ri amɨk, agú.
Bɛyǎ bhó bághɔ́ ndu bɔ́ bárɔ̀ŋ. Bárɨ́ŋɨ bɛ́ chí Yesu nɛ bǒbhi bhɔ, nɛ bárɨŋɨ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bárɔ̀ŋ. Bɛyǎ bho báfú ndǔ bɛtɔk nɛ bɛtɔk, báfa nɛ bɛkak, bárɔk ntiɛ́t ntiɛt, báre noŋ bɔ ambɨ.
Ndǔ mpok yɔ, chɔŋ bo mándɛm ntá njiɛ ɛgho bɛ, ‘Kwɛ́n ká bay bhɛsɛ́’; nɛ ntá bɔ̌njiɛ bɛ, ‘Kutí ká bhɛsɛ.’
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛcha bɛchak mɛnkɛm chi bɛ mǎndɔk ambɨ bɛkɔŋ batɨ nɛ batɨ ayɛka ankɛm tɛ̌ndu ɛkɔŋ ɛ́kùti bɛyǎ bɛbʉ́.
Bɔ̌ chi amɔt bati tándrámɔt báchí nyaka fá. Anɛ mbɨ abháy ngɔrɛ́, agú ɛnɛ́ yi abhɨkɨ bhɔŋ yɛ̌ mmɔ́. Anɛ ákòŋo yi, asɔt kɛ́nkwɛ́sɛ́ wu ndǔ nɛbhay.
Mmu anɛ ányìɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ákɛ́ byak anɛ apu nyiɛ mbɔk mɛnyɨŋ. Nɛ mmǔ anɛ apu nyiɛ mbɔk mɛnyɨŋ ákɛ́ ji anɛ ányìɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm aka yi.
Mpok Yesu Acha átwɔ̀, bo Mandɛm mankɛm báchyɛ̀ yi kɛnókó nɛ bǒ abhɛn mánókó mámbak maknkay bɛ bághɔ́ yi. Bě nkwɔ bǎbhak chɔŋ nɛ bhɔ mbɔnyunɛ mǎnókó mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn sɛ́ghátí bhe.
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “María!” María ayibhiri mmʉɛt arɛm ndǔ ɛyɔŋ bo Israɛl bɛ, “Rabóni!” [Nɔ chí “Ntɔŋ”].
Kaká ka batɨ sayri mbɔ bo Mandɛm.
mǎngati mbɔŋɔ́kɛt bɛ, ‘Ntɔŋ ǎto bhɛsɛ bɛ sɛ́mbɛp wɔ bɛ, mɔ́kɛrɛ́ mankɔ anɛ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛ́nyiɛ Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ nɛ baghɔk abha achí fá?’
Ndu ákɔ́ŋ bhɛsɛ, anáŋ atɨ nyaka bɛ sɛ́mfʉ́ɛ́t ntá Yesu Kristo sɛmbak bɔ̌bhi. Akʉ nɔ bɛkoŋo ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi átɨ́ nyaka bɛkʉ,
Kɛ yɛ̌ mmu apú kwáy bɛkɛm nɛ́rí ɛni. Nɛ́rí nɛ́bɛp nɛ́chá. Nɛ́chí mbɔ babhé amɛn mmu ányìɛ angú.
Kɛ́ chwe ndǔ kɛ́mbwɔ́bhɛ́ ɛkɛ́n kɛ́pú chyɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó. Ɛ́nyu kɛ́mbwɔ́bhɛ́ ɛkɔ kɛ́kʉ̀ bo mánsap nɛkɔ nɛ Mandɛm.
nɛ bɛbhɔŋ amɨ́k abʉ́abʉ nɛ batɨ, nɛ bɛkwɛn mmɛ́m, nɛ bɛpǎ ɛbhɛn bɛ́tò bo ndǔ ɛpúsí, nɛ mɛnyɨŋ bɛchak mbɔ ɛbhɔ. Nchí ya be batú mbɔ ɛnyu ɛsɨ́ bɛ́, bo abhɛn bákʉ̀ mɛnyǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bápú kway bɛbhɔŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti nɛ Mandɛm.
Nchí ghati bhe bɛ, yɛ̌ agha anɛ ághàti njiɛ bɛ, ‘Fǎ fá dɔ́k kwɛ́n awu amɛm manyu,’ nɛ yí kɛ makati ndǔ ntɨ ɛni kɛ anoko bɛ Mandɛm ǎkʉ nɔ ntá yi, Mandɛm ǎkʉ yɔ ntá yi mbɔnyunɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ makati bɛ Mandɛm ǎkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi arɛmɛ ɛmfakari.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ákʉ̀ barak abʉ́abʉ ǎpap ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́. Apú rɔŋ ɛbhak ɛnɛ ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛchi ndǔ ápú yaŋ bo mangɔ mɛnyɨŋ yi ákʉ̀.
Ɛchi nɔ mbɔnyunɛ yí mmu Mandɛm átó, árɛ̀m chi Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm achyɛ́ yi Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ njɛnti ti.
Ndǔ bábɨ̀k, bábhó bɛfok ndɛn ɛyap nkwɔ nɛ báre toko mfok mántak nɔkɔ amfay.
Ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ́ Pɔ̌l nɛ Banábas bábhó bɛ́rɛm kɛbhɔŋ bɛcháy bɛ, “Bě bo Israɛl kɛ sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́yámbɨ bɛ́gháti Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm. Kɛ tɛ̌ndu bǎbyàk yɔ́, nɛ bǎyɨ́ŋɨ mmʉɛt ayɛka bɛ́ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ kwáy bo abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛ́nti, sɛ́rɔ̀ yɛ be nɛ sɛ́rɔ̀ŋ ntá bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl nɛ yɔ.
Mɛ mmǔ Kristo nchí rɛm chi tɛtɛp, mpú sénse. Ntɨ̌ ɛna nkwɔ́ nɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ nchí rɛm chi tɛtɛp, nɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ árɛ̀m chi ɛnyumɔt.
Ɛ́yɔ kɛ ɛ́kʉ́ bo Israɛl bákɛ́m mɛ amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm, nɛ báré yaŋ bɛ́wáy mɛ.
Arɛ́, are kɛm ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ bo Israɛl bɛsí bo mankɛm. Adɛbhɛ nɔkɔ bɔ amɨk ndu ɛpʉ́ítí ɛyɔ nɛ are sɔt mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm bɛtɔŋ kpoŋoroŋ bɛ Yesu kɛ achí Mpɛmɛ anɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò.
Nɛ bǎtɔ̀ŋ kpoŋoroŋ bɛ́ Kristo kɛ ásɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛkáti ɛnɛ ató bhɛsɛ nɛ yɔ́. Abhɨ́kɨ́ sɨŋ yɔ nɛ ɛnɔkɛ́kati. Asɨŋ yɔ chi nɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm mmu áchyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m. Abhɨ́kɨ́ sɨŋ yɔ ndǔ bɛ́gbáká batay. Asɨŋ yɔ chi amɛm batɨ̌ bakwǎŋwaŋ.
Bɛrɨ̌ndu Yesu Acha mɛ́mbák nɛ bhe.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ arɛm bɛ, “Nchí ghati bhe bɛ, ɛwak ɛnɛ Mandɛm átàŋ bǒ mmɨk, chɔŋ angɔ́ ntínso nɛ bǒ ɛtɔk Sódom ɛncha bǒ ɛtɔk ɛyɔ.” 
Baghɔrɛ́ abhɛn bághátí nyaka bǒnto Yesu mbok yɔ chi María anɛ áfú ɛtɔk Mágdala, nɛ Joana, nɛ María nnɔ Jems, nɛ baghɔrɛ́ báchák abhɛn báchi nyaka nɛ bhɔ.
Kɛ báchyɛ́ ngɔrɛ́ wu bɛbhap bɛpay ɛbhɛ́n nnɛ́m ɛbhɔkɔ bɛ yi ándé, ámbʉ́ɛ́ nnya mbʉ́mbʉ andɔk amɛm baso, ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛne yi ndǔ mamiɛ́ arat nɛ ɛbhɔk ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ nnya mbʉ́mbʉ apu kway bɛkʉ yi yɛ̌nyɨŋ.
Mandɛm ǎchyɛ chɔŋ yi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛyǎ bɛcha ɛbhɛn yi anɛmɛ fá amɨk. Nɛ chɔŋ ambɔ́ŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti ndǔ mmɨk nkɔ.” 
Mbák mmu anɨ́ŋɨ́ wɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́, chyɛ̌ yi yɔ. Nɛ mbák mmu atwɔ ntá yɛ bɛ ɔ́mpúɔ yi ɛnyɨŋ ɔ́kɛ́ nisi bɛkʉ nɔ.” 
Mǔnti batɛmɛ́ nɛnu wu arɛm ntá Pɔ̌l bɛ, “Nchɔ́ŋtí bɛyǎ nkáp kɛ báchyɛ́ mɛ bɛtaŋ mbɔ mmu Rom”, Pɔ̌l akɛmɛ yí bɛ, “Kɛ mɛ Pɔ̌l nchí mmu Rom tɛ nɛbhě ɛna.”
Nywɔp nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt bo Israɛl nɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, María mmɔ̌ ɛtɔk Mágdala afa nɛ nɛyǐnywɔp arɔk ndǔ nnɛm Yesu. Aghɔ́ bɛ́ mǎnáŋ bábɨ́ŋɨ́rí ntay ɛnɛn nɛchi anyǔ nnɛm báfɛrɛ.
Yɛ̌ chí mpok anɛ batɨ yɛsɛ́ átàŋ bhɛsɛ bɛ sɛ́chí bǒ bɛbʉ́, sɛ́pú bhɔŋ bɛcháy bɛsí Mandɛm mbɔnyunɛ nkaysi Mandɛm achá anɛ achi amɛm batɨ yɛsɛ nɛ yímbɔŋ arɨ́ŋɨ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ.
arɔk ntá Páílet bɛ anchyɛ bɛtaŋ amfɛrɛ ɛrɛnɛ Yesu ndǔ ɛkotákátí. Páílet achyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ́ mámfɛ́rɛ́ Yesu ndǔ ɛkotákátí manchyɛ yi.
Nɨk nɔkɔ ka mmʉɛt bɛ ngátí bho yɔ mbɔ ɛnyǔ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ, ɛnyu ɛnɛ bághòk mánjwimɛm.
Acha akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Mmǔ bɛtok anɛ achi tɛtɛp nɛ ndɨŋɨndak chí anɛ? Chí anɛ chi-bɛtɨk ywi áchyɛ́ yi bɛtaŋ bɛ anjɨŋɨ nɔkɔ batɨ̌ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk abhɛn bachi amɛm ɛfo yi, anchyɛ nɔkɔ bhɔ awap ákɔrɛ nɛnyíɛ́ ndǔ mpok.
Bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu arɛmɛ, bápɔ́p! Bɔ́ kɛbhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ́mɛ́, ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ yi ankwɛn anyu bɛ bɔ mánkɛ́m yi bɛsí bho. Bárɔp kpákpǎkpak. 
Ghɔ́ yɛ bɛ́ ɔfɛ́rɛ́ ntí ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛsak báfyɛ̀ ngoŋo arɛ́. Kʉ ntɨ bɛ́bhak chak bɛsí Mandɛm, nɛ ndu bɛbhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Yesu, nɛ bɛkɔŋ bo báchák. Kʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn, ɔ́mbak sayri nɛ bo abhɛn bábhɨ̀ŋɨ nnyɛ́n Ɛta nɛ batɨ pɛ́pɛ́p bɛ́ ánkwak bhɔ.
Yɛ̌ nɔ, bǎpú ka bɛ́twɔ ntá ya bɛ mǎmbɔ́ŋ nɛpɛ́m.
Nɛ tɛ̌ndu sɛ́chí bɔ Mandɛm, chɔŋ sɛ́mbɔŋ áfɔ́k anɛ yi ábhʉ́rɛ́ ntá bɔ̌bhi, nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm ábhʉ̀rɛ ntá Kristo. Mbák sɛ́nká bɛ́chɛm mmʉɛt nɛ Kristo ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛyi, chɔŋ sɛ́nchɛm nɛ yi ndǔ kɛnɛ́m ɛki. 
Bɛyǎ bho báré rɔŋ ambɨ, bachak mankoŋo nɔkɔ ansɛm. Yesu abhak nɛ́ntɨ́ ɛnap. Bɔ́ mankɛm báré bɨk mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Sɛ́mbɨ́tí Nyiɛ̌ nɛwú Mfɔ Debhít! Mandɛm ánjɛ́t mmu anɛ átwɔ̀ ndǔ nnyɛ́n Acha! Sɛ́mbɨ́tí Mandɛm mfay!”
Ɛ́kʉ́ Yesu abhɨŋɨ bhɔ mankɛm arɛm bɛ, “Bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ ntá bǒ mmɨk, bafɔ bábhɔŋ bɛyǎ bɛtaŋ amfay bǒbhap, nɛ bǒbati básɔ̀t bɛyǎ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ bǒbhap mángók bhɔ.
Sɛ́bhàka ntɨ nɛ bhe, nɛ sɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ bɛcháy mbɔnyunɛ sɛrɨŋɨ bɛ ndǔ bǎká bɛbhɔŋ ɛsɔŋɔri mbɔ bhɛsɛ, Mandɛm ǎchyɛ bhe nkwɔ nɛpɔptǐntɨ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi ákʉ̀ nɛ bhɛsɛ.
Yɛ̌ mmú ákɛ́ kʉ ntɨ bɛbʉ́ ndǔ ndaká kɛbhʉrɛ anɛ́, nɛ yɛ̌ mmu ákɛ́ nyiɛ ntɨ ɛ́bhɔ́ŋ! Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ Yesu Acha ǎkɛmɛ kɛ́mbé ntá bo abhɛn bákʉ̀ mɛnyǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɔ mɛnkɛm nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ sɛ́náŋ sɛ́gháti bhe bɛ mǎnsɔt mpok.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ árɛ́m bɛ nɛkǎy ɛnɛn nɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ, “Mbuɔt chi Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm.
Nchí ghati bhe bɛ, mbɔk yɛka báchí fá te abhɛn bápú gu kpátɛ mǎngɔ́ Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm ndu nchí twɔ fá amɨk mbɔ Mfɔ bǒ mankɛm.”
Bachyɛ mmʉɛt ndu bɛ́ghɔ́k mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǒnto Yesu bátɔ̀ŋ. Bɔ́ mankɛm abhɛn manókó babhak ndu nsoŋ amɔt ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ, ndǔ Nɛnyiɛ Acha nɛ ndu nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt. 
Ngɔ́ mpɔŋɔndɨ́k anɛ pɛ́pɛ́p nɛ mmǔ anɛ ákɔ̀ yɔ. Mmu wu abhak nɛ nkʉɛt awɔ́. Báchyɛ́ yi nta kɛfɔ. Afa arɔk ndu bɛ́pɛt mɛnu bɛsɔt awɔ́nɛm.
Nɛ́nɛ, Mandɛm ákʉ́ bo mandɨŋɨ kpoŋoroŋ ɛnyǔ mmu ákway bɛbhak chak bɛsí bhi. Ɛyɔ ɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛkʉ nɛ ɛbhé yɛ̌ndu bɛbhé Moses nɛ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ mɛnáŋ báté ntísiɛ ɛnyǔ Mandɛm ákʉ̀ bo mámbák chak.
Mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ntíánwɔ́p ɛ̌ti Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ mbɔnyunɛ yɔ achi bɛtaŋ Mandɛm ndǔ bɛpɛmɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ánókó yɔ bɛbho nɛ bo Israɛl, nɛ bɛghaka ntá abhɛn bapu bo Israɛl nkwɔ.
Mbák ndu sɛ́yaŋ bɛbhak chak bɛsí Mandɛm kɛ sɛ́bhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Kristo, kɛ ɛ́mfakari bɛ bɛsɛ babhɔŋ sɛ́kʉ̀ bɛbʉ́, nɔ Kristo ǎtó bhɛsɛ ndǔ bɛbʉ́ kɛ? Wáwák!
Pɔ̌l abhɛ́p bhɔ́ bɛ, “Ntí anɛ bájwítí yɛ nyaka bhe achi bɛ yi?” Bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Chí ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Jɔ̌n ághàti bho kɛ bájwítí bhɛsɛ.”
Bǒ bhɔ bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ yɛ bɛ Yesu nɛ bakoŋo bhi, bápɛ́t bapu arɛ́, bɔ babhɔŋ báchwé amɛm bachwi yɔ, barɔk Kapɛ̌naum ndu bɛ́yaŋ Yesu.
Bɛyɨŋɨ bachiǎkap abhɛn bachi bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ Lɛ́vi, bɔ́ mankɛm abhɛn básɔt akap anɛ ndu-amɔt ntá bho, bágù mbɔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu achak. Kɛ bɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ Mɛlkísɛdɛk, mmu ásɔ́rɛ́ nyaka nkwɔ akap wu, Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛsɛ bɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛni nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.
Bě baghɔrɛ́ abhɛn bachí bakoŋo Yesu, barɨ́ŋɨ́ ná mbák ɛ̌ti ɛyɛká kɛ Mandɛm ǎkwáy bɛ́pɛ́mɛ manɛ́m abhɛka abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ noko Mandɛm? Nɛ be babhakanɛm abhɛn bachí bakoŋo Yesu, barɨ́ŋɨ́ ná bɛ́ ɛ̌ti yɛká Mandɛm ǎkwáy bɛ́pɛ́mɛ baghɔrɛ́ bhɛka abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ noko Mandɛm? 
Bɔ̌ma, ɛ́kɛ́ bhak yɛ ɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ntá yɛka mbák bǒ mmɨk bápàp bhe.
Yesu arɛm barak anɛ mpok yi áchí amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí ɛnɛ ɛtɔk Kapɛ̌naum átɔ̀ŋ bo. 
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Nkʉ ɛrɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛ́mɔt manyu áchok bhe.
Tɛtɛp, sɛchi anyǔ nɛwú mpoknkɛm ɛ̌ti Yesu, nɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ̀ Mandɛm ántɔ́ŋ ɛnyǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn mbɔŋ Yesu Acha nɛ́kʉ̀ bɛtɨk ndǔ mmʉɛt ɛyɛsɛ́ ɛnɛ ɛ́pú tat fá amɨk.
Ángɛl anɛ ájwí manwi afe ayi mmbá nɛ ɛbhɔ́kɔ́ mmok ɛ́mɔt ndu bɛrat, ɛrɔp chi pyɔɔ. Ɛbhɔ́kɔ́ ntaŋ ɛ́mɔt ndǔ bɛrat ɛrɔp chi pyɔɔ. Ndǔ amɔt ndǔ barǔ mambe arat árɔ́p chi pyɔɔɔ. Ɛbhɔ́kɔ́ nywɔp ɛ́mɔt ndǔ bɛrat ɛ́rɔp chi pyɔɔ. Ɛ́bhak ɛnyumɔt nɛ ɛbhɔ́kɔ́ bɛti ɛ́mɔt.
Nɛ bǎkɛ́ bhɨŋɨ ntɨ mǔnkwɔ bɛ, ‘Ɛta mbɔnyunɛ bǎbhɔŋ chí chi amɔt, yí mmú áchí amfay.’
Yesu arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Fú, twɔ́ fá ambɨ.”
Mpok ákwáy nɔkɔ, bo bachɛm nɛfí ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm. Báre nɨkmʉɛt ɛnɛ́ Sakaría achi amɛm ásɔ̀ŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛrɨ́tí ɛriɛp ɛyɔ.
Mbák mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ nɛpɛ́m mbɔ mbaŋ bɛ́fé nɛ nɛkɨ́ŋ bɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ chyɛ ɛrɨ́tí ɛyɔŋ, ná mmu ákway bɛrɨŋɨ nɛkwáy ɛnɛn báfè nɛ mbaŋ, nɛ ɛnɛ́n bákwɛ̀t?
Yesu aghati yí bɛ, “Píta, dɨŋɨ bɛ́ nkɔk apɛrɛ́ kók bɛtǐ ɛbhɛn, chɔŋ ɔ́ndɛm ndɔŋ ɛ́rát bɛ ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mɛ.” 
Kɛ Yesu kɛfyɛ́ ntí ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bárɛ́mɛ́. Aghati yi bɛ, “Ɔ́kɛ́ cháy. Dɔ́kɔ́ rɔŋ ambɨ mɛnoko.”
Mpok Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n anɛnɛ ɛbhánɛ́ ɛnɛ ɛjwi bɛrat, ngók ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛjwi bɛrat ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Twɔ́!” Njɨŋɨ ngɔ́ mpɔŋɔndɨ́k pyɔ. Mmu anɛ ákɔ̀ yɔ abhak nɛ *ɛ́rúmɛ́ awɔ.
Nkoŋo anɛ Yesu ákɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka arɛm ntá Píta bɛ, “Chi Acha!” Píta ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ chi Yesu Acha, asɔt ndɛn ayi afyɛ́ amʉɛt, adók, akwɛn amɛm manyu. Afɛ́rɛ́ nyaka yɔ amʉɛt ndu bɛkʉ bɛtɨk.
Ndu bágháká antítɔk, bághɔ́ ndǔ bo bápɔ́kɔ́ ngú báfù ɛtɔk bɛrɔŋ bɛbhɛmɛ. Ngú wu abhak njaŋamɔ ntá máyi anɛ achí nyaka kɛ́nkwɛ́sɛ́. Tóntó bo ɛtɔk ɛyɔ báré koŋo nkɔ́kɔ́ngu.
Ɛ́chí sáyrí ntá mmu wu bɛ mánsɔt ntay nɛgho mánsɛt ɛmɨ ɛyi, mámɛsɛ yí amɛm manyu ɛcha yi bɛbhak nɛpɛ́m ankʉ mmǔ amɔt anɛ ánókó Mandɛm ankwɛn ndǔ bɛbʉ́.
Nnáŋ ngáká awu, chɔŋ nsɨŋ ɛkáti nchyɛ́ ntá bo abhɛn bǎyábhɛ́ bɛto Yerúsalɛm nɛ akap aywɛka.
Bápànyu, mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi chi ɛchɨŋti. Mánù nkwɔ bɛrwɔ bo abhɛn báyàŋ bɛfap mmʉɛt nɛ nkwɔ bho abhɛn bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bɛchi nɛ bhɔ. Mánù mɛ́ŋɔ́kɔ́ti bhɔ bɛ́ mánkʉ nɔ́kɔ́ bɛpɔ̌ barak ɛ́pusi anɛ mmʉɛt ɛyap ɛ́ŋwaka bɛ bɔ mánkʉ mbɔ ɛnyǔ bɔ́ babhɔŋ bákʉ̀.
Mbák mǎnkʉ́ nɔ, pú kɛ́rɨ́ŋámík nɔ bǎtɔ̀ŋ nɛ́ntɨ ɛnɛká? Ɛ́rɨ nɔ? Nɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ́ nkaysi yɛká abhɨ́kɨ́ rɨ.
Bo abhɛn bachi atú ɛtɔk ɛyɔ bárɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ Yesu achi arɛ. Bátó ɛyɔŋ mbǎnkɛm bɛkʉ bo mántwɔ́ ntá yi nɛ bǒmame.
Bǒ abhɛn bati apay bábhɔŋ bɛtaŋ bɛkɛm manyiɛp bɛ akɛ kwɛn ndǔ manywɔp ankɛm anɛ bɔ bághàti bǒ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm afyɛ́ bhɔ antɨ. Babhɔŋ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ manyiɛp andɔp chi manoŋ. Nɛ bábhɔŋ bɛtaŋ bɛchyɛ bǒ mmɨk mɛnyǔ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm.
Bafɔ bhɔ mankɛm bati byo báká ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt bɛchyɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhap nɛ kɛfɔ ɛkap ntá yi.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ akwɛnɛ ndǔ ntay ɛnɛn, ǎsìɛpti ndǔ mbɨŋ, nɛ mmu anɛ ntay ɛnɛn nɛ́kwɛ́nɛ́ yi amʉɛt, nɛ́chɔ̀kɔti yi.” 
Tímɔti mmu ákʉ̀ bɛtɨk Kristo nɛ mɛ ǎtò be bakak. Batɨ̌ bo Israɛl bha, Lusiɔs nɛ Jáson nɛ Sɔsipatɛ bátò nkwɔ be bakak.
Bɛyɨŋɨ bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛn sɛ́ghɔ́ nɛ́nɛ, bɛ́pú yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛnɛ mmu ákway bɛyɛnti nɛ kɛnɛ́m ɛkɛn Mandɛm ákʉ chɔŋ sɛ́mbɔ́ŋ.
Mpok anɛ bo Israɛl mányìɛ̀ ɛpǎ Brɛt anɛ kɛbhɔŋ yís arɔp kɛkwɔt. Bábhɨŋɨ ɛpǎ yɔ bɛ, *Nɛkɨŋɨ.
Nkúbhɛ́ bɛti ɛbhɔ, asɔt bhɔ́ tɛ́mté aso bɛfʉɛt ɛbhap. Pɔ̌l nɛ Sáilas bájwiti yi nɛ ɛfo ɛyi ɛnkɛm.
Bǒ Rom bádɛ́n mɛ nɛ ɛ́kpa kɛnɔŋ ndɔŋ ɛ́rát. Bo bátɛ́mti mɛ nɛ batay ndu bɛway ndɔŋ amɔt. Achwi abɛt anyɛ́n nɛ mɛ ndɔŋ ɛ́rát. Achwi árákáti amɛm manyu ɛkʉ ngɔ́kɔ́nyɛn ndǔ bɛti mɛ́mɔt nɛ nywɔp nɛ́mɔt.
Yesu arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Bǎbhɨkɨ jwimɛm ndǔ nɛkay ɛnɛn, chɔŋ mǎnjwimɛm chí ndǔ bakay anɛ́fu?
Bɛtɨk bɛchak ɛbhɛn yi áchyɛ́ mɛ chi bɛ nkʉ́ bǒ mankɛm mángɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm mmu ághókó mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ábhʉ́rɛ́ nyaka bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ ndǔ mpoknkɛm anɛ áfʉɛ́rɛ́ ansɛm.
“Mpok yɔ kɛ bábhé Moses. Arɨ́ tontó nɛ Mandɛm akɔŋ yi. Máne yí ɛkɛt ɛtayi ndǔ bataŋ árát.
Bɔtá, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka ámbɔ́ŋ yɛ́ nɛtaŋántɨ. Mbɔ̌ŋ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm, nɛ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ chɔŋ ɛ́mbak mbɔnyǔ yí árɛ́mɛ́.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Sɔt ká mpok bɛ yɛ̌ mmu ywɛka ákɛ́ kʉ bɛrɨ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áyàŋ yi ankʉ bɛsi bho ndu bɛtɔŋ mmʉɛt. Mbák mmu ankʉ nɔ, apú bhɔŋ nsáy anɛ Ɛtayɛka Mandɛm mfay áchyɛ̀.
Kɛ́m ká mɛnyɨŋɨ́ nɛnu mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áchyɛ̀, bɛ́ mǎnkwáy mɛnu nɛ Satan, mǎnte kpirí mpok yi áyàŋ bɛrwɔ bhe.
Ɛ̌ti yɔ, Mandɛm ǎto ɛtati ɛ́njwi bɔ antɨ ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ bárɔbhɛ noko chi baraká nsé.
Amɨ́k Mandɛm Acha áchí amʉɛt bo abhɛn bachi chak, nɛ yi ǎghòk yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt ɛnap, kɛ ǎtɨknsɛm ntá bo abhɛn bákʉ̀ bɛbʉ́.”
Kʉ ká yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ bɛ yɛ̌ mmu ákɛ́ rɔ bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm mɛmfʉɛt yi. Kʉ ka yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ bɛ yɛ̌ mmu ákɛ́ nɛn mbɔ kɛ́ngɔ́-bɛchi. Mɛnyǔ bo bhɔ bátwɔ̀ nɛ ɛsɔŋɔri mánchɔŋti bapɛ́m bɛyǎ bho.
Yɛ̌ nɔ, mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ɛsáyrí ɛnyɨŋ bɛsɨŋ ntá Mfɔ Rom ɛ̌ti yi. Ɛ̌tiyɔ kɛ ntwɔ́ nɛ yí bɛsí ɛbhɛka, nɛ sayri sayri, bɛsí ɛbhɛ, Mfɔ Agripa! Ntwɔ nɛ yi bɛ sɛ́njɨ́ŋɨ́ nyé ɛni ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ nchí kway bɛbhɔŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ́sɨ̀ŋ.
Bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Kwáé, wɔ mmu bábhé ndǔ bɛbʉ́, ɔ́yàŋ bɛtɔŋ bhɛsɛ?” Bapuri yí bátɛ́n nɛfí bɛ ámfú ɛkɛt nɛnɨkímʉɛt ɛyap. 
Nɛ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Mandɛm árɛ́mɛ́ bɛ mmu abhɔŋ bɛ́gu ndɔŋ amɔt, nɛ ánáŋ ángú, andɔbhɛ noŋ chi manyé,
Nɛrɔ anɛ Yesu árɔ̀ nɛbhʉɛt wu, batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm nɛ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi babho bɛchiti yi nɛ bɛbhɛ́p, mányɔŋti nɔkɔ yi bɛkʉ yi ankwɛn anyu.
Ntɨkɨ nsáy mmu ábhɔ́ŋ mbák abhɔŋ mmɨk nkɛm kɛ anɛ́m nɛpɛ́m ɛni? Yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛ́pú.
Ghatí bhɔ́ bákɛ́pɛrɛ chɔŋti mpok yap ndǔ bɛrɔ́rí mbok ɛ̌ti bachǐmbɨ bhap. Bɛrɔ́rí mbok ɛbhɔ bɛ́pú kwak bo mánkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm áyaŋ bɔ́ mánkʉ. Mmu ǎkway bɛ́koŋo nkaysi Mandɛm chí mbák abhɔŋ nɛka nɛ yi.
Píta ate nɛfí ndǔ nyǔ-ɛbhá. Ɛ́kʉ́ nkoŋo achák wu, anɛ mǔngo bachiǎkap árɨ́ŋɨ́ apɛtnsɛm nɛfí, arɛm kɛpɨ nɛ ngɔsɔ́ŋ anɛ áchí anyǔbhá. Asɔt yɛ Píta áchwé amɛm nɛ yi.
Kɛ yɛ̌ndu sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ mandɛm nsé abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ nɛpɛ́m, mbɔk bho báchí ndǔ nkwɔ́ ywɛsɛ́ abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ nɔ. Mpok mányìɛ̀ nɛnyíɛ́ mandɛm nsé, ɛ́bhàk amɛm batɨ yap chí mbɔ bɛ bɔmandɛm nsé chí bɔmándɛ́m abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛpɛ́m tɛtɛp. Nɛ ndǔ bábhɨ́kɨ́ re sɛnɛ ndǔ mbi Mandɛm, bákàysi bɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́ mandɛm nsé nɛ́chɔŋti bɔ́ bɛsí Mandɛm.
Kɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛpɛt ɛrɛm ndɔŋ anɛ ájwi ɛpay bɛ, ‘Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm akʉ bɛ ɛmbak pɛ́pɛ́p, yɛ̌ mmu ákɛ́ rɛm bɛ ɛpu pɛ́pɛ́p.’
ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛyɔ ɛ́rɔ̀ŋ yɛ, ɛ́nsɔt bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ́chák tándrámɔt ɛbhɛn bɛ́bɛ́bhɛ́ bɛcha yɔ. Bɔ́ mɛnkɛm mɛndɔk mɛnchwe mmu wu amʉɛt mɛ́mbak nɛ yi, nté yi ambɛp ancha anɛ mbɨ.” 
Bák yɛ́ ka pě! Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mbɔ̌ŋ mpok anɛ chi ɛkɛt ápɛ̀tnsɛm. Kɛ chí beku-a, kɛ nɛ nɛ́ntɨ bɛti-a, kɛ manɛ́mnkɔk-a, kɛ chi nɛyǐnywɔp-a, yɛ̌ mmu abhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ.
Kɛ́nkwɛ́sɛ́ anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ mmu anɛ ákwàk yi ǎrɔ nɛpɛ́m ɛni nɛnkɛm ntá Mandɛm nɛ ǎnɨ̀kmʉɛt bɛti nɛ ngósí bɛ́ Mandɛm ánkwak yi.
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, Yesu arɛm yɛ bɛ, “Kɛfɔ Mandɛm kɛ́chí mbɔ yi? Chɔŋ njɛnti kɔ nɛ yí?
Bɔ́ bárɛ́m bɛ, “Sɛ́pɛ́t sɛ́yàŋ batísiɛ́ mántwɔ́ mándɛ́m ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ákʉ́ ndaká yí? Bɛsɛ́ babhɔŋ sɛ́ghok nɛ batú ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fú yi anyu.”
Nchí ghati bhe mɛnyɨŋ mbɔ mmu anɛ árɛ̀m ɛnyɨŋ ntá bɔ́bhi. Nɛnɛ́ ká batɨ ntá yɛsɛ, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ sɛ́kɔ́ŋ bhe.
Nsay akɛ́m yi, are yáŋ ɛnyɨŋ mɛ́nyiɛ́ mpok anɛ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛbhʉɛt angó, aghɔ́ kɛnɔ́ amɨ́k ántífú.
Abhɔ́ŋ ɛkwak mɛnyiɛ yɛ̌ chi bɛchɔkɔti ɛbhɛn bɛ́kwɛ̀nti amɨk mpok mǔnkáp anyiɛ nɛnyiɛ. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛchak abhak bɛ mmú mǔnkáp ɛ́ré rɔŋ ɛ́nɨŋɨ nɔkɔ bɛfʉɛt ɛbhi.
Akparɛnja anɛ ácháp arɛ fú yi anyu. Akparɛnja wǔ kɛ yi ásɔt anu nɛ bǒ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛtɔk ansɔt awɔ́nɛm. Chɔŋ yi ankɛ́m kɛfɔ amfǎy yap nɛ mɔ́nɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ anɛ baghoko nɛ ɛsé awɔ́. Chɔŋ anjati bhɔ́ amɨk mbɔ báyàt kɛpɛmɛ́ grep amɛm nɛyarɛ́ grep ndu bɛtɔŋ bɛ Mandɛm Bɛtaŋ Mɛnkɛm aběntɨ tontó.
“‘Mfay, bɔ́ŋ maŋák. Bǒ Mandɛm nɛ bǒnto nɛ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ, bɔ́ŋ ká maŋák mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm achɔ́ŋtí Bábilɔn ɛ̌ti bɛbɛ́pti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ́ bhe.’”
Mbák mǎmfyɛ́ amɨ́k ntá anɛ áchí mǔnkáp mǎndɛm bɛ, “Ɛta twɔ́ chɔkɔ́ fá”, kɛ ntá nchɛ́bhɛ́ mmu mǎndɛm chí bɛ, “Tě awu. Mbák ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ te awu, twɔ́ sɛbhɛrí fá”.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́káysí ɛ̌ti barak anɛ, dɔ̌ yɔ ɛ́njɨ́ŋɨ́ chí wɔ nɛ Mandɛm. Ɛ́rɨ ɛcha ntá mmu anɛ árɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ákʉ̀ ɛchi chak, nɛ ntɨ ɛni nɛpu sɔŋɔri yi amɛm ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛyɔ.
Ngɔrɛ́ amɔt abhak atú ɛtɔk wu anɛ apu mmu Israɛl, kɛ abhak mmu Kánǎn. Arɔk ntá Yesu, ambɨk nɔkɔ bɛ, “Acha, mmɔ̌ Mfɔ Debhít, ghɔ́ mɛ́ ntínso! Ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri mɔ́wa tontó.”
Bɛsɛ́ mankɛm abhɛn sɛ́chí nyaka amɛm áchwí sɛ́bhák bo bɛsa byó nɛ bɛ́rát nsɛm nɛkú nɛ amɔt.()
Yesu abhɛ́p chimɔ bɛ, “Ɛfóŋó ɛnɛ ɛ́naŋ ɛtat yi amʉɛt ná?” Chi mɔ́wu akɛmɛ bɛ, “Tɛ kɛmbɔ́ ɛki.
Sɔt ká mpok bɛ bǎkɛ byak mmǔ anɛ ághàti bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn. Bo Israɛl báchòk nyaka batú ntá mmu anɛ áyɛ̀p bhɔ batú fá amɨk. Mbák bɔ́ bápú kway nyaka bɛ́bʉɛ bɛ bákɛ́ chwe ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri, nɔ chɔŋ ɛntaŋ mbɔŋ ɛncha bɛ sɛ́mbʉ́ɛ mbák sɛ́byàk mmu anɛ achi amfay, nɛ áyɛ̀p bhɛsɛ batú?
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Ntɔ̌ŋ be bɛyǎ bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nkʉ́ ndǔ nnyɛ́n Ɛtaya. Ndu mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm, ɛnɛ́ ɛ́kʉ́ bǎyaŋ bɛway mɛ nɛ batay chí ɛnɛ́?”
Nká yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛ̌ti bǒ abhɛn Mandɛm ayabhɛ bɛ mámbak abhi. Nká ɛsɔŋɔri bɛ́ Yesu Kristo ámpɛ́mɛ́ bhɔ nkwɔ mámbák nɛ Mandɛm mmú áchyɛ bhɔ kɛnókó ngwɛnti ti.
Mandɛm kɛ̌ ághókó tákɔ nɛ bɛrɨ ɛbhi, tákɔ anɛ ákway bɛbhak ɛchɔŋ, mbúrɛ́ angwɔsi, mámfyɛ́ ango. Bǎkáysí bɛ́ be kɛ̌ Mandɛm apu kwáy bɛ́kwák mǎmbɔ́ŋ ndɛn bɛ́fyɛ́ amʉɛt kɛ? Nɛka ɛnɛká nɛ Mandɛm nɛ́gʉ́psi nɛcha!
bǎkɛ́ gwɔt batɨ amɛm mbɔnyu bachǐmbɨ bhɛka bágwɔ́rɛ́ nyaka batɨ yap nɛ Mandɛm mpok bághàp amɛm baso. Bátáŋntɨ nɛ mɛ nɛ, mamɔ mɛ.
Manywɔp yɔ apay áfʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, arɛm ntá bakoŋo bhi bɛ, “Sɛ́mpɛ́tnsɛm atú Judɛ́ya.”
Bɔ̌ma, tɛ̌ndu bǎbhɔŋɔ nɛka nɛ Yesu Kristo Acha ywɛsɛ mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ kɛnókó kɛnkɛm, bǎkɛ́ chyɛ kɛnókó ntá bo abhɛn bǎghɔ́ bɛ́ báchí sayri, mǎmbyak abhɛn ɛyap ɛ́pú.
Nɛ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ɛ́tàka atú Masidónia nɛ atú Akáiya ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎkʉ́, kɛ ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ may nɔ. Mbok nɛka ɛnɛka nɛ Mandɛm akɔ mbankɛm, ɛnyu ɛnɛ sɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛrɛm ndu bɛtɔŋ ɛnyǔ mǎnoko.
Nkáysí bɛ mǎnaŋ bǎghok ɛ̌ti bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áchyɛ́ mɛ ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhi bɛ nkʉ ndǔ bɛkwak bhe.
Sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ mɛ́mɔ́ Acha mbɔ ɛnyǔ mbɔk ɛyap bákʉ̀ nyaka, ɛ́kʉ́ Mandɛm ató nnyɔ́, nɛ nnyɔ́ ɛre waytí bɔ́.
Kɛ mbák sɛ́kɔ̀ ndǔ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyu yímbɔŋ áchɨ́ Bɛdiɛrɛ sɛ́bhɔŋ nɛchɛmɛ́mʉɛt nɛ batɨ. Nɛ manoŋ Mɔ́ywi Yesu anso bhɛsɛ amfɛrɛ ndǔ bɛbʉ́ mɛnkɛm.
“Kɛnókó kɛ́mbák nɛ Mandɛm amfay; kpák ambak fá amɨk nɛ bo abhɛn bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhi bɛchi nɛ bhɔ!”
Akwɛsɛ mbɛ́ntí amɔt arɛ́. Báre pɔ̀kɔ yi yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ yi árɔ̀ŋ. Abhak ɛnyu yɔ ndu mamiɛ́ ánɛ̀n. Aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Aénias.
‑ Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎpày ndǔ bɛkáti ɛbhɛsɛ chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi bhɛsɛ antɨ, sɛbhɨkɨ bhɛsɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Yɛ̌ bǎbhɨkɨ jwimɛm nɛ́nɛ bɛyɨŋɨ ɛnyǔ bo sɛchi, nókó ká bɛ chɔŋ mǎnjwimɛm sayri ɛwak ɛ́mɔt, bɛ nywɔp Yesu Acha átwɔ̀, mǎnkwáy bɛdɛp awɔ antɨ ɛ̌ti yɛsɛ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ bɛsɛ́ sɛ́dɛ̀p mburɛ awɔ antɨ ɛ̌ti yɛka.
Yɛ̌ nɔ́, Yesu achɔkɔ kpák, akɛrɛm yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm apɛt abhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Wɔ kɛ ɔ́chí Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò, wɔ kɛ ɔ́chí Mmɔ Mandɛm Mmu sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛbɨti?”
Yesu akɛmɛ bɛ, “Bě batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm, chɔŋ ɛmbɛp ntá yɛka nkwɔ ɛncha! Nti achi bɛ mǎnyìɛ̀rɛ bo mámpɔ́kɔ́ mɛnwɔ́ptí batu anɛ́ be babhɔŋ bǎpú kwak bo mámbʉ́rɛ́ bɛbhé bhɔ yɛ̌ mandú.
Syɛ ka abhɛ́nɛ́fú fɛrɛ́ ndǔ ngó Satan, mǎmpɛmɛ bhɔ. Ghɔ́ ká bachak ntínso, kɛ mǎnsɔ́t mpok bɛ bɔ bákɛ́ charɛ bhe nɛ bɛbʉ́ bhap. Pap ka yɛ̌ chi ndɛn ɛyap ɛnɛ́ mánɔ́ nɛ bɛpɔ̌ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn máŋwaka, mánkʉ nɔkɔ. 
Bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ Mandɛm apɛ́mɛ́ bhe. Bɛrɨŋɨ nɔ ǎbhák ndǔ nkaysi ayɛka mbɔ kɛndɛ́n anɛ ntɛmɛ́ nɛnu ákùti ntí ywi nɛ yɔ. Sɔt ka nkwɔ́ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ɛnɛ́ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ áchyɛ́ bhe mbɔ akparɛnja nsɛm ɛpay anɛ ntɛmɛ́ nɛnu.
Ɛ̌ti yɔ, Mandɛm akósí yí áchyɛ́ yí bɛtaŋ amfǎy mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm, achyɛ yi nnyɛ́n kɛnókó ɛnɛ́n nɛ́chá manyɛ́n ankɛm.
Mmʉɛ́t mmǔ wu are kɔt ŋwaŋwǎŋwaŋ mbɔ batay anɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ jáspa nɛ kanɛ́lian.   Mbaŋátámfoŋ átée ághabhɛri ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ ɛyɔ ánkɔt nɔkɔ mbɔ ntay ɛ́meral.
Yesu akɛmɛ bɛ, “Mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ. Mɛ̌chyɛ̀ Ɛtaya kɛnókó, kɛ bǎchɔŋti nnyɛ́n ɛna.
Nchí ghati bhe nɛ ntɨ ɛna nɛnkɛm bɛ mǎnɨ́k nɔ́kɔ́ mmʉɛt ɛ̌ti ya bɛ Mandɛm ankwak mɛ mpɛt ntwɔ ntá yɛka mandú mpok.
Akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Nnáŋ ngáti bhe, kɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ noko, ndaká yí bǎpɛt bǎbhɛ̀p mɛ? Bě nkwɔ́ báyàŋ bɛbhak bakoŋo bhi?”
Chɔŋ ɔ́mpɔkɔ mɛniɛ, ɔ́mbe mɔ́mbakanɛm, nɛ ɔbhɔŋ bɛbhɨŋɨ yí bɛ Yesu.
Bǎkɔŋ yi yɛ̌ndu bǎbhɨkɨ re ghɔ yi. Mǎnoko yi yɛ̌ndu bápú ghɔ́ yi nɛ́nɛ, nɛ bábhɔ̀ŋ maŋák amɛn ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ njɛnti nɛ amɛn mmu apú kwáy bɛrɛm ɛnyu mɔ achi.
Bárɔŋ nɔkɔ ntá Yesu bárɛm bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ ɔchí mmu tɛtɛp, nɛ ɔpú tɔŋ kɛ́rɨ́ŋámík. Sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ ɔpú yɨŋɨ mmu ndǔ bɛsí ɔ́ncháy yi, kɛ ɔ̌tɔ̀ŋ tɛtɛp ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áyàŋ bo mánkʉ. Ghatí bhɛsɛ, ɛbhé yɛsɛ ɛ́ka bɛ sɛ́nchíɛ nkábhɛ́nti ntá Mfɔ Rom kɛ ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ ka?”
Mánɛ́nɛ yɛ ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chí amfay. Ngɔ́ ɛkʉbhɛ́ nku amɛm. Myamyaŋ áre kɔt. Nɛbu nɛ́re rɛmti, nɛfaŋ ansay nɔkɔ. Nɛnyɨkɨsǐ mmɨk nɛgho nɛ́kwɛ́n. Amaŋá nɛbu áré kwɛnti tontó.
Kɛ Tímɔti anáŋ áfǔ awu apɛtnsɛm fá, nɛ ɛrɨ́tí ntó bɛ bǎtaŋ ndǔ nɛsɨkɨ́ntɨ ɛnɛka nɛ Kristo nɛ ndǔ ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ batɨ. Nɛ aghátí bhɛsɛ bɛ bǎkàysi bhɛsɛ nɛ maŋák mpoknkɛm nɛ bǎbhɔŋ ɛkwak bɛghɔ bhɛsɛ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛkwak bɛghɔ bhe.
Mpok anɛ sɛ́kòŋo nyaka mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bakwǎŋwaŋ báyàŋ sɛnkʉ, ɛbhé ɛ́kú sɛ́ré ŋwaka bɛkʉ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ nɛ mmʉɛt ɛyɛsɛ bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ mɛntwɔ bhɛsɛ nɛ nɛwú.
Bárɔ́ŋɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ntá yi nɛ mɔ́wu, Yesu ásáy ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ yɔ, bɛ́ ɛ́ndɔ́ yi. Ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ́rɔ́ yi, ataŋ tɛ́mté.
Nchí bhak ndǔ nɛtarɛ́nsay ndɔŋ ɛ́páy ndu sɔ́nde amɔt. Nɛ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbha mɛnkɛm nchí chyɛ ndu amɔt amfay baru byo mbɔ akap ntá yɛ.’
Ndǔ tɛtɛp Kristo achi nɛ mɛ, nchí rɛm bɛ yɛ̌ mmu apú kway bɛkʉ mɛ mbɔt bɛdɛp awɔ antɨ ndǔ atú Akáiya ankɛm.
Nɛchwe yí áchwé Yerúsalɛm, ɛtɔk ɛnkɛm ɛ́nyɨ́kɨ́si tɨkɨ̌tɨk. Bo bábhó bɛbhɛp batɨ bɛ, “Anɛ mmu átwɔ̀ chi agha?”
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Kɛfɔ̌ bakáp nɛ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ mmɨk kɛ́kway bɛ́twɔ nɛ bɛbɛ́pti mɛnyɨŋ kɛ nchí ghati bhe bɛ, mǎnsɔ́t kɔ mǎnkʉ bo mámbák mamʉɛrɛ bhɛka bɛ́ mpok kɛ́máy, Mandɛm ánsɔt bhe ndǔ bɛchɔ́kɔ́ bhi ɛbhɛn bɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.
Yesu árɛ́mɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, asɛmti yɛ bakoŋo bhi bati byo nɛ apay bɛ bákɛ́ kʉ yɛ̌ mmu andɨŋɨ bɛ yi chí Mpɛmɛ anɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò. 
Nɛchyɛ anɛ yi áchyɛ́ mmʉɛt mbɔ akap ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ ákʉ́ yi ate nɛntɨ Mandɛm nɛ nkwǎ ndǔ Nku Nkɔ ndu bɛkʉ bɛ bo abhɛn Mandɛm abhɨŋɨ, mámbɔ́ŋ bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi afyɛ́ bariɛp bɛchyɛ bhɔ, tɛ̌ndu nɛwú nɛ́fɛ́rɛ́ bho ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛn Nku Nsɨ́.
Bágháká nɔ́kɔ́ arɛ́ bárɛm bɛ, “Bǒbhɛn chí bo Israɛl nɛ báchyɛ̀ ɛsɔŋɔri amɛm ɛtɔk ɛyɛsɛ́.
Mpok yɔ, Jɔ̌n Njwiti abhak ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ. Ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò ákʉ̀, ató mbɔk bakoŋo bhi bɛ mándɔ́k mámbɛ́p Yesu bɛ,
Ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt nɛ́chák, Yesu achwe amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí bo Israɛl antɔŋ nɔkɔ bo Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́. Mmǔ amɔt abhak arɛ́ anɛ awɔ́nɛm aywi ágú.
Nnɔ Yesu nɛ bɔ̌mayi bátwɔ́ bátee nɛfí, báto ɛyɔŋ bɛ mámbɨ́ŋɨ́ yi.
Mǔngo Ɛtǒpia wu akɛmɛ bɛ, “Mɛ̌kwáy bɛjwimɛm ná ɛnɛ́ yɛ̌ mmu ábhɨ́kɨ́ nɛ́nɛ angati mɛ?” Abhɨŋɨ yɛ Fílip ánkó ánchɔ́kɔ́ nɛ yí amɛm ɛ́kárɨ́k.
Bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ bɛyǎ bo bárɔ̀ŋ ntá Yesu bábho yɛ bɛrɛm nɛ batɨ bɛ, “Sɛ́wày chí mmʉɛt. Yɨ́ŋɨ́, mmɨk nkɛm arɔbhɛ koŋo chi yi.”
Kɛ bǎghàti bho bɛ mbák mmu ándɛ́m ntá ɛtayi, yɛ̌ máyi bɛ, ‘Nsɔt ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ mbʉ bɛkwak wɔ nɛ yɔ, nchyɛ́ ntá Mandɛm’,
Tɛ́mchok bǒ bati apay bábhési bare rɛm kɛpɨ nɛ Yesu. Babhak Moses nɛ Ɛláija.
Bo abhɛn báchi Ɛ́fɛsɔs mankɛm, bo Israɛl nɛ abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ndak anɛ́ áfákárí, bɛcháy bɛ́kɛ́m bɔ́ bábhó bɛchyɛ nnyɛ́n Yesu Acha kɛnókó.
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ nkɔŋ be nɛ mpabhamɨ́k anɛ Mandɛm. Nsɔt be mbɔ ngɔsɔ́ŋ anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mbakanɛn nɛ nnáŋ mfyɛ́ bariɛp nɛ mmǔ amɔt anɛ ábháy bhe. Mmǔ wu chi Kristo.
Ntí apu anɛ mɛ̌sɨŋ be ɛ̌ti nɛkwak ɛnɛn bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛchyɛ nkwɔ Kristo abhɛn Yerúsalɛm.
Ɛnɛ́ sɛ́náŋ sɛ́chí arɛ ndu mpǎy manywɔp, ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm amɔt anɛ aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Ágábɔs afú atú Judɛ́ya atwɔ arɛ́.
Ató anɛfu anɛ akʉ́ batí arat. Yí wu, bákɛ́m báwáy. Arɔk ambɨ bɛ́tó bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk abhɛnɛfu. Bákʉ ɛnyumɔt nɛ bhɔ́. Bádɛn mbɔk, báwáy abhɛnɛfu.
Mbák sɛ́chí nɛpɛ́m, chi bɛ sɛ́nchíɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó. Nɛ mbák sɛ́gù, sɛ́gù chi bɛ sɛ́nchíɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó. Ndǔ ɛchi nɔ, yɛ sɛ́chí chí nɛpɛ́m, yɛ sɛ́gù gu, sɛ́chí chí awɔ Mandɛm.
“Bǎkɛ́ kaysi bɛ ntwɔ fá amɨk chi bɛkʉ bo mámbák ndu kpák nɛ batɨ. Ǎe. Ntwɔ chi bɛ bo mánú nɛ batɨ.
Ɛnyǔ mmu wu chí mmu ɛpʉ́ítí mpoknkɛm nɛ bho báchák. Batɨ̌ mɛnyǔ bo bhɔ ábɛp amɛm nɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ rɨŋɨ mbɔ̌ŋ ndaká Mandɛm. Bákaysi bɛ bɛ́kʉ mbɔ ɛnyu Mandɛm áyàŋ chí mbi bɛyaŋ nkáp.
Bě nkwɔ́ bǎbhɔŋ yɛ bɛbhak pě mpoknkɛm, mbɔnyunɛ, Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm, nchí twɔ́ chí mpok anɛ yɛ̌ mmu apu kway bɛkaysi bɛ mɛ̌twɔ.” 
Nɛ́nɛ, nchí ŋák, mbɔnyunɛ mbákántɨ nɛ bhe ndu yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbi.
Sɔ̌l afate amɨk, anɛnɛ amɨ́k, kɛ yi kɛkwáy bɛghɔ mbaŋ. Bákɛ́m yi ndu awɔ, baya barɔk ɛtɔk Damáskɔs.
Fɛstɔs ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ Pɔ̌l árɛ́mɛ́, abhɨŋɨ bataŋá manyé abhi bárɛ́m kɛpɨ. Aghati yɛ Pɔ̌l bɛ, “Ɔrɛm bɛ́ nyé ɛnɛ nɛ́ndɔ́k ntá Mfɔ Rom, nɛ chɔŋ ɔ́ndɔk ntá Mfɔ Rom.” 
Akʉ yɛ bárɔ́k ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ, bafɛrɛ ntí Jɔ̌n Njwiti,
Asɔt yɛ amokó mmɛm, áchyɛ nɔ́kɔ́ bakak ntá Mandɛm, abho bɛchyɛ ntá yap, andɛm nɔkɔ bɛ, “Sɔt ka nyu, bě mankɛm.
Páílet arɛm yɛ ntá yi bɛ, “Ɔpú kɛmɛ mɛ yɛ̌ ɛyɔŋ? Ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛ mbɔ̌ŋ bɛtaŋ bɛrɛm bɛ mándɔ́ wɔ mándɔ, nɛ mbák ndɛ́m bɛ mángó wɔ́ ndǔ ɛkotákátí, bágò?”
Ɛwak Mandɛm átàŋ bǒ mmɨk, mfɔ ngɔrɛ́ anɛ áchí nyaka ɛtɔk Shɛ́ba ǎfate andɛm bɛ be bo mkpáká mmɨk anɛ ɛchɔŋ bǎkʉ́ bɛbʉ́ mbɔnyunɛ yi afu nyaka nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ arɔk bɛghok mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mfɔ Sólomon átɔ̀ŋ bho nɛ bɛyǎ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak. Nɛ nchí ghati bhe bɛ mmu achi fá nɛ́ntɨ́ ɛnɛka anɛ acha Sólomon, Yɛ̌ nɔ́, bǎpú ka bɛghok yi.
Nɔ́ kɛ ɛ́chí nɛ bɛrɨ ɛbhɛn mmu ákʉ̀. Bɛ́ghɔ̀ kpoŋoroŋ. Kɛ yɛ̌ chí ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́chí bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́, bɛ́pú rɔp bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ mpoknkɛm.
Yesu aghati baghɔkɔ́ bhi bɛ, “Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ mǎnɨkmʉɛt, dɛm ka bɛ́: ‘Ɛta, kʉ bo mánchyɛ́ nnyɛ́n ɛnɛ kɛnókó. Kʉ bo mándɔ́ wɔ ɔmbak Mfɔ wap.
‑ Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ mmǔ ywɛka ánɨ̀kmʉɛt, ámfóŋórí yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ákʉ́ yi bɛbʉ́. Mbák bǎkʉ̀ nɔ, chɔŋ Ɛtayɛka Mmu achi amfay ámfoŋori be nkwɔ́.” 
Nɛ mpok yɔ, chɔŋ bɛyǎ bakoŋo bha mánkɛmɛ mmʉɛt ansɛm, mánti nɔkɔ batɨ ntá bǒbati ɛtɔk, nɛ mámpabhɛ nɔkɔ batɨ.
Bǎrɨŋɨ nkwɔ bɛ mpok sɛ́chí nɛ bhe sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ sɔt sɛ́rwɔrɛ́nyu bɛkʉ mǎmbɔ́ŋ maŋák. Nɛ mbɔŋ Mandɛm achi ntísiɛ bɛ sɛ́pú ghati nyaka bhe Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ chí nɛ nkaysi bɛbhɔŋ nsáy anɛ áfù ntá yɛka.
Báchák báfáte yɛ básé nsé amʉɛt Yesu bɛ,
Kɛ mbák wɔ Tímɔti, ɔ́kɛ́ rɔ bɛ́kóŋo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bátɔ́ŋɔ́ wɔ nɛ ɔnoko bhɔ́ sayri. Ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ bo abhɛn bátɔ̀ŋ wɔ bhɔ.
Mɔ́ywi arɔp nyaka kɛkwɔt bɛgu. Nɛ ndiɛrɛ mɔ́wu kɛ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka. Abhak mɔ́ngɔsɔ́ŋ anɛ achí mamiɛ́ byo nɛ apay. Ndu Yesu árɔ̀ŋ arɛ́ bɛyǎ bo bákáp yi bɛbhe bɛpay.
Dɛmɛ́triyɔs abhɨŋɨ bhɔ báchɛ́m nɛbhʉɛt amɔt, arɛm bɛ, “Bɔtá, bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ́ kɛnɛ́m ɛkɛsɛ́ kɛnkɛm kɛ́fù chí ndǔ awɔ́-bɛtɨk anɛ.
Tɛ́mté wu, Hɛ́rɔd ató mbabhɛri ywi amɔt nɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ́ ándɔk ántwɔ nɛ ntí Jɔ̌n. Arɔk, afɛrɛ ntí ywi amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ,
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ rɨ bɛkʉ nɔ! Sɛ́noko bɛ́ Mandɛm ǎpɛ̀mɛ bhɛsɛ́ chí ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhɛn Yesu Acha átɔ́ŋɔ́ bhɛsɛ́ nɛ nkúbhɛ́ ɛnyu yɔ kɛ ǎpɛ̀mɛ bɔ nkwɔ.”
Bɔ̌ma, ndu bɛrɔŋ ambɨ, yɛ̌ yí yɛ̌ yi, bɔ́ŋ ká maŋák ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu Acha ákʉ́. Yɛ̌ndu nchí ghati bhe chí nkúbhɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn njámbɨ ngati bhe, ɛyɔ ɛ́pú chyɛ mɛ ɛsɔŋɔri tɛ̌ndu ɛ́kʉ̀ bɛ bǒmpap bákɛ́ bhɔŋ mbi nɛ bhe.
Mɛ Pɔ̌l, mɛ̌nɨ̀kmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm ɛ̌ti yɛka bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl. Nchí mǔkɛnɔŋ mbɔnyunɛ nchí ghati bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo ndu bɛkwak bhe.
Ɛ̌, be bho bǎtɔ̀ŋ bo bachak, ndaká yí bǎpú tɔŋ mmʉɛt ɛyɛka? Bǎghàti bo bɛ bákɛ́ ghɛ́p aghɛp, kɛ bě babhɔŋ bǎpú ghɛ́p aghɛ́bhɛ́?
Yɛ̌ antwɔ́ chí nɛ nɛ́ntɨ́ bhiti, yɛ̌ chí mpok nkɔk ɛ́kòk, kɛ antɛmɛri bhɔ pě, ɛ́rɨ ɛncha ntá bǒ bɛtok bhɔ!
María mmɔ̌ ɛtɔk Mágdala arɔk aghati bakoŋo Yesu bɛ, “Ngɔ Yesu Acha.” Nɛ aghati bhɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Yesu aghati yi. 
Nchí yáŋ yɛ́ be mǎndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ mbák Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm achí nɛ mmu, apú kway bɛ́rɛm ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo. Nɛ yɛ̌ mmu apú kway bɛ́rɛm bɛ Yesu chí Acha mbák Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ apú nɛ yi.
Yesu abhɨŋɨ mandú mɔ, akʉ yi ate bɛsí bhap.
Arɛm nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ bɛ, “Ɛrɛm ɛtɔk Bábilɔn ɛ́kwɛn buúp! Ɛ́rɔp chi bɛchɔkɔ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ. Ɛ́rɔp chi bɛchɔkɔ bɛbɛ́ptí bɛfóŋó nɛ bɛpɔ̌ kɛnɛn ɛkɛn bo babhɨkɨ kɔŋ.
Bɔ̌ma, yɛ̌ mmu akɛ yoŋ mmʉɛt. Mmu ákɛ́ yɔkɔ ntɨ, nɛ mmu akɛ yɨŋɨ ntɨ nɛ amɨ́k abʉ́abʉ.
nɛ chɔŋ mǎndɨŋɨ tɛtɛp anɛ Mandɛm, nɛ tɛtɛp wu amfɛrɛ be ndǔ kɛsɛm.”
Ɛnyɨŋ Yesu árɛ́mɛ́ ɛ́kʉ́ báré yaŋ bɛkɛm yi, kɛ yɛ̌ mmu abhɨ́kɨ́ tɔk yi awɔ amʉɛt, mbɔnyunɛ mpok ayi abhɨ́kɨ́ re kway nyaka.
Sɔt tɛtɛp kʉ bɔ́ mámbák nyáŋá. Ɛyɔŋ ɛyɛ ɛchi tɛtɛp.
Ghatí ká mɛ. Bǎrɔŋ nyaka amɛm baso bɛ́ghɔ ntɨkɨ ɛnyʉ̌ mmu? Ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ? Ɛ́chi tɛtɛp. Kɛ dɨŋɨ ka bɛ mmu anɛ bǎghɔ́ achá ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ. Bě bǎrɔ́k yɛ bɛghɔ kpɨk yi? Bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ bǎrɔ́ŋ nyaka chi bɛghɔ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ? Kɛ dɨŋɨ́ ka bɛ, Jɔ̌n acha barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ báchák.
Ndu ɛ́chí nɔ, fyɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ yɛ́ka batɨ ntɨ mǎnkwak nɔkɔ batɨ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ bǎkʉ̀ nɔ. 
Ngɔrɛ́ bɛtok wu aghó yi arɛ́, apɛt abho bɛrɛm ntá bo abhɛn báchi arɛ téé bɛ, “Mmǔnɛ achi mmǔ ywi nkwɔ.”
Kɛ mbák chí bǒnkwɔ bakoŋo Satan abhɛn bárɛ̀m bɛ́ báchí bo Israɛl ɛnɛ́ bápú kɛ básè chi nsé, chɔŋ nkʉ bɔ́ mántwɔ mántɛp mánɛ́n bɛsí ɛbhɛká nɛ nkʉ bɔ mándɨŋɨ bɛ nkɔŋ be.
Píta nɛ Jɔ̌n báyɨŋɨ yi diíí. Píta arɛm yɛ bɛ, “Yɨŋɨ́ bhɛsɛ!”
Kɛ nɛ́nɛ nchí pɛtnsɛm ntá mmu anɛ átó mɛ, Yɛ̌ nɔ, yɛ̌ mmu ywɛka abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɛp mɛ bɛ, ‘Ɔ̌rɔ̀ŋ fá?’
Nɛ mbák ayap bhɔ chi ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhi, nɔ chi bɛ, abhɨ́kɨ́ yap bhɔ ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bɔ bákʉ́. Mbɔ ayap bhɔ chi ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bákʉ́, mbʉ ɛ́pú bɛ ǎkʉ̀ bɔ bɛrɨ ndɛ́ndɛm.
Kɛ mmu anɛ ábhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Acha, ǎbhɔ́ŋ nkaysi amɔt nɛ yi.
Akɛmɛ yí bɛ, “Bǒbatí bo Israɛl báte ɛyu bɛ mángáti wɔ ɔ́nsɔt Pɔ̌l ɔnsɛp nɛ yí ndu ɛchɛmɛ́ bataŋá manyé ɛgho mburɛ mbɔ bɛ báyàŋ chí bɛ́rɨŋɨ ndaka ywi sayri.
Nɨk nɔ́kɔ́ ká mmʉɛt bɛ barak anɛ ákɛ́ fakari nɛ ɛso ndu ɛ́bè mmʉɛt bɛ́bʉɛ mpok yɔ.
Bo Israɛl, bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Sɛ́bhɔ̌ŋ ɛbhé, nɛ bɛkoŋo ɛbhé yɔ, abhɔŋ bɛ́gu mbɔnyunɛ ákʉ́ mmʉɛt yi Mmɔ Mandɛm.”
Ɛ́mbák yɛ ɛnyumɔt nɛ bhe. Mǎnáŋ mǎnkʉ bɛtɨk mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn báchyɛ́ bhe, bǎbhɔŋ bɛrɛm chi bɛ, ‘Sɛ́chí chí bǒ bɛtok, yɛ̌ ndak áchák ápú. Sɛ́kʉ́ chí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́kʉ.’” 
Ɛ́rɨ ɛcha ntá bǒ abhɛn batɨ yap áchí amɛm pɛ́pɛ́p, mbɔnyunɛ chɔŋ Mandɛm ankʉ bɔ́ mángɔ́ yi!
Átɛ́n nɔ́kɔ́ mmʉɛt ambɨ mandú, aghɔ́ Jems nɛ mɔ́mayi Jɔ̌n, bɔ̌ Sɛbɛdi. Báchí nyaka amɛm áchwí mángoko nɔkɔ bɛyǎ nkáp yap.
Ɛnyu yɔ kɛ̌ mmǔ anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ Josɛ́f akʉ nyaka. Abhak mmu nnɛrɛ́kɛt Lɛ́vi nɛ mmu ɛtɔk Sáyprɔs. Bǒnto Yesu bádú yí nnyɛ́n bɛ́ Banábas, nɔ́ chí, “Mmǔ anɛ afyɛ́ bo ntɨ.”
Bǎkʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ mbɔ ɛtayɛka.” Bágháti yi bɛ, “Mandɛm kɛ achi ɛtayɛsɛ, sɛ́pú bɔ̌-ɛnɔŋ.”
Mɛ Júd kɛ nchí sɨŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ. Nchí mǔbɛtok Yesu Kristo nɛ nchí manɔ Jems. Nchí sɨŋ ntá yɛka bo abhɛn Mandɛm mmu achi Ɛtayɛsɛ abhɨ́ŋɨ́. Yí akɔŋ be nɛ ákʉ́ bɛ Yesu ámbák Mbabhɛri ywɛka.
Bɔ́ mankɛm bághɔ nyaka yi, bɛcháy bɛ́kɛm bhɔ. Tɛ́mté wu, Yesu afyɛ́ bhɔ ntɨ arɛm bɛ, “Chi mɛ, bǎkɛ́ chay!”
Acha Mandɛm Bɛtaŋ Mɛnkɛm ǎrɛ̀m bɛ, “Mɛ kɛ Nchi kʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mbo bɛbhak nɛ Mɛ kɛ nchi kʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛntwɔ ndǔ Ngwɛnti.”   Yi achí nɛ́nɛ, achí tɛ̌ mpok mmɨk ábhɨ́kɨ́ re bho, nɛ ǎtwɔ̀ chɔ́ŋ. 
Mbɔk baghɔkɔ́ bhi báré rɛm ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ̌ ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm, mánkak nɔkɔ bɛrɨtí batay anɛ́ básɔ́rɛ́ báté yɔ́ nɛ ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bo báchyɛ́ bɛ mánsɔ́bhɛ́rí ɛkɛt ɛ́rɛ. Kɛ Yesu arɛm ntá yap bɛ,
Akɛmɛ Yesu bɛ, “Ɛta, yɛ̌ amɔt.” Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Mɛ nkwɔ́ mbɨ́kɨ́ rɛm bɛ mángwáy wɔ. Dɔ́k, kɛ ɔ́kɛ́ pɛrɛ kʉ bɛbʉ́”. 
Nɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ nchí kʉ, chɔŋ ndɔk ambɨ bɛkʉ yɔ, bɛ́ mkpɔt bɛkak bo abhɛn bárɛ̀m bɛ bákʉ̀ bɛtɨk ɛbhap nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ mɛ́kʉ̀ ɛbha.
Dɔ̌ ká yɔ ambak, mpok ánáŋ ánkwáy, chɔŋ ndɛm bǒ abhɛn báfɛ̀rɛ nchwi ɛbhɨ mánjámbɨ mamfɛrɛ nchaŋ ɛyɔ mányokoti ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt amɔt, mánsɔ́ŋ. Kɛ mǎmfɛrɛ nchwi mǎmbʉrɛ anywɔ́p.’” 
Kʉ ka yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ bɛ yɛ̌ mmu ywɛka akɛ chwe ndǔ barak ɛpúsí nɛ bɛ yɛ̌ mmu ákɛ́ bhák anɛ apu bhɔŋ mpok nɛ Mandɛm, mbɔ Isau mmu átí kɛsénsí ɛki ntá manɔ anɛ mɔ́nkwɛn ɛ̌ti nchaŋ nɛnyíɛ́ amɔt.
Dɔ̌ ká sɛ́ngɔ́ ndǔ Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò, Mfɔ bo Israɛl, áfa ndǔ ɛkotákátí ansɛp amɨk. Mbák ánsɛ́p amɨk, chɔŋ sɛ́noko bɛ́ Mandɛm kɛ átó yi.” Baghɛ́p abhɛn bati apay báre sɔkɔti Yesu nkwɔ. 
Ɛ́rɨ ɛcha ntá mmǔ-nɛ ápày nɛ ɛyɔŋ amfay bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛ́n-nɛ bɛ́rɛ̀m ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛbhɔŋɔ bɛfakari. Ɛ́rɨ ɛcha ntá bo abhɛn bátà batú bɛghok ndǔ bápày ɛkáti ɛnɛ nɛ mámbʉrɛ mɛnyɨŋ abhɛn básɨ́ŋɨ́ amɛm ɛkáti ɛnɛ mbɔnyunɛ mpok anɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛbhɔŋɔ bɛfakari arɔp chi kɛkwɔt. 
Ɛ́fákari bɛ mbǎyngɔrɛ́ anɛ bɔ mankɛm mánòŋ abhɨkɨ twɔ́ áyák. Ɛ́kʉ́ bábhó mɛmɔk kɛnɔ́, kpát bákwɛ́n kɛnɔ́.
Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛ́ mmʉɛt ɛyɛka chí ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm ɛnɛ́ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ áchɔ̀kɔ arɛ́? Mandɛm achyɛ́ bé Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ bɛ ámbák nɛ bhe, nɛ́nɛ, bǎrɔp chí bo Mandɛm. Bǎpɛt bǎpu ndǔ mmʉɛt ɛyɛka.
Bɔ, ghók nɔ́kɔ́ ka bachi nɛ manɔ bhɛka ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bághàti be mǎnkʉ, mbɔnyunɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́chyɛ̀ Yesu Acha maŋák.
Mandɛm apɛt arɛm ntá Mɔ́ywi bɛ, “Wɔ, Acha, kɛ ɔ́ghókó mmɨk ndǔ nɛbhǒnɛt. Nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi amfay, chí awɔ-bɛtɨk aywɛ.
Yesu anáŋ arɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛti yi. Ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ yi árɛ́mɛ́ bɛ, “Puyɛ̌ be mankɛm kɛ bǎchí pɛ́pɛ́p.”
Mbák mmu abhɔŋ ntɨ bɛ́chyɛ akap, Mandɛm ǎsɔt ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi áchyɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ amɔ́ yi átɔ̀ŋ. Apú bhɛp mmu ánchyɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ.
Kɛ tɛ̌ndu sɛ́chí chí bǒ ngósí, sɛ́nkɛ́m mmʉɛt. Sɛ́ndɔ́k ambɨ mɛ́nóko Yesu nɛ bɛ́bhɔŋ ɛkɔŋ nɛ bo, bɛ ɛyɔ ɛmbák mbɔ kɛndɛ́n anɛ ntɛmɛ́ nɛnu ákɛ́mɛ́ bɛchyɛt mmʉɛt. Sɛ́mbáká ntɨ bɛ chɔŋ Yesu ampɛmɛ bhɛsɛ, nɛ bɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́mbák ntá yɛsɛ́ mbɔ ntá ntɛmɛ́ nɛnu anɛ ákuti ntí ywi.
Nɛ mmu anɛ árɛ̀m ɛnyɨŋ, anjɨkɨ ambɨŋɨ nnyɛ́n ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm, abhɔŋ bɛrɨŋɨ bɛ, ayɨ́kɨ́ nɔ́ nkwɔ chi ndǔ nnyɛ́n Mandɛm mmu achi amɛm ɛkɛrákap,
Ngɔ́ yɛ bɔángɛl tándrámɔt abhɛn bachi bɛsí Mandɛm. Báchyɛ́ bhɔ mbá tándrámɔt.
Bárɛ́m nɔ ndu mɛmɔ yi bɛ mámbɔ́ŋ mbi bɛbhat ndak yi amʉɛt. Yesu atɛp ntí amɨk, ansɨŋɨ nɔkɔ ɛnyɨŋ amɨk nɛ sɛnɔŋ awɔ.
Bakoŋo Yesu bhɔ bápɛtnsɛm ndǔ bɛkɛt ɛbhap. 
Bɔ̌ma, mɛ̌yaŋ mǎndɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ kɛka mǎnkaysi bɛ bǎbhɔŋ bɛyǎ kɛboŋ. Ɛchi bɛ bo Israɛl abhɛn bágwɔ́rɛ́ nyaka batɨ yap bápú gwɔt chɔŋ yɔ mpoknkɛm. Ɛ́bhak chɔŋ chi kpatɛ bɛghaka mpok anɛ mpǎy bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl, abhɛn Mandɛm áyábhɛ́, mánoko.
Kɛ ɛkɛrákap ɛnɛ́ Yesu árɛ́mɛ́ ɛ́bhak chi mmʉɛt yi.
Nɛ́nɛ, ɛnɛ́ mǎnáŋ bafɛ́rɛ́ bɛbʉ́ antɨ ndǔ bǎkòŋo tɛtɛp Mandɛm, bɔ́ŋ ká ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ́ tɛtɛp nɛ batɨ. Kɔŋ ka batɨ nɛ batɨ yɛka ankɛm.
Yesu abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Bǎbhɔŋ bɛkpɔkɔ́ brɛt afɔ mɛni?” Bákɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Sɛ́bhɔŋ bɛkpɔk tándrámɔt.”
Yesu abhɨŋɨ bakoŋo bhi arɛm bɛ, “Nchí ghati bhe bɛ, akap kɛ́nkwɛ́sɛ́-nɛ ácha anɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu.
Bɔ̌ma, sɔt ka mpok bɛ ndǔ nkwɔ ywɛka, yɛ̌ mmu ákɛ́ bhak anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛbɛ́ptí ntɨ, nɛ akɛka bɛ́sɨ́kɨ ntɨ nɛ Mandɛm, ɛ́nyu ɛnɛ́ yi arɔ mbi Mandɛm mmu achí nɛpɛ́m.
Nɛ́nɛ, bǎkwáy bɛchɛm mmʉɛt nɛ mɛ ndu mɛnu nkúbhɛ́ nɛnu ɛnɛn mɛ̌nù nyaka ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo, nɛ bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ mbʉɛ́t ndǔ nɛnu ɛnɛn fá amɛm ɛkɛt ɛnɛ́ nchí arɛ́ mbɔ mǔkɛnɔŋ.
Bǒbati apay, mbák ɛpu nɔ, batí arat, mándɛm mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm aghati bhɔ, bachak mánde chak mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ bárɛ̀m.
Yesu aghati Píta bɛ, “Nchí ghati wɔ bɛ, nkɔk apɛrɛ́ kok nkúbhɛ́ bɛti ɛbhɛn, chɔŋ ɔ́ndɛm ndɔŋ ɛ́rát bɛ ɔbhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ mɛ.”
Bǒ abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ fá amɨk bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ nyaka yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛ̌ti nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak Mandɛm ɛnɛn. Mbɔ bárɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka ɛ̌ti nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak Mandɛm ɛnɛn mbʉ́ bábhɨ́kɨ́ gó Acha ywɛsɛ mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ kɛnókó kɛnkɛm ndǔ ɛkotákátí.
Bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, mmʉɛt agú bhɔ́ tontó, bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Agha ákwày yɛ bɛbhɔŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛ́n nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛ́nti?”
Yesu aghɔ́ bɛ bo báyàŋ bɛ́kɛm yi nɛ bɛtaŋ bɛ mánkʉ yi Mfɔ, afa, akó njiɛ, abhak arɛ́ aywǐnti. 
Nɛ bǎkóŋo ɛkakánɛkɔ ɛyɛsɛ nɛ ɛkakánɛkɔ Yesu Kristo Acha. Yɛ̌ndu bǎghɔ̀ nyaka bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri, bǎsíɛ́pti Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm nɛ maŋák amɛn Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ áchyɛ̀.
Bɛsɛ́ kɛ sɛ́chí bo Mandɛm tɛtɛp, yɛ̌ndu bábhɨ́kɨ́ syɛp bhɛsɛ. Sɛ́chí bo Mandɛm mbɔnyunɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ kɛ ákwàk bhɛsɛ sɛ́nɨ́kmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm. Sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ fyɛ nti ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mmǔ mmɨk ághɔ́kɔ́ mmʉɛt arɛ́ mbɔ ɛpɨŋ bɛsyɛp babhakanɛm. Sɛ́pànyu chi ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ Yesu Kristo ákʉ́ ndu bɛ́pɛ́mɛ bhɛsɛ.
Bǎsap nyaka nɛkɔ nɛ Mandɛm, kɛ nɛ́nɛ, Mandɛm abhat be nɛ Yesu Kristo, ákʉ mǎmbák kɛkwɔt nɛ yi bɛfʉɛt ndǔ manoŋ Kristo amɛn árɔ́ŋɔ́ amɨk.
Mɛnɔk kɛfɔ ɛsǎ nsɛm mɛnwi bɛ́káp ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ ɛyɔ. Bǒbatí ɛsa nsɛm anwi báchɔ́kɔ ndǔ mɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap abhak nɛ nkú pɛ́pɛ́p amʉɛt, nɛ ntǎ-kɛfɔ anti anɛ bághókó nɛ pú.
Bǒ Mandɛm báchák mankɛm abhɛn báchí fá Rom nɛ mɛ, sayri sayri, abhɛn báchi bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk ntá mfɔ-ngo anɛ Rom, bátó nkwɔ bhe bakak.
Asɔt mandú mmɔ́ ate nɛ́ntɨ́ nap, apɔkɔ yɛ yí amʉɛt, arɛm ntá yap bɛ,
Mandɛm arɛm bɛ, ‘Wɔ Bɛ́tlɛhɛm ndǔ mmɨk Júda, puyɛ̌ wɔ kɛ ɔ́chí ansɛm ndǔ bɛtɔk Júda mɛnkɛm, mbɔnyunɛ ntá yɛ kɛ̌ Mfɔ áfù. Mfɔ anɛ ákɛ̀m bǒbha, bo Israɛl, mbɔ ɛrɨ́tɨ́ mbabhɛri bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n ákɛ̀m bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n yi.’”
Manyu áchók bǒ abhɛn bachi arɛ ndǔ bághɔ́ bɛ́ babhók bábho bɛrɛm kɛpɨ, nɛ bɛ bǒ abhɛn bachi bhʉrɛ báfàte kpɛrɛp, nɛ bakɛm bábho bɛkɔ, nɛ manɛ́mámík babho bɛghɔ mbaŋ. Bábhó bɛbɨti Mandɛm, Mmu bo Israɛl báchyɛ̀ kɛnókó. 
Babhɛrí nɔ́kɔ́ ká bǒnkwɔ abhɛn Mandɛm afyɛ́ amɔ́ yɛka mbɔ mmu anɛ ábhàbhɛri nkwɔ́ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n. Kʉ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ká mbɔ bo abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ntɨ bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm áyàŋ mankʉ. Ɛ́kɛ́ bhak chi mbɔ bɛ mányiɛrɛ bhe nyirɛ. Kʉ nɔ́kɔ́ ká nɔ nɛ ntɨ nɛnkɛm kɛfyɛ́ ngoŋo ndǔ bɛbhɔŋ nsáy.
Ndǔ ɛchi nɔ, mbák yɛ̌ mmu angati bhe bɛ, ‘Yɨŋɨ́ ka Kristo awu amɛm baso’, bǎkɛ́ noko mǎmfá bɛrɔŋ arɛ. Yɛ̌ mmu andɛm chi bɛ, ‘Yɨŋɨ́ ká Kristo fá amɛm mɔ́kɛt’ bǎkɛ́ noko ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ̀m.
Bǎchí batísiɛ́ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm nɛ bǎbhɔŋ bɛ́gháti bo bachak bɔ mɛnkɛm.
Chɔŋ mɛnyǔ bo mɛnkɛm mámpap bhe ɛ̌ti bǎchí bakoŋo bha. Kɛ mmu anɛ átè kákátí tɛ ndǔ ngwɛnti, Mandɛm ǎpɛmɛ yi.” 
mǎnɨk nɔkɔ mmʉɛt mpoknkɛm.
Mmu anɛ ányù chi amɨ, ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ɛka ndu bɛrɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi chak bɛsí Mandɛm mbɔnyunɛ achí mmɔ́.
Ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu ákʉ́ kɛ Mandɛm áyábhɛ́ mɛ bɛ mbak mǔnto, bɛ́ ngátí nɔ́kɔ́ bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo nɛ bɛ ntɔŋ nɔkɔ bǒ bɛtɔk mɛnkɛm bɛ́ mánókó mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi tɛtɛp. Nchí rɛm chi tɛtɛp, mpú sénse.
Tɛ́mté wu, Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm akʉ yí arɔk amɛm baso.
Kɛ mbɛbhɛ́ nkabhɛ́nti ate nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ. Ntí, yi kɛ yoŋ amfay, nɛ adɛp awɔ́ antɨ arɛm bɛ, ‘Ɛta Mandɛm, nchí mmǔ bɛbʉ́. Ghɔ́ mɛ ntínso!’
Mbák mǎmfóŋórí mmu bɛbʉ́ ɛbhi, Mandɛm nkwɔ ǎfoŋori yi. Mbák bǎbhɨkɨ foŋori bɛbʉ́ mmu, bɛ́rɔ̀p yi anti.” 
Mandɛm abhɨ́kɨ́ to Mɔ̌ywi fá amɨk bɛ ántwɔ́ ántáŋ bǒ mmɨk andɛm bɛ babhɔŋ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́. Atǒ yí chi bɛ́ ámfʉɛ́t ntá yi, ampɛmɛ bǒ mmɨk.
Cháá! Mmu Mandɛm ánkʉ́ manyé nɛ ntɨ, bɛ́ bo Mandɛm mándɔk mánte bɛsí bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ noko Yesu Kristo mántáŋ bɔ́?
Nɛ mbák nywɔp nɛ́njí nɛbu nɛ́ngiri, bǎrɛm bɛ, ‘Chɔŋ nywɔp nɛ́mbɛ́p tontó.’ Bǎrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ nɛbu mǎndɛm mbák manyiɛp ǎkwɛn chɔŋ, nɛ mbák apu kwɛn. Kɛ bǎghɔ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fàkari ɛchɔŋ, be kɛrɨŋɨ ntí anɛ bɔ bɛ́fàkari.
Bɛsɛ bho sɛ́sɛ́nɛ́ ndǔ nɛka ɛnɛsɛ, sɛ́bhɔŋ bɛkwak nɔkɔ bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́re sɛnɛ ndǔ nɛka ɛnap nɛ Mandɛm. Sɛ́kɛ́ kʉ nɔkɔ chi ndiɛrɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chyɛ mmʉɛt ɛyɛsɛ maŋák.
Pɔ̌l arɛm bɛ, “Bɔtá nɛ bɔmá, Tá ká batú mǎngok ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛrɛm ndu bɛ́táŋa mmʉɛt bɛsí ɛbhɛka.”
“Ɛwak ɛ́mɔt ndu nchí nɨkmʉɛt awu ɛtɔk Jopa, ngɔ́ kɛnɔ́ amɨ́k antífú. Ngɔ́ ndu ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́fú amfay ɛ́sɛ̀p. Ɛbhak mbɔ ntěndɛn nɛgho ɛnɛn bákɛ́mɛ́ bati yi anwi básɛ̀bhɛ amɨk. Ɛgháká nɔ́kɔ́ kɛkwɔ́t nɛ mɛ ɛ́te.
Nɛ Yesu aghati yi bɛ, “Mmǔfu anak nyaka ɛrɛm ɛpa, abhɨŋɨ bɛyǎ bho.
Bǒbhɛn bábhɨkɨ kwáy nyaka mɛ́nóko, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyu Aisáya apɛt árɛ́mɛ́ nyaka bɛ
Ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́ Yesu afǔ atú Judɛ́ya átwɔ̀ Gálili, arɔk are nɨk yi mmʉɛt bɛ ándɔ́k Kapɛ̌naum ámbú mɔ́ywi. Mɔ́wu arɔp nyaka chi kɛ́kwɔ́t bɛ́gu.
Sɛ́ŋák, sɛ́ŋák tontó, sɛ́nchyɛ yi kɛnókó mbɔnyunɛ mpok nɛbhay Mɔ́nkwɔmɛn akway, nɛ ngɔrɛ́ ywi anáŋ atóŋtí mmʉɛt.
Ɛkʉ yɛ chi nɛ nnɔ bárɛm chi bɛ, “Ápú mandú mmɔ́. Bɛ́p ká yímbɔŋ angati bhe.”
Yesu apɛt nɔkɔ nsɛm ɛbhě manyu ɛchak, bǒ abhɛn mánòŋ yi, basyɛpti yi.
Yesu arɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bɔ bakaysi. Ɛ́kʉ asɔt mandú mmɔ́, ate nɛpakámʉɛt ɛni.
Bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ mɛnkɛm chi bɛbʉ́. Kɛ bɛbʉ́ bɛchi ɛbhɛn bɛpu twɔ nɛ nɛwú.
Nɔ bǎrwɔ chí mmʉɛt mbɔnyunɛ mbák mmu ǎghok Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm kɛ yi kɛbháká kʉ ndiɛrɛ yɔ́ ɛ́ghàti yí, ǎbhák chí mbɔ mmu anɛ ásɔ́rɛ́ mpok bɛ́yɨŋɨ mmʉɛt ndu ɛ́kírísú angɔ́ bɛsí ɛbhi mbɔ ɛnyu bɛ́chí.
Ɛfóŋó ɛya ɛ́ŋàk ɛ̌ti Mandɛm Mpɛmɛ wa.
Chɔŋ ɛrɛm ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ yi achi arɛ́ ɛ́nkʉ bɔ́ mámbɔ́ŋ bɛcháy bɛ ɛ́kway bɛfakari nɛ bhɔ ɛnyu ɛyɔ, mánte nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ, mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ bɛ, ‘Ɛrɛm ɛ́tɔk Bábilɔn, ɛ́bɛp ntá yɛ ɛ́cha! Ndǔ mandú mpok Mandɛm atɛ́msí wɔ́ ndak yɛ ámay!’
Yi bɛ ‘Chɔŋ sɛ́njáŋ yi, kɛ sɛpu ghɔ, nɛ bɛ́ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ yi árɔ̀ŋ, sɛ́pú kway bɛrɔŋ arɛ. Nɔ́ bɛ yi?’” 
Tɛ̌ndu mbɨ́kɨ́ ghaka mbɔ yɛ̌ mmu Mandɛm achak, yi atɔŋ mɛ bɛrɨ̌ndu, áchyɛ́ mɛ bɛtɨk bɛghati bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl áfɔ́k anɛ áfù ntá Kristo. Áfɔ́k wu áya ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ mmu apu kway bɛjwimɛm ndǔ wu ankɛm achi.
Yesu afú yɛ, arɔk nɛ ntá kɛfɔ nsěnse yɔ antí, nɛ nkú chú yɔ amʉɛt. Páílet arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Yɨ́ŋɨ́ mmǔ ywɛka nɔ!”
Apɛt arɛm bɛ, “Mpú pɛrɛ tɨk chɔŋ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhap nɛ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ bákʉ̀ wáwák!”
Are tɔ́ŋ andɛm nɔkɔ bɛ, “Ɛ́rɨ ɛcha ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ághɔ́ bɛ bɛsí Mandɛm, yi apu yɛ̌nyɨŋ, mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm achi Mfɔ ywi!
Ndu mpok yɔ, Mfɔ Hɛ́rɔd abho bɛ́chyɛ nɛnyok ntá mbɔk bǒnkwɔ.
Ɛnɛ́ Pɔ̌l ánòŋ Tímɔti nɛ Sáilas ɛtɔk Atɛns, ntɨ nɛ́ré sɔŋɔri yi amɛm bɛghɔ bɛ́ ɛtɔk ɛ́jwí nɛ bɛbhó njɔ ɛnɛ bo básɔt mbɔ bɔmandɛm.
Tó yɛ bo Jopa bɛ mandɔ́k mámbɨ́ŋɨ́ mmu anɛ ákà nnyɛ́n bɛ́ Símun anɛ nnyɛ́n ɛni nɛchak nɛchi bɛ Píta.
Yí achi nyaka Mmɔ Mandɛm tɛtɛp, yɛ̌ nɔ, aghɔ́k bɛghok Mandɛm ndǔ bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛn yi ághɔ̀.
Mɛ, nnu sayri. Njɛt, nkóŋó barak Mandɛm tɛ ndǔ ngwɛntí nkɛ kɛmɛ mmʉɛt ansɛm.
Yi ǎtwɔ̀ mɛ ansɛm. Mbɨ́kɨ́ kway mmu anɛ nchí kaŋari nkwɔbhɛ́nya bɛkak ɛbhi.”
Baghɔrɛ bhɔ bárɔ́ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ nnɛm nɛchi ntiɛ́t ntiɛt. Bɛcháy bɛ́kɛ́m bɔ, kɛ maŋák nkwɔ ajwi bhɔ antɨ. Bájɛt barɔk bɛ́yáŋ bakoŋo Yesu bɛ mángátí bhɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ángɛl Mandɛm ághátí bhɔ.
Nɛ ɛ̌ti yap, nchyɛ́ mmʉɛt ntá yɛ bɛbhak nyáŋá bɛ́ bɔ́ nkwɔ́ mankway bɛbhak nyáŋá tɛtɛp.
Mǔngo batɛmɛ́ nɛnu akɛ́m yí ndu awɔ́ aya bárɔk ansɛm, abhɛ́p yí ansɛm ansɛm bɛ, “Ntɨkɨ ndak ɔ́yàŋ bɛghati mɛ?”
Bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Ɛta, sɛ́yàŋ ɔ́nkʉ́ amɨ́k yɛsɛ ánɛ́nɛ́.”
Bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ɛwat ɛyɔ, bárɔk ntiɛ́t ntiɛt bɛ́ghɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fàkari. Bábhak maknkay bɛghók ndǔ bakoŋo Yesu bárɛ̀m bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk nyáŋá nyáŋá ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap ághòk ndu ɛyi ɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bárɛ̀m.
Ngók yɛ́ ɛwat ɛnɛ ngɛ́mtáy bho ɛnɛ ɛchi mbɔ ɛwarɛ́ tutunyɛ́n nɛ mbɔ nɛfaŋ anɛ ásày. Bǒbhɔ báre bɨk bɛ, “Haleluya! Mandɛm Acha Bɛtaŋ Mɛnkɛm aywɛsɛ achi Mfɔ bǒ mankɛm.
Ndu Mandɛm ákʉ́ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ, nchí kwɛn bɛsí Mandɛm Ɛtayɛsɛ ndǔ mɛ̌nɨ̀kmʉɛt ɛ̌ti yɛka.
Yesu arɛm yɛ ntá bǒbhɔ bɛ, “Ɛbhé yɛsɛ́ ɛ́rɛm bɛ́ sɛ́nkʉ yi ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt? Chí bɛ́kʉ bɛrɨ kɛ bɛkʉ bɛbʉ́? Chí bɛ́pɛ́mɛ mmu kɛ chí bɛ́chɔŋti nɛpɛ́m ɛni?”
Bo báré rɛm bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti yi. Mbɔk mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Yí achi ɛrɨ́tí mmu.” Báchák bɛ, “Nsé, ǎrwɔ̀ bho bɛ mánɛ́m ɛbhɨ!”
Nɛchwe Yesu áchwé anywɔ́p, bágháti yí bɛ nnɔ ngɔrɛ́ Símun achí bhʉ́rɛ́ nɛ mbʉ́ɛ́p amʉɛt.
Mbɔŋɔ́nkɨ ató mmɔ̌-bɛtɨk achak. Bákɛ́m awu nkwɔ bádɛ́n báfyɛ́ yi bɛfʉɛt anti nɛ báchyɛ yi ntíánwɔ́p.
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ, ɛwak ɛnɛ Mandɛm átàŋ bǒ mankɛm, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ǎghati yí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ́ kɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛpɔ̌ ɛyɔŋ ɛ́fú yi anyu.
Nɛ mbák Kristo abhɨ́kɨ́ pɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, nɔ nɛka ɛnɛsɛ nɛchi chi ndɛ́ndɛm, nɛ nɔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛka bɛbhʉɛt be anti.
Mandɛm akʉ nɔ bɛ nɛ́nɛ, bɛfʉɛt ntá nkwɔ Kristo, ántɔ́ŋ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ nɛ bafɔ bhap nɔ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ amfay ndu nɛbhʉɛt anɛ Yesu achi Mfɔ arɛ ɛnyǔ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ákʉ̀.
Abhɔŋ yɛ bɛchyɛ nɔkɔ akap ɛ̌ti bɛbʉ́ ɛbhi yímbɔŋ, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyu áchyɛ̀ akap ɛ̌ti bɛbʉ́ bo abhɛn yi áté ndǔ ntí wap.
Abhɔŋ bɛbhak chí ngɔrɛ́ anɛ bo bárɛ̀m bɛ ǎkʉ nyaka ɛrɨ́rɨ́ mbɔ mɛ́ne bɔ̌bhi sayri, nɛ bɛtok bo Mandɛm, nɛ bɛ́kwak bo abhɛn báchí ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri. Ɛnyǔ kɛ́nkwɛ́sɛ́ wu abhɔŋ bɛbhak ngɔrɛ́ anɛ áchyɛ́ nyaka nɛpɛ́m ɛni nɛnkɛm ndu bɛ́kʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ bɛrɨ.
Ndǔ mbaŋ ábhó bɛ́kaŋari, Pɔ̌l anɨk bɔ́ mankɛm mmʉɛt bɛ mányiɛ nɛnyíɛ́. Arɛm bɛ, “Ɛchɔŋ chí manywɔp byó nɛ anwi ɛnɛ́ bǎbhɨkɨ tɔk awɔ anyu ndǔ bǎbhɔŋɔ bɛcháy antɨ.
Bákɛ́mɛ bɛ, “Acha ǎyàŋ yɔ.”
Chɔŋ mámbok bhé ndǔ bɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt ɛbhap. Mpok ǎtwɔ̀ anɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ áwày bhe, akaysi bɛ́ ǎkʉ̀ chí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm áyàŋ.
Nɛ mánchwe mánaŋa bhe nɛ bɔ̌bhɛka mankɛm, mámokoti ɛtɔk ɛnkɛm ɛnyunɛ́ yɛ̌ ntay nɛ́pú rɔp amfǎy ntɨ. Chɔŋ ɛ́mfakari nɔ, mbɔnyunɛ́ bǎbyak Mandɛm mpok yi átwɔ́ bɛ́pɛ́mɛ bhe.” 
Yesu abhɛ́p yɛ bɛyǎ bǒbhɔ bɛ, “Bǎtwɔ bɛkɛm mɛ nɛ bɔakparɛnja nɛ nkɨ́k mbɔ bɛ nchí ngɛ́bhɛ́ ntantaŋ? Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛwak, nchí chɔkɔ ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm, ntɔŋ nɔkɔ bho mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti Mandɛm, bǎrɔ nyaka kɛkɛ́m mɛ?
Ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm, ntɔŋ be bɛ sɛ́bhɔŋ bɛkʉ bɛtɨk bɛ sɛ́nkwák bo abhɛn mmʉɛt apu bhɔ, nɛ sɛ́kɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu Acha árɛ́mɛ́ bɛ, ‘Ɛ́rɨ̌ ntá mmu anɛ áchíɛ ɛcha mmu anɛ ásɔrɛ sɔt.’”
Nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́, Pɔ̌l asɔt yɛ bǒbhɔ batí anwi, bɔ́ mankɛm básó bɛsí nɛ Mandɛm. Arɔk yɛ amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm bɛkʉ bǒ batí mándɨ́ŋɨ kpoŋoroŋ nywɔp ɛnɛn nɛsǒ-bɛsí ɛnap nɛ Mandɛm nɛ́may, kɛ mánchyɛ akap ɛ̌ti yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap ndǔ nkwɔ bho bati anwi. 
Nɛ ndu sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ kwáy bɛkʉ yi anjibhiri ntɨ̌ ɛni, sɛ́rɔ, sɛ́rɛm bɛ, “Ɛ́mbák mbɔ ɛnyǔ mbɔŋ Mandɛm Acha áyàŋ.”
Ndɔk ntá ángɛl wu, ngati yi bɛ anchyɛ mɛ mɔ́kati nɛ́nɛ́p wu. Aghati mɛ bɛ́, “Sɔt yɔ́ nyíɛ́. Chɔŋ ɛ́mbak wɔ anyu mbɔ bawɛrɛ́ bɛtu, kɛ amɛm mɛnyiɛ ɛ́ndɔbhɛ nɛnɛnɛ́n!”
Ɛnɛ́ bárɛ̀m mánkɛm nɔkɔ ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ batɨ, mbɔŋ Yesu arɔk kɛkwɔt nɛ bhɔ ankɔ nɔkɔ nɛ bhɔ.
Nɛ mánɔbhɛri nɔkɔ yí ndu bɛkʉ yi ákwɛ́n ndǔ ɛyɔŋɔ́nyu.
Yesu achi nyaka kɛ́kwɔ́t ɛkʉbhɛ́ nkáp amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm anjɨŋɨ nɔkɔ ndu bo báfyɛ̀ bakáp amɛm. Aghɔ́ ndǔ bɛyǎ bǒ nkáp bátwɔ̀, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap amfyɛ nɔkɔ bɛyǎ nkáp amɛm.
“Mbák bǎkɔ̀ŋ chi bo abhɛn bakɔŋ be, bakak amɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́chyɛ bhe ǎbhák bɛ yi? Yɛ̌ chí bǒ bɛbʉ́ bákɔŋ bo abhɛn bakɔŋɔ bhɔ!
Bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chi tɛtɛp. Bɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Mbák sɛ́gu nɛ yi, chɔŋ sɛ́mbak nkwɔ nɛpɛ́m nɛ yi.
Nɛnyiɛ́ mbɔŋ nɛchi chi ntá baseansi. Bɔ́ kɛ mánáŋ bághɔ́kɔ́sí mmʉɛt nɛ bárɨŋɨ ɛwupsi ɛnɛ ɛchi ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛrɨ́ nɛ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́bhɛ́bhɛ́.
Kɛnókó ɛkɛn bɔ báchyɛ̀ mɛ kɛchi chi ndɛ́ndɛm, mbɔnyunɛ bɛbhé ɛbhɛn bakwǎŋwaŋ báfyɛ́ kɛ̌ bɔ bátɔ̀ŋ bho mbɔ bɛ bɛchi Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm.’
Yesu árɛ́mɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, abɨk bɛ, “Lásárɔs, fú twɔ́!”
Bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm bábhat Yesu bɛyǎ barak amʉɛt bɛsí Páílet.
Kɛ mmu Samária fú ǎsɛ̀p nyaka nkwɔ ndǔ mbi wu. Ágháká nɔ́kɔ́ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ mmu wu achi, aghɔ́ yi, nɛ abhɔ́ŋ ntínso nɛ yí.
Bɛfóŋó ɛbhɔ chi bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ. Bɛ́kʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay nɛ bɛ́rɔ́k ntá bafɔ̌ mmɨk mankɛm ndu bɛkʉ bɔ manchɛm nɛbhʉɛt amɔt bɛ mánu nɛ Mandɛm Bɛtaŋ Mɛnkɛm ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɛn yi átàŋ chɔŋ bo.
Kpátɛ mpok yɔ, bɔ́ bábhɨkɨ re jwi nyaka mmɛm ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ́mɛ́ bɛ́ Yesu abhɔŋ bɛpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.
Bátwɔ́ bɛghók mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi átɔ̀ŋ nɛ bɛ yi ámbu bhɔ. Nɛ bo abhɛn bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri bhɔ, bataŋ.
Mmɔ̌ Hɛródias anɛ mɔ́ngɔrɛ́ arɔk ndǔ ɛpǎ ɛyɔ, abhɛ́n nɛbhɛ́n ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ Hɛ́rɔd nɛ mankɔ̌ bhi bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛyǎ maŋák. Hɛ́rɔd arɛm ntá mɔ́ngɔsɔ́ŋ wu bɛ, “Ghatí mɛ, yɛ̌ ɔ́yàŋ yi, chɔŋ nchyɛ́ wɔ.”
Chɔŋ bǒ mmɨk mankɛm mánchyɛ yɔ kɛnókó, nɔ chi bo abhɛn bábhɨkɨ sɨŋ manyɛ́n ayap amɛm ɛkátǐ nɛpɛ́m tɛ mpok mmɨk ábhɨ́kɨ́ re bho. Ɛkáti yɔ chi ɛnɛ́ Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n mmu báwáy nyaka.
Nɛ mmu anɛ ánáká bhe antwɔ́ andɛm bɛ, ‘Faté chyɛ ɛpok ɛnɛ ntá mmǔ-nɛ.’ Mbák ɛ́mfákárí ɛnyu yɔ, ɔ̌faté nɛ bɛyǎ ntíánwɔ́p bɛ́rɔŋ bɛchɔkɔ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ yɛ̌ mandú kɛnókó.
Mbɔŋ bɛkʉ manyé nɛ ntɨ, ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ́ mǎnáŋ bǎkwɛn ndǔ mbi Mandɛm. Mmu ánká bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ ɛbhɛ́n ntɨ ákʉ́ yí, nɔ ɛ́bɛp kɛ? Mmu ányíɛ́ wɔ́ nsɛm amɔt, ɛyɔ ɛ́nkʉ yi?
Barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ abhɛn bárɛ̀m nyaka ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhɛn Mandɛm afyɛ́ bariɛp bɛtɔŋ bhe, báyàŋ nyaka, mámbɛbhɛ nɔkɔ ndu bɛ́rɨŋɨ ɛ̌ti nɛpɛ́m nɛkɔ ɛnɛn.
Moses ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, abʉɛ́ arɔk achɔkɔ ɛtɔk Mídia. Arɛ́ kɛ yi ábháy ngɔrɛ́ abhɔ́ŋ bɔ̌ babhakanɛm bati apay.
Jɔ̌n Njwiti abhésí nyaka amɛm baso angati nɔkɔ bho Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm bɛ bɔ́ mántɨ́knsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhap mánjwítí bhɔ bɛ Mandɛm amfoŋori bɛbʉ́ bhap.
Ángɛl atɔ́ŋ yɛ nnyɛ́n nɛgho ɛnɛ́n manyiɛbhɛ́ nɛpɛ́m. Nɛ́re ŋaŋari mbɔ amaŋá nɛbu. Nɛ́fú ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ Mandɛm nɛ Mɔ́nkwɔmɛn.
Mfɔ Debhít asɨŋ nyaka ɛ̌ti yi bɛ, “Nchí ghɔ nyaka Acha mpoknkɛm bɛsí bha, abhak ɛbhe awɔ́nɛm ɛya, bɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛkɛ nyɨkɨsi mɛ.
Báté nkok nɛ batay ŋaŋaŋ anɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ jáspa. Mbɔ̌ŋ ɛtɔk ɛbhak chi nɛ pú, ɛ́ŋaŋari nɔkɔ mbɔ glas.
Yesu apɛt arɔk are nɨkmʉɛt bɛ, “Ɛtaya! Mbák nkɔ́p ɛsɔŋɔri anɛ apú kway bɛfʉɛt mɛ ansɛm ntí, nká bɛ́ ɛ́mfákárí mbɔ ɛnyu ɔ́yàŋ.”
Sɛ́pú kɔ bɛghati bho ɛ̌ti mmʉɛt ayɛsɛ. Sɛ́ghàti bho chi ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo nɛ bɛ yi achi Acha. Mbák chi bhɛsɛ babhɔŋ, ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ sɛ́ghàti bhe chi bɛ sɛchi chi bǒ bɛtok bhɛka ɛ̌ti Yesu.
Dɔ̌ ká mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎghókó tɛ nɛbhǒnɛt mɛ́mbak amɛm batɨ yɛka. Mbák mǎndɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎghókó tɛ nɛbhǒnɛt mɛ́mbák amɛm batɨ ayɛka, bǎpú rɔ bɛbhak ndǔ nɛbharɛ́mʉɛt nɛ Mmɔ nɛ Ɛta.
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Ɔghɔ̌ bɛrɛm bɛkɛt ɛbhɛn? Mpok ǎtwɔ̀ anɛ ɛkɛrákap ɛnɛ ɛ́rɔ̀ŋ amɨk ɛnkɛm yɛ̌nyɨŋ kɛrɔp téé.” 
Bárɔ́k ntá Yesu bárɛm bɛ, “Jɔ̌n Njwiti ató bhɛsɛ́ bɛ sɛ́mbɛp wɔ bɛ, ‘Wɔ kɛ ɔ́chí Mpɛmɛ anɛ Jɔ̌n árɛ́mɛ́ bɛ ǎtwɔ, kɛ chi bɛ sɛ́bhɔŋ mɛnoŋ mmu achak?’”
Chɔŋ nkʉ mǎngɔ bɛrɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ kpoŋoroŋ bɛ nchí rɛm chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fú ntá Kristo. Apú kɛm be mbɔ mmǔ anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ. Ǎtɔŋ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi mpok áchí nɛntɨ ɛnɛka.
arɛm ntá bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk abhi atú Gálili ɛ̌ti Yesu bɛ, “Jɔ̌n Njwiti kɛ apɛrɛnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ̌ yí ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay.”
Táytɔs anáŋ abho bɛsɔt bakap ntá yɛka ndǔ bɛkwak bachɛ́bhɛ́bho. Ɛ́kʉ sɛ́ghátí yɛ yi bɛ ampɛtnsɛm awu ankwak be mǎndɔk ambɨ mɛnaŋa bɛtɨkɨ́ bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhɛn bǎbhó.
Báfáte tɛ́mté bápɛtnsɛm Yerúsalɛm. Bághɔ́ bǒnto Yesu bati byo nɛ amɔt nɛ bakoŋo bhi abhɛ́nɛ́fú abhɛn báchí nɛ bhɔ́ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt amɔt.
Ɛ́tárɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, áfú arɔk anyǔbhá ɛnɛ́ sɛnta. Arɛ́, mmɔ̌-bɛtɨk Mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm achák, ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ yi arɛm ntá bo abhɛn bachi arɛ́ téé bɛ, “Tánkwǎnɛ achí nyaka nkwɔ nɛ Yesu mmǔ Násárɛt wu.” Mmɔ̌ bɛtɨk anɛfú wu nkwɔ abhak chi ngɔrɛ́.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm áyàŋ mǎnkʉ chi bɛ mǎnókó mmu anɛ yi átó.”
Sɛ́ndɔ́k mbɔnyunɛ sɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ɛtɔk ɛnɛ ɛbhak mpoknkɛm fá amɨk. Sɛ́yàŋ chi ɛtɔk ɛnɛ ɛbhɔŋɔ bɛ́twɔ.
Bɛ́bhó mpok yɔ, Júdas abho bɛ́yáŋ mbi bɛkwak bɔ mánkɛ́m Yesu. 
Mpok ɛyɔ, chɔŋ bo mándɔ bɛghok tɛtɛp anɛ Mandɛm áyaŋ bo mándɨŋɨ, mándɔbhɛ fyɛ́ ntí bɛ́ghok chí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn batɔŋɔ́ nse bátɔŋ.
Ɛbyɔk ɛ́kwɛn amɛm áchá mbɔnyunɛ bɛyǎ bho bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ nyaka mbɔ̌ŋ ndak anɛ achi amɨk. Ɛbhak yɛ bɛ mbɔk bábɨ̀k mándɔkɔ nɔkɔ ɛyap ɛbhe, báchák mántaŋ mandɔkɔ nɔkɔ ɛyap.
Bǎkɛ́ nɔ́k bɛsyɛpti mankɔ, sayri mbɔnyunɛ mbɔk bho básìɛpti nyaka mankɔ nɛ ɛ́fákári bɛ básiɛ́pti bɔángɛl kɛrɨŋɨ bɛ chi bɔángɛl.
“Mbák mmu abhɔŋ ndak nɛ wɔ, antí wɔ, dɔ́k tɛmɛrí yi ayak mǎnsokori ndak wu, mǎmbak ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt. Mbák ɔ́bhɨ́kɨ́ kʉ nɔ, mpok ámfʉɛ́t, yi andɔk ntá ntaŋá manyé nɛ wɔ, afyɛ́ wɔ amɔ yi, nɛ yi anchyɛ wɔ ntá bo mbɨ̌ŋ nkú, nɛ bɔ́ mámfyɛ wɔ ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ.
Píta abhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ghatí mɛ tɛtɛp, nkáp ankɛm anɛ́ wɔ nɛ nnɛ́m aywɛ bǎtí mmɨk nɛ?” Akɛmɛ bɛ, “Ɛɛ, yɨŋɨ wu ankɛm nɔ.”
Ɛwak ɛ́mɔ́t ndǔ manywɔp ɛyɔ, bakoŋo Yesu bákɛ́m ɛchɛmɛ. Bábhák batí bɛsa bɛtandat. Arɛ, Píta afate arɛm bɛ,
Dɨŋɨ́ yɛka bɛ́, mbák mmu ákʉ́ ntɨ mmu nkwɔ bɛbʉ́, anchɔŋti ntɨ ɛni ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ re taŋ amɛm, nɔ́ ákʉ́ Kristo nkwɔ bɛbʉ́.
“Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ bǎtàt nsay ndu mɛnɨkmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm, bɛsí ɛbhɛka bɛ́kɛ́ bhak mbɔ bǒ abhɛn ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri bhɔ. Bǎkɛ́ bhak mbɔ bǒ bɛtábhá. Bágwɔt bɛsí bhap chi bɛ bo mángɔ́ bɛ bɔ bachi ndǔ nɛtarɛ́nsay. Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ, nɛghɔ́ anɛ bo bághɔ̀ bɛ bɔ bátàt nsay, chí awap akap anɛ mǎnáŋ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́.
Bɛběntɨ nkwǎ bɛ́chɛt yí mbi bɛ ákɛ́ kʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áyàŋ yí ánkʉ́.
Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ yap mɛ, mɛ kɛ njábhɛ́ bhe ntó bɛ́ mǎndɔ́k mǎnyú kɛpɛm, nɛ bɛ́ kɛpɛm ɛkɛka kɛ́mbák mpoknkɛm. Kʉ ka nɔ́ bɛ Ɛtaya ánchyɛ́ bhe yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎbhɛbhɛ yi ndǔ nnyɛ́n ɛna.
Galío árɛ́m nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, abók bhɔ́ bɛ mámfú amɛm acha manyé.
Mpok bábhɛ́mɛ́ mmu, bábhɛ̀mɛ mmʉɛt bǒ mmɨk. Mpok Mandɛm ákʉ bawú mámpɛ́tnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, mmu ǎbhɔ̀ŋ chi ɛnyǔ mmʉɛt ɛnɛ amfay. Mbák mmʉɛt bǒ mmɨk achi, nɔ mmʉɛt ɛnɛ amfay ɛbhɔŋ bɛbhak nkwɔ.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Mbák mɛ̌chyɛ̀ mmʉɛ́t ɛya kɛnókó, nɔ́ kɛnókó ɛka kɛ́pú yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Ɛtaya kɛ áchyɛ̀ mɛ kɛnókó, nɛ nkúbhɛ́ yi kɛ bǎrɛ̀m bɛ achi Mandɛm aywɛka.
Mpú rɛm nɔ chi ndu bɛtaŋ be bɛ bǎkʉ bɛbʉ́. Nnáŋ njámbɨ ngátí bhe bɛ́ sɛ́kɔŋ be nɛ batɨ yɛsɛ́ ankɛm, nɛ yɛ̌ chi nɛwú yɛ̌ chi nɛpɛ́m, yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛ́pú kɔrɛ bhɛsɛ nɛ bhe.
Tɛ́mté wu, ángɛl Mandɛm aguɛ́p yi nɛme amʉɛt mbɔnyunɛ arɔ́ bo mánchyɛ yi kɛnókó ɛkɛn babhɔŋɔ bɛchyɛ chi ntá Mandɛm. Kɛ́nyoŋo kɛ́nyíɛ́ yi, agú.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Mpú kwáy bɛkʉ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ndǔ bɛtaŋ ɛbha. Ɛnɛ́ mɛ̌kʉ̀ nchí kʉ chi ndǔ bɛtaŋ Mandɛm mmu átó mɛ. Mɛ̌tàŋ bo mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi aghati mɛ ntaŋ bo. Nɛ mɛ̌tàŋ bo chí ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ ɛchí chak, mbɔnyunɛ mpú kʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛmbɔŋ nchí yaŋ bɛkʉ. Nchí kʉ chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mmu anɛ átó mɛ áyàŋ nkʉ.
Awu áfʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, ngɔ́ ɛrɛmɛ́ ɛrɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛnɛ ɛ́bhésí amfay. Ɛ́bhak chí ngɔrɛ́ anɛ afyɛ́ mmok amʉɛt mbɔ nkú. Ntaŋ ábhák antɛn bɛkak ɛbhi, nɛ nta kɛfɔ anɛ áchí yi anti abhɔ́ŋ mambe byo nɛ apay.
Yesu arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Twɔ́ ká bhák bakoŋo bha, nɛ chɔŋ ntɔŋ be ɛnyǔ bǎkʉ bɛ́ bo bachak mámbák bakoŋo bha.”
Bo Israɛl bárɛ́m bɛ, “Cháá, báté ɛkɛt ɛnɛ ndǔ mamiɛ́ bɛsa bɛpay nsɛm atandat, ɔbhɛ́ ɔ̌kway bɛte yɔ ndǔ manywɔp ararɛ?”
Bo Israɛl bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Sɛ́pú yaŋ bɛ́wáy wɔ nɛ batay ɛ̌ti ɛrɨ́tí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́kʉ́, kɛ ɛ̌ti ɔ́rɛ̀m bɛ ɔchí Mandɛm yɛ̌ndu ɔ́chí nkwǎŋwaŋ.”
Mpok yɔ, bo abhɛn bachi chak bɛsí Mandɛm bághɔ̀ mbɔ mmok ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ Ɛtayap achi Mfɔ. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ áyàŋ bɛghok ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ̌rɛ̀m, ántá batú ángók sayri!” 
“Sɛ́nsɔ́t bɛ mmǔ ywɛka amɔt abhɔŋ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n bɛsa bɛtay. Mbák amɔt anɛm ɛbhɨ, ǎkʉ̀ yi? Pú ǎrɔ̀ anɛ́ bɛsa mɛnwi nsɛm nɛkʉ nɛ anwi, andɔk bɛyaŋ awu ámɔt kpát ambɔŋ wu?
Ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ manyé, chɔŋ bɛyǎ bho mándɛm ntá ya bɛ, ‘Acha, Acha, pú sɛ́ghàti nyaka bho Ɛyɔŋ ɛyɛ ndǔ nnyɛ́n ɛna? Pú sɛ́bòk nyaka bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ ndǔ nnyɛ́n ɛna? Nɛ sɛ́kʉ̀ nyaka mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ndǔ nnyɛ́n ɛna!’
Yɛ̌ mmu apú kʉ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ mbák ǎyàŋ bo mándɨ́ŋɨ́ yi. Tɛ̌ndu ɔ́kʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay, kʉ nɔ́kɔ́ bhɔ kpoŋoroŋ bɛ mmɨk nkɛm ángɔ́.”
Nɛ yɛ̌ mǎnɨk chí mmʉɛt bɛ́ Mandɛm ánchyɛ́ bhe ɛnyɨŋ, bǎpú bhɔ́ŋ yɔ́. Bǎpú bhɔ́ŋ yɔ́ mbɔnyunɛ bǎpú bhɛ́p nɛ nkaysi ndɨ́ndɨ́. Bǎbhɛ̀p chí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎfyɛ̀ ngoŋo arɛ́.
Mpɛt nchí rɛm bɛ, yɛ̌ mmu ákɛ́ kaysi bɛ ntí ábhɨ́kɨ́ kway mɛ amɛm. Mbák bǎkaysi nɔ, sɔt ká mɛ ɛnyu ɛnɛ bǎkway bɛghok ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mmu anɛ ntí abhɨkɨ kway yi amɛm árɛ̀m, bɛ́ mɛnkwɔ ndɛp awɔ antɨ mandú.
Símun Píta nɛ nkoŋo Yesu achák báré koŋo Yesu. Ndǔ nkoŋo Yesu achák wu achí mmǔ anɛ mǔngo bachiǎkap árɨŋɨ sayri, yí akoŋo Yesu kpát arɔk achwe amɛm sɛnta mǔngo bachiǎkap.
María anɛ ɛtɔk Magdala nɛ María nnɔ Jóses bághɔ́ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bábhʉrɛ Yesu.
ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛyɔ ɛ́rɔ̀ŋ yɛ, ɛ́nsɔt bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ́chák tándrámɔt ɛbhɛn bɛ́bɛ́bhɛ́ bɛcha yɔ. Bɔ́ mɛnkɛm mɛndɔk, mɛnchwe mmu wu amʉɛt, mɛ́mbak nɛ yi, nté yi ambɛ́p ancha anɛ mbɨ. Nɔ, kɛ̌ ɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́fákari nɛ be bo bɛbʉ́ abhɛn mkpák anɛ ɛchɔŋ.” 
Nɛ mbák sɛrɨŋɨ bɛ sɛ́nɨ̀kmʉɛt yi ángók bhɛsɛ, sɛ́bhɔŋ yɛ bɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ bɛ yi anáŋ áchyɛ́ bhɛsɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ sɛ́nɨ̀kmʉɛt bɛ yi anchyɛ bhɛsɛ.
Sará abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka ɛnyu ɛpɨŋ ɛyɔ, ambɨŋɨ nɔkɔ nnɛ́m ɛ́ywi Ábraham bɛ acha. Nɛ bǎchi bɔ̌ Sará nɛ́nɛ, mbák bǎkòŋo ɛrɨ́tí ɛpɨŋ ɛyi kɛbhɔŋ bɛcháy.
Yɛ̌ mmu apu kway bɛchwe amɛm ɛkɛt ɛnɛ mmǔ ntantaŋ angɛ́p ɛnyɨŋ, ampɔkɔ, andɔk nɛ yɔ́, mbák abhɨ́kɨ́ yambɨ ankɛm yi angwɔt.
Mɔ̌mbɨ wu abéntɨ, anisi bɛchwe anywɔ́p. Chi afú arɔk are anɨk yí mmʉɛt bɛ anchwe anywɔ́p.
Básɔ́t achwǐnyɛ́n bɛfu Atália bápɛtnsɛm Antiɔk. Amɛm ɛtɔk Antiɔk kɛ̌ bǒnto Yesu mánɨ́kɨ́mʉɛt ɛ̌ti Banábas nɛ Pɔ̌l bɛ bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm mɛ́mbák nɛ bhɔ ndǔ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn bákʉ́ kɛ bápɛtnsɛm Antiɔk.
Báyámbɨ bárɔ́k ntá Ánas, chi ngɔrɛ́ Káyfas. Káyfas abhak mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm ndu mmiɛ ɛnɔ.
Nɛka Moses nɛ Mandɛm kɛ nɛ́kʉ́ bɛ mpok yi ágó aghaka ɛsakámu akɛ ka bo mámbɨ́ŋɨ́ yi bɛ mmɔ̌ mɔ̌mfɔ Íjip anɛ ngɔrɛ́.
Yɛ̌ nɔ, ndu árɔ̀ŋ, are ghati bho mbǎnkɛm ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛfakari. Akʉ Yesu kɛpɛrɛ kwáy bɛchwe ɛtɔk kpoŋoroŋ. Arɔp chi bhɛsɛ́ bhɛsɛ́ ndǔ mbaŋ ɛnɛ bo bápú arɛ́. Yɛ̌ nɔ, bo báré fú mbǎŋ nɛ mbaŋ mándɔk nɔkɔ ntá yi.
Kɔŋ ka batɨ mbɔ bǒ nnɛrɛkɛt Mandɛm. Bɔ́ŋ ká bɛyǎ ɛkwak ndu bɛchyɛ batɨ kɛnókó.
Yesu ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ mɛnɨkmʉɛt ɛnyu ɛyɔ, afa nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi, bákɨŋɨ mɔ́nyɛn anɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ Kídrɔn. Mɔ́nkɨ áchí nyaka arɛ anɛ yí achwe amɛm nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi.
Aisáya ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm arɛm nyaka ɛ̌ti bo Israɛl bɛ, “Yɛ̌ndu bo Israɛl baya mbɔ ɛ̌siɛ́p ɛnɛ ɛchi angɔkɔ manyu, Mandɛm ǎpɛmɛ chɔŋ chi bǎru bhap.
Kɛ bɔ kɛkwáy bɛkɛmɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ́mɛ́ nɛ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnɛn Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ achyɛ yi.
Ɛnyumɔt kɛ ɛchi nkwɔ nɛ babhakanɛm. Bárɔ baghɔrɛ́ bárɔbhɛ ŋwaka bɛbhʉrɛ chi nɛ batɨ̌ babhakanɛm, ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛbhɨkɨ kway. Bákʉ̀ baraka ntíánwɔ́p nɛ batɨ̌ babhakanɛm. Bákʉ̀ nɔ mámbɔŋ nɔkɔ ntɛmsi anɛ akway nɛ bhɔ.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ̀ mǎndɨŋɨ mbák Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm achi nɛ mmu chí bɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ árɛ̀m kpoŋoroŋ bɛ Yesu Kristo asɔt nyaka mmʉɛt nkwǎŋwaŋ atwɔ́ fá amɨk, Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm achi nɛ yi.
Ndu mamiɛ́ ápay gbók, Pɔ̌l abhak ndu ɛkɛt ɛnɛ́ yi ásɔ́rɛ́ áchɔkɔ arɛ, yímbɔŋ anchyɛ nɔkɔ nkábhɛ́ ɛkɛt. Ansyɛpti nɔkɔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ arɔŋ bɛghɔ yi.
Sɛ́rɔ́k sɛ́chwé áchwí anɛ áfú Adramatium. Abhɔ́ŋ nyaka bɛ́tɛ́mɛ ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nɛchyɛ̌nyɛ́n atú Esia. Sɛ́fá sɛ́ré rɔ́ŋ. Arístakɔs mmu Masidónia wu áfú Tɛsalónika abhak nɛ bhɛsɛ́.
Ɛ́chí yɛ bɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ ábhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Mmɔ Mandɛm, ǎbhɔ́ŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti. Nɛ mmu anɛ abhɨkɨ bhat mmʉɛt nɛ Mmɔ Mandɛm abhɨkɨ bhɔŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɔ. 
Bɛbʉ́ bɛ́fʉɛt ntá mmu amɔt kɛ bɛ̌twɔ fá amɨk, nɛ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhi bɛ́twɔ́ nɛ nɛwú. Nɔ kɛ ɛchi bɛ nɛwú nɛ́pɔ̀kɔ bo mankɛm mbɔnyunɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ákʉ bɛbʉ́.
Tɛtɛp, sɛ́chi ndǔ nɛdǐ kɛbhɔ fá amɨk nɛ sɛ́nòŋ nɛ bɛyǎ ɛkwak bɛ Mandɛm anchyɛ bhɛsɛ mmʉɛt ɛkɔ ɛnɛ ɛchi amfay,
Nchí sɔt nyaka nkáp ntá bakwɔ́ bho achak ndǔ bɛkwak bhe.
Mmu anɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm achi nɛ yí, ǎkwáy bɛrɨŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm, kɛ bǒ abhɛn Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm apu nɛ bhɔ, bápú kwáy bɛrɨŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mmu anɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm achi nɛ yi ákʉ̀.
Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́ghàti bhɛsɛ bɛ, “Adam, mmu Mandɛm áyámbɨ aghoko, achí nyaka nkwǎŋwaŋ anɛ achi nɛpɛ́m.” Kɛ Adam anɛ áfú ansɛm chí Ɛfóŋó nɛ yi ǎchyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m.
Chɔŋ mbak ɛkuti ɛyɛ mpoknkɛm, nɛ bǒbhɛ bápú kway bɛkʉ wɔ yɛ̌nyɨŋ, nɛ yɛ̌ chí bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl. Nchí to wɔ ntá yap nɛ́nɛ.
Kɛ Yesu arɔk, atɔk bhɔ arɛm bɛ, “Faté ká, bǎkɛ́ cháy.”
Kɛ mbɔk bákóŋo yí. Bɔ́bhɔ mánóko. Dionisiɔs, mmǔ ɛchɛmɛ́ Ariyopagɔs, nɛ ngɔrɛ́ anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ́ Damarís nɛ bo báchák babhak ndǔ nkwɔ bho abhɛn bakoŋo Pɔ̌l.
Manywɔp tándrámɔt anɛ Pɔ̌l afyɛ́ árɔ́p nɔ́kɔ́ kɛkwɔt mɛmay, mbɔk bo Israɛl abhɛn bafu atú Esia bághɔ́ Pɔ̌l amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm. Mányɨ́kɨ́si batɨ̌ bo bɛ mánkɛ́m Pɔ̌l, nɛ bákɛ́m yi,
Kɛ mbɔ̌ŋ bɛbhak fá Ɛ́fɛsɔs kpatɛ mpok Ɛpǎ Pɛntɛkɔs ankwáy.
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Bǎcháy yi? Nɛka ɛnɛka nɛ́gʉpsi nɛcha!” Afate yɛ asáy mbʉ́ɛ́p nɛ mpɛ́rɛ́nyɛn, nnyɛ́n nɛkwɛn tɨɨɨ.
Mpok ǎtwɔ̀, nɛ mpok ɛyɔ anáŋ aghaka anɛ bo abhɛn báchyɛ̀ Ɛta Mandɛm kɛnókó, bákʉ̀ nɔ ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chí tɛtɛp bɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm ǎtɔ̀ŋ bhɔ mbi. Mɛnyǔ bo bhɔ kɛ̌ Mandɛm áyàŋ mánchyɛ́ yi kɛnókó.
Ángɛl anɛ́ ajwi bapay afe ayi mmbá. Nɛ básɔt ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi mbɔ njiɛ ngo, ɛnɛ́ ɛ́dù mbɔ ngó, mámɛ́sɛ amɛm manyu. Ɛbhɔ́kɔ́ manyu ɛ́mɔt ndǔ bɛrat ɛ́yíbhíri ɛrɔp chi manoŋ manoŋ.
Kɛ ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛbhak ɛnyu yɔ ndǔ nkwɔ ywɛka. Mmu anɛ áyàŋ bɛbhak mǔngo ywɛka, abhɔŋ bɛbhak mǔbɛtok ywɛka,
Mmu anɛ ághókó ɛyɔŋ ɛya kɛ yi kɛkʉ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yí ághókó, mpú táŋ yí. Mbɨ́kɨ́ twɔ fá amɨk bɛ́táŋ bo, ntwɔ chi bɛpɛmɛ bho.
Mbakanɛm ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ bɛ́kúti ntí ndǔ mpok nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt tɛ̌ndu Mandɛm ághókó mbakanɛm bɛ ámbák mbɔ yímbɔŋ ndǔ bɛyǎ babhi. Mbakanɛm abhɔŋ bɛkʉ́ bo mangɔ́ mɛnwɔp Mandɛm, kɛ ngɔrɛ́ ǎtɔ́ŋ chí mɛnwɔp ɛbhɛn nnɛ́m ywi.
Mpǎy babhakanɛm abhɛn mányíɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɔ abhak mbɔ nká ɛnwi kɛfyɛ́ mǎmbɔ nɛ baghɔrɛ́.
Ɛchi tɛtɛp bɛ mbɔ̌ŋ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ̌kwáy bɛ́ghɔ́kɔmʉɛt arɛ́. Mbɔ ɛchi bɛ mmu abhɔŋ bɛghɔkɔ mmʉɛt chi ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ̀, mbʉ mbɔŋ bɛdɛp awɔ́ antɨ bɛ ɛya ɛnyu ɛcha ɛnɛ batɨ.
Bǒ nkwɔ́ bábhɔŋ bɛ́chyɛ bǒ batí abhɛn bákʉ̀ bɛtɨk ɛbhap ɛrɨrɨ kɛnókó nɛ ɛrɨ́tɨ́ akap. Ɛ́mbák ɛnyu yɔ, sayri sayri nɛ abhɛn báfyɛ̀ bɛtaŋ bɛ́gháti nɛ bɛ́tɔŋ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm.
Mánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ mɛ́nyiɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́, asɔt nkɔ́p nɛ mmɛ̌m amɛm, achyɛ bakak ntá Mandɛm nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yí ákʉ́ nɛ nɛnyíɛ́, abho bɛ́chyɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap andɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Nɛ́ chí nku nkɔ anɛ Mandɛm ányú nɛ bǒ mmɨk ɛ̌ti nɛwú ɛna. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ mǎnyu mmɛm ndu nkɔ́p anɛ kʉ ka nɔ́ ndu bɛ́tɨ́k mɛ.”
Chɔŋ Mandɛm antwɔ́, antáŋ bo fá amɨk, yi kɛ chɔŋti mpok, ndak amay.”
Ɛtaŋtí bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ ɛbhɔ bɛ́kʉ́ nkɛpɛrɛ kwáy bɛghɔ mbaŋ. Bǒ nkɔ́ nɛ bhɔ́ bárɔ́bhɛ́ kɛm mɛ chí ndǔ awɔ́ kpátɛ sɛ́gháka Damáskɔs.
Chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛp ntá yɛka bǒ mǎnyìɛ mǎnjwi nɛ́nɛ, mbɔnyunɛ chɔŋ nsay anu bhe! Chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛp ntá yɛka bo bǎwày ámɛ́n nɛ́nɛ, mbɔnyunɛ chɔŋ mǎndɔp ndǔ basɛ́mɛ́ nɛ nɛdǐ kɛbhɔ!
Mɔ́ngo anɛ áfù ndǔ insɛns awɔ́ ángɛl are kó nɛbhʉɛt Mandɛm áchí nɛ bɛyɔŋɔ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt bo Mandɛm.
Mbɔŋɔ́nkɨ akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, ‘Dɔ̌ ká. Mbák mǎndɔ́k bɛfɛrɛ nchaŋ ɛyɔ, bǎkway bɛ́fɛ́rɛ mbɔk nchwi nkwɔ.
Mmu anɛ abhɨkɨ kɔŋ bo, abhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ Mandɛm mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm chi Mmǔ ɛkɔŋ.
Sayri sayri, bákà nɛ mɛ bɛ mpok ntwɔ́ awu, mpú sɔt nyaka mɛnyɨŋ ntá yɛka, yɛ̌ nɔ mbɔk bárɛ̀m bɛ nchí mmu bɛtábhá, nɛ bɛ nchí sɔt mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛka ndu ngwáy.
Achyɛ́ bhɛsɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ mmu yi áchyɛ̀ bɔ̌bhi. Ɛ̌ti yɔ, sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ Mandɛm ǎfɛrɛ chɔŋ bɛsɛ mankɛm bo sɛ́chí bɔ̌bhi ndǔ kɛsɛm. Ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ́ bo báre bɨti Mandɛm ndǔ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi bɛyǎ bɛcha. 
Nkúbhɛ́ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm amɔt kɛ áchyɛ akap anɛ ankɛm. Yí ǎchyɛ akap ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu mbɔ ɛnyu yí áyàŋ. 
Mpokófu, Yesu ǎbók ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ́ mmu akwɛnɛ kɛbhok. Ɛ́fú nɔ́kɔ́ mbók wu abho bɛrɛm kɛpɨ. Bo abhɛn bachi arɛ babhak maknkay.
Mbɔ akap wu ákʉ̀ bo mambak pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí Mandɛm mbʉ bábhʉɛt bɛchyɛ wu? Mbʉ batɨ̌ bho ápú pɛrɛ taŋ bɔ ɛ̌ti bɛbʉ́ bhap.
Bɔ̌ma, mbák ntwɔ́ ntá yɛka ndɛmɛ nɔkɔ chi bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛbhɛn mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ, chɔŋ nkwak be ná? Mbɔŋ bɛkʉ mǎndɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm ákʉ́ mɛndɨ́ŋɨ́, nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ndɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛ̌ti Mandɛm, nɛ ɛbhɛ́n yi afyɛ́ mɛ antɨ bɛ ngati bho, nɛ mbɔŋ bɛtɔŋ Ɛyɔŋ ɛyi.
Yesu aghati yɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bɛ, “Mbák mmu ǎyàŋ bɛbhak nkoŋo wa, ángɔ́kɔ́ntɨk mmʉɛt yi, ampɔkɔ ɛkotákátí yi, ankoŋo mɛ.
Bo Israɛl bághɔ̀ nyaka bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ Mandɛm, yɛ̌ nɔ, bágwɔ́t batɨ̌ yap amɛm. Ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ ɛchi nɛ bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ bhap kpátɛ ɛchɔŋ. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ bápày bɛkáti Mandɛm ɛbhɛn nku nsɨ́, ɛ́bhak chi mbɔ bɛ ndɛn ɛyɔ akútí batɨ yap, nɛ ɛ́kʉ bɔ bákɛ́ jwimɛm ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bápày. Ndiɛrɛ Kristo kɛ ákway bɛfɛrɛ ɛkúti ɛyɔ ndǔ batɨ yap.
Jɔ̌n akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Yɛ̌ mmu apu kway bɛbhɔŋ ɛnyɨŋ kpátɛ Mandɛm anchyɛ yi yɔ.
Nɛ ndǔ Yesu nɛ bɔPíta básɛ̀p njiɛ, Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Bǎkɛ́ ghati yɛ̌ mmú ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm ákʉ́ bǎghɔ́ fá, kpátɛ yi ankʉ Mmu anɛ áfú ntá yi ampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.”
Asá awɔ́ bɛ mánchɔ́kɔ́ kpák. Báchɔkɔ kpák kpák. Abho yɛ bɛ́gháti bhɔ ɛnyǔ Mandɛm afɛrɛ yi ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ. Ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́, aghati bhɔ́ bɛ mángátí Jems nɛ bǒnkwɔ́ bachak ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́fákári. Arɔ yɛ bhɔ́, arɔk ɛbhak ɛchák.
Píta arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Aénias, Yesu Kristo ǎkʉ̀ wɔ ɔ́ntáŋ nɛ́nɛ. Faté pɛ́t ɛ̌sák ɛyɛ.” Tɛ́mte wu, atɛ́m afate.
Mbɔk bo abhɛn báté kɛ́kwɔ́t báyɨ̀ŋɨ, bághók nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ Yesu ábɨ́kɨ́ ɛnyu ɛyɔ, báré rɛm nɛ batɨ bɛ, “Ǎbhɨ̀ŋɨ Ɛláija!”
Mɛ̌yáŋ mǎnsɔ́t mɛ nɛ Apólos mbɔ bǒ bɛtok Yesu Kristo. Mandɛm achyɛ́ bhɛsɛ tɛtɛp ywi anɛ áchí bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ bɛ́ sɛ́nkʉ bo mánjwimɛm.
Yesu akɛmɛ bɔ́ bɛ, “Pú básɨŋ amɛm ɛkáti bɛbhé ɛyɛka bɛ Mandɛm arɛm bɛ, ‘Mɛ ndɛm bɛ́ bǎchí bɔmandɛm’?
Ágháká nɔ́kɔ́ arɛ́, abhak arɛ kpátɛ Mfɔ Hɛ́rɔd agú. Mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́fákárí nyaka ɛnyu ɛyɔ bɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm ághátí ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ andɛm, ɛmfu tɛtɛp bɛ, “Mbɨ́ŋɨ́ mɔ́wa bɛ ámfá ɛtɔk Íjip”.
