Arɛ́, chɔŋ mǎndi kɛbhɔ nɛ mǎmbak ndǔ nɛnyiɛ ámɛ́n mpok bǎghɔ Ábraham nɛ Áisek nɛ Jekɔ́p nɛ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ mankɛm chɔkɔ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛ́rɛ́ kɛfɔ̌ Mandɛm, ɛnɛ́ bátiɛ́bhɛ́ be nɛfí.
Sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ tɛ̌ndu Mandɛm akʉ Kristo apɛtnsɛm ndu nɛpɛ́m, yi apú pɛrɛ gu wáwák. Nɛwú nɛbhɨkɨ pɛrɛ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛni.
Bághɔ bɛ́ mbɔk bakoŋo Yesu mányìɛ̀ nɛnyíɛ́ kɛso amɔ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɛpɨŋɨ́ bǒ bhap ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ.
Bɔ̌ma, ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛbhak ɛnyu yɔ! Nnyu amɔt ámbɨti Mandɛm, nkúbhɛ́ nnyu wu ámbɨk mmu ɛyak.
Kɛ bábhó bɛbɨk ɛ̌ri, báchók batú nɛ amɔ, bádú bárɔ́k bákɛ́m yi.
Kɛ nɛ́nɛ, ɛnɛ́ Mandɛm ánáŋ áfɛ́rɛ́ be ndǔ bɛbʉ́, bǎrɔp chi basɛm abhi, nɛ nsáy anɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ chi nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛchi nyáŋá, nɛ ndǔ ngwɛnti, bǎbhɔŋ chi nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.
Kɛ Pɔ̌l amyák awɔ́, nnyɔ́ yɔ akwɛ́n ango, yɛ̌nyɨŋ kɛkʉ yi.
Páílet ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn, abhɛ́p bhɔ mbák Yesu achi mmu atú Gálili.
Ndǔ mpok anɛ áfʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ ansɛm, apú nyaka yɛ̌nyɨŋ ntá yɛ, kɛ nɛ́nɛ achí mmu anɛ ákway bɛkwak wɔ, nɛ ǎkwáy bɛkwak mɛ nkwɔ.
Kɛ Pɔ̌l kɛka bɛ́ ɛ́chi sayri bɛ́sɔt yi mbɔnyunɛ arɔ́ nyaka bhɔ ɛtɔk Pamfília ɛnɛ́ bábhɨ́kɨ́rɛ naŋa bɛtɨk ɛbhap.
Ɛsakámú amɔt anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ Yútikɔs abhak ndǔ ɛchɨ́kɨ́ ɛnɛ nyɛ́sɛ́kɛt chɔ́kɔ́. Mɔ́kɛt anɛ sɛ́chí arɛ abhak ndǔ nɛŋɔk ɛkɛt ɛnɛn nɛjwi arat. Ndǔ Pɔ̌l árɔ̀ŋ ambɨ bɛ́gháti bhɔ mɛnyɨŋ ndǔ ɛrɔri mpok, Yútikɔs abho mɛmɔk kɛnɔ́. Ákwɛ́n nɔ́kɔ́ kɛnɔ́, amok akwɛ́n amɨk nɛfí. Bápɛ́rɛ sɛp bɛ mámpɔ́kɔ́ yi agú.
Bɛti bɛ́pú pɛrɛ bhak chɔŋ arɛ. Nti apu bɛbhɔŋ ɛrɔŋɔ nɛ mmok mbɔnyunɛ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ Mandɛm bɛ́ghɔ̀ arɛ́. Nɛ chɔŋ bɔ̌bɛtok Mandɛm mámbak bafɔ mpoknkɛm. 
Aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Gʉɛ́p ká asɨ ɛbhe awɔ́nɛm áchwí, chɔŋ mǎnkɛ́m nsi.” Bágʉɛ́p asɨ ɛbhe awɔ́nɛm. Bɛyǎ nsi ɛkwɛn, kpát ɛ́chá bhɔ́ bɛyǎ bɛyǎ nkáp ɛbhɨ.
Bě bachǐbhɔ, mmu ywɛka anɛ mbák mɔ́ywi ámbɛ́p yi brɛt, ansɔt chi ntay anchyɛ yi, chi agha?
Sɔt ka bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn nchyɛ́ bhe, mǎngɔ́k mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ̌tɔ̀ŋ bhe mbɔnyunɛ nchí kpák ndǔ ɛpɨŋ ɛya nɛ nɛyoŋómʉɛt nɛ́pú mɛ antɨ. Kʉ ka nɔ́ chɔŋ mǎmbɔŋ nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt.
Mandɛm ákʉ́ nyaka Yesu apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, nɛ ndǔ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi, chɔŋ ankʉ bɛsɛ́ nkwɔ́ sɛ́mpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m nɛ mmʉɛt ɛkɔ.
Bátée angɔkɔ manyu wu mánkway nɔkɔ nɛkwáy Moses mmɔ̌bɛtok Mandɛm nɛ ɛnɛn Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n bɛ, “Acha, Mandɛm Bɛtaŋ Mɛnkɛm, mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ɔ́kʉ́ chi manɛm mɛnyɨŋ nɛ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay! Wɔ, Mfɔ bɛtɔk mɛnkɛm, mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ɔ́kʉ̀ bɛ́bhak chi chak. Nɛ ɔchí tɛtɛp.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ntábhɛ́nɔk awa anɛ́ ápú nyu kɛpɛm, Ɛtaya ǎkpɔt angʉɛp. Nɛ ntábhɛ́nɔk anɛ ányù kɛpɛm, ǎkpɔti batap rɔrɔt amfɛrɛ bɛ́ wú ányú kɛpɛm ancha ɛnyu ɛsɨ́.
Mbok ɛ̌ti ndak anɛ ataka atú ɛtɔk wu ankɛm. 
Ghatí ká mɛ, be bo bǎyàŋ bɛ bɛbhé mɛmbɔŋ bɛtaŋ amfay yɛka, bǎpú ghok ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛbhé ɛ́rɛ̀m-ɛ?
Dɨŋɨ́ bɛ mbák ɛ́mfákárí ɛnyu ɛyɔ, ɔpú fu wawak kpátɛ ɔnchyɛ ákwɔ́ ywɛ ankɛm, yɛ̌nyɨŋ kɛrɔp.” 
Yesu ágháká nɔ́kɔ́ ndu bɛtɛm ɛbhɔ, aghɔ́ mmu wu bhʉ́rɛ́. Arɨŋɨ bɛ́ yi anáŋ atat arɛ́ ndǔ ɛrɔ́rí mpok. Abhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ɔ̌yáŋ bɛ́ ɔ́ntáŋ?”
Matá akɛmɛ bɛ, “Acha, nnókó. Nnókó bɛ́ ɔchí Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò, Mmɔ Mandɛm anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka bɛ́twɔ fá amɨk.” 
Ɛ́chí yɛ́ bɛ́ mmu anɛ ábháy ngɔrɛ́ anɛ yí átɨ́, akʉ sayri. Kɛ mmu anɛ áchɔ́kɔ́ kɛbháy ngɔrɛ́, akʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́rɨ́ ɛ́chá.
Mmǔ anɛ achi chɔkɔ ndǔ ɛkpɔkɔ́ nɛbhaŋ áfoŋ yɛ ngak anɛ achi yi awɔ ndǔ bɛtɔkɔ́ mmɨk áfɛ́rɛ́ mbwɔt nkɛm.
Kɛ ásɔ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nkaysi nɛ mmʉɛt yi arɛm bɛ, ‘Ghɔ́ ká mɛ-á, bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk ɛtaya báchí awu mányìɛ̀ nɛnyíɛ́ mmʉɛt ngɔkngɔk, mándɔ nɔkɔ mbɔk, nsay átwɔ way mɛ fá!
Yesu are rɔ́ŋ yɛ antɔŋ nɔkɔ bo amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nywɔp. Bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm, nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses, nɛ bǒbati ɛtɔk bachak báre yáŋ mbi bɛway yi.
Bǎkɛ́ sénse ntá batɨ tɛ̌ndu mǎnáŋ bǎrɔ ɛsɨ́ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛka nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nɔ nɛ́tò nyaka be mǎnkʉ nɔkɔ,
Bárɔ́ bɛchyɛ kɛnókó ntá Mandɛm mmu apu gu, bárɔ́bhɛ chyɛ kɛnókó chi ntá mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ bághókó nɛ amɔ. Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ bɛchi mbɔ nkwǎŋwaŋ nɛ bɛchak bɛchi mbɔ kɛnɛn nɛ bɛ́chák mbɔ nnya ɛnɛ́ bɛkak mɛnwi, nɛ ɛbhɛ́nɛ́fú mbɔ nnya ɛnɛ ɛ́su mɛniɛ amɨk. Bɔ mɛnkɛm bɛ́gùgu.
Ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ yi ákway nyaka bɛfɛrɛ bho ndǔ bɛcháy nɛwú. Báchí nyaka basɛm ndǔ bɛcháy ɛbhɔ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnap nɛnkɛm.
Yí bɛ, “Mbák Mandɛm achi nɛ bho mbɔ Mfɔ wap, mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́bhak mbɔ ɛnyu ɛchi ndǔ nɛkay ɛnɛn. Mfɔ amɔt anak nyaka ɛpǎ nɛbhay ntá mɔ́ywi.
Bɔ̌ma, Koŋó nɔ́kɔ́ ká ɛkakánɛkɔ ɛya nɛ fyɛ́ ká amɨ́k amʉɛt bo abhɛn bákòŋo bɛkaká nɛkɔ ɛbhɛsɛ. Bǎrɨŋɨ ndǔ bɛpɨŋ ɛbhɛsɛ bɛchi nyaka mpok sɛ́chí awu nɛ bhe.
Bábày bho mɛnwɔ́ptí batu anti bɛ mámpɔ́kɔ́, ndǔ bɛyǎ bɛbhé ɛbhɛn bɔ báfyɛ̀, kɛ bɔ́ babhɔŋ bápú kwak bo mámbʉ́rɛ́ bɛbhé bhɔ yɛ̌ mandú.
Bǎkɛ́ noko bɛ́ ɛ́chí tɛtɛp mbɔnyunɛ chɔŋ bǒ bɛtábhá mantwɔ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap andɛm nɔkɔ bɛ yi kɛ achi Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎto. Chɔŋ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ nsé nkwɔ mantwɔ. Nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap ǎtwɔ, ankʉ nɔkɔ bɛrɛmɛ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ndu bɛrwɔ bho. Nɛ mándwɔ́ yɛ̌ chí bǒ abhɛn Mandɛm áyábhɛ́ bɛ mámbák abhi, mbák bábhɔŋ mbi bɛkʉ nɔ.
Mbɔ̌ŋ mmu Krɛt wap amɔt, anɛ básɔ́rɛ́ mbɔ ndɨŋɨndak arɛm ɛ̌ti yap tɛntɛp bɛ, “Bǒ Krɛt báchí basěnsi mpoknkɛm! Báchi nyǎbhɨ, bábhɔ̀t abhɔt, mányiɛ nɔkɔ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ ngoŋo.”
Ɛpáfras, ntɨ mǔkɛnɔŋ ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo ǎtò wɔ bakak.
Nɛ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ nɛtaŋántɨ mmǔ amɔt nɛ́kʉ́ bo mankɛm mámbák bǒ bɛbʉ́, mmu amɔt anɛ ákʉ́ mbɔ ɛnyu Mandɛm aghati yi, akʉ bo mankɛm mámbák chak.
Ndu bɛrɔŋ ambɨ Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Mmǔfú abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɔ̌ babhakanɛm bati apay.
Píta asɔt bɔ́ árɔk anywɔ́p nɛ bhɔ. Nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́, Píta afa are rɔ́ŋ nɛ bɔ́. Mbɔk bǒ nkwɔ́ Yesu abhɛn Jopa bárɔ́k nɛ yi.
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, ndaká yi Mandɛm achyɛ yɛ bɛbhé? Achyɛ́ bɛbhé bɛ mɛ́nkʉ bɛsɛ sɛndɨŋɨ ɛnyǔ bɛbʉ́ bɛchi. Nɛ bɛbhé bɛbhɔŋ nyaka bɛbhak chi ndu mandú mpok, mɛnoŋ nɛtwɔ́ anɛ ɛbhárɛ́mɔ Ábraham. Ntá yi kɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛchyɛ akap wu. Mandɛm achyɛ nyaka bɛbhé ntá bɔángɛl bɛ mansɔt mantwɔ nɛ bhɔ, nkwǎŋwaŋ abhak nɛntɨ Mandɛm nɛ bǒ mmɨk.
Nɛ bɛ bábhɔŋ bɛghati bǒ bɛtɔk mɛnkɛm ndǔ nnyɛ́n ɛni bɛbho Yerúsalɛm bɛ Mandɛm ǎfòŋori bo abhɛn bátɨ́knsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhap.
Bárɔ́ yɛ barɔk báfyɛ́ ɛrɨŋ ndǔ ntay, nɛ bárɔ bɔ arɛ bɛ mambabhɛri nɔkɔ nnɛm.
Pɔ̌l aghɔ nɔkɔ bɛ mbɔk bǒ bati bhɔ bachi chí bǒnkwɔ Sádusi nɛ bɛ báchak babhak bǒnkwɔ Fárisi, abɨk bɛsí bǒ ɛchɛmɛ arɛm bɛ, “Bɔ̌ma, nchí mǔnkwɔ Fárisi nɛ mmɔ̌ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi. Nté fá acha manyé chí ndu nnókó bɛ́ chɔŋ Mandɛm ankʉ bawú mámpɛtnsɛm ndu nɛpɛ́m.”
Mandɛm akʉ bɔ́ mandɨŋɨ bɛ bě kɛ bǎbhɔŋ nsáy ndǔ bɛtɨk ɛbhap, puyɛ̌ bɔ babhɔŋ. Nsáy yɔ afʉ̌ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bo abhɛn bághàti Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ bághátí bhe ndǔ bɛtaŋ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ mmu Mandɛm átó. Yɛ̌ chi bɔángɛl bábhɔŋ nyaka ɛkwak bɛrɨŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn tɛntɛp. 
Nɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm árɛ̀m ɛ̌ti Mɔ́ywi chi bɛ yí áchyɛ́ bhɛsɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti nɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɔ nɛ́fù chi ntá Mɔ́ywi.
Mmǔfu aghók ɛ̌ti nɛkatínɛt ɛnɔ. Abhak mmɔ̌ manɔ Pɔ̌l. Afa arɔk amɛm ɛbhǎ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu aghati Pɔ̌l.
Nɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ̀ sɛ́ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ sɛ́chi nɛ Mandɛm mpoknkɛm nɛ bɛ yí achí nɛ bhɛsɛ mpoknkɛm chí Ɛfóŋó yi ɛnɛ yi achyɛ bhɛsɛ.
Ɛ́bhàk ɛnyu ɛyɔ mbɔnyunɛ, yɛ̌ mmu apu kway bɛbhak chak bɛsí Mandɛm nɛ ntɨ bɛ ǎkʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ɛbhé ɛ́yàŋ yi ankʉ. Ɛbhé ɛ́kʉ̀ mmu andɨŋɨ bɛ yi achi mmu bɛbʉ́. 
Yesu ághók ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bárɛ̀m, akɛmɛ bhɔ nɛ nɛkay bɛ, “Bǒ abhɛn bápú me, bápú yaŋ ngaŋ. Bǒ mame kɛ báyàŋ ngaŋ.”
Sɔ̌l afa yɛ are rɔ́ŋ. Agháká nɔ́kɔ́ kɛ́kwɔ́t nɛ Damáskɔs, bɛdíɛ́rɛ́ bɛfú amfay tɛ́mchok bɛsɛp bɛ́káp yi.
Kɛ bǒ abhɛn Mandɛm áyábhɛ́ bɛ mámbák abhi mpoknkɛm, yɛ̌ chí bo Israɛl, yɛ̌ chí bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl, bárɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ amʉɛt Yesu Kristo kɛ̌ bo bághɔ̀ bɛtaŋ Mandɛm nɛ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak Mandɛm.
Nté fá ɛchɔŋ bǎtàŋ mɛ chí mbɔnyunɛ mbákántɨ ndǔ bariɛp amɛn Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka ntá bachǐmbɨ abhɛsɛ.
Afɛ́rɛ́ bɛrɛmɛ́ bafɔ ndǔ mɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ ɛbhap, ákosi bo abhɛn bápú yɛ̌nyɨŋ.
Bɛfʉɛt nkárɛ́nká ɛ́rát bɛghaka nkárɛ́nká ɛ́tandat betí Yesu abho bɛkɔ amfǎnyɛ́n bɛrɔŋ bɛtɛmɛri bhɔ.
Báchí bo Israɛl. Bɔ́ kɛ Mandɛm ásɔ́rɛ́ bɛ mámbák bǒbhi. Ntá yap kɛ̌ yi átɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ bhi. Anyǔ nku chi nɛ bhɔ. Ntá yǎp kɛ̌ yi achyɛ bɛbhé. Bɔ kɛ̌ yi atɔŋɔ ɛnyǔ bo babhɔŋɔ bɛchyɛ yi kɛnókó nɛ, nɛ bɔ́ kɛ̌ yi afyɛ́ bariɛp.
Bápɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nsɛm ntá Páílet nɛ Yesu, Páílet ató bábhɨ́ŋɨ bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ bǒbati ɛtɔk nɛ bǒ ɛtɔk.
Nchí ntísiɛ Ɛpáfras bɛ ákʉ́ tontó ɛ̌ti yɛka nɛ bǒnkwɔ Laodísia, nɛ abhɛn Hiɛrapolis.
Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ chí bɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ághàti mɛ bɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ nchwɔ́bhɛ́ chɔŋ bo mámfyɛ́ mɛ ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ nɛ mánchyɛ mɛ ɛsɔŋɔri.
Bo abhɛn bákɔ̀ nɛ yi babhak Sopátɛ mmɔ̌ Pírɔs mmu ɛtɔk Bɛ́roa, nɛ bǒ Tɛsalónika bati apay, nɔ chi Arístakɔs nɛ Sɛkúndus, nɛ Gáyɔs mmu ɛtɔk Dɛ́be, nɛ Tímɔti, nɛ bo atú Esia bati apay, nɔ chi Tíkíkɔs nɛ Trofímɔs.
Ngɔrɛ́ amɔt achi nyaka ɛtɔk Jopa anɛ aka nnyɛ́n bɛ́ Tabíta,   [Nɔ́ chí Dɔ́kas ndu ɛyɔŋ Grik] abhak nkoŋo Yesu. Ǎkʉ nyaka bɛrɨ, ankwak nɔkɔ bachɛ́bhɛ́bho mpoknkɛm.
Ntɨkɨ nsáy mmu ábhɔ̀ŋ mbák abhɔŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ fá amɨk, kɛ anɛ́m nɛpɛ́m ɛni?
Ɛchi mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Wɔ, nkongɔrɛ́, wɔ mmu ɔpú bhe, bɔ́ŋ maŋák. Nnɔ anɛ ápú bhɔŋ bɛbě nɛbhe, kway nɛ maŋák, mbɔnyunɛ ngɔrɛ́ anɛ bárɔ́ ndu nɛbhay, bɔ̌bhi baya bacha. Abhɛn ngɔrɛ́ anɛ abhay nnɛ́m.”
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Mɛnkwɔ mbɔ̌ŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mɔt bɛbhɛp be. Mbák mǎnkɛ́mɛ́ mɛ yɔ, chɔŋ mɛnkwɔ ngati be mmu anɛ áchyɛ́ mɛ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ̌kʉ̀.”
Mmǔ amɔt ndǔ nkwɔ bo bhɔ abho bɛbɨk andɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, nnɨkmʉɛt, bú mɔ́wa. Achí mbakanɛm nɛ ndiɛrɛ yí kɛ mbɔ́ŋɔ́!
Kɛ nchí ghati bhe bɛ, mbák mmu akʉ wɔ bɛbʉ́, ɔ́kɛ́ kɛmɛ yi. Mbák mmu adɛp wɔ atá ndǔ ɛbhe awɔ́nɛm, tɔ́ŋ yi ɛbhe ɛ́chák nkwɔ.
Ananías atwɔ́ ntá ya, ate mɛ nɛ́kú mmʉɛt arɛm bɛ, ‘Manɔ́ wa Sɔ̌l, pɛt bo bɛghɔ mbaŋ.’ Tɛ́mté wu amɨ́k ánɛ́nɛ mɛ mpɛt mbo bɛ́ghɔ mbaŋ. Ngɔ́ yɛ́ yi.
Ɛyɔ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ Mandɛm áfʉ̀ɛt nyaka ntá Kristo bɛkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ámpɛ́tnsɛm ambɔŋ kpák nɛ yi. Abhɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ yɨŋɨ nyaka ndǔ bɔ bapu bhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé. Nɛ afyɛ́ ntó amɔ yɛsɛ ɛnɛ́n nɛ́kʉ̀ bo mámpɛ́tnsɛm mámbɔŋ kpák nɛ yi.
Dɔ̌ ká bhɔ awu! Báchí chí manɛ́mámɨk abhɛn báyàŋ bɛya bho mbi. Nɛ mbák nnɛ́mámik ánjá ntɨ nnɛ́mámik mbi, bɔ́ mankɛm bákwɛn amɛm nɛpi.”
Mandɛm ǎkway bɛkʉ ɛncha mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn sɛ̌kwáy mɛnɨkmʉɛt bɛ yi ankʉ ndǔ bɛkwak bhɛsɛ, nɛ ɛncha ɛnyǔ ɛnɛ sɛ́kway bɛkaysi bɛ chɔŋ yi ankʉ. Ǎkʉ̀ nɔ nɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi ɛbhɛn bɛ́kʉ̀ bɛtɨk amɛm nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛsɛ.
Baghɔk Yesu bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fákárí, bábhák maknkay tontó. Bábhó bɛrɛm nɛ batɨ bɛ, “Yi ɛ́kʉ́ ɛnɔk fig ɛnɛ ɛgu tɛ́mté ɛnyunɛ?”
Yɛ̌ chí Yerúsalɛm mbɨ́kɨ́ ko ndɔk bɛghɔ bo abhɛn báyámbɨ bɛbhak bǒnto kɛ mɛ̌twɔ ansɛm. Ndɔkɔ́rɔ́ŋ téé atú Arébia, kɛ ɛ́tárɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, mpɛtnsɛm Damáskɔs.
Batɨ yap ájwí nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ ndak abʉ́abʉ mbɔ bɛkʉ bɛbʉ́ nɛ bɛfyɛ amɨ́k ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ bo bachak, nɛ ɛpɨŋ bɛyaŋ bɛkʉ batɨ bɛbʉ́, nɛ mpabhamɨ́k, nɛ bɛway bho, nɛ bɛtaŋa ɛbhɛn mmu ábhɔ̀ŋ nɛ batɨ ndu áyɛ̀nti mmʉɛt nɛ bhɔ, nɛ bɛrwɔ bho, nɛ ɛpɨŋ bɛkʉ batɨ bɛbʉ́, nɛ ɛnáŋtí.
Bɔ́ mankɛm bábɨ́k mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Dɔ̌ mángwáy yi. Fɛrɛ́ bhɛsɛ chi Barábas!”
Bǒ abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ akap bɛrɛm mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fú ntá Mandɛm bákwáy bɛkɛm mmʉɛt manchɔkɔ kpák, bɛ mándɨ́ŋɨ́ mpok anɛ bákway bɛrɛm kɛpɨ.
Mmǔ wu arɔ, arɔk, aghati bǒbati bo Israɛl bɛ Yesu kɛ ábú yi.
nɛ mmu anɛ árɛ̀m ɛnyɨŋ anjɨkɨ, ambɨŋɨ mfay, abhɔŋ bɛrɨŋɨ bɛ ǎyɨkɨ nɔ chi ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ Mandɛm nɛ Mandɛm mmu áchɔ̀kɔ arɛ.”
Bo mankɛm bábhák maknkay bɛghɔ bɛtaŋ Mandɛm. Bo barɔk ambɨ bɛbhak maknkay ɛ̌ti yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu ákʉ́. Yesu arɛm ntá baghɔkɔ́ bhi bɛ,
Mbák mmʉɛt nkɛm achí chí nyɛ́sɛ́, mmu ǎkwáy bɛ́ghok mbaŋ ná? Nɛ mbák mmʉɛt nkɛm áchí chí átú, mmu ǎkwáy bɛ́ghok ɛriɛp ná?
Nchí yaŋ bɛ mbát mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu sayri. Puyɛ̌ chí ɛ̌ti mɛ̌bhʉ̀ɛrɛ bɛbhé bo Israɛl kɛ Mandɛm ákʉ́ bɛ mbák chak bɛsí bhi. Ɛ̌ti nɛka ɛnɛ nɛ Kristo kɛ Mandɛm ákʉ́ bɛ́ mbák chák bɛsí bhi.
Sɔt yɛka mpok bɛ́ bǎkɛ́ kʉ bɛtɨk ndɛ́ndɛm, kɛbhɔŋ nsáy ndǔ bɛtɨk ɛbhɔ. Sɔt ká mpok ɛnyu ɛnɛ bǎbhɔ̀ŋ nsáy yɛka nkɛm.
Mbák ɛ́pú nɔ́, bɛ́p bo abhɛn bachi fá téé, bɛ bɔ babhɔŋ mandɛm bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ ɛbhɛn baghɔ ɛbhe ɛya mpok ntée amɛm ɛchɛmɛ́ bǒbati ɛtɔk.
Mpok mɛniɛ Ɛlísabɛt bɛghaka bataŋ atandat, Mandɛm ató ángɛl Gábriɛl ɛtɔk Násárɛt, atú Gálili.
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu nɛ Sakio báchí anywɔ́p, Sakio afate arɛm ntá Yesu bɛ, “Acha, ghók, chɔŋ nkɔ́rɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbha ndǔ baru apay, nchyɛ́ ndu amɔt ntá bachɛ́bhɛ́ bho. Nɛ mbák nsɔt ɛnyɨŋɨ́ mmu ndǔ mangwɔ, chɔŋ nkɛmɛ yɔ ndɔŋ ɛnwi.”
Ángɛl Mandɛm árɔŋɔ nɔkɔ, Kɔnéliɔs nkwɔ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk abhi batí apay nɛ ntɛmɛ́ nɛnu amɔt anɛ achi nyaka nɛ yi mpoknkɛm ankwaka nɔkɔ yi. Ntɛmɛ́ nɛnu wu abhak mmu anɛ áchày Mandɛm.
Bǎbhɔŋ bɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ nywɔp Yesu Acha átwɔ̀ nɛ́bhak chɔŋ mbɔ ngɛ́p anɛ átwɔ̀ nɛ bɛti.
Ndǔ ngwɛnti, Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Mmu anɛ áyàŋ bɛghok, ántá batú angok sayri.” 
Bɔ̌ma, mɛmbɔ̌ŋ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ bɛrɨ ɛbhɛn bǎkʉ̀ bɛyǎ nɛ bɛ bǎrɨ̀ŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti Mandɛm sayri ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ bǎkway bɛtɔŋ batɨ bǒnkwɔ.
Yi afyɛ́ nnyɛ́n ɛni ndǔ manɛrɛ́kɛt ankɛm, awu amfay nɛ fá amɨk.
“Ghɔ́k ká ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛnɔkárɛm ɛnɛ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ́ ‘Fig’ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bhɛsɛ. Ɛ́náŋ ɛ́mbó bɛtɛm bɛtɔ́, bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ́ ɛso ɛ́rɔp chi kɛkwɔt.
Mbɔk bǒnkwɔ Fárisi nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm bábhɛ́p Yesu bɛ, “Ndaká yí baghɔkɔ́ bhɛ bápú koŋo bɛpɨŋ ɛbhɛn bachǐmbɨ bhɛsɛ? Ndaká yí mǎnyìɛ nɛnyíɛ́ kɛso amɔ mbɔ ɛnyu ɛ́yàŋ?”
Aghɔ́ bɔángɛl Mandɛm bati apay chɔ́kɔ́ nɛ ndɛn pɛ́pɛ́p amʉɛt ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bábhʉ́rɛ́ nyaka Yesu. Amɔt abhak ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt ntí ywi achi nyaka. Achák ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt bɛkak.
Pɔ̌l arɔk achwe amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí ɛyɔ. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak yí árɔ́ŋɔ́, ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ yí ákʉ̀ nyaka. Ndǔ bɔsɔnde barat are fyɛ́ mbok nɛ bhɔ ndu bɛkʉ bɔ mámbɔŋ nɛjwǐmɛm ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm,
Bɔ̌ma, bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ ndǔ bo Akáiya mankɛm, ɛfo ɛnɛ Stɛfánas kɛ ɛ́yámbɨ bɛkoŋo Yesu Kristo, nɛ báchíɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnap ndu bɛkǔ bɛtɨk bɛ mánkwak bo Mandɛm.
Mɛ Pɔ̌l nɛ Tímɔti, bɛsɛ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk Yesu Kristo kɛ sɛ́sɨ̀ŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ. Sɛ́sɨ̀ŋ ntá yɛka bo Mandɛm mankɛm, bě bhó bǎbhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu awu ɛtɔk Fílipi. Sayri sayri, sɛ́sɨ̀ŋ ntá yɛká bǒ batí nɛ be bho bǎkwàk bǒ batí bɛkʉ bɛtɨk Mandɛm ndǔ nkwɔ bakoŋo Yesu abhɛn Fílipi.
Nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́, batɛmɛ́ nɛnu abhɛn bákɔ́ chi nɛ bɛkak bápɛtnsɛm amɛm ɛbhá. Bárɔ́ abhɛn bákɔ̀ amfay mpɔŋɔ́ndɨ́k mándɔ́k Seséria nɛ Pɔ̌l.
Bák ká maŋák mpoknkɛm,
Pɔ̌l nɛ Sáilas nɛ Tímɔti baghat bafʉɛt atú Frijia nɛ atú Galéshia mbɔnyunɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ ka bɛ mángati bo Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm atú Esia.
Bǒ mmɨk bákòŋo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn kɛ dɨŋɨ́ ka bɛ Ɛtayɛka arɨŋɨ bɛ bǎbhɔŋ bɛbhɔŋ bɔ́.
Kɛ mbák chi bhe, bǎpú ɛnyu ɛyɔ, mbɔnyunɛ Mmǔ anɛ achi Nyáŋá   anɛ́nɛ́ bhe amɨk, nɛ be mankɛm bǎrɨ̀ŋɨ tɛtɛp Mandɛm.
“Mfɔ Agripa, nkáysɨ́ bɛ́ ɛrɨ ɛcha bɛ nté bɛsí ɛbhɛ ɛchɔŋ ndu bɛ́táŋa mmʉɛt ndǔ barak anɛ́ bo Israɛl bábhàt mɛ amʉɛt.
Kɛ bárɔ́k ambɨ bɛkpɛmɛ, mambɨkɨ nɔkɔ bɛ Páílet andɔ mango yi ndǔ ɛkotákátí. Bǎri map anyiɛrɛ Páílet, awupsi ntɨ.
Arɛ́, bágó Yesu ndǔ ɛkotákátí. Bágó bo báchák nkwɔ bati apay, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap ndǔ ɛyi ɛkotákátí, amɔt ɛbhe awɔ́nɛm Yesu, achák ɛbhe awɔghɔ.
Kɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ mɛnkɛm nyaka nkáysí bɛ́ bɔ́ kɛ bɛ́kʉ̀ mɛ́mbak mmu Mandɛm, bɛ́rɔp chí bɛpɔ̌ mɛnyɨŋ ntá ya ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu Kristo akʉ ntá ya.
Wɔ kɛ ɔ́kʉ́ nyaka bɛ mǔbɛtok ywɛ Mfɔ Debhít, chi-mbɨ ywɛsɛ́, ándɛm ndǔ bɛtaŋ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ bɛ: ‘Ndaká yí bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl bábèntɨ nɛ wɔ Mandɛm? Ndaká yí bǒbhɛn bátè bɛyu ɛbhɛn bɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ntí nɛ nnɛt?
Bɛsɛ́ sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ngǎngaŋ bɛbhay baghɔrɛ́ bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ ywɛsɛ ánkɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɛ ngɔrɛ́ anɛ achi ntɨ mmu nkwɔ, mbɔ bɔ̌nnɔ Yesu Acha nɛ mbɔ Sɛ́fas nɛ bǒnto bachak?
Mmʉɛrɛ ywɛ wu ankɛmɛ bɛ, ‘Kɛ́pɛrɛ sɔŋɔri mɛ. Nnáŋ mfe mbǐnywɔp nɛ nnáŋ mbʉrɛ nɛ bɔ̌bha. Mpú kway bɛfate bɛ nchyɛ́ wɔ yɛ̌nyɨŋ.’
Kɛ mǔngo bachiǎkap aywǐnti kɛ áchwè amɛm mɔ́kɛt anɛ achi Nyáŋá Acha ndɔŋ amɔt ndǔ mmíɛ́. Nɛ abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɛchwe arɛ̌ chi nɛ manoŋ amɛn yi áchyɛ̀ ɛ̌ti bɛbʉ́ bhi nɛ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛn bo bákʉ́ kɛrɨŋɨ bɛ chi bɛbʉ́.
bɛ, “Kɛ́ ghati yɛ̌ mmu ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fákárí, kɛ dɔ́k ntá nchiakap Mandɛm bɛ yi ángɔ́ bɛ ɛbhaŋákwa yɛ ɛ́may. Ánáŋ ámbyó wɔ, ɔ́ndɔk, ɔnchyɛ yɛ akap ntá Mandɛm bɛkoŋo ɛbhé Moses. Chɔŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́mbak ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bho bɛ ɛbhaŋákwa yɛ ɛ́may.”
Ndǔ mǎnyú bɛyǎ kɛpɛm, bǎtɔŋ bɛ bǎchí bakoŋo bha, nɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ̀ bo mánchyɛ Ɛtaya kɛnókó.
Ndǔ mpok anɛ áfʉɛ́rɛ́ ansɛm, básɔt nyaka chi manoŋ mmɛ́n nɛ amɛn nnɛ́m mpɔŋ nɛ batwɔp amɛn mɔ́ngɔ̌ mpɔŋ anɛ básɔ́ŋɔ́, mámyakati amʉɛt mmu anɛ apú pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí Mandɛm, bɛ ambak yɛ pɛ́pɛ́p.
Mpok nchí nɛ bhe amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm nɛ́nji nɛnji, bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ kɛm mɛ. Kɛ mpok yɛka nɛ Satan, mfɔ ɛjuri, akway nɛ́nɛ.” 
Tɛ́mchok, Moses nɛ Ɛláija, barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm abhɛn tɛsáy bábhési, mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ kɛpɨ nɛ Yesu.
Báre kɛm ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ batɨ bɛ, “Chɔŋ sɛ́ndɛm bɛ yi? Mbák sɛ́ndɛm bɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn Jɔ̌n bɛ́fú nyaka ntá Mandɛm, ǎbhɛ́p bhɛsɛ bɛ, ‘Kɛ ndaká yi bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ noko ɛyɔŋ ɛyi?’
Babho bɛrɛm nɛ batɨ bɛ, “Nyakányɛt maŋák achi mbʉ bhɛsɛ antɨ mpok yi árɛ̀m kɛpɨ nɛ bhɛsɛ ambi, anɛnɛ nɔkɔ basɨŋ ntá yɛsɛ!”
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ sɛ́rɛ̀m ɛ̌ti mmʉɛt ɛyɛsɛ ɛ́kɛ́ kʉ mǎnkaysi bɛ sɛ́pɛt sɛ́yàŋ chi bɛ mǎndɨŋɨ ɛnyu bho sɛ́chi. Bo báchí abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́twɔ be nɛ bɛkáti ɛbhɛn bɛ́rɛ̀m ɛrɨ́rɨ́ ɛ̌ti ɛya. Mɛnyǔ bo bho, bápɛt báyàŋ nɔ chi bɛ mǎnchyɛ bhɔ bɛkáti bɛ mántɔŋ ntá bo bachak? Bɛsɛ sɛ́pu nɔ.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ akap anɛ́ árɨ́ ndǔ babhi ankɛm áfù chí amfay. Mandɛm mmu ághókó bɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ mfáy kɛ̌ áchyɛ̀ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛrɨ́tí akap, nɛ yí ápú yibhiri ɛnyu mbɔ ndɨ́kándi. Mmok ákɔ̀ amfay, bɛsap ndɨ́kándi mɛ́ngupsi nɔkɔ.
Sɛ́pú kʉ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́chɛ̀t mmu mbi nɛ Mandɛm bɛ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bɛ́kɛ́ bhak ndǔ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛsɛ.
Ɛ́kʉ́ bakoŋo Jɔ̌n bárɔ́k ntá yi barɛm bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, mmu anɛ achi nyaka nɛ wɔ ɛbhé Nyɛ́n Jɔ́dan ɛnɛ́ awu ɔ́ngati nɔkɔ bo mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti yi, ǎjwiti bho nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu árɔ̀ŋ ntá yi.”
Kɛ mbɔ ɛnyu ɛ́chi, bɛ́pókómʉɛt bɛ́yǎ, kɛ ndiɛrɛ mmʉɛt amɔt kɛ achi.
Nchí ghati yɛ bhe bɛ manyíɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́ bɛ nɛnchyɛ bhe bɛtaŋ. Yɛ̌ ɛkak ɛmɛnɛ́nti mmǔ yɛka ɛpu nɛm.”
Símun akɛmɛ bɛ, nkáysi bɛ, “Chi anɛ barɛm ami áyá.” Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Ɔrɛm tɛtɛp.”
Ndǔ nɛbhǒnɛt, ntaŋá manyé wu kɛfyɛ́ ntí. Kɛ ansɛm mpok, achɔkɔ diíí arɛm nɛ mmʉɛt yi bɛ, ‘Yɛ̌ndu mpú chyɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó, nɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ mpok nɛ ntɨ nkwǎ,
Mbabhɛri nnyǔbha, ǎnɛ̀nɛ nyǔbhá ntá yi. Bághɔ́ŋɔ́mɛn árɨŋɨ ɛyɔŋ ɛyi. Ǎbhɨŋɨ yɔ́ ndǔ manyɛ́n ayap, ansɔt yɔ́ amfu nɛ yɔ.
Ɛtayi nɛ máyi bábhák maknkay tontó. Kɛ Yesu asɛmti bhɔ bɛ bákɛ́ ghati yɛ̌ mmu ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fákárí.
Ǎtwɔ̀ nɛ nchán myákátí awɔ bɛ́chák nkway ndǔ bɛ́fáp ɛnɛ ɛ́rɨ́ nɛ bɛkpáfu. Ánáŋ ánkʉ́ nɔ́, ǎsɔt mbwɔt antɛn ndǔ nkpánɛ́, anyɔ mmɨk, ansɔt bɛkwɔp ɛbhi amfyɛ ndǔ ngo anɛ apu nɛmɛ.” 
Páílet apɛt arɔ áchá ywi afú nɛfí ntá bo Israɛl arɛm bɛ, “Ghok ka, nchí ntwɔ́ nɛfí nɛ yi ntá yɛka bɛ mǎndɨŋɨ bɛ́ mbɨ́kɨ́ ghɔ ɛbɛ́ptí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ákʉ́ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́yàŋ bɛ mángwáy yi.”
Lásárɔs mmu anɛ ánáŋ ágú nyaka, afú ndǔ nnɛm, nɛ ndɛn ɛnɛ mánɛ́bhɛ́ yí amɔ nɛ bɛkak nɛ bɛsí kɛ bábhɛ́mɛ yi. Yesu aghati bɔ bɛ, “Kaŋarí ká ndɛn ɛyɔ yi amʉɛt, bɛ yi ándɔ́k.” 
Mbɔ Ábraham achi nyaka chak bɛsí Mandɛm ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ́tí bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ́, mbʉ ntí achi anɛ yi ápanyu. Kɛ ápu kway nyaka bɛkʉ nɔ bɛsí Mandɛm.
Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bákɔ́ baghaka ndǔ bɔ̌bɛtɔk Bɛtfágɛ nɛ Bɛ́tani ndǔ Njiɛ Mɛnok Ólif, kɛkwɔt Yerúsalɛm. Ató baghɔkɔ́ bhi bati apay ambɨ.
Ághoko nɔkɔ nɔ, apɔp, arɔbhɛ rɔ́ŋɔ́rɔŋ nɛ basɛ́mɛ́ antɨ mbɔnyunɛ abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ
Kɛ anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ chi-bɛtɨk áyàŋ yi ankʉ, mbák akʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́yàŋ mantɛmsi yi, báchyɛ yi chi mandú ntɛmsi. Bábhɛp tontó ntá mmu anɛ báchyɛ́ yi tontó. Nɛ báfyɛ amɨ́k tontó ntá mmu anɛ báfyɛ́ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ amɔ́ yi.” 
Abhɨ́kɨ́ ghɔkɔntɨk bɛghɔ Ábraham ntínso, nɛ bɛbhárɛ́ bɔ̌bhi mankɛm, mpoknkɛm!”
Barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ nsé chí bǒ mmɨk anɛ. Ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ̌ bɔ bátɔ̀ŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi chi nkaysi bǒ mmɨk nɛ bǒ mmɨk bághòk bhɔ.
Akʉ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay arɛ́. Bo baghɔ nɔkɔ nɔ, bɛyǎ bhap báre tá batú sayri ndu bɛghok mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yí árɛ̀m.
Bábhɔŋ bɛfyɛ mmɛ̌m bakɔ chi amɛm ɛbhǎ mmɛ́m ɛnɛ́ ɛkɔ.
Bakoŋó Jɔ̌n bati apay bághók nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ́mɛ́, bárɔ́ yi bábho bɛkoŋo Yesu.
Bɛsɛ mankɛm sɛchi ndu mmʉɛt amɔt, sɛbhɔŋ chi Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ amɔt. Nɛ ɛchi ɛnyu ɛ́mɔt nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mɔt kɛ ɛchi ɛnɛ sɛ́bháká ntɨ arɛ, bɛ Mandɛm abhɨŋɨ bɛsɛ bɛ sɛmbɔŋ chɔŋ yɔ.
Bákɛ́mɛ bɛ, “Moses arɛm bɛ mmu ǎkwáy bɛrɔ ngɔrɛ́ ywi mbák achyɛ́ yi ɛkáti ɛnɛ́ awáy nɛbhay?”
Nɛ mmu ywɛka ákɛ́ ka batɨ mámbɨ́ŋɨ́ yi bɛ, ‘Ntɔŋ’   mbɔnyunɛ bǎbhɔŋ chi amɔt, Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò.
Nɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ bɛ́ ndǔ bǎchi nɛ amɨ́k ambi mǎnòŋ Yesu Kristo Acha ámpɛ́tnsɛm, bǎbhɔŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ akap anɛ́ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ áchyɛ̀.
Bɛ́rɔŋ ndǔ ngwɛnti, Yesu arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ bághoko nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt ɛ̌ti nkwǎ, bábhɨ́kɨ́ ghoko nkwǎ ɛ̌ti nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt.
Ángɛl wu asɔt mɔ́nchán pú wu, afyɛ́ ngo amɛm anɛ áfú ndǔ ɛ́fɛ́mɛ́ akap, amɛsɛ amɨk. Nɛbu nɛbho bɛrɛmti, nɛfaŋ ansay nɔkɔ tontó, miámiaŋ ankɔt nɔkɔ, mmɨk anyɨkɨsi nɔkɔ. 
Bɔ̌ma, nchí rɛm nɔ́ mbɔnyunɛ mbɔk bo abhɛn báfú ɛkɛt Klóe bághátí mɛ́ kpoŋoroŋ, bɛ́ bǎtáŋ nɛ batɨ.
Manywɔp apay anɛ Yesu achi nɛ bo Samária áfʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, afa bɛrɔŋ atú Gálili.
Báchɔ́kɔ yɛ amɨk mámbabhɛri nɔkɔ yí.
Arɛm nta yap bɛ, “Kɛ bě babhɔŋ bǎrɛ̀m bɛ mɛnchí agha?” Símun Píta akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Wɔ kɛ ɔ́chí Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò.” 
mámbɨk nɔkɔ bɛ, “Bo Israɛl, kwak ka bhɛsɛ́! Ghɔ́ ká mmu anɛ ákɔ̀ antɔŋ nɔkɔ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti bo bhɛsɛ́ nɛ bɛbhé Moses nɛ ɛ̌ti ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm ɛnɛ. Akʉ kpát nɛ́nɛ asɔt bǒ abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl achwe fá amɛm ɛkɛrákap ɛnɛ nɛ bhɔ. Anyɔ̌p Ɛkɛt Mandɛm nɛ ɛ́pɛt ɛpu ɛkɛrɛ́ bɛdyɛrɛ!”
Apɛt anɨk mmʉɛt. Mandɛm akʉ yɛ nɛbu nɛ́nɛ́nɛ, manyiɛp asɛp gbokórókórók achwe amɨk, mmɨk apɔp, abho bɛchyɛ nɛnyíɛ́.
Ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ syɛpti mɛ nɛ kɛnókó mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɔ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ, kɛ yi abhʉ́ɛ́t mɛnyɔti bɛkak ɛbha.
Nchí yaŋ mǎndɨŋɨ mɔ́mayɛsɛ Foibe mmu ákù bɛtɨk ntá Nkwɔ Kristo anɛ ɛtɔk Kɛnkreya.
Nɛyí nɔ́kɔ́ afɛrɛ nkáp achyɛ ntá mmu anɛ ayɨŋɨ ɛkɛt ɛyɔ arɛm bɛ ‘Yɨŋɨ́ mɛ́ yi. Nnáŋ mpɛtnsɛm chɔŋ nkɛmɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛchak ɛnɛ ɔ́chɔŋti yi amʉɛt.’”
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Bɛbʉ́ ná nɛ mkpáká bho anɛ ɛchɔŋ! Bápú kʉ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Mandɛm áyàŋ. Báyàŋ bɛghɔ chi ɛrɨŋɨ́ maknkay! Kɛ yɛ̌ ɛ́mɔt mpú tɔŋ be, ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ fʉɛt chi ɛnɛ Jóna, ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm.
Yesu arɛm yɛ ntá ngɛ́mtay bho abhɛn bachi arɛ bɛ, “Mǎnáŋ mǎngɔ́ nɛbu ndǔ nɛ́gírí ndǔ ɛbhě nɛbu ɛnɛ mmok ánɛm arɛ, bǎrɛm bɛ ‘Manyiɛp átwɔ kwɛn’; nɛ ɛ́mbak ɛnyu yɔ.
Abho bɛtɔŋ bhɔ mɛnyɨ. 
Yesu aghati bhɔ́ mángúrɛ́. Tɛ́mté wu, Yesu nɛ bakoŋo bhi báchwe amɛm áchwí bárɔ́k atú Dalmanúta. 
Yɛ̌ndu bɔángɛl bacha bhɔ ndǔ bɛtaŋ bápú rɛm bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ. Bápú sɔkɔti bhɔ́ nɛ bápú rɛm ɛbʉbʉ ɛ̌ti yap bɛsí Ɛta Mandɛm.
Ɛ́kʉ́ Yesu abhɛ́p baghɔkɔ́ bhi bati byo nɛ apay bɛ, “Ná nɛ bhe, bǎrɔŋ nkwɔ?”
Bo abhɛn báfʉɛrɛ fʉɛt, bághaka nyaka arɛ mánte, mámɔk nɛ bati, mánsɔkɔti yi nɛ mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ,
Mpok nnya mbʉ́mbʉ ághɔ́ bɛ básɔt yi báfɛmɛri amɨk, abho bɛkoŋo ngɔrɛ́ anɛ ábhé mɔ́mbakanɛm anɛt.
Kɛ tɛ̌ndu mɛ̌ghàti bhe chí tɛtɛp Mandɛm, bǎpú noko ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ̌rɛ̀m.
Ɛnyu yɔ kɛ ɛ́chí nɛ Bǒ nkwɔ́ Yesu. Yɛ̌ agha anɛ árɔ́ bɛbʉ́ akʉ ntɨ ɛni nɛ́mbak amɛm pɛ́pɛ́p, Mandɛm ǎchyɛ yí kɛnókó. Mandɛm ǎkʉ nɔ nɛ yi, mbɔnyunɛ achyɛ́ nɛpɛ́m ɛni nɛnkɛm ntá Mandɛm mmu áchí mbɔŋɔ́kɛt. Ɛnyǔ mmu wu abhɔŋ ntɨ bɛ́kʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ bɛrɨ.
Bápɔ́kɔ́ yi bápɛtsɛm Shɛ́kɛm, bábhɛ́mɛ ndǔ nnɛm ɛnɛn Ábraham ákú nyaka ntá bɔ Hamɔ amɛm ɛtɔk Shɛ́kɛm nɛ nkáp sílbhá.
Bábhó bɛbhat yi barak amʉɛt mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Sɛghɔ̌, mmǔ-nɛ ndu ákʉ̀ bɛ bǒ bhɛsɛ bákɛ́ bhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé ɛtɔk. Ǎkàŋ nkwɔ bɛ́ bo bákɛ́ chyɛ nkábhɛ́nti ntá Sísa, Mfɔ Rom. Nɛ árɛ̀m bɛ yí achi Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò, nɔ́ chi bɛ achí Mfɔ.”
Ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, apɔp, arɔbhɛ rɔ́ŋɛ́rɔ́ŋ mbɔnyunɛ abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ.
Bo abhɛn báfʉɛrɛ́ fʉɛ́t, bágháká nyaka arɛ mántě, mánka nɛ batí, mánsɔkɔti nɔkɔ yi bɛ, “Aha! Wɔ mmu ɔ́kway mɛmokoti ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm, nɛ ɔ́nte yɔ́ ndǔ manywɔp arat!
Ɛyá ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ ɛ́bɛp ɛcha! Chɔŋ agha ámfɛrɛ mɛ ndǔ bɛtaŋá nkaysi bɛkʉ bɛbʉ́ anɛ átwɔ̀ mɛ nɛ nɛwú?
Ɛ̌ti barak abʉ́abʉ yɔ kɛ Mandɛm ǎbè chɔŋ ntɨ, antɛmsi bho.
Kɛ Yesu kɛka. Aghati yí chí bɛ, “Pɛtnsɛm ntá bǒbhɛ ghati bhɔ ɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛnɛ Mandɛm ákʉ́ ntá yɛ.”
Mbɔk bǒnkwɔ Sádusi bárɔ́k ntá Yesu babhɛp yi ɛ̌ti nɛpɛrɛ́nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Bǒnkwɔ Sádusi bábhɨ́kɨ́ noko nyaka bɛ chɔŋ bawú mámpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Babhɛp yi bɛ,
Mbuɔt anɛ ákwɛ́ntí ndǔ mmɨk sɛtárɛ́bhɛ́ até ndǔ bo abhɛn bághòk Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm, mánoko tɛ́mté nɛ bɛyǎ maŋák. Kɛ bɔ kɛbhɔ́ŋ bakaŋ amɨk. Mánoko chi ndu mɔ́mbɨŋɨ́ mpok. Nɛmɔ nɛtwɔ nɔkɔ, mánkwɛn ansɛm.
Nsɔt yí ndɔk ndu áchá manyé agho wap bɛ́rɨŋɨ ndak anɛ yí akʉ.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mmu wu árɛ́mɛ́ ɛ̌ti bǒ ɛtɔk ɛyi Krɛt ɛ́chí tɛtɛp. Ɔbhɔŋ yɛ bɛghati bhɔ sayri bɛ mándɔ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bhap. Kʉ nɔ bɛ mankɛm Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm nɛ bɛtaŋ,
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, chí ɛbhé ɛnɛ ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “‘Kɔŋ Mandɛm Acha ywɛ nɛ ntɨ ɛnɛ nɛnkɛm, nɛ ɛfóŋó yɛ ɛnkɛm, nɛ nkaysi yɛ nkɛm’.
Chɔŋ mfay amfʉɛt, mmɨk amfʉɛt, kɛ Ɛyɔŋ ɛya ɛ́pú fʉɛt wáwák. 
Bɛyǎ bo abhɛn báchí arɛ bárɛ́m bɛ, “Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́ghati bhɛsɛ bɛ, ‘Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò apú gú. Ndaká yí ɔ́rɛ̀m bɛ chɔŋ mánsɔt mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm mango ndǔ ɛkotákátí? Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm chi agha?’”
Yesu arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ yi? Ɔ̌pay arɛ́ bɛ yi?”
Ángɛl anɛ ájwí batandat apɨkɨri ɛyǐ ɛkwɔp amɛm nyɛ́n nɛgho ɛnɛn bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ Yufretis. Nnyɛ́n nɛ́wɔ́ nɛnkɛm bɛ́ bafɔ abhɛn báfú atú anɛ mmok áfù mambɔŋ mbi bɛkɨŋɨ.
Mmufú achí nyaka ɛtɔk Lístra. Abhak mbɛ́ntí tɛ nɛbhe ɛni.
Ná nɛ bǒ batí nɛku-nɛ-arat abhɛn ɛkɛrɛ́mfáy ɛnɛ ɛchi nɛpak ɛ̌ntɨ́ŋnyɛn Sílom ɛ́kwɛ́nɛ́ ɛ́wáy? Bǎkáysí bɛ́ ɛfákárí nyaka nɛ bhɔ ɛnyu yɔ chí ndu bákʉ́ bɛbʉ́ bacha bo bachak abhɛn bachi ɛtɔk Yerúsalɛm yɔ kɛ?
mbɔnyunɛ, ǎtɔŋ nyaka bakoŋo bhi angati nɔkɔ bhɔ bɛ, “Bákɛ̀m chɔŋ Mmǔ anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm mámfyɛ yi amɔ́ bǒ mmɨk mángwáy yi, nɛ ɛ́ghaka nɔkɔ manywɔp arat ampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.”
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, Mandɛm akʉ bɛ́ Mɔ́ywi ánchá bɔángɛl nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ nnyɛ́n ɛnɛn yi áchyɛ́ yi nɛcha ɛnɛn bɔángɛl.
Ángɛl anɛ ajwi batay afe ayi mmbá. Ngɔ́ nɛmbe ndu nɛ́fú amfay nɛ́kwɛ́nɛ́ amɨk. Báchyɛ nɛmbe ɛnɔ ɛfɨŋɨ́ mɛ́nɛ́nɛ nnyǔ nɛpi ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.
Nɛ mbák mmu ánɛ́m nɛpɛ́m ɛni, ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ yí ákwày bɛsɔt anchyɛ bɛ yi ampɛt ambɔŋ nɔ́?
Ɛwupsi ɛchak ɛchi bɛ, bachiǎkap abhɛn mbɨ baya nyaka nɛ ntí bɛ báchí nyaka bo abhɛn nɛwú nɛ́káŋ bɔ bákɛ́ rɔŋ ambɨ nɛ bɛtɨk ɛbhap.
Bǎkɛ́ cháy bǒ mmɨk. Bákway bɛway chi mmʉɛt nkwǎ. Bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ndu Ɛfóŋó mmu. Mandɛm kɛ̌ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́cháy. Yí kɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ bɛchyɛ mmʉɛt mmu nɛ ɛfóŋó mmu ɛsɔŋɔri amɛm nɛpǐngo.
Arɔk ambɨ bɛkʉ nɔ ndǔ bɛyǎ manywɔp kpát ntɨ nɛ́bé Pɔ̌l, ayibhiri mmʉɛt asáy ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chí ngosɔ́ŋ wu amʉɛt bɛ, “Ndǔ nnyɛ́n Yesu Kristo nchí ghati wɔ bɛ ɔ́mfú yí amʉɛt.” Tɛ́mté wu ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ yɔ ɛ́rɔ́ ngɔsɔ́ŋ wu.
Nchí kʉ nɔ ndak yi? Chi bɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ kɔŋ be kɛ? Wáwák! Mandɛm arɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ nkɔŋ be!
Mmu anɛ bátɔ̀ŋ yi Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm abhɔŋ bɛchyɛ mmu anɛ átɔ̀ŋ yi aywi ákɔ́rɛ́ bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́.
Kɛ Acha akɛmɛ yi chi bɛ, “Matá, Matá! Ɔ̌fyɛ́ ntí nɛ ɔ̌dɛ̀n mmʉɛt ɛ̌ti bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ.
Nɛ́yi nɔ́kɔ́, mbɔk bo Israɛl bákɛ́m ɛchɛmɛ báte ɛyu bɛway Pɔ̌l. Mányú nku bɛ bapu nyiɛ nɛnyiɛ nɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bápú nyu kpátɛ mangway yi.
Mpok Yesu achi fá amɨk, arɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka bɛ Mandɛm abhɔŋ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ nɛwú nɛmfʉɛt yi ansɛm. Anɨkmʉɛt nɛ ntɨ nɛnkɛm kpát ɛyɔŋ ɛyi ɛre ko amfay, babhɛsɛ ansɛp nɔkɔ. Mandɛm aghok nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt ɛni mbɔnyunɛ asɛ́ptí nyaka mmʉɛt, anchyɛ nɔkɔ Mandɛm kɛnókó.
Nchí rɛm nɔ mbɔnyunɛ mbák nchí nɨkmʉɛt ndǔ ɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛnɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ, ɛfóŋó ɛya kɛ ɛ́nɨ̀kmʉɛt ɛnɛ́, ndǔ nkaysi ya, mpú jwimɛm ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ́rɛ̀m.
Mpok yɔ, bǒ-nsé bhɔ bárɛ̀m chɔŋ bɛ nɛbhay nɛbhɨkɨ rɨ, nɛ bɛ́ bo bákɛ́ nyiɛ́ mbɔk mɛnyǔ mɛnyɨŋɨ́nyiɛ, nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛ́n Mandɛm ághókó bɛ́ bo abhɛn mánókó Yesu nɛ bárɨŋɨ nɛtɔ́ŋ ɛ́nɛ́n tɛtɛp mányíɛ́, mánchyɛ nɔkɔ Mandɛm bakak.
Áchwɔ́bhɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ntá Símun Píta, Píta arɛm bɛ, “Acha, ɔ̌yàŋ bɛso bɛkak ɛbha?”
Bɔ́ nɛ Pɔ̌l báfyɛ́ nywɔp nɛ́chák ɛnɛ́n bɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́tɛ́mɛri. Nywɔp ɛnɔ nɛ́kwáy nɔ́kɔ́, bɛyǎ bhap barɔk ɛkɛt ɛnɛ Pɔ̌l áchɔ̀kɔ. Bɛ́bhó bětí kpát bɛ́gháka beku. Pɔ̌l are ghati bhɔ́ ɛnyǔ Mandɛm ábhàk nɛ bo mbɔ Mfɔ wap. Nɛ are tɔ́ŋ bɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti Yesu mbɔ ɛnyu bɛ́chí amɛm basɨ́ŋɨ́ Moses nɛ amɛn barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ, anu nɔkɔ bɛkʉ bɔ́ mánókó mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yí ághàti bhɔ.
mbɔnyunɛ bápú pɛrɛ kway bɛgu. Bábhak mbɔ bɔángɛl Mandɛm, bábhak bɔ̌ Mandɛm abhɛn yi akʉ bápɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.
Báfa yɛ báre rɔ́ŋ amɛm áchwí ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ yɛ̌ mmu achak apu.
Ndi bɛyǎ kɛbhɔ mbɔnyunɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ ghɔ yɛ̌ mmu anɛ ákwáy mɛ́nɛ́nɛ ɛkáti nɛ́nɛ́p ɛyɔ, nɛ yɛ̌ chi bɛpay basɨŋ amɛn achi arɛ́.
Are kʉ ɛnyu ɛyɔ ndǔ mamiɛ́ ápáy kpátɛ̌ Pɔ́síɔ́s Fɛ́stɔs ásɔ́t ɛ́pók ɛyi mbɔ gɔ́bhanɔ. Ndu Fɛ́liks ayaŋ bo Israɛl mámbɔŋ maŋák nɛ yi, arɔ Pɔ̌l ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ.
Ɛchi mbɔ ɛnyu básɨ́ŋɨ́ amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm bɛ, “Ghɔ́ ká! Nchí bhʉrɛ ntay ɛnɛn nɛ́kɛm ɛkɛt fá amɛm ɛtɔk Síɔn, chí ntay ɛnɛn njábhɛ́ nɛ nɛ́rɨ nɛcha. Mmu anɛ ánókó yi, bápú kʉ yi ámbɔ́ŋ ntíánwɔ́p wawak.”
Mǔnkáp wu akók yɛ arɛm bɛ, ‘Ɛta, Ábraham, ghɔ mɛ ntínso. Tó Lásárɔs ántáp sɛnɔŋ awɔ ndǔ manyiɛp antwɔ ankwɛnɛ mɛ ntɨ mandú. Nchí ndǔ bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri amɛm ngó-nɛ.’
Kɛ Yesu ayibhiri mmʉɛt ayɨŋɨ anɛ ngɔrɛ́ wu, arɛm ntá Símun bɛ, “Yɨŋɨ́ mɔ́ngɔrɛ́-nɛ. Tɛ nchwé ɛkɛt ɛyɛ, ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ chyɛ mɛ manyiɛp nsó bɛkak, kɛ yí asó bɛkak ɛbha nɛ babhɛsɛ mi, atɛsɛ nɛ ɛmɛnɛ́nti yi.
Kɛ ɛwak ɛnɛ Yesu ápɛ̀tnsɛm fá amɨk, bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nte-bɛkɛt ákʉ́ bɛ́fù kpoŋoroŋ. Ɛwak ɛyɔ, Mandɛm ǎkʉ̀ ngó ántɔ́ŋ ɛnyǔ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛ́n yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu bɛ́chí.
Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi báfa báre ko bɛrɔŋ Yerúsalɛm, yi ambɨ, bɔ́ ansɛm. Mmʉɛt agú baghɔkɔ́ bhi nɛ bɛcháy bɛ́kɛm bo abhɛn bákòŋo bhɔ. Apɛt asɔt baghɔkɔ́ bhi bati byo nɛ apay nɛpak abho bɛghati bhɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛbhɔŋɔ bɛfakari ntá yi bɛ,
Sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ bɛ́chwé ndǔ barak ɛ́púsí mbɔ ɛnyǔ mbɔk ɛyap bákʉ̀ nyaka, ɛ́kʉ́ nká bo ɛsa nsɛm ɛ́rát () ndǔ nkwɔ́ wap bágú ndǔ nywɔp nɛ́mɔ́t.
Baghɔkɔ́ bhi bábhó bɛkɛm ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ batɨ ndu bɛrɨŋɨ mmu wap anɛ áchá bachak.
Bɛcháy bɛ́kɛ́m baghɔrɛ́ bhɔ tontó. Bátɛ́p bati amɨk. Bǒ-bhɔ bábhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Ndaká yí báyàŋ mmu anɛ achi nɛpɛ́m ndǔ nkwɔ́ bawú?
Ɛnɛ́ yi átàk árɔ̀ŋ, mbɔk akwɛnti ndǔ mɔ́mbi anɛ áchí amɛm nkɨ. Kɛnɛn kɛ́twɔ́ kɛ́bwɔ́pti nchwi yɔ nkɛm.
Kɛ bágháká nɔ́kɔ́ amʉɛt Yesu, bághɔ́ bɛ́ anáŋ agu, bɔ́ kɛsyɛpti bɛkak ɛbhi.
Mpú sɨŋ be bɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ tɛtɛp. Nchí sɨŋ be chi ndǔ bǎrɨŋɨ tɛtɛp nɛ bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ baraká nsé apu fu ndǔ tɛtɛp Mandɛm.
Bě babhɔŋ mǎngɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ basɛ́mɛ́ amɛn Mandɛm akɔŋɔ ákʉ́ ntá yɛka. Nɛ́nɛ, bǎbhɔŋ bɛyǎ ɛkwak bɛ́yíbhiri mɛnyɨŋ. Ɛ́kʉ bǎso amɔ ndǔ ndak anɛ nɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋ bɛyǎ bɛběntɨ́ ɛ̌ti ndak anɛ́ mmu wu ákʉ́ nɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋ bɛcháy ɛ̌ti ndak anɛ áfákárí. Bǎbhɔ́ŋ bɛyǎ ɛkwak bɛghɔ mɛ nɛ bǎyàŋ tontó bɛ mántɛ́msí mmǔ anɛ átwɔ́ nɛ ndak.
Mandɛm apɛ́mɛ́ bhɛsɛ, mpok sɛ́bhàka ntɨ nɛ yi. Mpok sɛ́ghɔ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn sɛ́bhàka ntɨ arɛ́ sɛ́pú pɛrɛ rɔŋ ambɨ bɛbhaka ntɨ arɛ. Agha ákway bɛbhaka ntɨ ndu ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ánáŋ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́?
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka ǎrɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Nchí mǔnkáp, mbɔ̌ŋ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ. Mbɨ́kɨ́ chɛp yɛ̌nyɨŋ.’ Kɛ be bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛ bǎchi ndǔ ɛkwɛt. Bǎchí bo abhɛn mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛghɔ be ntínso, bachí bachɛ́bhɛ́bho, bachí manɛmamɨ́k, bachí bɛbhó bɛwɔ́.
Ɔ́kɛ́ chwe ndǔ bɛpʉítí ɛbhɛn bɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ntí nɛ nnɛt. Mɛnyǔ bɛpʉítí bhɔ bɛ́twɔ̀ chi nɛ bɛ́táŋá.
“Ɛbhé ɛyɛsɛ ɛ́ká bɛ mánchyɛ́ mmu ntɛmsi ɛnɛ́ bábhɨ́kɨ́ re taŋ yi, mándɨ́ŋɨ́ sayri sayri ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ yi ákʉ?”
Nkwɛ́n bɛkak ɛbhi ndǔ bɛchyɛ yi kɛnókó, kɛ aghati mɛ bɛ, “Ɔ́kɛ́ kʉ nɔ wáwák! Mɛ nkwɔ nchí chi nkʉbɛtɨk mbɔ wɔ. Nchí chí ntɨ mmu anɛ nte kpirí ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Yesu ákʉ́ bo bárɨŋɨ. Mandɛm kɛ̌ ɔ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́chyɛ́ kɛnókó.” Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Yesu ákʉ́ bo barɨŋɨ kɛ bɛ́chyɛ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm bɛtaŋ bɛghati bho Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm. 
atwɔ́ nɛ wu amɛm nchán myákátí, barɔk bachyɛ ntá mmɔ̌ Hɛródias. Asɔt, arɔk achyɛ ntá máyi.
Bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu arɛmɛ, bápɔ́p! Bárɔ́ yi, barɔk ɛbhak ɛyap. 
Nɛ mpok sɛ́nɨ̀kmʉɛt sɛ́pú makati mbɔnyunɛ sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ sɛ́nɨ̀kmʉɛt ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ, ǎchyɛ bhɛsɛ yɔ mbák ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ sɛ́yàŋ ɛ́kɔ ndɔ́ŋ amɔt nɛ nkaysi yi.
Bágháká nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ njiɛ anɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ *Ɛ̌nkɔ́nti, bágó Yesu ndǔ ɛkotákátí. Bágó nkwɔ́ bakʉ̌ bɛbʉ́ bhɔ bati apay, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap ndǔ ɛyi ɛkotákátí, amɔt ɛbhě awɔ́nɛm Yesu, achák ɛbhě awɔ́ghɔ.
Yesu arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Kɛ́kɛm mɛ, mbɔnyunɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ re rɔŋ amfay ntá Ɛtaya. Kɛ dɔ́k ntá bɔ̌maya ghatí bhɔ bɛ́ mɛ̌pɛtnsɛm ntá Ɛtaya, nɛ ɛtayɛka. Ntá Mandɛm awa, nɛ Mandɛm aywɛka.”
Mpok ɛyɔ, chɔŋ bo mánti batɨ ntá bǒmpap abhap, nɛ mámbak bo tákátáká, nɛ chɔŋ mánkʉ nɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋ kɛ yambɨ mánsɔt nkaysi arɛ́. Chɔŋ bo mánde yoŋ mmʉɛt nɛ mánkɔŋ mɛ́nyiɛ chi nɛpɛ́m, kɛkɔŋ Mandɛm.
Mpok yi apɛrɛnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, atɔ́ŋ mmʉɛt ntá yap ndǔ bɛyǎ ndɔŋ ndǔ manywɔp bɛsa bɛpay. Bághɔ́ yi kpoŋoroŋ ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ bápú kway mɛmakati bɛ, sayri sayri, apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Apɛt nyaka nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m antɔŋ nɔkɔ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm bɛkʉ bo mándɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛnyǔ Mandɛm ábhák nɛ bho mbɔ Mfɔ wap.
Mbaŋ ákáŋári nɔ́kɔ́, bághɔ́ ngɔkɔnyɛ́n kɛ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk kɛrɨŋɨ mmɨk ɛyɔ. Kɛ bághɔ́ ɛ̌fabhɛ́ nyɛ́n nɛ ɛ̌siɛ́p arɛ, bákáysi bɛ ngufú bákwày bɛ́tɛ́mɛ arɛ́ mámfu mǎnkó ɛbhɨ.
Bě bǒnkwɔ Fárisi, chɔŋ ɛmbɛp ntá yɛka ɛncha! Bǎkɔŋ bɛchɔkɔ ndǔ mɛnɔk kɛnókó amɛm bɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt bo Israɛl, nɛ bǎkɔ̀ŋ bɛ bo mankaka nɔkɔ bhe nɛ kɛnókó nɛfísiɛ.
Bǒ mankɛm bábhák maknkay, nɛ babho bɛbhɛp batɨ bɛ, “Ɛyɔŋ ɛnɛ́ mmǔ-nɛ ɛ́chí nɛ́ ná e? Ǎsay bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ nɛ bɛtaŋ bɛ́ mɛ́mfu bo amʉɛ́t, nɛ mɛ́mfú.”
Bo Israɛl bhɔ báchɛ̀t bhɛsɛ mbi bɛ sɛkɛ ghati bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ Mandɛm ámpɛ́mɛ́ bhɔ. Bákʉ́ bɛbʉ́ kpát mánáŋá. Kɛ bákʉ́ kpát bɛběntɨ Mandɛm bɛchi nɛ bhɔ. 
Bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi tɛtɛp nɛ ɛrɨ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anoko bhɔ́ sayri.
Nnya anɛ ájwí ɛpay akʉ nkwɔ́ bɛ mámfyɛ́ ɛrɨŋ, yɛ̌ ndǔ awɔ́nɛm, yɛ̌ ndǔ nɛfɔ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu. Yí mánkʉ nɔ ntá ndɛ́ndɛmɛ bho nɛ manɛ́m bho, nɛ ntá bǒ bakáp nɛ bachɛ́bhɛ́bho, nɛ ntá bo abhɛn bápu basɛm nɛ abhɛn bachi basɛm.
Apɛt arɛm bɛ, “Chɔŋ nsɨkɨ ntɨ nɛ Mandɛm.” Nɛ bɛ, “Ghɔ́ mɛ́ nɛ́, nɛ bɔ̌ abhɛn Mandɛm achyɛ mɛ.”
Bɛbhé Mandɛm bɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Ɔ́kɛ́ kwɛn bɛrwɔp” nɛ, “Ɔkɛ́ way mmu” nɛ, “Ɔkɛ́ ghɛp aghɛp” nɛ, “Ɔkɛ́ fyɛ amɨ́k ndǔ ɛnyɨŋɨ́ mmu achak.” Ɛbhé ɛ́mɔt ɛ́pɔ́kɔ́ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm nɛ bɛchak nkwɔ. Nɛ ɛbhé ɛyɔ ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Kɔŋ ntɨ nkwǎ mbɔ mmʉɛt ɛyɛ.”
Ɛnyɨŋɨ́ mbɨ ɛnɛ́ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́rɛm ɛchi bɛ: Bághátí mɛ bɛ mpok bǎchɛmti mbɔ bǒ nkwɔ́, bǎkɔ̀rɛ mmʉɛt ndǔ bakwɔ́, mǎnkɛm nɔkɔ ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ batɨ. Nɛ nnókó bɛ́ tɛtɛp achí ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bághátí mɛ́.
Bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Kʉ ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ bɛsɛ sɛ́chɔkɔ nɛ wɔ, amɔt ɛbhé awɔ́nɛm, achák ɛbhé awɔ́ghɔ mpok ɔ́bhak ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ ɛyɛ nɛ kɛnókó.”
Chɔŋ nchyɛ́ ɛyɔŋ bɛ mándɛ́n yi, mámfɛrɛ yi amɔ.” [Ɛpɨŋɨ́ bo Israɛl ɛ́chí nyaka bɛ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ bɔ́ mányìɛ̀ Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ, Páílet abhɔŋ bɛ́fɛ́rɛ mmu amɔt anɛ bǒ Yerusalɛm báyàŋ yi amfɛrɛ ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ.]
Tɛ̌ndu Mandɛm mmu abhɨ́ŋɨ́ bhe achi nyáŋá, be nkwɔ bǎbhɔŋ bɛbhak nyáŋá ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn bǎkù,
Ɛ́tat nɔkɔ, bárɨŋɨ ɛnyu mmu yi áchi. Bápɛtnsɛm ɛtɔk ɛgho bágháti bakoŋo bhi báchák, kɛ yɛ̌ mmu wap kɛ noko bɛ ɛchi tɛtɛp. 
Nɔ chi bɛ bǎkɛ́ nyiɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn nɛfǔ ndʉ̌ akap anɛ́ báchíɛ ntá mandɛm nsé, nɛ bǎkɛ́ nyiɛ́ manoŋ, nɛ yɛ̌ chi nnya anɛ manoŋ ami ábhɨ́kɨ́ rɔŋ amɨk. Nɛ bɛ mǎndɔ́ ɛpúsí. Mbák mǎndɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn, chɔŋ ɛ́mbak ɛrɨ́rɨ́ nɛ bhe. Mǎnchɔkɔ sayri.”
Mbák bo mándɨ́ŋɨ́ Yesu Kristo mmu áchí Acha nɛ Mpɛmɛ ywɛsɛ, nɛ mámbʉɛ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ mmɨk ɛbhɛn bɛ́gwɔ̀t bho gwɔt, kɛ mámpɛt mándɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ mɛngwɔt bhɔ nɛ bɛtaŋ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnap, nte anɛ bɔ bábhák arɛ́ ǎbɛp ancha anɛ bɔ́ bachi nyaka arɛ mpok bábhɨ́kɨ́ re rɨŋɨ Yesu Kristo.
Yesu ásáy nɔ́kɔ́ ɛfóŋó ɛbʉbʉ yɔ, abhɛp mmu wu bɛ, “Nnyɛ́n ɛnɛ bɛ yi?” Akɛmɛ bɛ, “Nnyɛ́n ɛna chi ngɛ́mtáy”; mbɔnyunɛ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛyǎ nyaka yi amʉɛt tontó.
Ɛnɛ́ yi ásɛ̀p árɔ̀ŋ, bǒ bɛtok bhi bátɛ́mɛ́ri yi ambi, baghati yi bɛ, “Mɔ́ywɛ achí nɛpɛ́m.”
Wɔmbɔŋ tɔ́ŋ bɔ́ ɛrɨ́tí ɛpɨŋ. Kʉ nɔ́kɔ́ chí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛrɨ. Mpok ɔ́tɔ̀ŋ bɔ, kʉ mándɨŋɨ bɛ́ ɔ̌chyɛ chi Mandɛm kɛnókó nɛ bɛ ɔ̌kwàk bɔ kwak. Kʉ bɔ́ mándɨŋɨ bɛ ɔ̌kʉ̀ sayri.
Ɛnyɨŋɨ́ mbɨ chi bɛ nchí kaka Mandɛm. Chi Yesu Kristo kɛ ákʉ̀ bɛ ɛmbak nɔ mbɔnyunɛ mmɨk nkɛm aghok ɛ̌ti ɛnyǔ nɛka ɛnɛn bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ Yesu.
Yesu kɛ kɛmɛ yí yɛ̌ ɛyɔŋ. Nɛ bakoŋo Yesu baghati Yesu bɛ, “Bók yi andɔ́k. Ǎchyɛ̀ bhɛsɛ ɛsɔŋɔri.”
Bʉrɛ́ bɛyɔŋ ɛbha sayri bɛ mɛ́nkwak wɔ ɔ́ntɨk ɛnyǔ nɛtɔŋ ɛnɛn tɛtɛp nɛchi. Kʉ nɔ dɔk nɔkɔ chi ambɨ ndu bɛ́bhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Yesu, nɛ ɔ́nkɔŋ bo báchák. Ɔ̌kway bɛ́kʉ nɔ mbɔnyunɛ ɔbhat mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Kristo.
Yesu ágháká nɔ́kɔ́ Bɛ́tani, arɛ́, aghɔ́ bɛ́ mǎnáŋ bábhɛ́mɛ Lásárɔs kpát ɛfʉɛt manywɔp anwi.
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, ɛnɛ́ bɛyǎ bho bápɛt báchɛ̀m nɛbhʉɛt amɔt, Yesu abhɨŋɨ bakoŋo bhi arɛm bɛ,
Ɛ́pú ɛnyu ɛyɔ wáwák! Mbɔ Mandɛm apu chak mbʉ ná yi ákway bɛtaŋ bo?
Arɔk, atɔk nkɔ́k anɛ́ bápɔkɔ ngú arɛ́. Bo abhɛn bápɔ́kɔ́ ngú báte. Yesu aghati ngú wu bɛ, “Ɛsakámu! Nchí ghati wɔ, faté.”
Ɛ́fákari nkúbhɛ́ ɛnyu ɛyɔ bɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ árɛ́mɛ́ nyaka ɛ́mfú tɛtɛp. Ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ arɛm nyaka bɛ,
Mpok Yesu ánáŋá bɛrɛm mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn atú Gálili, afa, apé Nyɛ́n Jɔ́dan, asɛp, arɔk atú Judɛ́ya.
Ɛ́kʉ́, ndu Yesu átɔ̀ŋ bho amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm, arɛm nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ bɛ, “Bǎrɨŋɨ mɛ, nɛ bǎrɨŋɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ mfú? Mbɨ́kɨ́ twɔ ndǔ bɛtaŋ ɛbha. Mmǔ anɛ átó mɛ achí mmǔ tɛtɛp. Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ yi.
Bɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chí ndǔ mpok anɛ, nchí rɛm bɛ́ mmu anɛ áchí ndǔ mmʉɛt mmʉɛt ɛyi, ámbák mbɔ ɛnyǔ áchí.
Nchí rɛm nɔ mbɔnyunɛ mmu anɛ árɛ̀m bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛbhɛn yi abhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ, apú rɛm mɛnyɨŋ ntá bho, ǎrɛ̀m chi ntá Mandɛm mbɔnyunɛ yɛ̌ mmu apu jwimɛm ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ̀m. Ǎrɛ̀m chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛyɨŋɨ Mandɛm nɛ bɛchi bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́, ndǔ bɛtaŋ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm.
Ɛnɛ́ Apólos áchí Kɔrint, Pɔ̌l are kɔ atú Esia. Akɔ kpát aghaka Ɛ́fɛsɔs. Atɛmɛri mpay bakoŋo Yesu arɛ́.
Nkwɔ ɛchɛmɛ bǒbati ɛtɔk bapɛt básɛ́mtí nɔ́kɔ́ bhɔ, báfɛrɛ bhɔ amɔ. Bɔ́ kɛbhɔŋ mbi bɛtɛmsi bɔPíta mbɔnyunɛ bǒ mankɛm bákàka nyaka Mandɛm ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛfakari.
Njɨkɨ ndǔ bɛběntɨ bɛ, ‘Bápú kway bɛchwe ndǔ nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt ɛna wáwák.’”
Kɛ bárɔ́k ambɨ bɛbɨk bɛ, “Dɛm mángó yi ndǔ ɛkotákátí! Mángó yi ndǔ ɛkotákátí!”
Ǎtwɔ̀ bɛchyɛ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ ntá bo abhɛn bachi ndǔ ɛjuri nɛ ndǔ bɛcháy nɛwú, nɛ ndu bɛya bhɛsɛ́ ndǔ mbi anɛ átwɔ̀ bhɛsɛ nɛ kpák.”
Bɔ agha bághókó nyaka Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm yɛ̌ nɔ, bátáŋ ntɨ? Pú bo Moses abhɛn yi áfú nyaka ɛtɔk Íjip nɛ bhɔ?
Bɛyǎ bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛn bǎghɔ̀ ɛ̌ti Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ mɛ́mbák ndɛ́ndɛmɛ́? Mbɨ́kɨ́ ka bɛ bɛchi nyaka chi ndɛ́ndɛm.
Ɛ́tárɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, Júdas mmu Gálili nkwɔ afú mpok básɔ̀t mpǎy bho. Aya mbɔk bho báré koŋo yí. Yi nkwɔ agú, nɛ bɛyǎ bo abhɛn bákòŋo nyaka yi bátáka.
Bɛfʉɛt ndǔ manoŋ Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n nɛ ndǔ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ baghati bho, bɔ̌mayɛsɛ mánu nɛ yi basɔt awɔ́nɛm. Báka nyaka bɛchyɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnap nkwɔ.
Arɛm yɛ ntá yap bɛ, “Yɛ̌ agha anɛ ásyɛpti mandú mmɔ́ mbɔ anɛ nɛ maŋák ndǔ nyɛ́n ɛnɛ, ǎsyɛpti mɛ́; nɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ ásyɛpti mɛ nɛ maŋák ǎsyɛpti mmu anɛ átó mɛ. Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ mmu ywɛká anɛ ásɛ̀pti mmʉɛt ntá abhɛnɛfu, kɛ áchí mǔngo sayri sayri ntá yɛka mankɛm.” 
Yesu arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Mmá, nɛka ɛnɛ̌ nɛ mɛ nɛ́kʉ ɔtaŋ. Mandɛm áchí nɛ wɔ, dɔ́k sayri, kɛ́pɛrɛ chay.”
Tɛ̌ndu mpú makati nyaka wáwák bɛ chɔŋ mǎnsɨkɨ ntɨ nɛ mɛ, mbɔ̌ŋ nkaysi bɛyambɨ bɛ́twɔ awu ntá yɛka bɛ maŋák bɛghɔ mɛ ámbák nɛ bhe ndɔŋ ɛpay.
Símun akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Ɛta, sɛ́dɛn mmʉɛt bɛti mɛnkɛm kɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ kɛm. Kɛ ndu bɛkoŋo ɛyɔŋ ɛyɛ, chɔŋ ngʉɛp básɨ ndǔ ɛɛntɛm.”
Pɔ̌l apɛt arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Bɔ̌ma, bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ Ábraham, nɛ beká bo bɛtɔk bɛ́chák abhɛn báchày Mandɛm, chi ntá yɛsɛ kɛ Mandɛm átó yɛ ntó ɛnɛ́n nɛ́ghàti bhɛsɛ ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ yi akway bɛpɛmɛ bhɛsɛ!
Yesu aghati yi bɛ, “Tɛtɛ̌tɛp, Mandɛm apú kway bɛbhak ntá mmu mbɔ Mfɔ ywi, kpátɛ mámbe yi ndɔŋ achak.”
Mfɔ andɛm yɛ ntá bo abhɛn báchi ɛbhe awɔ́nɛm ywi bɛ, ‘Twɔ́ ká fá, be bhó Ɛtaya áyɛ́rɛ́! Twɔ́ ká mǎmbak nɛbhʉɛt anɛ Mandɛm achí nɛ bo abhɛn yi achi Mfɔ wap. Yí ághókó nɛbhʉɛt wu chi ntá yɛka tɛ nɛbhǒmɨk.
“Bɔ̌bha, bǎkɛ́ chay, yɛ̌ndu bǎchi nkwɔ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n anɛ abhɨkɨ ya. Mandɛm abhɔŋ maŋák bɛchyɛ be akɔrɛ ndǔ kɛfɔ ɛki.
Mpok mǎnaŋ bǎchyɛ mmʉɛt ɛnkɛm ntá Mandɛm, chɔŋ sɛ̌ntoŋti mmʉɛt bɛ́tɛ́msi yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ anɛ átaŋntí nɛ Kristo.
Kɛ, amɛm ɛkáti ɛnɛ, nsɨ̌ŋ ntá yɛka nkɛbhɔŋ bɛcháy ɛ̌ti mbɔk mɛnyɨŋ mbɔnyunɛ nchí yaŋ bɛ́tɨ́k be bhɔ. Nsɨ̌ŋ ɛnyu ɛyɔ ɛ̌ti bɛyǎ bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm ntá ya.
Ntí anɛ Mandɛm átàŋ bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ noko Mɔ́ywi chi bɛ́ ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛ́twɔ fá amɨk kɛ bo bákɔŋ ɛjuri bácha ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́, mbɔnyunɛ barak abʉ́abʉ kɛ bɔ bákʉ̀.
Mmu wu abhat mmʉɛt nɛ Píta nɛ Jɔ̌n kpát bárɔk baghaka amɛm nɛbhʉɛt ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm anɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ Áchá Sólomon. Bo mankɛm bare rɔŋ arɛ ntiɛ́t ntiɛt bɛghɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fàkari. Babhak maknkay tontó.
Mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ batú, ángók ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm ághàti bákwɔ́ bo Kristo.”
Yi kɛ bo mankɛm bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́chyɛ́ kɛnókó ngwɛnti ti. Amen. 
Ɛ́chí wɨkɨrɨk bɛ mpɔŋɔ baso ámfʉɛ́t ndǔ mbok mbíábhan ɛ́cha mǔnkáp bɛ́ka Mandɛm ambak Mfɔ ywi.”
Ɛ́chí ɛnyu yɔ mbɔnyunɛ mbák bawú bapu pɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, nɔ Mandɛm abhɨ́kɨ́ kʉ nyaka Kristo ampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.
“Ghók ká, sɛ́rɔ̀ŋ nɔ chi Yerúsalɛm, nɛ mpok sɛ́gháká arɛ́, chɔŋ mánti Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm, mánsɔt yi mamfyɛ amɔ bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ ntá batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses, mándɛm bɛ mangway yi, mámfyɛ yi amɔ́ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl.
Ndǔ bǎkʉ nɔ, bǎsɔt bɛpɨŋ ɛbhɛn bachǐmbɨ bhɛka bɛbyak Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm. Nɛ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ bɛchak ɛbhɛn bǎkʉ bɛ́chí mbɔ ɛbhɔ.” 
Kɛ tɛ̌ndu Kristo achi nɛ bhe, yɛ̌ mmʉɛt ɛyɛka agǔgú ɛ̌ti bɛbʉ́, bɛfóŋó ɛbhɛka bɛchi nɛpɛ́m, mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm ákʉ́ bǎchi chak bɛsí bhi.
Ɛ́chí sayri bɛghɔ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛ̌ti ɔ́kʉ̀ bɛrɨ mbák nɔ kɛ Mandɛm áyàŋ, ɛcha bɛbhɔŋ ɛsɔŋɔri nɛ ntí bɛ ɔ̌kʉ̀ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ.
Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mmʉɛt nkwǎ átò mmu ankʉ bɛ́pú bhɛsɛ. Bɛchi chi bɛbʉ́ kɛbhʉ́rɛ́, nɛ bɛpɔ̌ nkaysi ndu baraká kɛbhʉrɛ nɛ mɛ́ŋwáka ndǔ baraká kɛbhʉrɛ.
Bárɔ́k ambɨ ɛnyuyɔ ndǔ bɛtɔk nɛ bɛtɔk kpát bákɨŋɨ ɛtɔk nɛntɨnyɛn Sáyprɔs ɛyɔ ɛnkɛm báchwɔp Pafɔs. Bátɛ́mɛri mmu Israɛl arɛ́ anɛ achi mǔnjɔ kɛ ǎpù bapu bɛ́ achí ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm. Aka nnyɛn bɛ́ Ba-Jesus.
Mbák mmu asɔt mmʉɛt yi mbɔ mmu Mandɛm kɛ yí kɛkɛ́m nɛ́rɨ́ ɛni, nɔ́ ǎrwɔ́ chi mmʉɛt nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ yí ákʉ̀ mbɔ mmu Mandɛm ǎchɔŋti chí mpok.
Tɛ́mté wu Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ abhak nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap tontó. Akʉ́ bábhó bɛ́rɛ́m bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛbhɛn bɔ babhɨkɨ ghɔk.
Nkʉ-bɛbʉ́ amɔt anɛ áchi nkwɔ́ kpaŋkpáŋ ndǔ ɛyǐ ɛkotákátí are way Yesu andɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Pú wɔ kɛ ɔ́chí Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò? Pɛmɛ́ mmʉɛt ɛyɛ, ɔ́mpɛmɛ bhɛsɛ́ nkwɔ bhɔ!”
Bɛbʉ́ kɛ bɛ́chyɛ̀ nɛwú bɛtaŋ. Bɛbhé Mandɛm kɛ bɛ́chyɛ̀ bɛbʉ́ bɛtaŋ.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ákʉ́ bɛbʉ́ nɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ ghaka ndǔ nte anɛ Mandɛm ághókó nyaka yi ambak.
Mmǔ achak arɛm bɛ, “Acha, chɔŋ nkoŋo wɔ, kɛ dɔ̌ kpɨ́k ndɔ́k anywɔ́p ndyɛ́p bǒbha.”
Bachɛ́bhɛ́bho báchí nɛ bhe mpoknkɛm. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ mmu ákɔ́ŋɔ́, ánkwák bhɔ. Kɛ mpú bhak chɔŋ nɛ bhe mpoknkɛm.
Yɛ̌ agha anɛ áyòŋ mmʉɛt, Mandɛm ǎsɛ̀pti yi amɨk. Nɛ mmu anɛ ásɛ̀pti mmʉɛt amɨk, Mandɛm ǎkòsi yi amfay.”
Amɨ́k ánɛ́nɛ bhɔ, bárɨ́ŋɨ yɛ bɛ chi yi. Kɛ anɛmsi bhɔ́ bɛsí.
Kɛ ɛwak ɛnɛ Mandɛm átàŋ bǒ mmɨk, chɔŋ angɔ́ ntínso nɛ bǒ-Taya nɛ Sídɔn ɛncha bhe.
Ntwɔ̌ ndǔ nnyɛ́n Ɛtaya, nɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ sɔt mɛ mbɔ mmu. Mbɔ mmu achák kɛ átwɔ́ nɔ́ árɛ̀m ɛ̌ti ndu mmʉɛt yi nɛ ndǔ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi mbʉ bǎsɔ́t yi mbɔ mmu ywɛka.
Bo abhɛn bachi arɛ bábhák maknkay tontó ɛ̌ti ɛnyu ɛnɛ yi átɔ̀ŋ. Ǎtɔ̀ŋ nyaka mbɔ mmu anɛ árɛ̀m ɛ́may, puyɛ̌ mbɔ batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses.
Ɛ́rɨ bɛ bɛsɛ bakoŋo Yesu bho sɛ́náŋ sɛ́sɛ́nɛ́ ndǔ mbi Mandɛm, sɛ́mbɔ́ŋ nkaysi amɔt ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn. Nɛ mbák mmu achí anɛ ayi nkaysi achi nyáŋá, chɔŋ Mandɛm ankʉ yí angɔ bɛ nkaysi ya ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn achi ɛrɨ́tí nkaysi.
Ndǔ ɛ́chí nɔ́, yɛ̌ mmu apú kwáy bɛ́panyu bɛsí Mandɛm.
Mɔ́wú agó ataŋ ndǔ nkwɔmʉɛt nɛ ndǔ Ɛfóŋó. Bɛchɔ́kɔ́ bhi bɛbhak amɛm baso, anoŋ nɔkɔ nywɔp ɛnɛ́n yi átɔŋ mmʉɛt ntá bo Israɛl.
Mbák mmu apú yɨŋɨ bǒbhi, sayri sayri bǒ nnɛrɛ́kɛt ywi, nɔ apú pɛrɛ koŋo nɛtɔ́ŋ ɛnɛn tɛtɛp. Ɛnyǔ mmu wu abɛp achá mmu anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ noko Yesu wáwák.
Ɛbhak ɛnyu yɔ kpatɛ mmu achak abhak Mfɔ Íjip anɛ abhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ nyaka Josɛ́f.
Nchí yaŋ bɛfyɛ bhe ntɨ, ndǔ bǎgwɔ́rɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ batɨ ndu ɛkɔŋ. Nchí yaŋ bɛ be mankɛm nɛ bhɔ mǎnjwimɛm sayri ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm ákʉ́ sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛ̌ti Kristo, bɛ mǎndɨŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti Kristo ɛbhɛn bɛchi bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ nɛ bɛ́kʉ̀ mǎmbɔŋ bɛyǎ áfɔ́k ndǔ bákòŋo mbi ywi.
Nchí rɛm ɛnyunɛ́ nɛ ntí bɛ, bǎkway bɛchyɛ bhɛsɛ́ ɛsɔŋɔri bɛ́ sɛ́twɔ́ nɛ ɛbyɔk ɛtɔk ɛnyu ɛnɛ́, mbák mámbɛ́p bhɛsɛ́, sɛpu bhɔ́ŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ sɛ́rɛ̀m.”
Mbák mmu ǎyàŋ bɛkʉ manyé nɛ wɔ bɛ ánsɔ́t nkú yɛ, kpɨk chyɛ̌ yi ndɛ yɛ nkwɔ.
“Sɔt ka mpok bɛ́ bǎkɛ́ fyɛ ntí ndǔ mɛ́nyiɛ nɛnyíɛ́ tontó, bǎkɛ́ fyɛ ntí ndu mmɛ́m nɛ bǎkɛ́ bhɔŋ basɛ́mɛ́ ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nɛpɛmɛ́ mmɨk ɛnɛn. Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́kway bɛkʉ bɛ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛtwɔ́ ɛna nɛ́mbák tɛ́mchok ntá yɛka ndǔ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ toŋti mmʉɛ́t, nɛ nɛ́mbayti bhe mbɔ ntá.
Báká yɛ bɛ yi anchwe amɛm áchwí. Nɛchwe yi áchwé, áchwí arɔk atɛmɛ angɔkɔnyɛ́n, ndǔ nɛchyɛ̌nyɛn ɛnɛn bɔ́ bárɔ̀ŋ arɛ́.
Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ bǎbhɔŋ ɛkwak bɛkwak nɛ ngátí nkwɔ Kristo abhɛn atú Masidónia ɛ̌ti yɛka ndɛp nɔkɔ awɔ antɨ bɛ běka bɔ̌mayɛsɛ mankɛm abhɛn atú Akáiya mǎnaŋ bǎtoŋti mmʉɛt ndu bɛchyɛ nɛkwak tɛ mmíɛ́ ɛyu. Nɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn bǎfyɛ̀ ndǔ ndak anɛ ndu mɛ́nyɨ́kɨ́si batɨ̌ bɛyǎ bhap bɛ mántóŋtí awap akabhɛ́ nkáp nkwɔ.
Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt bo Israɛl, arɔk ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí, abho bɛtɔŋ bo Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm. Bɛyǎ bho bábhák arɛ́. Bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi átɔ̀ŋ, bɛyǎ bhap bábhak maknkay. Ɛ́kʉ báré bhɛp bɛ, “Aré fú fá nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm? Ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak nɛ́ báchyɛ́ yi? Ná yi ákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛbhɛ́n?
Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bo abhɛn básábhɛ́ nɛkɔ nɛ Mandɛm bátɔ̀ŋ bɛ́chí mbɔ nsak ntá bo abhɛn bɔ́ bátɔ̀ŋ, nɔ chí, mbɔ nsak anɛ ányiɛ mmʉɛt andɔk nɔkɔ chi ambɨ. Himɛ́neɔs nɛ Filɛ́tɔs báchi mɛnyǔ bo bhɔ.
Bátwɔ́ nɛ batísyɛ ákwárɛ́ abhɛn bárɛ́mɛ́ bɛ, “Mmǔ-nɛ apú rɔ bɛrɛm ɛbʉ́bʉ mpoknkɛm ɛ̌ti ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm ywɛsɛ́ nɛ nɛ ɛ̌ti ɛbhé Moses.
Mbɔk bo Israɛl nɛ abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl báchɛ́m nɛ bǒ batí bhap báká ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt bɛ mánchyɛ bǒnto Yesu ɛsɔŋɔri nɛ bɛ mantɛmti bhɔ nɛ batay mángwáy.
Nchyɛ́ yí mpok bɛ ántɨ́knsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhi, kɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ ka bɛtɨknsɛm ndǔ barak ɛpúsí yi.
Chɔŋ bakǒsiɛ mándɛm ntá bǒbhɔ bɛ, ‘Bɛrɨ́tɨ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ɔ́kɔ́ŋ nyaka bɛrɔŋ mɛnkɛm. Mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn bɛ́kʉ̀ nyaka wɔ ɔ́ndɨ́ bɛsí bho bɛ́chɔŋɔ nɛ kɛnɛ́m ɛkɛ kɛnkɛm kɛnɛ́m. Ɔpú pɛrɛ kway bɛghɔ bhɔ wáwák.
Mpok Mandɛm akʉ yi ámpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, kɛ̌ bakoŋo bhi bátɨk bɛ yi arɛm nyaka bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn. Ɛ́kʉ́ bɔ mánóko mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm nɛ ɛbhɛn Yesu árɛ́mɛ́. 
Bo báré chyɛ nnya mbʉ́mbʉ kɛnókó mbɔnyunɛ yɔ́ achyɛ́ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi ntá nnya mbémbé yɔ. Báre chyɛ kɛnókó ntá nnya mbémbé mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Agha áchí mbɔ nnya mbémbé nɛ? Agha ákway mɛnu nɛ yɔ́?”
Nɛ nsoŋo Yesu akɔ ataka atú ɛtɔk wu ankɛm. 
Kɛ mbák chí mǔnkáp ámbɔ́ŋ maŋák chí bɛ́ Mandɛm asɛ́ptí yí, akʉ yi ángɔ́ bɛ́ áchí nchɛ́bhɛ́ mmu bɛsí Mandɛm. Nchí rɛm nɔ mbɔnyunɛ bǒ bakáp báfʉɛ̀t mandú mpok mbɔ bɔchuchu ndu tákɔ. Bábhak sayri, kɛ mandú mpok mángu.
Abhɛn ɛkɔŋ, ɛbhé ɛnɛ mɛ́sɨ̀ŋ ntá yɛka nɛ́nɛ ɛ́pú ɛbhé ɛkɔ. Chí nkúbhɛ́ ɛbhé ɛnɛ bǎrɨŋɨ tɛ mpok anɛ bǎbho bɛkoŋo Yesu. Ɛbhé ɛ́rɛ́ chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mǎnaŋ bǎghókó nɛ batú.
Yɛ̌ mmu kɛghati yi nkaysi bǒbhɔ mbɔnyunɛ yímbɔŋ arɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka ndǔ ntɨ̌ nkwǎ nɛchi amɛm.
Nɛ Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Mɛnkwɔ́ mpú ghati yɛ be mmu anɛ áchyɛ́ mɛ́ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nɛ́ mɛ̌kʉ̀.” 
Ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ ntó yi ntá yɛka bɛ ankʉ mǎndɨŋɨ ɛnyu sɛchi, nɛ bɛ ámfyɛ́ be ntɨ.
Nɛ ndu bɛ́rɔŋ ambɨ, mpok bɔtáyɛsɛ abhɛn fá amɨ́k báchyɛ̀ bhɛsɛ ntɛmsi ndǔ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ ɛbhɛn sɛ́kʉ̀, sɛ́chyɛ̀ bhɔ kɛnókó, ná nɛ Ɛtayɛsɛ anɛ amfay? Sɛ́bhɔŋ bɛchyɛ yi mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛfóŋó ɛbhɛsɛ kɛnókó ɛncha, nɛ chɔŋ sɛ́mbɔŋ nɛpɛ́m.
Ɛkɛrákap mandɛm nsé Sús ɛ́chí nyaka nɛfí bɛfʉɛt nkok ɛtɔk. Nchiakap mandɛm nsé Seus asɔt manɛ́m mpɔŋ nɛ bɔchuchu abhɛn mánɨ́ arɔk antí ɛtɔk mbɔnyunɛ yí nɛ ngɛ́mtáy bhó abhɛn báchi arɛ báyàŋ nyaka bɛchyɛ akap ntá Banábas nɛ Pɔ̌l.
Tɛtɛ̌tɛp, “Mmu anɛ asɨkɨ ntɨ nɛ mɛ, ǎkway bɛ́kʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ̌kʉ̀. Ǎkwáy bɛ́kʉ yɛ̌ chí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chá ɛbhɛn, mbɔnyunɛ mɛ̌rɔ̀ŋ ntá Ɛtaya.
Kaká ká nkwɔ batɨ̌ bo Israɛl bha, Androníkɔs nɛ Júnias bo báchí nyaka ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ nɛ mɛ. Báchí manɛ́m bo ndǔ nkwɔ bǒnto Yesu Kristo nɛ báyámbɨ bɛbhak bakoŋo Kristo kɛ mɛ̌twɔ ansɛm.
Yɛ̌ ɛ́mbak bɛ yi, mɛ̌tee kpɨrí ɛ̌ti bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn Yesu áchyɛ̀ mɛ.
Bǎbhɨ̀ŋɨ mɛ bɛ, ‘Ntɔŋ’ nɛ ‘Acha’ nɛ ɛ́chí tɛtɛp. Nchí Ntɔŋ nɛ Acha ntá yɛka.
Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Mpok Ábraham abhɔ̌ŋ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm, Mandɛm asɔt bɛ yi achi chak bɛsí bhi.”
Yesu arɛm yɛ ntá yap bɛ, “Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm kɛ̌ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛrɛm ɛnyǔ mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ nɛ ɛbhé ɛnɛ ɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ́ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt.” 
Jɔ̌n akɛmɛ bhɔ́ bɛ, “Mɛ̌jwìti bhe nɛ manyiɛp. Kɛ mmu anɛ acha mɛ ǎtwɔ̀. Mbɨ́kɨ́ kwáy mmu anɛ nchí kaŋari nkwɔbhɛ́nya bɛkak ɛbhi. Ánáŋ ántwɔ́, chɔŋ anjwiti bhe nɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ nɛ ngó.
Sɛ́ghàti bo chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi tɛtɛp. Bɛtaŋ Mandɛm bɛ́chi nɛ bhɛsɛ. Sɛ́chí chak bɛsí Mandɛm nɛ ɛyɔ ɛchi mbɔ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ nɛnu ɛbhɛn bɛ́kwàk bhɛsɛ sɛ́nu nɛ bǒmpap abhɛsɛ, sɛ́nchɛt bɔ mbi bɛbhɔŋ bhɛsɛ.
Nɛ mmu anɛ achi ɛbhɨ ákʉ̀ bɛtɨk, ákɛ́ rɔ́ŋ kpɨ́k anywɔ́p ndu bɛbwɔp ndɛ yi.
Nkúbhɛ́ mpok ɛyɔ Josɛ́f nɛ María bárɔk nɛ mmɔ́. Ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ mɔ̌rɛ́, achyɛ bakak ntá Mandɛm andɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti mmɔ́, ntá bo abhɛn mánòŋ nyaka bɛ Mandɛm amfɛrɛ bǒ Yerusalɛm ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri.
Sɛ́chí ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri, yɛ̌ nɔ, sɛbhɔŋ maŋák mpoknkɛm. Sɛ́chí amɔ apay, yɛ̌ nɔ sɛ́kʉ̀ bɛyǎ bo bábhɔ̀ŋ bɛyǎ áfɔ́k. Ɛchi mbɔ bɛ sɛ́bhɨkɨ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ, yɛ̌ nɔ, sɛ́bhɔŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ.
Mǔngo batɛmɛ́ nɛnu akɛ́m yi nɛ achyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ́ mámfé yi nɛ ngɛm ɛpay. Abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Mmǔ-nɛ chi agha? Akʉ yi?”
Bárɔ́bhɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, mǔbɛtɨk anɛ yí áchyɛ́ bɛbhǎ nkáp bɛtay abho bɛkɔ ɛsiɛ nɛ wu tɛ́mté. Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, abhɔ́ŋ nsáy bɛbhǎ nkáp bɛ́chák bɛtay.
Arɛm nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, arɔ bhɔ́ apɛt achwe amɛm áchwi, are pé bɛ́rɔŋ ɛbhě manyu ɛ́chák. 
Ntɨk yɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu Acha árɛ́mɛ́ nyaka bɛ, ‘Jɔ̌n ǎjwiti bo nɛ manyiɛp, kɛ chɔŋ mánjwiti bhe nɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ.’
Josɛ́f áŋɛ́mɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ kɛnɔ́, akʉ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ ángɛl Mandɛm aghati yi. Asɔt María ndǔ nɛbhay.
Batɛmɛ́ nɛnu nkwɔ báré way Yesu, mándɔkɔ nɔkɔ bɛchyɛ yi mmɛ̌m amɛn ábáká.
Bɛyǎ bho báfú atú Judɛ́ya ankɛm, nɛ bǒ Yerúsalɛm mankɛm mándɔk nɔkɔ ntá Jɔ̌n ndu bɛghok ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ̀m. Báré su bɛbʉ́ bhap, Jɔ̌n anjwiti nɔkɔ bhɔ amɛm Nnyɛ́n Jɔ́dan.
Sɔt nɔ́kɔ́ yɛ́ ka yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ntɨ mǔnkwɔ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Kristo ásɔ́rɛ́ bhe. Ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ̀ bo mánchyɛ́ Mandɛm kɛnókó.
Bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm bárɔ́k bábwɔ́pti nkáp wu, bárɛ́m bɛ, “Nkáp anɛ chí nkáp manoŋ nɛ ɛbhé ɛyɛsɛ ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ ka bɛ mánchɛ́m nkáp manoŋ nɛ anɛ́ ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm.”
Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛ́ ɛwak ɛ́mɔ́t, chɔŋ bɛsɛ bo Mandɛm sɛ́ntàŋ bɔángɛl? Bǎrú bɛkpɨ́kɨ́ri abhɛn bǎbhɔ́ŋ nɛ batɨ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛ́n fá amɨk kɛ̌ báchá be bɛ́táŋ?
Bɔ mankɛm, manɛ́m bo nɛ ndɛ́ndɛ́mɛ́ bho bare tá batú bɛghok mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ághàti bhɔ, mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Mmǔ-nɛ chi mmu Mandɛm anɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ Ɛtaŋtǐ mʉ.”
Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Mbɔ Mandɛm achi ɛtayɛka, mbʉ bǎkɔ̀ŋ mɛ, mbɔnyunɛ mfú chí ntá Mandɛm. Mbɨ́kɨ́ twɔ́ chí ndǔ mmʉɛt ya, yi kɛ átó mɛ.
Be bábhɔŋ, ghɔ́ yɛka! Mandɛm achyɛ́ bǒbhɔ nkúbhɛ́ akap anɛ́ yi achyɛ́ nyaka bhɛsɛ mpok sɛ́nókó Yesu Kristo Acha. Nchí yɛ́ nyaka agha bɛchɛt Mandɛm mbi?”
Yí nkwɔ agú, kɛbhɔŋ mmɔ́ nɛ kɛ́nkwɛ́sɛ́ wu. Ɛ́fákari ɛnyumɔt nɛ anɛ ájwí bati arat, nɛ bɔ̌mayi bachak nkwɔ.
Sɛ́chwe áchwi anɛ árɔ̀ŋ Troas. Sɛ́rɔk téé sɛ́gháká Samótras, ɛtɔk ɛnɛ́ nnyɛ́n nɛ́kábhɛ́. Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ ntɨnywɔp, sɛ́gháká Neápolis.
Arɛm nyaka ntá Moses bɛ, “Nchí ghɔ ntínso nɛ mmu anɛ mɛ̌yaŋ bɛghɔ yi ntínso, ntɔŋ bɛrɨ̌ntɨ ntá anɛ mɛ́yaŋ bɛtɔŋ bɛrɨ̌ntɨ.”
Mandɛm kɛ ákʉ́ bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm mɛ́mbák ɛnyu ɛyɔ. Yí kɛ átó Kristo ánkʉ sɛ́mpɛ́tnsɛm ntá yi, nɛ achyɛ́ bhɛsɛ bɛtɨk bɛkʉ bo mámpɛ́tnsɛm mámbɔŋ kpák nɛ Mandɛm.
Bɔ̌ma, mɛ̌yáŋ mǎndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́fákárí nɛ mɛ fá, ɛ́kwak Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu ándɔ́k chí ambɨ.
Bɛ́bhó amʉɛ́t Ábraham bɛghaka amʉɛt Debhít, mkpák bachǐmbɨ Kristo ɛ́chí yɛ nyaka byo nɛ ɛnwi. Bɛ́bhó amʉɛt Debhít bɛghaka mpok bápɔ́kɔ́ bo Israɛl bɛ mándɔ́k mánchɔ́kɔ́ ɛtɔk Bábilɔn, ɛ́bhák byo nɛ ɛnwi. Bɛ́bhó mpok bo Israɛl bárɔ́ Bábilɔn bápɛtnsɛm ɛtɔk ɛyap, bɛ́chúɔp mpok Kristo, Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò, mkpák bachǐmbɨ Yesu ɛbhak byo nɛ ɛnwi. 
Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mmʉɛt nkwǎ áŋwaka bɛ bo mankʉ bɛ́pú kɔ ndɔŋ amɔt nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ áyàŋ bo mankʉ, nɛ ɛnyumɔt kɛ ɛchi bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ áyàŋ bo mankʉ bɛ́pú kɔ ndɔŋ amɔt nɛ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mmʉɛt nkwǎ áŋwaka bɛ mmu ankʉ. Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛpay bɛpu kɔ ɛkak ɛ́mɔt, nɛ ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ bǎpú kway bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ ntɨ bɛkʉ.
Manyǔbhá abhak arat. Árát ábhak ɛbhě ɛnɛ mmok áfu, arat ɛbhě mmok ánɛ̀m. Árát abhak ɛbhě mfay, árát anɛfu ábhak ɛbhě ntɛn.
Gɔ́bhanɔ abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka ɛpɨŋ bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmíɛ́, ndǔ mpok Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ, ǎfɛrɛ mǔkɛnɔŋ amɔt anɛ bo báyàŋ yí ámfɛ́rɛ́.
Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mbɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́ghati bǒ abhɛn bárɛ̀m bɛ mɛmpú mǔnto Yesu chí bɛ
Mfɔ Agripa, pú ɔnókó ɛnyɨŋ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ básɨ́ŋɨ́? Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ ɔnókó!”
Bǎkɛ́ rɔ barak abʉ́abʉ ambɔŋ bɛtaŋ amfǎy yɛka. Kʉ nɔ́kɔ́ ká chi bɛrɨ bɛ, mǎmbɔŋ bɛtaŋ amfǎy barak abʉ́abʉ.
Nɛ bǎrɨŋɨ sayri bɛ mǎnyurɛ bɛchɨŋtǐ bho nɛ bɛ bǎtɔ̀ŋ bo abhɛn báchí mǎmbɔ ndǔ mbi Mandɛm mbɔnyunɛ bǎkàysi bɛ ɛbhé ɛ́kʉ bǎrɨŋɨ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ nɛ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ be tɛtɛp nkɛm.
Yi ǎrɛ̀m mbɔ ɛnyǔ básɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ, “Mpok ákwáy nɔ́kɔ́ bɛtɔŋ be bɛrɨ̌ndu, ngók nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt ɛnɛka, nywɔp bɛ́pɛ́mɛ bho nɛkwáy nɔkɔ, nkwak bhe.” Ghók ká, nɛ́nɛ chi mpok anɛ Mandɛm áyàŋ bɛtɔŋ be bɛrɨ̌ndu, nɛ́nɛ chi mpok anɛ Mandɛm áyàŋ bɛpɛmɛ bhe.
“Mmǔ achi amɛm baso ǎbɨ̀k andɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ́, ‘Toŋtí ká mbi anɛ Acha áfʉɛ̀t arɛ́. Kʉ́ ka mbi ywi ambak chak.’”
Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́ghàti bhɛsɛ́ bɛ, “Ɔ́kɛ́ gwɔt nnyǔ mpɔŋ bɛ́ ákɛ́ nyiɛ́ nchwi mpok yɔ ákʉ̀ bɛtɨk amɛm nkɨ̌ nchwi.” Ɛ́pɛt ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Nkʉ bɛtɨk abhɔ̌ŋ ngǎngaŋ bɛ mánchyɛ yi akap.”
Kɛ sɛ́ghɔ̀ Yesu mmu bákʉ́ bɔángɛl máncha yi ndǔ mɔ́mbɨŋɨ mpok. Báchyɛ́ yi kɛnɛ́m nɛ kɛnókó mbɔ mfɔ ɛ̌ti ɛsɔŋɔri nɛwú. Chi ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm kɛ yi ágú ɛ̌ti bo mankɛm.
Bǎbhɔŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ndu mbi Mandɛm bǎcha. Bǎbhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Yesu ɛrɨ́rɨ́. Bághàti bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu sayri. Bǎrɨŋɨ tɛtɛp Mandɛm. Bǎchyɛ́ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛka nɛnkɛm ndu bɛkʉ bɛtɨk Mandɛm nɛ bǎkɔŋ bhɛsɛ tontó. Kʉ yɛka nkwɔ bɛtɨk ndu bɛchyɛ nɛ bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhɛn bɛya bɛcha.
Kɛ Mandɛm ánáŋ ánkʉ́ mpɛ́tnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, chɔŋ njambɨ atú Gálili, mǎntɛmɛri mɛ arɛ́.’”
Abho nyaka mbɔ ɛnyǔ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Aisáya ásɨ́ŋɨ́ amɛm ɛkáti yi bɛ, Mandɛm arɛm nyaka bɛ, Yɨŋɨ́, chɔŋ ntó mpɔkɔntó wa wɔ ambɨ, bɛ ángókó mbi ywɛ kɛ ɔ́ntwɔ. ✡
Mmu anɛ ákʉ̀ bɛrɨ ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛcháy bǒbati. Bo abhɛn bákʉ̀ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ bábhɔŋ bɛbhɔŋ bɛcháy. Mbák ɔ̌yàŋ bɛ ɔ́kɛ́ bhɔŋ bɛcháy nɛ bǒbati, bák mmǔ anɛ ákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi chak. Mbák ɔ̌kʉ̀ nɔ, bǒbati bábhɔ̀ŋ maŋák nɛ wɔ.
Mandɛm anɛ, apɛrɛ́ chyɛ mmu ɛnyɨŋ, ǎchyɛ kɛrɔ mbɔk ansɛm, achyɛ bɛsɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ tontó bɛfʉɛt ntá Mɔ́ywi, Yesu Kristo Mpɛmɛ ywɛsɛ́,
Ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ̀ bɛ yɛ̌ mmu akɛ ji bhe nɛ bɛ bǎkɛ́ bhɔŋ bakwap bɛsí Mandɛm. Ɛ́kʉ nkwɔ bɛ be bɔ̌ Mandɛm abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ nɛ́ntɨ́ bǒ abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛpɔ̌ bɛpɨŋ, mǎmbák mbɔ bɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ ntá yap.
Kɛ bɛ́koŋo bariɛp Mandɛm, sɛ́nòŋ mfay nkɔ nɛ mmɨk nkɔ. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ábhákántɨ arɛ́, ǎbhak chak bɛsí Mandɛm.
Báre kɛm ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ batɨ bɛ, “Chɔŋ sɛ́ndɛm bɛ yi? Mbák sɛ́ndɛm bɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn Jɔ̌n bɛ́fú nyaka ntá Mandɛm, ǎbhɛ́p bhɛsɛ bɛ, ‘Kɛ ndaká yí bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ noko ɛyɔŋ ɛyi?’
Bɔ̌ma, ndǔ nnyɛ́n Yesu Kristo Acha, nchí nɨk be mmʉɛt bɛ́ mǎndɔ́ bɛ́kɛm kɛfě nɛ batɨ, mǎmbák ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt. Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ rɨ́ bɛ ákɔ́rɛ́ ámbák nɛ́ntɨ́ ɛnɛká. Nchí nɨk be mmʉɛt, bák ká ntɨ nɛ́mɔ́t, mǎnkoŋo nɔkɔ chi nkaysi amɔt.
Bo abhɛn báchi fá nɛ mɛ bátó wɔ bakak. Kaká bǒ nkwɔ́ abhɛn bákɔ́ŋ bhɛsɛ́ nɛ manoko ɛnyumɔt mbɔ bɛsɛ. Mandɛm ántɔ́ŋ bé bɛrɨ̌ndu.
Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Tɛtɛp, chɔŋ mǎnyú nkɔ́p ɛsɔŋɔri anɛ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛnyu, kɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ bɛyap bo abhɛn babhɔŋɔ bɛchɔkɔ ɛbhe awɔ́nɛm ɛya nɛ abhɛn babhɔŋɔ bɛchɔkɔ ɛbhe awɔghɔ. Bɛbhak ɛbhɔ bɛchi ntá bǒ abhɛn Ɛtaya aghoko bhɔ́ ábhʉ́rɛ́ ntá yap.”
Batɨ ábé bhɔ mbɔnyunɛ Píta nɛ Jɔ̌n bátɔ̀ŋ mángati nɔkɔ bo bɛ́ Yesu apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m bɛtɔŋ bɛ chɔŋ bawú mámpɛtsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.
Kɛ ngáti bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́ mpok anaŋ ánkwáy anɛ bɔ bɛ́fàkari, mǎntɨk bɛ nnáŋ ngátí bhe. “Mbɨ́kɨ́ ghati bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mpok bǎhó bɛkoŋo mɛ mbɔnyunɛ nchí nyaka nɛ bhe.
Ɛ̌tiyɔ, kɛ Mandɛm, ndǔ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛni, árɛ́mɛ́ bɛ ‘Chɔŋ ntó barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ nɛ bǒnto bha ntá bo Israɛl; nɛ chɔŋ mǎngwáy mbɔk ɛyap, nɛ mánchyɛ abhɛ́nɛ́fú bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri.’
Jɔ̌n aghati bhɔ mbɔnyǔ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Asaya arɛmɛ nyaka bɛ, “Nchí mmǔ anɛ achi amɛm baso ábɨ̀k nɛ ɛyɔŋ amfay andɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, ‘Nyabhɛ́ ká mbi Acha ambak chak.’”
“Ɛbhé Moses ɛpɛt ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Yɛ̌ agha anɛ árɔ ngɔrɛ́ ywi ndǔ nɛbhay, abhɔŋ bɛchyɛ yi ɛkáti ndu bɛtɔŋ bɛ awǎy nɛbhay.’
Bɔ̌ma, be bho bǎchi nyáŋá, mmu anɛ achi amfay abhɨ́ŋɨ́ be bɛ mǎmbak bǒbhi. Kaysí yɛ ka mmu anɛ Yesu achi. Yi kɛ Mandɛm átó mbɔ mǔngo bachiǎkap anɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛ́bhɛn sɛ́nókó, mbɔnyu sɛ́ghàti bho kpoŋoroŋ.
Mmu anɛ áká bɛtok mɛ, abhɔŋ bɛ́kóŋo mɛ. Nɛ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ mɛ̌bhák, arɛ́ kɛ̌ nkʉbɛtɨk awa ábhák nkwɔ. Mbák mmu ántók mɛ, Ɛtaya ǎkʉ yi ambɔŋ kɛnókó.” 
Ɛnɛ́ bo báchák báchɛ̀m arɛ́ mándɔk nɔkɔ chi ambɨ, Yesu abho bɛrɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Mkpáká bho anɛ ɛchɔŋ ábɛp acha! Bábhɛ̀p bɛ mántɔ́ŋ bhɔ́ ɛrɨŋɨ́ maknkay. Kɛ yɛ̌ ɛmɔ́t mpu tɔŋ bhɔ, ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ fʉɛt ɛnɛ Jóna.
Mpok yi aghaka mamiɛ́ byo nɛ apay, bárɔ́k ndǔ ɛpǎ ɛyɔ mbɔ ɛnyu ɛsɨ́.
Mmok ásɔ́ŋ bǒ mbɔ ngó, Yɛ̌ nɔ bɔ kɛtɨ́knsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhap. Bɔ́ kɛka bɛchyɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó ɛ̌ti kɛnɛ́m ɛki. Báre rɛm chi ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti Mandɛm mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ amfǎy bɛghori ɛbhɔ.
Anɛ ɛkɔŋ, ɔ́kʉ̀ bɛtɨk Mandɛm ɛrɨ́rɨ́ ndǔ ɔ́kɛ̀m bǒnkwɔ ɛrɨrɨ, sayri sayri, abhɛn bachi mankɔ.
Píta arɛm bɛ, “Ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛso mɛ bɛkak wáwák.” Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Mbák mbɨ́kɨ́ so bɛkak ɛbhɛ, nɔ mɛmay nɛ wɔ sɛ́may.”
Báchyɛ yi mbɨŋɨ́ nsi anɛ bágwɔ́.
Sɛ́ghok ndǔ yi árɛ̀m bɛ chɔŋ Yesu Mmǔ Násárɛt wu amokoti ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm ɛnɛ, nɛ angupsi bɛpɨŋ ɛtɔk ɛbhɛn Moses árɔ́ ntá yɛsɛ.”
Ndǔ ngwɛnti, ngɔrɛ́ wu nkwɔ agú.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Nnáŋ ngáti bhe, kɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ noko. Bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn mɛ̌kʉ̀ ndǔ nnyɛ́n Ɛtaya bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ be ɛnyǔ mmu nchí.
Puyɛ̌ ndiɛrɛ nɛtwɔ Táytɔs kɛ Mandɛm ásɔ́rɛ́ bɛchyɛ bɛsɛ nɛpɔptǐntɨ́. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛchak ɛ́chí bɛ bǎchyɛ́ Táytɔs nɛpɔptǐntɨ́ mpok yi achi awu nɛ bhe. Ágháti mɛ ɛnyǔ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛkwak bɛ ntwɔ́ awu, nɛ ɛnyǔ batɨ ábè bhe amɛm nɛ áyɔ́mɛ. Apɛt aghati mɛ ndǔ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ ntɨ tontó bɛte nɛ mɛ. Ɛ́kʉ́ maŋák ama apɛt aya acha.
Kɛ mmǔ wa anɛ achi chak ǎbhak chɔŋ nɛpɛ́m ndu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛka nɛ mɛ. Kɛ mbák ánjá mmʉɛt ansɛm, mpú bhɔŋ maŋák nɛ yi.
Ndǔ ngwɛnti, mbɔŋɔ́nkɨ arɛm nɛ mmʉɛt yi bɛ, ‘Chɔŋ ntó mbɔŋ mɔ́wa. Yɛ̌ yí, bábhɔŋ bɛ́chyɛ yi kɛnókó.’ Afɛrɛ yɛ mɔ́ywi ató.
Yɛ̌ mmu apu kway bɛghɔ Mandɛm. Mɔ́ywi kɛ ákʉ́ sɛ́njwimɛm ɛnyu Mandɛm achi. Nɛ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ mɔ̌mbɨ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt, nɔ kɛ Mɔ́ywi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ amfǎy mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn Mandɛm ághókó.
Abraham achi nkwɔ chi-mbɨ ntá bǒ abhɛn basyɛp bhɔ mbák bákòŋo bayarɛ́kak yi ndu babhɔŋɔ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi áchi nyaka yɛ̌ chi ndu mpok anɛ babhɨkɨ re syɛp yi. 
Ɛ́bhɔŋ bɛbhak ɛnyu ɛyɔ bɛ Satan ákɛ́ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ amfay yɛsɛ. Bɛsɛ́ babhɔŋ sɛrɨŋɨ nkaysi yi. 
Bɔ́ bághók ndǔ yi árɛ̀m chí ɛyɔŋ bo Israɛl. Mbǎŋ akwɛn chák. Pɔ̌l arɔk yɛ ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ,
Ɛyɔŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́rɛ́mɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyu yɔ, baghɔk Yesu baghɔ bɛ yi arɔp chi aywǐnti. Báchók manyu kɛ ghati yɛ̌ mmu ndǔ manywɔp yɔ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛbhɛn bɔ baghɔ. 
Tɛ̌ndu mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ̌kʉ̀ chi ɛbhɛn mbɨ́kɨ́ kɔŋ bɛkʉ, ɛyɔ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ nká bɛ ɛbhé chi ɛrɨ́tí ɛnyɨŋ.
Ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ ɛchi nɛ bhɛsɛ. Yɛ̌ndu sɛ́yá, sɛ́chí mbɔ mmʉɛt amɔt mbɔnyunɛ sɛ́chɛm mmʉɛt nɛ Kristo. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu achi nɛ batɨ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛpókómʉɛt ɛchi nɛ bɛchak.
Mɛ nɛ Ɛtaya sɛ́chí mmu amɔt.”
Mpoknkɛm anɛ nchí fá amɨk, nchí ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ ntá bǒ mmɨk.”
Yɨŋɨ́ ká bo Israɛl, báwày nnya mánchyɛ mbɔ akap ntá Mandɛm. Pú bo mankɛm abhɛn mányìɛ̀ nnya yɔ báchɛ̀m mmʉɛt nɛ Mandɛm amfay ɛfɛmɛ akap ndǔ akabhɛ wu?
Ɛgháká nɔ́kɔ́ manywɔp ánɛn, básyɛp mɔ́, bádu yi nnyɛ́n bɛ, Yesu, nnyɛ́n ɛnɛn ángɛl arɛmɛ nyaka bɛ babhɔŋ bɛchyɛ yi tɛ mpok babhɨkɨ re pɔkɔ́ mɛniɛ ɛbhi. 
Kɛ bɛti mɛ́mɔt, bakoŋó Sɔl basɔt yi báfyɛ́ amɛm ɛkay bákʉ yi áfʉɛ́t ndǔ mbok anɛ́ áchi ndǔ nkok anɛ ákábhɛ́ ɛtɔk, básɛ́bhɛ yi amɨk ansɛm ɛbhá. Abʉɛ́. 
Bǒ Ɛ́fɛsɔs bhɔ bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, báka bájwíti bhɔ mbɔ bo abhɛn mánóko Yesu Acha.
Mbák sɛ́nsu bɛbʉ́ bhɛsɛ ntá Mandɛm, ǎfoŋori bhɛsɛ, nɛ amfɛrɛ bɛsɛ́ bɛbʉ́ antɨ, ankʉ sɛ́mbak pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí bhi. Yí apú nɔ́k bɛbhʉrɛ bariɛp ami, nɛ ndiɛrɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi chak kɛ̌ yi ákʉ̀.
Bakoŋó Jɔ̌n bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fákári, bárɔk basɔt ɛrɛnɛ́ Jɔ̌n, barɔk babhɛmɛ. 
Dɨŋɨ́ bɛ Acha ǎnyurɛ mmu anɛ yi akɔŋɔ, nɛ ǎtɛmsi yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ anɛ yí ásɔ́rɛ́ bɛ mɔ́ywi.”
Mbɔŋ Mandɛm kɛ̌ ákʉ́ sɛ́mbák bo abhɛn sɛ́kwày bɛ́bhɔ́ŋ mmʉɛt nkɔ yɔ. Achyɛ́ bhɛsɛ́ Ɛfóŋó ɛyi mbɔ nkɛm bɛ́ chɔŋ anchyɛ bhɛsɛ mmʉɛt nkɔ yɔ nkwɔ tɛtɛp.
Nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɔ́tó mɛ fá amɨk, nɔ́ kɛ̌ nchí to bhɔ amɨk.
Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Sɔt ka mpok nɛ yís anɛ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi,   mǎnsɔt mpok nɛ yís anɛ bǒnkwɔ Sádusi.”
Ngɔrɛ́ wu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ nnɛ́m.” Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Ɔrɛm tɛtɛp bɛ́ ɔbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ nnɛ́m.
Ndɛn ɛyi nkwɔ ɛ́ré diɛrɛ pɛ́pɛ̌pɛ́p ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ yɛ̌ mmu ápú kwáy bɛso ndɛn yɛ̌ chí nɛ babhé ɛ́ndiɛrɛ ɛnyu yɔ.
Mmǔ wu abhɔŋ bɛtɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́, ándɔ́bhɛ kʉ chi bɛrɨ, ánú bɛbhak kpák nɛ bho, andɔk ambɨ bɛkʉ nɔ.
Bǒbha mankɛm chí abhɛ, nɛ abhɛ chí abha. Nɛ bɔ́ kɛ̌ nɛpɛ́m ɛnap nɛ́kù bo mángɔ́ kɛnókó ɛka.
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Bǎrɛm bɛ́ yi ɛ̌ti ndak anɛ? Mmu amɔt achi nyaka nɛ bɔ̌bhi bati apay. Bábhák bɔ̌ babhakanɛm. Ɛwak ɛ́mɔt abhɨŋɨ anɛ mbɨ aghati yi bɛ, ‘Mɔ́wa, dɔ́k kʉ́ bɛtɨk amɛm nkɨ ɛchɔŋ.’”
Tɔmás akɛmɛ yí bɛ, “Acha nɛ Mandɛm awa!”
Ɛ́náŋ ɛ́mfákárí ɛnyu ɛyɔ, Mandɛm ǎpɛmɛ bo Israɛl mankɛm. Ɛchi mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Chɔŋ mmu amfú ɛtɔk Síɔn anɛ ǎfɛrɛ bo Mandɛm ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri. Chɔŋ yi amfɛrɛ ɛpɨŋ bɛ́byak Mandɛm amʉɛt bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ Jekɔ́p.”
Chɔŋ mánkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛchi bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ ɛmfu kpoŋoroŋ. Nɛ chɔŋ mánɛnɛ ɛnɛ bákútí.
Lɛ́vi mmɔ̌ Símiɔn, Símiɔn mmɔ̌ Júda, Júda mmɔ̌ Josɛ́f, Josɛ́f mmɔ̌ Jónam, Jónam mmɔ̌ Ɛliákim,
Chɔŋ bo mámbɔŋ bɛcháy kpátɛ mbɔk mámfe ndu bárɨŋɨ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́bhó bɛfakari fá amɨk. Chɔŋ bɛtaŋ mfáy mɛ́nyɨkɨsi.
Bɛsɔŋɔri bɛchak bɛ́chí kɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ yaŋ bɛrɛm ɛ̌ti bɛsɔŋɔri yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛwak. Puyɛ̌ chi ndiɛrɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn. Mbɔ̌ŋ bɛyǎ basɛ́mɛ́ bɛyɨŋɨ ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ běka bakwɔ́ Kristo bǎchi.
Kɛ mbák sɛ́bháká ntɨ ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ sɛbhɨkɨre ghɔ́, sɛ́rɔŋ ambɨ mɛnoŋ yɔ nɛ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ́.
Mandɛm Ɛtayɛsɛ ayap be tɛsáy bɛkoŋo nkaysi anɛ yi ánáŋ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka ɛ̌ti yɛka. Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ákú mǎmbák nyáŋá bɛ mǎmbák bo abhɛn bághòk Yesu Kristo nɛ bɛ ansɔt manoŋ mi ánkʉ mǎmbák pɛ́pɛ́p. Mandɛm ántɔ́ŋ be bɛyǎ bɛrɨ̌ndu, anchyɛ be kpák tontó tonto. 
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ̌yáŋ bɛkʉ mǎndɨ́ŋɨ́ chí bɛ bǎchí ndǔ bakwɔ́, bǎbhák bɛyɔŋ bɛyɔŋ. Mbɔk ayɛká bárɛ̀m bɛ, “Bákòŋo chí Pɔ̌l”, báchák bɛ, “Mɛ̌kòŋo chí Apólos”, abhɛ́nɛ́fú bɛ, “Mɛ̌kòŋo chí Píta”, nɛ nkwɔ́ áchák bɛ, “Mɛ̌kòŋo chí Kristo”.
Bárɛm bɛ, “Ɔ̌bhokori!” Kɛ arɔk chi ambɨ bɛ́gháti bhɔ bɛ́, “Chí Píta tɛtɛp.” Afɔ̌ kɛ barɛmɛ bɛ, “Chi ángɛl aywi.”
Kɛ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm bábhɨ́kɨ́ ka nyaka bɛ Jɔ̌n anjwiti bhɔ. Ɛnyu ɛyɔ, bábyak nkaysi anɛ Mandɛm abhɔŋɔ nɛ bhɔ.
Bɔ̌ma, nɛ́nɛ, bɛyɨŋɨ mɛnyǔ akap anɛ́ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ áchyɛ̀, mbɨ́kɨ́ yaŋ mǎmbák ndǔ ɛjuri.
Ɛrástɔs arɔp ɛtɔk Kɔ́rint. Ndɔ́ Trofímɔs ɛtɔk Milɛ́tɔs mbɔnyunɛ ǎme.
Bǒ abhɛn báchí nyaka amɛm bɛtɔk ɛbhɛn Yesu ákʉ́ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay, bábhɨ́kɨ́ tɨ́k nyaka nsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhap. Ɛ́kʉ Yesu abho bɛji bhɔ andɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ,
Běti, ɛnɛ Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi báfʉɛ̀t bɛpɛtnsɛm, bághɔ ɛnɔk fig ɛnɛ́ Yesu arɛmɛ bɛ́ ɛpu pɛrɛ kwáy mɛ́nyu kɛpɛm, ndu ɛ́náŋ ɛ́gú tɛ nɛ bakaŋ.
Mpok Yesu áchwɔ́bhɛ́ Gálili, bǒ Galili básɔt yi nɛ maŋák ndu bághɔ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ákʉ́ Yerúsalɛm mpok bárɔ́ŋɔ́ arɛ ndǔ Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ. Bɔ́ nkwɔ bárɔŋ nyaka ndǔ ɛpǎ yɔ.
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Yɛ̌ agha anɛ ányù manyiɛp amɛn, apú rɔ bɛ́bhɔŋ ɛkwaká manyiɛp.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Mbák bǒ mmɨk bápap bhe, dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ báyambɨ bápap mɛ.
Yɛ̌ nɔ, bɛbʉ́ bɛ́bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ amfǎy bo mankɛm bɛbho mpok Adam kpát bɛghaka mpok Moses, nɛ yɛ̌ chi bo abhɛn bɛbʉ́ bhap bɛpu nyaka mbɔ ɛbhɛn Adam mmu ákwɛ́nɛ́ ɛbhé Mandɛm abhak mbɔ anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka bɛ́twɔ. Kɛ apɛt abhak kɛkúrí nɛ mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́twɔ.
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, mpok Mandɛm ákʉ̀ bawú mámpɛ́tnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, ngɔrɛ́ wu ǎbhák anɛ agha? Ndu bɔ́ mankɛm, bati tándrámɔt, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap abhay nyaka yi.”
Abhɛn ɛkɔŋ, Mandɛm apɛ́mɛ́ bhe. Bǎghók yɛ ɛnyǔ Kristo ásɛ́ptímʉɛt bɛsí Mandɛm. Bǎghók nyaka mɛ mpok nchí nɛ bhe. Nɛ́nɛ, ndǔ mpɛ́t mpú nɛ bhe, bǎkɛ́ gʉɛ́p ɛyɔŋ ɛyá ɛbhɨ. Ghók ká mɛ ɛ́nchá ɛnyu ɛsɨ́. Nu ká bɛkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎkwáy bɛkʉ ndu bɛ́chyɛ́ Mandɛm kɛnókó nɛ batɨ ayɛká ankɛm. Ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ̀ bɛ́ Mandɛm ámbɔ́ŋ mbi bɛkʉ bapɛm ayɛka ambak mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi áyàŋ.
Yɛ̌ mmu abhɨ́kɨ́ re ghɔ Mandɛm. Njaŋamɔ ywi mmu achi nɛbhʉɛt amɔt nɛ yi kɛ ákʉ́ bo mandɨŋɨ mmu yi achi. 
Mandɛm arɛm bɛ, ‘Chiɛ́ ɛ́táyɛ nɛ máyɛ kɛnókó’ nɛ bɛ ‘Yɛ̌ agha anɛ árɛ̀m ɛbɛ́ptí ɛyɔŋ ntá ɛtayi, yɛ̌ máyi, bábhɔŋ bɛway yi.’
Bɛsak báchwe, mánɛ́p yi nɛ ndɛn, bápɔ́kɔ, barɔk babhɛmɛ.
Mbák ɛ́chí tɛtɛp bɛ bawú bapu pɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, nɔ́ Kristo abhɨ́kɨ́ pɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.
Píta arɛm ntá Yesu bɛ, “Acha, ɔ́kɛ́ so chi ndiɛrɛ bɛkak ɛbha, sǒ amɔ́ ya nɛ ntí wa nkwɔ!”
Bɔ̌ma, ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́chák chi bɛ mǎnɨk nɔkɔ mmʉɛt ɛ̌ti yɛsɛ bɛ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu Acha antaka ayak nɛ bɛ́ bo abhɛn bághòk yɔ mánsyɛpti yɔ nɛ kɛnókó, mbɔ ɛnyu ɛ́fákárí nyaka nɛ bhe.
Josɛ́f asɔt yɛ Yesu anɛ́p nɛ ɛ́síɛndɛn nkɔ.
Nɛbhě ɛnɛn nkwǎ chi nɛbhě nkwɔmʉɛt, kɛ nɛbhě Ɛfóŋó chí ɛnɛn nɛ́fú ntá Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm.
Acha abhak nɛ bhɔ́, akwak bɛyǎ mánoko bábho bɛkoŋo mbi ywi.
Bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ Mandɛm bachi maknkay bɛ nɛ́nɛ, bǎpú pɛrɛ chɛm mmʉɛt nɛ bhɔ ndǔ ɛpɔ̌ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɔ. Ɛkʉ bɔ bárɛ̀m bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti yɛka.
Ghɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ̀ sɛ́ndɨŋɨ bo abhɛn bachi bɔ̌ Mandɛm nɛ abhɛn bachi bɔ̌ Satan nɔ. Yɛ̌ agha anɛ ápú kʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi chak bɛsí Mandɛm apú mmɔ́ Mandɛm. Ɛchi ɛnyumɔ́t nɛ mmǔ anɛ abhɨkɨ kɔŋ ntɨ. 
Bɛyǎ bo Samaria abhɛn báfú ɛtɔk mánóko Yesu ɛ̌ti nɛrɛm anɛ ngɔrɛ́ wu arɛmɛ bɛ, “Aghátí mɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ nkʉ́ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛna.”
Mpú sɨ́ŋ be mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn chí ndu bɛkʉ ntíánwɔ́p ánkɛ́m bé ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎkʉ. Nchí sɨ́ŋ chí bɛ́chyɛ́ be maníɛ́ mbɔnyunɛ bachí bɔ̌bha abhɛn nkɔ́ŋɔ́ tontó.
Yɛ̌ nɔ, Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Mmu atɔk mɛ. Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ nɔ mbɔnyunɛ ngók ndǔ bɛtaŋ bɛ́fú mɛ amʉɛt.”
Ɛ́chí tɛtɛp bɛ́ mmʉɛt nkwǎŋwaŋ abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ chi ɛ́pókómʉɛt ɛ́mɔt. Abhɔ̌ŋ bɛyǎ bɛ́pókómʉɛt.
Ɛsɔŋɔri ɛ́yá kpát sɛ́rɔ́bhɛ noŋ chi nɛwú. Kɛ ɛfakari nyaka nɔ chi bɛkʉ sɛ́ndɨŋɨ bɛ sɛ́pú kwáy bɛkwak mmʉɛt ɛyɛsɛ. Sɛ́ghɔ́ bɛ́ sɛ́bhɔŋ bɛsɨkɨ ntɨ nɛ Mandɛm mmu ákwày bɛkʉ bawú mampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.
Bɛfóŋó bɛpay ɛbhɛn bághókó mbo bɔángɛl bɛbhak amfay ɛkʉbhɛ yɔ. Bɛbhap ɛbhap mɛ́nyábhɛ amfay nɛbhʉɛt anɛ Mandɛm áfoŋori nyaka bɛbʉ́ bho arɛ. Kɛ sɛ́pú kway bɛrɛm yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nɛ́nɛ.
Hɛ́rɔd ásɔ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ Hɛródias ndǔ nɛbhay, Jɔ̌n aré ghati yi bɛ, “Ɛbhé ɛyɛsɛ bo Israɛl ɛbhɨkɨ ka bɛ ɔ́mbay Hɛródias ngɔrɛ́ mɔmáyɛ.”
Ndu bárɔ̀ŋ arɛ, Píta are koŋo bhɔ tɛ ansɛm, kpát aghaka ndǔ sɛnta Mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm. Achwe arɛ́, arɔk achɔkɔ nɛ bo abhɛn bábhàbhɛri sɛnta wu, anoŋ nɔkɔ bɛghɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bákʉ̀ chɔŋ ntá Yesu.
Ɛta, mbɔ ɛnyǔ mɛmbɔ̌ŋ nkwɔ́ nnáŋ nkóŋó mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm sayri ndǔ ɛrɔri mpok, nkáysí bɛ́ ɛrɨ bɛ nsɨŋ ngati wɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mɔt ɛ́mɔt ɛnyu ɛfakari.
Mpok bo bárɛ̀m bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti yɛsɛ́, sɛ́kɛ̀mɛ bhɔ́ chí nɛ ɛyɔŋɔ́ ɛkɔŋ. Sɛ́rɔp chi kɛbí bɛsí bǒ mmɨk. Kpát tɛ̌ ɛchɔŋ, sɛ́rɔp chi mbɔ mɛ́nyɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛbhɛn mányɔ́ bɛto ndǔ ɛbhwɔ́rɛ́ mɛnyɨŋɨ́.
Kɛ Mandɛm aghati yi bɛ, ‘Wɔ ɛchɨŋtɨ́mu! Nkúbhɛ́ bɛti ɛbhɛn, nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛ nɛ́may. Kɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n ɔ́bhʉ́rɛ́ bɛ́rɔ̀p chɔŋ chi ɛbhɛn bo bachak!’
Yesu arɨŋɨ nkaysi yap. Abhɛ́p bɔ́ bɛ, “Ndaká yí bǎkàysi mɛnyǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ?
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu achi amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm, ayɨŋɨ aghɔ́ ndǔ bǒ bakáp báfyɛ̀ akap amɛm ɛkʉbhɛ́ nkáp.
Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ mámfyɛ́ bho ndǔ bakwɔ́, mánkʉ bɔ manchɔkɔ amɨk ndu tákɔ.
Mbák yɛ̌ mmǔ ywɛka abhɔŋ mɛnyǔ bɛkpɨ́kɨ́ri ɛbhɔ, ákɛ́ sɔt bɔ bɛsí bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ kɛnókó bɛsí bǒnkwɔ Yesu bɛ́ mántáŋ bɔ́.
Ɛ́bhak ɛnyu ɛyɔ bɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Aisáya árɛ́mɛ́ tɛntɛp bɛ́ chɔŋ ɛ́mfakari, ɛ́mfú tɛtɛp. Nɔ chí bɛ, “Ɛta Mandɛm, agha ánókó ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ sɛ́gháti bhɔ? Agha ághɔ́ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛ?”
Nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu abhɔŋ bɛrɛm kpoŋoroŋ bɛ chi Yesu Kristo kɛ achi Mfɔ bo mankɛm. Chɔŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́nkʉ bɛ bo mánchyɛ́ Mandɛm Ɛtayɛsɛ́ bakak nɛ kɛnókó. 
Bo abhɛn bachi arɛ́, báfɛ́rɛ ndɛn mfǎmʉɛt ɛyap baghay ambi. Báchák báré kpɔt bɛ́wuɔ́kɛ́ndé mángay nɔkɔ ndǔ mbi anɛ yí áfʉɛ̀t arɛ. Báchák báré kpɔti kɛfɛ́bhɛ́ ɛkɛn kɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛyé mángay nɔkɔ ambi.
Nnɨk nyáka Táytɔs nɛ mɔmáyɛsɛ bɛ mántwɔ́ awu ntá yɛka. Átwɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ asɔt mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛka ndǔ ngwáy kɛ? Mɛ nɛ Táytɔs sɛ́bhɔŋ chi nkaysi amɔt. Pú nɔ́? Bɛsɛ nɛ yi sɛ́bhɔŋ chi ɛkakánɛkɔ ɛ́mɔt. Pú nɔ́?
Awu áfʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, ngɔ́ nnya mbʉ́mbʉ ndu áfù amɛm manyu. Abhɔ́ŋ bati tándrámɔt nɛ babhaŋ byo nɛ bɔ̌ntǎ-kɛfɔ byo ndu babhaŋ ayi. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ntí ywi ábhɔ́ŋ nnyɛ́n ɛnɛn nɛ́rɛ̀m ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti Mandɛm.
Kɛ nɛ́nɛ, ǎtɔ́ŋ bo bɛ yi achi chak nɛ ǎkʉ̀ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ abhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Yesu ambak chak bɛsí bhi.
Ápáy nɔ́kɔ́ ɛkáti yɔ, abhɛp Pɔ̌l bɛ, “Ayɛ̌ atú ɛtɔk chi anɛ?” Pɔ̌l akɛmɛ yí bɛ, “Silísha.” Ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ,
Sayri sayri, nsěnse chi agha? Chi mmu anɛ abhɨkɨ ka bɛ Yesu chi Mpɛmɛ anɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò. Ɛnyǔ mmu wu kɛ achi mǔmpap Kristo. Ábhɨ́kɨ́ noko Ɛta nɛ Mmɔ.
Nywɔp Ɛpǎ Brɛt anɛ kɛbhɔŋ yís yɔ, baghɔk Yesu bárɔ́k ntá yi bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ɛta, sɛ́ndɔ́k sɛ́ntóŋtí ɛbhak ɛnɛ ɔ́nyìɛ Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ fá?”
Arɛ́, ngɔ́ bɛ́ abhɨkɨ kʉ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́yàŋ bɛ mángwáy yí, nɛ yɛ̌ chi ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ̀ mámfyɛ yi amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ. Báre rɛm chi barak anɛ ayɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛbhé bhap.
Yesu abhɛ́p bo abhɛn bátwɔ bɛkɛm yi bɛ, “Bátwɔ bɛkɛm mɛ nɛ bɔakparɛnja nɛ nkɨ́k mbɔ bɛ nchí ngɛ́bhɛ́ ntantaŋ?
Bárɔ́k ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ́ Golgóta, nɔ́ chi “Nɛbhʉɛt Ɛnkɔ́nti.”
Nɨk nɔkɔ ká mmʉɛt bɛ Mandɛm ankwak bo abhɛn bárɛ̀m ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti yɛka.
Bǎtwɔ́ ntá Yesu mmu áté nɛntɨ Mandɛm nɛ bǒ mmɨk kɛ Mandɛm anyú nku nkɔ nɛ bhɔ. Bǎtwɔ́ ndǔ manoŋ Yesu amɛn yi amyakati be amʉɛt.   Manoŋ mi atéé ndu ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́rɨ́ ɛchá ɛnɛ́ manoŋ Ábɛl atee ndu ntí ywi.
Yesu akɛmɛ yi nɛ nɛkay ɛnɛn bɛ, “Mmǔfu afǔ nyaka ɛtɔk Yerúsalɛm ǎsɛ̀p Jɛríko. Ndu árɔ̀ŋ, akwɛ́n amɔ baghɛ́p bataŋataŋ. Báfɛ́rɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ yí amʉɛt, bádɛ́n yí, bárɔ́k, barɔ yi mpok árɔbhɛ kɛkwɔt bɛgu.
Nɛ mbák ɛrɨ bɛ mɛnkwɔ ndɔ́k, chɔŋ ndɔk nɛ bhɔ. 
Bǎrɨŋɨ ɛrɛmɛ́ ndak anɛ́ áfákárí atú Judɛ́ya ankɛm, bɛ́bho atú Gálili, mpok Jɔ̌n ánáŋ ánáŋá nyaka bɛghati bo bɛ mántɨ́knsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhap yi anjwiti bhɔ.
Bǒbhɔ bákʉ̀ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ndu bɛyibhiri batɨ yɛka bɛ mǎnkóŋó bhɔ́, kɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ɛrɨ́tí nkaysi. Báyàŋ chi bɛkʉ mǎndɔ bhɛsɛ mǎnkoŋo bhɔ.
“Kɛ yɛ̌ mmu abhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ mbɔ̌ŋ mpok anɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́fàkari. Bɔangɛl Mandɛm bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ, Yɛ̌ chí Mmɔ Mandɛm abhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ. Ɛta aywǐntí kɛ̌ arɨŋɨ.
Nɛ chɔŋ ngɔ́ bhɔ ntínso, mfóŋórí bɛbʉ́ bhap nkɛpɛrɛ tɨk bhɔ́ wawak.”
Nɛnu nɛ́kwɛ́n amfay. Máykɛl nɛ bɔángɛl abhɛn bachi antɛn yi báre nu nɛ nnya mbʉ́mbʉ nɛ bɔángɛl abhɛn bákòŋo yi.
Mmǔ anɛ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ́fú yi amʉɛt are nɨk Yesu mmʉɛt bɛ ándɔ́ yi ankoŋo yi. Kɛ ndu Yesu aghati yi ampɛtnsɛm, arɛm ntá yi bɛ,
‑ Mbák ɛkak ɛyɛ ɛ́tò wɔ ndǔ bɛbʉ́, kpɔ́t yɔ fɛrɛ́. Ɛ́chí sayri bɛ ɔ́nchwe ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti nɛ ɛkak ɛ́mɔt ɛcha bɛ́ mámɛ́sɛ wɔ amɛm nɛpǐngo nɛ bɛkak bɛpay.
Mǔnkwɔ Fárisi ate ɛyǐ ɛbhak anɨk mmʉɛt bɛ, ‘Mandɛm, nkáká wɔ́ bɛ mpú mbɔ bo báchák abhɛn bachi baghɛ́p, bakʉ̌ bɛbʉ́, nɛ bakwɛnɛ́ bɛrwɔp. Nkáká wɔ bɛ mpú mbɔ yɛ̌ chí mbɛbhɛ́ nkabhɛ́nti anɛ áté nɔ́ awu.
bɛsɛ́ bǒnto sɛpú bo abhɛn sɛkway mɛnyiɛ, sɛnyu mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎchyɛ̀ wu bhɛsɛ ɛ̌ti bɛtɨk ɛbhɛ́n sɛ́kʉ̀ kɛ?
Pú bǎrɛm bɛ mǎnáŋ bǎbhɔŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ? Mǎnaŋ bájwí nɛ akap anɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ áchyɛ̀ bhɔ́! Bǎkwɛn bafɔ, yɛ̌ndu sɛ́pú bafɔ. Kɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ̌yaŋ chi bɛ mǎmbák bafɔ tɛtɛp ndǔ baraka Mandɛm bɛ bɛsɛ bǒnto Yesu nkwɔ sɛ́mbák bafɔ nɛ bhe.
Ato mɛ bɛ́ mbé ntá bho bɛ mpok anɛ yi átɔŋ bɔ́ bɛrɨ̌ndu bhi akway.”
Nɛ sɛ́pú kʉ nyaka yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛ́ yɛ̌ chi be, yɛ chi bo báchak, mánkaka bhɛsɛ. Sɛ́kwáy nyaka bɛbhɛp be mɛnyɨŋ mbɔ bǒnto Kristo.
Sɛ́rɔ́k yɛ sɛ́chwé amɛm áchwí, bɔ bápɛtnsɛm bɛkɛt ɛbhap.
Ɛyɔŋ ɛnɛ bɛ, “Ndɔŋ achak” ɛ́tɔŋ bhɛsɛ kpoŋoroŋ bɛ chɔŋ Mandɛm amfɛrɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́kway mɛnyɨkɨsi, mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn yi ághókó, bɛ ɛbhɛn bɛpu nyɨkɨsi mɛ́ndɔp.
Bátát nɔ́kɔ́ árɛ́ mpǎy manywɔp, Fɛstɔs aghati Mfɔ Agripa ɛ̌ti nyé Pɔ̌l bɛ, “Mmǔfú achí fá anɛ Fɛ́liks arɔ ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ.
Sáilas akwak mɛ bɛsɨŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ. Nsɔt yí mbɔ ntɨ manɔ anɛ mɛ̌kwáy bɛsɨkɨntɨ nɛ yi. Ntí anɛ nsɨ́ŋɨ́ bhe mɔ́mbɨŋɨ́ ɛkáti ɛnɛ chi ndu bɛ́fyɛ bhe ntɨ nɛ bɛghati bhe ɛnyu Mandɛm áyɛ̀t bho. Tě ká kpirí arɛ́.
Kɛ mbák ápú arɨarɨ, mmʉɛt yɛ nkɛm ǎbhák chi amɛm ɛjuri. Kɛ mbák ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛyɛ ɛ́girigíri, nɔ́ ɛjuri ɛnɛ ɔchí arɛ ɛya ɛcha.” 
Ɛnyu bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn mbʉ́mbʉ abhɔŋɔ mɛ́naŋ bɛ́kʉ̀ bɛtɨk fá amɨk bhɛsɛ́ bhɛsɛ́. Kɛ mmu anɛ áchɛt bo mbi bɛ bǎkɛ́ bhʉrɛ bɛbhé Mandɛm ǎrɔŋ chɔŋ ambɨ bɛkʉ nɔ kpatɛ mpok anɛ Mandɛm áfɛrɛ yi ambi.
Dɨŋɨ́ ká, nɛ ɛ́chí tɛtɛp bɛ bákway bɛ́fóŋóri bɛbʉ́ bo mankɛm nɛ bɛbɛ́ptí bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fù bho anyu.
Bábhák maknkay tontó, babho bɛrɛm bɛ, “Ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ mmu nɛ́? Yɛ̌ chí mbʉ́ɛ́p ághòk yi, mpɛ́rɛ́nyɛn ɛ́ngok yí!” 
Yesu ayoŋ amɨ́k ayɨŋɨ bakoŋo bhi arɛm bɛ, “Ɛ́rɨ ɛcha ntá yɛka bachɛ́bhɛ́bho; mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm achi Mfɔ ywɛka.
Yesu Acha ámbák nɛ wɔ. Bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm mɛ́mbák nɛ be mankɛm.
Nɛ nɛ́ntɨ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛrɔŋɔ bhɔ, ngɔ́ mmǔfú. Abhak mbɔ Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm. Abhɔ́ŋ *ɛ́wɛt amʉɛt ɛnɛ ɛ́ghaka yi tɛ ndǔ mɛmɨ̌-bɛkak. Agwɔ́t mgbat nkʉɛt anɛ bághókó nɛ pú ambeápak.
Nɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ nkwɔ ǎtè ntísiɛ bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi tɛtɛp. Ayámbɨ arɛm bɛ,
Bárɔ yɛ bɛyǎ bho, bátɛmɛri Yesu amɛm áchwi, bábho bɛ́rɔŋ nɛ yi. Báchwi áchák anɛ́ áchí nyaka arɛ́ áre koŋo bhɔ́.
Básɔt bhɔ bɛsí bǒnto Yesu. Bǒnto mánɨkmʉɛt mányáŋa bɔ́ amɔ anti.
Ghatí bɔ́ mánkʉ nɔ́kɔ́ bɛrɨ. Mánkʉ́ nɔkɔ bɛrɨ ndǔ bɛyǎ babhi. Bákɛ́ taŋ awɔ́. Mánkɔrɛ nɔkɔ nɛ batɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ maŋák.
Nɛrɔ́ŋ anɛ bɔ́ bárɔŋɔ arɛ́ ndɔŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛjwi ɛ́páy, Josɛ́f akʉ bɔ̌mayi bárɨŋɨ yí, nɛ Mfɔ Íjip arɨŋɨ nnɛrɛ́kɛt Josɛ́f.
Nsɨŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ntá yɛka bo mǎnókó Mmɔ Mandɛm ndu bɛkʉ mándɨŋɨ bɛ mǎnaŋ bǎbhɔŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.
Adók ate kpɛrɛp, abho bɛkɔ. Are kɔ andokoti nɔkɔ, nɛ ambɨtɨ nɔkɔ Mandɛm, kpát arɔk achwe amɛm ɛkɛrákap nɛ bhɔ.
Mbák mǎnkʉ nɔ nkaysi bɛkʉ bɛbʉ́ apu pɛrɛ bhɔŋ chɔŋ bɛtaŋ amfǎy yɛka, tɛ̌ndu ɛbhé ɛbhɨkɨ pɛrɛ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ ndu nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛka, nɛ ndiɛrɛ bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm kɛ bɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ ndu nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛka. 
Ɛ́kʉ́ are rɔŋ ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí bo Israɛl yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nywɔp ankɛm nɔkɔ ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ bhɔ nɛ bǒ Grik abhɛn mánóko nyaka Mandɛm nkwɔ. Ǎrɔŋ nyaka nkwɔ nɛfísiɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nywɔp ankʉ nɔkɔ ɛnyumɔ́t nɛ bo abhɛn bátwɔ̀ árɛ́.
Awu áfʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, ngɔ́ ɛkpɔkɔ́ nɛbhaŋ ɛnɛn pɛ́pɛ́p nɛ mmǔ arɛ chɔkɔ mbɔ Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm. Nta kɛfɔ anɛ bághókó nɛ pú abhak yi anti, nɛ ngak anɛ ácháp abhak yi awɔ ndu bɛkpɔt mbwɔt.
Tɛ̌ndu bɛyǎ bo bápànyu ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bakwǎŋwaŋ básɔ̀t bɛ bɛbhɔŋ mɛnwɔp be mǎngok nɔkɔ nsé yap, bǎbhɔŋ yɛ bɛghok mɛnyɨŋɨ́ tɛtɛp ɛbhɛn mbɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́gháti bhe ɛ̌ti mmʉɛt ɛya.
Sɛ́ghókó nɔ́kɔ́ ndak wu, bɛsɛ́ bho sɛ́kɔ̀ nyaka nɛ yi nɛ bǒnkwɔ abhɛn bachi Seséria sɛ́nɨ́k Pɔ̌l mmʉɛt bɛ́ ákɛ́rɔŋ Yerúsalɛm.
Yɛ̌ mmu, yɛ̌ chi anɛ achi amfay nɛ Mandɛm nɛ yɛ̌ chi anɛ áchí amɨk nɛ yɛ̌ chi anɛ achi ɛtɔkɔ́ bawú kɛkwáy mɛ́nɛ́nɛ yɔ́. Yɛ̌ mmu kɛkwáy bɛ́pay ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ básɨ́ŋɨ́ amɛm.
Kɛ mbɔk bo Israɛl abhɛn báfú atú Esia bábhak arɛ́. Bɔ babhɔŋ bɛ́twɔ fá mántɛbhɛ mɛ bɛsí bhɛ mbák bághɔ bɛ nkʉ ɛbɛ́ptí ɛnyɨŋ.
Atɛp bɔ amɨ́k amʉɛt nɛ nkaysi bɛ́ chɔŋ manchyɛ yi ɛnyɨŋ.
Ngɔrɛ́ nɛ nnɛ́m bákɛ́ kaŋ yɛ batɨ kɛbhʉ́rɛ́, ɛbhɨkɨfʉɛt ndǔ mpok anɛ báká ɛyɔŋ ɛmɔt bɛ báyàŋ bɛ́chwé ndǔ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt ntá Mandɛm. Mpok yɔ ánáŋ ámfʉɛ́t, bǎbhɔŋ bɛpɛt bɛchɛm mmʉɛt, bɛ Satan ákɛ́ rwɔ bhe mǎnkwɛ́n ndǔ nɛmɔ ndǔ bǎpú kway bɛkɛm mmʉɛt.
Nɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ rɔŋ amfay ndu bɛchyɛ mmʉɛt mbɔ akap ndɔŋ nɛ ndɔŋ mbɔ ɛnyǔ mǔngo bachiǎkap áchwe nyaka ndǔ mɔ́kɛt anɛ achi Nyáŋá Acha yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmíɛ́ nɛ manoŋ amɛn apu ami.
Batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bákʉ nɔ. Nnɔ Yesu abhak téé kɛ́kwɔ́t nɛ ɛkotákátí, nɛ manɔ́ máyi, María, ngɔrɛ́ Klopas, nɛ María mmɔ̌ ɛtɔk Mágdala.
Báyáŋ nɔ́kɔ́ yi kɛghɔ, bápɛtnsɛm Yerúsalɛm ndu bɛyaŋ yí arɛ́.
Ɛrɛmɛ́ nkwɔ́ bakók ányìɛ nyaka ambɨ njiɛ anɛ achi kɛkwɔt.
Jɔ̌n Njwiti kɛ̌ Aisáya ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm árɛ̀mɛ nyaka ɛ̌ti yi bɛ, “Mmu achi amɛm baso ǎbɨ̀k nɛ ɛyɔŋ amfay andɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, ‘Toŋtí ká mbi anɛ Acha áfʉɛ̀t arɛ. Kʉ́ ka mbǐ ywi ambak chak.’”
Mmyamyaŋ are kɔt. Nɛfaŋ are sáy, nɛbu nɛ́ndɛmti nɔkɔ. Nɛ ɛrɛmɛ́ nɛnyɨkɨsǐmɨk nɛ́kwɛ́n. Tɛ Mandɛm ághókó bǒ, ɛnyǔ nɛnyɨkɨsǐmɨk ɛnɔ nɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ re fakari. Ɛnɔ nɛ́táŋ nɛcha.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ bakoŋo bha bati apay, bati arat, báchɛ́mɛ́ ɛ̌ti ya, nchí arɛ́ nɛ bhɔ.” 
Pɔ̌l nɛ Banábas báre ghati bo Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu amɛm ɛtɔk Dɛ́be. Bɛyǎ bo mánoko nɛ bábho bɛ́kóŋo Yesu. Bɔ Pɔ̌l bápɛt yɛ nsɛm Lístra nɛ Ikɔ́niɔm nɛ Antiɔk anɛ Pisídia.
Anɛfú arɛm bɛ, ‘Nɛ́nɛ kɛ mbáy ngɔrɛ́. Mpú kwáy yɛ bɛ́twɔ.’
Ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ̌ mɛ̌tɨk yɛ wɔ bɛ́ ɔ́nkʉ bɛ akap anɛ Mandɛm áchyɛ́ wɔ mpok nyáŋá wɔ amɔ anti ambak mbɔ ngó anɛ́ áyaŋ mɛnɛmɛ kɛ báfok wu ádù.
Píta arɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Bɔ̌ma, nchí kway bɛghati bhe kpoŋoroŋ ɛ̌ti Mfɔ Debhít, chi mbɨ ywɛsɛ. Agu nyaka, bábhɛ́mɛ yi, nɛ nnɛm ɛni nɛbhʉɛt fá nɛ bhɛsɛ kpatɛ ɛchɔŋ.
Yesu aghati Matá bɛ, “Matá, pú ngátí wɔ́ bɛ mbák ɔnókó, chɔŋ ɔ́ngɔ́ bɛtaŋ Mandɛm?”
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ngɔrɛ́ abhɔŋ yɛ bɛsɛpti mmʉɛt ntá nnɛ́m aywi ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ, mbɔ ɛnyǔ bǒnkwɔ básɛ̀pti mmʉɛt ntá Kristo.
Are rɛm nɔ́, mbɔnyunɛ Yesu arɛm bɛ́ ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri yí ɛ́ndɔ́ yi.
Ghatí bhɛsɛ, ɛbhé yɛsɛ ɛka bɛ sɛ́nchíɛ nkábhɛ́nti ntá Mfɔ Rom kɛ ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ ka?”
Kɛ Sakaría abhɛ́p ángɛl bɛ, “Chɔŋ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ anɛ́ ndak achí tɛtɛp ná. Mɛ nɛ ngɔrɛ́ wa sɛ́kɔk tontó.”
Kɛ bǎpú kʉ ɛnyu yɔ. Bǎpá chí nyu mǎnjoŋ nɔkɔ mmʉɛt. Nɛyoŋómʉɛt ɛnɛka ɛnɔ nɛnkɛm nɛ́bhɨkɨ rɨ.
Báfáte bákɛ́m yi, bafu ɛtɔk nɛ yi. Ndǔ ɛtɔk yap ɛchi amfǎy njiɛ, básɔ́t yi barɔk ndǔ nkókónjiɛ bɛ́ mámpúrí yi ankwɛn arɛ́.
Mpok ɛyɔ, bakoŋo Yesu bárɔŋ nyaka ɛtɔk ndu bɛ́kú nɛnyíɛ́.
Yesu abho yɛ mɛnɛnɛ ntá yap bɛ manjwimɛm ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn básɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛ̌ti yi amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm, bɛ́bho ndǔ Basɨŋɨ Moses bɛrɔ́ŋ bɛghaka ndǔ amɛn barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm mankɛm.
Kɛ María abhʉrɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ mɛnkɛm antɨ, ankaysi nɔkɔ bhɔ.
Ápɛ́rɛ to bhɔ, aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Mbuɔt bɛ́fɛ́rɛ ɛbhɨ aya, kɛ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk bábhɨ́kɨ́ ya. Nɨk yɛka mmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm mmu achi mbɔŋɔ́nkɨ bɛ ántó bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk, mámfɛ́rɛ́ mbwɔt ɛbhɨ.
