Mandɛm Ɛta nɛ Yesu Kristo mántɔ́ŋ bɛsɛ́ bɛrɨ̌ndu, mángɔ́ bhɛsɛ́ ntínso, nɛ mánchyɛ bhɛsɛ kpák ndu sɛ́kòŋo tɛtɛp Mandɛm nɛ ndǔ sɛ́bhɔ̀ŋ ɛkɔŋ nɛ batɨ.
Nɛ ndǔ Yesu nɛ bɔPíta básɛ̀p njiɛ, Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Bǎkɛ́ ghati yɛ̌ mmu ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎghɔ́ fá, kpátɛ Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm ampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.”
Bárɔ mbi anɛ achi chak, mánɛ́m ɛbhɨ. Bákʉ̀ chi mbɔ Bálam,   Mmɔ Boas ákɔ́ŋ nyaka bɛ́kʉ bɛbʉ́ bɛ ámbɔ́ŋ nsáy-nkáp,
Hɛ́rɔd ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ Yesu, ábhɔ́ŋ maŋák tontó, mbɔnyunɛ anáŋ ǎghòk nyaka ɛ̌ti yi nɛ abhɔ́ŋ ɛkwak tɛntɛp bɛghɔ yi nɛ amɨ́k. Ǎbhàka nyaka ntɨ bɛ chɔŋ Yesu ankʉ ɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay yí angɔ́.
Abhé mɔ́mbakanɛm anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkɛm bǒ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛtɔk mbɔ Mfɔ nɛ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ ɛyi ɛnɛ bághókó nɛ ɛse awɔ. Báfɔ́ŋɔ mɔ́wu tɛ́mté bárɔk nɛ yi ntá Mandɛm bɛsí ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ ɛyi.
Kɛ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ɛchí mbɔ nɛbhʉ́ɛ́rɛ́mɨk ɛnɛn baghoko sayri ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛ́pú kway mɛnyɨkɨsi nɔ́ kɛ báte ɛkɛt arɛ́. Básɨŋ ndǔ ntay ɛnɛn bápɨ́ arɛ bɛ, “Ɛta Mandɛm arɨ́ŋɨ́ bo abhɛn bachi abhi.” Básɨŋ nkwɔ bɛ, “Yɛ̌ agha anɛ árɛ̀m bɛ achi mmu Acha ándɔ́ bɛbʉ́.”
Yɛ̌ndu Yesu ádɨ́k nyaka nka bho ɛtay nɛ bɛkpɔkɔ́ brɛt, bɔ kɛjwimɛm ndǔ ɛnyǔ mmu yi achi. Bɔ́ kɛnɛnɛ batɨ̌ yap amɛm. 
Yesu arɛm ntá ɛnɔk ɛyɔ bɛ, “Bɛbho ɛchɔŋ, ɔpú pɛrɛ nyu kɛpɛm.” Baghɔk abhi bághok ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ́mɛ́. 
Nikɔdɛ́mɔs abhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ɛyɔ ɛkway bɛ́fàkari ná?”
Bo Israɛl bábhó bɛrɛm nɛ batɨ bɛ, “Atɨ bɛ́rɔ́ŋ fá, ɛnɛ́ sɛ́pú kway chɔŋ bɛghɔ yi? Atɨ bɛrɔŋ chi ɛtɔkɔ́ mankɔ ɛnɛ́ bǒ bhɛsɛ bátáká bárɔ́ŋɔ́ arɛ́ kɛ? Ǎyàŋ bɛrɔŋ bɛ́tɔŋ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl arɛ́ kɛ?
Nkúbhɛ́ ɛnyǔ yɔ kɛ ɛchi nɛ Kristo. Puyɛ̌ yímbɔŋ kɛ áyóŋó nyaka mmʉɛt bɛ́ ámbák mǔngo bachiǎkap ambɔ́ŋ kɛnókó nchiakap. Mandɛm kɛ ábhɨ́ŋɨ́ yi, arɛm bɛ, “Wɔ, ɔchí Mɔ́wa, nɛ ɛchɔŋ nchí rɛm bɛ ndɔp chi Ɛtayɛ”.
Bɔ̌ma, yɛ̌ndu bákʉ́ sɛ́rɔ́ nyaka bhe ndu mɔ́mbɨŋɨ́ mpok, batɨ yɛsɛ ábhʉ́ɛ́t nyaka nɛ bhe, nɛ ɛ́kʉ́ ɛkwak bɛpɛt bɛghɔ bhe bɛsí nɛ bɛsi ɛ́re yá ɛ́ndɔk nɔkɔ chi ambɨ nɛ sɛre nu bɛghɔ bhe.
Ɛmɛnɛ́nti yi ɛbhak pɛ́pɛ̌pɛ́p mbɔ ɛtɔkɔfiɔŋ. Ntí ywi ábhák ɛnyumɔt. Amɨ́k ayi ábhák mbɔ ngó anɛ ádù.
Nɛ tɛ̌ndu ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ ɛ́rɨ bɛ manywɔp ɛya ándɔ́k ambɨ ɛ̌ti yɛká, ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ chɔŋ mbak nɛpɛ́m, ndɔk ambɨ bɛbhak nɛ bhe ndu bɛ́kwák mǎmbɔŋ nɛka nɛ Yesu ɛ́nchá ɛnyu ɛsɨ́, bɛ́ maŋák amɛká anjá ancha.
Mandɛm bachǐmbɨ bhɛsɛ, Mandɛm Ábraham nɛ Áisek nɛ Jekɔ́p kɛ achyɛ mǔbɛtok ywi Yesu kɛnókó. Achyɛ́ yi kɛnókó yɛ̌ndu be bǎrɛ̀m nyaka bɛ bǎbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛkʉ nɛ yi mpok Páílet áyàŋ bɛfɛrɛ yi amɔ. Bǎsɔ́t yi bǎchyɛ́ ntá bǒbati Rom bɛ mángwáy.
Mǎmbák ɛnyu ɛyɔ bɛ́ bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ noko mánchyɛ́ bhe kɛnókó nɛ bɛ́ bǎkɛ́ kɔ bɛsɨ́kɨ́. 
Mamiɛ́ nka amɔt yɔ áfʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, mándɔ Satan amfu ndǔ kɛnɔŋ ɛkɛn bafyɛ yi arɛ́.
Chɔŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛ́bhɛn mɛ́nkway bɛfakari nɛ bhe kɛ yɛ̌ ɛkǎk ɛmɛnɛ́nti mmu ywɛka ɛpu nɛm.
Sɨ́ŋ yɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́ghɔ́, ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́chí, nɛ ɛbhɛn bɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́fákari ansɛm mpok.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ kɛ básɨ́ŋɨ amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm bɛ, “Ábraham anókó nyaka Mandɛm, ɛ́kʉ́ Mandɛm arɛm bɛ́ Ábraham achí chak bɛsí bhi, nɛ bo báré bhɨŋɨ Ábraham bɛ́ mmʉɛrɛ Mandɛm”.
Mbák mmu achi amɛm ɛkɛt ɛyɔ anɛ ákɔ́ŋɔ́ kpák, chɔŋ Mandɛm ankʉ kpák ambak nɛ yí. Kɛ mbák yɛ̌ mmu apú, áfɔ́k wu ǎpɛtnsɛm ntá yɛka.
Nɛ bo Yesu Kristo mánaŋ báfɛrɛ ntí ndǔ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ máŋwàka nyaka bɛkʉ. Ɛchi mbɔ bɛ bágo mmʉɛt nkwǎ nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yɔ áyàŋ mmu ankʉ ndu ɛkotákátí.
Páílet arɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka sayri bɛ́ bǒbati bo Israɛl bákɛm Yesu bárɔ̌ŋ ntá yi nɛ yi chi ɛ̌ti mpabhamɨ́k.
Ntá ya, bɛbhak nɛpɛ́m chí bɛ́chyɛ Kristo kɛnókó, kɛ bɛ́gu arɨ mbɔŋ achá.
Chí nkúbhɛ́ bariɛp amɛn manɛrɛ́kɛt yɛsɛ́ byo nɛ apay babhaka ntɨ arɛ́ bɛ́ chɔŋ amfú kpoŋoroŋ ndǔ mánɨ̀kmʉɛt mánchyɛ nɔkɔ Mandɛm kɛnókó bɛti nɛ ngósí. Mfɔ, mbɔ̌ŋ ɛsɔŋɔri nɛ bo Israɛl ɛchɔŋ chi ɛ̌ti mbákántɨ ndǔ bariɛp amɔ.
Mmu anɛ apu nɛ mɛ, achi chi mǔmpap wa. Nɛ mmu anɛ ápú kwak mɛ ndu mɛ̌nyókóti bho, ǎtàkatak.” 
Mmok abhɔŋ ɛbhi bɛrɨ, ntaŋ ábhɔ́ŋ ɛbhi bɛrɨ, mambe ábhɔ́ŋ ɛbhap bɛrɨ, nɛ mambe ábhɔ́ŋ bɛrɨ kɛkúrí kɛkúrí.
Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bo báfyɛ̀ ngoŋo arɛ́ ndǔ bɛ́chyɛ̀ bhɔ maŋák, nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn amɨ́k ayɛsɛ ákwɛ̀n arɛ ɛnkʉ sɛ́mbɔ́ŋ ɛkwak bɛbhɔŋ bhɔ, nɛ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́kʉ̀ bo abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bhɔ báyòŋmʉɛt, bɔ́ mɛnkɛm bɛ́fù chi ndǔ mmɨk bɛbʉ́-nɛ. Bɛ́pú fu ná Ɛta.
Ntɨkɨ ɛnyu bakak sɛ́kway bɛchyɛ Mandɛm ɛ̌ti maŋák mankɛm amɛn sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛsí bhi ɛ̌ti yɛka?
Bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bárɛm yɛ ntá yi bɛ, “Wɔ mbɔŋ ɔ́rɛ̀m ɛ̌ti mmʉɛt yɛ. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɔ́rɛ̀m puyɛ̌ ndak.”
Ɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ manywɔp atandat, Yesu asɔt Píta, nɛ Jems nɛ Jɔ̌n, akó amfay njiɛ ngo nɛ bhɔ. Bábhák arɛ́ bɔ́bhɔ́. Bápɛ́rɛ yɨŋɨ, bɛsí Yesu bɛ́yíbhiri.
Ndu ɛ́rɔ́bhɛ́ kɛ́kwɔ́t bɛ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu manchwe amɛm ɛbha, Pɔ̌l abhɛ́p mǔngo wu bɛ, “Ɛ́tá, chɔŋ ɔ́nka bɛ́ ngátí wɔ, ndak-a?” Mǔngo wu aghok nɔkɔ ndǔ yi árɛ̀m chi Grik, abhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛyɔŋɔ́ Grik-ɛ?
“Mmǔ bɛtɨk wu arɛm nɛ mmʉɛt yi bɛ, ‘Chɔŋ nkʉ yi? Mmʉɛt ápú mɛ́ bɛ́kʉ bɛtɨk bɛtaŋ bɛtaŋ, nɛ ntí ánwɔ̀p mɛ mɛnɨŋɨ mɛnɨŋɨ.
Mǎnáŋ mǎmbák ɛnyu ɛyɔ, Yesu Kristo ǎkʉ mǎmbɔ́ŋ ɛrɨ́tí ɛpɨŋ. Kʉ nɔ́kɔ́ ká chí bɛyǎ bɛrɨ bɛ́ bo mángɔ́ bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎkʉ mánchyɛ nɔkɔ Mandɛm kɛnókó nɛ mándɛm nɔkɔ bɛ́, “Mandɛm abhɔŋ bɛtaŋ achá.” 
Bɛcháy bɛ́pɛt bɛkɛm bɔ́ tontó. Bábho bɛbhɛp batɨ bɛ, “Ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ mmú nɛ? Yɛ̌ chí mbʉ́ɛ́p ághòk yi, mpɛ́rɛ́nyɛn ɛ́ngok yi!”
Tɛ́mté wu, Símun nɛ manɔ́ barɔ bɛyǎ nkáp yap, bakoŋo Yesu.
Batɛmɛ́ nɛnu básɔ́t bɔ̌batábhɛ́nɔk abhɛn báchí nsěnse, mánɨ́ ntá bábáy yi anti, barɛm bɛ chi nta kɛfɔ. Básɔ́t nkú chu bafyɛ́ yi amʉɛt, bárɛm bɛ chí ayi nkú kɛfɔ.
Ndu sɛ́jɛ̀t, sɛ́ntɛ́p amɨ́k amʉɛt Yesu. Yí kɛ ánɛ́nɛ́ mbi bɛ sɛmbɔŋ nɛka nɛ yi. Nɛ yírɛ kɛ̌ nɛka ɛnɛsɛ́ nɛ́jwi pɔɔt mbɔ ɛnyu nɛbhɔŋɔ bɛbhak. Aká nyaka bɛgu ndǔ ɛkotákátí, abyák ntíánwɔ́p anɛ achi ndu ɛnyǔ nɛwú ɛnɔ, mbɔnyunɛ arɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka bɛ maŋák achi ambɨ amɛn Mandɛm abhʉ́rɛ́ ntá yi. Nɛ́nɛ, achí ɛbhe awɔ́nɛm Mandɛm ndu ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ̌ ɛyi.
Bǎgú nɛ Kristo, nɛ Mandɛm afɛ́rɛ́ bhe antɛn bɛfóŋó ɛbhɛn bɛbhɔŋɔ bɛtaŋ fá amɨk. Ndu ɛ́chí nɔ, ndaká yi bǎchi mbɔ bǒ mmɨk? Ndaká yí bǎbhʉɛt bɛkoŋo bɛbhé bǒ mmɨk, mbɔ ɛbhɛn bɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ,
tɛ̌ndu ɛchi amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm bɛ, ‘Chɔŋ Mandɛm anchyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɔángɛl bhi mántwɔ́ manchyɛ wɔ nɛkwak.’
Pɔ̌l nɛ Banábas báyap bǒ batí ndu yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛkɛrɛ́ Mandɛm. Báfyɛ́ bhɔ́ amɔ Yesu Acha mmu bɔ́ básɨ́kɨ́ ntɨ nɛ yi ndu nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt nɛ nɛtarɛ́nsay.
Bo abhɛn bákɔ̀ nɛ yi báré kɛmɛ mandɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Chí Yesu, Ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm anɛ áfú Násárɛt, atú Gálili.” 
Ɛchi ɛnyumɔt nɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm ákʉ́. Ǎyàŋ nyaka bɛ bɔ mándɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ yi ǎbè ntɨ mpok bo bákʉ́ bɛbʉ́ nɛ bɛ ábhɔ̀ŋ bɛtaŋ bɛ́tɛ́msi bǒ bɛbʉ́. Kɛ abhɔŋ bɛyǎ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ́ nɛ bo abhɛn yi aghoko.
Mbák Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ sɛ́ghàti bho achi chi mbɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́, ǎbhák ɛnyu ɛyɔ chi ntá bo abhɛn bachi ndu mbi nɛwú.
Mandɛm ayap be bɛ mǎmbak bǒbhi, bǎchi nyáŋá, nɛ akɔŋ be tontó. Ndu ɛchi nɔ, bǎbhɔŋ bɛghɔ batɨ ntínso, mǎntɔŋ bɔ bɛrɨ̌ntɨ nɛ nɛsɛptǐmʉɛt, nɛ ɛpɨŋ bɛsɔt mɛnyɨŋ pɛtii, nɛ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ.
Mpok ɛyɔ, chɔŋ ɛ́mfakari bɛ mmʉɛt ɛyɛsɛ ɛnjibhiri ɛnyu yɔ, bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́ghati bhɛsɛ ɛ́mfú tɛtɛp. Nɔ chi bɛ, “Mámɛn nɛwú. Básɔt awɔ́nɛm amfǎy nɛwú ndak amay.”
Abhɛn ɛkɔŋ, kɛ mbák chi bhe, bǎkɛ ghɔkɔntɨk mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǒnto Yesu Kristo Acha ywɛsɛ bárɛ́mɛ́ tɛntɛp bɛ bɛ́bhɔŋ bɛ́fákári.
Yesu akɛmɛ yɛ yi bɛ, “Ɔchí ngɔrɛ́ anɛ ɔ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛka nɛ mɛ tɛtɛp, nɛ chɔŋ Mandɛm ankʉ ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́yàŋ.” Tɛ́mté wu, mɔ́ywi ataŋ. 
Acha aghɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ngɔrɛ́ wu, ntínso nɛ́kɛ́m yi tontó, arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Kɛ́pɛrɛ di.”
Fú ká mbɔnyunɛ bɛbʉ́ bhap bɛghaka tɛ amfay, nɛ Mandɛm ábhɨ́kɨ́ ghɔkɔntɨk bhɔ́.
Yesu Kristo Acha ántɔ́ŋ be bɛrɨ̌ndu, nɛ ɛkɔŋ Mandɛm ɛmbak amɛm batɨ yɛka, nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt ɛnɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ áchyɛ̀ ɛmbak nɛ be mankɛm.
Ghatí bǒbhɛn mándɔ́k ndǔ bakɨ nɛ bɔ̌bɛtɔk abhɛn báchí fá kɛkwɔt manku ɛnyɨŋ mɛnyiɛ.”
Ndiɛrɛ ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Kristo áfʉɛ́rɛ́ ntá ya ákʉ́ kɛ nchí rɛm ndǔ bɛyǎ mɛnyu ntá bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl bɛ mángúpsí bɛpɨŋ ɛbhap, mankʉ nɔkɔ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Mandɛm áyàŋ.
Yesu árɛm nɔkɔ nɔ, ɛfóŋó yɔ ɛ́bɨk, ɛ́nyɨkɨsi mɔ́wu gbogbǒgbok, ɛ́fú yi amʉɛt. Arɔp mbɔ ngú. Bo abhɛn báchi arɛ barɛm bɛ, “Ágú.”
Wɔ nɛ mɛ sɛ́gù ɛ̌ti bɛpɔ̌ barak ayɛsɛ, kɛ mmǔ-nɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ kʉ yɛ̌ ɛbɛ́ptí ɛnyɨŋ?”
“Mpǒk yɔ, mɔ́ywi anɛ nsénsí abhak ɛbhɨ. Ágháká nɔ́kɔ́ kɛkwɔ́t nɛ ɛkɛt ndǔ yi afu ɛbhɨ ápɛtnsɛm anywɔ́p, aghók ndǔ nkɛnkwɛt nɛ nɛbhɛ́n nɛ́chí anywɔ́p.
afyɛ́ bhɛsɛ ɛrɨŋ amʉɛt, bɛtɔŋ bɛ sɛchi bɔ̌bhi. Akʉ nɔ ndu áchyɛ́ bhɛsɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ mmu achi amɛm batɨ yɛsɛ́ ndu bɛtɔŋ bɛ chɔŋ anchyɛ bhɛsɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛchak.
Nkɛmɛ bɛ, ‘Acha chí wɔ agha?’ Ɛyɔŋ ɛ́kɛ́mɛ bɛ, ‘Chí mɛ Yesu Mmu Násárɛt kɛ ɔ́chyɛ̀ nɛnyok.’
Mpok báchɛ̀m mɛnyiɛ nɛnyiɛ́-ɛkɔŋ nɛ batɨ, bábhak mbɔ bakwap amɛn áchɔŋti nɛnyíɛ́. Bátwɔ̀ mánchɔkɔ mɛnyiɛ nɛ mɛnyu, mánkaysi nɔkɔ chi ndiɛrɛ mmʉɛt ɛyap. Bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ntíánwɔ́p. Báchí mbɔ bɛkpɔkɔ́ nɛbhaŋ ɛnɛn mbʉ́ɛ́p ápɔ̀kɔ amfay kɛ yɛ̌ manyiɛp kɛfú arɛ ánkwɛ́n. Báchí mbɔ mɛnɔk ɛbhɛn bɛ́pú nyu kɛpɛm yɛ̌ chi ndǔ mpok anɛ mɛnɔk mɛnyu kɛpɛm. Báchí mbɔ mɛnɔk ɛbhɛn bághɛ́mɛ́ nɛ bakaŋ nɛ bɛ́gú ndak ámay.
Tɛtɛ̌tɛp, mǔbɛtok apú cha chi-bɛtok aywi, nɛ mǔnto apú cha mmǔ anɛ átó yi.
Mbaŋ are kwɛn, Yesu arɔk ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm, are kɔ ndu mɔ́kɛt mambarɛnkók anɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ́ mɔ́kɛt mambarɛnkók Sólomon.
Bo mánaŋ bátat nyaka kɛnyiɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́, ɛ́kʉ́ Pɔ̌l afate ate nɛ́ntɨ́ ɛnap arɛm bɛ, “Bɔta, mbɔ bǎghók ɛyɔŋ ɛya mbʉ́ sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ fá Krɛt sɛmbɔŋ nchɔŋtí nɛ mbʉ́ mɛ́nɛ́mɛ́ ɛbhɛn bɛ́pú.
Nɛ nkúbhɛ́ ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ̌ mbɔk yɛká báchí nyaka. Kɛ nɛ́nɛ, Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ anáŋ asó bɛbʉ́ bhɛka afɛ́rɛ́, akʉ bɛ́ mǎmbák bo Mandɛm. Nɛ ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ Yesu Kristo Acha ákʉ́, Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ akʉ nkwɔ́ bɛ́ be mǎmbák chak bɛsí Mandɛm.
Ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ ngáti be bɛ́ chɔŋ mǎngú ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛka. Chɔŋ mǎngú ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛka mbák bǎbhɨkɨ noko bɛ́ nchí mmu anɛ nchí.”
Ángɛl anɛ mbɨ árɔ́ŋ nɔ́kɔ́ achak abhesi andɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Ɛrɛm ɛtɔk Bábilɔn ɛ́kwɛn bǔp. Ɛ́chɔ́ŋtí bǒ bɛtɔkɔ́ mmɨk mankɛm nɛ bɛpɔ̌ barak ɛpúsí yi. Ɛ́chí mbɔ bɛ ɛ́chyɛ́ bhɔ mmɛm bataŋbataŋ mányu.”
Bárɛ́m ntá Yesu bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, bákɛ̌m ngɔrɛ́ ndu ákwɛ̀n bɛrwɔp.
Yesu arɛm yɛ ntá bo Israɛl abhɛn mánóko yi bɛ, “Bǎchí bakoŋo bha tɛtɛp mbák mǎndɔ́k ambɨ bɛkoŋo bɛyɔŋ ɛbha,
Afɔ̌ kɛ̌ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bárɔ́ yi bábʉɛ́.
Chi bɛkwak bǒnkwɔ kɛ̌ Mandɛm áchyɛ̀ akap anɛ́ átɔ̀ŋ bɛ́ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ achí nɛ mmu.
“Ɛ́bɛp ntá bǒ mmɨk ɛcha, mbɔnyunɛ bɔ́ bátwɔ̀ nɛ mamɔ anɛ ákʉ̀ bo mankwɛn ndǔ bɛbʉ́! Mamɔ ápú nɔk bɛ́twɔ, kɛ chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛ́p ntá mmu anɛ átwɔ̀ nɛ mamɔ ɛncha!
Sɛ́rɔ́ yɛ Táya, áchwí ápɔ́kɔ bhɛsɛ kpát sɛ́gháka Tolemays. Sɛ́rɔ áchwí sɛ́kó ɛtɔk sɛ́káka bakoŋo Yesu abhɛn bachi arɛ, nɛ sɛbhak nɛ bhɔ́ ndǔ nywɔp nɛmɔt.
Ɔkɔŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛchí chak nɛ ɔpap ɛpɨŋ ɛnɛ bo bapu bhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé. Mɛ Mandɛm ywɛ nkʉ yɛ wɔ ɔ́mbɔ́ŋ maŋák mbɔnyunɛ nchyɛ́ wɔ kɛnókó ɛkɛ́n kɛ́chá ɛkɛn mamʉɛrɛ bhɛ mankɛm.”
andɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Mpok anɛ Mandɛm ábhak nɛ bho mbɔ Mfɔ wap arɔp chi kɛkwɔt. Tɨ́k ká nsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛka, mǎnókó Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́!”
Yesu nɛ bakoŋo bhi báfʉɛ́t báré rɔŋ ndǔ bɔ̌bɛtɔk abhɛn bachi kɛkwɔt Seséria Fílipi. Ambi, Yesu abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Bo bárɛ̀m bɛ mɛ nchí agha?”
Nɛ nɛ́rɨ́ kɛ sɛ́bɨti Mandɛm Ɛtayɛsɛ. Nɛ nkúbhɛ́ nɛrɨ́ kɛ sɛ́sɔ̀t bɛrɛm bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ntá bo abhɛn Mandɛm ághókó, akʉ mǎmbák mbɔ yímbɔŋ ndǔ bɛyǎ babhi.
Baghɔkɔ Yesu babho bɛkɛm ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ batɨ ndu bɛ́rɨŋɨ mmu wap anɛ áchá abhɛnɛfu.
Yesu ayibhiri mmʉɛt arɛm ntá bakoŋo bhi bɛ, “Nchí ghati bhe bɛ ɛ́bè mmʉɛt tontó bɛ mǔnkáp anka Mandɛm ambak Mfɔ ywi.
Mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ batu ángók ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm ághàti bɛká bǒnkwɔ.’” 
Bágó ngɛ́bhɛ́ ntantaŋ amɔt ndǔ ɛyi ɛkotákátí ɛbhe awɔ́nɛm Yesu. Bákʉ́ ɛnyu ɛ́mɔ́t nɛ achák ɛbhe awɔghɔ yi.
Mmu Israɛl amɔt anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ Apólos atwɔ́ Ɛ́fɛsɔs. Ɛtɔk nɛbhe ɛyi ɛ́bhák Aleksándriya. Yi achí nyaka mmu anɛ árɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛrɛm kɛpɨ nɛ arɨŋɨ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm sayri.
Kɛ Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Koŋó mɛ. Dɔ̌ bawú mámbɛ́mɛ́ ngú wap.” 
Yesu ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́pay ɛkáti yɔ, akuti yɔ́, akɛmɛ ntá mǔnti arɔk achɔkɔ amɨk. Bǒ mankɛm abhɛn bachi amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí bátɛp yi amɨ́k amʉɛt.
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bákɔ̀ bárɔ̀ŋ báchwɔ́p ndu mɔ́tɔkɔ́fú. Ngɔrɛ́ amɔt anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ Matá abhak arɛ. Asyɛpti Yesu amɔ ápay amɛm ɛkɛt ɛyi.
Ndu árɛ̀m nɔ, bǒ bati anwi bátwɔ́ nɛ mbɛ́ntí amɔt anɛ bápɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ bɛkpaka.
Mbɔ̌ŋ bɔ̌maya batí atay. Ghatí yi ándɔ́k ánsɛmti bhɔ bɛ bákɛ́ twɔ nkwɔ́ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛ́t nɛnyiɛ́ ámɛ́n anɛ.’
Ɛchi ɛnyumɔt ɛchɔŋ. Bǎru bo bachi ndǔ nkwɔ bo Israɛl abhɛn Mandɛm áyábhɛ́ ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhi.
Nnɛ́mámɨk wu ayók ndɛ yi amɛsɛ awu, afate, báyá yi arɔk ntá Yesu.
Nɛ aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛtɔk ɛnɛ́ básíɛptí bhe arɛ́, bák ká amɛm ɛkɛt ɛ́mɔt kpátɛ mǎndɔ ɛtɔk ɛyɔ.
Nɛ bǎrɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kɛ̀m yi ansɛm. Abhɔŋ bɛ́bhési chi mbák mpok yi akway.
Mbɔk bho bábhák arɛ́ abhɛn báyàŋ mbi bɛrɛm bɛ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bɛchi nɛ Yesu. Bátɛ́p yɛ yi amɨ́k amʉɛt bɛghɔ mbák chɔŋ Yesu ambú mmǔ wu ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt.
Nɛ Mandɛm mmu árɨ́ŋɨ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi bhɛsɛ antɨ arɨ́ŋɨ́ nkwɔ nkaysi Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ, mbɔnyunɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ǎnɨ̀kmʉɛt ɛ̌ti bo Mandɛm kɛ ǎkoŋo chi nkaysi Mandɛm.
“Sɛ́ghok ndǔ yi árɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Chɔŋ mmokoti ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm ɛnɛ báté nɛ amɔ, nɛ bɛkʉ manywɔp arat, nte ɛ́chák ɛnɛ́ puyɛ̌ bo kɛ báté.’”
Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛ yɛ̌ ɛwak, Mandɛm apú bhák Mfɔ ntá bǒ abhɛn bápú chak kɛ? Mmu ákɛ́ rwɔ mmʉɛt. Yɛ̌ agha anɛ ákʉ̀ barak ɛpʉsi, yɛ̌ agha anɛ ákòŋo bɔmandɛm bachak, nɛ bakwɛnɛ́ bɛrwɔp, nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbakanɛm anɛ ákʉ̀ kɛbhʉ́rɛ́ nɛ ntɨ mbakanɛm nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ngɔrɛ́ anɛ ákʉ̀ kɛbhʉ́rɛ́ nɛ ntɨ ngɔrɛ́,
Nɛ ɛbhé ɛyi chi bɛ sɛ́nókó Yesu Kristo mmu achi Mɔ́ywi nɛ bɛ sɛ́nkɔŋ batɨ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔnyǔ yi aghati bhɛsɛ bɛ sɛnkʉ.
Asɛnɛ nɛ mɛniɛ, ambɨkɨ nɔkɔ ndǔ ánòŋsi nɛ bɛyǎ bɛbe.
Mɛ Símun Píta, mǔbɛtok, nɛ mǔnto Yesu Kristo kɛ nchí sɨŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ. Nchí sɨŋ ntá bo abhɛn mánoko Yesu Kristo mbɔ bhɛsɛ. Yi mmu achi Mandɛm ywɛsɛ nɛ Mpɛmɛ ywɛsɛ kɛ akʉ bɛsɛ́ mankɛm sɛ́bhɔŋ nɛka nɛ yi. Yi achi chak ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ yi ákʉ.
Pɔ̌l are yáŋ bɛrɔŋ ndǔ nchɛmti-bǒ bhɔ bɛ ádɛm ɛnyɨŋ, kɛ bakoŋo Yesu kɛchyɛ yí mbi bɛ ánkʉ nɔ.
Babhabhɛri bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n bápɛtnsɛm. Báre kway mámbɨti nɔkɔ Mandɛm mbɔnyunɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn bághɔ́ nɛ ɛbhɛn baghoko, bɛchi ɛnyumɔt mbɔnyu ángɛl aghati bhɔ. 
Nɛfú anɛ Yesu áfú amɛm áchwí asɛbhɛ angɔkɔnyɛ́n, mmǔ amɔt anɛ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri afú ndǔ nɛbhʉɛ́rɛ́ manɛm arɔk atɛmɛri yi.
Mbɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɛyǎ maŋák ndu bɛtɛmɛri mbɔk bɔ̌bhɛ nɛ bɛghɔ bɛ bɔ́ bákòŋo tɛtɛp Mandɛm nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Mandɛm Ɛta ághátí bɛsɛ sɛ́nkʉ́.
Mbák sɛ́ndɛ́m bɛ sɛpu bǒ bɛbʉ́, nɔ́ sɛ́rwɔ̀ chi mmʉɛt nɛ tɛtɛp apú amɛm batɨ yɛsɛ.
Ɛnyɨŋ Mandɛm áyàŋ chi bɛ mǎmbák nyáŋá, bɛ bǎkɛ́ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛkʉ nɛ barak ɛ́pusi.
Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mmu afyɛ́ anyu, ɛ́nsɛp yí mɛniɛ, ǎjì yɔ amfɛrɛ?
Ɛ́chí ɛnyu ɛyɔ mbɔnyunɛ bɛsí Mandɛm Ɛtayɛsɛ, sɛ́pú ghɔkɔntɨk bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn bǎkʉ̀ ndǔ bǎbhɔŋɔ nɛka nɛ Yesu, nɛ ɛnyǔ bǎdɛ́nɛ́ mmʉɛt ndǔ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛka ɛ̌ti ɛkɔŋ, nɛ ɛnyǔ bǎte kpirí ndǔ nɛbhakántɨ́ ɛnɛka nɛ Yesu Kristo Acha.
mbɨ́kɨ́ rɔ bɛkaka Mandɛm ɛ̌ti yɛka ndǔ mpok anɛ mɛ̌nɨ̀kmʉɛt.
Mbɔ̌ŋ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ bɛchak ɛbhɛn nchí kway bɛrɛm ɛ̌ti Yesu mǔngo bachiǎkap ywɛsɛ. Kɛ chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́bè mmʉɛt bɛkʉ be mǎnjwimɛm tɛ̌ndu bǎrɔ́bhɛ́ chi bo abhɛn bapu kɛm ɛnyɨŋ ayak.
Ɛchi yɛ bɛ mmu ǎghok kɛ anoko, nɛ mpok bághàti bho ɛ̌ti Kristo, bo bághòk Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́.
Bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ Yesu atwɔ́ nyaka fá amɨk chí bɛfɛrɛ bɛsɛ ndǔ nɛpɛmɛ́ bɛbʉ́, nɛ bɛbʉ́ bɛ́pú nɛ yí.
Nchí rɛm nɔ mbɔnyunɛ Jɔ̌n Njwiti atwɔ́ nyaka ntá yɛka bo Israɛl mankɛm, bɛtɔŋ bé ɛnyǔ mmu ákwáy bɛbhʉrɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛni chak bɛsí Mandɛm, kɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ noko ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ̀m. Babhɛbhɛ́ nkabhɛnti nɛ baghɔrɛ́-nɛkɔ kɛ̌ mánókó ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ̀m. Yɛ̌ndu bǎghɔ́ bɛ́ babhɛbhɛ́ nkábhɛ́nti nɛ baghɔrɛ́-nɛkɔ mánóko Jɔ̌n, bǎkɛ tɨ́knsɛm bɛ mǎnókó ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yí árɛ̀m.” 
Bɛbhɛ́ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áchyɛ́ ntá Moses bɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ kway nyaka bɛpɛmɛ bhɛsɛ ndǔ bɛbʉ́ nɛ ntí bɛ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛsɛ mbɔ bakwǎŋwaŋ, sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ nyaka bɛtaŋ bɛbhʉrɛ bhɔ. Mandɛm kɛ ápɛ́mɛ́ bhɛsɛ ndǔ átó mbɔŋ Mɔ́ywi, nɛ yí atwɔ́ fá amɨk nɛ nɛpɛmɛ́ nkwǎnwaŋ mmu ákʉ̀ bɛbʉ́. Nɛ ndu atwɔ́ ɛnyu yɔ, akʉ bɛ bɛbʉ́ bɛkɛpɛrɛ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ amfǎy bho.
Ɛkʉ mbɔk batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm abhɛn bachi arɛ bábho bɛrɛm nɛ mmʉɛ́t ɛyap bɛ, “Ǎrɛm kpát mbɔ bhɛ́ achi Mandɛm! Mandɛm aywǐnti kɛ̌ ákway bɛ́fóŋóri bɛbʉ́ mmu!”
Achák akwɛnti ndǔ mmɨk sɛtárɛ́bhɛ́ anɛ ntɔp abhɨkɨ ya arɛ. Awakari achak.
Símun aghoko nɔkɔ nɔ, akɛmɛ Píta nɛ Jɔ̌n bɛ, “Bɔta, nɨk ka Mandɛm mmʉɛt ɛ̌ti ya bɛ́ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛ́mɔt ɛnɛ bǎrɛ́mɛ́ ɛ́kɛ́ fakari nɛ mɛ.”
Babhak arɛ́ nɛ bakoŋo Yesu ndǔ mpǎy bataŋ.
Yesu arɛm yɛ bɛ, “Ghók ká, mɛ́twɔ̀ mandú mpok! Nchí twɔ́ nɛ akap bɛ nkáp yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu bɛ́kóŋo bɛtɨk ɛbhɛ́n yi ákʉ́.
Bǒfú bátwɔ́ nɛ mbɛ́ntí amɔt anɛ bápɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ bɛkpaka ntá yi. Yesu ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyǔ nɛka ɛnɛ́n bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ yi bɛ abhɔŋ bɛtaŋ bɛbu mmu wu, arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Mɔ́wa, ɔ́kɛ́ chay, mfóŋórí bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛ.”
Ntá mmu amɔt Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ǎchyɛ akap bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay, ntá achák anchyɛ akap bɛghati bho mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛfu ntá Mandɛm. Ntá mmu amɔt ǎchyɛ akap bɛrɨŋɨ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ nɛ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ, ntá achák anchyɛ akap bɛrɛm bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛbhɛn yi abhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ, nɛ ntá anufú anchyɛ akap mɛ́nɛ́nɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mmu arɛmɛ ndǔ ɛyɔŋ ɛtɔk ɛnɛ yi abhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ.
Nɛ bě bho Kapɛ̌naum, bǎkaysi bɛ bǎkway bɛyoŋ mmʉɛt, mǎnkó kpát mǎntɔk nɛbu? Nsé! Chɔŋ Mandɛm amɛsɛ bhe amɛm ɛtɔkɔ́ bawú! Mbɔ amɛm ɛtɔk Sídɔn kɛ nkʉ́ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛbhɛn-nɛ nkʉ ntá yɛka, mbʉ yɔ ɛbhʉɛt téé tɛ̌ ɛchɔŋ!
Ɛ́kʉ́ Yesu aghati yɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Mǎnáŋ mǎnjoŋ Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm amfay, chɔŋ mǎndɨŋɨ bɛ́ nchí mmu anɛ nchí, nɛ bɛ́ mpú kʉ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ndǔ bɛtaŋ ɛbha. Nchí rɛm chí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛta ágháti mɛ ndɛ́m.
Yesu arɨŋɨ bapu amap, abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Ndaká yí mǎmɔ̀ mɛ? Tɔ́ŋ ká mɛ ɛbhɔ́kɔ́ nkáp.”
Kaká ká María mmu ákʉ́ bɛyǎ bɛtɨk ndǔ nkwɔ ywɛka.
Mbuɔt anɛfu akwɛnti ndǔ mmɨk anɛ tákɔ nsěnse ágò arɛ. Achak are gó, kɛ tákɔ nsěnse agó áchók yɔ. Akɛ fyɛ́.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛ́gháti Jɔ̌n bɛ, “Sɨ́ŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ tó ntá ángɛl anɛ ábhàbhɛri bǒnkwɔ abhɛn ɛtɔk Filadɛ́lfia. Sɨ́ŋ kʉ́ bɔ mándɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fù ntá mmǔ anɛ achi Nyáŋá, mmǔ tɛtɛp, yí mmu ákɛ́mɛ́ ɛfɨŋɨ́ Mfɔ Debhít. Mpok yi ánɛ́nɛ́ yɛ̌ mmu apu kway bɛtyɛp, nɛ mpok yi atyɛbhɛ, yɛ̌ mmu apú kwáy mɛ́nɛ́nɛ.”
Bě bǒnkwɔ Kristo atú Judɛ́ya bǎbhɨkɨ re ghɔ nyaka mɛ nɛ amɨ́k.
Ɛkʉ báré rɛm nɛ batɨ bɛ, “Sɛ́kɛ́ dakati nkú anɛ. Sɛ́ngʉɛ́p chí ɛbháŋá, sɛ́ngɔ́ mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛsɔt yɔ.” Ɛ́fákárí ɛnyunɛ bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ́mɛ́ ɛ́mfú tɛtɛp. Nɔ́ chí, basɨ̌ŋ amɛn árɛ̀m bɛ, “Básɔ́t ndɛn aya bákɔ́rɛ́. Bágʉɛ́p ɛbháŋá bɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́sɔt nkú aya.”
Bɛyǎ bo bátwɔ̀ chɔŋ mánsɔt nnyɛ́n ɛna mántɛn ambɨ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap andɛm nɔkɔ bɛ ‘Yi kɛ achi Mpɛmɛ anɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtó!’ Nɛ mándwɔ bɛyǎ bhó bɛ mánjibhiri batɨ yap.
Yɛ̌ ɔchí agha, mpok ɔ́tàŋ bo abhɛn bákʉ̀ mɛnyu mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ, kɛ wɔmbɔŋ ɔ́nkʉ nɔkɔ bhɔ, ɔkaysi bɛ ɔ̌kway bɛbʉɛ ɛnyu ɛnɛ Mandɛm apu chyɛ wɔ ntɛmsi kɛ?
Yesu aghati baghɔkɔ́ bhi bɛ, “Ntí apu bɛghati bhɔ bɛ mándɔ́k mánjáŋ nɛnyíɛ́. Bě babhɔŋ, chyɛ̌ ká bhɔ nɛnyíɛ́ mányíɛ́.”
Apólos ákʉ ntɨ bɛ́rɔ́ŋ Akáiya. Bǒbati bakoŋo Yesu abhɛn Ɛ́fɛsɔs báfyɛ́ yi ntɨ nɛ básɨ́ŋ ɛkáti ntá bakoŋo Yesu abhɛn Akáiya bɛkʉ bɛ mánsyɛpti yi sayri. Aghaka nɔkɔ arɛ́, akwak tontó bo abhɛn Mandɛm atɔŋ bɔ bɛrɨ̌ndu nɛ mánóko.
Mɛ̌tò wɔ mmu awu. Mbák ɛ́pú Atɛ́mas, chɔŋ ɛ́mbak Tíkíkɔs. Nɛghɔ́ anɛ ɔ́ghɔ́ mmu wap, ɔ́kɛ́ nɔ́k bɛ́twɔ ayak ndu bɛtɛmɛri mɛ ɛtɔk Nikópolis. Arɛ́ kɛ̌ mɛ̌bhák mpok manyiɛp áyá nɛ mbǎŋ ǎkwɛn tontó.
Mpok yɔ, áchwí anɛ ápɔ́kɔ́ baghɔkɔ́ bhi anaŋ arɔŋ nyaka nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ bɛfu angɔkɔnyɛ́n. Mbʉ́ɛ́p ataŋataŋ ɛre fú bhɔ ambɨ. Ɛ́kʉ́ mpɛ́rɛ́nyɛn ɛya ɛ́cha, bɔ mánu nɔkɔ nɛ yɔ.
Sɛ́kɛ́pɛrɛ bhák bo abhɛn bachi mbɔ mɔ́áchwi anɛ mpɛ́rɛ́nyɛn ɛ́dɛ̀p ɛ́ntɛn ɛbhé ɛ́mɔt, ɛ́ndɛp ɛntɛn ɛbhé ɛchak mpok batɔŋɔ́ nse bárwɔ̀ bhɔ nɛ nsé yap. Batɔŋɔ́ nse bhɔ bákʉ̀ bo manɛm ɛbhɨ ndu bákòŋo baraká nse anɛ bɔ́ bátɔ̀ŋ.
Ntɔ̌ŋ be chi ɛrɨŋ bɛ be nkwɔ mǎnkʉ́ nɔ́kɔ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ nkʉ.
Chɔŋ ɛ́ndɨ ɛncha ntá bo abhɛn Mandɛm akʉ mánjámbɨ mampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Báchi nyáŋá nɛ nɛwú ɛnɛn nɛjwi apay nɛ́pú kway bɛtɔk bhɔ. Chɔŋ bɔ mámbak bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ Kristo. Chɔŋ bɔ́ mámbak bafɔ nɛ Kristo ndu mamiɛ́ nka amɔt. 
Kaká mɛ Príska nɛ Akwíla. Kaká ɛfo ɛnɛ́ Ɔnɛsifórɔs nkwɔ́.
Símun Píta abhʉɛ́t nyaka téé, angwaka nɔkɔ ngo. Mbɔk bo abhɛn bachi arɛ bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Pú wɔ nkwɔ́ ɔchí nkoŋo ywi?” Píta ataŋa, arɛm bɛ, “Cháá, mpú nɛ yi”
Ɛchi mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ Mandɛm arɛm nyaka bɛ, “Nkɔŋ Jekɔ́p, kɛ mpap Isau.”
Yesu arɔk ɛtɔk ɛ́chák achwe amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí ɛyap.
Ntɔŋ ɛbhé arɛm ntá Yesu bɛ, “Ntɔŋ ɔrɛm sáyri! Ɛ́chi tɛtɛp mbɔnyu ɔ́rɛ́mɛ́ bɛ́ Mandɛm Acha achi amɔt, achák apú.
Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ beku ndǔ nkúbhɛ́ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt ɛnɔ, bakoŋo Yesu bábhak amɛm ɛkɛt ɛ́mɔt nɛ babhǐnywɔ́p femfé ndu báchay bǒbati bo Israɛl. Yesu arɔk ate bɔ́ bɛsí, arɛm bɛ, “Kpák ámbák nɛ bhe.”
Kɛ nɛtɨ́k yi atɨ́kɨ́nsɛm ndǔ ɛ́kírísú, antɨŋ angɔkɔntɨk ɛnyǔ yi achi.
Puyɛ̌ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́chwè anyu kɛ̌ ɛ́kʉ̀ mmu ákɛ́ bhák pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí Mandɛm. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fú mmu anyu kɛ ɛ́kʉ̀ mmu ákɛ́ bhák pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí Mandɛm.”
Ndǔ manywɔbhɛ́ yɔ, Yesu akó amfǎy njiɛfú ndu mɛnɨkmʉɛt. Anɨkmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm bɛtǐ mɛnkɛm.
Kɛ yɛ̌ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛ́pú arɛ́. Yɛ̌ bábhɔŋ chí ɛrɨ́tí nkaysi yɛ̌ bábhɔŋ chí nkaysi mbʉ́mbʉ, nnɛ́m ɛnyɨŋ chí bɛ́ bo bághòk Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo. Ɛyɔ ɛ́chyɛ̀ mɛ maŋák.
Sɛ́bhaka nyaka ntɨ bɛ yí kɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́fɛ́rɛ bo Israɛl ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri. Ɛ́chí nɛ́nɛ manywɔp arat ɛnɛ́ ndak anɛ́ áfákárí.
Bakoŋo bhi mánók mbɔ bɔkilomɛta batay nɛ batandat. Bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ yi ákɔ̀ anyɛ́n átwɔ̀ kɛkwɔt nɛ bhɔ, bɛ́cháy bɛ́kɛ́m bhɔ tontó.
Yesu atɛ́m bɔ nɛkay nkwɔ bɛ, “Nnɛmámɨ́k apu kway bɛyǎ ntɨ nnɛ́mámɨ́k mbi. Mbák ándɔ́k bɛkʉ nɔ, bɔ́ batí apay bápú kwɛn amɛm nɛpi?
Yesu aghati yi bɛ, “Ɔnáŋ ɔghɔ̌ yi, nɛ yí kɛ árɛ̀m kɛpɨ nɛ wɔ nɛ́nɛ.”
“Bákway mbʉ bɛti bawɛrɛ́riɛp amɛn anchyɛ nkáp anɛ́ nkʉbɛtɨk ányiɛ ndǔ mmíɛ́. Ndaká yí bábhɨ́kɨ́ tí mɔ́ mánsɔt nkáp mánchyɛ ntá bachɛ́bhɛ́bho?”
Ngók ndǔ bɔ bákwày nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ bɛ “Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n anɛ báwáy nyaka, akwǎy mmu anɛ bo bárɛ̀m ɛ̌ti yi bɛ, yí kɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ mɛnkɛm. yi kɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm yi kɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak nɛnkɛm yi kɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ kɛfɔ kɛnkɛm. yi kɛ bo babhɔŋɔ bɛchyɛ kɛnókó, nɛ mámbɨti yi kɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛyǎ mɛnwɔp!”
‘Sɛ́kwáy bakwáy nɛbhay bɛ mǎmbɛn nɛbhɛ́n kɛ bǎbhɨkɨ bhɛn. Sɛ́kwáy bakwáy nɛwú, kɛbhɔ bě kɛdi!’
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Bě mkpaká bho anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ nɛka nɛ mɛ, bě bho bǎyìbhiri tɛtɛp ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛchak, chɔŋ mpɛt ntat nɛ bhe ná? Chɔŋ nkɛ́pntɨ nɛ bhe ngaka fá?” Kɛ ǎrɛm bɛ, “Twɔ́ ká nɛ mɔ́wu fá ntá ya.”
Ɛwak ɛ́mɔt, Pɔ̌l arɛm ntá Banábas bɛ, “Sɛ́mpɛtnsɛm ndu yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛtɔk ɛnɛ sɛ́ghátí ɛyɔŋ Acha arɛ sɛ́ngɔ́ ndǔ bǒnkwɔ́ báchí.”
Mpok ákwáy nɔ́kɔ́, Yesu achɔkɔ ndu ɛ́fɛ́mɛ́ nɛnyiɛ nɛ bǒnto.
Nkaysi Mandɛm anɛ bakwǎŋwaŋ básɔ̀t bɛ́ chi ɛpɔ̌ndak, chí nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnɛ́n nɛ́yá tontó nɛ́chá nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnɛn bǒ mmɨk. Nɛ bɛtɨk Mandɛm ɛbhɛ́n bo básɔ̀t bɛ́ bɛ́pú yɛ̌nyɨŋ, bɛ́bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́yǎ bɛ́chá bɛtaŋá bǒ mmɨk.
Dɨŋɨ́ yɛ́ ka bɛ, ɛwak ɛnɛ Mandɛm átàŋ bǒ mmɨk, chɔŋ angɔ́ ntínso nɛ bǒ ɛtɔk Sódom ancha bhe.” 
Mbok akɔ aghaka ntá bǒnkwɔ Yesu abhɛn Yerúsalɛm. Bátó Banábas ɛtɔk Ántiɔk.
Yɛ̌ mɛmbɔŋ mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ nyaka bɛ chi yí, kɛ ntí anɛ ntwɔ́ njwiti nɔkɔ bho nɛ manyiɛp chí ndu bɛkʉ bo Israɛl mandɨŋɨ mmu yi achi.”
Bǎghɔ́kɔ́ntɨk ndu ndɨ́kɨ́ nka bho ɛtay nɛ bɛkpɔkɔ́ brɛt bɛtay? Anɛ árɔ́bhɛ́ abhak bɛkay mɛ́ni?” Bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Bió nɛ bɛpay.”
Arɛm nyaka bɛ, “Chɔŋ Ngɔsɔ́ŋ anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ re rɨŋɨ mbakanɛm ampɔkɔ mɛniɛ ambé mɔ́mbakanɛm, nnyɛ́n ɛni nɛmbak bɛ Ɛmánuɛl”, nɔ́ chí bɛ, “Mandɛm achi nɛ bhɛsɛ.”
Ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ ɔ́kʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ ɔ́kʉ̀ bhɔ́, sɛ́ka bhɔ nɛ sɛ́kàka wɔ.
Ɛrɛmɛ́ nsáy achí nɛ mmu anɛ ábhʉ̀ɛrɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛni mbɔ ɛnyu Mandɛm áyàŋ nɛ ambɔ́ŋ maŋák nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́.
Mmǔ wu árɛm bɛ́ “Nnáŋ nchí bhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm.”
Ngoko bɛtě ntɔp ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ amfay ntɔp ndu bɛkʉ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi akɔŋɔ nɛ ntɔp anɛ yi aghoko? Apú kway mɛnyɔbhɛri ntɔp ansɔt mbɔk anɨ́ ɛte ɛnɛ́ bábhʉ̀ɛrɛ nyáŋá ndǔ bɛpa, ansɔt ntɔp áchák anɨ ɛte ɛnɛ bákʉ mɛnyɨŋ nɛ yɔ manywɔp ankɛm-ɛ?
Achyɛ nyaka mmʉɛt bɛ́ anku bo mankɛm ámfɛ́rɛ́ ndǔ kɛsɛmɛ́ bɛbʉ́. Akʉ nɔ ndǔ mpok Mandɛm áyábhɛ́ bɛ́tɔŋ kpoŋoroŋ bɛ́ ǎyaŋ bɛ́pɛ́mɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu.
Bɛ́fu Bɛ́tani bɛ́gháka Yerúsalɛm achi nyaka mbɔ nɛkɔ̌ bɔkilomɛta babay nɛ ɛbhɔk,
Mmu anɛ nchí nsɛm nta yi apú. Yɛ̌ nɔ́, mɛmbɔŋ nkʉ mmʉɛ́t ɛya nsɛm ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ndǔ nchí yaŋ bɛ́kwák bɛyǎ bo mántwɔ́ ntá Yesu Acha.
“Yɛ̌ mmu apu kwáy bɛtok bachi bati apay ndɔŋ amɔt. Mbák ámbɔ́ŋ bachi bapay, ǎkɔŋ amɔt ancha anɛfú, mbák ɛ́pú nɔ́, ǎchyɛ kɛnókó ntá amɔt, ambyák anɛfu. Mmu apu kwáy bɛtok Mandɛm antok nɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋ mmɨk.
Bɔ Pɔ̌l bágháti yɛ yí nɛ ɛfo ɛyi Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu Acha.
Ndɔp yɛ chi mǔmpap aywɛka ndu ngátí bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi tɛtɛp kɛ?
Pú bɔ́ bhɔ kɛ bárɛ̀m bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ndu bɛ́chɔ́ŋti ɛrɨ́tɨ́ nnyɛ́n Ɛtayɛka mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bhe?
Mánaŋ mámfóŋórí bɛbʉ́ bho, ntí apu pɛrɛ bhak anɛ bɔ báchyɛ akap. 
Nɛ nɛ́nɛ, chɔŋ Mandɛm andɔ ɛkɛt ɛyɛka, ɛ́ndɔp ɛnyu yɔ.
Mbɔnyunɛ mbák mmu andɛm kpoŋoroŋ bɛ Yesu achi Acha, nɛ anoko amɛm ntɨ ɛni bɛ Mandɛm akʉ nyaka yi áfú ndǔ nɛwú apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, Mandɛm ǎpɛmɛ yi.
Bɔ̌ chi amɔt bati tándrámɔt báchí nyaka. Anɛ mbɨ abháy ngɔrɛ́, agú kɛbhɔŋ yɛ̌ mmɔ́.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛpɛt ɛ́kʉ̀ sɛngɔ kpoŋoroŋ bɛ ɛbhé ɛ́yíbhiri, chi nɛtwɔ anɛ nchiakap achak átwɔ́ mbɔ Mɛlkísɛdɛk.
Sɛ́ndɔ́k yɛ kɛkwɔt kɛbhɔŋ bɛcháy ntá Mandɛm mmu achi ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ ɛyi. Achí Mandɛm bɛrɨ̌ndu nɛ chɔŋ angɔ́ bhɛsɛ ntínso, antɔŋ bhɛsɛ bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhi ndu bɛkwak bhɛsɛ́ ndǔ mpok anɛ sɛ́chɛ́bhɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ.
Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Bě bo Israɛl bǎkʉ̀ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl bárɛ̀m ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti Mandɛm.”
Kpátɛ mpok ɛyɔ, nkɛ rɨŋɨ bɛ́ chí yí. Kɛ Mandɛm mmu átó mɛ njwiti bho nɛ manyiɛp, anáŋ aghati nyaka mɛ bɛ, ‘Mmu anɛ ɔ́ghɔ́ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm asɛbhɛ arɔp nɛ yi, yí wu kɛ achi mmu anɛ ájwìti bho nɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ.’
Kaysí ka Yesu mmu bǒ bɛbʉ́ báre kʉ yi bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ, yɛ̌ nɔ ate kpirí ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ mɛnkɛm, bɛ batɨ ákɛ́ nɛ́m be amɛm, mǎmfɛrɛ amɔ.
Bǒ abhɛn bághɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́fákári, báré ghati abhɛn batwɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fákárí kɛ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ́rɔ́ mmu anɛ bɔ bɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri nyaka, yi ataŋ.
Mpok akway anɛ Mandɛm átàŋ mmɨk nɛ, mpok ákway anɛ báfɛ̀rɛ mfɔ mmɨk nɛ ndǔ kɛfɔ ɛki.
Yɛ̌ mmu ápú chyɛ mmʉɛt kɛnókó andɛm bɛ yi ǎkway bɛbhak mǔngo bachiǎkap. Mandɛm kɛ áyap mmu, ankʉ yí ambak mǔngo bachiǎkap nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyu ákʉ́ nyaka nɛ Árɔn.
“Chɔŋ njɛnti mkpáká bho abhɛn ɛchɔŋ nɛ yi? Báchí mbɔ bɔ̌ abhɛn báchɔ́kɔ́ nɛfísiɛ bákʉ̀ ntok. Ɛka ɛ́mɔt barɛm ntá abhɛn ɛka ɛchak bɛ,
Nchí sɛmti wɔ bɛ́ ɔ́ngátí nɔ́kɔ́ bho Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm. Kɛ́rɔ bɛ́ghati bhɔ́. Mpok yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́kɔ̀ sayri, ghati bho. Yɛ̌ chí mpok anɛ mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́pu kɔ sayri, ghatí bhɔ́. Kʉ bo mándɔ bɛbʉ́ bhap. Ji bhɔ́ mandɔ́ bɛbʉ́ bhap. Kɛ fyɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bɔ́ ntɨ nkwɔ́. Kʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nɛ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ nɛ ntɨ bɛtɔŋ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm.
Samuɛl nɛ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ abhɛn báfú yi ansɛm, mankɛm bárɛm nyaka nkwɔ́ ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́fàkari manywɔp anɛ́ ɛchɔŋ.
Bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi arɛmɛ báchyɛ bakak ntá Mandɛm. Barɛm yɛ ntá Pɔ̌l bɛ, “Manɔ́, wɔmbɔ̌ŋ ɔghɔ ndǔ bɛyǎ nká bo Israɛl mánókó Yesu, nɛ bábhʉɛt bɛfyɛ bɛtaŋ ndu bɛbhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé Moses sayri.
Yesu Kristo áchyɛ́ bhɛsɛ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ sɛ́ndɨŋɨ Mandɛm mmu ábhɨ́ŋɨ́ bhɛsɛ bɛ sɛ́mbɔ́ŋ kɛnɛ́m nɛ yi, nɛ bɛ sɛ́nkoŋo ɛpɨŋ ɛyi ɛnɛ́ ɛrɨ ɛcha. Ndu sɛ́rɨ̀ŋɨ yi, ǎchyɛ bhɛsɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chɛ́bhɛ́ bhɛsɛ. Nɛ ǎchyɛ bhɛsɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi bɛ sɛ́mbɔ́ŋ nɛpɛ́m nɛkɔ nɛ ɛpɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bo Mandɛm bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛbhɔŋ.
Mandɛm ántɔ́ŋ be bɛrɨ̌ndu andɔk nɔkɔ chi ambɨ, anchyɛ bɛ kpák anɛ ájwi amɛm batɨ yɛka ndǔ bǎrɨ̀ŋɨ yi nɛ Acha ywɛsɛ Yesu Kristo. 
Yí ápú syɛp nkɔ́rɛ́-tákɔ́ anɛ abho bɛwɔsi, arɔp chi bɛ́gu. Nɛ apú nɛmɛ ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛnɛ bawɛt amay amɛm, ɛ́rɔ́p chi mandú mɛ́nɛ́mɛ. Ɛnyu yɔ kɛ̌ yi arɔŋ ambɨ bɛghɔ bhɔ ntínso, kpátɛ yi ankʉ nkaysi anɛ achi tɛtɛp ansɔt awɔ́nɛm.
Mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Mandɛm ánjɛ́t mmu anɛ átwɔ̀ ndǔ nnyɛ́n Acha! Mandɛm Mfay kɛ áchyɛ̀ kpák. Sɛ́nchíɛ yí kɛnókó!”
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Ngátí bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́ bǎkɛ́ kwɛn ansɛm.
Bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ yi ákɔ̀ anyɛ́n átwɔ̀, bɛ́cháy bɛ́kɛ́m bɔ́ tontó. Bábho bɛbɨk, mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Chí ɛfóŋó-ngú! Chi ɛfóŋó-ngú!”
Akɛ́m nnyɔ́ anɛ tɛ nyaka, yɔ́ nɛ achi mfɔ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ nɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ Satan agwɔ́t nɛ ngɛm. Abhak ɛnyu yɔ ndǔ mamiɛ́ nka amɔt.
Mandɛm abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɨŋɨ bhɛsɛ chí bɛ sɛmbak bǒ ɛpúsí, abhɨ́ŋɨ́ bhɛsɛ bɛ sɛ́mbak nyáŋá bɛsí bhi.
Are tɔ́ŋ yɛ bho andɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Pú basɨ́ŋ Mandɛm arɛm bɛ, ‘Ɛkɛt ɛya ɛ́bhɔŋ bɛbhak chi ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí ntá bo bɛtɔkɔ́ mmɨk mɛnkɛm’, kɛ bǎyíbhírí yɔ́ ɛ́rɔp chi ɛkɛt ɛnɛ́ baghɛ́p bábhɛ̀sɛ arɛ!”
Mmu akwáy bɛbhɛp bɛ, “Chɔŋ Mandɛm ankʉ bawú mámpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ná? Bápɛ̀tnsɛm nɛ ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ mmʉɛt?”
Ángɛl anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛyǎ bɛtaŋ asɔt yɛ ɛrɛmɛ ntay ɛnɛn nɛchi mbɔ ntay bɛkɔk mɛnyɨŋ amɛsɛ amɛm manyu, arɛm bɛ, “Ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ kɛ básɔt chɔŋ ɛrɛm ɛtɔk Bábilɔn mándɛp amɨk nɛ bɛtaŋ, bǒ kɛpɛrɛ kway bɛghɔ yɔ.
Kɛ bǒnto básɔ́t ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ baghɔrɛ́ bhɔ bárɛ́mɛ́ mbɔ ɛráká ndak, bɔ́ kɛnókó wáwák.
Manɛ́m, kɔŋ ka baghɔrɛ́ bhɛka, nɛ bǎkɛ́ bhak bɛbebɛbe nɛ bhɔ.
Mpú yaŋ bɛ ntwɔ́ ngɔ́ bhe mfʉɛrɛ fʉɛt. Mbɔ̌ŋ ntɨ bɛ́twɔ bɛtat nɛ bhe, mbák Mandɛm ankwak.
Bě babhɔŋ bǎghɔ̀ nɛ bǎghòk ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ Pɔ̌l ákʉ̀, puyɛ̌ chí ndiɛrɛ fá Ɛ́fɛsɔs, kɛ atú Esia ankɛm. Akʉ bɛyǎ bo báka nɛ yi ndu yi árɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Bɔmandɛm abhɛn bo bághókó nɛ amɔ bápú bo mandɛm wáwák!’
Mbák bǒ nkwɔ́ mándɛ́m bɛ́ mǔnti akʉ ndak, kɛ́tɨŋɨ ka, kpatɛ batísiɛ mámfú mbɔ batí ápay nɛ arat.
Ǎchɔ̀kɔ nɛ Símun ngoko nkwɔbhɛ́nya. Ɛkɛt Símun wu ɛchi angɔkɔ manyu.”
ankwak bɔ bɛkʉ manto Pɔ̌l Yerúsalɛm. Mǎnaŋ batɨ nyaka bɛ bo mámbɛ́sɛ́ ambi mankɛm yi mangway.
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu árɔ́ nɛbhʉɛt wu árɔ̀ŋ ambɨ, manɛ́mámɨk bati apay babho bɛkoŋo yi mámbɨk nɔkɔ bɛ, “Mmɔ̌ Mfɔ Debhít, ghɔ́ bhɛsɛ ntínso!”
Nchí ghati bhe bɛ Mandɛm ásɔ́t nyaka bɛ mbɛbhɛ́ nkabhɛ́nti wu achí chak bɛsí bhi. Ɛ́kɛbhák nɔ nɛ mǔnkwɔ Fárisi mbɔnyunɛ́ Mandɛm ǎsɛ̀pti yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ áyòŋ mmʉɛt, kɛ ǎkòsi yɛ̌ agha anɛ ásɛ̀pti mmʉɛt amɨk.” 
Mpok Ɛlísabɛt aghoko bakak María, mmɔ́ ayoŋ mmʉɛt amɛm mɛniɛ ɛbhi nɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ abhak nɛ yi tontó.
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ, mbák mmu abhɨ́kɨ́ rɔ Mandɛm ankɛm yi mbɔ mɔ́nkwɛn apú kway bɛbhak ndǔ mpǎy bo abhɛn Mandɛm achi Mfɔ wap wáwák. 
Bǎrɨŋɨ ɛnyu sɛ́kɛ̀m nyaka yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka mbɔ ɛnyǔ chi bhɔ ákɛ̀m bɔ̌bhi.
Ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ sɛ́kway bɛrɨŋɨ bɛ ɛkɔŋ Mandɛm ɛjwi bɛsɛ antɨ pɔɔt chi bɛ nywɔp Mandɛm átàŋ bo sɛpú bhɔŋ bɛcháy, mbɔnyunɛ sɛ́chí mbɔ Mɔ́ywi ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛsɛ́ fá amɨk.
Mbɔk bǒbatí ɛtɔk bábhák mamʉɛrɛ bhi. Bɔ́bhɔ bátó nkwɔ́ ɛyɔŋ mɛnɨk yi mmʉɛt bɛ akɛ sá ɛkak amɛm áchá.
Yɛ̌ ɛbɛ́ptí ɛyɔŋ ɛ́kɛ́ fu be anyu. Dɛm nɔ́kɔ́ ká chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́kwàk bo mántaŋ ndǔ mbi Mandɛm mbɔ ɛnyǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛgo. Mmu abhɔŋ bɛrɛm chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kwak abhɛn bághòk yi.
Ángɛl achak áfú amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm arɛm nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ ntǎ mmǔ anɛ achi chɔkɔ ndǔ ɛkpɔkɔ́ nɛbhaŋ bɛ, “Bo bɛ́kpɔt mbwɔt anɛ anaŋ ape nɛ ngak ayɛ mbɔnyunɛ mpok bɛfɛrɛ yɔ ndu bɛtɔkɔ́ mmɨk aghaka.”
Sɛ́fá Sírakɔs, sɛ́ghabhɛri sɛchwɔp ndǔ nɛchyɛ̌nyɛ́n ɛnɛn ɛtɔk Rejiɔm. Nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́, mbʉ́ɛ́p anɛ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ mbʉ́ɛ́p saut abho mɛnu, nɛ ndǔ ntɨnywɔp, sɛ́chwɔ́p ndǔ nɛchyɛ̌nyɛ́n ɛnɛn ɛtɔk Putioli, atú Itali. Sɛ́fú ndu áchwí sɛ́chwe ɛtɔk.
Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛpɛt ɛ́rɛ̀m ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt achak bɛ, “Bě bho bǎpú bo Israɛl, ŋák ka nɛ bo Mandɛm”,
Bǒbati bo Israɛl kɛnókó bɛ amɨ́k anaŋ anɛmɛ nyaka yi kɛ apɛt abho bɛghɔ mbaŋ, kpatɛ mpok bábhɨ́ŋɨ́ máyi nɛ ɛtayi,
Andru asɔt Símun arɔk ntá Yesu nɛ yi. Yesu ayɨŋɨ yí, arɛm bɛ, “Wɔ ɔchí Símun, mmɔ̌ Jɔ̌n. Chɔŋ nnyɛ́n ɛna nɛ́chák nɛ́mbak bɛ Sɛ́fas” [nɔ chí Sɛtárɛ́bhɛ́]. 
Ɛ́kʉ́ bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm báté ɛyu bɛ mángwáy Lásárɔs nkwɔ.
Chɔŋ manyǔbha ambak fúú mpoknkɛm. Bɛti bɛ́pú bhak arɛ.
Abho yɛ bɛ́rɔ́ŋ ndǔ bɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt bo Israɛl tɛ́mté angati nɔkɔ bo ɛ̌ti Yesu bɛ́, “Yesu áchí Mmɔ Mandɛm.”
Aghati bhɛsɛ́ ndu yí ághɔ́ ángɛl Mandɛm ɛkɛt ɛyi nɛ ángɛl wu ágháti yi bɛ ántó bo Jopa mámbɨŋɨ mɛ Símun Píta bɛ
Kɛ mbák bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛn sɛ́kʉ̀ bɛ́kʉ̀ bo mangɔ kpoŋoroŋ bɛ Mandɛm achi chak, chɔŋ sɛ́ngati bhɔ bɛ Mandɛm apu chak ndu bɛ́bentɨ anchyɛ bhɛsɛ ntɛmsi? [Nchí rɛm nɔ chi nɛ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnɛn bakwǎŋwaŋ.]
Yesu árɛ́mɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, bakoŋo bhi bákókósi mmʉɛt nɛ yi, barɛm bɛ, “Ɛta, ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ nɔ́ bɛ ndak anɛ ɔ́rɛ́mɛ́ ákʉ batɨ ábè bǒnkwɔ Fárisi?”
Mbɔ̌ŋ bɛcháy bɛ ngufú mpok ntwɔ́ awu bɛghɔ bhe nchí kway bɛtɛmɛri bhe ndu nte anɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ káysi bɛtɛmɛri bhe, nɛ be nkwɔ mǎngɔ bɛ mpú ndu nte anɛ bǎkaysi bɛghɔ mɛ. Ngufú, nchí kway bɛtɛmɛri bhe ndǔ bǎgwà, nɛ ndǔ bǎbhɔ̀ŋ mpabhamɨ́k nɛ batɨ, nɛ ndǔ ɛchókóntɨ, nɛ ndǔ mǎŋɛm mɛŋɛ́mɛ́, nɛ ndǔ bǎchɔŋti manyɛ́n batɨ, nɛ ndǔ ɛnaŋti, nɛ ndǔ ɛpɨŋ bɛkáysi bɛ bǎcha batɨ, nɛ ndǔ bǎkʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ táká táká.
Arɛ́, abhɔ́ŋ bɛtaŋ amfǎy bɔángɛl mankɛm nɛ bafɔ bhap, nɛ amfǎy yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ awu amfay nɛ fá amɨk. Abhɔŋ bɛtaŋ amfǎy bafɔ mankɛm, abhɛn bakwǎŋwaŋ nɛ abhɛn bachi bɛfóŋó nkwɔ amfǎy bo abhɛn báchí ndǔ nɛŋɔkɔ́mɨk ɛnɛn mfay ɛnɛn nɛ́twɔ̀.
Akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Mmu anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ Yesu kɛ ányɔ́bhɛ́rí ntɔp, asɔt, achɔri mɛ amɨ́k, arɛm bɛ ndɔ́k ndǔ ɛ̌ntɨ́ŋnyɛ́n Sílom nsó bɛsí arɛ. Ndɔk arɛ́ nso bɛsɨ́, mbo bɛghɔ mbaŋ.”
Mmu anɛ árɛ̀m bɛ, “Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ Mandɛm” kɛ yi kɛbháká kʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áyàŋ bo mankʉ achí nsěnse nɛ tɛtɛp apu nɛ yi.
Nɛ ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo ákʉ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm áyàŋ nyaka bɛ yi ankʉ, achyɛ mmʉɛt yi mbɔ akap ndɔŋ amɔt ndak amay, sɛ́rɔ́p chi pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí Mandɛm.
Yesu anaŋa nɔkɔ bɛtɛm bakay yɔ ndu bɛtɔŋ bo mɛnyɨŋ, afa atú ɛtɔk wu.
“Bě kɛ̌ bǎté nɛ mɛ ndǔ bɛsɔŋɔri bha mɛnkɛm.
Kɛ nɛ́nɛ, nchí ghati bhe bɛ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ ywɛka ámbɔ́ŋ nɛtaŋántɨ́! Chɔŋ áchwí ánɛm kɛ yɛ̌ mmu apu gu.
Yɛ̌ mmu ywɛka ákɛ́ ka mámbɨ́ŋɨ́ yi bɛ, ‘Ntɔŋ! Bǎbhɔŋ chi ntɔŋ amɔt, nɛ be mankɛm bǎchi chi batɨ bǒnkwɔ.’
Ɛnyu yɔ nkwɔ kɛ ɛ́chí nyaka nɛ Yesu. Aghɔ̌ nyaka ɛsɔŋɔri, agu chi nɛfí, puyɛ̌ amɛm ɛtɔk. Akʉ nɔ bɛ manoŋ mi ankʉ bo mámbák nyáŋá.
‑ Mbák awɔ ywɛ ákʉ̀ ɔnkwɛn ndǔ bɛbʉ́, kpɔ́t wu fɛrɛ! Ɛ́chí sayri bɛ ɔnchwe ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti nɛ awɔ amɔt ɛcha mɛmɛsɛ wɔ amɛm nɛpǐngo anɛ apu nɛmɛ nɛ amɔ apay!
Anɛfú abhak Joana, ngɔrɛ́ Kusa, mmǔ anɛ achi nkɛ́mfɔ ntá Mfɔ Hɛ́rɔd. Anɛfú abhak Susana. Nɛ bɛyǎ baghɔrɛ́ bachak. Bɔ básɔt nyaka nkáp awap mánkwak nɔkɔ bɛ Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi mámbɔ́ŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchɛbhɛ bhɔ. 
Mɛ Píta, mǔnto Yesu Kristo kɛ nchí sɨ́ŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ. Nchí sɨ́ŋ ntá yɛka bo Mandɛm, be bho bǎchi mankɔ nɛ bǎtáká mbaŋ nɛ mbaŋ, mbɔk atú Pɔ́ntɔs, báchák atú Galéshia, abhɛnɛfu atú Kapadóshiya, báchák atú Esia, nɛ abhɛnɛfu atú Bitínia.
“Tɛ̌ndu Bábilɔn ápànyu ɛnyu ɛyɔ, chɔŋ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́twɔ̀ ntá yi mɛ́ntwɔ mɛnkɛm ndǔ nywɔp nɛmɔt. Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ chi ɛghorǐ nɛme, nɛ nsay nɛ basɛ́mɛ́ nɛwú. Chɔŋ Mandɛm mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ mɛnkɛm antáŋ yi. Chɔŋ mánsɔŋ yi nɛ ngó.
mambe ámfu amfay ánkwɛnti, nɛ bɛtaŋ mfáy mɛ́nyɨkɨsi.
Yɛ̌ mmu ywɛka ákɛ́ kɛmɛ bɛbʉ́ amfǎy bɛbʉ́. Mbák mu asɔk wɔ, ɔ́kɛ́ sɔk yi. Kɛ nɨkmʉɛt bɛ Mandɛm ankʉ yi bɛrɨ. Mandɛm abhɨ́ŋɨ́ wɔ́ chi bɛ ɔ́mbak nɔ bɛ́ yi anjɛt wɔ.
Bǒ mankɛm abhɛn bábhʉ̀rɛ bɛbhé Mandɛm chí bǒ abhɛ́n bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛbharɛ́mʉɛt nɛ yi, yí abhɔ́ŋ nɛbharɛ́mʉɛt nɛ bhɔ. Nɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bhɛsɛ bɛ Mandɛm achi nɛ bhɛsɛ chí Ɛfóŋó yi mmu yi achyɛ bhɛsɛ.
Abhɔŋ yɛ bɛrɔp nyaka mbɔ bhɛsɛ bakwǎŋwaŋ ndu yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbi, bɛ́ ámbák mǔngo bachiǎkap anɛ ábhʉ̀rɛ bariɛp ami bɛsí Mandɛm ndu bɛtɨk ɛbhi nɛ bɛ ánkway bɛchyɛ akap ɛ̌ti bɛbʉ́ bǒ mankɛm.
Kɛ mbák chi Kristo, ǎkɛm ɛkɛt Ɛtayi nɛ ntɨ nɛmɔt mbɔ Mɔ́ywi. Nɛ bɛsɛ bǒ Mandɛm sɛ́chí bo ɛkɛt ɛyi ɛnkɛm mbák sɛ́nté kpirí ndu mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn sɛ́sɨ́kɨ́ ntɨ nɛ sɛ́bháka ntɨ arɛ nɛ sɛ́dɛ̀p awɔ antɨ bɛ chɔŋ sɛ́mbɔŋ bɔ.
Bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Mbɔk bárɛ̀m bɛ ɔchí Jɔ̌n Njwiti. Bachak bɛ Ɛláija, nɛ abhɛnɛfu bɛ ɔchí ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ amɔt.”
Kaká ká batɨ sayri nɛ ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ Yesu. Kpák ámbák nɛ be mankɛm abhɛn bǎchɛ́mɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Kristo.
Kɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nkaysi yap abhɔŋ bɛ́kwɛnɛ́kwɛn mbɔnyunɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ǎghɔ chɔŋ ɛchɨŋti yap. Ɛnyu yɔ kɛ ɛ́fákárí nyaka nɛ Jánɛs nɛ mmʉɛrɛ yi Jámbrɛs. 
Mmu anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ ka bɛpɔkɔ ɛkotákátí ɛyi ankoŋo ndǔ bayarɛ́kak aya, abhɨ́kɨ́ kway bɛbhak nkoŋo wa.
Kɛ akap anɛ báchyɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmíɛ́, áchí nyaka chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ̀ bo mántɨk bɛbʉ́ bhap.
Kɛ Yesu arɔk kɛ́kwɔ́t nɛ mɔ́wu, akɛ́m awɔ ywi, abhɨŋɨ yi bɛ, “Mɔ́wa, faté.”
Mbɔk bo bachi nyaka ndu nkwɔ́ bakoŋo Yesu abhɛn báte bɛ bábhɔŋ bɛ́siɛ́p yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu mbɔ bɔ́ bo Israɛl, kɛ ankwáy bɛ́bhak mmu Mandɛm. Píta ápɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nsɛm Yerúsalɛm, bǒbhɔ báré ji yí mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ,
Batɨ̌ yɛsɛ achi amɛm pɛ́pɛ́p, nɛ sɛ́rɨŋɨ tɛtɛp anɛ Mandɛm. Sɛ́bhɔŋ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ́ nɛ bho, nɛ sɛ́bhɔŋ bɛrɨ̌ntɨ. Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ achi nɛ bhɛsɛ, nɛ sɛ́kɔŋ bo tɛtɛp.
Chɔŋ yɛ̌ chí bachi nɛ manɔ bhɛka, nɛ bɔ̌mayɛka, nɛ bǒ nnɛrɛ́kɛt, nɛ mamʉɛrɛ bhɛka mámfyɛ be amɔ́ bǒmpap abhɛka. Nɛ chɔŋ mángwáy mbɔk yɛka.
Nchí sɛmti wɔ, tɔ́ŋ bo Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm mbɔnyunɛ mpok ǎtwɔ anɛ bo bápú pɛrɛ kɔŋ bɛghok nɛtɔ́ŋ ɛnɛn tɛtɛp. Mpok yɔ, chɔŋ bo mándɔbhɛ koŋo chí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ́ babhɔŋ bákɔ́ŋɔ́, mánjaŋ batɔŋ abhɛn bátɔ̀ŋ bɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ́nyɨ̀ŋɨ bhɔ batú.
Sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ yaŋ bɛsɔt chi bɛtaŋ bɛghati bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛ́nóko. Sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ́ bǎbhɔŋ bǎte kpirí ndǔ nɛka ɛnɛka nɛ Yesu. Sɛ́yàŋ chi bɛ sɛ́nchɛm amɔ́ nɛ bhe sɛnkʉ bɛtɨk bɛ maŋák amɛka anja.
Bɛbʉ́ mbɔk bho bɛchi kpóŋóróŋ nɛ bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ chɔŋ mántáŋ bɔ́, kɛ bɛbʉ́ bo bachak bɛchi bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ ɛnyu ɛnɛ ɛ́tat kɛ bo mándɨŋɨ bhɔ.
Chɔŋ Mɔ́wu anjambɨ kɛ Acha antwɔ́, nɛ chɔŋ yí ambɔ̌ŋ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn Ɛfóŋó mbɔ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Ɛláija, bɛ́ yi ankʉ bachǐbhɔ mánkɔŋ bǒbhap, ankʉ bo abhɛn bátàŋti nɛ Mandɛm mámbɔ́ŋ kɛboŋ, mámbak mbɔ bo abhɛn bachi chak bɛsí Mandɛm. Chɔŋ yí ankʉ bo mámbák ndǔ nté anɛ bákway bɛsyɛpti Acha.”
Yesu afa yɛ atú Táya nɛ Sídɔn apɛtnsɛm angɔkɔ manyu Gálili. Akɔ, afʉɛ́t arɛ́, akó achɔkɔ ambɨ njiɛ.
Nnɛ́m ɛnyɨŋ achí bɛ bapɛm ayɛka ámbák mbɔ ɛnyǔ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo ághàti bhe. Ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ̀ bɛ yɛ̌ ntwɔ́ awu ntá yɛká, yɛ̌ mbɨ́kɨ́ twɔ́, mɛ̌yáŋ ngók chí bɛ́ bǎté kpirí ndǔ nkaysi amɔt, nɛ bɛ́ mǎnu nɛ ntɨ ɛnɛká nɛ́mɔ́t bɛ́ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo ándɔ́k ambɨ.
Tímɔti ánáŋ ántwɔ́ awu, kɛ́m ká yi sayri, ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ yi ábhɔŋ maŋák bɛbhak nɛ bhe. Yi chí mmǔ anɛ ákʉ̀ bɛtɨk Mandɛm mbɔ mɛ.
Mmǔ anɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ kɔŋ mɛ, apú bhʉɛrɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛya. Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bǎghoko mɛ ntɔ́ŋɔ́, bɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ fu ntá ya. Bɛ́fu chi ntá Ɛtaya mmu átó mɛ.
nɛ yɛ̌ chi bɔgɔ́bhanɔ abhɛn yi átó bɛ mántɛ́msí nɔ́kɔ́ bo abhɛn bákʉ̀ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ, mánkaka nɔkɔ abhɛn bákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi chak.
Atwɔ́ ntá yɛsɛ asɔt mgbat anɛ Pɔ̌l agwɔ́t amɔ nɛ bɛkak ɛbhi yímbɔŋ arɛm bɛ, Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ arɛm bɛ, “Ɛnyunɛ́ kɛ̌ bo Israɛl bágwɔt chɔŋ mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ mgbat anɛ awu Yerúsalɛm mámfyɛ yi amɔ bo abhɛn bápu bo Israɛl.”
Ɛwak ɛ́mɔt, Yesu abhak téé angɔkɔ Ɛ̌ntɨŋnyɛn Gɛnɛ́sarɛt.   Bo báré nu bɛbhak kɛkwɔt nɛ yi bɛ mangok Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm.
Yesu apɛt abho bɛghati bhɔ mɛnyɨŋ ndǔ bakay.
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Nkwánɛ, agha ábhʉ́rɛ́ mɛ́ ntaŋá manyé nɛ nkɔ́rɛ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ nɛwú ntá yɛka?”
Basɛ́mɛ́ amɛn Mandɛm ákɔ́ŋɔ́ ǎkʉ̀ mmu ántɨ́knsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhi, antwɔ́ ntá yi bɛ́ yí ámpɛ́mɛ́ yi, nɛ apu twɔ nɛ áyɔ́mɛ. Kɛ basɛ́mɛ́ bǒ mmɨk ǎtwɔ̀ chi nɛ nɛwú.
Ɛ́rɨ yɛ bɛ mbák awɔ ywɛ amɔt, nɛ yɛ̌ chi ɛkak ɛyɛ kɛ̌ ɛ́kʉ̀ ɔnkwɛn ndǔ bɛbʉ́, kpɔ́t awɔ wu, nɛ yɛ̌ chí ɛkak gʉɛp! Ɛ́chí sayri bɛ́ ɔ́mbák nɛ Mandɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti, yɛ̌ chí nɛ awɔ amɔt, yɛ̌ chí nɛ ɛkak ɛ́mɔt, ɛ́chá bɛ́mɛ́sɛ wɔ amɛm ngó anɛ apu nɛmɛ, nɛ amɔ apay, bɛkak bɛpay.
Mandɛm ǎkʉ̀ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi átɨ́ bɛkʉ. Ayap bhɛsɛ tɛntɛp ndu ákɔ́ŋ nyaka bɛkʉ nɔ, bɛ́ sɛ́mbák bɔ̌bhi ndǔ yi ábhárɛ́ bhɛsɛ nɛ Kristo mbɔnyunɛ yi ákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi átɨ́ nyaka bɛkʉ bɛkoŋo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi áyàŋ bɛkʉ.
Yɛ̌ agha anɛ ápú nɛ mɛ, achí chí mǔmpap awa. Nɛ yɛ agha anɛ ápú kwak mɛ mɛnyokoti bho, ǎtàkátak.
Twɔ́ ka! Mpǒk nsay ánù mɛ, bǎchyɛ́ mɛ nɛnyíɛ́; mpǒk manyiɛp ákwàk mɛ, bǎchyɛ́ mɛ manyiɛp nnyú; nɛ mpok ntwɔ́ mbɔ kɛnkɔ, bǎsɔ́t mɛ mbɔ mɔmáyɛka.
báchák báfú Krɛt, abhɛ́nɛ́fú Arébia. Yɛ̌ nɔ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ ywɛsɛ ǎghòk ndu bɔ́ bárɛ̀m mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛbhɛn Mandɛm ákʉ́ ndu ɛyi ɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk.”
Bɔ̌ma, abhɛn ɛkɔŋ, ndǔ ɛ́chí nɔ, tě yɛ ka kpirí, kɛ́ fɛrɛ amɔ́. Dɔ́k ká ambɨ bɛkʉ bɛtɨk Acha nɛ batɨ yɛka ankɛm mpoknkɛm, tɛ̌ndu bǎrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ bɛtɨk Yesu Kristo Acha ɛbhɛn bǎkʉ̀ bɛpu nɛm ndɛ́ndɛm.
Bǎbhɨkɨ fu bɛsɛ antɨ, be kɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ kɔŋ bhɛsɛ.
Achí mbɔ mmǔ anɛ áyámbɨ átɛ́mɛ́ nɛbhʉ́ɛ́rɛ́kɛt kpát nɛ́chwé nɛ́ghaka ndǔ sɛtárɛ́bhɛ́ kɛ ǎte ɛkɛt. Nɛ mpok nnyɛ́n nɛ́gbókó kpát nɛ́ghaka ndǔ ɛkɛt, ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ moko ɛ́nkwɛ́n mbɔnyunɛ até yɔ sayri.
Ɛ́wɛt ɛnɛ yi afyɛ́ ɛbhak ɛnɛ bábáy amɛm manoŋ nɛ nnyɛ́n ɛnɛn bo bábhɨ̀ŋɨ yi nɛ́bhák bɛ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm.
Bǎkà bo abhɛn bábhʉ̀rɛ bhe mbɔ basɛm nɛ mányiɛ bhe nsɛm amɔt, nɛ mányìɛrɛ be amɨk, nɛ báyɨŋɨ be fúú kpát bádɛn be.
Ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnwi ɛbhɛn bɛchi nɛpɛ́m, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛ́mɔt ɛ́bhɔ́ŋ bɛbhap bɛtándat. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhap ɛ́bhák nɛ amɨ́k fúúú, anɛ́ amfǎy bɛbhap, nɛ anɛ́ amɛm bɛbhap. Báre kway nɛkwáy bɛti nɛ ngósí kɛywěmʉɛt bɛ, “Nyáŋá, nyáŋá, nyáŋá chi Ɛta Mandɛm Bɛtaŋ Mɛnkɛm yi mmu achi nyaka, nɛ achi, nɛ átwɔ̀ chɔŋ!”
Arɔk aghati bhɔ́, kɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap arɔbhɛ ghati yi chí bɛ ndak akɛm yi. Anɛ mbɨ arɛm bɛ ‘Nku nkɨ nɛ mbɔŋ bɛ́rɔŋ bɛyɨŋɨ wu. Nɨkmʉɛt, ghatí ɛtayɛ bɛ ákɛ́ bentɨ.’
Mɔ́ywi wu áchwé nɔkɔ amɛm nkɨ, bákɛ́m báwáy báfɛ́mɛri ansɛm ɛbhá.
Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ nɛ bɛti Yesu Acha atwɔ́ ate nɛpakámʉɛt Pɔ̌l arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Ɔ́kɛ́ chay! Nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyu ɔ́rɛ́mɛ́ ɛ̌ti ɛya fá Yerúsalɛm, ɔbhɔŋ bɛ́kʉ ɛnyuyɔ amɛm ɛtɔk Rom nkwɔ́.” 
Yi akʉ bɛsɛ bho sɛchi maŋɔkɔ́kɛt nyáŋá nyáŋá sɛ́bhàt mmʉɛt nɛ batɨ sayri ɛnyu ɛnɛ ɛkɛrákap ɛ́té sɛnɛ nɛ ɛ́gò bɛbhak nyáŋá ndǔ ɛchi ntá Acha.
Ɛnɛ́ kɛ ɛchi ɛbhé mbɨ, nɛ yɔ́ kɛ ɛ́chá bɛchak mɛnkɛm.
Ayoŋ amɨ́k are yɨŋɨ ángɛl wu nɛ bɛcháy, abhɛp yi bɛ, “Ɛta chí yi?” Ángɛl Mandɛm akɛmɛ bɛ, “Mandɛm aghok nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt ɛnɛ, aghɔ́ nɛkwak ɛnɛ́n ɔ́chyɛ́ ntá bachɛ́bhɛ́bho nɛ abhɔŋ maŋák nɛ wɔ.
Kɛ mbák mǔbɛtok arɛm bɛ, chi-bɛtɨk awa ǎtat bɛ́twɔ, ambo bɛdɛn bɔ̌-bɛtok bachak, abhɛn baghɔrɛ́ nɛ abhɛn babhakanɛm, nɛ ambo mɛ́nyiɛ, anyu nɔkɔ, kpát mmɛm ánkɛm yi,
Kɛ nkúbhɛ́ mmu anɛ mfɔ wu áfóŋórí áfú nɔ́kɔ́, arɔk atɛmɛri ntɨ nkʉbɛtɨk anɛ ákɛ̀m yi manyǔ nkáp anɛ ápú yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Akɛ́m yi angoŋo arɛm bɛ, ‘Kwɔ barɛm amɛn ɔ́kɛ̀m mɛ nɛ́nɛ.’
Pú básɨŋ amɛm ɛkáti bɛ, Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò chi ɛbhárɛ́mɔ Mfɔ Debhít nɛ abhɔŋ bɛ́fu chi Bɛ́tlɛhɛm, ɛtɔk nɛbhe Mfɔ Debhít?”
Atwɔ́ yɛ aghati Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ árɛ̀m bɛ kpák achi nɛ bě bho bǎchi nyaka nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ nɛ abhɛn bachi kɛkwɔt.
Ɛ́kʉ́, bábho bɛbhɛp batɨ bɛ, “Mmǔfú atwɔ yi nɛ nɛnyíɛ́ kɛ́?”
Ɛ́fákárí ɛnyu ɛyɔ bɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛchí amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́mfú tɛtɛp. Nɔ́ chí, ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ básɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka bɛ, “Yɛ̌ ɛghɛp ɛyi ɛ́mɔt bápú syɛp.”
Bɔ̌ma, be bo Yesu Acha ákɔ́ŋɔ́, sɛbhɔŋ bɛkaka Mandɛm ɛ̌ti yɛka yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok mbɔnyunɛ ayap be bɛ́ ámpɛ́mɛ́ bhe tɛ mpok anɛ yi ábhɨ́kɨ́ re ghoko mmɨk. Ayap bɛpɛmɛ bhe bɛfʉɛt ndǔ bɛtaŋá Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ Mmu ákʉ̀ mǎmbák nyáŋá nɛ ɛ̌ti mǎnókó tɛtɛp anɛ ayɨ́ŋɨ́ Yesu Kristo.
Mmu anɛ ághòk ɛnyɨŋ mɛ̌rɛ̀m ánkʉ mbɔ ɛnyu yi ághókó, yi kɛ áchí mmu anɛ ákɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛ. Nɛ Ɛtaya akɔŋ mmu anɛ akɔŋ mɛ. Mɛnkwɔ́ nchí kɔŋ bɛ yi ántwɔ́ ntá yi, nkʉ yí ándɨŋɨ mɛ.”
Kɛ́chí mbɔ mɔ́sɛpɛmɛ́nɔk anɛ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ mɔ́stat. Sɛ́gʉpsi sɛ́cha kɛpɛmɛ́nɔk kɛ́chák kɛnkɛm fá amɨk.
Bɛtaŋ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ bɛbhak nɛ Sɔ̌l anɛ nnyɛ́n ɛni nɛ́chák nɛ́chí nyaka bɛ́ Pɔ̌l. Pɔ̌l atɛp yi amɨ́k amʉɛt,
Kaká ká Ampliátɔs. Achí mmʉɛrɛkɔŋ awa nɛ abhat mmʉɛt nɛ Acha mbɔ mɛ.
Yesu abhɛ́p bhɔ́ bɛ, “Ndaká yí bǎbhʉ̀rɛ kɛnɔ́? Faté ká, mǎnɨkmʉɛt bɛ nɛmɔ nɛ́ntwɔ́, bǎkɛ́ kwɛn.” 
Abhɨŋɨ bǒ barɛm abhɛn chi-bɛtɨk ywi amɔt amɔt. Abhɛ́p anɛ mbɨ bɛ, ‘Yi ɔ́kɛ̀m chi-bɛtɨk wa?’
Kristo ɛ́rɛ kɛ sɛ́ghàti bho mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti yi. Ndu sɛ́kʉ̀ nɔ, sɛ́yà batú yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛkʉ nɛ sɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ. Sɛ́sɛ̀mti bhɔ, nɛ sɛ́tɔ̀ŋ nɛ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak nɛnkɛm bɛ́ sɛ́nkwáy bɛkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap ánkwáy ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbi, mbɔ mmu anɛ ábhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Kristo, ndǔ mpok anɛ sɛ́te bɛsí Mandɛm nɛ yi.
Bo bábhák arɛ́ tee mámkpɔkɔ nɔkɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́fàkari. Kɛ bǒbati báré way yí way mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Ǎpɛ̀mɛ nyaka bo bachak! Ámpɛ́mɛ́ mmʉɛt ɛyi mbák achi Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò, Mmu Mandɛm Ayabhɛ!”
Nywɔp Brɛt anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ yís nɛ́kwáy. Ndu nywɔp ɛnɔ kɛ̌ báwày nyaka mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n anɛ Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ,
Chɔŋ nkʉ ɛnyu ɛnɛ ntá mmu anɛ ánú asɔt awɔ́nɛm. Chɔŋ mbak Mandɛm aywi, yi ambak mɔ̌wa.
Tɔ́ŋ ká batɨ bɛrɨ, mǎngɔ bhɔ ntínso. Nɛ foŋorí nɔ́kɔ́ ká batɨ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Mandɛm áfʉɛ́rɛ́ ntá Kristo afoŋori bhe.
Mfárɛ́káŋ anyiɛ bakáp ayɛká. Mfárɛ́káŋ anɛ ányíɛ́ nɔ́ wú, mpok Mandɛm átàŋ bé, kɛ̌ yi ásɔ̀t mbɔ ntísiɛ ndu bɛ́chyɛ́ bhe ntɛ́msí. Nɛ mfárɛ́káŋ yɔ kɛ ányìɛ mmʉɛt ɛyɛká mbɔ ngó ányìɛ ɛnyɨŋ.
Kɛ nchí kaka bhe ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mɔt. Bǎpap mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bakoŋó Níkolas bákʉ̀ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔnyu mpábhɛ́ bhɔ.
Kɛ Píta abhɛp yi bɛ, “Ananías, ndaká yí ɔ́rɔ́ Satan ánkó wɔ́ antí bɛ ɔ́nsé nsé ntá Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ nɛ ɔrɔ mbɔk nkáp anɛ ɔ́tí mmɨk ansɛm?
Mánɨ́k yɛ mmʉɛt bɛ́, “Acha, ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ nkaysi yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu. Ndǔ bǒbhɛn batí apay, ntɨkɨ mmu ɔ́yábhɛ́
“Nɔ́ kɛ̌ nchí ghati bhe bɛ, mmu ákɛ́ bhɔŋ basɛ́mɛ́ ɛ̌ti nɛpɛ́m ɛni andɛm bɛ́, ‘Chɔŋ nyíɛ yi? Chɔŋ nyú yi? Chɔŋ mfyɛ́ yi?’ Nɛpɛ́m nkwǎ nɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ cha nɛnyíɛ́? Nɛpɛ́m nkwǎ nɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ cha ndɛnɛ́?
Kɛ mpok Pɔ̌l áyàŋ bɛrɛm ɛnyɨŋ bɛ́ ántáŋá mmʉɛt, Galio arɛm ntá bo Israɛl bɛ, “Bě bo Israɛl, mbɔ yí akʉ chi ɛbɛ́ptí ɛnyɨŋ nɛ yɛ̌ ndak abʉ́abʉ, mbʉ nkáá nɛ bhe.
Ɛnyǔ mmu wu, mmu batɨ ápáy, ákɛ́ kaysi bɛ ǎkwáy mɛnɨkmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm ambɔ́ŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi áyàŋ.
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Nchí ghati bhe bɛ, akap kɛ́nkwɛ́sɛ́-nɛ ácha anɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu.
Yɛ̌ndu bákʉ́ bǎrɨŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm ndɔŋ amɔt, nchí yáŋ bɛtɨk be bɛ Ɛta Mandɛm afɛ́rɛ́ nyaka bo Israɛl ámɔ́ bo Íjip kɛ bágháká nɔ́kɔ́ ambi, anaŋa abhɛn babhɨkɨ noko.
Yesu apɛt abho bɛghati bho bɛ, “Ɛtaya achyɛ́ mɛ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm. Yɛ̌ mmu abhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mmu anɛ Mmɔ áchí ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ fʉɛt chí Ɛtayi. Nɛ yɛ̌ mmu abhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ mmu Ɛta áchí ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ fʉɛt chí Mɔ́ywi nɛ bǒ abhɛn yi áyábhɛ́ ndu bɛkʉ bɔ mándɨ́ŋɨ́ Ɛtayi.
Mpok áŋáŋ ánkwáy, ǎtó bǒ bɛtɨk nɛ ngak tɛ́mté, mándɔk mámfɛ́rɛ́ yɔ́ ɛbhɨ.” 
Faté ká, mmu anɛ átí mɛ anáŋ achi kɛ́kwɔ́t. Sɛ́ndɔ́k sɛ́ntɛ́mɛ́rɨ́ yi.” 
Átɛ́mɛ́rí nɔ́kɔ́ bhɛsɛ Asɔs, achwe nkwɔ́ ndu áchwi anɛ sɛchi amɛm nɛ bɛsɛ́ mankɛm sɛ́rɔ́k Mitilene.
Yi bɛ, “Bo bati apay bárɔŋ nyaka mɛnɨkmʉɛt amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm. Amɔt abhak mǔnkwɔ Fárisi, anɛfú abhak mbɛbhɛ́ nkabhɛ́nti.
María abho bɛ́bɨti Acha bɛ, “Ntɨ ɛna nɛ́kwày ndu bɛ́káka Mandɛm Acha nɛ maŋák.
Bɛjɔ̌ manyiɛp bɛtandat bɛchi nyaka arɛ téé. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛjɔ ɛ́sɔ̀t nyaka mbɔ líta manyiɛp bɛsǎ byo. Bɛ́kóŋo ɛpɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bo Israɛl, básɔ̀t nyaka manyiɛp ndǔ bɛjɔ ɛbhɔ ndu bɛ́so bɛ́pókó mmʉɛt.
Bápɛ́rɛ ghɔ́ mbʉ́ɛ́p ataŋataŋ átwɔ, ákʉ mpɛ́rɛ́nyɛn ɛ́bho bɛdɛp áchwí, manyiɛp anchwe nɔkɔ amɛm, kpát árɔp kɛkwɔt bɛbɛt.
Nɛ mbák nyɛ́sɛ́ ɛnɛ nɛ́kʉ̀ ɔ́nkwɛ́n ndǔ bɛbʉ́, poŋórí nɔ́ gʉɛ́p. Ɛ́chí sayri bɛ́ ɔ́nchwe ndǔ Kɛfɔ Mandɛm nɛ nyɛ́sɛ́ nɛmɔt ɛcha bɛ mámɛ́sɛ wɔ amɛm nɛpǐngo nɛ amɨ́k apay.
Yɛ̌ nɔ, ndǔ nchɛmti bǒnkwɔ, ɛrɨ ntá ya, bɛghati bho mɛnyɨŋ nɛ bɛyɔŋ bɛtay ɛbhɛn bo bághòk mánjwimɛm, ɛcha bɛrɛm mɛnyɨŋ nɛ bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn bɛya bɛcha nka byo ndǔ ɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛnɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ.
“Tɔ́ŋ ká mɛ ɛbhɔ́kɔ́ nkap.” Bátɔ́ŋ nɔ́kɔ́ yi abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Ntí ághá nɛ́ arɛ́? Nɛ nnyɛ́n chí ɛnɛn ághá?” Bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Chí ntí Sísa, Mfɔ Rom. Nɛ nnyɛ́n, chi ɛni.”
Kwáé! Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ bɛkɛt ɛbhɛn mǎnyiɛ́ mǎnyú arɛ́ kɛ? Bǎyàŋ bɛ́byak chí bǒ nkwɔ́ Mandɛm mǎnchyɛ bǒ abhɛn ɛyap ɛ́pú ntíánwɔ́p kɛ? Bǎyàŋ ngátí bhe bɛ yi ɛ̌ti ndak anɛ? Bǎyáŋ bɛ mbɨ́tí bhe kɛ́? Nse. Mpú kwáy bɛ́bɨti bhe wáwák!
Bátɔ́ŋ yí nɛrɨŋɨ́ kɛpɨ bo Íjip nɛnkɛm, ágó abhak ɛrɨ́tí ndɛmɛ kɛpɨ nɛ nnɛ́m mmu ndu mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ̀.
Ángɛl anɛ ájwí bárát, afe ayi mmbá, nɛ ɛrɛmɛ́ nɛmbe nɛ́fú amfay, nɛ́ngɔɔ nɔkɔ mbɔ sɛsay. Nɛ́fú nɛ́kwɛ́n amɛm ndǔ manyɛ́n amɔt ndu árát. Nɛ́kwɛ́n nkwɔ ndǔ bɛbhak ɛbhɛn manyiɛp ǎnyày amɨk.
Nɛchwe anɛ bǎchwe anywɔ́p, kaká ka bǒ abhɛn bachi arɛ mǎndɛm bɛ, ‘Áfɔ́k Mandɛm ámbák nɛ bhe.’
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ́ bɛ, “Moses aghati nyaka bhe bɛ yi ɛ̌ti awáy nɛbhay?”
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Bě batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses, nɛ be bǒnkwɔ Fárisi, bǒ bɛtábhá, chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛ́p ntá yɛka ɛncha! Bachǐmbɨ bhɛka baway nyaka barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ nɛ bo abhɛn bachi chak bɛsí Mandɛm. Bǎtè manɛm ayap nɛ́nɛ, mǎngwati nɔkɔ mbɨ arɛ́ bɛkʉ yɔ ándɨ́ amɨ́k.
Mpok ɛyɔ, Jɔ̌n abhak Áénɔn, kɛkwɔt nɛ Sálim, anjwiti nɔkɔ bho. Abhak arɛ́ mbɔnyunɛ manyiɛp aya nyaka ɛbhak ɛyɔ. Bo báré rɔŋ ntá yi, anjwiti nɔkɔ bhɔ.
Yǐ ataŋ acha nɛ abhɔŋ bɛyǎ áfɔ́k. Mɛ̌nɨ̀kmʉɛt bɛ yi ankʉ batɨ̌ yɛka antaŋ amɛm ndu bɛtaŋ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ,
Kɛ mbák chí be nkwɔ achak amɛm ɛtɔk Tiatíra abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ te kákátí ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n Jɛ́sɛbɛl átɔ̀ŋ, be bho bábhɨ́kɨ́ ghɔk mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mbɔk bǒ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ barak Satan anɛ áré bhɛsɛ, nchí ghati bhe bɛ, mpú chyɛ be yɛ̌ ntu áchák.
Bɔ́ kɛ bátwɔ̀ nɛ ákɔ́rɛ́ nɛntɨ ɛnɛka. Mɛnyɨŋɨ́ mmɨk kɛ bɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnap, puyɛ̌ chi Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm.
Mmǔ anɛ ákɔ̀ŋ bo apú kʉ bhɔ bɛbʉ́. Ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ ɛchi bɛ bɛkɔŋ bo chi bɛbhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé mɛnkɛm.
Bapɛ́m ayɛsɛ achi mbɔ bawɛt ɛrɨ́tí ɛriɛp amɛn Kristo áchyɛ́ ntá Mandɛm. Ɛriɛp ɛyɔ ɛ́tàka ndǔ nkwɔ bo abhɛn Mandɛm ǎpɛ̀mɛ nɛ ndǔ nkwɔ́ bo abhɛn bákɔ̀ chi ndǔ mbi nɛwú.
Bɔ bághók nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ nɛ Dɛmɛ́triyɔs arɛmɛ, batí átáka bɔ amɛm, bábho bɛ́bɨk mandɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Atɛ́mis, mandɛm bǒ Ɛ́fɛsɔs, chi mandɛm ngo!”
Báyàŋ bɛ́bhak batɔŋ ɛbhé ɛnɛ Mandɛm áchyɛ́ nyaka Moses, kɛ bábhɨkɨ bhɔŋ nɛjwǐmɛm ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fù bɔ anyu, yɛ̌ndu bátɔ̀ŋ nɛ ntɨ nɛnkɛm mánkaysi nɔkɔ bɛ́ bárɨŋɨ.
Akʉ nɔ ndu áchyɛ́ mɛ bɛtaŋ bɛtɔŋ bɛrɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛtaŋ Mandɛm nɛ ndu bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ndǔ bɛtaŋ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ bɛ nnáŋ nnáŋá bɛghati bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Kristo, bɛbho Yerúsalɛm kpátɛ Iliríkɔm.
Mɛnyɨŋ bɛchak chi bɛkoŋo bɔmandɛm nsé, nɛ baraká babú, nɛ bɛpap batɨ, nɛ bɛ́táŋá, nɛ mpabhamɨ́k, nɛ bɛbentɨ, nɛ nkaysi anɛ mmu abhɔŋ chi ndyɛrɛ ɛ̌ti mmʉɛt ɛyi, nɛ bɛ́kɔ́rɛ mmʉɛt ndǔ bakwɔ́, nɛ ɛpɨŋ ákɔ́rɛ́,
ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Chɔŋ mpɛtnsɛm ɛbhak ɛnɛ mfú.’ Nɛ ɛ́náŋ ɛ́mpɛ́tnsɛm, ɛ́ngɔ́ bɛ yɛ̌ mmu apu amɛm ɛsɨ́ ɛkɛt ɛyi, nɛ bɛ, mányɔ yɔ, bághókó sayri,
Nku anɛ Mandɛm ányú ɛ̌ti Yesu ɛnyuyɔ ǎtɔ̀ŋ bɛ, mpok sɛ́ghɔ̀ Yesu, sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ yi achi sɛbhaŋ ɛsɛn Mandɛm achyɛ ndu bɛtɔŋ bɛ nku yɔ atéé acha anɛ nsɨ.
Yesu ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́ bo bátwɔ̀ chi tontó tontó, ásáy ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ yɔ bɛ, “Wɔ ɛfóŋó ɛnɛ́, ɛfóŋó kɛbhók nɛ batú chóchók, ghók. Fú yi amʉɛt, nɛ yɛ̌ ɛwak, ɔ́kɛ́ pɛrɛ twɔ́ yi amʉɛt!”
Ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ nchí ghɔ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ ɛnkɛm. Kɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ntíánwɔ́p mbɔnyunɛ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ mmu anɛ nnókó. Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ yí abhɔŋ bɛtaŋ bɛkɛm bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn yi achyɛ mɛ sayri kpátɛ bɛghaka ɛwak ɛnɛ yi átwɔ̀.
Nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ bǒ bágù mbɔnyunɛ bachi bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ Adam, nɔ kɛ Mandɛm ákʉ chɔŋ bǒ mankɛm abhɛn bábhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Kristo mámpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.
Kaká mɔmáyɛsɛ Afia, nɛ Akipɔs, ntɨ ntɛmɛ́ nɛnu Yesu mbɔ bhɛsɛ, nɛ ɔ́nkaka bǒnkwɔ abhɛn báchɛ̀m nɔkɔ ɛkɛt ɛyɛ ndu mɛnɨkmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm.
Mpok anɛ Sakaría ábhak ndǔ bɛtɨk áfúɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, agurɛ anywɔ́p.
Naŋá yɛ ká bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn bǎbho mbɔ ɛnyǔ amɔ́ ayɛka átɔ̀ŋ, bɛ nɛkʉ ywɛka ánkɔ ɛnyumɔt nɛ ɛkwak bɛkʉ mbɔ ɛnyǔ bǎtɨ́
Nágai mmɔ̌ Máat, Máat mmɔ̌ Matátias, Matátias mmɔ̌ Sémen, Sémen mmɔ̌ Jósɛk, Jósɛk mmɔ̌ Jóda,
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Ɛ́chí tɛtɛp bɛ Ɛláija abhɔŋ bɛyambɨ antwɔ́, anyurɛ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ambʉrɛ, kɛ ná básɨ́ŋɨ́ amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm bɛ́ Mmǔ anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm abhɔŋ bɛ́ghɔ ɛsɔŋɔri nɛ bɛ́ bábyak chɔŋ yi?
Kɛ ntɨkɨ ángɛl Mandɛm ánáŋ ághátí yi bɛ, “Chɔkɔ́ fá ɛbhě awɔ́nɛm awa kpatɛ nkʉ bǒmpap abhɛ mándɔp mbɔ ɛnɔk ɛnɛ ɔ́nyàŋa bɛkak arɛ?”
Chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛp ntá yap ɛ́ncha! Bákòŋo chi bayarɛ́kak Ken. Bákʉ̀ nkwɔ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ndǔ bɛbhɔŋ nsáy mbɔ Bálam ákʉ̀ nyaka. Bágù mbɔnyunɛ bátàŋntí nɛ Mandɛm mbɔ ɛnyǔ Kóra akʉ nyaka, agú.
Ɛ́kʉ́ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋ bɛbhɛp yí mɛnyɨŋ báfɛ́rɛ yi amɔ tɛ́mté, bɔ́ kɛpɛrɛ bhɛ́p yi yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Bɛcháy bɛ́kɛ́m mǔngo batɛmɛ́ nɛnu nkwɔ́ mpok yí árɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ Pɔ̌l mmu yí ákʉ́ bákɛ́mɛ́ báfyɛ́ ngɛm amɔ chí mmu Rom. 
Yesu ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛtɛm nɛkay ɛnɛn, aghati bakoŋo bhi bɛ, “Nɔ́ kɛ̌ Ɛtaya mmu achi amfay ákʉ̀ nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ ywɛka anɛ ánísí bɛghɔ ntɨ ntínso, kɛ́ka bɛfoŋori yi nɛ ntɨ nɛnkɛm.”
Agha áchá ntɨ? Mmǔ anɛ báfʉɛ̀t yi nɛnyíɛ́ kɛ anɛ áfʉɛ̀t nɛnyíɛ́? Pú anɛ áchɔkɔ mámfʉɛt yi nɛnyíɛ́? Kɛ nchí nɛ bhe mbɔ mǔbɛtok.
Mbák mbɔk ayɛká bárɛ̀m chí bɛ́ bákòŋo chí mɛ́ Pɔ̌l, báchák mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ chí bɛ́ bákòŋo Apólos, nɔ́ ɛ́tɔŋ bɛ́ bǎchí chí mbɔ bǒ mmɨkɨ nɛ.
Mbák ngɔrɛ́ anɛ ánókó abhɔŋ mánkwɛ́sɛ́ ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt ywi, ánkwak bhɔ́. Ákɛ́ rɔ ntǔ wap ntá bakoŋo Yesu báchák. Mbák mánkʉ nɔ, nkwɔ́ Yesu bábhɔŋ mbi bɛ́kwak mánkwɛ́sɛ́ abhɛn kɛbhɔ́ŋ nɛkwak.
Ndiɛrɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ kʉ ntá yɛka ɛnɛ́ nkʉ ntá bakwɔ́ Kristo bachak ncha chi bɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɛp bhe nɛkwak? Foŋorí ká mɛ ndǔ nɛfʉɔp ɛnɔ!
Bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Sɛ́bhɔŋ chi bɔ̌bɛkpɔkɔ́ brɛt batay nɛ nsi ɛpay. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛchak ɛ́pú”.
Yesu aghaka nɔkɔ ɛkɛt Jairɔs, yi kɛka yɛ̌ mmu ánchwe anywɔ́p nɛ yi, ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ fʉɛt Píta, nɛ Jɔ̌n, nɛ Jems nɛ chimɔ nɛ máyi.
kɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ bɛyap bo abhɛn bábhɔŋɔ bɛchɔkɔ ɛbhé awɔ́nɛm ɛya nɛ abhɛn bábhɔŋɔ bɛchɔkɔ ɛbhé awɔghɔ. Mandɛm kɛ áchyɛ bɛbhak ɛbhɔ ntá bo abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛbhak arɛ.”
Nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Jóna achi nyaka amɛm mɛniɛ̌ nsǐ-ngo ndǔ manywɔp arat, nɔ́ kɛ bábhɛmɛ chɔŋ Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm, mbak amɛm nnɛm ndǔ manywɔp arat.
Ndǔ ɛ́chí nɔ, mmǔ anɛ átàŋti nɛ bǒbati ǎtàŋti nɛ bo abhɛn Mandɛm afyɛ́ bɛ mankɛm ɛtɔk. Bo abhɛn bákʉ̀ nɔ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ chi ntɛmsi amʉɛt.
Agha akway bɛrɛm bɛ bo abhɛn Mandɛm ayabhɛ bɛ mambak abhi bákwɛ́n manyé? Mandɛm kɛ ákʉ̀ bhɔ mámbák chak.
Kɛ baghɔk Yesu kɛjwimɛm yɛ̌ chi ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mɔt ndǔ ɛbhɛn yi árɛ́mɛ́. Bɛ́bhak bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ ntá yap nɛ bɔ́ kɛkɛ́m ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi arɛmɛ. 
Páílet nkwɔ arɛm básɨ́ŋ ɛnyɨŋ ndǔ ɛbhɔ́kɔ́nɔk bábhát ndǔ ɛkotákátí, amfay ntí Yesu. Básɨ́ŋ amɔ ábhák bɛ, “Yesu mmu Násárɛt, Mfɔ bo Israɛl.”
Bárɔ Pɛga bárɔk ambɨ kpát báchwɔ́p Antiɔk atú Pisídia. Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt bo Israɛl, bárɔk bachwe ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí báchɔkɔ amɨk.
Mbɔk yɛsɛ́ sɛ́chí bo Israɛl, báchák bápú bo Israɛl. Mbɔk yɛsɛ́ sɛ́chí basɛm, báchák bápú basɛm. Kɛ bájwítí bhɛsɛ́ mankɛm chí ndǔ bɛtaŋ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ɛ́rɛ́ amɔt, nɛ sɛ́rɔp chí mmʉɛt amɔt mbɔ mmu amɔt.
Yesu akɛmɛ yí bɛ, “Ndaká yí ɔ́bhɨ́ŋɨ́ mɛ bɛ mmǔ ndɨ́ndɨ́? Mmǔ ndɨ́ndɨ́ apú. Mandɛm aywǐnti kɛ achi Mmǔ ndɨ́ndɨ́.
Jɔ̌n aji Mfɔ Hɛ́rɔd bɛ akwɛn ɛbhé Mandɛm ndu ásɔ́rɛ́ Hɛródias ngɔrɛ́ mɔ́máyi ábhay. Aji yí ɛ̌ti barak abʉ́abʉ achak ankɛm anɛ yi ákʉ́.
Sɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ́ ɛrɨ ntá yap ɛcha mbɔnyunɛ báté nyaka kpirí. Bǎrɨŋɨ ndǔ Job áté nyaka kpirí, nɛ ndǔ ngwɛnti, Mandɛm akʉ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛyi ɛ́máy ɛnkɛm, ɛ́rɨ́ yɛ ntá yi ɛcha. Tɛtɛp, Mandɛm abhɔŋ bɛyǎ ntínso nɛ bɛsɛ́.
arɛm bɛ, ‘Ɛ̌ti yɔ, mbakanɛm abhɔŋ bɛ́rɔ ɛtayi nɛ máyi, ambat mmʉɛt nɛ ngɔrɛ́ ywi,
Ɛ́chí ɛrɨ́rɨ́ bɛ́ mbɔ̌ŋ ɛnyǔ bakaysi amɛn ákʉ̀ nɨkmʉɛt ɛ̌ti yɛka nɛ bɛyǎ maŋák. Ɛ́chí ɛnyu ɛyɔ mbɔnyunɛ nkɔŋ be tontó nɛ ntí bɛ be mankɛm bǎchɛm mmʉɛt nɛ mɛ ndǔ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn. Mandɛm atɔŋ mɛ bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhi ndǔ áchyɛ́ mɛ bɛtɨk ɛbhi nkʉ́. Bǎchɛm mmʉɛt nɛ mɛ nɛ́nɛ, ɛnɛ́ nchí mǔkɛnɔŋ, nɛ mpok anɛ nchí nyaka ndǔ mmʉɛ́t ɛya nte nɔkɔ ndu áchá manyé bɛtɔŋ bɛ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ achí tɛtɛp, nɛ bɛkʉ bo mánóko yɔ sayri.
Bápɛ́rɛ ghoko yɛ̌nyɨŋ, yi achi. Nɛ yi kɛ ákɛ̀m mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm bɛ mɛ́mbak mbɔ ɛnyu bɛbhɔŋɔ bɛbhak.
Bárɔ́k ntá Yesu mánɨkmʉɛt nta yi nɛ nɛsɛptímʉɛt mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Ɛta, dɔ́k kwák mǔnti-nɛ. Achi mmu anɛ ákwáy bɛ́bhɔŋ nɛkwak.
Kɛ mmu anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ fyɛ ntí chi ndǔ bɛtɨk kɛ abhɔ̌ŋ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm mmu ákʉ̀ bɛ́ bǒ bɛbʉ́ mambak chak, chɔŋ ansɔt yi bɛ achi chak ɛ̌ti nɛka ɛnɛn yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ yi.
Yesu áfú nɔkɔ ndǔ nɛwú beti bheti ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ mbɨ ndǔ sɔ́nde, ayambɨ atɔ́ŋ mmʉɛt ntá María anɛ ɛtɔk Magdala. Yi kɛ achi nyaka ngɔrɛ́ anɛ Yesu ábókó bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ tándrámɔt bɛ́rɔ yi.
Tɔ́ŋ yɛ bo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn. Fíɛ́ bhɔ́ ntɨ nɛ ghatí bhɔ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bhap. Kʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áchyɛ́ wɔ mɛnkɛm. Ɔ́kɛ́ rɔ yɛ̌ mmu ámbyák wɔ.
Mbák bo báchí abhɛn bárɛ̀m bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛbhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ, ɛrɨ bati apay, nɛ yɛ̌ bati arat mandɛm. Nɛ bábhɔŋ bɛrɛm mɛnyɨŋ mmǔ amɔt amɔt, nɛ mmǔ achak ambak anɛ ánɛnɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bárɛ̀m.
Yesu abɨk arɛm bɛ, “Ɛtaya, ndɔ́ nɛpɛ́m ɛna amɔ́ yɛ!” Árɛ́m nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, asɛbhɛ.
Chi nɛ nnɔ babhak maknkay bɛghok mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Símiɔn arɛmɛ ɛ̌ti Yesu.
Báyàŋ nyaka bɛ mángwáy Lásárɔs nkwɔ mbɔnyunɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛfakari nɛ yi ɛ́kʉ́ nyaka batɨ̌ bo Israɛl bábʉɛ̀ bhɔ, mánoko nɔkɔ Yesu. 
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ́ bɛ, “Ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Aisáya arɛm nyaka ndaká yí tɛtɛp ɛ̌ti yɛka! Bǎchi bǒ bɛtábhá nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyu yi ásɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ Mandɛm arɛm bɛ, ‘Bǒbhɛn báchyɛ̀ mɛ kɛnókó chi nɛ bɛyɔŋɔ́nyu bhap, batɨ yap ásap nɛkɔ nɛ mɛ.
Kɛ ndǔ ngwɛnti mpok anɛ sɛchɔkɔ nɛ bhɔ, sɛrɔ bhɔ bɛrɔŋ. Bɔ́ mankɛm, baghɔrɛ́ nɛ babhakanɛm nɛ bɔ bárɔ́k bɛ́tɨk bhɛsɛ́ kpát bágháka angɔkɔnyɛ́n. Bɛsɛ́ mankɛm sɛtɛp manɛ́n amɨk sɛ́nɨkmʉɛt, sɛ́káka batɨ.
Hɛ́rɔd, gɔ́bhanɔ Gálili, aghók yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fakari. Ntí átáka yi amɛm mbɔnyunɛ mbɔk bo bárɛ̀m nyaka bɛ, “Yesu chí Jɔ̌n Njwiti kɛ ápɛ́rɛ́nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.”
Chɔŋ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bo bákʉ̀ mɛ́nja kpát bo kɛpɛrɛ kɔŋ batɨ.
Kɛ́chyɛ ka Satan mbi bɛ́ ándwɔ́ mmu ankʉ bɛbʉ́.
Mandɛm ǎkʉ chí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchí chak. Nɛ chɔŋ yi ankɛmɛ kɛ́mbé ntá bo abhɛn báchyɛ̀ bhe ɛsɔŋɔri.
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, toŋtí ká mmʉɛt ndu bɛkʉ bɛtɨk Mandɛm, mǎmbɔŋ nɛkɛ́mɛ́mʉɛt, mámbaka ntɨ sayri ndǔ bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhɛn bɛ́twɔ̀ bhe ambɨ mpok Yesu Kristo ábhesi.
Yesu ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́tɛ́m nɛkay ɛnɛn, arɛm yɛ bɛ, “Ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ ɛchi bɛ chɔŋ bɛyǎ bayǎmbɨ mándɔp ansɛm, nɛ bɛyǎ barɔbhɛ́nsɛm mándɔp ambɨ.” 
Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ beku ndǔ nkúbhɛ́ ɛwak ɛyɔ, Yesu arɛm ntá bakoŋo bhi bɛ, “Sɛ́mpé sɛ́ndɔ́k ɛbhě manyu ɛnɛ́ awu.”
Mbɔk batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses abhɛn báfú Yerúsalɛm báre rɛm bɛ, “Bɛlsɛbul, mfɔ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ, kɛ̌ áchyɛ́ Yesu bɛtaŋ bɛbok bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ.”
Tɛ̌ndu Mandɛm ákʉ́ bǎfú ndǔ nɛwú bápɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m nɛkɔ nɛ Kristo, bʉrɛ́ ká ntɨ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi amfay, ɛbhak ɛnɛ Kristo áchɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt kɛnókó, ɛbhe awɔ́nɛm Mandɛm.
Yǎ yɛ́ ka mbɨ bɛfyɛ ntí bɛrɔ Mandɛm ámbák Mfɔ ywɛka, mǎmfyɛ́ ntí bɛkʉ chi yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi áyàŋ bo mankʉ, nɛ chɔŋ yi anchyɛ bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm nkwɔ.
Yɛ̌ mmǔ ywɛka ákɛ́ kʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́kwák yí aywǐntí. Mmu ywɛká apɛrɛ́ kʉ́ ɛnyɨŋ, ánkʉ́ chí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́kwàk bo báchák nkwɔ́.
Bɛsɛ́ mankɛm sɛ́kwɛ́nti amɨk. Tɛ́mté wu, ngók ɛyɔŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́rɛ̀m ndǔ ɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk Hibru bɛ, ‘Sɔ̌l, Sɔ̌l, ndaká yí ɔ́chyɛ̀ mɛ nɛnyok? Ɔkáysí bɛ́ ɔ̌kwáy mɛ́nú nɛ mɛ? Mbák ɔ́nsɔ́t ɛkak ɔndɛp sɛtárɛ́bhɛ́ wɔ kɛ ɔ́ghòk bɛbe.’
Yesu akɛmɛ bɛ, “Mandɛm ato mɛ́ bɛ ntwɔ nkwak chi bo Israɛl, bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n yi anɛ ánɛ́mɛ́ ɛbhɨ.”
Bǒbati bo Israɛl bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ kʉ nɛfwɔp bɛrɛm bɛ ɔchí mmu Samária nɛ bɛ́ ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri wɔ?”
Nɛ bě bho Kapɛ̌naum, bǎkaysi bɛ bǎkway bɛyoŋ mmʉɛt, mǎnkó kpát mǎntɔk nɛbu? Nsé! Chɔŋ Mandɛm amɛsɛ bhɛ amɛm ɛtɔkɔ́ bawú!”
Yɛ̌nyɨŋ sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ twɔ fá ammɨk nɛ yɔ́, nɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ mmu apú rɔŋ nɛ yɔ.
Ɛ́fákari bɛ Píta ǎkɔ̀ nyaka mbǎŋ nɛ mbaŋ ndu bɛ́byo bo Mandɛm. Ɛwak ɛ́mɔ́t, arɔk bɛbyo abhɛn bachi ɛtɔk ɛnɛ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ Lída.
Mbák mmu ywɛka ǎme, ámbɨ́ŋɨ́ bǒbati Nkwɔ Kristo. Ámbɨ́ŋɨ́ bhɔ bɛ mánɨkmʉɛt ɛ̌ti yi, mángwati yi bawɛt amʉɛt ndǔ nnyɛ́n Yesu Acha.
Bǒmpap bhɔ báfù chi ndǔ nkwɔ ywɛsɛ. Kɛ bápú nyaka mbɔ̌ŋ bǒ-bhɛsɛ. Mbɔ báchí bǒnkwɔ ywɛsɛ tɛtɛp, mbʉ bárɔp nɛ bhɛsɛ. Kɛ bárɔ́ bhɛsɛ bɛ ɛ́mbák kpoŋoroŋ bɛ bápú nɛ bhɛsɛ.
Nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt nɛfʉɛrɛ nɔkɔ, baghɔrɛ́ bati arat báku bawɛrɛ́riɛp ndu bɛrɔŋ bɛwati Yesu amʉɛt. Bábhák María anɛ ɛtɔk Mágdala nɛ María nnɔ Jems nɛ Salome.
Mpok ngɔrɛ́ nɛ mɛniɛ ánòŋsi, ǎbhɔ́ŋ basɛ́mɛ́ antɨ mbɔnyunɛ mpok nɛbhe akway. Kɛ ánáŋ ámbé, maŋák ǎbhák nɛ yi bɛ mɔ́nkɔ átwɔ́ fá amɨk. Ɛ́nkʉ angɔkɔntɨk bɛbě nɛbhe.
Mandɛm ángɔ́ bhe ntínso, ánchyɛ bhe kpák nɛ ɛkɔŋ ɛyi tontó tontó. 
Ɛ́tárɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, Mátio abhɨŋɨ Yesu ɛkɛt ɛyi. Anak mamʉɛrɛ bhi nɛ babhɛbhɛ́ nkábhɛ́nti bachak, nɛ bakʉ̌ bɛbʉ́ bachak. Yesu, achɔkɔ anyiɛ nɔkɔ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ bhɔ, nɛ bakoŋo bhi nkwɔ.
Bábhɛ́mɛ yi nɛ ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ manywɔp arat, Mandɛm akʉ yí apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ́mɛ́ nyaka bɛ chɔŋ ɛ́mfakari.
Yesu akɛmɛ bɛ, “Bǎkɛ́ kaŋ mmu mbɔ awu mbɔnyunɛ yɛ̌ mmu apú anɛ ákʉ ɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ndǔ nnyɛ́n ɛna antɨŋ anjibhiri mmʉɛt andɛm bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti ya.
Jems, nɛ mɔ́mayi Jɔ̌n, bɔ̌ Sɛbɛdi [Yesu achyɛ bhɔ́ nnyɛ́n nɛ́chák bɛ́ Boanɛjis, nɔ chi bɔ̌nɛfaŋ]; nɛ
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ mɛ̌ghati bhe nɛ́nɛ ɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ́ bakwǎy bho nɛ mánkwɛ́sɛ́. Puyɛ̌ chí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́fú ntá Yesu Acha. Nchí ghati bhe chí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ nkáysí. Kɛ bǎbhɔŋ bɛghok mɛ́ mbɔnyunɛ nchí mmu anɛ nchí rɛm ndak mángók, nɛ ntí bɛ́ Yesu Acha achí nɛ mɛ.
Yerúsalɛm nɛ Iduméya. Báchák báfú ɛbhěnyɛn Jɔ́dan, abhɛ́nɛ́fú báfú atú bɛtɔk Táya nɛ Sídɔn. Bo mankɛm abhɛn mámè bárɔ́k ntá Yesu ndu bághókó mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ̀.
Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ aghati Fílip bɛ, “Dɔ́k awu kɔ nɔ́kɔ́ kɛ́kwɔ́t nɛ ɛkarɨk ɛyɔ.”
Abhɛn ɛkɔŋ, ndu nchí yáŋ tontó bɛsɨŋ be ɛ̌ti nɛpɛmɛ anɛ Mandɛm ápɛ́mɛ́ bhɛsɛ mankɛm, ngɔ́ bɛ mbɔŋ bɛsɨŋ ngáti bhe bɛ mǎnkɛ́m tɛtɛp anɛ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ bɛ ambak mbɔ ɛnyǔ báchyɛ́ yɔ ntá bo Mandɛm ndɔŋ amɔt ndak ámáy.
Kɛ ntɛmɛ́ nɛnu amɔt asɔt nɛkɔŋ ayɛm Yesu ambeápak. Tɛ́mté wu, manoŋ nɛ manyiɛp abho bɛfu.
Yí kɛ áchɛ̀m bǒbhi mankɛm ndǔ nkwɔ amɔt bɛ mámbák mbɔ mmu amɔt nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ mmʉɛt nkwǎ achi nɛ maŋɔk anɛ áfáŋá byoŋómʉɛt mɛnkɛm bɛ́ mmʉɛt ambak amɔt. Nɛ ndǔ mmʉɛt nkwǎ, mpok yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nɛbhʉ́ɛ́rɛ́mʉɛt ákʉ̀ ɛbhi bɛtɨk sayri, mmʉɛt ǎgò ɛrɨrɨ. Ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ ɛchi nɛ bǒnkwɔ Kristo. Mpok bɔ́ bákɔ̀ŋ batɨ nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ǎkʉ̀ ɛbhi bɛtɨk sayri, bákwàk batɨ mánsɛ́nɛ́ ndǔ nɛka ɛnɛn babhɔŋɔ nɛ Yesu. 
mǎntɔŋ nɔ́kɔ́ bhɔ bɛ mánkʉ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ngátí be mǎnkʉ́ nɔkɔ. Nɛ nchí bhák nɛ bhe mpoknkɛm, tɛ ndǔ ngwɛnti mmɨk.”
Ángɛl amɔt ndǔ abhɛn tándrámɔt abhɛn bakɛmɛ bɛkwɔp ɛbhɛn bɛjwi nɛ bɛghori ɛbhɛn ngwɛnti tándrámɔt atwɔ́ aghati mɛ bɛ, “Twɔ́ ntɔ́ŋ wɔ́ ngɔrɛ́ anɛ Mɔ́nkwɔmɛn ábhay.”
Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ nkárɛ́nká byo nɛ ɛpay nɛ ngósí, mmok ánɛ́m, ɛjuri ɛ́kwɛn ɛkuti ɛtɔk ɛnkɛm kpátɛ nkárɛ́nká ɛ́rát beku,
Mɛ́jwìti bhe nɛ manyiɛp, kɛ chɔŋ yí anjwiti bhe chí nɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ.” 
Mandɛm akʉ ɛnyu yɔ bɛ́ bɔ́ mánjáŋ yi nɛ ndu báyàŋ yi mbɔ mmǔ anɛ ámɔ̀ nɛ amɔ́ bɛyaŋ ɛnyɨŋ amɛm ɛjuri, mánkwáy bɛrɨŋɨ yi. Kɛ sayri sayri, Mandɛm abhɨ́kɨ́ sap nɛkɔ nɛ yɛ̌ mmu ywɛsɛ amɔt.
Atɛmɛri mmu Israɛl amɔt arɛ́ anɛ aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Akwíla, mmǔ atú Pɔ́ntɔs. Ɛbhɨkɨre tat nyaka, ɛnɛ́ Akwíla nɛ ngɔrɛ́ ywi Prisíla bárɔ́ ɛtɔk Ítali mbɔnyunɛ Klaudiɔs Mfɔ Rom, achyɛ nyaka ɛyɔŋ bɛ́ bo Ju mankɛm mámfá Rom. Pɔ̌l arɔk bɛghɔ bhɔ.
Kaká ká Ɛtayɛsɛ Mandɛm mpoknkɛm ɛ̌ti yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ndǔ nnyɛ́n Yesu Kristo Acha. 
Ɛ́fákárí nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyu ɛyɔ, ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm Jeremáya árɛ́mɛ́ nyaka ɛ́fú tɛtɛp. Jeremáya arɛm nyaka bɛ, “Básɔ́t bɛbhɔ́kɔ́ nkáp ɛsa nsɛm byo, manyǔ nkáp anɛ mbɔk bo Israɛl bághɔ́ bɛ ákway bɛ́chyɛ́ ntá mmu anɛ ati yi.
“Bɛkak ɛbhap bɛ́wàkari bɛpɔkɔ bɔ bɛ mandɔk mangway bo.
mbɔnyunɛ abhʉ́rɛ́ nywɔp ɛnɛn yi átàŋ bǒ mankɛm ɛnyu ɛnɛ ɛchi chak. Anáŋ ayap mmu anɛ átàŋ manyé yɔ, nɛ atɔ́ŋ ɛrɨŋ bɛkʉ bǒ mmɨk mankɛm mándɨ́ŋɨ́ mmu wu, ndu ákʉ́ yi ápɛ́rɛ́nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.”
Mbɔk bo bachi bagú-bhó tɛ amɛm mɛniɛ. Abhɛ́nɛ́fú báchí bagú-bhó mbɔnyunɛ bo bachak kɛ bákʉ́ bɔ mámbák nɔ. Kɛ báchák bábhɨ́kɨ́ ka nɛbhay ndu báchyɛ́ mmʉɛt bɛkʉ bɛtɨk Kɛfɔ̌ mfáy. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ákwày bɛkoŋo ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ndɛ́mɛ́, ánkóŋó yɔ́.” 
Píta akɛmɛ bɛ, “Bafɔ básɔ̀t nkábhɛ́nti ntá mankɔ.” Yesu arɛm yɛ bɛ, “Ɛyɔ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ́ babhɔ̌ŋ bɔ̌mɨk bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛchyɛ nkábhɛ́nti.
Mbokónyɛ́n ámɔt ápú kwáy bɛchyɛ ɛrɨ́tí manyiɛp, ámpɛt ánchyɛ nɔkɔ manyiɛp amɛn áchí ngáŋ ngaŋ.
Ndu mbárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Kristo, nchí kway bɛghati wɔ ɔ́nkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ.
Bǎkɛ́ yoŋ yɛ mmʉɛ́t nɛ bo abhɛn bachi mbɔ batábhɛ́nɔk anɛ bákpɔ́t bágʉɛ́bhɛ́ ɛbhɨ. Mbák bǎyòŋ mmʉɛt, bǎkɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk bɛ puyɛ̌ be kɛ bǎkɛ́mɛ́ bakaŋ ɛnɔk. Bakaŋ ɛ́nɔk kɛ ákɛ́mɛ́ bhe tɛ̌ndu bǎchi chi batábhɛ́ ɛnɔk.
Agha ákway bɛrɛm bɛ mántɛ́msí bhɛsɛ? Chí Yesu Kristo mmu ágú nyaka kɛ Mandɛm akʉ yi apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m nɛ achi ɛbhé awɔ́nɛm ɛywi, nɛ sayri sayri, ǎnɨ̀kmʉɛt ɛ̌ti yɛsɛ kɛ?
Páílet abhɛ́p Yesu bɛ, “Tɛtɛp chí yí?” Páílet árɛ́m nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, arɔ Yesu apɛt afú nɛfí ntá bo Israɛl aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Mbɨ́kɨ́ ghɔ ɛbɛ́ptí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi akʉ.
Nu bɛ́twɔ, kɛ́chɔŋti mpok.
nɛ Júdas mmɔ̌ Jems, nɛ Júdas Iskariɔt anɛ átí nyaka Yesu. 
mbɔnyunɛ sɛ́ghok bɛ bǎbhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Yesu Kristo nɛ bǎkɔŋ bo Mandɛm mankɛm.
Nchí bhɛp yɛ bɛ Mandɛm agʉɛp bo Israɛl ɛbhɨ kɛ? Wáwák! Mɛmbɔ̌ŋ nchí mmu Israɛl nɛ ɛbhárɛ́mɔ Ábraham nɛ mfǔ ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt amɔt anɛ Bɛnjamin achí chi-mbɨ.
Ɛyɔ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ́ puyɛ̌ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnɛn bǒ mmɨk kɛ nɛ́kʉ́ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛka nɛ Yesu. Chi bɛtaŋ Mandɛm. 
Júdas aka nɛ bhɔ́. Abho bɛyaŋ mbi ndu bɛ́tí Yesu ntá yap ndǔ mpok anɛ ngɛ́mtay bho bapu ghɔ. 
Ɔ́kɛ́ bhɔŋ yɛ ntíánwɔ́p bɛghati bho ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛ̌ti Acha ywɛsɛ Yesu. Ɔ́kɛ́ bhɔŋ ntíánwɔ́p ɛ̌ti ya, yɛ̌ndu nchí mǔkɛnɔŋ ɛ̌ti nsɨkɨ ntɨ nɛ yi. Kɛ dɔ̌ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áchyɛ wɔ mɛ́nkwák wɔ ɔ́nka ɛsɔŋɔri mbɔ mɛ ɛ̌ti Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ Yesu.
Kɛ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ yi, bábhó bɛrɛm nɛ batɨ bɛ, ‘Yɨŋɨ́ mbɔ̌ŋ mɔ́ywi nɛ́, nɛ yí kɛ̌ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛ́nyiɛ́ nɛwú ɛtayi. Twɔ́ ká sɛnkɛm yi sɛ́ngwáy bɛ́ ɛtayi ánáŋ ángú, mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhi mɛ́ndɔp chi ɛbhɛsɛ.’
ndǔ nnyɛ́n Yesu Kristo Acha, nɛ nchi bhák nɛ bhe ndǔ nkaysi ya mpok bǎchɛm ndu bɛchyɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó. Chɔŋ bɛtaŋ Yesu Acha ywɛsɛ mɛ́mbak nkwɔ́ nɛ bhe.
Kɛ Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Dɔ̌ ká yi. Ndaká yí bǎsɔŋɔri yi? Akʉ mɛ ɛrɨ́tí ɛnyɨŋ.
Babhabhɛri abhɛn ɛkɛrákap báchwɔ́p arɛ, kɛghɔ bhɔ. Bápɛtnsɛm nɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ,
chyɛ̌ máyɛ nɛ ɛtayɛ kɛnókó. Nɛ ɔbhɔŋ bɛkɔŋ ntɨ nkwǎ mbɔ ɛnyu ɔ́kɔ́ŋɔ́ mmʉɛt ɛyɛ.’”
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu achi chɔ́kɔ́ ambɨ Njiɛ Mɛnɔk Ólif. Bakoŋo bhi bárɔ́k ntá yi. Yɛ̌ mmu achak kɛbhak nɛ bhɔ. Bárɛ́m bɛ, “Ɛta, ghati bhɛsɛ, chɔŋ ɛ́mfakari nɔ ntɨkɨ mpok, nɛ ntɨkɨ ɛrɨŋ ɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ bo mándɨŋɨ bɛ mpok anɛ ɔ́twɔ̀ arɔp kɛ́kwɔ́t, nɛ bɛ́ mandú mpok mmɨk ǎmay?”
Bɔ kɛrɔ bɛtɔŋ nɛ bɛ́gháti bo Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ bɛ Yesu chi Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò. Báre kʉ nɔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nywɔp amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm nɛ amɛm bɛkɛt ɛbhap.
Ghatí nɔ́kɔ́ ka bo Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ ákʉ̀ bɔ mambɔŋ kpák bɛsí Mandɛm. Ndǔ bǎkʉ̀ nɔ, ɛbhak mbɔ mpok ntɛmɛ́ nɛnu afyɛ́ bɛtaŋtí nkwɔbhɛ́nya bɛ́ ákɛ́ kwɛn amɨk mpok ájɛ̀t ntyɛt.
Bo báfú nɔ́kɔ́ ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí, bɛyǎ bo Israɛl nɛ bo abhɛn bápu bo Israɛl kɛ báchày Mandɛm, báré koŋo Pɔ̌l nɛ Banábas. BɔPɔ̌l básɛ́mti bhɔ́ bɛ́ mánté kpirí, mándɔkɔ nɔkɔ chi ambɨ bɛghɔkɔ mmʉɛt ndu bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm.
Chɔŋ sɛ́ndɛm bɛ yi ɛ̌ti barak anɛ? Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ sɛ́rɛ̀m chi bɛ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl, bábhɨ́kɨ́ fyɛ nyaka bɛtaŋ ndu bɛyaŋ mbi bɛbhak chak bɛsí Mandɛm. Yɛ̌ nɔ, bábhak chak bɛsí Mandɛm bɛfʉɛt ndǔ nɛka ɛnɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ Yesu.
Nɛ mǔbɛtok anɛ árɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ chi-bɛtɨk áyàŋ yi ankʉ, kɛ yi kɛ toŋti mmʉɛt ankʉ mbɔ ɛnyu ɛ́yaŋ, bátɛmsi chɔŋ yi sayri.
Nɛ ndu bárɛ̀m kɛpɨ nɛ Píta, Píta achwe anywɔ́p, aghɔ́ bɛyǎ bo.
Abhɛ́p bɔ́ bɛ, “Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́re jwimɛm?” 
Mandɛm mmu áchyɛ̀ bho kpák ambak nɛ bhe mankɛm. Amen.
Nchí ghati bhe chí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ngɔ́ ntá Ɛtaya, kɛ bǎkʉ̀ chí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ɛtayɛka ágháti bhe.”
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ambɨ ɛbhak mbɔ nkʉ, ɛnɛ ɛ́kòŋo ɛbhak mbɔ nnɛ́m mpɔŋ. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́jwí bɛ́rát ɛbhɔ́ŋ bɛsí mbɔ nkwǎŋwaŋ, nɛ ɛnɛ ɛjwi mɛnwi ɛbhak mbɔ ɛbhɔkɔ ɛnɛ ɛ́rè amfay.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Mbák Mandɛm achi nɛ bho mbɔ Mfɔ wap, mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́bhak mbɔ ɛnyu ɛ́chí ndǔ nɛkay ɛnɛn. Nɛkǎy ɛnɛn nɛchi bɛ, mbɔŋɔ́nkɨ̌fú achi nyaka. Ɛwak ɛ́mɔt, afa beti beti arɔk bɛyaŋ bǒ abhɛn bákʉ̀ bɛtɨk amɛm nkɨ ywi.
Ángɛl Mandɛm wu apɔkɔ mɛ ndǔ Ɛfóŋó arɔk amɛm baso. Arɛ́, ngɔ́ ngɔrɛ́ amɔt chɔkɔ amfay nnya mbʉ́mbʉ anɛ ápe chuuu. Nnya mbʉ́mbʉ yɔ abhɔ́ŋ bati tándrámɔt nɛ babhaŋ byo. Manyɛ́n anɛ básɨ́ŋɨ́ abhak amʉɛt nnya yɔ nɛ ábhák manyɛ́n anɛ árɛ̀m ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti Mandɛm.
Ɛwak nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt bo Israɛl, Yesu áre tɔŋ bo amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí ɛyap.
Arɛm ntá mmu achak bɛ, “Koŋó mɛ́.” Kɛ mmu wu arɛm bɛ, “Acha, dɔ̌ kpɨ́k ndɔ́k mbɛ́mɛ́ Ɛtaya.”
Ɛ́kʉ́ kpát bo babho bɛsɔt bɛbhɔ́kɔ́ ndɛn ɛbhɛn bɛ́tɛ́sɛ bɛsí nɛ nkú yi, mámbarɛ nɔkɔ amʉɛt bǒmame, nɛ bɔ́ mántaŋ nɔkɔ, nɛ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ mɛ́mfu nɔkɔ bo amʉɛt.
Ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ́ mbɔ̌ŋ nɛ bhe ɛ́fǔ ntá Yesu Kristo. Mbɔŋ Mandɛm arɨ́ŋɨ́ nɔ.
Yesu ápɛ́rɛ fú ndǔ nnyɛ́n Jɔ́dan, ajwi nɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ. Yí akʉ Yesu arɔk amɛm baso,
Ɛ́tárɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ Yesu nɛ bakoŋo bhi báré nyiɛ nɛnyíɛ́ amɛm ɛkɛt Lɛ́vi. Bɛyǎ babhɛbhɛ́ nkábhɛ́nti nɛ bakʉ̌ bɛbʉ́ báchák bákóŋo Yesu, mányiɛ nɔkɔ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ yi.
Baghɔk abhi Jems nɛ Jɔ̌n, bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, bárɛm ntá Yesu bɛ, “Acha, ɔ̌yàŋ sɛ́mbɨ́ŋɨ́ ngó ámfú amfay antwɔ ansɔŋ bǒbhɛn-ɛ?”
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, Yesu atɛmɛri yi amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm, aghati yi bɛ, “Yɨŋɨ́, ɔnáŋ ɔtaŋ! Dɔ̌ bɛbʉ́ bɛ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chá ɛyɔ ɛ́kɛ́ tɛmɛri wɔ.”
Asɔt yɛ bɛkpɔkɔ́ brɛt ɛbhɔ tándrámɔt nɛ nsi. Áchyɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bakak ntá Mandɛm, abho bɛ́bɔ́kɔ́ti bhɔ anchyɛ nɔkɔ ntá bakoŋo bhi, bɛ́ mánkɔ́rɛ́ ntá bǒbhɔ.
Mmu anɛ ápɨ́ chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchyɛ mmʉɛt yi maŋák, ǎghɛm chi nɛwú. Kɛ mmu anɛ ákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm áyàŋ yi ankʉ ǎghɛm nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.
Pɔ̌l abho bɛ́táŋa mmʉɛt andɛm nɔkɔ bɛ, “Bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bɛ́pú nɛ mɛ wáwák bɛyɨŋɨ ɛbhé bo Israɛl nɛ ɛbhé ɛkɛrákap nɛ yɛ̌chi ɛbhé Mfɔ Rom.”
Bo mányìɛ̀ nyaka mányù nɔkɔ, abhɛn bábhày baghɔrɛ́ mámbay nɔkɔ, nɛ abhɛ́n bátòk bhɔ mántoko nɔkɔ kpatɛ nywɔp ɛnɛn Nóa áchwé amɛm áchwí, nɛ manyiɛp átwɔ́ akuti mmɨk awáy bǒ mankɛm.
Tɛ̌ndu yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm ághókó ɛ́rɨ, bo bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ bɛbyak yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Sɛ́kway mɛ́nyiɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ sɛ́nchyɛ nɔkɔ bakak ntá Mandɛm,
Mɛnyǔ bɛbhé ɛbhɔ bɛ́fʉɛrɛ fʉɛt. Mɛnyǔ bɛbhé ɛbhɔ bɛ́fù chi ntá bǒ mmɨk nɛ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ bátɔ̀ŋ.
Bɛbhé ɛbhɛn bɛpay bɛ́kútí yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm áyàŋ bo mándɨ́ŋɨ́, mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɛchi ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn Moses ásɨ́ŋɨ́, nɛ ɛbhɛn barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm básɨ́ŋɨ́.” 
Mɛ̌nɨ̀kmʉɛt bɛ mǎndɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ Kristo, yɛ̌ndu sɛ́pú kway bɛrɨŋɨ yɔ ɛnkɛm, bɛ́ mǎnkwáy bɛrɔp chi mbɔ Mandɛm ndǔ ɛpɨŋ ɛyɛka.
Mmu wap amɔt anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ Klópas abhɛ́p yɛ yi bɛ, “Ndiɛrɛ wɔ kɛ ɔ́chí kɛnkɔ̌ anɛ átwɔ́ Yerúsalɛm anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛfakari arɛ́ ndǔ manywɔbhɛ́-nɛ?”
Mánáŋ badɛn bhɛsɛ, mánáŋ báfyɛ̌ bhɛsɛ ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ. Mǎnaŋ bágʉɛ́p ɛbyɔk bɛ bǒ mánchyɛ́ bhɛsɛ ɛsɔŋɔri. Sɛ́yaŋá gu bɛtɨk. Mpok nɛ mpok, sɛ́kɛ bhɔŋ mbi bɛbhʉrɛ kɛnɔ́ nɛ ɛ́nchɛbhɛ nɔkɔ bhɛsɛ tɛ nɛnyíɛ́ mɛnyiɛ.
Kɛ mbák bǎkʉ̀ chi mbɔ nyǎbhɨ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́nɛmti, ɛndakati nɔkɔ batɨ, sɔt ka mpok bɛ bǎkɛ́ bho bɛway batɨ. 
Ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ noko bɛ nchí babhát nɛ Ɛtaya nɛ Ɛtaya achi babhat nɛ mɛ? Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ́ghàti bhe, mpú kʉ nɔ chi ndǔ mmʉɛ́t ɛya. Ɛtaya mmu achí babhat nɛ mɛ ǎkʉ̀ bɛtɨk ɛbhi.
Bě babhɔŋ bǎkwáy yɛ́ bɛ́ghɔ bɛ́ bɛrɨ ɛbhɛn mmu ákʉ̀ kɛ bɛ́kʉ̀ Mandɛm ánsɔ́t yí mbɔ mmu anɛ áchí chak bɛsí bhi. Púyɛ chí nɛrɛm yí árɛ̀m nɛ nyu bɛ́ áká nɛ Mandɛm.
Ɛchí mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ Ábraham anókó nyaka Mandɛm, nɛ ɛ̌ti ɛyɔ, Mandɛm asɔt yi bɛ achi chak bɛsí bhi.
Mɛnyǔ bǒbhɔ bapu kʉ chi bɛtɨk Acha Kristo. Bákʉ̀ chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ babhɔŋ bakɔŋɔ. Nɛ básɔ̀t chi sɛ́rwɔ́rɛ́nyu nɛ ɛrɨ́tí ɛyɔŋɔ́nyu bɛrwɔ bo abhɛn amɨ́k ayap ábhɨ́kɨ́re nɛ́nɛ.
Nɛ bɛ́pókómʉɛt ɛbhɛ́n sɛ́kàysi bɛ́ bɛ́pú yɛ̌nyɨŋ, bɔ́ kɛ̌ sɛre sɔt mpok bɛ́kɛ́m. Nɛ bɛ́pókómʉɛt ɛbhɛ́n sɛ́bhɛ̀sɛ bɛ́ bo bákɛ́ ghɔ́ nɛ amɨ́k, bɔ kɛ sɛ́kɛ̀m sayri ɛncha,
Yí arɔk ntá Páílet bɛ́ ánchyɛ́ yi bɛtaŋ amfɛrɛ Yesu amfǎy ɛkotákátí. Páílet áchyɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ yi bɛtaŋ,
Kɛ ɛchí tɛtɛp bɛ Mandɛm akʉ Kristo apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ndu bɛtɔŋ bɛ chɔŋ yí ankʉ bawú mámpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.
Kɛ chɔŋ sɛ́ndɛm bɛ yi? Sɛ́ndɛ́m bɛ, ‘Bɛ́fǔ nyaka ntá nkwǎ?’ Bápú kway nyaka bɛrɛm ɛnyu ɛyɔ ndu báchày ngɛ́mtáy bo abhɛn báchí arɛ́ mbɔnyunɛ bɔ́ mankɛm mánoko nyaka sayri bɛ Jɔ̌n achi ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm.”
Sɛ́chí yɛ bo abhɛn Kristo afyɛ́ ntó ɛnɛn bhɛsɛ́ amɔ. Mbɔŋ Mandɛm kɛ áfʉɛ̀t yɛ ntá yɛsɛ́, ndu ábhɨ̀ŋɨ be nɛ ɛkɔŋ. Ndǔ nnyɛ́n Kristo, sɛ́nɨ̀k be mmʉɛt, pɛt ka nsɛm ntá Mandɛm.
Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ bǎtè kpirí nɛ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ nɛ bǎkà bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛn bǎghɔ̀ ɛ̌ti ya kɛpɔp bɛkʉ nɔ.
Mmu amɔt abhak arɛ́ anɛ aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Sakio. Abhak mǔnti babhɛbhɛ́ nkábhɛ́nti. Abhɔ́ŋ bɛyǎ nkáp.
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi mányìɛ nɛnyíɛ́, asɔt ɛkpɔkɔ́ brɛt akɛ́m awɔ́. Achyɛ bakak ntá Mandɛm abho bɛ́bɔ́kɔ́ti anchyɛ nɔkɔ bhɔ́ nɛ bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ, “Sɔt ka nyiɛ́. Nɛ́ chi mmʉɛ́t ɛya.”
Kɛ Pɔ̌l abɨk arɛm bɛ, “Ɔ́kɛ́ way mmʉɛt. Bɛsɛ́ mankɛm sɛ́chí fá!”
Mpok anɛ bǎchɛm nɛbhʉɛt amɔt, puyɛ̌ chí nɛnyíɛ́ Acha kɛ̌ mǎnyìɛ.
Ɛchi nyaka ɛ̌ti yɛsɛ nkwɔ ndu sɛ́nókó Mandɛm mmu ákʉ́ nyaka Yesu Acha ywɛsɛ apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.
Mǔnti abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛbhak mɔ̌nkɔ ndǔ Nkwɔ Yesu mbɔnyunɛ ǎkway bɛyoŋ mmʉɛt nɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́nkʉ Mandɛm antɛmsi yi mbɔ ɛnyu átɛ́msí nyaka Satan.
Ɛ́kʉ, bo Israɛl bárɛm ntá mmu anɛ bábú yi bɛ, “Ɛchɔŋ chi nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt nɛ ɛbhé ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ ka bɛ ɔ́mpɔ́kɔ́ ɛ̌sák ɛyɛ.”
Ɛnyu ɛ́mɔt kɛ Moses amyakati nyaka manoŋ ndǔ ɛtɛm nɛ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn básɔ̀t nyaka bɛchyɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó nɛ bhɔ.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Yɛ̌ ɛ́mbak bɛ nchí rɛm chi ɛ̌ti mmʉɛ́t ɛya, ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ mɛ́rɛ̀m chí mbɔŋ ndak, mbɔnyunɛ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ mfú nɛ ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ mɛ́rɔ̀ŋ. Kɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ mfú nɛ ɛbhak anɛ mɛ̌rɔ̀ŋ.
Mbák mǎnté kákátí, chɔŋ mǎmpɛmɛ mmʉɛt ɛyɛka. 
Kɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fù mmu anyu, ɛ́fù yi chi antɨ, nɛ yɔ kɛ̌ ɛ́kwày bɛkʉ yi ákɛ́ bhak pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí Mandɛm.
Mpok yɔ, chɔŋ ntó bɔángɛl abha, mándɔk ndǔ mmɨk nkɛm, bɛbho ndǔ ɛbhɔ́kɔ́ mmɨk ɛ́mɔt bɛghaka ndu ɛchak, mánsɔt bo abhɛn Mandɛm áyábhɛ́ mánchɛm nɛbhʉɛt amɔt. 
“Nnáŋ ntat nyaka mpǎy mamiɛ́ kɛrɔ́ŋ Yerúsalɛm. Ndɔk yɛ arɛ́ nɛ nkáp bɛ́chyɛ́ nɛkwak ntá bachɛ́bhɛ́bho ɛtɔk ɛya, nɛ bɛ́chyɛ́ akap ntá Mandɛm.
Kaysí ka bǒbati bhɛka, bɔ́ bho bághàti nyaka bhe Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm. Kaysí ká bɛrɨ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fú ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnap, mǎmbɔŋ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm mbɔ bhɔ.
Bo Israɛl bachak abhɛn bachi bakoŋo Yesu babho bɛkʉ bɛtábhá mbɔ Píta, ɛnyu ɛnɛ́, yɛ̌ chi Banábas nkwɔ akʉ́ ɛnyumɔt mbɔ bhɔ.
Afɛrɛ Barábas mmu ágʉ́ɛbhɛ́ ɛbyɔk ɛtɔk nɛ awáy mmu, ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ, mbɔ ɛnyu bɔ báyàŋ. Achyɛ Yesu ntá bo Israɛl bɛ mánkʉ nɛ yi mbɔ ɛnyu bákɔ́ŋɔ́. 
Bákɛ́mɛ yí bɛ, “Nokó Yesu Acha nɛ chɔŋ Mandɛm ampɛmɛ wɔ nɛ ɛfo ɛyɛ ɛnkɛm.”
Mmǔ ntí batɛmɛ́ nɛnu Rom ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ achyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu mansɔt Pɔ̌l manchwe nɛ yí amɛm ɛbhá ɛyap. Aghati bɔ mandɛn yi nɛ ɛ́kpá bɛkʉ yí ángátí bhɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yí akʉ́ kɛ bo Israɛl báré bé ntɨ nɛ yí kpát mámbɨkɨ nɔkɔ ɛnyuyɔ.
Moses akʉ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay, nɛ atɔ́ŋ bɛrɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́tɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ Mandɛm amɛm ɛtɔk Íjip. Afɛrɛ bo Israɛl arɛ́, akʉ báfʉɛ́t ndǔ Manyu Chu, nɛ amɛm baso ndǔ mamiɛ́ bɛsa bɛpay.
Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fákárí chi ɛtɔk Bɛ́tani, ɛbhě Nyɛ́n Jɔ́dan, nɛ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ Jɔ̌n ájwìti nyaka bho. 
Bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Sɛ́chí bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ Ábraham, nɛ yɛ̌ mpok apú anɛ sɛ́chí basɛm ntá mmu. Ndaká yí ɔ́rɛ̀m bɛ chɔŋ sɛ́mfú ndǔ kɛsɛm?”
Yesu ate, abhɨŋɨ bhɔ, abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Bǎyàŋ bɛ́ nkʉ bhe yí?”
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ, yɛ̌ mmu amɔt ndǔ bo abhɛn njambɨ kɛ bɔ́ kɛtwɔ́, apú kwáy bɛ́ghókóti ɛnyɨŋ ndǔ ɛpa ɛya-nɛ.’” 
Yesu asɛp antɛ̌n njiɛ ndǔ mmɨk nɛbhʉɛt nɛ bhɔ́. Ngɛ́mtay bakoŋo bhi bábhák arɛ́ nɛ ngɛ́mtay bo bachak abhɛn báfú Yerúsalɛm nɛ abhɛn báfú atú Judɛ́ya ankɛm. Bo báfú ndǔ bɛtɔk bɛ́páy ɛbhɛn bɛchi kɛkwɔt nɛ manyu ɛbhɛn bábhìŋɨ bɛ Táya nɛ Sídɔn.
Ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ nchí kʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ bɛ́ ntɨ ɛna nɛ́mbák pɛ́pɛ́p nɛ Mandɛm, nɛ́mbak pɛ́pɛ́p nɛ bo.
abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Chɔŋ mǎnchyɛ mɛ yi mbák nkwák be mǎnkɛ́m yi?” Bápay nkáp silbha bɛbhɔ́k ɛsǎ nsɛm byo bachyɛ yi.
Ɔnáŋ ɔbhɔ̌ŋ manɛ́m batay, nɛ mmǔ anɛ ɔ́chí nɛ yi nɛ́nɛ, abhɨkɨ bhay wɔ. Ɔrɛm tɛtɛp!”
Bɛsɛ́ babhɔŋ sɛ́chí bo Israɛl, bɔtayɛsɛ nkwɔ bo Israɛl. Sɛ́pú bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl, bɔ́ bhǒ bo bárɛ̀m bɛ báchi bǒ bɛbʉ́.
Bɛ́fʉɛ́t ndǔ kɛnɛ́m ɛki nɛ ɛrɨ́tɨ́ ɛpɨŋ ɛyi, Mandɛm ǎchyɛ bhɛsɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛrɨ bɛcha, ɛbhɛn yi afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛchyɛ bhɛsɛ. Akʉ nɔ bɛ mǎmbʉ́ɛ́ bɛpɔ̌ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bo máŋwaka bɛkʉ fá amɨk, mǎndɔbhɛ bhɔŋ chi ɛpɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm.
Ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt nɛmɔt, ɛnɛ́ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ achi nɛ mɛ, ngók ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ ndǔ ɛ́fú mɛ ansɛm. Ɛbhák mbɔ ɛyɔŋɔ́ mmba.
Kɛ́p yɛ́ ka ntɨ ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ bǎghɔ̀. Chi mbi anɛ Mandɛm ányùrɛ bhe. Ɛyɔ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ Mandɛm asɔt be mbɔ bɔ̌bhi. Ntɨkɨ mmɔ́ ɛtayi apu nyurɛ yi mbák ákʉ́ ɛbɛ́ptí ɛnyɨŋ?
Mpok anɛ bakoŋó Jɔn Njwiti nkwɔ bághókó mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fàkari bágháti yi bɔ́ mɛnkɛm.
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu ábhʉɛ́t bɛrɛm kɛpɨ nɛ ngɔrɛ́ wu, bǒnto abhɛn báfú ɛkɛt Jáyrɔs, bátwɔ́ bágháti yi bɛ, “Mɔ́ywɛ anáŋ águ, ɔbhʉɛt bɛsɔŋɔri Ntɔŋ yi?”
Bě bho bǎpú kʉ mbɔ ɛnyu Mandɛm áyàŋ! Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛ́ mmu anɛ ányìɛ ɛkɔŋ nɛ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ mmɨk chí mmu anɛ ákʉ̀ mmʉɛ́t yi mǔmpap Mandɛm-ɛ? Tɛtɛp, mmu anɛ ányìɛ ɛkɔŋ nɛ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ mmɨk, chí mmu anɛ ákʉ̀ mmʉɛ́t yi mǔmpap Mandɛm.
Mpok Yesu átɔ̀ŋ bho amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm kɛ yi árɛ́mɛ́ bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn. Achí nyaka kɛ́kwɔ́t nɛ bɛkʉbhɛ akap. Yɛ̌ mmu kɛtɔk yí mbɔnyunɛ mpok yi abhɨ́kɨ́ re kway nyaka. 
Mɔ́wa Tímɔti, mɛ̌ghati wɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ɔ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ. Bɛ́kɔ̀ ndɔ́ŋ ámɔt nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bo antɨ nɛ bárɛm ɛ̌ti yɛ. Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn-nɛ mɛ̌ghàti wɔ bɛ́bhɔŋ bɛ́bhák ntá yɛ mbɔ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ nɛnu ndu bɛkʉ ɔ́nu sayri nɛ bo abhɛn bátɔ̀ŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́pú tɛtɛp.
Ɛkáti ɛnɛ ɛ́rɛ̀m ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛbhɔŋɔ bɛfakari mandú mpok. Mandɛm achyɛ́ nyaka Yesu Kristo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ bɛ yi antɔŋ bɔ ntá bǒbɛtɔk abhi. Yesu ató yɛ ángɛl akʉ mmɔ̌bɛtok aywi Jɔ̌n arɨŋɨ bhɔ.
Ndǔ ngwɛnti, Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Mmu anɛ áyàŋ bɛghok, ántá batú ángók sayri.” 
Akɛ́m mambe tándrámɔt nɛ awɔ́nɛm aywi. Akparɛnja nsɛm ɛ́páy anɛ áchap are fú yi anyu, nɛ bɛsí bhi bɛre ghɔɔ mbɔ mmok anɛ ngósí.
“Kɛ bachǐmbɨ bhɛsɛ kɛka bɛghok yi. Bápúri yi batɛn nɛpak, kɛ bápɛ́tnsɛm Íjip amɛm batɨ̌-yap.
Bǒ mankɛm abhɛn bachi arɛ babhak maknkay tontó, bábho bɛbhɛp batɨ, mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Ɛbhárɛ́mɔ Debhít nɛ́ kɛ?”
Ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ Yesu, abɨk, arɔk akwɛ́n yi bɛkak, arɛm nɛ, ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ bɛ, “Yesu Mmɔ Mandɛm Acha! Ɔ́bhɔ̌ŋ ntɨkɨ ndak nɛ mɛ? Nɨkmʉɛt ɔ́kɛ́ chyɛ mɛ ɛsɔŋɔri!”
Mǔnti nkwɔ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bɛsa bɛtay anɛ áté áyìŋɨ Yesu aghɔ́ ɛnyu yi ágú. Ɛkʉ arɛm bɛ, “Tɛtɛp, mǔnɛ achi mbʉ chi Mmɔ Mandɛm!”
Chɔŋ bɛyǎ bho mánkoŋo bɛpɔ̌ barak ɛpúsí yap nɛ ɛyɔ ɛnkʉ bo bachak mándɛm bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti mbi anɛ tɛtɛp.
Yɛ̌ agha anɛ árɨŋɨ ɛrɨ́tí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ yí ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ, kɛ yí kɛkʉ yɔ́, bɛsí Mandɛm, akʉ bɛbʉ́.
Kɛ Pɔ̌l ayap chi Sáilas. Bǒnkwɔ́ Yesu mánɨkmʉɛt bɛ bɛrɨ̌ndu Acha mɛ́mbak nɛ bhɔ.
Ɛ̌ti bɛyǎ bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhi, achyɛ́ bhɛsɛ áfɔ́k ndɔŋ nɛ ndɔŋ.
Mpok yɔ, mǔkɛnɔŋ amɔt anɛ bo báré rɨŋɨ ɛ̌ti barak anɛ yí áré kʉ, abhak ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ. Aka nnyɛ́n bɛ́ Barábas.
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Mbák ndɛm ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́pú chak, ghatí mɛ yɔ. Kɛ mbák ndɛm ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi chak, ɔdɛp mɛ ndáká yí?”
“Mɛmbɔŋ ngɔ nyaka bɛ, ɛ́chí ɛpók ɛya bɛkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ndu mɛnu nɛ bo abhɛn mánókó nnyɛ́n Yesu mmu Násárɛt.
Mbák bawú bápú pɛtnsɛm chɔŋ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, ntí anɛ bájwìti bho ndǔ ntí bo abhɛn bawú achi bɛ yi?
