Yesu arɛm nɛ ɛyɔŋ amfay bɛ, “Mmǔ anɛ ánókó mɛ, abhɨ́kɨ́ noko chí mɛ, anókó mmu anɛ ato mɛ nkwɔ.
Sɔ̌l arɨŋɨ nkaysi yap. Báre noŋ yi bɛti nɛ ngósí ndu manyǔbhá anɛ Damáskɔs bɛ mpok yi áyàŋ bɛfʉɛt, mankɛm yí mangway.
Ɛwak ɛ́mɔ́t, anɛ mɔ́nkwɛn arɛm ntá ɛtayi bɛ, ‘Ɛta, chyɛ awa ákɔ́rɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́.’ Ɛtayap akɔrɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhi ntá yap bati apay.
Kɛ nchí kʉ chí mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛtaya ághátí mɛ, bɛ́ bǒ mmɨk mándɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ nkɔŋ yi. Faté ká sɛ́ndɔ́k.”
Chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛ́p ntá yɛka, be bho bo bǎrɛ̀m ɛrɨ́rɨ́ ɛ̌ti yɛka, mbɔnyunɛ ɛnyu yɔ kɛ̌ bachǐmbɨ bhap bárɛ̀m nyaka ɛ̌ti barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ nsé.” 
Kɛ́ yɨkɨ ɔmbɨŋɨ ntí ywɛ mbɔnyunɛ ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ ɛkaká ɛmɛnɛ ɛ́mbák pɛ́pɛ́p, nɛ ɔbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ yɔ ɛmbak pyɔ.
Ɔchí agha bɛji mmɔ̌bɛtok mǔchak? Mmu anɛ akway bɛrɛm bɛ mmɔ̌bɛtok akʉ sayri, nɛ yɛ̌ chi ɛbʉ́bʉ, chí chi-bɛtɨk aywi. Mmɔ̌ bɛtok apú kwɛn mbɔnyunɛ Acha abhɔ̌ŋ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ yi ánté sɛnɛ́.
“Bakak ámbák nɛ Mandɛm Acha bo Israɛl, mbɔnyunɛ atwɔ ndu bɛkwak bǒbhi, nɛ ndu bɛ́fɛ́rɛ bhɔ ndǔ kɛsɛm.
Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ abhɔŋ bɛ́gháka bɛtɔkɔ́ mmɨk mɛnkɛm kɛ ngwɛ́nti antwɔ́.
Kɛ nɛghɔ́ anɛ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk bághɔ́ yi, bábhó bɛrɛm nɛ batɨ bɛ, ‘Yɨŋɨ́ mbɔ̌ŋ mɔ́ywi nɛ́, nɛ yí kɛ̌ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛ́nyiɛ́ nɛwú ɛtayi. Twɔ́ ká sɛ́nkɛm yi sɛ́ngwáy bɛ́ ɛtayi ánáŋ ángú, mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhi mɛ́ndɔp chi ɛbhɛsɛ.’
arɛm ntá yi bɛ, ‘Fǎ ɛtɔk ɛyɛ, dɔ̌ nnɛrɛ́kɛt aywɛ dɔ́k atú anɛ mɛ́tɔ̀ŋ chɔŋ wɔ.’
Kɛ máyi arɛm bɛ, “Nnyɛ́n ɛni nɛbhɔŋ bɛbhak chi Jɔ̌n.”
Mbɨ́kɨ́ bhʉɛrɛ ntɨ bɛ́ bo mánchyɛ́ mɛ kɛnókó. Kɛ mmǔ achí anɛ áyàŋ bɛ́ bo mánchyɛ́ mɛ kɛnókó, nɛ yí kɛ ákway bɛrɛm ɛnyǔ mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́bhak.
Nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ mǎnɨkmʉɛt bɛ Mandɛm anchyɛ bhe, apú rɔ bɛchyɛ bhe, mbák mǎnókó.” 
Bakwɔ́ bho Kristo abhɛn Ésia bátó be bakak. Akwíla nɛ Príska nɛ bǒnkwɔ abhɛn báchɛmɛ nɔkɔ ɛkɛt ɛyi bátó be bɛyǎ bakak ndǔ nnyɛ́n Acha.
“Mpok anɛ Mandɛm abhɔŋɔ bɛkʉ bariɛp amɛm yi afyɛ́ nyaka nɛ Ábraham aghaka nɔkɔ kɛkwɔt, mpǎy bo Israɛl abhɛn bachi Íjip bɛpɛt baya tontó.
Yesu achɔkɔ abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Kɛfɔ Mandɛm fá amɨk kɛchi mbɔ yi? Chɔŋ sɛ́nsɔt ntɨkɨ nɛkay bɛtɔŋ ɛnyu kɔ kɛchi?
Babhʉɛ́p áchyɛ́ bhɛsɛ bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri, sɛ́ré rɔ́ŋ pɛti pɛti, sɛ́mfʉɛrɛ nɔkɔ ɛbhě Krɛt ɛyɔ kpát sɛ́chwɔ́p ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ́ Ɛrɨ́tɨ́ Nɛchyɛ̌nyɛ́n, kɛ́kwɔ́t nɛ ɛtɔk Lásea.
Apɛt arɔ bhɔ́ arɔk anɨkmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm ɛnyumɔt mbɔ ndɔŋ anɛ mbɨ.
Matá árɛ́mɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, arɔk abhɨŋɨ mɔ́mayi María, aghati yí ndǔ ɛyu bɛ, “Ntɔŋ atwɔ, nɛ ǎyáŋ bɛghɔ wɔ́.”
Ɛkʉ bɔ̌mayi bárɛ́m ntá yi bɛ, “Fǎ fá, dɔ́k atú Judɛ́ya bɛ bakoŋo bhɛ mángɔ́ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛbhɛn ɔ́kʉ̀.
Mbák ɛ́chí tɛtɛp bɛ bawú bapu pɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, nɔ sɛ́sè chi nsé ɛ̌ti Mandɛm, ndu sɛ́ghàti bho bɛ Mandɛm akʉ Kristo apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Mbák ɛchí tɛtɛp bɛ bawú bapu pɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, nɔ Mandɛm abhɨ́kɨ́ kʉ Kristo ampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m nɛ nɔ nɛka ɛnɛsɛ nɛchi chi ndɛ́ndɛm.
Ɛ̌ti ɛyɔ kɛ̌ nchí tó bé Tímɔti mmu áchí mɔ́wa ndǔ ábhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Acha mbɔ mɛ. Nkɔŋ yí tontó, nɛ achí mmú tɛtɛp. Nchí tó yi bɛ antwɔ antɨk be ɛnyǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛna, mbɔ mmǔ Yesu Kristo nɛchi, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ mɛ̌tɔ̀ŋ bǒnkwɔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak.
Mbák mmu abhɔ̌ŋ ntíánwɔ́p ɛ̌ti ya nɛ ɛ̌ti Ɛyɔŋ ɛya ndǔ mkpáká bho anɛ́ ápú kʉ mbɔ ɛnyu Mandɛm áyàŋ, mkpáká bho bɛbʉ́, chɔŋ Mmɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm mbɔ̌ŋ ntíánwɔ́p ɛ̌ti yi mpok nchí twɔ nɛ kɛnɛ́m Ɛtaya nɛ bɔángɛl bhi.”
Bě bǒ bɛtabha! Bǎrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ nɛbu mǎndɛm mbák manyiɛp ǎkwɛn chɔŋ, nɛ mbák apu kwɛn. Ndaká yí bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm ákʉ̀ ndǔ mpokó-nɛ? 
Ɛ̌ti yɔ, mbɔŋ yɛ bɛyǎ ɛkwak ndu bɛghati be nkwɔ bǒ bǎchi Rom Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́. 
Nɛka ɛni kɛ nɛ́kʉ́ yi achɔkɔ atú anɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ bariɛp bɛchyɛ yi. Abhak arɛ́, achɔkɔ ndu bɛ́tɛ́m mbɔ bɛ achi chi kɛnkɔ. Ɛnyumɔt, mɔ́ywi Áisek, nɛ ɛbhárɛ́ mɔ́ywi Jekɔ́p, bo Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛchyɛ bhɔ mmɨk yɔ nkwɔ, báchɔ́kɔ ndu bɛ́tɛ́m nɛ yi Ábraham.
Nɛ ɛrɛm ɛyɔŋɔ́ mmba ɛ́nkwɛn. Chɔŋ ntó bɔángɛl abha ndǔ mmɨk nkɛm, mánsɔt bo abhɛn Mandɛm áyábhɛ́, bɛbho ndǔ ɛbhɔ́kɔ́mɨk ɛ́mɔt bɛghaka ndu ɛchak, mánchɛm nɛbhʉɛt amɔt. 
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Bǎkaysi bɛ mankɔ̌ abhɛn bachi ndǔ ɛpǎ nɛbhay bakway bɛbhak ndǔ nɛtarɛ́nsay? Nsé! Tɛ̌ndu mbǎyngɔrɛ́ abhʉɛ́t nɛ bhɔ, bápú kway bɛtat nsay.
Yɛ̌ ɛmbak chi bɛ nchí yaŋ bɛdɛp awɔ antɨ mpú bhak ɛchɨŋtímu mbɔnyunɛ nchí rɛm chi tɛtɛp. Kɛ mpú kʉ nɔ́ ndǔ mpú yáŋ bɛ yɛ̌ mmu ánkáysí bɛ ncha ɛnyǔ mmu ɛnɛ yi ághɔ̀ nɛ ɛnɛ́ yi ághòk mɛ̌rɛm bɛ nchí.
Yi amfú arɛ́ andɔk bɛrwɔ bǒ bɛtɔk mɛnkɛm. Bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛtɔkɔ́ mmɨk ɛbhɔ bɛ Gɔ́g nɛ Mágɔg. Satan anchɛm yɛ bǒ bɛtɔk ɛbhɛn mankɛm ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt amɔt bɛ mandɔk nɛnu nɛ Mandɛm. Bǒ bɛtɔk ɛbhɔ báya mbɔ ɛ̌siɛ́p ɛnɛ ɛchi angɔkɔ manyu.
Nɛ Mandɛm abhɨ́kɨ́ ghoko mbakanɛm ɛ̌ti ngɔrɛ́, kɛ aghókó ngɔrɛ́ ɛ̌ti mbakanɛm.
Bɛyǎ bo bátwɔ̀ chɔŋ mánsɔt nnyɛ́n ɛna mántɛn ambɨ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap andɛm nɔkɔ bɛ, ‘Mɛ kɛ nchí Mpɛmɛ anɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtó!’ Nɛ mándwɔ bɛyǎ bho bɛ mánjibhiri batɨ yap.
Ndǔ bǎchɛ́mɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Kristo, afɛ́rɛ́ ɛbɛ́ptí ɛpɨŋ amɛm batɨ yɛka. Ɛyɔ chí ɛrɨŋ bɛtɔŋ bɛ bǎchi bǒbhi. Puyɛ̌ chi ɛrɨŋ ɛnɛ mmu afyɛ́ amʉɛt mpok báyaŋ bɛsyɛp yi mbɔ ɛnyǔ bo Israɛl bákʉ mpoknkɛm. Chí Kristo kɛ afyɛ́ ɛrɨŋ ɛyi amɛm batɨ ayɛka.
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, mmǔ achak aghɔ́ Píta arɛm bɛ, “Wɔ nkwɔ ɔchí mmǔ ywi amɔt.” Píta akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Cháá, mpú nɛ bhɔ”
Yesu ayɨŋɨ bhɔ dǐǐ, abhɛp bɛ, “Ntí basɨŋɨ́ amɛn achi bɛ yi? Basɨŋɨ́ amɛn árɛ̀m bɛ: ‘Nkúbhɛ́ ntay ɛnɛn batɛ̌kɛt bágʉɛ́bhɛ́ bɛ́ nɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ rɨ, nɔ́ kɛ nɛ́rɔ́bhɛ́ ntay ɛnɛn nɛ́kɛ́mɛ́ ɛkɛt nɛchá batay áchák ankɛm.’
Mbák gɔ́bhanɔ ángók ndak anɛ, chɔŋ sɛ́ndɨŋɨ ndǔ sɛ́chòk nnyu ywi bɛ ntɨ nɛndɨ yi amɛm, ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ bǎpu chwe ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri.”
Akʉ bɛsɛ sɛ́mbák bǒbhi abhɛn yi achi Mfɔ wap. Akʉ bɛ́ sɛ́mbák bachiǎkap ntá Ɛtayi Mandɛm. Kɛnɛ́m nɛ kɛfɔ chí ɛki mpoknkɛm. Amen.
Mmu anɛ Mandɛm áchí ɛtayi, ǎkɔŋ bɛghok ɛyɔŋ ɛyi. Ntí anɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ kɔŋ bɛghok Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm achí bɛ bǎpú bɔ̌bhi.”
Kɛ Kristo achyɛ́ bhe Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ Mmu achi nɛ bhe. Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ chɛp yɛ mmu anɛ ákway bɛtɔŋ bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi tɛtɛp. Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ǎtɔ̀ŋ bhe mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi átɔ̀ŋ bhe ɛchi tɛtɛp. Nsé apu arɛ. Nchí ghati yɛ bhe bɛ, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ átɔ̀ŋ bhe, bǎkɛ́ rɔ bɛbhak ndǔ nɛbharɛ́mʉɛt nɛ Mmɔ.
Himɛ́neɔs nɛ Aleksánda báchí nkwɔ́ mbɔ bo abhɛn bábyàk ɛnyǔ ntɨ ɛnɛn nɛpu twɔ nɛ áyɔ́mɛ. Ndɔ́ bhɔ́ bati apay amɔ Satan bɛ mándɔ́ bɛrɛm ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti Mandɛm.
Manyɛ́n yap áchí nyaka bɛ: Símun anɛ Yesu áchyɛ́ nnyɛ́n nɛchak bɛ Píta, nɛ mɔ̌máyi Andru, nɛ Jems nɛ Jɔ̌n, nɛ Fílip nɛ Batolómio,
Ɛkáti nɛwú-bɛ́su ɛchi mbɔ nku. Mbák sɛ́kʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mmu ásɨ́ŋɨ́ arɛm ɛnyǔ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkɔrɛ nɛwú ɛni, bápú kway bɛkoŋo yɔ kpatɛ ɛ́mbak kpoŋoroŋ bɛ yi ánáŋ ágú.
Mmɛ Jɔ̌n, nchí sɛmti yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ághòk bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi amɛm ɛkáti ɛnɛ ɛbhɛn bɛ́rɛ̀m ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛfakari. Mbák mmu ámáká ɛnyɨŋ ndǔ ɛbhɛn bɛchi amɛm ɛkáti ɛnɛ, chɔŋ Mandɛm amaka yi ntɛmsi achak. Chɔŋ antɛmsi yi nɛ bɛghori ɛbhɛn ntáká amɛm ɛkáti-nɛ.
Arɛm nɔkɔ nɔ, ɛpʉ́ítí ɛ́kwɛ́n nɛ́ntɨ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi nɛ bǒnkwɔ Sádusi nɛ ɛchɛmɛ ɛ́kɔ́rɛ.
Yesu asɔt yɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi, afú ɛtɔk nɛ bhɔ. Bárɔ́k bachwɔp ɛtɔk Bɛ́tani. Arɛ́, ayoŋ amɔ amfay, are yɛt bhɔ.
Dɔ́k ka! Nchí to be ntá bǒ mmɨk mbɔ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n nɛntɨ nkwɔ.
Bɛyǎ bhó bátwɔ̀ nyaka mándɔk nɔkɔ ɛnyunɛ́ Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ yɛ̌ ɛpok mɛnyiɛ nɛnyíɛ́. Ɛ́kʉ arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Sɛ́ndɔ́k ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ achi kpák bɛ mǎnjwémʉɛt mandú.”
Ɛnɛ́ bɛyǎ bǒbhɔ báté angɔkɔnyɛ́n, abho bɛghati bhɔ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ ndǔ bakay bɛ,
Nɛ́nɛ, Táytɔs apɛt akɔŋ be áchá, sayri sayri, mpok yi átɨ̀k ɛnyǔ bǎsíɛ́ptí yi nɛ bɛcháy, mǎngwɛrɛ nɔkɔ, nɛ ɛnyǔ bǎkʉ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ághátí bhe.
Mbák ngɔrɛ́ achi nɛ mmu achak mpok nnɛ́m ábhʉɛ́t nɛpɛ́m, nɔ achi nkwɛnɛ́ bɛrwɔp. Kɛ mbák nnɛ́m agu, ɛbhé ɛnɛ́ ɛ́gwɔ́rɛ́ yi nɛ nnɛ́m ɛpu pɛrɛ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ amfay yi. Nɛ mbák abhay mmǔ chak, apú bhak nkwɛnɛ́ bɛrwɔp.
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Chi mmu anɛ mɛ̌tap chɔŋ brɛt anɛ amɛm nchán nnok nchyɛ́ yí.” Yesu asɔt yɛ ɛkpɔkɔ́ brɛt atap ndǔ nnok, achyɛ Júdas, mmɔ̌ Símun Iskariɔt.
Yesu ayibhiri mmʉɛt aghɔ́ yi, aghati yi bɛ, “Mɔ́wa, kɛ́chay. Nɛka ɛnɛ nɛ mɛ nɛ́kʉ ɔtaŋ.” Tɛ́mté wu ngɔrɛ́ wu ataŋ.
bɔ́ batí apay mándɔp mbɔ mmǔ amɔt. Bɔ́ kɛpɛrɛ bhak yɛ bati apay, kɛ mmǔ amɔt.’
Yesu akɛmɛ nɔkɔ nɔ, mǔngo bachiǎkap wu akɛ́m ndɛn ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chi yímbɔŋ amʉɛt adak. Arɛm bɛ “Sɛ́pɛ́t sɛ́yàŋ batísiɛ́ mántwɔ́ mándɛ́m ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ákʉ́ ndaká yí?
Kɛ ɛnɛ́ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bábhàbhɛri Píta ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ, bakoŋo Yesu báré nɨkmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm nɛ batɨ yap ankɛm ɛ̌ti yi. 
Nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́, apɛtnsɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm běti běti. Bǒ mankɛm bárɔ́k ntá yi. Achɔkɔ amɨk, abho bɛtɔŋ bhɔ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm.
Mbák ɔchí nyaka chí nsɛm mpok Mandɛm ábhɨ́ŋɨ́ wɔ́, ɛyɔ ɛ́kɛ́ sɔŋɔri ntɨ ɛnɛ amɛm. Mbák ɔbhɔŋ mbi bɛkʉ bɛ́ ɔ́kɛ́ pɛrɛ bhák nsɛm, dɔ́k ambɨ.
Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Ɛyɔŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́twɔ́ ɛ̌ti yɛka. Ɛbhɨkɨ twɔ ɛ̌ti ya.
Mɛnyǔ bǒbhɔ puyɛ̌ bǒnto abhɛn tɛtɛp. Chi bo abhɛn báyíbhírí mkpá, nɛ bárwɔ̀ bho ndǔ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn bɔ bákʉ bɛ báchi bǒnto Kristo.
Bɛbɛpti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm bɛ́fù mmu chi antɨ nɛ bɔ́ kɛ bɛ́kʉ̀ mmu akɛ bhak pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí Mandɛm.” 
Tɛ̌ndu sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ nkúbhɛ́ ɛfóŋó nɛka mbɔ mmǔ anɛ arɛmɛ mbɔ ɛnyu ɛchi amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm bɛ, “Nnókó, nɛ ɛ̌ti yɔ ndɛm”. Bɛse nkwɔ sɛ́noko, nɛ ɛ̌ti yɔ sɛ́ghàti bo Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́.
Mmu ákɛ́ fyɛ yɛ ákɔ́rɛ́ nɛntɨ bo abhɛn Mandɛm áchɛ́mtí.”
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Mɛ nkwɔ mbɔ̌ŋ ɛnyɨŋ bɛbhɛp be. Ghatí ká mɛ.
Nɛ nɛka ɛnɛn Jekɔ́p nɛ Mandɛm kɛ nɛ́kʉ́ yi áyɛ́rɛ́ bɔ̌mɔ́ywi Josɛ́f bati apay mpok yi arɔbhɛ kɛkwɔt bɛgu, aghɔkɔ mmʉɛt ndǔ ntɛm ɛni, achyɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó.
Ɛbhɨkɨ tat, mmu amɔt achwe aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Ghók ká, bo abhɛn bǎfé ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ ɛ́yu, báchí awu amɛm ɛkɛrákap téé bátɔ̀ŋ bo.”
Achí ɛrɔŋɔ bɛtɔŋ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl mbi bɛrɨŋɨ wɔ, nɛ bɛ kɛnókó kɛ́ntwɔ́ ntá bǒbhɛ, bo Israɛl.”
Ɛ́rɨ ɛcha ntá bo abhɛn básó ndɛn ɛ́yap bɛ mánkwáy bɛ́bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ bɛfʉɛt ndǔ manyǔbha anɛ ɛtɔk ɛyɔ mǎnchwe amɛm manyíɛ́ kɛpɛm ɛkɛ́n ɛ́nɔkɔ́ nɛpɛ́m.
abhɨ́kɨ́ fu ntá nkwǎ, nɛ yɛ̌ nkwǎŋwaŋ abhɨkɨ tɔŋ mɛ. Mbɔŋ Yesu Kristo kɛ ákʉ́ mɛndɨ́ŋɨ́ yɔ.
Mbák mǎnkɔ́ŋ batɨ, chɔŋ ɛ́nkʉ bǒ mankɛm mándɨŋɨ bɛ bǎchí bakoŋo bha.” 
Chiɛ́ bhɛsɛ bɛtaŋ bɛbú bǒmame, nɛ bɛtɔŋ bɛrɨŋɨ́ maknkay nɛ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ndǔ nnyɛ́n mǔbɛtok ywɛ Yesu, mmu achi nyáŋá.”
Ndu bɛkʉ bɛ nkɛ́ pányu ɛ̌ti bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ́ mɛndɨ́ŋɨ́, áchyɛ́ mɛ ɛsɔŋɔri. Mbák mbɔ mmu anɛ báfyɛ́ yi nsé amʉɛt. Ɛsɔŋɔri ɛyɔ ɛbhak ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Satan átó bɛ ɛ́nyíɛ́rɛ́ mɛ amɨk, ɛ́nkaŋ mɛ nkɛ pányu.
Mandɛm ákʉ̀ nyaka nɔ bɛtɔŋ ɛnyǔ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛyǎ kɛnɛ́m nɛ ɛnyǔ áchyɛ bhɛsɛ mbɔk kɛnɛ́m ɛki. Atóŋtí nyaka bhɛsɛ ambɨ ambɨ bɛ sɛ́mbɔ́ŋ mbi bɛchwe ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt kɛnókó yi.
Bariɛp amɛn Mandɛm afyɛ́ tɛsáy bɛ chɔŋ bǒbhi mǎnchwe ndǔ nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt ɛni abhʉɛ́t. Sɛbhɔŋ yɛ bɛsɔt mpok bɛ yɛ̌ mmu ywɛka akɛ bhak anɛ bárɛm ɛ̌ti yi bɛ abhɨkɨ kway mmu anɛ achwe ndǔ nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt ɛnɔ.
Fíɛ́ ká ntí chi bɛ Mandɛm ámbák Mfɔ ywɛka, nɛ chɔŋ yí anchyɛ be mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm nkwɔ. 
Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ nɛ achí ɛ̌ti Mɔ́ywi. Yí achi nyaka ɛbhárɛ́mɔ Mfɔ Debhít ndǔ nɛtwɔ́ anɛ yi átwɔ́ fá amɨk mbɔ nkwǎ.
Ɛ́rɨ yɛ bɛ ɔ́nchyɛ́ ɛyɔŋ bo mandɔk mambabhɛri nɔkɔ nnɛm ɛni kpátɛ manywɔp arat amfʉɛt. Bakoŋo bhi bákway bɛrɔŋ mángɛp yi mámpɔkɔ, mándɔk, mámbo yɛ bɛghati bho bɛ yi apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Nɛ mbák ɛ́mfákárí nɔ́, nsé yap yɔ ǎchɔŋti mɛnyɨŋ ancha nsé anɛ mbɨ.”
Nɛ bápú nyu ɛsɨ́ mmɛ́m mánjaŋ amɛn bakɔ mbɔnyunɛ bákaysi bɛ ɛsɨ́ mmɛ́m arɨ̌ achá amɛn bakɔ.”
Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ sayri bɛ́ mbok nɛwú Yesu ndǔ ɛkotákátí chí ɛchɨŋti ntá bǒ abhɛn báchí ndǔ mbi nɛwú. Kɛ ntá yɛsɛ́ bǒ Mandɛm ǎpɛ̀mɛ, sɛ́ghɔ̀ bɛtaŋ Mandɛm ndǔ nɛwú Yesu.
Nɛchyɛ̌ nyɛ́n ɛnɛ́n bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ́ Ɛrɨtí Nɛchyɛ̌nyɛ́n nɛ́chí nyaka raŋáraŋa kɛbhák sayri bɛ́ sɛ́nchɔ́kɔ́ arɛ́ sɛ́nóŋ mpok anɛ mbʉ́ɛ́p ataŋataŋ anɛ anu mpok mbaŋ ákwɛ̀n ámáy. Ɛ́kʉ́ bɛyǎ bo abhɛn bákʉ̀ bɛtɨk amɛm áchwí báré yáŋ mbi bɛ́rɔ́ŋ Foiniks. Foiniks abhak nɛchyɛ̌nyɛn Krɛt ɛnɛn áchwí ate arɛ́ bɛcháy ti, yɛ chí ndǔ mpok yɔ. 
Fɛrɛ́ yɛ́ ka ɛsɨ́ mkpá ayɛka anɛ áchyɛ̀ nyaka be ɛbɛ́ptí ɛkakánɛkɔ. Bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mǎŋwaka nyaka bɛkʉ bɛ́rwɔ̀ nyaka bhe nɛ mɛ́nchɔŋti nɔkɔ batɨ̌ yɛka amɛm.
Nkɔŋ be mbɔnyunɛ bɛsɛ́ sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ tɛtɛp anɛ ǎbhák amɛm batɨ ayɛsɛ nɛ abhak nɛ bɛsɛ tɛ ndǔ nɛŋɔkɔ́mɨk ɛnɛn nɛ́twɔ̀.
chɔŋ yi nkwɔ anyú mmɛ́m bɛběntɨ Mandɛm amɛn Mandɛm afyɛ́ ndu nkɔp anjwi tɛ́p yi kɛ chɔpti mɔ nɛ manyiɛp ndu áyaŋ mántaŋ. Nɛ chɔŋ yi wu ambɔ́ŋ nnɛ́m ɛsɔŋɔri amɛm ngó anɛ ádù nɛ *sɔ́lfɔ, bɛsí bɔángɛl Mandɛm nɛ bɛsí Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n.
Mbyaká bɛbhé Mandɛm wu ǎtwɔ bɛkʉ bɛtɨk Satan. Nɛ chɔŋ ansɔt bɛtaŋ ɛbhi ankʉ baraká maknkay anɛ bapu mɛnyu nɛ mɛnyu ndu bɛ́rwɔ bho.
Yesu achí nyaka nyáŋá nɛ chak bɛsí Mandɛm, Yɛ̌ nɔ be kɛka bɛ Páílet ándɔ́ yi andɔk. Bǎrɛ́m bɛ Páílet ándɔ́ chí ngwayti bho andɔk.
Kaká ká nkwɔ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk Yesu Acha abhɛn baghɔrɛ́, Trifína nɛ Trifósa. Kaká ká mmʉɛrɛkɔŋ awa Pɛ́sis mmu ákʉ́ bɛyǎ bɛtɨk ntá Acha.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bɔ bághɔ́ ɛ́bhak ɛnyɨŋ bɛ́chay tontó, kpát Moses yímbɔŋ arɛm bɛ, “Mmʉɛt ǎwɛt mɛ gbagbǎghak nɛ bɛcháy.”
Mbɔ̌ŋ bɛcháy bɛ nnáŋ mpɛt ntwɔ awu chɔŋ Ɛta Mandɛm ánkʉ mbɔ́ŋ ntíánwɔ́p bɛsí ɛbhɛka, nɛ mbak ndǔ nɛdǐ kɛbhɔ ɛ̌ti bɛyǎ bǒ ahbɛn bákʉ̀ nyaka bɛbʉ́ nɛ bábhʉɛt bɛkʉ bɛpɔ̌ mɛnyɨŋ, nɛ ɛpúsí, nɛ mányiɛ bɛpǎ ɛpusi.
Bárɛ́m ntá yi bɛ, ‘Acha, pú yi abhɔŋ bɛbhǎ byo?’
Jɔ̌n ǎrɛ̀m nyaka nkwɔ bɛ, “Mmǔ ǎtwɔ mɛ ansɛm anɛ áchá mɛ. Mbɨ́kɨ́ kwáy yɛ̌ bɛ́chóti yi bɛkak bɛ́ nkáŋárí nkubhanya bɛkak ɛbhi.
Píta atɨ́k nɔkɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ Yesu árɛ́mɛ́ ntá ɛnɔk fig ɛyɔ, arɛm bɛ, “Acha, yɨŋɨ́! Ɛnɔk ɛnɛ́ ɔ́rɛ́mɛ́ bɛ ɛpu kwáy mɛnyu kɛpɛm ɛ́gu.”
Símiɔn anaŋ ághátí bhɛsɛ ɛnyǔ Mandɛm ábhó bɛtɔŋ bɛ́ akɔŋ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl nkwɔ, nɛ ayap mbɔk ɛyap bɛ mámbák bǒbhi.
Ángɛl Mandɛm abhesi bɔ́ bɛsí, bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ Mandɛm bɛghɔ bhɔ́ amʉɛt nɛ bɛcháy bɛkɛm bɔ́ tontó.
Baway nɔkɔ Stífin, mbɔk bo abhɛn báchyɛ̀ Mandɛm kɛnókó bápɔ́kɔ yi bárɔ́k bábhɛ́mɛ, nɛ bádi yi tontó.
Ɛ́kʉ́ nkwɛ́n amɨk ngók ɛyɔŋ ndǔ ɛ́rɛ̀m ntá ya bɛ, ‘Sɔ̌l! Sɔ̌l! Ɔ́chyɛ̀ mɛ nɛnyok ndaká yí?’
Ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ́nyɨkɨsi yi gbogbǒgbok, ɛ́bɨk nɛ bɛtaŋ, ɛ́rɔ́ yi.
Ɔ́kɛ́pɛrɛ chɔŋti yɛ mpok. Faté mánjwítí wɔ, ɔ́ndɔ Mandɛm anso bɛbʉ́ bhɛ, ɔmbɨŋɨ nɔkɔ nnyɛ́n Acha.’ 
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Pú maŋɔkɔ́ nywɔp áchi byo nɛ apay bɛ́bho beti bɛ́gháka beku? Mmu anɛ ákɔ̀ nɛ ngósí, apú chɨŋti nɛkwɛn mbɔnyunɛ ǎghɔ̀ ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ mmɨk.
Bǒ bhɔ barɔk *bákɛ́m Yesu bábáyti.
Bě bo Samaria, bǎchyɛ̀ kɛnókó ntá ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎbhɨ́kí rɨŋɨ. Bɛsɛ bo Judeya sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ mmu anɛ sɛ́chyɛ̀ kɛnókó mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm ǎfʉɛt chí ntá bo Judeya bɛ́pɛ́mɛ bho.
Tɛ̌ndu sɛ́chí yɛ chak bɛsí Mandɛm nɛ́nɛ ndu sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛka nɛ Yesu, sɛ́chí ndu kpák nɛ Mandɛm ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Acha ywɛsɛ Yesu Kristo ákʉ́ ntá yɛsɛ.
“Mpok mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fàkari, chɔŋ mánkɛm be mámfyɛ amɔ́ bǒbati ɛtɔk bɛ mányok bhe sayri, mángwáy bhe. Nɛ chɔŋ bǒ bɛtɔkɔ́ mmɨk mankɛm mámpap bhe ɛ̌ti bǎchí bakoŋo bha.
Ɛ́kʉ́ Páílet afú amɛm sɛnta ywi arɔk atɛmɛri bhɔ nɛfí, abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ mmǔ-nɛ akʉ́?”
Pɔ̌l asɔt Sáilas bárɔk Síria nɛ Silísha ɛnɛ́ yi afyɛ́ ntɨ nta bakwɔ́ Yesu abhɛn báchí arɛ ntɨ.
Ngɔ́ yɛ bawú, manɛ́m bho nɛ ndɛ́ndɛmɛ́ bho. Bábhak tě bɛsí ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ. Mánɛ́nɛ bɛkáti. Mánɛ́nɛ ɛkáti ɛchak nkwɔ, nɔ chi ɛkáti nɛpɛ́m. Bátáŋ bo abhɛn manaŋ bagu nyaka bɛ́kóŋo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ wap ákʉ, mbɔ ɛnyu basɨŋɨ amɛm bɛkáti.
Mandɛm bachǐmbɨ bhɛsɛ́ akʉ Yesu mmu báwáy ndu bago yi ndu ɛkotákátí ampɛtnsɛm ndu nɛpɛ́m.
Pú wɔ́ ɔ́chí mmu Íjip? Pú wɔ kɛ ɔkʉ bo bágʉɛ́bhɛ́ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛtɔk nɛ ɔkʉ bawǎy bho nka ɛnwi bárɔ́k nɛ wɔ amɛm baso?”
Mbák bǒmpap abhap báyàŋ bɛkʉ bhɔ ɛnyɨŋ, ngó áfù bhɔ anyu ámɛn bhɔ. Ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ báway yɛ agha anɛ áyàŋ bɛkʉ bhɔ ɛbɛ́ptí ɛnyɨŋ.
Sɛ́bhɔŋ bɛkʉ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn mmu anɛ átó mɛ ndǔ mpok anɛ bɛti bɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ re twɔ. Bɛti bɛ́twɔ̀, nɛ mɛ́náŋ mɛ́ntwɔ́, yɛ̌ mmu apú pɛrɛ kway bɛkʉ bɛtɨk.
Kristo abhɔŋ yi bɛkʉ nɛ Satan? Mmu anɛ ánókó Yesu abhɔŋ yi bɛkʉ nɛ mmu anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ noko?
Kɛ ɛ̌ti ɔ́gwɔ̀t ntɨ ɛnɛ amɛm ɔkɛ ka bɛ́tɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛ, ɔ̌kʉ̀ bɛběntɨ Mandɛm nɛ wɔ mɛnja mɛndɔk nɔkɔ chi ambɨ. Nɛ chɔŋ mɛ́mfú kpoŋoroŋ ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɛn Mandɛm átɔ̀ŋ bɛběntɨ ɛbhi, antáŋ bo ɛnyu ɛnɛ ɛchi chak.
Píta arɛm bɛ, “Ná wɔ nɛ nnɛ́m aywɛ bǎká ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt mɛmɔ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm Acha ɛnyǔ ɛyɔ? Ghok! Bo abhɛn bábhɛ́mɛ́ nnɛ́m aywɛ, báchi afɔ ambǐnywɔp, nɛ chɔŋ mampɔkɔ wɔ nkwɔ.”
Bábhɛp yi bɛ, “Akʉ́ yi ntá yɛ? Ná yi ákʉ́ kɛ ɔ̌ghɔ mbaŋ?”
Yɛ̌ agha anɛ ághókó mbok mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fákárí abhʉɛrɛ bhɔ antɨ, ambɛbhɛ nɔkɔ mmʉɛ́t ɛyi bɛ, “Ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ mmú yi abhak chɔŋ?” Ɛ́bhak kpoŋoroŋ bɛ bɛtaŋ Mandɛm Acha bɛ́chí nɛ yi. 
Pɔkɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ká batu batɨ. Mbák mǎnkʉ nɔ, nɔ bábhʉ̀rɛ ɛbhé Kristo.
Píta arɔk ndu áchwí, aya bɛyǎ nkáp, akó ɛbhɨ nɛ wu. Ájwí nɛ nsi ɛgho ɛbhak bɛsa tándrámɔt nsɛm byo nɛ ɛ́rát. Kɛ yɛ̌ndu nsi ɛyɔ ɛ́yá nɔ́, ásɨ kɛdakati.
Mbɔ ɛnyu ɛ́fákárí nyaka mpok Nóa, nɔ́ kɛ̌ ɛ́fàkari chɔŋ kɛ Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm ambesi.
“Ɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ mamiɛ́ bɛsa bɛpay, ángɛl Mandɛm abhesi ntá yi amɛm baso, kɛkwɔt Njiɛ Sináy. Ángɛl wu abhak amɛm ngó anɛ ádù ndǔ mɔ́nɔk amɔt anɛ ágò ɛbhɨ.
Nɛ bǎkɛ́ kʉ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ Mandɛm ambɔŋ kɛsɔ́ti. Mandɛm achyɛ́ bhe Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ mbɔ ɛrɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ bǎchi bǒbhi nɛ bɛ chɔŋ anaŋa bɛfɛrɛ bhe ndǔ kɛsɛm ɛwak ɛ́mɔt.
Chɔŋ mbak nɛ bhɔ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɔ́chí nɛ mɛ, bɛ sayri sayri, mándɔp chi mmu amɔt, bɛ́ mmɨk ankway bɛrɨŋɨ bɛ wɔ kɛ ɔ́tó mɛ, nɛ bɛ́ ɔkɔŋ bɔ́ mbɔnyu ɔ́kɔ́ŋ mɛ.
Kɛ Yesu kɛgʉɛ́p mmʉɛt ntá yap, mbɔnyunɛ, arɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka ɛnyǔ nkwǎŋwaŋ achi.
Kɛ bɔ́ kɛbhɔ́ŋ mbi mbɔnyunɛ́ bo mankɛm bábhɔ̌ŋ nyaka ɛkwak bɛ́ghok mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn Yesu árɛ̀m.
nɛ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt achak amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm yɔ́ ɛ́pɛ́t ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Bě mankɛm abhɛ́n bápú bo Israɛl, bɨ̌tí nɔ́kɔ́ ka Acha. Bo mankɛm, bɨ̌tí nɔ́kɔ́ ká yi.”
Mandɛm mmu árɨ́ŋɨ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ abhɨ́kɨ́ ka bɛ́ bǒ mmɨk mánsɔ́t chí ndyɛrɛ kɛboŋ ɛkap mándɨ́ŋɨ́ yí. Yí arɛm bɛ́ ǎpɛmɛ chí bǒ abhɛn mánóko Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ́ bhɛsɛ́ sɛ́ghàti bhɔ, yɛ̌ndu mbɔk bho básɔ̀t Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ chí mbɔ ɛchɨŋti.
Bě bo Kɔrint, sɛ́ghati bhe yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ kpoŋoroŋ nɛ sɛ́nɛnɛ batɨ yɛsɛ ntá yɛka.
Ɛ́chí tɛtɛp bɛ́ nɛyɨŋɨ anɛ mbɔk ɛyap báyɨ̀ŋɨ mɛ nɛ amɨ́k abʉ́abʉ nɛ nɛyɛnti bɔ́ báyɛ̀nti mmʉɛt nɛ mɛ kɛ̌ ákʉ́ bɔ́ bághàti Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Kristo, kɛ mbɔk báchi abhɛn bághàti Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ nɛ ɛrɨ́tí nkaysi.
Yesu afa are rɔ́ŋ Kapɛ̌naum. Ágháká nɔ́kɔ́ arɛ́, mmu amɔt anɛ áchí mǔnti ɛká batɛmɛ́ nɛnu Rom bɛsa bɛtay arɔk ntá Yesu, abho mɛnɨkmʉɛt ntá yi,
Mpok babhɔŋɔ bɛ́chwe ɛtɔk Kánǎn akʉ mánáŋa manɛrɛ́kɛt bo tándrámɔt anɛ achi arɛ, achyɛ bo Israɛl mmɨk Kánǎn.
Ɛ́tɔŋ yɛ bɛ mbák mmu átwɔ̌ ntá yɛka anɛ átɔ̀ŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛpu ndɔ́ŋ amɔt nɛ ɛbhɛn Kristo átɔ́ŋɔ́, yɛ̌ mmu ywɛka ákɛ́ syɛpti mmǔ wu amɛm ɛkɛt ɛyi. Yɛ̌ chí bɛkaka yi bǎkɛ́ kaka.
Agú bɛ́kʉ bɔ mámbák pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí Mandɛm ndu ásó bhɔ nɛ manyiɛp nɛ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm.
Sɛ́kɔŋ be tontó, kpát ɛ́kʉ́ sɛ́ká bɛ sɛbhɔŋ bɛchyɛ be, puyɛ̌ chí ndiɛrɛ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm, kɛ yɛ chi mmʉɛt ɛyɛsɛ nkwɔ ndǔ bǎchí bhɛsɛ antɨ tontó.
Ɛkʉ bare byak yi byak. Yesu aghati yɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Bo báchyɛ̀ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm kɛnókó yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak. Ndiɛrɛ ɛtɔk ɛyi, nɛ ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt ywi, kɛ bápú chyɛ yi kɛnókó.”
Bo abhɛn basyɛphɛ bhɔ bápú bhʉɛrɛ mbɔŋ bɛbhé mɛnkɛm. Kɛ báyàŋ bɛsyɛp bhe bɛ mámpányu bɛ́ bǎchi bakoŋo bhap.
Mbák sɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ sɛ́bhɔŋ nɛbharɛ́mʉɛt nɛ Mandɛm, kɛ sɛ́nkɔ nɔkɔ amɛm ɛjuri, nɔ sɛ́sè chi nsé, nɛ sɛpu koŋo tɛtɛp anɛ Mandɛm ákʉ́ sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́.
Tɛ́mté wu, bɔPíta báyɨ́ŋɨ, kɛ bákɛpɛrɛ ghɔ́ yɛ̌ mmu, ɛbhiki fʉɛt chi Yesu aywǐnti.
Hɛ́rɔd arɛm nɛ mmʉɛt yi bɛ, “Nchyɛ́ nyaka ɛyɔŋ nɛ bákpɔ́t ntí Jɔ̌n. Kɛ mmǔ anɛ mɛ̌ghòk nɛ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛbhɛn ɛ̌ti yi chí agha?” Are yáŋ mbi bɛghɔ Yesu. 
Nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ mɛnyɨŋ nkáp bɛ́jwi amɛm mɔ́kɛrɛ nkáp, nɔ́ kɛ̌ nkaysi ndɨ́ndɨ́ ájwì antɨ mmu ndɨ́ndɨ́, nɛ bɛrɨ kɛ bɛ́fu arɛ.
Ngɔ́ yɛ bɛ mfay anɛ́nɛ́. Ngɔ́ mpɔŋɔndɨ́k anɛ pɛ́pɛ́p arɛ. Mmǔ anɛ ákɔ̀ yɔ aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Mbʉɛrɛ baryɛp nɛ Anɛ Tɛtɛp. Áchyɛ̀ bo ntɛmsi ɛnyu ɛnɛ ɛchi chak. Nɛ ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ yi ánù nɛ bǒmpap abhi.
Mandɛm arɛm nyaka chi ɛ̌ti mmu achák, anɛ yi ákʉ́ ápɛ́rɛ́nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m anɛ mmʉɛt ayi abhɨkɨ pɔɔ.
Ghatí bhɔ́ ɛnyu yɔ́ mbɔnyunɛ ndǔ mpok anɛ áfúɛ́rɛ́ ansɛm, bɛsɛ babhɔŋ sɛ́chí nyaka amɨ́k nɛ́mɛ́ nɛ́mɛ́ ndǔ baraka Mandɛm. Sɛ́tàŋ nyaka ntí. Nɛ bo bárwɔ̀ nyaka bhɛsɛ sɛ́nkʉ́ nɔkɔ bɛbʉ́. Sɛ́bhák ndǔ kɛsɛmɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mmʉɛt ɛyɛsɛ ɛ́nŋwaka bɛ́ sɛ́nkʉ. Sɛ́kaysi nyaka bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ bɛ́chyɛ̀ bhɛsɛ maŋák. Sɛ́kʉ̀ nyaka bɛbʉ́ nɛ sɛ́bhɔ́ŋ mpap amɨ́k. Bo bápàp nyaka bhɛsɛ, bɛsɛ́ nkwɔ sɛ́mpap nɔkɔ batɨ.
Chɔŋ mɛmbɔŋ ntɔŋ yí ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnkɛm ɛnɛ́ yí ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛghɔ ɛ̌ti ya.”
Mbɔ̌ŋ Debhít asɨ̌ŋ amɛm Ɛkáti Bakway bɛ: ‘Mandɛm Acha arɛm nyaka ntá Acha wa bɛ, chɔkɔ fá ɛbhě awɔ́nɛm ɛya ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ-kɛnókó,
Árɨ́ŋɨ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́ Yesu afǔ atú ɛtɔk ɛnɛ Hɛ́rɔd achi mfɔ arɛ́, achyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ mandɔk nɛ yi ntá Hɛ́rɔd. Mbɔŋ Hɛ́rɔd achi nyaka Yerúsalɛm mpok yɔ.
Mbák mǎnáŋ básyɛp nyaka mmu kɛ Mandɛm ǎbhɨŋɨ yí, ákɛ́ nu bɛbhak mbɔ mmu anɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ syɛp yí. Nɛ mbák mmu achí anɛ Mandɛm ábhɨ́ŋɨ́ yí ɛnɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ re syɛp yí, ákɛ́ nu bɛ́ mánsíɛ́p yí bɛkoŋo ɛpɨŋ ɛnɛ bo Israɛl.
Ayibhiri mmʉɛt ayɨŋɨ bo abhɛn báchɔkɔ bákábhɛ yi arɛm bɛ, “Máya chi bǒbhɛn, nɛ bɔ̌maya chi bǒbhɛn,
Árɛ́mɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, aghati bhɔ́ bɛ́ mángúrɛ́. Ɛchɛm ɛ́táka.
Ngɔ́ yɛ ángɛl achák ndǔ áfú atú anɛ mmok áfù anko nɔkɔ amfay. Akɛ́m ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ básɔ̀t bɛfyɛ bɛrɨŋ amʉɛt bo Mandɛm mmu achi nɛpɛ́m. Ángɛl wu asáy abhɨŋɨ bɔángɛl manwi abhɛn Mandɛm achyɛ bɛtaŋ bɛ mánchɔŋti mmɨk nɛ bɔmanyu.
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Ndɛm mɛnyɨŋ kpoŋoroŋ ntá bo mankɛm. Ntɔ́ŋ bo amɛm bɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt nɛ amɛm ɛkɛrákap mpoknkɛm ndǔ mbaŋ ɛnɛ bo Israɛl báchɛ̀m arɛ. Mbɨ́kɨ́ rɛm yɛ̌nyɨŋ bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́.”
Ɛyɔŋ, ɛ́yíbhiri nkwǎ, atwɔ́ achɔkɔ nɛ bhɛsɛ. Sɛ́ghɔ́ mɛnwɔp ɛbhi ɛbhɛn bɛjwi nɛ bɛrɨ̌ndu nɛ tɛtɛp. Ɛyɔŋ chi Njaŋamɔ anɛ áfú ntá Ɛta.
Mǔnti ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́ Yesu akʉ mɔ́ngɔrɛ́ wu ataŋ ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt ɛnap, abé ntɨ, abho bɛrɛm nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ ntá bo abhɛn bachi arɛ bɛ, “Sɛ́bhɔŋ manywɔp átándat ndǔ bɛ́kʉ bɛtɨk. Mmu ámbɔ́ŋ nɛme, ántwɔ́ chí amɛm manywɔp ayɔ bɛ mámbú yi. Ɛ́kɛ́pɛrɛ bhak chi ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt.”
Sɛ́nsɔt ndaká nɛnyiɛ mɛnyiɛ. Mmǔ amɔt ǎkway mɛnoko bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́rɨ mɛnyiɛ. Achák anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ sɛnɛ ndǔ baraká Mandɛm andɛm bɛ yí ǎnyiɛ chi nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn bákwáŋá.
Nɛ mbák bábhɨkɨ syɛpti bhe ndǔ yɛ̌ ɛkɛt nɛ yɛ̌ chi ɛtɔk, kwɛt ka mfok anɛ áchí bhe bɛkak, mǎmfa arɛ.
Ángɛl anɛ ajwi bapay apɨkɨri ɛyǐ ɛkwɔp amɛm manyu. Manyu ayibhiri arɔp mbɔ manoŋ amɛn ngú, nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi nɛpɛ́m amɛm manyu ɛ́gú.
Mbɔk baghɔ bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ̀m ɛchi tɛtɛp, kɛ báchák kɛnókó.
Mpú yáŋ nɔ chi kɛnókó ntá nkwǎ.
Chɔŋ mǎnyiɛ nɛ mǎnyú nɛ mɛ nɛbhʉɛt amɔt ndǔ ɛpǎ kɛfɔ ɛya, nɛ mǎnchɔkɔ nkwɔ ndǔ mɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ ndu bɛkɛm manɛrɛ́kɛt Israɛl byo nɛ apay.” 
Yesu arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Ɔbhɛ́ yɛ̌ chí nɛwú ɔká bɛ́gu ɛ̌ti ya? Tɛtɛ̌tɛp, nkɔk apɛrɛ́ kok nkúbhɛ́ bɛti ɛbhɛn, chɔŋ ɔ́ndɛm ndɔŋ ɛ́rát bɛ ɔbhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ mɛ.”
Apú bhak mbɔ mmu anɛ ánù bɛ bo mángók yi. Apú bhak mbɔ mmu anɛ bághok ɛyɔŋ ɛyi nɛfí.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka ánú bɛbhak kpák nɛ bo mankɛm, anu bɛbhak nyáŋá bɛsí Mandɛm, mbɔnyunɛ mmu anɛ apu nyáŋá apú kway bɛghɔ Acha.
Arɔk ɛtɔkɔ́ bawú, abhak ndǔ bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri arɛ́. Áyóŋ nɔ́kɔ́ amɨ́k amfay, aghɔ́ Ábraham nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ nɛ Lásárɔs abhak yí nɛpaká mmʉɛt.
Kɛ ángɛl arɛm ntá ya bɛ, “Ndaká yí ɔchí maknkay tontó? Chɔŋ ngati wɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ ɛ̌ti ngɔrɛ́ nɛ nɛ nnya mbʉ́mbʉ anɛ bati tándrámɔt anɛ apɔkɔ yi nɛ babhaŋ byo.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Puyɛ̌ chi bɛ́ mmǔ-nɛ akʉ bɛbʉ́, nɛ puyɛ̌ chí bɛ ɛtayi nɛ máyi bakʉ bɛbʉ́. Amɨ́k ánɛmɛ yi chi bɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́nkwak bo mángɔ ɛnyǔ ɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛnɛ Mandɛm aywǐnti ákway bɛkʉ.
Kristo akʉ sɛ́bhɔŋ mbi bɛbhak ɛnyu ɛnɛ bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm bɛbhak nɛ bhɛsɛ bɛfʉɛt ndu nɛka ɛnɛn sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ yi. Nɛ sɛbhɔŋ maŋák mbɔnyunɛ sɛbhaka ntɨ ndǔ kɛnɛ́m ɛkɛn sɛ́bhɔŋ chɔŋ nɛ Mandɛm.
chɔŋ Mandɛm anchyɛ yi bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ fá amɨk, nɛ chɔŋ ampɛt ambɔ́ŋ bɛkɛt, bɔ̌nnɔ abhɛn babhakanɛm nɛ abhɛn baghɔrɛ́, nɛ mánɔ́, nɛ bɔ, nɛ bakɨ, ndɔŋ bɛsa bɛtay. Chɔŋ bo mánchyɛ yi bɛyǎ nɛnyok, kɛ ndǔ mmɨk nkɔ Mandɛm anchyɛ yi nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛ́n nɛbhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ngwɛ́nti.
Yɛ̌ ángɛl apú anɛ Mandɛm ághátí yi bɛ, “Wɔ, ɔchí Mɔ́wa, nɛ ɛchɔŋ nchí rɛm bɛ ndɔp Ɛtayɛ.” Nɛ yɛ̌ chí bɛ́rɛ́m bɛ, “Chɔŋ mbak Ɛtayi nɛ ɔ́mbak Mɔ́wa”, abhɨ́kɨ́ rɛm ntá bɔángɛl.
Yɛ̌ bǎbhɔ́ŋ chí bɛyǎ bo báchák abhɛn bátɔ̀ŋ be mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti Kristo, bǎbhɔŋ chí chi amɔt. Bǎbhɔŋ chí chi amɔt mbɔnyunɛ be bho bǎbhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Kristo nɛ́nɛ, mɛ kɛ̌ ntwɔ́ ngátí nyaka bhé Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ kɛ mǎnókó.
Atwɔ́ ɛnyu ɛyɔ bɛkʉ bo abhɛn bachi nyaka antɛnɛ́ bɛbhé, bɛ Mandɛm ansɔt bɛsɛ mbɔ bɔ̌bhi.
Anɛ ɛbhǎ nkáp atwɔ́ nkwɔ arɛm bɛ, ‘Ɛta, ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ ɔchí mmu mbeápak. Ɔkɔŋ bɛghɛm nɛbhʉɛt anɛ ɔ́bhɨ́kɨ́ pɨ, ɔ̌nyokoti nɛbhʉɛt anɛ ɔ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tak mbwɔt arɛ.’
Ná ɛ́chí bɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛsɛ ǎghòk ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bɔ́ bárɛ̀m ndǔ ɛyi ɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk?
Fɛstɔs arɔk Seséria bɛ́bhó bɛtɨk mbɔ gɔ́bhanɔ atú Judéya. Ɛfʉɛrɛ nɔkɔ manywɔp arat, afa akó Yerúsalɛm.
Nɛyí nɔ́kɔ́ mpok Yesu nɛ bɔ Píta básɛ́bhɛ́ njiɛ, bɛyǎ bho bárɔk batɛmɛri Yesu.
Mpók anɛ Hɛ́rɔd achí mfɔ atú Judɛ́ya, nchiakap Mandɛm abhak anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ́ Sakaría. Ǎkʉ̀ nyaka bɛtɨk Mandɛm nɛ nkwɔ bo abhɛn babhɨŋɨ bɛ Nkwɔ́ Abíja. Nnyɛ́n ngɔrɛ́ ywi nɛbhak bɛ Ɛlísabɛt. Yí nkwɔ afú ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt Arɔn, nnɛrɛ́kɛt bachiǎkap Mandɛm.
Awu áfʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, ngɔ́ Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n téé amfǎy njiɛ Síɔn. Bǒ nka bɛsa tándrámɔt nsɛm nka ɛnwi bábhak nɛ yi (,). Básɨ́ŋ nnyɛ́n Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n nɛ ɛnɛ́n Ɛtayi ndǔ nɛfó yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap.
Mpú rɛm nɔ́ chi bɛ nnáŋ ngaka ɛnyu mmu anɛ mɛ́yàŋ bɛbhak, nɛ mpú rɛm nɔ chi bɛ nnáŋ nsɛ́nɛ́ ndǔ mbi Mandɛm. Kɛ nchí nu ndɔk nɔkɔ chí ambɨ, bɛ́ ɛyɔ ɛ́nkwak mɛ mbak ɛnyu mmu Yesu Kristo áyàŋ nyaka bɛ mbak mpok yi ayabhɛ mɛ bɛ́ mbák mmǔ ywi.
Ɛchi mbɔ ɛnyǔ bárɛ́mɛ́ ɛ̌ti Kristo bɛ, “Wɔ, ɔchí nchiakap Mandɛm ngwɛnti ti mbɔ Mɛlkísɛdɛk.”
Píta nɛ Jɔ̌n mányáŋa amɔ́ antí bǒbhɛn manɨkmʉɛt, Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ atwɔ́ abhak nɛ bhɔ.
Nɛ ngɔrɛ́ anɛ, yɛ̌ ǎnɨ̀k chí mmʉɛt yɛ̌ ǎghati chí bho mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fú ntá Mandɛm, mbák ǎkʉ̀ nɔ kɛkuti ntí, nɔ́ apu chyɛ mǔnti ywi kɛnókó, nɛ achí ɛnyumɔt mbɔ ngɔrɛ́ anɛ ámú ntí.
Kɛ ndaká yí ɔ́bhɨ́kɨ́ fyɛ nkáp awa amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́nkap bɛ nnáŋ ntwɔ́, mbɔ̌ŋ nsáy arɛ?’
Kɛ bɔ̌bha, bǎchí bo Mandɛm, nɛ mǎnaŋ mǎnu nɛ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ nsé bǎsɔt awɔ́nɛm, mbɔnyunɛ mmǔ anɛ achi nɛ bhe ataŋ achá anɛ achi fá amɨk.
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, ngɔrɛ́ Sɛbɛdi asɔt bɔ̌bhi bati apay, arɔk ntá Yesu nɛ bhɔ. Atɛp mánɛ́n bɛsí bhi are bhɛ́p yi bɛ ankwak yi.
Mandɛm apú gú. Bɛchɔ́kɔ́ bhi bɛ́bhɔŋ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ ɛbhɛn mmu ápú kwáy bɛyɨŋɨ. Yɛ̌ mmu abhɨ́kɨ́ re ghɔ yi nɛ mmu apú kwáy bɛ́ghɔ yi. Kɛnókó kɛnkɛm kɛchi ɛki nɛ bɛtaŋá kɛfɔ bɛchi ɛbhi mpoknkɛm. *Amen.
Batɛmɛ́ nɛnu abhɛn bábhàbhɛri Yesu bábho bɛyɔkɔ yi nɛ mándɛnɛ nɔkɔ yi nɛ ɛ́kpá.
Sɛ́nɨ̀kmʉɛt nɛ batɨ yɛsɛ ankɛm bɛti nɛ ngósí bɛ́ Mandɛm ánkwak sɛmpɛt sɛngɔ bhe bɛsí nɛ bɛsi, nɛ sɛ́ntɔŋ be mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎbhɨ́kɨ́re rɨŋɨ, ndu bɛkwak mǎmbɔŋ nɛka nɛ Kristo mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɛ́yaŋ.
Ndǔ nnyɛ́n Yesu, sɛ́nchíɛ nɔ́kɔ́ Mandɛm bakak mbɔ aywɛsɛ akap. Akap wu chí nɛrɛm anɛ sɛ́rɛm nɛ manyu yɛsɛ bɛ yi kɛ achi Acha.
Ɛnɛ́ mányìɛ̀ nɛnyíɛ́, Yesu asɔt ɛkpɔkɔ́ brɛt, achyɛ bakak ntá Mandɛm. Abho bɛ́bɔ́kɔ́ti anchyɛ nɔkɔ ntá baghɔkɔ́ bhi, andɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Sɔt ka, nyiɛ́. Nɛ́ chi mmʉɛ́t ɛya.”
Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bákɔ́ baghaka ndǔ bɔ̌bɛtɔk Bɛtfágɛ nɛ Bɛ́tani, ndǔ Njiɛ Mɛnok Ólif, kɛkwɔt nɛ Yerúsalɛm. Aré, ató baghɔkɔ́ bhi bati apay ambɨ.
Bǎrɨŋɨ nkwɔ bɛ Mandɛm anáŋá nyaka bo Sódom nɛ Gomóra mpok yi átó ngo arɛ. Ásɔ́ŋ bhɔ krokotok, bɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́mbák mbɔ ɛrɨŋ ntá bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ mpok nɛ yi.
Ntɨ nywɔp, Yesu akʉ ntɨ bɛ́rɔŋ atú Gálili. Arɔk aghɔ́ mmu anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ Fílip. Aghati yi bɛ, “Twɔ́ bhák nkoŋo wa.”
Aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Dɔ́k ká ndǔ mɔ́tɔk anɛ achi afɔ ambɨ. Nɛchwe anɛ bǎchwe arɛ́, chɔŋ mǎngɔ mɔ́mpɔŋɔ batu sɛsɛ́t, anɛ yɛ̌ mmu abhɨkɨre kɔ nɛ yɔ́. Kaŋarí ká, twɔ́ nɛ yɔ́.
Chɔŋ sɛ́mpɛt sɛ́ndɛm ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛchak? Mbák Mandɛm achi nɛ bhɛsɛ, agha ákway mɛnu nɛ bhɛsɛ ansɔt awɔ́nɛm?
“Mpok bǎghɔ́ bakwɔ́ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu ndu bákábhɛ́ Yerúsalɛm, dɨŋɨ́ yɛ́ ka bɛ mpok bɛchɔŋti Yerúsalɛm akway.
“Ɛ́rɨ ɛcha ntá yɛka mpok bo básɔ̀kɔti bhe nɛ mpok anɛ báchyɛ̀ bhe ɛsɔŋɔri, mámbarɛ nɔkɔ bhe barak amʉɛt ndɛ́ndɛm ɛ̌ti ya.
Bɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn báchyɛ ntá bɔmandɛm nse, bɛsɛ́ mankɛm sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ mandɛm nsé apu yɛ̌nyɨŋ nɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ nɛpɛ́m. Mandɛm amɔt kɛ achi, achák ápú.
Mmu ǎbhák mmu Israɛl tɛtɛp chí ndǔ ntɨ ɛni nɛ nsyɛ́p anɛ tɛtɛp ǎbhak chí antɨ. Chí bɛtɨk Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm, puyɛ̌ ɛbhɛn nkwɔmʉɛt. Mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛnyǔ nsyɛp ɛyɔ Mandɛm kɛ ábɨti yi, puyɛ̌ nkwǎŋwaŋ.
Yesu arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Chɔŋ mǎntɛm mɛ nɛkay ɛnɛn ɛ̌ti ya bɛ, ‘Ngaŋ, bú mmʉɛt ɛyɛ. Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn sɛghoko bɛ ɔkʉ awu ɛtɔk Kapɛ̌naum, kʉ bhɔ́ fá amɛm ɛtɔk ɛyɛ nkwɔ.’”
arɔk yɛ asɛbhɛ Yesu amɨk, anɛ́p yi nɛ ɛsyɛ̌ndɛn, arɔk afyɛ́ amɛm nnɛm ɛnɛ́n bátɛ́mɛ́ ndǔ sɛtárɛ́bhɛ́, kɛ kɛre bhɛmɛ yɛ̌ mmu arɛ́.
Nkúbhɛ́ mmu anɛ áchyɛ́ Píta bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn ntá bo Israɛl, kɛ áchyɛ́ mɛ nkwɔ bɛtaŋ, bɛkʉ bɔ ntá abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl.
Ghatí bhɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bɛ́kɛ́ bhak nɛ bhɔ́.
Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fákárí nyaka nɛ bachǐmbɨ bhɛsɛ́ chí bɛ́ mɛ́nsɛ́mtí nɔ́kɔ́ bhɛsɛ bɛ sɛ́kɛ́ ŋwaka bɛkʉ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ mbɔ bɔ́.
Ghɔ́ ká batɨ ntínso, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Mandɛm ághɔ̀ bhe ntínso.” 
Ɔ́kɛ́ rɔ mmu ámbyak wɔ bɛ́ ɔchí mɔ́nkwɛn. Bák ɛrɨŋ ntá abhɛn mánoko Yesu, ndǔ ɛyɔŋɔ́nyu yɛ, nɛ ndǔ nɛkʉ ywɛ, nɛ ndǔ ɛkɔŋ ɛyɛ, nɛ ndǔ nɛka ɛnɛ nɛ Yesu, nɛ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛ ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ bakwap.
Mpok yɔ nɔ, bǒbati bachiǎkap nɛ bǒbati ɛtɔk báré ghati bɛyǎ bhó abhɛn báchí arɛ́ bɛ́ bákɛ́ rɔ bɛbhɛp Páílet ándɔ́ chí Barábas ándɔ́k, anchyɛ bɛtaŋ bɛ mángwáy Yesu.
Ndiɛrɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mɔt kɛ nchí ghati bhe. Tě ká kpirí ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mǎnókó kpátɛ mɛ̌mpɛtnsɛm.
Ɛ́chí ɛnyumɔt nɛ bhe. Mbák mǎndɛm ɛnyɨŋ ndǔ ɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛnɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ, bo bápú kway bɛjwimɛm. Ná bɔ bákway yɛ bɛrɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bárɛ̀m? Ɛ́bhak ntá yap chi mbɔ bɛ bǎrɛ̀m kɛpɨ nɛ mbʉ́ɛ́p, nɛ́ ɛ́pú bhɔŋ ntí.
Kɛnókó kɛ́mbák nɛ Mandɛm mmu áchí Ɛ́táyɛsɛ́ mpoknkɛm. Amen. 
Moses aghátí nyaka bhe bɛ mǎnsyɛ́bhɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bɔ̌bhɛka. Yɛ̌ nɔ, ɛbhé yɔ ɛbhɨkɨ fu nyaka ntá Moses. Ɛ́fú chí ntá bachǐmbɨ abhɛka. Nɛ bǎsìɛp mmu ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt.
Yesu áfú amɛm áchwí, akó ɛbhɨ. Aghɔ́ bɛyǎ bho, ntínso nɛ́kɛ́m yi nɛ bhɔ́. Abú abhɛn mámè.
Bǒnto Yesu nɛ bǒbatí bapɛt bachɔkɔ bɛyɨŋɨ ndaka wu.
Ɛnɛ́ nchí Yerúsalɛm ndu batí barak ayɔ ápáy kɛ̌ bághɔ́ mɛ amɛm ɛkɛrákap. Bághɔ́ mɛ ndǔ nchí naŋa bɛkʉ mbɔ ɛnyu ɛbhé Moses ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ́ mmu ankʉ bɛso bɛsí nɛ Mandɛm. Ɛká bho ɛ́pú nyaka arɛ nɛ mɛ, nɛ yɛ̌ chi ɛbyɔk.
Bɔ́ mankɛm báré nyiɛ́ nkúbhɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́ maknkay ɛnɛ́n nɛ́fù ntá Mandɛm.
Babhabhɛrǐ nnɛm báré wɛt nɛ bɛcháy nɛ bárɔp mbɔ bawú.
Píta arɔk ambɨ bɛ́rɛm baya mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́chák ansɛmti nɔkɔ bhɔ bɛ́ “Fɛrɛ́ ká mmʉɛt ndǔ ntɛmsi anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́twɔ ntá bǒ bɛbʉ́ abhɛn fá ammɨk.”
Chɔŋ ɛndɨ ɛncha ntá mǔbɛtok wu anɛ chi-bɛtɨk ywi átwɔ antɛmɛri yi ndu ákʉ̀ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ baghati yi ankʉ!
Báre ghɔ nɛ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ Mandɛm nɛ mándɛm nɔkɔ kɛpɨ nɛ Yesu ɛ̌ti nɛrɔŋ anɛ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛrɔŋ Yerúsalɛm angu arɛ.
Bábhak maknkay mbɔnyunɛ bághók ndu bobhɔ́ bárɛ̀m bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk bɛ́chák bɛ́chák ɛbhɛ́n bɔ́ bábhɨkɨ ghɔ́k, mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Mandɛm ataŋ nɛ arɨ achá!” Ɛ́kʉ Píta arɛm bɛ́,
Nɛpɛ́m nɛ́fù chí ntá yi mmu bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ Ɛyɔŋ. Nɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛ́bhak ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́kʉ̀ bo mángɔ́ tɛtɛp.
Mmu abhɔŋ yɛ bɛsɛpti mmʉɛt ntá bǒbati. Nɛ mmu ákɛ́ kʉ nɔ chi ndu áchày bɛ Mandɛm akɛ kʉ bo mántɛmsi yi. Ntí achak achi bɛ ntɨ̌ mmu nɛ́ghàti yi bɛ ɛrɨ bɛkʉ nɔ.
Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ nkárɛ́nká byo nɛ ɛpay nɛ ngósí, ɛjuri ɛ́kwɛ́n ɛtɔk ɛnkɛm. Ɛ́bhák kpátɛ nkárɛ́nká ɛ́rát nɛ ngósí.
Tɛ̌ndu mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm bɛbhɔŋɔ chɔŋ bɛsayri, mɛ́nɛmsi ɛnyu ɛyɔ, ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ rɨ nɔ bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ ywɛka ámbʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ nɛpɛ́m ɛni pɛ́pɛ́p, ambak mbɔ ɛnyǔ mmu Mandɛm ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛbhaka?
Mandɛm mmu mɛ̌kʉ̀ bɛtɨk ɛbhi nɛ ntɨ ɛna nɛnkɛm ndu nchí ghati bo Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Mɔ́ywi achi ntísiɛ wa bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ mɛ̌nɨ̀kmʉɛt, mpú rɔ bɛfyɛ bhe ndǔ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt ɛnɛ.
Kɛ Mandɛm Mpɛmɛ ywɛsɛ́ átɔ́ŋ nɔkɔ bhɛsɛ́ bɛrɨ̌ntɨ ɛbhi nɛ ɛkɔŋ ɛyi,
Bákáŋári yɛ bɔángɛl manwi bhɔ bɛ́ mámfá mándɔ́k mángwáy mmǔ amɔt ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ bo bati arat. Bábhʉrɛ nyaka bɔ arɛ́ mɛnoŋ nɛŋɔkɔ́ nywɔp ɛnɔ, ndǔ nkúbhɛ́ nywɔp ɛnɔ, ndǔ ntaŋ wu, nɛ ndǔ mmíɛ́ ɛnɔ.
Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ abhak nɛ Sakaría, chi Jɔ̌n. Abho bɛ́rɛm kɛpɨ̌ntɨ bɛ,
Awu áfʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, báchyɛ mɛ ɛnɔkɔ́ njɛnti nɛ bághati mɛ bɛ, “Dɔ́k yɛnti ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm, ɔ́njɛnti ɛfɛmɛ-akap, ɔ́mpay bo abhɛn báchyɛ̀ Mandɛm kɛnókó arɛ.
Mbák ákɔ́rɛ́ ánkwɛ́n ɛtɔk, bo mánu nɔkɔ nɛ batɨ, ɛtɔk ɛyɔ ɛ́pú te.
Mpok mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ ndɛn, bǎchyɛ́ mɛ ndɛn; mpok mɛ̌me, bǎkókóri mɛ; mpok nchí ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ, bǎré twɔ bɛghɔ mɛ.’
Kɛ ɛ̌ti bo Israɛl, Mandɛm arɛm bɛ, “Nywɔp nɛnkɛm, nsá amɔ, nnɨ́k nɔkɔ mmʉɛt bɛ mámpɛtnsɛm ntá ya, kɛ bɔ bátɔ̀ŋ chi nɛtaŋántɨ. Bǒbhɛn bákʉ̀ chi ɛyap ɛnyu.”
Ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ ɛchi bɛ Mandɛm ayap nyaka mǔbɛtok ywi, ayambɨ átó yi chi ntá yɛka bɛ́ ánjɛ́t be ndǔ ákʉ̀ be mandɔ́ nɛpɛ́m bɛbʉ́ ɛnɛka.”
Ɛ́rɔ́bhɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ kɛ́kwɔ́t bɛ Jɔ̌n ánaŋa bɛtɨk ɛbhi, abhɛ́p bo bɛ, ‘Bǎkáysí bɛ́ mɛ kɛ nchí Mpɛmɛ anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́twɔ kɛ? Chao! Puyɛ̌ mɛ! Ghók ka, yí átwɔ̀ mɛ ansɛm, nɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ kway mbɔ̌ŋ mmu anɛ áchoti, bɛfɛrɛ nkwɔbhánya bɛkak ɛbhi.’”
Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ mbɔ nkárɛ́nká byo nɛ ɛpay, nɛ nkarɛnka ɛ́rát ɛnɛ ngósí, mbɔŋɔ́nkɨ wu akʉ ɛnyumɔt. Nɔ́ chí, asɔt bǒ bɛtɨk bachak ató ɛbhɨ.
Tɛ́mté wu, Yesu arɨŋɨ nkaysi yap, abhɛp bhɔ bɛ, “Ndaká yí bǎkàysi mɛnyǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ?
Ɛ́rɨ ɛchá ntá mmu anɛ ápú rɔ bɛ́sɨ́kɨ ntɨ nɛ Yesu Kristo ndǔ átè kpirí mpok bɛsɔŋɔri bɛ́twɔ̀ ntá yi. Ɛrɨ ntá yi mbɔnyunɛ ǎnu kpát ansɔt awɔ́nɛm, Mandɛm anchyɛ yí akap anɛ́ yi afyɛ́ bariɛp bɛ́chyɛ́ bǒ abhɛn bákɔ́ŋ yi, nɔ chi, nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.
Bě bǎbhɔŋ bǎrɨŋɨ ɛnyǔ bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhɛn Yesu Kristo Acha átɔ́ŋɔ́ bhɛsɛ. Yɛ̌ndu yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ, ayibhiri arɔp nchɛ́bhɛ́ mmu ɛ̌ti yɛka bɛ kɛchɛp ɛki kɛ́nkʉ mǎmbák bo abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ bɛsí Mandɛm.
Bɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ bɛbhé Moses, bɛchi mbɔ ndɨ́kándi bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛbhɔŋɔ bɛ́twɔ, puyɛ̌ mbɔŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ. Ɛnyu ɛsɨ́ ɛnɛ ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ mánchyɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ akap ndɔŋ nɛ ndɔŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmíɛ́ ɛ́pú kway nyaka bɛkʉ bo abhɛn bátwɔ ntá Mandɛm ndu bɛchyɛ yi kɛnókó mánkwáy bɛsí bhi ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbi wáwák.
Mandɛm kɛ̌ ághókó tákɔ nɛ bɛrɨ ɛbhi, tákɔ anɛ ákway bɛbhak ɛchɔŋ, mbúrɛ́ angwɔsi, mámfyɛ́ angó. Bǎkáysí bɛ́ be kɛ̌ Mandɛm apu kwáy bɛ́kwák mǎmbɔ́ŋ ndɛn bɛ́fyɛ́ amʉɛt kɛ? Nɛka ɛnɛká nɛ Mandɛm nɛ́gʉ́psi nɛcha!
Nchí rɛm nɔ mbɔnyunɛ, bɛyǎ bo bátɔ̀ŋ nɛtaŋántɨ, sayri sayri mbɔk bo Israɛl abhɛn mánóko mbok Yesu Kristo. Bárɛ̀m mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ntí nɛ nnɛt nɛ bárwɔ̀ bo bɛ mánókó kɛ́mbwɔ́bhɛ́ kap.
“Sɔt ka mpok nɛ bǒ-nsé abhɛn bárɛ̀m bɛ báchí barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm. Bákɔ̀t ngɛpti bɛ báchí bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n, kɛ sayri sayri, báchí chí nkwɔ ɛnɛ nsay ánu yɔ.
Yesu aghɔ nɔkɔ bɛ ntɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm anɛ akɛmɛ yi sayri nɛ kɛboŋ, arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Ɛ́rɔp wɔ chí mandú bɛ́rɔ Mandɛm ambak nɛ wɔ mbɔnyu Mfɔ ábhàk nɛ mmu anɛ áchí antɛn ɛyi.” Bɛbho mpok ɛyɔ, yɛ̌ mmu kɛpɛrɛ mɔ bɛbhɛp yi yɛ̌nyɨŋ. 
Mbák bǎchyɛ̀ bo báchák nɛnyíɛ́, pú bɛsɛ́ sɛ́bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ bɛ́bhɛp be mɛnyɨŋ ɛ́cha bo bachak abhɔ? Yɛ̌ nɔ, sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɛp be mɛnyɨŋ mbɔ ɛnyu sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛbhɛp. Sɛ́ká yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ ɛsɔŋɔri. Ɛyɔ ɛ́rɨ ntá yɛsɛ́ ɛ́chá bɛ́kʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́kwày bɛchɛt be mbi bɛyɨŋɨ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ Kristo.
Kɛ ná nɛ be? Mandɛm arɨ́ŋɨ́ yɛ̌ chí mpǎy bɛkaká ɛmɛnɛ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chí yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka anti. Bǎkɛ́ chay yɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bo bakway bɛkʉ bhe. Bɛsí Mandɛm, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka abhɔŋ mɛnwɔp tontó achá ngɛ́mtáy kɛnɛn. 
Bɛkʉ ɛnyu ɛyɔ, ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ bǎchi ɛnyumɔt mbɔ bachǐmbɨ bhɛka abhɛn báwáy nyaka barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm ndǔ bǎtè bɛrɨ́ti manɛm ntá yap.
Anɛ ákòŋo asɔt kɛ́nkwɛ́sɛ́ wu ndǔ nɛbhay. Yí nkwɔ agú kɛrɔ mmɔ. Ɛ́fákári ɛnyumɔ́t nɛ anɛ ajwi bati arat.
Mmʉɛt mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi amfǎy ɛ́chí kɛkúrí nɛ mmʉɛt mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi fá amɨk. Nɛ bɛrɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn amfay bɛ́chí kɛkúrí nɛ bɛrɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn fá amɨk.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛghati baghɔkɔ́ bhi bɛ, “Mandu mpok, bǎpú pɛrɛ ghɔ mɛ. Kɛ mandú mpok, chɔŋ mǎmpɛt mǎngɔ mɛ.”
Yesu asɔt mɔ́mpɔŋɔ batu, achɔkɔ yɔ́ ansɛm nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyu básɨŋɨ amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm bɛ,
Sɛ́nɨ̀kmʉɛt ɛnyu ɛyɔ bɛ yi ankʉ batɨ ántáŋ be amɛm nɛ bɛ́ bǎkɛ́ bhɔŋ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́, nɛ bɛ́ mǎmbák nyáŋá bɛsí Mandɛm Ɛtayɛsɛ, kɛ mpok anɛ Yesu Kristo Acha átwɔ̀ nɛ bo Mandɛm ankway.
Mbɔŋ Yesu Acha mmu áchyɛ̀ kpák ánchyɛ be kpák ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbi mpoknkɛm. Yesu Acha ámbák nɛ bhe mankɛm.
Kɛ fyɛ́ ká nti ndǔ bɛbhɔŋ akap anɛ acha achak. Nɛ́nɛ, chɔ́ŋ ntɔŋ be mbi anɛ árɨ́ áchá áchák ankɛm, bɛ mǎnkoŋo chí wu.
Áchɔ́ŋtí nɔ́kɔ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ, ɛrɛmɛ́ nsay ɛ́kwɛ́n ɛtɔk ɛyɔ ɛnkɛm, arɔp amɔ apay.
Nɛ ndu bɛrɔŋ ambɨ, yi kɛ bakwɔ́ bho Kristo mbankɛm báyábhɛ́ bɛ́ ankɔ nɔkɔ nɛ bhɛsɛ ndǔ bɛtɨkɨ́ bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhɛn sɛ́kʉ̀. Sɛ́kʉ̀ bhɔ ndu nkwɔ ɛnyu ɛyɔ bɛ́ sɛ́nchyɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó nɛ bɛ́tɔŋ bɛ sɛbhɔŋ ntɨ bɛ́kwak bho.
Kɛ akɛmɛ mɛ bɛ, “Bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbha bɛ́kway nɛ wɔ mbɔnyunɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbha bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ kpoŋoroŋ chi amʉɛt bo abhɛn mmʉɛt apú bhɔ.” Ndu ɛchi yɛ̌ nɔ, chɔŋ ndɔk ambɨ bɛdɛp awɔ́ antɨ nɛ maŋák ɛ̌ti mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ, bɛ bɛtaŋ Kristo mɛ́mbak nɛ mɛ.
arɛm bɛ, “Acha, ghɔ́ ntínso nɛ mɔ́wa. Ǎkwɛn ntímɛn, nɛ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛ́nɛ́ yí ábhɔ̀ŋ ɛya ɛcha. Bɛyǎ mpok, ǎkwɛn angó, ndɔŋ ɛchak, ǎkwɛn anyɛ́n.
Nchí rɔ kpák ámbák nɛ bhe. Nchí chyɛ bhe kpák anɛ áfù ntá ya. Puyɛ̌ ɛnyǔ mmɨk áchyɛ̀ bho kpák kɛ̌ mɛ̌chyɛ. Bǎkɛ rɔ batɨ ánsɔ́ŋɔ́rí bhe amɛm, nɛ bǎkɛ rɔ bɛcháy mɛ́mbak amɛm batɨ yɛka.
Nɛ mmǔfu ághátí nɔ́kɔ́ mɛ ansɛm ansɛm bɛ́ bo Israɛl báte ɛyu bɛway yi, tɛ́mté wu ndɛm bɛ́ mbɔŋ bɛto yi ntá yɛ. Ngátí bo abhɛn bábhárɛ́ yí ndak amʉɛt bɛ mántwɔ́ ntá yɛ mangati wɔ ndak anɛ yi ákʉ́.”
“Nu ka bɛ́fʉɛ́t ndǔ nyǔbhá anɛ áchí mábhɛ́rí. Nchí ghati bhe bɛ bɛyǎ bho báyàŋ chɔŋ bɛfʉɛt manchwe kɛ bápú bhɔŋ mbi.
Bákɔ, bárɔk, báchwɔp ɛkɛt Jáyrɔs. Yesu aghɔ́ ɛbyɔk ɛnɛ ɛchi arɛ́ ndǔ bo bádì, mámbɨk nɔkɔ.
Kʉ nɔ, mbɔnyunɛ nɛghɔkɔsǐ mmʉɛt ɛnɛ́n nkwɔmʉɛt nɛ́chyɛ̀ mmu mandu nsáy, kɛ bɛghɔkɔsǐ mmʉɛt ndu bɛ́kʉ̀ mmu ámbák anɛ ákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áyàŋ, ǎchyɛ̀ mmu nsáy ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbi. Ɛchí ɛnyu yɔ mbɔnyunɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɔ nɛ́bhɔŋ bariɛp amɛm nsáy ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn fá amɨk nɛ ɛnɛ́n nɛ́twɔ̀ ambɨ.
Mǔngo batɛmɛ́ nɛnu abhɨŋɨ yɛ bǒ batí batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bhi bapay aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Sɔt ka batɛmɛ́ nɛnu batí bɛsa byo, bǒ batí bɛsa bɛ́rát nsɛm byo abhɛn bákɔ̀ nɛ mpɔŋɔ́ndɨ́k, nɛ batɛmɛ́ bakɔŋ bɛsa byó. Toŋtí ká mmʉɛt bɛ́sɔt Pɔ̌l ndu nkarɛnka nɛ́nɛnamɔt beti ɛbhɛn ɛchɔŋ, mǎndɔ́k Seséria nɛ yi.
Foŋorí yɛ́ ka yi, mǎnchyɛ yi nɛpɔptǐntɨ́ bɛ mɛnyɨŋ bɛkɛ taŋ mɛncha yi ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ yi ákpɨkɨ fɛrɛ amɔ.
Nɛ ntá bo abhɛn báfyɛ mmɛ́m ndǔ bɛbhǎ nkwɔbhanya, bápú fyɛ mmɛ̌m bakɔ amɛm ɛbhǎ nkwɔbhɛnya ɛnɛ ɛsɨ. Mbák mánkʉ́ nɔ, ɛbha ɛ́sɛn, ɛnchɔŋɔ, nɛ mmɛm andɔk amɨk. Báfyɛ mmɛm bakɔ chi ndǔ ɛbhǎ nkwɔbhɛnya ɛnɛ ɛkɔ. Mbák mánkʉ nɔ, mmɛm ápú rɔŋ amɨk nɛ ɛbha ɛpu sɛn ɛnchɔŋɔ.” 
Kɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Yi akó amfay”, ɛghati bhɛsɛ bɛ yi? Ɛyɔ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bhɛsɛ bɛ anáŋá asɛp nyaka ndǔ ɛtɔkɔ́ bawú.
Chɔŋ antɛsɛ bɔ́ babhɛsɛ mankɛm amɨ́k, nɛwú kɛpɛrɛ bhák. Nɛdǐ kɛbhɔ nɛ bawú bɛ́di kɛpɛrɛ bhák, nɛ bo kɛpɛrɛ ghok bɛbe mbɔnyunɛ mɛnyɨŋ bɛsɨ́ bɛ́rɔŋ.”
Ansɛm mpok, Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi báfá báre rɔŋ ɛtɔk Naín. Ngɛ́mtay bo báre rɔŋ nɛ bhɔ́.
Ndǔ ndɔŋ anɛ ájwí ɛ́rát Páílet arɛm bɛ, “Ntɨkɨ ɛbɛ́ptí ndak yi ákʉ́? Mbɨ́kɨ́ ghɔ́ yɛ̌ ɛ́bɛ́ptí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ákʉ́ ɛnɛ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ́ mángwáy yi. Chɔŋ nchyɛ́ ɛyɔŋ mándɛ́n yi nɛ ɛ́kpá, mámfɛrɛ yi amɔ.”
Arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Bě babhɔŋ bǎrɨŋɨ ndu ɛbhé ɛyɛsɛ ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ mmu Israɛl abhɨkɨ bhɔ́ŋ bɛfyɛ mmʉɛt nɛ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl nɛ abhɨkɨ bhɔŋ yɛ̌ chi bɛrɔŋ bɛghɔ bhɔ. Kɛ Mandɛm atɔŋ mɛ kpoŋoroŋ bɛ, nkɛ́ yɨŋɨ yɛ̌ mmu mbɔ bɛ abhɨkɨ kway bɛsí bha.
Sɛ́nsɔ́t bɛ́ mmu anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́re sɛnɛ ndǔ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm aghɔ wɔ mmu ɔ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ndǔ ɔ́chí amɛm ɛkɛt mandɛm nsé ɔ́nyìɛ nɛnyíɛ́. Wɔ ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ ɛyɔ ɛ́pú kʉ yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Kɛ ɔkáysí bɛ́ ɛ́pú kʉ yi ánkwɛ́n ndǔ ntá anɛ mɛnyiɛ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn bachyɛ ntá mandɛm nsé? Mbák ɛ́mfákárí nɔ, ɛ́pú chɔŋti ntɨ ɛni amɛm bɛsí Mandɛm?
‑ Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ápày ndǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛbhak bɛ́: “Achí nyaka mbɔ ághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n anɛ bakɛmɛ bárɔŋ bɛway, mbɔ mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n anɛ báfɛ̀rɛ ɛmɛnɛ ɛyi, yɛ̌ bɛbɨk yɔ kɛbɨk. Akɛ nɛ́nɛ ɛyɔŋ. Báyɔ́rɛ yi, bataŋ yi, bákpɔ́t nyé ɛni, bachyɛ yi ɛsɔŋɔri ndɛ́ndɛm. Agha ákway bɛtɔŋ bɛ, Yɨŋɨ́ mɔ̌wa nɛ́, ɛnɛ́ bákpɔ́rɛ́ nɛpɛ́m ɛni ambɨ ambɨ fá amɨk?”
Satan ámɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ Yesu ndǔ bɛyǎ babhi kɛkɛ́m yi, arɔ kpɨ́k yi. 
Asɨ́kɨ́ ntɨ nɛ Mandɛm. Mandɛm ampɛmɛ yi nɛ́nɛ mbák ǎyaŋ bɛpɛmɛ yi, mbɔnyunɛ arɛm bɛ achi Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm.”
Bɛyǎ bho báfú, bárɔ́k ntá Jɔ̌n ndu bɛghok ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ̀m. Báfú ɛtɔk Yerúsalɛm, nɛ atú Judɛ́ya ankɛm, nɛ bɛtɔk mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn bɛchi kɛkwɔt nɛ Nnyɛ́n Jɔ́dan.
Kɛ mbák, sayri sayri mɛ̌bòk bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ chi ndǔ bɛtaŋ Mandɛm, nɔ chi Mandɛm anáŋ achi nɛntɨ ɛnɛka mbɔ Mfɔ.
Chɔŋ sɛ́ndɛm yɛ bɛ yi? Sɛ́ndɔ́k ambɨ bɛkʉ bɛbʉ́ bɛ bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm mɛnja mɛncha kɛ?
Ángɛl anɛ mbɨ arɔk apɨkɨri ɛyǐ ɛkwɔbhɛ́ bɛběntɨ Mandɛm amɨk. Nkúbhɛ́ mpok yɔ bɛfʉɛt ɛbhɛn mɛ́nɛ̀m tontó bɛ́té amʉɛt bo abhɛn baka nyaka bɛ mamfyɛ bɔ ɛrɨŋ ɛnɛ nnya mbʉ́mbʉ amʉɛt nɛ báchyɛ́ mandɛm nsé yi kɛnókó.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́bhák bɛsí ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ mbɔ manyu. Ɛ́ngɔ nɔkɔ mbɔ glas anɛ áŋaŋari. Mɛnyɨŋ mɛ́nwí ɛbhɛn bɛchi nɛpɛ́m bɛ́tée bɛkáp ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ, ɛnyu ɛnɛ ɛ́mɔt ɛchi ambɨ, ɛ́mɔt ansɛm, ɛchák ɛbhě awɔ́nɛm, ɛnɛ́fú ɛbhe awɔ́ghɔ. Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ bɛ́bhɔ́ŋ bɛyǎ amɨ́k ambɨ nɛ ansɛm.
Páílet afɛrɛ yɛ Barábas mmǔ bo Israɛl nɛ bǒbati bhap báyàŋ yi amfɛrɛ. Achyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ́ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu mándɛn Yesu nɛ ɛ́kpá, mánsɔt yí, mándɔk, mángó ndǔ ɛkotákátí.   
Yesu ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛghati baghɔk abhi bati byo nɛ apay ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bɔ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ, afa nɛbhʉɛt yi achi nɛ bhɔ arɔk ndǔ bɛtɔk Israɛl bɛ́chák ndu bɛghati bo Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́.
Mpok básɔ́rɛ́ bhe ambɨ ndu bɛ́táŋ be, bǎkɛ́ sɛmɛ bɛ, ‘Chɔŋ sɛ́ndɛm bɛ yi nɛ yɛ̌ chí bɛ chɔŋ sɛ́ndɛm ná?’ Bǎkɛ́ sɔŋɔri mmʉɛt mbɔnyunɛ mpok ánkwáy, Mandɛm ǎghati bhe ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛrɛm.
Bɔ̌ma, ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ yɛ bɛkʉ chi bɛ, mpok bǎchɛ́mɛ́ nɛbhʉɛt amɔt ndu mɛnɨkmʉɛt, mbák mmu amɔt achyɛ́ nɛkwáy, achak antɔ́ŋ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm, anɛfu andɛm ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm akʉ yi andɨŋɨ, nɛ mbák achak andɛm kɛpɨ ndǔ ɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛnɛ yi abhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ, anɛfú ánɛ́nɛ́ yɔ ndǔ ɛyɔŋɔ́mbɔŋ. Kʉ ká yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛmbak anɛ ɛchyɛ bo mankɛm bɛtaŋ ndú baraka Mandɛm.
Nchí nɨk be mmʉɛt bɛ bǎkɛ́ puri mɛ bɛ mbák bɛběbɛbe nɛ bhe mpok ntwɔ́ awu. Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ mbɔŋ bɛ́bhak bɛběbɛbe chi nɛ bo abhɛn bákàysi bɛ sɛ́kʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ mbɔ bǒ mmɨk.
Tɛ̌ndu bɛbʉ́ mmu amɔt bɛkʉ nɛwú nɛ́bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ amfǎy bo mankɛm, ɛchi mbɔ̌ŋ tɛtɛp ɛcha, bɛ bo mankɛm abhɛn Mandɛm átɔŋ bɔ bɛyǎ bɛrɨ̌ndu nɛ ǎchyɛ bhɔ akap ndɛ́ndɛm ndu bɛkʉ bɔ mambak chak bɛsí bhi, mámbɔŋ bɛtaŋ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnap ndu bɛsɔt awɔ́nɛm amfǎy yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mmu amɔt, Yesu Kristo ákʉ́.
Mandɛm Ɛtayɛsɛ nɛ Yesu Kristo Acha mántɔŋ be bɛrɨ̌ndu, mánchyɛ bhe kpák.
kpát Hɛ́rɔd ayɨkɨ bɛ, “Chɔŋ nchyɛ́ wɔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́yàŋ nchyɛ́ wɔ.”
Ngók yɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fú ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Bě bɔ̌bɛtok Mandɛm mankɛm nɛ be bho báchyɛ̀ yí kɛnókó, manɛ́m bho nɛ ndɛ́ndɛmɛ bho, bɨtí ká Mandɛm aywɛsɛ.”
Ndǔ ngwɛnti, bɔ́ŋ ká nkaysi amɔt, mǎmbɔŋ nɔkɔ ntínso nɛ batɨ, mánkɔŋ batɨ bǒnkwɔ, mǎmbɔŋ bɛrɨ̌ntɨ nɛ batɨ, nɛ mǎmbɔŋ nɛsɛptímʉɛt.
Chi bɛfʉɛt ntá Yesu kɛ̌ bariɛp Mandɛm mankɛm áfù tɛtɛp. Ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ sɛ́rɛ̀m ndu nnyɛ́n Yesu Kristo bɛ́ “Amen”   ndu bɛchyɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó.
Ɛnɛ́ Píta abhʉɛ́t bɛyaŋ bɛrɨŋɨ ntí kɛnɔ́ amɨ́k antífú ɛkɔ, bǒ abhɛn Kɔnéliɔs átó, bare bhɛp ɛbhak ɛnɛ Símun áchí. Bárɔ́k kpát báchwɔp ndǔ nyǔbha ɛkɛt ɛnɛ yi achi arɛ.
Bǎkɛ́ bhak maknkay bɛghok mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn. Mpok ǎtwɔ̀ anɛ bawú mankɛm bághok ɛyɔŋ ɛya amɛm manɛm ayap.
Yesu atɛ́m bɔ́ nɛkay ɛnɛn bɛ, “Yɛ̌ mmu apú kway bɛsɔt ɛbhɔ́kɔ́ndɛn nkɔ bɛchok mbok ndǔ ɛsɨ́ ndɛn, mbɔnyunɛ mbák ánkʉ nɔ ɛbhɔ́kɔ́ndɛn anɛ nkɔ ɛ́ŋati, anɛ nsɨ́ andaka, mbok ámpɛt anchɨk ancha.
Kɛ ɛ́bhák mbɔ bɛ́ bágwɔt amɨ́k ayap. Bɔ́ kɛrɨŋɨ bɛ́ chí Yesu.
Ángɛl anɛ́ mbɨ afe mmbá yi. Tɛ́mté wu, amaŋá nɛbu achɛm nɛ ngó nɛ manoŋ, bɛre kwɛ́nti amɨk. Ɛbhɔ́kɔ́mɨk ɛ́mɔt ndu bɛrat ɛ́sɔ́ŋɔ. Ndǔ mɛnɔk amɔt ndǔ baru arat ásɔ́ŋɔ, nɛ tákɔ nkɛm nkwɔ asɔŋɔ.
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, nchí ghati bhe bɛ bǎkɛ́ fɛrɛ amɔ ɛ̌ti bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛn mɛ̌ghɔ̀ ɛ̌ti yɛka ndu bɛkwak bhe. 
Bághóko ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi mbɔ mɔ́mpɔŋ, bare chyɛ yɔ akabhɛ́ nya, nɛ mányíɛ́ ɛpa ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ baghoko nɛ amɔ.
Nɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ́mɛ́ ɛ́kɔ ndɔŋ amɔt nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ bárɛ́mɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyu básɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ
Bɛyǎ bǒ abhɛn bákʉ̀ baraká mandɛm nsé, bátwɔ́ nɛ bɛkátǐ-njɔ ɛbhap mɛnkɛm básɔ́ŋ bhɔ bɛsí bo mankɛm. Nɛ mbɔ báti nyaka bhɔ ti mbʉ bɛchyɛ nkáp anɛ aghaka bɛbhɔk silbha nka bɛsa bɛpay nsɛm byo (.).
Báchɔ́kɔ kpák, mbɔnyunɛ bákɛ̀m nyaka ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ batɨ ankɔŋɔmbi ndu bɛrɨŋɨ mmǔ wap anɛ áchá báchák.
Pɔ̌l abhak Ɛ́fɛsɔs ndǔ bataŋ árát andɔk nɔkɔ ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt bɛghati bhɔ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm kɛbhɔŋ bɛcháy ankɛm nɔkɔ ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ bhɔ ndu áyàŋ bɛ bɔ́ mándɨ́ŋɨ́, mánoko, ɛnyǔ Mandɛm áyàŋ bɔ mambak nɛ yi mbɔ Mfɔ wap.
Kɛ mpok anɛ bakoŋo Yesu bárɔ́ŋɔ́ arɛ bákap yi, afate apɛtnsɛm ɛtɔk Lístra nɛ bhɔ́. Nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́, Banábas nɛ yi bárɔ bárɔk Dɛ́be. 
Jɔ̌n ápɛ́rɛ tó bǒ bɛtɨk bhi, basɨŋ amɛn Moses nɛ amɛn barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ ǎrɛm nyaka ɛ̌ti Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ bariɛp bɛ ǎto.
Mpɛt nchí yaŋ bɛ ɔ́ngoko mɔ́kɛt ɔmbʉrɛ ntá ya. Nnókó bɛ́ chɔŋ Mandɛm angók nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt ɛnɛka, ankʉ ńtwɔ awu. 
Yɛ̌ chí nɛ́nɛ, sɛtɨ sɛ́chí bhʉ́rɛ́, nɛ bákway bɛkpɔt yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnɔk ɛnɛ ɛpu nyu bɛrɨ́tí kɛpɛm tɛ ndǔ bakaŋ, mángʉɛp angó.”
Bo Israɛl abhɛn báchí anywɔ́p nɛ María báwaka nɛ yi, bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ yi afate áyák áfú nɛfí, bákóŋo yi nɛ nkaysi bɛ ǎrɔ̀ŋ ndǔ nnɛm bɛdi kɛbhɔ arɛ.
Mandɛm achi ntísiɛ wa bɛ mpú sénse. Ntí anɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ pɛtnsɛm Kɔrint chi bɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ yaŋ mpɛt nchyɛ́ bhe ɛsɔŋɔri ɛ́chák.
Ángɛl Mandɛm abhesi ntá yi, ate ɛbhe áwɔnɛm, ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt ɛfɛmɛ-akap atú anɛ básɔ̀ŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛrɨ́tí ɛriɛp ɛyɔ.
Dɔ́k ká ambɨ bɛkʉ nɔ mbɔnyunɛ yɛ̌agha anɛ ákʉ̀ bɛbʉ́ ǎbhɔŋ nsáy ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhi, nɛ Mandɛm ǎtaŋ bo kɛtɔ́ŋ kɛ́rɨ́ŋámík.
Bɛrɔŋ ambɨ Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Mbák ntɨ mǔnkwɔ ánkʉ́ wɔ bɛbʉ́, dɔ́k tɛmɛrí yi, mǎmbák ndiɛrɛ be bati apay. Mbák ɔkʉ yi ángɔ́ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bhi mǎnsokori ndakárɛ́, nɔ ɔwɛ́nɛ́ ntɨ mǔnkwɔ.
Nkúbhɛ́ bɛti ɛbhɛ́n Hɛ́rɔd árɔ́bhɛ́ nóŋ chi bɛ nywɔp nɛ́njí mámfɛ́rɛ́ Píta ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ mántáŋ yi bɛsí bho, Píta abhak bhʉrɛ nɛ́ntɨ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bati apay, femfé nɛ ngɛm. Ngɛm amɔt abhat yi nɛ ntɛmɛ́ nɛnu amɔt ndǔ ɛbhěmʉɛt ɛ́mɔt, achák abhat yi nɛ ntɛmɛ́ nɛnu anɛfú ndǔ ɛbhěmʉɛt ɛ́chák. Batɛmɛ́ nɛnu báchák bábhak anyǔbhá mámbabhɛri nɔkɔ ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ.
“Mmu anɛ áfú amfay, achá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu achak. Mmǔ mmɨk afu fá amɨk, nɛ ǎrɛm chi barak anɛ́ mmɨk. Mmu anɛ áfú amfay achá bǒ mmɨk mankɛm.
Mandɛm afɛ́rɛ́ be ndǔ kɛsɛmɛ́ bɛbʉ́ nɛ bǎrɔp chi basɛm abhi bɛ mǎnkʉ nɔkɔ chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chí chak bɛsí bhi.
Kɛ nɛ́nɛ, ɛnɛ́ mǎnaŋ bǎrɨŋɨ Mandɛm, nɛ mbɔ̌ŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛrɛm chi bɛ, nɛ́nɛ, ɛnɛ́ Mandɛm árɨ́ŋɨ́ bhe, ná bǎkway bɛpɛt bɛbhak basɛm ntá bɛfóŋó ɛbhɛn bɛbhɔŋɔ bɛtaŋ fá amɨk, ɛnɛ́ mbɔ̌ŋ bɛtaŋ ɛbhap bɛ́pú yɛ̌nyɨŋ, nɛ bɛpú kway bɛkwak bhe?
Tɔmás anɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ Ɛfák, arɛm ntá batɨ bakoŋo Yesu abhɛ́nɛ́fú bɛ, “Sɛ́ndɔ́k ká nkwɔ bɛ Yɛ̌ chí nɛwú, sɛ́ngú nɛ yi.” 
Nchí ghati bhe bɛ mpú pɛrɛ nyu mmɛ́m amɛn, kpátɛ ɛwak ɛnɛ mɛ̌nyú mmɛ̌m bakɔ nɛ bhe ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt bɛchɔkɔ Ɛtaya”.
Júdas mmu átí yi arɨŋɨ nkwɔ ɛbhak ɛyɔ mbɔnyunɛ Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bátɛmɛri nɔkɔ nyaka arɛ.
Yesu anyabhɛ awɔ atɔk yi arɛm bɛ, “Nkɔŋ bɛkʉ wɔ ɔ́ntáŋ, nɛme ɛnɛ nɛ́máy.” Tɛ́mté wu, ataŋ.
mbɔnyunɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ Mandɛm áchyɛ́ nɛpɛ́m nɛkɔ ǎnù nɛ mmɨk ansɔrɛ nɔkɔ chi awɔ́nɛm. Nɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ́ sɛ́nù sɛ́nsɔt awɔ́nɛm chí ndu sɛ́bhɔŋ nɛka bɛ Yesu achí Kristo.
Mbák mánkʉ ɛnyʉ yɔ, nɔ bábhʉ̀ɛrɛ ɛrɛmɛ́ kɛfɔ ɛkɛ́n kɛ́chí ntá yap, kɛfɔ ɛkɛ́n bábhɔ̀ŋ amfay ndǔ mpok anɛ átwɔ̀ ambɨ. Mbák mánkʉ nɔ, chɔŋ mámbɔŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn tɛtɛp.
Akɛmɛ bɛ, ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Kɔŋ Mandɛm Acha ywɛ nɛ ntɨ ɛnɛ nɛnkɛm, nɛ ɛfóŋó yɛ ɛnkɛm, nɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛ mɛnkɛm, nɛ nkaysi yɛ nkɛm, nɛ kɔ́ŋ nkokosi yɛ mbɔ ɛnyu ɔ́kɔ́ŋɔ́ mmʉɛt ɛyɛ.”
Bǎghɔ yɛ̌ mǔnti ɛtɔk amɔt anókó yi? Bǎghɔ yɛ̌ mǔnkwɔ Fárisi anókó yi?
Bo barɔk ambɨ bɛ́fú ndǔ bɛtɔk nɛ bɛtɔk mántwɔ nɔkɔ ntá Yesu. Ngɛ́mtay bho báchɛ́mɛ́ nɛbhʉɛt amɔt. Yesu atɛ́m bhɔ nɛkay ɛnɛn bɛ́:
“Ghatí bo Síɔn   bɛ́ mfɔ wap ǎtwɔ̀. Abhɔŋ nɛsɛptǐmʉɛt, ǎtwɔ chɔkɔ amfǎy mpɔŋɔ batu, amfay mɔ́mpɔŋɔ batu.”
Ɛ́fákari bɛ mmu amɔt arɔk ntá Yesu, abhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, ntɨkɨ ɛrɨ́tí ɛnyɨŋ mɛ̌kwáy bɛkʉ kɛ Mandɛm anchyɛ mɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti?”
Anɛ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ Fílip arɔk ɛtɔk ɛ́gho atú Samária angati nɔkɔ mbok ɛ̌ti Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò.
Bɛpɨŋ ɛbhɛka bɛbhɔŋ bɛbhak ɛnyu ɛ́mɔt mbɔ ɛnɛ Yesu Kristo ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka.
Nɔ kɛ ɛchi bɛ Mandɛm ǎyɛt yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛka nɛ Kristo, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi áyɛ́rɛ́ nyaka Ábraham ndu yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛka nɛ yi.
Yesu átɛ́n nɔ́kɔ́ mmʉɛt ambɨ mandú, aghɔ́ bɔ̌ nnɔ amɔt chi amɔt bachak bati apay, nɔ chi, Jems nɛ Jɔ̌n, bɔ̌ Sɛbɛdi. Bábhák amɛm áchwí chɔkɔ nɛ ɛtayap Sɛbɛdi, mángoko nɔkɔ bɛyǎ nkáp yap. Yesu abhɨŋɨ bhɔ nkwɔ bɛ mámbák bakoŋo bhi.
Nsɔt yɛ mɔ́kati nɛ́nɛ́p wu awɔ ángɛl nyiɛ́. Ɛ́ré nyɨŋti mɛ anyu mbɔ bawɛrɛ́ bɛtu. Kɛ nnyiɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, ɛ́kʉ́ mɛniɛ ɛbha bɛ́rɔ́bhɛ nɛnɛnɛ́n.
bɛbho nɛ Ábɛl kpát bɛghaka amʉɛt Sakaría mu báwáy nɛntɨ ɛ́fɛ́mɛ́ akap nɛ ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm. Nchí ghati bhe bɛ chɔŋ Mandɛm antɛmsi mkpáká bho abhɛn ɛchɔŋ ɛ̌ti bawú yɔ ankɛm!
Mɔ́wa Tímɔti, dɔ̌ yɛ Mandɛm anchyɛ wɔ bɛtaŋ. Ǎkwáy bɛ́kʉ nɔ ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhi nɛ wɔ ndu ɔ́bhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Kristo.
Yi abhɨkɨ yaŋ nyaka bɛghok Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ɛnɛ sɛ̌ghàti bho wáwák. Wɔ mbɔŋ ɔbhɔŋ bɛ́kɛm mmʉɛt nɛ yi.
Nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ nkáp ájwi amɛm mɔ́kɛrɛ́ nkáp, nɔ́ kɛ̌ nkaysi ndɨ́ndɨ́ ájwì antɨ mmǔ ndɨ́ndɨ́, nɛ bɛrɨ bɔ́bhɔ́ kɛ bɛ́fù arɛ́. Kɛ mbák mmú abhɔ̌ŋ ɛbɛ́ptí ntɨ, barak abʉ́abʉ kɛ áfù yi anyu, mbɔnyunɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́jwí mmu antɨ, yɔ́ kɛ ɛ́fù yi anyu.” 
Sɔt yɛ ka mpok bɛ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ ɛbhɛn bǎkaysi bɛ bɛchi be antɨ bɛ́kɛ́ bhak ɛjuri.
Bábhé Yesu ɛtɔk Bɛ́tlɛhɛm atú Judɛ́ya. Mpok yɔ, Hɛ́rɔd abhak Mfɔ atú wu. Nɛbhé bábhé Yesu, bo abhɛn bárɨŋɨ ɛ̌ti mambe báfú atú mmok áfù batwɔ Yerúsalɛm, mámbɛbhɛ nɔkɔ bɛ,
Píta abho bɛrɛm ntá Yesu bɛ, “Acha, ɛ́rɨ tontó bɛ sɛchi fá. Mbák ɔkɔŋ, chɔŋ nte bɛtɛm barat. Ɛmɔt ntá yɛ, ɛchak ntá Moses, nɛ ɛnɛ́fú ntá Ɛláija.”
Agʉ́ɛ́p yi amɛm nɛpi ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti. Achók nyǔ nɛpi, aghaŋa, bɛ Satan ákɛ́ bhɔŋ mbi bɛfu arɛ andɔk ambɨ bɛrwɔ bǒ mmɨk mankɛm. Ɛbhak bɛ Satan abhɔŋ bɛbhak amɛm nɛpi kpatɛ mamiɛ́ nka amɔt amfʉɛt kɛ mandɔ yi ndu mɔmbɨŋɨ mpok.
Tímɔti, nchí sɨ́ŋ ntá yɛ, wɔ mmu ɔ́chí mbɔ mɔ́wa tɛtɛp ndu ɔ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛka nɛ Yesu mbɔ mɛ. Mandɛm Ɛtayɛsɛ nɛ Yesu Kristo Acha ywɛsɛ mántɔŋ wɔ bɛrɨ̌ndu nɛ ntínso, mánchyɛ wɔ kpák. 
Yesu ǎrɛ̀m nyaka nɔ ɛ̌ti Júda, mmɔ̌ Símun Iskariɔt, mbɔnyunɛ Júda, mmu amɔt ndǔ nkwɔ́ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bati byo nɛ apay, abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka nkaysi bɛti yi.
Ndǔ mpok anɛ áfʉɛ́rɛ́ ansɛm, bǎkʉ̀ nyaka mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl bákɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ. Ɛyɔ ɛkway! Bǎchyɛ̀ nyaka nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛka ndu bɛpɔ̌ baraka ɛpúsí, bǎbhɔ́ŋ bɛyǎ ɛkwak ndu bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ, bǎbhák manyǔ mmɛ́m, mǎnkoŋo nɔkɔ bɛpǎ ɛpusi nɛ bɛchɛmɛ́ manyǔ mmɛ́m, mǎnchyɛ nɔkɔ kɛnókó ntá bɔmandɛm nsé, ɛnɛ ɛbhé Mandɛm ɛpu ka nɔ.
“Ágháká nɔ́kɔ́ mamiɛ́ bɛsa bɛ́páy, nkaysi atwɔ́ yi antɨ bɛ ándɔ́k ángɔ́ bɔ̌mayi, bo Israɛl.
Mpú rɛm bɛ Mandɛm ǎnɔk bɛbhʉrɛ bariɛp amɛn yi afyɛ́ nyaka nɛ bo Israɛl. Puyɛ̌ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu Israɛl kɛ achi mmǔ Mandɛm.
Bakʉ̌ bɛbʉ́ mándɔk ambɨ bɛkʉ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhap, bɛpɔ̌ bho mándɔk ambɨ bɛ́bhak bɛpɔ̌ bho. Bo abhɛn bachi chak bɛsí Mandɛm mándɔk ambɨ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi chak nɛ bo abhɛn bachi nyáŋá mándɔk ambɨ bɛbhak nyáŋá.
Mbák ngɔrɛ́ apú yaŋ bɛkuti ntí, ámkpɨk andɔk mamu wu. Kɛ tɛ̌ndu mɛ́mu ntí chí ɛnyɨŋɨ́ ntíanwɔ́p ntá ngɔrɛ́ abhɔŋ yɛ́ bɛkuti ntí.
Mpɔŋɔndɨ́k achák afú yɛ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ. Are pe chuuu. Báchyɛ́ mmu anɛ ǎkɔ̀ yɔ́ bɛtaŋ ndu bɛfɛrɛ kpák ámɨk bɛ bǒ mámbo bɛway batɨ. Nɛ báchyɛ́ yi ɛrɛmɛ́ akparɛnja.
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, mfǎy, bɔ́ŋ yɛ maŋák. Bě mankɛm abhɛn bǎchi amfay, bɔ́ŋ ká maŋák! Kɛ mbák chi mmɨk nɛ manyu, ɛyak ɛchí nɛ bhe mbɔnyunɛ Mfɔ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ asɛp atwɔ ntá yɛka nɛ bɛyǎ ɛchók mbɔnyunɛ yi arɨŋɨ bɛ mpok ayi arɔp chi kɛkwɔt!”
Mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́páy bɛ́chí mɛ antɨ nɛ nchí mbɔ mmu anɛ áchí ndǔ manyé mbi kɛrɨŋɨ mbi anɛ yí ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkoŋo. Mpok nɛ mpok, nchí bhɔ́ŋ nkaysi bɛ ɛ́rɨ bɛ mbák nɛpɛ́m, kɛ mbɔ̌ŋ ntɨ bɛ́rɔŋ bɛbhak nɛ Kristo, nɛ ɛyɔ kɛ̌ ɛ́rɨ́ ntá ya ɛ́chá.
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ chɔŋ mbɔŋ Yesu Acha amfú amfay antwɔ́ anchyɛ ɛyɔŋ nɛ bɛtaŋ. Mfɔ bɔángɛl Mandɛm andɛm nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ, nɛ mmbá Mandɛm ankwɛ́n. Ɛ́mfakari yɛ bɛ́ bakoŋó Kristo abhɛn bágú mánjambɨ mámpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m,
Nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́, ɛbyɔk ɛ́kwɛ́n ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ. Batɛmɛ́ nɛnu abhɛn bábhàbhɛri Píta, báré makati mámbɛbhɛ nɔkɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fákárí nɛ yi.
Bɔ̌ma, mpok anɛ bǎchɛmti bɛ mǎnyiɛ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛkɔŋ kɛ mǎnyiɛ nɛnyíɛ́ Acha, bo abhɛn báyámbɨ, bábhɔŋ mɛnoŋ batɨ.
Bɛkɔŋ Mandɛm chi bɛbhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé bhi. Nɛ bɛbhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé bhi puyɛ̌ ɛtaŋtí ɛnyɨŋ,
Ntá bǒ abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ nɛbhay, nɛ mánkwɛ́sɛ́, nchí rɛm bɛ mándɔ́p mmʉɛ́rɛ́mʉɛt ayap mbɔ mɛ.
Kɛ tɛ̌ndu sɛ́pú yáŋ bɛkʉ bǒbhɛn mambe ntɨ, sɛp, dɔ́k manyu, gʉɛ́p áwám anyɛ́n. Nsi mbɨ anɛ ɔ́kɛ́mɛ́ nɛnɛ́ nnyu ywi. Chɔŋ ɔ́ngɔ́ nkáp arɛ anɛ akway bɛchyɛ awa nkábhɛ́nti anɛ ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm nɛ aywɛ. Sɔt wu chyɛ bhɔ.”
Kɛ mbák Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ áyà bhe mbi, nɔ bǎpu antɛnɛ́ bɛbhé.
Kɛ ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ Mandɛm átɔ̀ŋ bhɛsɛ bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛ̌ti Kristo ɛchi kɛkúrí nɛ ɛnyu ɛnɛ Adam ákʉ́ bɛbʉ́. Bɛyǎ bo bágu nyaka ɛ̌ti bɛbʉ́ mmu amɔt, kɛ bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm bɛyǎ mbɔŋ bɛcha. Ɛnyu ɛnɛ kɛ Mandɛm áchyɛ̀ áfɔ́k ntá bɛyǎ bho ndɛ́ndɛm bɛkoŋo ɛnyǔ mmu amɔt, Yesu Kristo, átɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛrɨ̌ndu.
Bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, ntɨkɨ mpok chɔŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fakari, nɛ ntɨkɨ ɛrɨŋ ɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ bo mandɨŋɨ bɛ mpok anɛ ɔ́twɔ̀ arɔp kɛ́kwɔ́t?”
Píta arɔk ambɨ bɛ́rɛ́m bɛ, “Bo Israɛl, ghók ká bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛ́n: ‘Yesu mmu Násárɛt chí mmu anɛ Mandɛm áyábhɛ́ nyaka. Atɔ́ŋ kpoŋoroŋ bɛ́ ayap yí ndǔ áchyɛ́ yi bɛtaŋ. Akʉ yɛ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay. Atɔ́ŋ bɛrɨŋ. Bě babhɔŋ bǎrɨŋɨ nɔ sayri mbɔnyunɛ akʉ nyaka mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛsí ɛbhɛka.
Júdas, [anɛ áchí kɛkúrí nɛ Júdas Iskariɔt] abhɛ́p Yesu bɛ, “Acha, ndaká yí ɔ́twɔ̀ chɔŋ chi ntá yɛsɛ bakoŋo bhɛ bɛ́kʉ sɛ́ndɨ́ŋɨ́ wɔ, kɛbhák bɛ́ ɔ̌kʉ nɔ chi ntá bǒ mmɨk bachak?”
Kɛ Ábraham akɛmɛ yi chí bɛ ‘Bɔ̌mayɛ babhɔŋ basɨŋ Moses nɛ amɛn barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ. Mángók mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn basɨŋɨ́ mɔ ághàti bhɔ.’
Símun anɛ mpɨ́kɨ́rí nnyɛ́n ɛni nɛchi bɛ Píta, ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay yɔ, arɔk atɛp mánɛ́n bɛsí Yesu, arɛm bɛ, “Acha, kɛ́twɔ kɛkwɔt nɛ mɛ, mbɔnyunɛ nchí mmǔ bɛbʉ́.”
Yesu arɛm yɛ ntá mɔ́ngɔrɛ́ wu bɛ, “Mfóŋórí bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛ.”
Píta ǎkoŋo nyaka bhɔ ansɛm nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ, kpátɛ amɛm sɛnta mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm. Arɛ́, arɔk achɔkɔ nɛ babhabhɛri angɔkɔ ngó angwaka nɔkɔ ngó.
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, tɨ́k ká nsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛka. Mbák ɛ́pú nɔ́, chɔŋ ntwɔ ntá yɛka mandú mpok, nsɔt akparɛnja nsɛm ɛpay wu nɔ áfù mɛ anyu nɛ ǎcháp, nnu nɛ bhɔ.
“Ngátí bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ɛnɛ́ mbʉɛ́t nɛ bhe.
Josɛ́f ató yɛ bábhɨŋɨ ɛ́táyi Jekɔ́p nɛ bǒnɛrɛ́kɛt ywi mankɛm, batí bɛsa bɛ́rát nsɛm nɛku.
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ yɛ̌ nkoŋo baghɔrɛ́, nɛ yɛ̌ chi mmu anɛ ntɨ ɛni nɛ́pú amɛm pɛ́pɛ́p, nɛ mmu anɛ afyɛ́ amɨ́k ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ bo bachak apú bhɔŋ ákɔ́rɛ́ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt kɛfɔ Kristo nɛ Mandɛm. Mmu anɛ afyɛ́ amɨ́k ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ bo bachak achi mbɔ mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɔmandɛm bachak mbɔnyunɛ akɔŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ acha Mandɛm.
Bákɛ́m yɛ́ yi, baya, báfú amɛm nkɨ nɛ yi, barɔk baway.”
Yɛ̌ agha anɛ árɛ̀m kpoŋoroŋ bɛ Yesu chi Mmɔ Mandɛm, Mandɛm ǎbhɔŋ nɛbharɛ́mʉɛt nɛ yi, nɛ yí ǎbhɔ́ŋ nɛbharɛ́mʉɛt nɛ Mandɛm.
Nchí nu nyaka tontó bɛ́kóŋo bɛpɨŋ abhɛn bachǐmbɨ bha. Nɛ nchí koŋo nyaka mbi Mandɛm bo Israɛl nɛ ntɨ ɛna nɛnkɛm, kpát ncha bo Israɛl báchák abhɛn ɛkaká nɛbhe ɛya.
Yesu aghók bɛ́ bábók mmu anɛ yi ákʉ́ amɨ́k ánɛ́nɛ́ batɛn nɛfí. Abho bɛyaŋ yi. Ághɔ́ nɔkɔ yi, abhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ɔnókó Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm?”
Mbák chi mɛ, bɛyɨŋɨ bɛbhé Moses ndɔp chi ngú, mbɔnyunɛ bɛbhɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛkʉ nɛ mɛ. Ɛ́fákári ɛnyu ɛyɔ bɛ́ mbák nɛpɛ́m bɛsí Mandɛm.
Bɛbhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm chi yi? Chí nɛka anɛ mmu ákà bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi abhaka ntɨ bɛ chɔŋ ambɔ́ŋ ɛ́bhɔŋ bɛ́fákári, nɛ mɛ́nóko nɛ ntɨ nɛnkɛm bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mmu apú ghɔ́ nɛ amɨ́k bɛ́chi tɛtɛp.
Bɛbʉ́ mɛ́naŋ bɛchi nyaka fá amɨk kɛ Mandɛm ákʉ bɛbhé bɛ́fʉɛ́t ntá Moses bɛ́twɔ́. Kɛ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ ɛbhé ɛpu bápú kwáy bɛrɛm bɛ mmu akwɛn ɛbhé.
mǔnti ɛpǎ nɛbhay ághókótí nɔ́kɔ́, aghɔ́ bɛ́ manyiɛp mɔ arɔp chi mmɛ́m. Yi kɛrɨŋɨ ɛbhak mɔ́ áfú, yɛ̌ndu bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk abhɛn bákò mɔ bárɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka bɛ manyiɛp kɛ ayibhiri ndǔ mmɛm. Mǔnti ɛpǎ nɛbhay abhɨŋɨ mbǎyngɔrɛ́,
Nɛ mpú sɔt nyaka chí nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnɛn bǒ mmɨk ndu bɛtɔŋ, ngati nɔkɔ bhe Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ndu nchi nu bɛkʉ mǎnókó. Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ kɛ̌ ásɔ́rɛ́ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi ákʉ́ mǎngɔ́ bɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ sɛ́ghàti bhe ɛ́chí tɛtɛp.
Ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ ywɛka ámbʉ́rɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ, bɛkoŋo nkáp anɛ yi ákʉ́ bɛtɨk ábhɔ́ŋɔ́, bɛ bǎkɛ́ chwɔp bakap chi ndiɛrɛ mpok anɛ ntwɔ́ awu.
Kɛ Yesu abhɨŋɨ mǔnkwɔ Fárisi wu bɛ, “Símun, mbɔ̌ŋ ndak bɛ́ghati wɔ.” Símun akɛmɛ bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, dɔ́k ambɨ.”
Nɛ chɔŋ Mmǔ anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm ambesi, ande twɔ́ amɛm nɛbháŋ, nɛ bɛyǎ bɛtaŋ nɛ kɛnókó.
Mǔngo batɛmɛ́ nɛnu ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, arɔk abhɛp Pɔ̌l bɛ, “Ghatí mɛ́, ɔchí mmu Rom tɛtɛbhɛ?” Pɔ̌l aka bɛ, “Nchí mmu Rom.”
Nɛ mpok Kristo mmu achi nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛsɛ ábhèsi, chɔŋ be nkwɔ mǎmbesi nɛ yi nɛ mǎmbɔŋ ákɔ́rɛ́ ndu kɛnɛ́m ɛki. 
Ɛ́bhak ɛnyu ɛyɔ mbɔnyunɛ mmʉɛt ɛyɛsɛ ɛnɛ ɛ́pɔpɔ́ɔ ɛbhɔŋ bɛyibhiri ɛndɔp mmʉɛt ɛkɔ ɛnɛ ɛ́pú gu wáwák. Nɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́gugu ɛbhɔŋ bɛyibhiri ɛndɔp chi ɛnɛ ɛ́pú gu wáwák.
Kɛ mmu anɛ ághókó ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ yi arɛmɛ anoko, ǎtɔŋ bɛ yi anókó ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm árɛ́mɛ́ bɛ ɛ́chí tɛtɛp.
Mmǔ wap amɔt ajiɛt arɔk asɔt ɛkuchá agwɔ́t antí mɔ́nɔk asɛbhɛ yɔ́ amɛm ɛchyɛ́ mmɛ́m. Asá amfay, atɛmɛ Yesu anyu bɛ́ ánsɔ́k. Arɛm bɛ, “Dɔ̌ sɛ́ngɔ́ mbák Ɛláija ǎtwɔ̀ bɛfɛrɛ yi ndǔ ɛkotákátí nɛ.”
Bǎkɛ́ koŋo ɛkakánɛkɔ ɛnɛ́ bǒ mmɨk. Dɔ́ ká Mandɛm ángúpsí nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛka. Ǎkʉ̀ nɔ ndu áchyɛ̀ bhe nkaysi nkɔ. Ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ̀ mǎndɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm áyàŋ. Yɔ́ ɛ́rɨ, yɔ́ kɛ ɛ́chyɛ̀ yi maŋák, nɛ yɔ́ kɛ ɛ́rɨ́ ɛ́chá ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbi.
Kɛ Yerúsalɛm anɛ amfay apú ndu kɛsɛm nɛ yi kɛ achi máyɛsɛ.
Mamɔ anɛ átwɔ̀ chi bɛkʉ bo mángɔ́ mbák bábhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm tɛtɛp. Yɛ̌ndu pú áchɔ̀ŋti, báfyɛ yi ango mánsɔŋ sayri mámfɛrɛ bakwap ndu bɛrɨŋɨ mbák chi pú tɛtɛp. Nɛka ɛnɛka nɛ Mandɛm nɛcha pú. Bǎbhɔŋ yɛ bɛghɔ ɛsɔŋɔri ndu bɛkʉ bo mandɨŋɨ mbák nɛka ɛnɛka nɛ Mandɛm nɛ́chí tɛtɛp nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyu básɔ̀ŋ pú ndu bɛghɔ mbák chi pú tɛtɛp. Ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ ɛchi bɛ mbák mánte kpirí ndǔ nɛka ɛnɛka nɛ Mandɛm, chɔŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́ntwɔ bhe nɛ bakak, nɛ kɛnɛ́m, nɛ kɛnókó ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɛn Yesu Kristo ápɛtnsɛm.
Sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ ɛbhé chí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛfóŋó ɛbhɛsɛ. Kɛ nchí chí nkwǎŋwaŋ anɛ achi ndǔ kɛsɛmɛ́ bɛbʉ́.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Yɛ̌ mmu apú kway bɛsɔt ɛbhɔ́kɔ́ndɛn nkɔ anchók mbok ndǔ ɛsɨ́ ndɛn? Mbák mmu ankʉ nɔ, ɛbhɔ́kɔ́ndɛn nkɔ ɛ́ŋàti, ɛnkʉ mbokó ndɛn ánchɨk ancha ɛsɨ́ mbok.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛta áyàŋ chí bɛ́ yɛ̌ agha anɛ ághɔ́ Mɔ́ywi, asɨkɨ ntɨ nɛ yi, ámbɔ́ŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti. Nɛ chɔŋ nkʉ yi ampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɛn ngwɛnti.”
Ghatí bɛsakábho sayri bɛ mántɔ́ŋ bɛ bábhɔŋ kɛboŋ nɛ bɛ mándɨ́ŋɨ́ ndu bákɛ̀m mmʉɛt.
Píta nɛ mamʉɛrɛ bhi bábhɛ́p Yesu bɛ, “Ndaká yí batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses bárɛ̀m bɛ Ɛláija abhɔŋ bɛpɛtnsɛm fá amɨk kɛ Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ bariɛp bɛ ǎtó antwɔ́?”
Bakáp ayɛká áchɔ́ŋtí, nɛ kɛngɔk anyiɛ bɛrɨ́tí ndɛn ɛyɛká.
Sɛ́kàka Mandɛm mmu Yesu Kristo Acha ywɛsɛ achi Mɔ́ywi, nɛ sɛ́nɨ̀kmʉɛt ɛ̌ti yɛka,
Mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ̌kʉ̀. Mpú kʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ́yàŋ bɛkʉ. Nchí kʉ chi nkúbhɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mpábhɛ́.
Bɔ̌ma, nɛ́ chi ɛkáti ɛnɛ́ ɛjwi bɛpay ndu bɛkáti ɛbhɛn nsɨŋɨ́ bhe. Ndu bɔ bɛpay mɛnkɛm, nchí tɨk be mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mǎnáŋ bǎrɨŋɨ, ndu bɛkwak mǎmbɔŋ nkaysi anɛ achi chak.
Nchí kʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm chí bɛ́ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo ántáká mbǎnkɛm, nɛ bɛ́ Mandɛm ánjɛ́t mɛ́ nkwɔ nɛ bɛrɨ ɛbhɛn bo abhɛn bákòŋo Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ bábhɔ̀ŋ.
Ɛ́tárɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, Yesu akó amfǎy njiɛ, abhɨŋɨ bakoŋo bhi mánkóŋó yi. Bárɔ́ŋ nɔ́kɔ́,
Nɛ mǔbɛtok Acha abhɨkɨ bhɔŋ bɛbhak ntaŋ-bɛ́táŋá. Abhɔŋ bɛbhak chi mmǔ anɛ átɔ̀ŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu bɛrɨ̌ntɨ nɛ, abhɔŋ bɛbhak ɛrɨ́tí ntɔ̌ŋ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm, nɛ ambak mmǔ anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ nɛ bǒ abhɛn báchyɛ̀ yi ɛsɔŋɔri.
Sɛ́ghɔ̀ fá bɛ mbɔ̌ŋ Debhít ǎbhɨ̀ŋɨ nyaka Mpɛmɛ́ bɛ Acha. Ná Achǎ-rɛ áyibhiri ambak ɛbhárɛ́mɔ ywi?” Bɛyǎ bo babhɔ̌ŋ maŋák bɛ́ghok mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Yesu átɔ̀ŋ. 
Ntó Tíkíkɔs andɔk Ɛ́fɛsɔs.
Ɛ̌ti bǒnkwɔ kɛ Mandɛm ákʉ́ bɛ mbak mǔbɛtok ndu bɛkʉ mǎndɨŋɨ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm sayri.
Ntá mmu amɔt Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ǎchyɛ nɛka, ntá mmu achák anchyɛ akap bɛ́bú bo mame.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛ́go nɛ bɛ́bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ. Abhɔ́ŋ bɛyǎ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak nɛ áfɔ́k Mandɛm abhak nɛ yi. 
“Sɔt ka mpok nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm. Bákɔŋ bɛghap mánkó mansɛp nɛ bɛwubhɛ wubhɛ́ ndɛn amʉɛt nɛfísiɛ bɛ bo mánkáká nɔ́kɔ́ bhɔ nɛ kɛnókó. Bákɔŋ nkwɔ́ bɛ́chɔkɔ ndǔ bɛbhaká kɛnókó amɛm bɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt nɛ ndǔ bɛpa.
Kɛ sɛ́nkáká Mandɛm bɛ achyɛ́ bhɛsɛ awɔ́nɛm amfǎy bɛbʉ́ ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu Kristo Acha ywɛsɛ ákʉ́.
Sɛ́ndɔ́ yɛ bɛyɨŋɨ nɔkɔ chi ndiɛrɛ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ mbɨ ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo, sɛ́ndɔ́k ambɨ ndu bɛchak bɛ sɛ́nsɛ́nɛ́ ndǔ nɛjwǐmɛm ɛnɛsɛ. Sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ bhɔŋ bɛsɔt mpok bɛrɛm ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́kɛ́mɛ́ nɛka ɛnɛsɛ mbɔ ɛbhɛn bɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ mmu abhɔŋ bɛtɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhi, andɔ bɛkʉ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́twɔ̀ yi chi nɛ nɛwú, nɛ bɛ mmu abhɔŋ bɛka nɛ Mandɛm.
Kɛ nɛ́nɛ, ɛnɛ́ nnáŋ nnáŋá bɛtɨk ndǔ mbaŋ ɛnɛ ɛnkɛm, mbɔ̌ŋ ntɨ bɛghɔ bhe mbɔ ɛnyǔ nnáŋ nchí yáŋ bɛkʉ ndǔ bɛyǎ mamiɛ́ anɛ áfʉɛ́rɛ́ ansɛm.
Ntɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm amɔt arɛm ntá Yesu bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, mpok ɔ́rɛ̀m mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn, ɔ́chyɛ bhɛsɛ nkwɔ ntíánwɔ́p!”
Kɛ abhɨkɨ tɔ́ŋ mmʉɛt chí ntá bo mankɛm. Atɔ́ŋ mmʉɛt ntá batísiɛ́ abhɛn Mandɛm ánáŋ áyábhɛ́, nɔ́ chí bhɛsɛ́ bo sɛ́nyíɛ́ nɛ sɛ́nyú nɛ yi mpok yi ápɛ́rɛ́nsɛm ndu nɛpɛ́m.
Nɛka Áisek kɛ nɛ́kʉ́ yi áyɛ́rɛ́ nyaka bɔ̌bhi Jekɔ́p nɛ Isau, aghati bhɔ ɛ̌ti áfɔ́k anɛ átwɔ ansɛm.
Bákɔŋ nkwɔ́ bɛ́chɔkɔ ndǔ bɛbhaká kɛnókó amɛm bɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt nɛ ndǔ bɛpa.
Ɛyɔŋ ɛ́bhak fá amɨk, nɛ báfʉ́ɛ́t ntá yi kɛ bághoko mmɨk. Yɛ̌ nɔ, mpok yi átwɔ́ fá amɨk, bǒ mmɨk kɛrɨŋɨ ɛnyu mmu yi achi.
Mandɛm arɛm bɛ ‘Ndǔ manywɔbhɛ́ ngwɛnti, chɔŋ nkʉ Ɛfóŋó ya antwɔ ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu. Bɔ̌bhɛka mángati barak anɛ́ mɛ mfyɛ́ bɔ́ antɨ. Bɛsak ɛbhɛka mángɔ́ kɛnɔ́ amɨ́k antifu, nɛ baseansi bhɛka mángɔ kɛnɔ́.
Bɔ̌ma, mmu ákɛ́ nywinti ámbɨ́ŋɨ́ nnyɛ́n ntɨ. Mmu anɛ ákʉ̀ nɔ́, ǎkwɛ́n manyé ɛwak Mandɛm átàŋ bo. Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ Ntaŋá-manyé achi ambǐnywɔp téé, apu nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ.
Asɔt Píta nɛ Jems nɛ Jɔ̌n arɔk nɛ bhɔ́. Arɔp nsónso nɛ basɛ́mɛ́ antɨ.
Ɛ́pɛ́t ɛtɔk Yesu tontó, afa, arɔk ndǔ nnɛm. Nnɛm ɛnɔ nɛ́bhak chi mbok anɛ achi ndǔ sɛtárɛ́bhɛ́. Mánaŋ básɔt nyaka ntay nɛgho bákúti nyǔnɛm.
Ghatí baséansi baghɔrɛ́ nkwɔ bɛ mambʉrɛ bapɛ́m yap ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ átɔ̀ŋ bɛ́ báchyɛ̀ Mandɛm kɛnókó. Bǎkɛ́ rɛm ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti batɨ nɛ bǎkɛ́ bhak manyǔmɛ́m. Tɔ́ŋ bo báchák bɛ́kʉ bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ.
Ghɔ yɛka ndǔ Mandɛm are bhɔŋ bɛrɨ̌ntɨ nɛ ndǔ yi achi kɨ́kɨ́rɨ́k nkwɔ nɛ bo. Achí kɨ́kɨ́rɨ́k nɛ bo abhɛn bákwɛ́nɛ́ ndǔ bɛbʉ́. Kɛ ntá yɛka, ǎtɔ̀ŋ bɛrɨ̌ntɨ mbák mǎndɔk ambɨ bɛkʉ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi áyàŋ. Mbák ɛ́pú nɔ, ǎkpɔt be nkwɔ amfɛrɛ ndǔ ɛnɔk.
Mandɛm anɛ bo bábɨ̀ti, yi mmu áchi Mfɔ anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ amfay yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ, Acha nɛ Mfɔ bafɔ, chɔŋ yí ankʉ Yesu ambesi ndǔ mpok anɛ yi áyábhɛ́.
Páílet apɛt abhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ɔ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛ́kɛ́mɛ? Ghok bɛbɛ́pti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bárɛ̀m bɛ́ ɔ̌kʉ!”
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Bɛsɔp bɛbhɔŋ babhok, kɛnɛn kɛ́bhɔ́ŋ manyay, kɛ Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ɛbhak bɛsoŋ ntí.”
Yɛ̌ nɔ, ɛ̌ti ɛkɔŋ, mɛ Pɔ̌l, mmǔ nsensi nɛ mǔkɛnɔŋ nɛ́nɛ ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo, nchí nɨk wɔ chi mmʉɛt.
Ɛyɔŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi nyaka bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ ntá mkpaká bho ɛnɛ ɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́ ansɛm, kɛ nɛ́nɛ, Mandɛm akʉ bǒbhi mándɨ́ŋɨ́ yɔ.
Yesu apɛt arɔk ɛtɔk Kána, atú Gálili, ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ yi ákú nyaka manyiɛp áyíbhírí mmɛ́m. Mǔnti amɔt abhak Kapɛ̌naum anɛ mɔ́ywi áme.
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ mbi, sɛnkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu bɛrɨ, sayri sayri, batɨ bǒnkwɔ. 
Bo mankɛm abhɛn bachi arɛ bághɔ́ yi ndu ákɔ̀ ambɨti nɔkɔ Mandɛm.
Yesu abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ re pay ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm? Básɨŋ bɛ, ‘Nkúbhɛ́ ntay ɛnɛn batěkɛt bágʉɛ́bhɛ́ bɛ́ nɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ rɨ, nɔ́ kɛ nɛ́rɔ́bhɛ́ ntay ɛnɛn nɛ́kɛ́mɛ́ ɛkɛt nɛchá batay áchák ankɛm. Mandɛm kɛ ákʉ́ bɛ́ ɛ́mbák ɛnyu yɔ, nɛ ɛchi ndaká maknkay tontó ntá yɛsɛ!’
Yesu asɔt yɛ nkɔ́p nɛ mmɛ́m amɛm. Áchyɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bakak ntá Mandɛm, achyɛ ntá bǒnto andɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Sɔt ka nyú, ntɨ anyǔ anchyɛ ntɨ.
Ɛ́kʉ́, yɛ Yesu aghati bhɔ kpoŋoroŋ bɛ, “Lásárɔs agu,
Asɔt bɛkpɔkɔ́ brɛt bhɔ bɛ́táy nɛ nsi ɛpay. Ayoŋ amɨ́k mfay. Achyɛ bakak ntá Mandɛm, abho bɛ́bɔ́kɔ́ti brɛt wu anchyɛ nɔkɔ ntá baghɔkɔ́ bhi bɛ mánkɔ́rɛ́ nɛ nsi ntá bɛyǎ bǒbhɔ.
Bɔ̌ma, mbák mmu ywɛká arɔ́ mbi Mandɛm anɛ́m ɛbhɨ, achák ánjá yí ámpɛtnsɛm.
Nɛ nɛyǐnwyɔp ndǔ Nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt, baghɔrɛ́ bhɔ básɔ́t bawɛrɛ́riɛp amɛn bɔ bághókó bárɔ́k ndǔ nnɛm Yesu nɛ nɛyǐnwyɔp.
Kɛ mbɔk yap báfá bárɔ́k ntá bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bághati bhɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu akʉ.
Ná nɛ nkwǎŋwaŋ mmu áchá ághɔ́ŋɔmɛn tontó? Ɛyɔ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ ɛbhé ɛyɛsɛ ɛ́pú káŋ mmu bɛkwak ntɨ ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt.”
Sɔt yɛ ka mpok! Nnáŋ ngati nɔ bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ambɨ ambɨ.
Ɛrɛmɛ́ ɛbyɔk ɛ́kwɛ́n, mbɔk batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm abhɛn báchí bǒnkwɔ Fárisi báfáte báre rɛm nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ bɛ, “Sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ ghɔ́ yɛ̌ ɛbɛ́ptí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mmǔ-nɛ ákʉ́. Ngufú ɛfóŋó kɛ ɛ́ghátí yi ɛnyɨŋ nɛ ngufu ángɛl kɛ árɛ́mɛ́ kɛpɨ nɛ yi!”
Mǔnti batɛmɛ́ nɛnu asɔt ɛká batɛmɛ́ nɛnu ɛyi, bárɔ́k, bákɛ́m Yesu bágwɔ́t. Babhabhɛrǐ ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm bábhák nɛ bhɔ.
Yɨŋɨ́ Ɛlísabɛt, mánɔ́ ywɛ ndu nnɛrɛkɛt. Yɛ̌ndu yi are kɔ́k nɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ yi bɛ́ nkongɔrɛ́, achí nɛ mɛniɛ ndǔ bataŋ átándát nɛ́nɛ, nɛ chɔŋ ambé mɔ́mbakanɛm.
Kɛ Pɔ̌l arɛm ntá bo mbɨ̌ŋ nkú bɛ, “Báway bhɛsɛ nɛ mantɛm bɛsí bho, mámɛsɛ bhɛsɛ́ ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ ɛnɛ́ bábhɨkɨ taŋ bhɛsɛ yɛ̌ndu sɛchi bǒ Rom. Nɛ́nɛ, báyàŋ sɛ́mfú sɛ́ndɔ́k bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́? Wáwák! Bɔ́ babhɔŋ bǒbatí bábhɔŋ bɛ́twɔ ndu mmʉɛt ɛyap mámfɛrɛ bhɛsɛ́.”
Kɛ mpok átwɔ̀ anɛ bo bhɔ bátè bɛsí Mandɛm ndǔ manyé bɛ mándɛm ɛnyu bákʉ́ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnap. Mandɛm até bɛ́taŋ bo abhɛn bachi pě nɛ bawú.
Ngɔ́ ɛrɛm ɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay mbɔ manyu. Ɛ́bhak mbɔ amaŋá nɛbu nɛ ɛ́nkɔt nɔkɔ ŋwaŋwǎŋwaŋ mbɔ glas anɛ ngó achi amɛm. Ngɔ́ bo abhɛn mánú nɛ nnya mbʉ́mbʉ nɛ ntíako yi nɛ mpǎy anɛ áté ndǔ nnyɛ́n nnya mbʉ́mbʉ, mánu basɔt awɔ́nɛm. Bǒbhɔ bátée angɔkɔ manyu wu nɛ bakɨ́ŋ anɛ Mandɛm áchyɛ́ bhɔ abhak bɔ amɔ́.
Akap anɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛ̌ti nɛka ɛnɛká nɛ Yesu chi nɛpɛmɛ yí ápɛ́mɛ́ bhe.
Sɛ́nsɔ́t bɛ́ bǒ bati apay bátwɔ ndǔ ɛchɛmɛ ɛyɛká. Amɔt ansɔbhɛri mmʉɛt nɛ ndɛn bɛyǎ nkáp nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ŋwaŋwǎŋwaŋ amʉɛt, nchɛ́bhɛ́mu nkwɔ́ antwɔ́ nɛ bɛsɨ́ ndɛn amʉɛt.
Yesu arɛm yɛ bɛ nchí ghati bhe bɛ bɔángɛl Mandɛm bábhɔŋ maŋák ɛ̌ti mmǔ bɛbʉ́ amɔt anɛ átɨ́kɨ́nsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhi.” 
Bágʉɛ́p yɛ ɛbhaŋa ɛ̌ti bǒbhɛn batí apay. Ɛ́ká Matías. Básɔ́t yɛ Matías báchɛm nɛ nkwɔ bǒnto Yesu bachak batí byó nɛ amɔt.”
Bɔangɛl tándrámɔt abhɛn bápɔ́kɔ́ bɛghori tándrámɔt amɔ báfú ndǔ ɛkɛrɛ́ Mandɛm ɛyɔ. Bábhák nɛ ndɛn pɛ́pɛ́p amʉɛt, nɛ *nkʉɛt ɛnɛ pú ambeápak.
Mandɛm Ɛtayɛsɛ nɛ Acha yɛsɛ Yesu Kristo mántɔ́ŋ be bɛrɨ̌ndu, mánchyɛ be kpák. 
Kʉ nɔ mbɔnyunɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ánɨkmʉɛt ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi áyàŋ, Mandɛm ǎchyɛ yi. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ áyàŋ ɛnyɨŋ, ǎghɔ yɔ. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ádɛ́bhɛ́ nɛkok, mánɛnɛ ntá yi.
Nɛ básɨŋ ndǔ bɛbhé Moses bɛ, “Mpok anɛ mpɔŋ ákʉ̀ bɛtɨk ɛbhɨ, bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ bɛ́gwɔ́t nnyu ywi bɛ́ ákɛ́ nyiɛ́ mbwɔt anɛ yɔ áyàti bɛ amfu ndu bɛkwɔp.” Mandɛm arɛm ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ chí ɛ̌ti mpɔŋ kɛ?
Nnɔ Yesu nɛ bɔ̌mayi bárɔk bɛghɔ yi. Kɛ bɔ́ kɛ kwáy bɛrɔŋ kɛkwɔt nɛ yi mbɔnyunɛ bo bayǎ nyaka bacha.
Yɛ̌ndu bárɛ̀m bɛ babhɔŋ kɛboŋ barɔp chi bɛchɨŋtǐ bho.
Mpok nɛ mpok, abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ bátì nyaka mánkɔrɛ nɔkɔ nkáp nɛ abhɛn ɛyap ɛ́pú ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap abhɔŋ ɛnyɨŋ.
Ntí abhak bɛ anáŋ abu nyaka bɛyǎ bǒmame. Bɛyǎ abhɛn bábhʉ́ɛt mɛme báré nu, mányirɛ nɔkɔ batɨ, bɛ mámbɔ́ŋ mbi bɛtɔk yi.
Bɔ́ bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Mbɔk bárɛ̀m bɛ ɔchí Jɔ̌n Njwiti. Bachak bɛ Ɛláija, nɛ abhɛnɛfu bɛ ɔchí ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ amɔt anɛ tɛ̌ nyaka kɛ ɔpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.”
Aghók ɛyɔŋ ndu ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Píta, faté, wáy nyìɛ.”
Mpok bábhɛ̀mɛ mmu, ɛrɛnɛ yi ɛ́bɛ̀p nɛ apú bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ. Mpok Mandɛm áku bawú mámpɛ́tnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, mmʉɛt ɛyɔ ǎrɨ, ambɔ́ŋ bɛtaŋ.
Básɨŋ amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm bɛ Acha arɛm bɛ, “Chɔŋ nsɔt bǒ bɛtɔk bɛchak abhɛn bárɛ̀m bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛbhɛn bǒbha bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ ndɛm kɛpɨ ntá yap. Yɛ̌ nɔ, bǒbha bápú tá chɔŋ batú bɛghok ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ́rɛ̀m.”
Árɛ́m nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, abhaka ntɨ bɛ ngufú chɔŋ Pɔ̌l anchyɛ yí bɛsɔŋ. Ɛkʉ are bhɨŋɨ yí mpok nɛ mpok andɛm nɔkɔ kɛpɨ nɛ yi.
Mandɛm anyú yɛ nku nɛ Ábraham. Ɛrɨŋɨ́ nku yɔ ɛbhak nɛsiɛ́p anɛ básiɛ̀p bɔ̌babhakanɛm. Ábraham abhé nɔ́kɔ́ yɛ Áisek, asiɛ́p yi mpok yi ágháká manywɔp ánɛn. Áisek ábhé Jekɔ́p, Jekɔ́p abhak chi ntá bɔ̌ bati byo nɛ apay abhɛn báchí nyaka bachǐmbɨ manɛrɛ́kɛt bo Israɛl.
Abhɛ́n ɛkɔŋ, tɛ̌ndu mánòŋ yɛ bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛmfakari, fyɛ́ ká bɛtaŋ ndu bɛkʉ Mandɛm angɔ bɛ bǎchi pɛ́pɛ́p, kɛbhɔ́ŋ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́, nɛ bɛ bɛsí Mandɛm kpák achi nɛ bhe.
Nɛ sɛ́yàŋ bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka ándɔ́k ambɨ bɛtɔŋ nkúbhɛ́ ntɨ ɛnɔ tɛ ndǔ ngwɛnti, nɛ bǎpú nɔ́k chɔŋ bɛbhɔŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎbhaka ntɨ bɛ chɔŋ mǎmbɔŋ.
Yi ɛ́kʉ̀ be bho bǎrɛm bɛ́ bǎchí bǒ Mandɛm mǎnù mǎntáŋ nɔkɔ nɛ batɨ? Pú bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎfyɛ́ ngoŋo arɛ́ kɛ bɛ́kʉ̀ mǎnu mpoknkɛm-ɛ?
Mpú rɔ bɛ́chyɛ bakak ntá Mandɛm mpoknkɛm ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhɛn yi átɔ́ŋɔ́ bé ndǔ bǎbhàt mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Kristo.
Yesu arɔk atú Seséria Fílipi nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi. Arɛ́, abhɛp bhɔ bɛ, “Bo bárɛ̀m bɛ́ Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm nchí agha?”
Yesu arɔk achwe amɛm áchwí nɛ bakoŋo bhi ndu bɛ́pe bɛrɔŋ ɛbhě manyu ɛchak.
Bághɔkɔntɨk bɛ́ Mandɛm aghókó mfay tɛ́ntɛp chi nɛ ɛyɔŋɔ́nyu ɛyi, akʉ mmɨk afú ndǔ manyiɛp amɛn achi nyaka mbǎnkɛm. Nɛ manyiɛp kɛ yi ásɔ́rɛ́ ághókó mmɨk.
Mpok yɔ kɛ mbyaká bɛbhé Mandɛm wu abhesi, kɛ Yesu Acha ánáŋ ántwɔ́, ǎfɛp chi ɛ̌yu, ɛyi ɛ́may. Mbɔ̌ŋ nɛtwɔ Yesu ǎnaŋa bɛtaŋ ɛbhi.
Bǎkɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk bɛ mpok bɛjɛt ntiɛt, bɛyǎ bo bájɛ̀t, kɛ ndiɛrɛ mmu anɛ ájɛ́rɛ́ áchá batɨ kɛ̌ ábhɔ̀ŋ akap. Nchí ghati yɛ bhe bɛ́ mamfyɛ́ bɛtaŋ bɛjɛ́t ntiɛt ɛnyu ɛnɛ bákway bɛ́bhɔ́ŋ akap.
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Mɛ kɛ nchí mbɔ̌ŋ nnɛrɛ́nɔk, nɛ Ɛtaya achi nkwaŋankɨ.
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu ábhʉɛ́t bɛ́rɛm kɛpɨ nɛ ngɔrɛ́ wu, mǔnto achwɔp anɛ áfú ɛkɛt ɛnɛ Jáyrɔs mǔnti arɛm ntá yí bɛ, “Mɔ́ywɛ agu. Ɔ́kɛ́pɛrɛ sɔŋɔri Ntɔŋ.”
Nɛka ɛnɛn Sará ngɔrɛ́ Ábraham kɛ nɛ́kʉ́ yi ákway nyaka bɛ́pɔ́kɔ mɛniɛ, yɛ̌ndu mamiɛ yi ánáŋ acha nyaka anɛ́ ngɔrɛ́ anɛ akway bɛpɔkɔ mɛniɛ. Ɛ́bhak ɛnyu yɔ mbɔnyunɛ anókó nyaka bɛ Mandɛm achi Mmǔ tɛtɛp, nɛ ǎbhʉ̀rɛ bariɛp ami.
Mpok Yesu aghoko bɛ bákɛ́m Jɔ̌n Njwiti báfyɛ ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ, afa atú Judɛ́ya apɛtnsɛm atú Gálili.
Bǎbhɔŋ bɛkɔŋ bo ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛka nɛnkɛm nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Kristo ákɔ́ŋɔ́ bhɛsɛ nɛ áchyɛ́ nɛpɛ́m ɛni ɛ̌ti yɛsɛ. Áchyɛ́ mmʉɛt mbɔ akabhɛ́nya anɛ áchyɛ́ Mandɛm bɛyǎ maŋák.
Ngɔrɛ́ Samária wu akɛmɛ Yesu bɛ, “Wɔ, ɔchí mmu Ju, atú Judɛ́ya, mɛ mbák ngɔrɛ́ atú Samária, ɛkɔ ná kɛ ɔ̌rɛm bɛ nchyɛ́ wɔ manyiɛp ɔ́nyú. Bǒ Judeya bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛkʉ nɛ bhɛsɛ bo Samaria!”
Mbák Mandɛm achyɛ́ mmu akap bɛkwak bho, ánkwák bho. Mbák chí akap bɛtɔŋ bho, ántɔ́ŋ bho.
Mpok nchí awu, nkʉ ntɨ ɛna bɛ́ mpú yáŋ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛchak, ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́fʉɛt chi bɛrɛm ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo nɛ, sayri sayri ɛ̌ti nɛwú ɛnɛn yí ágú amfay ɛkotákátí.
Sɔt ka mpok bɛ yɛ̌ mmu ákɛ́ sɔt nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnɛn bǒ mmɨk nɛ sɛ́rwɔrɛ́nyu andwɔ be mǎmbák basɛm ntá mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ bátɔ̀ŋ be. Ɛnyǔ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnɔ nɛ́fù chi ndǔ nkaysi bakwǎŋwaŋ nɛ ntá bɛfóŋó ɛbhɛn bɛbhɔŋɔ bɛtaŋ fá amɨk, nɛ́pú fu ntá Kristo.
Bɔ̌ma, nkɔŋ be tontó nɛ mbɔ̌ŋ bɛyǎ ɛkwak bɛghɔ bhe mbɔnyunɛ be kɛ̌ bǎchí maŋák ama, nɛ be kɛ̌ bǎchí nsáy bɛtɨk ɛbha. Tě yɛka kpirí, mǎnkʉ nɔkɔ mbɔ ɛnyu ngátí be bho bǎbhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu.
Jems nɛ Jɔ̌n, batɨ̌ bawáy nsi, bábhák nkwɔ́ maknkay. Báchí nyaka bɔ̌ Sɛbɛdi. Yesu arɛm ntá Símun bɛ, “Kɛ́cháy. Bɛbho ɛchɔŋ ɔrɔbhɛ ya chí bo bɛ mantwɔ ntá ya.”
Ngók ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ. Ɛ́fú ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ ɛndɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Ghɔ́ ká, bɛchɔ́kɔ́ Mandɛm bɛchi nɛntɨ bǒbhi. Chɔŋ yi ambak nɛ bhɔ́, nɛ bɔ́ mámbak bǒbhi. Nɛ chɔŋ mbɔŋ Mandɛm ambak nɛ bhɔ.
Mǔnti wu ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ bo bárɛ̀m ɛ̌ti Yesu, ató bǒbati bǒ Israɛl bɛ mánɨ́kmʉɛt nta yi bɛ ándɔ́k ámbú mǔbɛtok aywi.
kɛ báji yi ɛ̌ti bɛbʉ́ ɛbhi. Ɛkʉ mpɔŋɔ batu anɛ apu rɛm kɛpɨ arɛm kɛpɨ ntá yi nɛ ɛyɔŋɔ́ nkwǎŋwaŋ, akʉ yi andɔ ɛbhokori ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ákʉ̀ nyaka.
Árɛ́m nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, asɔt Píta nɛ bɔ̌ Sɛbɛdi bati apay, arɔk nɛ bhɔ. Arɔp nsónso nɛ bɛyǎ basɛ́mɛ́ antɨ.
Agha ákway bɛfɛrɛ bhɛsɛ ndǔ ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ Kristo ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ bhɛsɛ? Chi nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛ́táŋá kɛ chi ɛsɔŋɔri? Chi nɛnyok ɛnɛn báchyɛ̀ bhɛsɛ kɛ chi nsay? Chi nchɛ́bhɛ́ ndɛn kɛ nɛpá anɛ bɔ bápà bhɛsɛ kɛ chi nɛwáy anɛ bo báyaŋ bɛway bhɛsɛ?
Mpok ɛyɔ chɔŋ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ántɔ́ŋ be ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛrɛm.” 
Ntí anɛ ndɔ́ wɔ Krɛt chí bɛ ɔ́nyábhɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́rɔ́bhɛ́ mɛ́nyábhɛ arɛ́, nɛ bɛ ɔ́mfyɛ́ bǒ batí bɛkɛrɛ́ Mandɛm ndu yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛtɔkɔ́ Krɛt. Kʉ nɔ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔnyu ngátí wɔ.
Bɔ̌ma, mpɛt nchí ghati bhe bɛ mǎnsɔt ɛyɔŋ ɛya ɛnɛ nsɨ́ŋɨ́ ndu bɛ́fyɛ bhe ntɨ nɛ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ. Mbɨ́kɨ́ sɨŋ ɛrɔ́rí ɛkáti.
Yesu arɛm nɔ ndu mɛmɔ Fílip mbɔnyunɛ yímbɔŋ árɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ.
Ngɔrɛ́ wu arɔ ɛtě manyiɛp ɛyi, arɔk ɛtɔk téé, abho bɛ́gháti bho bɛ,
Ǎkʉ nɔ bɛ bo mankɛm mánchyɛ́ Mmɛ Mɔ́ywi kɛnókó nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ báchyɛ̀ yi kɛnókó. Mmǔ anɛ apu chyɛ Mmɛ Mɔ́ywi kɛnókó, apú chyɛ kɛnókó ntá Ɛtaya mmu ato mɛ.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Yɨŋɨ́ ká, nɛchwe anɛ bǎchwé ɛtɔk, chɔŋ mǎngɔ́ mmu anɛ ápɔ́kɔ́ ɛjɔ̌ manyiɛp. Koŋó ká yi kpátɛ ɛkɛt ɛnɛ́ yi áchwe,
Bɛyǎ bhap babhɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ. Bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bhɔ bɛ́fú bɛyǎ bho amʉɛt mɛ́mbɨkɨ nɔkɔ bɛ́, “Wɔ ɔchí Mmɔ Mandɛm!” Kɛ Yesu are sáy bhɔ, kɛka mɛ́ndɛm yɛ̌nyɨŋ, mbɔnyunɛ bɛ́rɨŋɨ nyaka bɛ yi achi Mpɛmɛ anɛ Mandɛm átó. 
Sɛ́nɨkmʉɛt bɛ Mandɛm Ɛtayɛsɛ yímbɔŋ nɛ Yesu Kristo Acha mánkʉ sɛ́ntwɔ ntá yɛka.
Báchí mbɔ bɔ̌ abhɛn báchɔ́kɔ́ nɛfí ɛsiɛ́. Kɛ mbɔk mámbɨŋɨ nɔkɔ abhɛnɛfu bɛ, ‘Sɛ́kwǎy bakwáy nɛbhay bɛ mǎmbɛn nɛbhɛ́n, kɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ bhɛn. Sɛ́kwáy bakwáy nɛwú, kɛbhɔ bě kɛdi!’
Kɛ Píta asɔt yi nɛpak, abho bɛji yi bɛ, “Acha, Mandɛm ákɛ́ ka! Awǔ ndak ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛfakari nɛ wɔ!”
Bɛtɨk Yesu Acha ɛbhɛ́n bo Mandɛm bákwày bɛkʉ bɛ́chí mɛnyu nɛ mɛnyu kɛ Acha ɛrɛ amɔt kɛ sɛ́kʉ̀ bɛtɨk ɛbhi.
Kɛ bárɔ́ŋ nɔ́kɔ́ bɛku amap bawɛt, mbǎyngɔrɛ́ achwɔp, asɔt abhɛn bati atay, abhɛn ɛbhap bɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́dù, achwe amɛm ɛpǎ nɛbhay nɛ bhɔ́. Bakʉ̌-bɛtɨk báya nɛkok batiɛp.
Bák ká nɔ mbɔnyunɛ tɛ̌ndu Mandɛm áfɛ́rɛ́ nyaka mbɔ̌ŋ batábhɛ́nɔk ɛnɛ bapɨ, chɔŋ amfɛrɛ be bho bábhárɛ́bhat nkwɔ mbák bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ noko.
Jɔ̌n kɛ achi mǔntó anɛ basɨŋ nyaka amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ̌ti yi bɛ, Mandɛm arɛm bɛ, ‘Yɨŋɨ́, chɔŋ ntó mpɔkɔntó wa wɔ ambɨ, bɛ ángókó mbi ywɛ kɛ ɔ́ntwɔ.’
“Nchí ghati wɔ, faté pɔkɔ́ bɛkpaka bhɛ gurɛ!”
Abhɛn ɛkɔŋ, tɛ̌ndu bǎrɨ́ŋɨ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ambɨ ambɨ, sɔt ka mpok bɛ́ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bo abhɛn bápú bhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé bɛ́kɛ́ pɔkɔ́ bhe mǎndɔp chi bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ te kpirí.
Nɛ bɛkɔŋ Mandɛm Acha ywɛ nɛ ntɨ ɛnɛ nɛnkɛm, nɛ nkaysi yɛ nkɛm, nɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛ mɛnkɛm, nɛ bɛ́ nkɔŋ ntɨ nkwǎ mbɔ ɛnyu ɔ́kɔ́ŋɔ́ mmʉɛt ɛyɛ arɨ acha. Bɛsí Mandɛm, bɛbhʉrɛ bɛbhé ɛbhɛn bɛpay achá akabhɛ́ nya bɛsɔŋ ankɛm nɛ akap achak anɛ bo báchyɛ̀ ntá yi”
Mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ batú ángók ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm ághàti bɛká bǒnkwɔ.” 
Bák ká mbɔ bɔ̌-bɛtok abhɛn mánòŋ bɛ chi-bɛtɨk awap amfu ndǔ ɛpǎ nɛbhay ɛnɛ yi árɔ́ŋɔ́ arɛ ampɛtnsɛm bɛ mánɛ́nɛ́ mbǐnywɔp ntá yi tɛ́mté, mpok yi átwɔ́ ádɛ́bhɛ́ nɛkok.
Yɛ̌ chí bɛ́ká nɛwú ka bɛ ntɛmsi Mandɛm ambak nɛ mɛ, nɛ bɛ yi amfap mɛ nɛ Kristo mbák ɛyɔ ɛ́kway bɛkwak bɔ mánókó Kristo.
Manɔ́, kʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ntá ya ndu nnyɛ́n Yesu Acha. Kʉ mbɔ ntɨ mmǔ Kristo bɛ ntɨ nɛ́mpɔ́p mɛ amɛm.
Páílet abhɛp yi bɛ, “Nɔ ɔchí mfɔ?” Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Ɔrɛm bɛ mɛnchí mfɔ. Ɛ̌ti ɛyɔ kɛ bábhé mɛ, nɛ ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ ntwɔ fá amɨk bɛghati bho tɛtɛp Mandɛm. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ anɛ ákòŋo tɛtɛp Mandɛm, ǎta batú bɛ́ghok ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ̌rɛ̀m.”
: Mmǔ anɛ ánú ásɔ́rɛ́ awɔ́nɛm, nɛ árɔ̀ŋ ambɨ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ndɛmɛ tɛ ndu ngwɛnti, chɔŋ nchyɛ́ yi bɛtaŋ amfay bǒ bɛtɔkɔ́ mmɨk, nkubhɛ mbɔ ɛnyu Ɛtaya áchyɛ́ mɛ bɛtaŋ amfǎy yap, chɔŋ yí ankɛ́m kɛfɔ amfay yap nɛ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ ɛnɛ baghoko nɛ ɛse awɔ. Anchɔkɔti bhɔ mbɔ ɛnyu bádɛ̀p ɛtě ntɔp amɨk ɛ́nchɔkɔti. Chɔŋ nchyɛ́ yi nɛmbe ɛnɛn nɛyǐnywɔp ndu bɛtɔŋ bɛ anu asɔt awɔ́nɛm.
Yi kɛ áchyɛ́ nyaka maníɛ́ ntá bo Israɛl bɛ, “Ɛ́rɨ bɛ mmu amɔt ángú ɛ̌ti bo mankɛm.” 
Nɛ bo abhɛn yi áyábhɛ́, abhɨ́ŋɨ́ bhɔ nkwɔ. Nɛ akʉ bo abhɛn yi ábhɨ́ŋɨ́ mámbák chak bɛsí bhi, nɛ bo abhɛn yi akʉ mámbák chak, akʉ mámbɔ́ŋ mbi bɛbhak ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt kɛnókó yi nɛ yi. 
Kɛ mbák, sayri sayri, mɛ̌bòk bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ chi ndǔ bɛtaŋ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm, nɔ́ Mandɛm anaŋ achi nɛntɨ ɛnɛka mbɔ Mfɔ.
Chɔŋ yí andɛm bɛ Mandɛm apú yɛ̌nyɨŋ nɛ bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bo báchíɛ kɛnókó mbɔ Mandɛm ɛpú yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Yí ǎrɛm mbúrɛ́ bɛ achá Mandɛm nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ mɛnkɛm, andɔk kpát anchɔkɔ amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm andɛm bɛ yímbɔŋ achi Mandɛm.
Yɛ̌ nɔ, bɛyǎ bo abhɛn bághókó ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Píta nɛ Jɔ̌n bághátí bhɔ, mánóko. Mpǎy bakoŋo Yesu mankɛm akó aghaka mbɔ nká ɛtay.
Mɔ́ngo anɛ áfù ndǔ ngó anɛ mmu wu achi amɛm apú may. Bo abhɛn báchyɛ̀ nnya mbʉ́mbʉ nɛ ntíako yi kɛnókó nɛ báka bɛ mámfyɛ́ ɛrɨ̌ŋ nnya yɔ bɔ amʉɛt bápú bhɔŋ chɔŋ nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛyap bɛti nɛ ngósí.”
Báfá báre kɔ bɛtɔk nɛ bɛtɔk mángati nɔkɔ bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ nɛ mámbu nɔkɔ bǒmame yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak. 
Bɔ̌bha, mpú pɛrɛ tat nɛ bhe. Chɔŋ mǎnjáŋ mɛ, kɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ngátí nyaka bǒbati bo Israɛl, nchí ghati bhe nɛ́nɛ bɛ, ‘Ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ mɛ̌rɔ̀ŋ, bǎpú kwáy bɛ́twɔ arɛ́’.
Bɛsɛ́ babhɔŋ sɛ́rɨŋɨ yɛ nɛ sɛ́nókó bɛ Mandɛm akɔŋ bhɛsɛ tontó. Mandɛm chi Mmǔ ɛkɔŋ, nɛ mmu anɛ ákɔ̀ŋ batɨ ǎbhɔŋ nɛbharɛ́mʉɛt nɛ Mandɛm nɛ Mandɛm ǎbhatmʉɛt nɛ yí.
Ate kɛ́kwɔ́t nɛ Yesu andi nɔkɔ kɛbhɔ. Babhɛsɛ mi are chɨtí bɛkak Yesu. Atɛp ntí amɨk antɛsɛ nɔkɔ bɛkak Yesu nɛ ɛmɛnɛ́nti yi, angwati nɔkɔ nɛ bawɛrɛ́riɛp.
Yesu aghati yi bɛ, “Mbák ɔ̌yáŋ ɔmbak chak ndǔ babhi ankɛm, dɔ́k tí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ mɛnkɛm, chyɛ̌ nkáp ntá bachɛ́bhɛ́bho. Mbák ɔ́nkʉ́ nɔ, chɔŋ ɔ́mbɔŋ kɛfɔ̌ mɛnyɨŋ amfay. Ɔ́ntwɔ́ yɛ ɔnkoŋo mɛ.”
“Bǎrɨ́ŋɨ́ ndǔ ɛbhé Moses ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Mmu abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛkwɛn bɛrwɔp.’
Mandɛm kɛ̌ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ bɛ́táŋ bo nɛfí, nɛ chɔŋ yí antáŋ bɔ́. Kɛ ɛ́mbák chí bhe bǒ nkwɔ́ Yesu, mankʉ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Bǎbhɔŋ bɛ́fɛ́rɛ mmu anɛ ákʉ̀ bɛbʉ́ ndǔ nkwɔ́ ywɛká.”
Bɔ̌ma, ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ ɛchi nɛ bhe. Ɛbhé ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ bhɔ́ŋ bɛtaŋ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛka mbɔnyunɛ, bɛyɨŋɨ ɛbhé, bǎgú nyaka nɛ Kristo mpok yi agu ndǔ ɛkotákátí. Nɛ́nɛ, bǎbhat mmʉɛt nɛ mmu anɛ Mandɛm ákʉ́ yi apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m bɛ ankʉ bhɛsɛ sɛ́mbák bo abhɛn sɛ́kʉ̀ bɛrɨ ndǔ bɛtok Mandɛm.
Bɛyǎ ndɔŋ ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ yɔ ɛ́kʉ̀ yi ankwɛ́n ango. Mpokófu ɛ́kʉ yi ankwɛn anyɛ́n ndu bɛway yi. Mbák ɔ̌kway bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ, ghɔ bhɛsɛ́ ntínso kwak bhɛsɛ́.”
