Kɛ mbɔk bo Israɛl bábhɔŋ mpabhamɨ́k nɛ bɔPɔ̌l. Manyokoti bo abhɛn bághabhɛ ghap nɛ bákʉ bo mángʉ́ɛ́p ɛbyɔk ɛtɔk. Bárɔ́k bádákáti babhǐnywɔp báchwe amɛm ɛkɛt ɛnɛ mmu anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ Jáson ndu bɛyaŋ Pɔ̌l nɛ Sáilas bɛ mánsɔt bhɔ mandɔk ndǔ nchɛmti bo abhɛn bachi nɛfí.
Mbɨ́kɨ́ yaŋ bɛ́chɔ́ŋti mpok ayɛ tontó, nchí nɨk chi mmʉɛt bɛ ɔ́nsɛ́bhɛ́ ntɨ ɛnɛ́ amɨk ɔ́ngɔ́k mbɨŋɨ́ ndak anɛ́ sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛghati wɔ.
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu ányìɛ nɛnyíɛ́ arɛ́, ngɔrɛ́ amɔt arɔk ntá yi nɛ bawɛrɛ́riɛp amɛn áré ya nkáp amɛm mɔɛ́nyɨŋɨ́fú. Bághókó nyaka mɔ́kpɛ́mɛ́ wu nɛ ɛnyǔ ntay ɛnɛn bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ alabásta. Ngɔrɛ́ wu atwɔ́ nɛ bawɛrɛ́ mɔ, atɛmti anti Yesu.
Bágháká nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ nyǔbha anɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ Ɛrɨ́tí Nyǔbha, bághɔ́ mmu anɛ áchí mbɛ́ntí tɛ nɛbhe ɛni arɛ́ chɔ́kɔ́. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛwak bo bápɔ̀kɔ nyaka yi mámbʉrɛ ndu nyǔbha wu bɛ́ ánɨ́ŋɨ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nkáp ntá bo abhɛn báfʉɛ̀t bɛrɔŋ amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm mɛnɨkmʉɛt.
Sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ Mandɛm apu ghok bǒ bɛbʉ́. Ǎghok chi mmu anɛ áchyɛ̀ yi kɛnókó, ankʉ nɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi Mandɛm áyàŋ.
Bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bápɛt bábhɛp yi ɛnyu ɛ́fákari kɛ yi ághɔ̀ mbaŋ. Aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Awátí ntɔp mɛ amɨ́k, nsó nɔ́kɔ́ bɛsí, mbo bɛghɔ mbaŋ.”
Nkoŋo Yesu achak arɔk ntá yi arɛm bɛ, “Acha, dɔ̌ kpɨ́k ndɔ́k mbɛ́mɛ́ Ɛtaya.”
Ɛ́fákári bɛ chi Pɔbliɔs achí amɨk bhʉrɛ ndǔ ámè. Abhɔ́ŋ mbʉ́ɛ́p nɛ mɔ́nɛ́m kɛbi. Pɔ̌l arɔk aghɔ yi. Ányáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ amɔ yi amʉɛt, anɨkmʉɛt ɛ̌ti yi. Ataŋ.
Bɔ̌ma, kɛ mbák chi bhe, bǎkɛ́ pɔp bɛ́kʉ bɛrɨ.
Mbák nchyɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhá mɛnkɛm ntá bho, nchyɛ́ yɛ̌ chí mmʉɛ́t ɛya bɛ mánsɔ́ŋ, kɛ nkɛ kɔŋ bo, ɛyɔ ɛpu kwák mɛ ndǔ yɛ̌ mbi.
“Nɨk mmʉɛt ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́yàŋ, chɔŋ Mandɛm anchyɛ wɔ. Yáŋ, chɔŋ ɔ́ngɔ. Dɛp nɛkok, chɔŋ mánɛnɛ ntá yɛ.
[Ɛnɛ́ yi ánɨ̀kmʉɛt nɔ, ángɛl Mandɛm abhesi yi bɛsí, afyɛ́ yi ntɨ.
Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, nchí ghati bhe bɛ, “Mmǔ anɛ árɔ́ yɛ̌ ɛkɛt, yɛ̌ ngɔrɛ́, yɛ̌ bɔ̌mayi, yɛ̌ ɛtayi nɛ máyi, nɛ yɛ̌ bɔ̌bhi ɛ̌ti Kɛfɔ Mandɛm,
Mpok achi nyaka anɛ básɔ̀kɔti, manchyɛ nɔkɔ bhe nɛnyok bɛsí bho. Mpok achak bǎre té ansɛm bǒ abhɛn báchyɛ bhɔ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnyu yɔ.
Ɛtaya akɔŋ mɛ mbɔnyunɛ nchí chyɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛna bɛ mpɛt mbɔŋ nɔ.
Bátwɔ́ yi nɛ ɛbhɔkɔ nkáp. Abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Ntí ághá nɛ́ arɛ́? Nɛ nnyɛ́n chi ɛnɛn ághá?” Bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Chí ntí Sísa, Mfɔ Rom. Nɛ nnyɛ́n, chi ɛni.”
Bɛsɛ́ babhɔŋ sɛ́pànyu ntá bǒnkwɔ Mandɛm báchák ɛ̌ti yɛka, ndǔ bǎté kpirí ndǔ nɛka ɛnɛka nɛ Yesu, yɛ̌ndu bo báchyɛ̀ bhe nɛnyok nɛ bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri.
Mpok yɔ, chɔŋ bo abhɛn báchí chák bɛsí Mandɛm mankɛmɛ yi bɛ ‘Acha, ntɨkɨ mpok sɛ́ghɔ́ bɛ́ nsay ǎnu wɔ, sɛ́chíɛ wɔ nɛnyíɛ́? Ntɨkɨ mpǒk manyiɛp ákwàk wɔ kɛ sɛ́chíɛ wɔ manyiɛp ɔ́nyú?
Fɛrɛ́ yɛ́ ka bɛbʉ́ bhɔ amʉɛt, bɛ́ bɛ́kɛ́ go mɛntaka ndǔ nkwɔ ywɛka. Fɛrɛ́ ká bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɔ bɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ ywɛka ambak pɛ́pɛ́p nɛ ntɨ nɛmɔt. Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ nɛwú Yesu ndǔ ɛkotákátí nɛ́kʉ bakoŋo Yesu bǎrɔp chi pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí Mandɛm. Yí Kristo, achí mbɔ mɔ́nkwɔmɛn anɛ bo Israɛl básɔ̀t nyaka manchyɛ mbɔ akap ntá Mandɛm ndǔ mpok anɛ mányìɛ Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ.
Mbák chí manɔ ywɛsɛ Apólos, ngátí yi bɛyǎ mpok bɛ ántwɔ́ awu nɛ bǒnkwɔ bachak mángɔ bhe, kɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ ka bɛ́twɔ nɛ́nɛ. Chɔŋ antwɔ́ mpok yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛpok. 
Ɛ́kʉ́ Yesu abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Bě nkwɔ́ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́re jwimɛm ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ́rɛ̀mɛ?
Barɛm bɛ sɛnsɔt   áchwí sɛndɔk Itali. Básɔt yɛ Pɔ̌l nɛ mbɔk bǒkɛnɔŋ báchyɛ́ ntá Juliɔs mǔnti ɛká batɛmɛ́ nɛnu ɛnɛ babhɨŋɨ bɛ ɛká batɛmɛ́ nɛnu Mfɔ Rom.
Kɛ mbák nchí kʉ chi bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mpu yaŋ bɛkʉ, ɛyɔ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ, sayri sayri, puyɛ̌ chi mɛ kɛ nchí kʉ bɔ, chí bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛn bɛchi mɛ antɨ.
Mmu anɛ ányìɛ nyamwʉɛ́t ya nɛ anyú manoŋ ma, achí babhát nɛ mɛ, nɛ mɛ nkwɔ́ nchí babhat nɛ yi.
Ábraham anaŋ aghaka nyaka mbɔ mamiɛ́ bɛsa bɛtay () nɛ arɔbhɛ sɔt mmʉɛt chi mbɔ ngú, nɛ árɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ ngɔrɛ́ ywi Sará achi nkongɔrɛ́. Yɛ̌ nɔ, ate kpirí ndǔ nɛka ɛni nɛ Mandɛm, anoŋ nɔkɔ bɛ Mandɛm ankʉ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi árɛ́mɛ́.
Bǒ abhɛn bachi arɛ́, bárɛ́m bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti yi, nɛ babhak maknkay ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ́tí kɛpɨ ɛkɛn kɛ́fú yi anyu. Kɛ bábho bɛbhɛp bɛ, “Pú mmɔ̌ Josɛ́f nɛ?”
Ɛchi mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́ghàti bhɛsɛ bɛ, “Mmǔ anɛ ápɔ́kɔ́ bɛyǎ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn nɛ́fú amfay ntá Mandɛm, ǎnyiɛ nyaka yɛ̌nyɨŋ kɛrɔp, anɛ ápɔ́kɔ́ chi mandú abhɔ́ŋ ɛnɛn nɛkwáy yi gbák.”   
Yesu apɛt arɛm bɛ, “Ntwɔ bɛgʉɛp chi ngó fá amɨk. Mbɔ ánaŋ akɛm, mbʉ nkɔŋ tontó!
Ɛkɔŋ ɛchak ɛ́pú ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chá ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ́ mmu ánchyɛ́ nɛpɛ́m ɛni ɛ̌ti mamʉɛrɛ bhi.
Bǎfyɛ̀ bɛtaŋ bɛpay Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm mbɔnyunɛ bǎkáysí bɛ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ be mbi nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti nɛ yɔ́ ɛ́rɛ̀m chi ɛ̌ti ya.
Fíɛ́ ká bɛtaŋ ndu bɛkʉ bɛtɨk, bǎkɛ́ bhak babhɔt. Kʉ ka bɛtɨk Yesu Acha nɛ batɨ ayɛka ankɛm.
Asɔt yɛ ɛkpɔkɔ́ brɛd. Achyɛ bakak ntá Mandɛm. Are bɔkɔti anchyɛ nɔkɔ ntá baghɔkɔ́ bhi, andɛm nɔkɔ bɛ, “Brɛt-nɛ até ndǔ mmʉɛt ɛya anɛ nchí chyɛ mbɔ akap ɛ̌ti yɛka. Mǎndɔp, mǎnkʉ nɔkɔ ɛnyunɛ ndu bɛ́tɨk mɛ.”
Nɛ ndǔ bɛyǎ basɛmɛ, are nɨkmʉɛt nɛ ntɨ ɛni nɛnkɛm. Nsɔ́ŋtí anɛ áfú yi amʉɛt are chɨti amɨk mbɔ bakɔŋ manoŋ.]
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ́yàŋ be mǎndɨŋɨ chí bɛ mmɔ́ anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛ́nyiɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛ́táyi achi ɛnyu ɛ́mɔt nɛ nsɛm mpok yi abhʉɛ́t chí mɔ́nkwɛn, yɛ̌ndu mɛnyɨŋ ɛ́táyi mɛnkɛm chí ɛbhi.
Mbák mmú ámbɛ́p be ntí anɛ bǎkàŋari yɔ́, ghati ka yí bɛ, ‘Acha kɛ áyàŋ yɔ.’”
Sɛ́kwáy mbɔŋ bɛ́rɛm bɛ Lɛ́vi mmu bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ bhi básɔt ɛnyǔ akap wu ntá bho, achyɛ́ nyaka ɛnyǔ akap wu ntá Mɛlkísɛdɛk tɛ̌ndu chi-mbɨ ywi Ábraham áchyɛ́ nyaka wu ntá Mɛlkísɛdɛk.
Bǒnto bárɨŋɨ nɔ́kɔ́ nkaysi yap, bábʉɛ́ bárɔk atú Likáonia, ndu bɛtɔk Lístra nɛ Dɛ́be nɛ mbaŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi kɛkwɔt arɛ,
Pɔ̌l akɛmɛ bɛ, “Bɔ̌ma, mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mbʉ bɛ chi mǔngo bachiǎkap. Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Ɔ́kɛ́rɛm ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti mǔnti bǒbhɛ.’”
Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́pɛt ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Chɔŋ mánkpʉɛp wɔ nɛ amɔ yap, bɛ́ ɔ́kɛ́ tɛm ɛkak ndǔ ntay.’”
Ngɛ́mtay bo abhɛn báchɛ́mɛ́ nyaka arɛ ndu bɛghɔ, bághɔ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛfakari. Bágúrɛ nɛ basɛ́mɛ́, mámbyaka nɔkɔ amɔ antɨ.
Nɛ yɛ̌ ɛ́mbak bɛ yi, chyɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ká Mandɛm bakak, tɛ̌ndu mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm chi ɛbhɛn yi áyàŋ mǎnkʉ́ ndǔ bǎchí bo Yesu Kristo.
Bágháká nɔ́kɔ́ Kapɛ̌naum, báchwe anywɔ́p. Ɛnɛ́ bachi arɛ́, Yesu abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Bǎkɛ̀m mbʉ ɛpʉ́ítí ambi ɛ̌ti yi?”
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́rɨ ntá mmu anɛ ntɨ ɛni nɛ́chi pɛ́pɛ́p, kɛ ntá mmu anɛ ntɨ ɛni nɛ́pú pɛ́pɛ́p nɛ abhɨkɨ noko Yesu, ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́rɨrɨ ɛpu. Bɛ́rɛm tɛtɛp, nkaysi yap nɛ batɨ̌ yap ánáŋ áchɔ́ŋɔ amɛm.
Sɛ́bhɔ̀ŋ maŋák mbák bǎtaŋ, yɛ ɛ́mbak chi bɛ sɛbhɨkɨ taŋ. Sɛ́nɨ̀kmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm bɛ nɛka ɛnɛka nɛ́ngó nɛnjwi pɔɔt.
Bɔ́ babhɔŋ kɛ bághɔ́ bɛ ɛrɨ bɛkʉ nɔ, nɛ sayri sayri, bábhɔŋ bɛkʉ nɔ tɛ̌ndu ɛchi bɛ, ɛ̌ti bo Israɛl bo báchí bo Mandɛm kɛ bǒ abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl bághókó Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu. Nɛ báchí nkwɔ bo Mandɛm nɛ́nɛ, nɛ Mandɛm ǎyɛ̀t bhɔ nɛ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ. Bábhɔŋ yɛ bɛkwak bo Israɛl abhɛn bachi bachɛ́bhɛ́bho nɛ mbɔk mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́.
Kɛ bɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ̌yàŋ bɛghati bhe nɛ́nɛ, mpú bɨti bhe mbɔnyunɛ mpok anɛ bǎchɛm nɛbhʉɛt amɔt ndu mɛnɨkmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm bǎpú kʉ nɔ chí ndu bɛ́ghóko, bǎchɔ̀ŋti chɔ́ŋti.
Achwe amɛm ɛkɛt Mandɛm, apɔkɔ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn báchyɛ́ mbɔ akap ntá Mandɛm akɔrɛ nɛ bɔ̌bhi mányíɛ́. Ɛbhé ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ ndiɛrɛ bachiǎkap Mandɛm kɛ bákway mɛnyiɛ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɔ.”
Baghɔsɔŋ bhɔ mankɛm bácháyti, maŋɛmɛ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap abho bɛ́kósi nnɨk-ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ ywi.
Mpok yɔ, Ábraham anáŋ akɔk nyaka tontó, ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ yi apu pɛrɛ kway bɛbhɔŋ bɔ. Yɛ̌ nɔ, bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ bhi báyá kpát mbɔ mambě mfay nɛ mbɔ ɛ̌siɛ́p ɛnɛ ɛchi angɔkɔnyɛ́n ɛnyu ɛnɛ yɛ̌ mmu apu kway bɛpay bhɔ.
Yi ɛ́kwày bɛchyɛ mɛ maŋák ɛ́ncha bɛghok bɛ bɔ̌bha bákòŋo tɛtɛp Mandɛm? 
Barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ nsé bachi mbɔ mɛnɔk ɛbhɛn bɛpu nyu bɛrɨ́tí kɛpɛm. Bǎrɨŋɨ bhɔ chi ndǔ bɛpɨŋ ɛbhap.” 
Ɛ́mbák chí nɔ́ mbɔnyunɛ mpok manyé akway, nɛ ábho chi ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt Mandɛm. Nɛ mbák ámbó nɛ bhɛsɛ, chɔŋ ɛ́mbak ná nɛ bo abhɛn bápú koŋo Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm?
Kɛ bɔ́ kɛbhɔ́ŋ mbi anɛ báfʉɛt mǎnchwe anywɔ́p ɛ̌ti bɛyǎ bho. Báko amfay ɛkɛt mánɛnɛ mbok arɛ́, básɛbhɛ yi bhʉɛrɛ ndǔ bɛkpaka bhi nɛntɨ bho, bɛsí Yesu.
Nywɔp nɛ́mɔt, Hɛródias abhɔ́ŋ mbi. Hɛ́rɔd anak ɛpa ndǔ bɛtɨk nywɔbhɛ́ nɛbhe ɛni. Abhɨŋɨ manɛ́m bǒ ɛtɔk, nɛ bǒ bagho, nɛ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu, nɛ manɛ́m bo Gálili.
Chi mɔ́wu atɨk bɛ́ ndǔ nkúbhɛ́ nɛŋɔkɔ́ nywɔp ɛnɔ kɛ̌ Yesu ághati yi bɛ, “Mɔ́ywɛ apú gú.” Ɛ́kʉ́ mǔngo wu nɛ *ɛfo ɛyi ɛnkɛm mánóko Yesu.
Yesu asá awɔ tɛ́mté akɛm yi arɛm bɛ, “Píta, nɛka ɛnɛ nɛ́gʉpsi nɛcha! Ndaká yí ɔ́mákátí bɛ mɛ̌kwáy bɛkʉ wɔ ɔ́nkɔ amfǎnyɛn?”
Mpok bátɛ́mɛ́rí Yesu, mánɨ́k yi mmʉɛt bɛ ámbák nɛ bhɔ, nɛ abhak nɛ bhɔ́ ndǔ manywɔp apay.
Nɛ puyɛ̌ chi ndiɛrɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm ághókó kɛ bɛ́ghòk bɛbe, mɛ́ntoŋ nɔkɔ. Bɛsɛ́ babhɔŋ bo Mandɛm achyɛ́ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ mbɔ akap anɛ mbɨ anɛ́ átɔ̀ŋ bɛ chɔŋ sɛ́mbɔŋ kɛnɛ́m ɛkɛn kɛbhʉɛ́t ambɨ, sɛ́tòŋ nkwɔ, sɛnoŋ nɔkɔ bɛ Mandɛm ansɔt bɛsɛ amʉɛt mbɔ bɔ̌bhi. Nɔ chi bɛ anchyɛ bhɛsɛ mmʉɛ́t nkɔ.
Mpok Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n áfɛ́rɛ ɛ́bhánɛ́ ɛnɛ́ ɛjwi bɛpay, ngók ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛjwi bɛpay ndu ɛbhɛn mɛnwi ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Twɔ́!”
Abhɔ́ŋ manɔ anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ María. María arɔk asibhiri ndǔ bɛkak Acha angoko nɔkɔ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ɛnɛ yi átɔ̀ŋ;
Kɛ mbák mbɔk bho báchí ndǔ nkwɔ́ ywɛká abhɛn bápú kwáy bɛ́kɛ́m mmʉɛt, ɛ́rɨ bɛ́ mámbɔ́ŋ nɛbhay. Ɛ́rɨ bɛ́ bɔ́ mámbɔ́ŋ nɛbhay ɛcha bɛchɔkɔ nɔ, ɛkwaká kɛbhʉ́rɛ́ ɛ́ndu nɔkɔ bhɔ antɨ.
Pú ɔ̌ghati yi chi bɛ, ‘Dɔ́k wupsí ndɛn, kʉ nɛnyíɛ́ twɔ nɛ nɔ. Nnáŋ nnyiɛ́ nnáŋá, ɔ́nsɔt ɛnɛ ɔnyiɛ’?
Yesu arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Mma, ɔ̌di yi? Ɔ̌yàŋ agha?” Ndǔ María ákáysí bɛ́ chí mmu anɛ áyɨ̀ŋɨ nkɨ, arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Ɛta, mbák ɔ́fɛ́rɛ́ yi, ghatí mɛ́ ɛbhak ɛnɛ ɔ́bhʉ́rɛ́ yi bɛ́ ndɔ́k nsɔt yí.”
“Bǎkɛ́ sɔt kɛfɔ̌ nkáp nɛ kɛfɔ̌ mɛnyɨŋ bɛchak mǎmbʉrɛ fá amɨk. Fá amɨk, kɛngɔk nɛ mfárɛ́káŋ báchɔ̀ŋti, nɛ baghɛ́p báwày ɛkɛt mámpɔkɔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ.
Ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt bo Israɛl kɛ Yesu ányɔ́bhɛ́rí nyaka ntɔp awati yi amɨ́k, amɨ́k anɛnɛ yi.
Mmǔ wap amɔt agwɔp akparɛnja ywi. Akpɔ́t atú nsɛ̌m mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm chwát agʉɛ́p amɨk.
Bǎkɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk nkwɔ ɛtɔk Sódom nɛ ɛnɛ́ Gomóra nɛ bɛtɔk bɛ́chák ɛbhɛn bɛ́kókósí nyaka nɛ bhɔ. Bo bɛtɔk ɛbhɔ báchyɛ́ nyaka mmʉɛt ndǔ barak ɛpúsí nɛ bɛpɔ̌ baraká kɛbhʉ́rɛ́ áchák anɛ bakwǎŋwaŋ babhɨkɨ bhɔŋ bɛkʉ. Bɔ́ nkwɔ bachi ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri amɛm ngó anɛ apu nɛmɛ, nɛ ɛyɔ chí ɛrɨŋ ntá bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ noko Mandɛm.
Chɔŋ mfay amfʉɛt, mmɨk amfʉɛ́t, kɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛya ɛ́pú fʉɛt wáwák. 
Bɔ̌ma, bɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ nɛtwɔ́ Yesu Kristo Acha nɛ nɛnyokoti anɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛ́nyókóti bhɛsɛ bɛ sɛ́ntɛ́mɛ́rí yi, sɛ́ghàti bhe bɛ,
Barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ nɛ batɔŋ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm báchi nyaka ndǔ Nkwɔ Yesu abhɛn Antiɔk. Bábhak Banábas, nɛ Símiɔn anɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ́ Ɛgírímɔ, nɛ Lusiɔs anɛ áfú Sírene, nɛ Manáen anɛ áchí nyaka mmʉɛrɛ kɛmbɔ́ anɛ Mfɔ Hɛ́rɔd Ántipas, nɛ Sɔ̌l.
Bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Mmǔ-rɛ́ achí fá?” Akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ.” 
Ghók nɔ́kɔ́ ka bǒbati bhɛka, mǎmbɔ́ŋ nɛsɛptǐmʉɛt bɛsí bhap, mbɔnyunɛ bɔ kɛ báyɨ̀ŋɨ bhe, mbɔ bo abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́ghátí Mandɛm ɛnyu bɔ bákɛ́mɛ́ bhe. Ghók nɔ́kɔ́ ká bhɔ bɛ mánkʉ bɛtɨk ɛbhap nɛ maŋák, nɛ bɛ bɔ bákɛ́ bhɔŋ kɛsɔ́ti.
Nɛ mányìɛ̀ mɛnyɨŋ mánkwɛ́sɛ́ ndǔ mangwɔ, mánkʉ nɔkɔ bɛrɔ́rí nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt bɛsí bhó mbɔ bɛ bachi bɛrɨtí bho. Chɔŋ ntɛ́msí yap anjá ancha.”
Ɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ mamiɛ́ byo nɛ anwi, mpɛt nkó ndɔk Yerúsalɛm nɛ Banábas. Nsɔt Táytɔs sɛ́rɔ́k nɛ yi.
Nɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́ndɨ ɛncha mbɔnyunɛ mɛnyǔ bǒbhɔ bápú kway bɛkɛmɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́kʉ́ ntá yap. Kɛ Mandɛm ǎkap wɔ mpok yi ákʉ̀ bo abhɛn bachi chak bɛsí bhi mámpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.” 
Mankɔ bhɔ bápɛ́rɛ́ gurɛ, Mandɛm asɛmti bhɔ ndǔ kɛnɔ́ bɛ́ bákɛ́ pɛtnsɛm ntá Mfɔ Hɛ́rɔd. Báfʉɛ́t chí ndǔ mbi achak kɛ bágurɛ ɛtɔk ɛyap. 
Yɛ̌ndu nsɨ́ŋɨ́ yɛ be ɛkáti, mbɨ́kɨ́ sɨŋ chi bɛkʉ mǎndɨ́ŋɨ́ mmu anɛ ákʉ́ nɛfwɔp nɛ mmu anɛ bǎkʉ́ yi nɛfwɔp. Nsɨŋ chi ɛ̌ti bǎghɔ́ bɛsí Mandɛm, bɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋ ntɨ nɛ bhɛsɛ tontó.
Kɛ Píta akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Ɛghori ɛ́mpɔ́kɔ́ wɔ́ nɛ nkáp aywɛ! Ɔkáysí bɛ́ ɔ̌kwáy bɛ́ku akap Mandɛm nɛ nkáp na?
Kɛ Pɔ̌l kɛka. Ate chí bɛ́ mambabhɛri nɔkɔ yi kpatɛ Mfɔ Rom antáŋ nyé ɛni. Nchyɛ́ ɛyɔŋ bɛ mambabhɛri nɔkɔ yi kpatɛ mpok anɛ mɛ́tò yi ntá Mfɔ Rom.”
Yesu aghati yɛ bho mankɛm bɛ, “Mbák mmú ǎyàŋ bɛbhak nkoŋo wa, abhɔŋ bɛ́ghɔ́kɔntɨk mmʉɛt yi, ampɔkɔ ɛkotákátí yi yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nywɔp, ankoŋo mɛ,
Ngátí nɔ́ bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nɛ́nɛ ɛnɛ́ bɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ re fakari, nɛ ntí bɛ mɛ́náŋ mɛ́mfákárí, mǎnókó.
“Amɨ́k áchí ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ̀ mmu ángɔ mbaŋ. Mbák mmu abhɔŋ amɨ́k arɨarɨ, ǎghɔ andɨŋɨ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ákʉ̀.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ nsɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka bɛkʉ be mǎndɨ́ŋɨ́ chi bɛ́ bǎkɛ́ bhɔ́ŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛkʉ nɛ mmu anɛ árɛ̀m bɛ yí achi nkoŋo Yesu, yɛ̌ nɔ, ankʉ nɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋ mbɔ barak ɛpúsí, nɛ bɛ́fyɛ́ amɨ́k ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ bo báchák, nɛ bɛbhɔŋ bɔmandɛm báchák, nɛ bɛrɛm bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti bo báchák, nɛ yɛ̌ chí bɛbhak nyǔmɛ́m, nɛ bɛghɛp aghɛp. Yɛ̌ chí nɛnyíɛ́, bǎkɛ́ nyiɛ́ nɛ ɛnyǔ mmu wu.
Yesu árɨ́ŋɨ́ nɔkɔ nɔ, afa atú Judɛ́ya apɛt atú Gálili.
Yesu apɛtnsɛm ndǔ ɛbhě manyu ɛchak. Ndu yi áchí angɔkɔnyɛ́n téé, bɛyǎ bo bárɔ́k bákáp yi.
Tɛtɛ̌tɛp, mmǔ anɛ ághókó ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ̌rɛ̀m, anoko mmu anɛ átó mɛ, ǎbhɔ̀ŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti. Mandɛm apú rɛm bɛ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bɛchi nɛ yi. Afǔ ndǔ nɛwú, achwe ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.
Fʉɛ́t Troas sɔt nkú mbʉ̌ɛ́p ya anɛ ndɔ́ ntá Kápɔs. Sɔt bɛkáti ɛbha nkwɔ́, sayri sayri nkúbhɛ́ nnya nɛ́nɛ́p ɛnɛ́ básɨ́ŋɨ́ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm arɛ́.
Kɛ nchí ghati bhe bɛ, yɛ̌ agha anɛ afyɛ́ amɨ́k amʉɛt ngɔrɛ́, ambɔ́ŋ nkaysi bɛbhʉɛrɛ nɛ yi, anáŋ akwɛn bɛrwɔp nɛ ngɔrɛ́ wu ndǔ ntɨ ɛni.
Kɛ batɨ ábé bǒnkwɔ Fárisi nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé tontó. Bábhó bɛsokori ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bákway bɛkʉ Yesu. 
Kɛ ngátí bhe bɛ yɛ̌ndu bǎghɔ́ mɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ noko mɛ.
Kɛ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi báré rɛm chi bɛ, “Chí mfɔ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ kɛ̌ áchyɛ́ Yesu bɛtaŋ bɛ́bok bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ.”   
Ɛta, ɛnyu yɔ kɛ̌ wɔmbɔŋ ɔ́yáŋá bɛ ɛmbak.”
Ndaká yí ɔ́yɨ̀ŋɨ mɔ́ɛ̌nyɨŋɨ anɛ achi anyɛsɛ ntɨ, ɛnɛ́ ɔ́pú fyɛ nti ndǔ nkɔkɔ́nɔk anɛ achi wɔ anyɛsɛ?
Mbák Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm ákʉ̀ mánchyɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó, mbɔ̌ŋ Mandɛm ǎkʉ̀ bo mánchyɛ Mmu anɛ áfú ntá yi kɛnókó, nɛ chɔŋ ankʉ nɔ tɛ́mté.
Mfɔ wu abhɔ́ŋ bɛyǎ bɛběntɨ. Ató batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bhi bárɔ́k báwáy bǒbhɔ, básɔ́ŋ ɛtɔk ɛyap.
Pɔ̌l arɛm nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ bɛ, “Faté tě chak!” Afate kpɛrɛp abho bɛ́kɔ.
Chɔŋ sɛ́ndɛm yɛ bɛ yi ɛ̌ti Ábraham mmu achí chi-mbɨ ywɛsɛ?
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Nɛ ndaká yí bǎrɔ̀ bɛbhé Mandɛm, mǎnkoŋo nɔkɔ chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bachǐmbɨ bhɛka batɔŋɔ?
Sayri sayri, puyɛ̌ Yesu kɛ ájwìti nyaka bho, chí bakoŋo bhi.
Afate yɛ, apɛtnsɛm ntá baghɔkɔ́ bhi abhɛn bati arat. Aghɔ bhɔ ndu bábhʉ̀rɛ kɛnɔ́. Aŋɛmɛ bhɔ́ abhɛp Píta bɛ, “Símun, bǎbhʉrɛ chi kɛnɔ́? Bǎpú kwáy bɛ́chɔkɔ pě yɛ̌ chí ndǔ nɛŋɔkɔ́ nywɔp nɛ́mɔ́t-ɛ?”
Mpok bátɛ̀mti Stífin nɛ batay, anɨkmʉɛt bɛ, “Yesu Acha, sɔt Ɛfóŋó ɛya!”
Bɛyǎ bo Israɛl abhɛn bakoŋo María bághɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu ákʉ́, mánóko yi.
Yesu arɛm yɛ ntá mmu anɛ ábhɨ́ŋɨ́ yí ndǔ ɛpa nkwɔ bɛ, “Mpok ɔ́bhɨ́ŋɨ́ bho ndǔ nɛnyíɛ́, ɔ́kɛ́ bhɨŋɨ chi mamʉɛrɛ bhɛ, nɛ bǒnɛrɛ́kɛt ywɛ, nɛ bǒ nkáp abhɛn bachi kɛkwɔt nɛ wɔ. Mbák ɔ́mbɨ́ŋɨ́ chi mɛnyǔ bo bhɔ, bɔ́ nkwɔ́ bákway bɛbhɨŋɨ wɔ bɛ́ ɔ́nyíɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ bhɔ nɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́mbak akap anɛ ɔ́bhɔŋ.
Chi ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ bǎchyɛ̀ nkwɔ nkábhɛ́nti. Bǒbati bákʉ̀ chi bɛtɨk Mandɛm ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bɔ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ.
Mmu Mandɛm anɛ áchí nchɛ́bhɛ́ mmu, ámbɔ́ŋ maŋák bɛ́ Mandɛm akósí yí ndǔ ákʉ́ yí ámbák mmu ywi.
Bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ́ ndǔ ndɔŋ anɛ mbɨ, nɛme kɛ nɛkʉ ngati bhe Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́.
Mmu anɛ árɛ̀m bɛ́ abhat mmʉɛt nɛ Mandɛm, abhɔŋ bɛbhʉɛrɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛni mbɔ ɛnyǔ Yesu ákʉ̀ nyaka. 
‑ Mmǔ amɔt achí nyaka Yerúsalɛm mpok yɔ. Aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Josɛ́f. Achi nyaka mmǔ Arimátia, ɛtɔk bo Israɛl. Abhak ndɨ̌ndu nɛ mmǔ chak nɛ ǎnòŋ nyaka mpok anɛ Mandɛm abhak Mfɔ bho. Abhak mmǔ amɔt ndǔ ɛchɛmɛ ɛgho ɛnɛ bǒ batí ɛtɔk. Kɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ ka nyaka nɛ bhɔ ndǔ nkaysi yap nɛ nɛkʉ wap.
Bǒbhɔ bákɛ́m yɛ́ Yesu, bábhó bɛrɔŋ ndǔ ɛkɛt ɛnɛ mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm. Píta are koŋo bhɔ ansɛm nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ.
Nɛ chɔŋ batɔŋɔ́ nse bhɔ mánsɔt bɛyɔŋɔ́ nse ndu bɛrwɔ bhe bɛ mányiɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛka nɛ ngwáy yap. Mandɛm ánáŋ átàŋ bɔ tɛ mpok anɛ afʉɛrɛ ansɛm nɛ ɛrɔp chi bɛ mámbɔ́ŋ ntɛmsi yap.
Bák ká pě, mǎnte kpirí ndǔ nɛka ɛnɛka nɛ Yesu. Bɔ́ŋ ká nɛtaŋántɨ, mánte sɛnɛ́.
Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ beku, Yesu atwɔ́ nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bati byo nɛ apay báchɔkɔ mɛ́nyiɛ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛpǎ ɛyɔ.
Wɔ mmǔ bɛtábhá, fɛrɛ́ kpɨ́k nkɔkɔ́nɔk anɛ achi wɔmbɔ̌ŋ anyɛsɛ, kɛ ɔ́ngɔ mbaŋ sayri bɛfɛrɛ mɔ́ɛ̌nyɨ́ŋɨ́ anɛ achi amɛm nyɛ́sɛ́ manɔ́ywɛ.
Ɛ̌ti Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ kɛ̌ Kristo ásɔ́rɛ́ mɛ, akʉ mɛ nté ndǔ ntí ywi, nɛ nchí mǔkɛnɔŋ nɛ́nɛ. Nɨk nɔ́kɔ́ ká mmʉɛt bɛ Mandɛm anchyɛ mɛ nɛtaŋántɨ bɛ ngátí nɔkɔ bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ mbɔnyu mbɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ. 
Bǒ-batí bo Israɛl bhɔ bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ yɛ̌ ɛkáti ɛnɛ ɛ́fú Judɛ́ya ɛ̌ti yɛ nɛ yɛ̌ mmu ywɛsɛ́ abhɨ́kɨ́ fu arɛ́ ántwɔ́ nɛ ɛyɔŋ ntá yɛsɛ bɛ ɔkʉ ɛbɛ́ptí ɛnyɨŋ.
Bě bo Galéshia, bɛchɨŋti bho! Agha ányíɛ́ bhe nɛ ɛpɛm akʉ mǎnɛ́m ɛbhɨ? Pú nkʉ bǎrɨŋɨ Yesu Kristo mbɔ bɛ ntɔŋ be kpoŋoroŋ ndu yi ágǔ amfay ɛkotákátí?
Mmu anɛ afyɛ́ ntí bɛghok mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ́tɔ̀ŋ ǎjwimɛm. Mɛ̌kʉ yi andɨŋɨ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ bɛchak. Kɛ mmǔ anɛ apu fyɛ ntí, yɛ̌ chi mandú ɛnyɨŋ anɛ yi arɨŋɨ básɔt ntá yi.
Yesu ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bhɔ, aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Dɔ́k ká ntá bachiǎkap Mandɛm bɛ mánchák bhe.” Ɛnɛ́ bárɔ̀ŋ, ɛbhaŋákwa yap ɛ́may.
Ɛta, wɔ mmu ɔ́chí chak, bǒ mmɨk bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ wɔ, kɛ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ wɔ, nɛ nkwɔ wa anɛ bárɨŋɨ bɛ́ wɔ kɛ ɔ́tó mɛ.
Ndu mpok anɛ áfʉɛ́rɛ́ ansɛm, arɔ́ nyaka bo bɛtɔkɔ́ mmɨk mankɛm mánkʉ mbɔ ɛnyǔ bákɔ́ŋɔ́.
Mbabhɛri ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ afate. Ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ babhǐnywɔp fúfú, akaysi bɛ́ bǒkɛnɔŋ mankɛm bábʉɛ. Agwɔp akparɛnja ywi ndu bɛway mmʉɛt.
Yɛ̌ agha anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ntɨ bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm áyàŋ, ǎrɨŋɨ bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n mɛ̌tɔ̀ŋ bɛ́fú chi ntá Mandɛm nɛ bɛ puyɛ̌ mɛmbɔŋ kɛ ntɨ́ bɛtɔŋ bhɔ.
Bápɛ́t yɛ nsɛm ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ báchɔ̀kɔ amɛm Yerúsalɛm. Bátóŋti bawɛt ɛrɨ́tí ɛriɛp amɛn báwati amʉɛt ngu. Nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt ɛnap nɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́, báywěmʉɛt mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɛbhé Moses ɛ́rɛ̀m.
Kaká ká bǒnkwɔ abhɛn ɛtɔk Laodisia, nɛ Nímfa, nɛ ɛka bǒnkwɔ abhɛn báchɛ̀m ɛkɛt ɛyi.
Twɔ́ ká ntá ya, bě mankɛm abhɛn bǎpɔ́kɔ́ mɛnwɔ́ptí batǔ bɛsɔŋɔri nɛ bǎpɔp, chɔŋ nsɛbhɛ yɔ amɨk, nchyɛ́ bhe nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt.
Bɛsí bo mankɛm abhɛn bághòk yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ, Yesu arɛm ntá baghɔkɔ́ bhi bɛ,
Júdas aták nkáp wu amɨk amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm, afú arɔk asuri.
Bě bho bǎchi barɨŋɨ́ndak, bǎchɔ̀kɔ mǎngoko nɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchɨŋtǐ bho bárɛ̀m nɛ maŋák.
Sɛ́mfyɛ́ ntí bɛ́ghɔ ɛnyǔ sɛ́kwáy mɛnyɨkɨsi batɨ anɛ batɨ̌ bǒnkwɔ ɛnyu ɛnɛ bákway bɛbhɔŋ ɛkɔŋ nɛ bho nɛ mánkʉ nɔkɔ bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ.
Básɨ́ŋ nnyɛ́n ndǔ nkú yi nɛ ndǔ ɛbhɔ́k anǎkak ɛyi ɛnɛ nɛfí. Nɛ́bhák bɛ, “Mfɔ bafɔ nɛ Acha Mfɔ.”
Aisáya arɛm nyaka nɔ mbɔnyunɛ aghɔ nyaka kɛnókó Yesu, nɛ are rɛm ɛ̌ti yi.
Jése abhak chi Mfɔ Debhít. Debhít achí nyaka chi Sólomon. Nnɔ Sólomon ayambɨ abháy Uria, kɛ ǎbhay Debhít. Sólomon achí nyaka chi Rehóboam, Rehóboam abhak chi Abíja, Abíja abhak chi Ása. Ása achí nyaka chi Jɛhósafat, Jɛhósafat abhak chi Jóram, Jóram abhak chi Úsia. Úsia achí nyaka chi Jótam, Jótam abhak chi Áhas, Áhas abhak chi Hesékia. Hesékia achí nyaka chi Manáse, Manáse abhak chi Ɛ́mɔs, Ɛ́mɔs abhak chi Josáya. Josáya achí nyaka chi Jɛkonáya nɛ bɔ̌mayi. Mpok yɔ kɛ̌ bápɔ́kɔ́ bo Israɛl bɛ mandɔk manchɔkɔ ɛtɔk Bábilɔn.
Arɔk tɛ́mté, aghɔ mɔ́mayi Símun, aghati yi bɛ, “Sɛ́ghɔ mmu anɛ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ, ‘Mɛsáya’”, nɔ chi, Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò.
Ɛbyɔk ɛyɔ ɛ́máy nɔ́kɔ́ Ɛ́fɛsɔs, Pɔ̌l abhɨŋɨ bakoŋo Yesu. Arɛm kɛpɨ nɛ bhɔ́ ndu bɛ́fyɛ́ bɔ́ ntɨ. Arɔ yɛ bhɔ́ abho bɛrɔŋ atú Masidónia.
Mmufú achí nyaka ɛtɔk Seséria, anɛ aka nnyɛ́n bɛ́ Kɔnéliɔs. Abhak mǔntí ɛ́ká batɛmɛ́ nɛnu Rom bɛsa bɛ́táy. Báré bhɨŋɨ ɛka ɛyɔ bɛ́ Ɛka Itália.
Píta asɛp arɔk ntá bǒbhɔ, arɛm bɛ, “Mɛ kɛ nchí mmu anɛ bǎyàŋ. Bǎtwɔ ndaká yí?”
Bǎrɔ̀ bɛbhé Mandɛm bǎkoŋo chi bɛpɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǒ mmɨk.”
Mɛnyɨŋ ɛ́bhɛn ngátí nɛ́ wɔ bɛ́chí tɛtɛp. Nchi yaŋ yɛ bɛ ɔ́ngáti bo abhɛn mánoko Mandɛm mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn sayri bɛ mámfyɛ́ ntí bɛ́kʉ bɛrɨ. Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́rɨ tontó nɛ bɛ́kwàk yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu.
Ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ yi, asɔt yí apɛtnsɛm Antiɔk nɛ yi. Sɔ̌l nɛ yi bábhak arɛ ndǔ mmíɛ́ nɛnkɛm nɛ nkwɔ Yesu, mántɔŋ nɔkɔ bɛyǎ bo Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́. Chi Antiɔk kɛ bábhó nyaka bɛbhɨŋɨ bakoŋo Yesu bɛ, “Nkwɔ Kristo.”
Mpok anɛ mmǔ ywɛka áyàŋ mɛnɨkmʉɛt, ánchwé anywɔ́p, ɛbhak ɛnɛ yi ábhak aywǐnti, antíɛ́p mbǐnywɔp anɨkmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm Ɛta yɛka mmǔ bápú ghɔ nɛ amɨ́k. Mbák mmu akʉ nɔ, chɔŋ Ɛtayɛka mmu ághɔ̀ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mmu ákʉ̀ bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ ankap yi.
Yesu abho yɛ bɛ́tɛm bɔ nɛkay nɛchak bɛ, “Mmǔfú achi nyaka. Atɨ nkɨ apɨ mɛnɔk vain arɛ. Afyɛ́ bo arɛ, bɛ mánkʉ bɛtɨk mankɔrɛ nsáy nɛ yi. Arɔ yɛ arɔk nɛkɔ ɛnɛn yi átàt, ɛtɔk ɛchak.
Ɛ̌ti yɔ, kɛ nchí to yi ntá yɛka bɛ ankʉ mǎndɨŋɨ ɛnyu bɛsɛ sɛchi, nɛ bɛ́ ámfyɛ́ bhe ntɨ.
Chɔŋ manɔ́ anchyɛ ntɨ manɔ ntá bǒbati bɛ mángwáy. Chɔŋ mbɔk bachi mánkʉ ɛnyumɔt nɛ bɔ̌bhap. Chɔŋ mbɔk bɔ mánte nɛnu nɛ bachi nɛ manɔ bhap, mánkʉ bɛ mángwáy bhɔ.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛghati ngɛ́mtáy bǒbhɔ bɛ, “Nchí ghati bhe bɛ, mbɔk bho báchi fá abhɛn bápú gu kpátɛ mángɔ ndǔ Kɛfɔ Mandɛm kɛ́twɔ̀ nɛ bɛtaŋ.” 
Ghatí ká mɛ. Ndǔ bɔ̌bhɔ bati apay, anɛ ághókó ɛ́táyi, akʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi áyàŋ chí anɛ́?” Bǒ mankɛm bakɛmɛ bɛ, “Anɛ nsénsí.” Yesu aghati bǒbati bo Israɛl bhɔ bɛ, “Dɨŋɨ́ ká tɛtɛp bɛ bǒ bɛbʉ́ mbɔ babhɛbhɛ́ nkábhɛ́nti nɛ baghɔrɛ́-nɛkɔ báyámbɨ bɛ́bhɔ́ŋ mbi bɛbhak bǒ abhɛn Mandɛm achi nɛ bhɔ mbɔ Mfɔ wap, ɛnɛ́ bǎrɔ̀p nsɛm.
Ɛchi yɛ bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu abhɔŋ bɛte bɛsí Mandɛm andɛm yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ákʉ́. 
Bǒnkwɔ mankɛm bábhɔ́ŋ maŋák ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǒnto barɛmɛ. Báyáp Stífin mmu amɔt anɛ abhɔŋɔ nɛka nɛ Yesu tontó nɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ achi nyaka nɛ yi mpoknkɛm. Báyap Fílip nkwɔ́, nɛ Prokórɔs, nɛ Nikanɔ́, nɛ Tímɔn, nɛ Pamɛ́nas, nɛ Níkolas, kɛnkɔ anɛ áfú nyaka Antiɔk. Anáŋ áchyɛ̀ nyaka Mandɛm kɛnókó mbɔ ɛnyǔ bo Israɛl bákʉ̀ kɛ ǎnoko Yesu.
Ndǔ mpok yɔ bo abhɛn báchyɛ̀ Mandɛm bakak nɛfí ɛkɛrákap bare noŋ Sakaría mámakati nɔkɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛkʉ yi áre tat amɛm ɛkɛrákap.
Ɛnyu yɔ kɛ ɛ́chí nɛ nɛka. Mbák mmu ǎrɛm bɛ ábhɔ̌ŋ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm, kɛ yí kɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm áyàŋ yi ánkʉ́, nɔ́ nɛrɛm yí árɛ̀m bɛ abhɔ̌ŋ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm achi chi ndɛ́ndɛm.
Bɔ́ŋ ká bɛyǎ ɛkwak ndu bɛkɛm nɛchɛmɛ́mʉɛt ɛnɛn Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ákʉ́ mǎmbɔŋ bɛfʉɛt ndǔ kpák anɛ ágwɔ̀t bhe nɛ batɨ̌ bǒ Kristo.
Mpok Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n afɛ́rɛ́ ɛ́bhánɛ́ ɛnɛ ɛjwi tándrámɔt, mbaŋ akwɛn arɔp nyímí nyímí nyímí amfay ndǔ ɛbhɔ́k nɛŋɔkɔ́ nywɔp ɛmɔt.
Wɔ ɛchɨŋtɨ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ, ɔ̌yàŋ mántɔ́ŋ wɔ́ bɛ mbák mmu anókó bɛ Mandɛm achi kɛ yi kɛbháká kʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áyàŋ bo mánkʉ́, nɔ nɛnoko yi ánókó bɛ Mandɛm achi, achí chí ndɛ́ndɛmɛ́?
Bǎyɨ̀ŋɨ ɛnɔ nywɔp, mǎnsɔt bɛ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛgho. Mǎnjɨŋɨ awǔ ntaŋ, mǎnsɔt bɛ ntaŋ agho. Mǎnjɨŋɨ ayɔ̌ mpok, mǎnsɔt bɛ mpok ɛpǎ ɛgho. Nɛ ɛnɔ̌ mmíɛ́, mǎnsɔt bɛ mmíɛ́ nɛgho.
Yesu abhak ɛtɔk Bɛ́tani, amɛm ɛkɛt Símun anɛ ánáŋ ámé nyaka ɛbhaŋákwa. Ɛnɛ́ yi ányìɛ nɛnyíɛ́ arɛ́, ngɔrɛ́ amɔt atwɔ́ nɛ ɛsáyrí ɛ́kpɛ́mɛ́ bawɛrɛ́riɛp amɛn áyá nkáp.   Mɔ́ngɔrɛ́ wu asiɛ́p ɛmɨ ɛ́kpɛ́mɛ́ bawɛt ɛyɔ, apɨkɨri mɔ anti Yesu.
Mbʉ́ɛ́p áfòk, ándɔk ɛbhak ɛnɛ wu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́rɔŋ. Ɔ̌ghok ndu wu áfʉɛ̀t kɛ ɔpú rɨŋɨ ɛbhak wu áfú nɛ ɛbhak ɛnɛ wú árɔ̀ŋ. Ɛ́chí ɛnyumɔt nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ bábhé yi ndu bɛtaŋ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ.”
Tɛ̌ndu mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔángɛl barɛmɛ bɛchi nyaka tɛtɛp, nɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ abhɨkɨ bhʉɛrɛ bhɔ nɛ mmu anɛ átàŋ ntí, abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka ntɛmsi anɛ ákwáy nɛ yi,
Yɛ̌ nɔ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ Ɛta áchyɛ́ mɛ, ǎtwɔ̀ ntá ya. Nɛ yɛ̌ mmu apú twɔ ntá ya mɛ̌mbók yi,
Bo bákʉ̀ bɛtɨk ndǔ bakɨ yɛka, be kɛchyɛ bakáp ayap. Ngway yɛká akʉ bɔ́ bádì kɛbhɔ bɛ́ Mandɛm ánkwák bhɔ́, nɛ Mandɛm Acha bɛtaŋ mɛnkɛm ǎghok kɛbhɔ ɛkap.
Mbok ɛ̌tí yi akɔ aghabhɛri mmɨk bo Judeya nkɛm kpát aghaka ndǔ bɛtɔk bɛchák ɛbhɛn bɛchi kɛkwɔt. 
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tɔŋ bɛ sɛ́pɛt sɛ́yàŋ bɛkʉ mǎndɨŋɨ mɛnyu bo sɛchi. Sɛ́yàŋ chi bɛkʉ mǎndɨŋɨ ntí anɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́panyu ɛ̌ti ɛyɛsɛ bɛ́ mǎndɨŋɨ ɛnyǔ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́kɛ́mɛ bo abhɛn bárɛ̀m ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti yɛsɛ. Mpányu yap apu yɨŋɨ ɛnyǔ ntɨ mmu nɛchi amɛm nɛ Mandɛm. Báyɨ̀ŋɨ bho chi ndǔ nté yap achi.
Kɛ mbɔk abhɛn bachi bo Sáyprɔs nɛ abhɛn bachi bo Sírene bárɔk Ántiɔk bábhó bɛ́gháti Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ Yesu ntá bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl nkwɔ́.
Nnya anɛ ajwi ɛpay yɔ ákʉ́ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay. Áre kʉ tɛ bɛ́ ngó amfu amfay antwɔ amɨk bǒ mángɔ nɔkɔ.
Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ mpok ndɔ́ bhe, chɔŋ nkwɔ ɛ́nchwe nɛntɨ ɛnɛka, nɛ ɛ́pú rɔ bhe.
ná sɛ́kwày bɛbʉɛ ntɛmsi anɛ átwɔ̀ mbák sɛ́mbyak ɛrɛmɛ́ nɛpɛmɛ anɛ Mandɛm áyàŋ bɛ́pɛ́mɛ́ bhɛsɛ? Mbɔŋ Yesu Acha kɛ áyámbɨ bɛrɛm kpoŋoroŋ ɛ̌ti nɛpɛmɛ anɛ Mandɛm ápɛ̀mɛ bho, kɛ bo abhɛn bághókó bákʉ bɛsɛ sɛndɨŋɨ bɛ ɛchi tɛtɛp.
“Mɛ̌jwìti bhe nɛ manyiɛp bɛtɔŋ bɛ́ bǎtɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛka. Kɛ mmǔ anɛ átwɔ̀ mɛ ansɛm achá mɛ ɛnyunɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ kway mmu anɛ nchí kaŋari nkwɔbhánya bɛkak ɛbhi. Ántwɔ́, chɔŋ anjwiti bhe nɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ nɛ ngó.
Bariɛp amɔ achi bɛ, “Mmǔ anɛ ábhʉ̀ɛrɛ ɛbhé ɛnɛ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛbhak sayri nɛ yi, nɛ ǎbhɔŋ ɛrɔri nɛpɛ́m fá amɨk.”
Mpok yɔ, bɛyǎ bo báfù, mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ báchí baghatǐ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm, ɛnɛ́ bárùɔ bho rwɔ́ bɛ mankoŋo bhɔ.
Arɛ́, arɔk achwe amɛm ɛ́kírí ɛnɛ ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm. Aghɔ́ bo abhɛn bátì mpɔŋ nɛ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n nɛ bɛbhóŋó. Bo básɔ̀t nyaka mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ ndu bɛchyɛ akap. Aghɔ́ bawupsǐ bakap nkwɔ arɛ́.
Yesu aghati Píta bɛ, “Kɛmɛ́ akparɛnja ywɛ amɛm kɛ́nkwɔ́p. Nkɛ́ nyu nkɔ́p ɛsɔŋɔri anɛ Ɛta áchyɛ́ bɛ mɛ nyu kɛ?” 
Ɛ̌tiyɔ kɛ ɛchi bɛ bariɛp Mandɛm achi chi ntá bo abhɛn babhɔŋɔ nɛka nɛ yi, bɛtɔŋ bɛ chi ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhi kɛ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi afyɛ́ bariɛp bɛkʉ ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhárɛ́mɔ Ábraham. Bariɛp ami apú chi ndiɛrɛ ntá bo abhɛn bákòŋo bɛbhé, kɛ ntá bo bachak mankɛm nkwɔ abhɛn babhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm mbɔ Ábraham, tɛ̌ndu bɛsɛ mankɛm sɛchi bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ bhi.
Ɛwak ɛ́mɔt, bo báré twɔ ntá Yesu ndǔ bakwɔ́. Aghɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bhɔ́, arɔk achɔkɔ ambɨ njiɛ. Bakoŋo bhi bákó bátɛ́mɛ́ri yi, bachɔkɔ nɛ yi.
Ngwɛnti mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm achi kɛkwɔt. Bǎkɛ́ bhak yɛ taka taka ndǔ nkaysi yɛka. Bák ká pě amɛm batɨ ayɛka bɛ mǎnkwáy mɛnɨkmʉɛt.
Bágháti yi bɛ, “Yesu anɛ Násárɛt kɛ áfʉɛ̀t.”
Páílet abhɛ́p bɔ́ bɛ, “Bǎyaŋ yɛ bɛ nkʉ yi nɛ mmu anɛ bǎbhɨŋɨ bɛ́ Mfɔ bo Israɛl?”
Mbák manoŋ nnya ǎkway nyaka bɛkʉ mmu ambak pɛ́pɛ́p, ná nɛ manoŋ Kristo, yi mmu achyɛ mmʉɛt anɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛ́bhɨkɨ nyɔ́p ntá Mandɛm mbɔ akap ndǔ bɛtaŋ Ɛfóŋó mmu achi mpoknkɛm? Manoŋ ami abhɔŋ bɛ́bhɔ́ŋ bɛyǎ bɛtaŋ ndu bɛkʉ bɛ batɨ yɛsɛ ambak pɛ́pɛ́p, nɛ bɛ́ sɛ́kɛ́pɛrɛ kʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́twɔ̀ bhɛsɛ nɛ nɛwú. Akʉ́ nɔ́ bɛ́ sɛ́ndɔ́bhɛ tok chi Mandɛm mmu achi nɛpɛ́m.
Abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Nɛka ɛnɛka nɛ mɛ nɛ́chí fá?” Bɛcháy bɛkɛm bɔ nɛ bábhak maknkay, bábho bɛbhɛp batɨ bɛ, “Ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ mmu nɛ? Ǎsay yɛ̌ chi mbʉ́ɛ́p nɛ mpɛ́rɛ́nyɛn, nɛ yɔ ɛ́nkʉ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi arɛmɛ!” 
Mpok Yesu árɔ́ ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm árɔ̀ŋ, baghɔkɔ́ bhi bábhɨ́ŋɨ yi, mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ yi ángɔ́ ndǔ ɛkɛt ɛyɔ ɛrɨ ɛcha!
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, bě bo Mandɛm, bě bho bǎbhʉ̀rɛ bɛbhé Mandɛm, bě bho bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛka nɛ Yesu, tě ka kpirí nɛ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ́.
Nchí yaŋ mǎndɨŋɨ bɛ báfɛ́rɛ́ mɔmáyɛsɛ Tímɔti ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ. Mbák yi antwɔ ayak, chɔŋ ntwɔ́ nɛ yi ndu bɛghɔ bhe.
Píta apɛt ataŋa. Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, bo abhɛn báté arɛ́ nɛ Píta bárɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Sayri sayri, ɔchí mmǔ ywi amɔt mbɔnyunɛ wɔ nkwɔ́ ɔchí mmu Gálili!”
Mandɛm achyɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu yɛsɛ ayi akap bɛkoŋo bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhi nɛ bhɛsɛ. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ánkʉ yɛ ɛbhi bɛtɨk nɛ aywi akap. Mbák Mandɛm achyɛ́ mmu akap bɛrɛm kɛpɨ̌ntɨ mmu wu abhɔŋ bɛkʉ nɔ bɛkoŋo ɛnyu ɛnɛ yi anoko Mandɛm.
Bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk bɛyǎ fá amɨk, nɛ bɛ́chí kɛkúrí kɛkúrí. Nɛ yɛ ɛ́mɔt ɛpu ɛnɛ bo abhɛn bárɛ̀m yɔ bápú ghok.
Ɛchi nɔ mbɔnyunɛ, mmu anɛ ánókó Yesu Kristo nɛ ntɨ ɛni, Mandɛm ǎkʉ̀ yi ámbák chak bɛsí bhi. Nɛ mbák ándɛm kpoŋoroŋ bɛ Yesu Kristo achi Acha, Mandɛm ǎpɛmɛ yi.
Bě baghɔrɛ́ nɛ manɛ́m, sɛptí nɔ́kɔ́ ka mmʉɛt ntá manɛ́m abhɛka ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ mbɔnyunɛ ɛyɔ kɛ ɛrɨ bɛsí Yesu Kristo Acha.
Mmǔ anɛ árɛ̀m bɛ, “Nchí kɔ amɛm bɛdiɛ́rɛ́” kɛ ampap nɔkɔ ntɨ manɔ́, abhʉɛ́t amɛm ɛjuri.
Ɛ́pú yɛ́ ɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay mbák bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk Satan bákʉ̀ nkwɔ mbɔ bɛ báchí bo abhɛn bákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi chak bɛsí Mandɛm. Ndǔ ngwɛnti yap bábhɔŋ chi nsáy bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn bɔ bákʉ̀. 
Nɛnɛ́ ká batɨ ntá yɛsɛ. Sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ kʉ yɛ̌ mmu ɛbɛ́pti ɛnyɨŋ, sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ chɔŋti ntí mmu amɛm, nɛ sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ nyiɛ́ mmu ɛbhɔ́ŋ.
Anɛfú akwɛnti ndǔ mmɨk anɛ tákɔ nsěnse ágò arɛ. Achak are gó, kɛ tákɔ nsěnse agó áchɛt yɔ kpát agú.
Mpok bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ re rɨŋɨ Mandɛm, bǎbhak ndǔ kɛsɛmɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi chi bɔmandɛm nsé.
Ndǔ árɔ̀ŋ, are fyɛ́ bakoŋo Yesu ntɨ amɛm bɛtɔk Masidónia mɛnkɛm, kpát achwɔp ɛtɔk Gris.
Kɛ Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Ɛ́chí amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm bɛ, ‘Puyɛ̌ nɛnyíɛ́ nɔ́nɔ́ kɛ nɛ́kɛ̀m nɛpɛ́m. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm árɛ̀m kɛ̌ ɛ́bhɔ́ŋ bɛtaŋ bɛkɛm nɛpɛ́m mmu.’”
Bětí běti ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ mbɨ amɛm Sɔ́nde, báfú báre rɔŋ ndǔ nnɛm. Báchwɔp arɛ́ mpok mmok ánáŋ áfúú
“Bǎrɨ́ŋɨ́ ndǔ ɛbhé Moses ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Ɔ́bhɔ́ŋ bɛ́kɔŋ mmǔ ɛtɔk ɛyɛ, ɔ́mpap mmu anɛ ápábhɛ́ wɔ.’
Tɛ̌ndu Mandɛm áchɛ́mɛ́ bhɛsɛ nɛ Kristo ndu nɛwú ɛni, chɔŋ sɛ́mbak nɛ yi mpok sɛ́pɛ́rɛnsɛm ndu nɛpɛ́m nkwɔ mbɔ yi.
Ndu sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ ǎtàŋ chɔŋ bo mankɛm, sɛbhɔŋ bɛcháy nɛ Yesu Acha. Bɛchay ɛbhɛn bɛ́kʉ sɛ́fyɛ̀ yɛ bɛtaŋ ndu bɛkʉ bɛ bo mánóko bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn sɛ́ghàti bhɔ bɛchi tɛtɛp. Mbɔŋ Mandɛm arɨ́ŋɨ́ bhɛsɛ́ sayri, nɛ nkáysí bɛ be nkwɔ bǎrɨŋɨ ɛnyǔ bo sɛ́chi.
Kɛ nɛ́nɛ, bǎkɛ́ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛkʉ nɛ mɛnyɨŋ mbɔ bɛběntɨ, nɛ ɛchoko-ntɨ, nɛ nkaysi bɛkʉ batɨ bɛbʉ́, nɛ bɛchɔŋti manyɛ́n batɨ, nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛkɛ fu be anyu.
Ntɨkɨ nsáy mmu ábhɔŋ mbák abhɔ̌ŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ fá amɨk, kɛ anɛ́m nɛpɛ́m ɛni? Nɛ mbák mmu ánɛ́m nɛpɛ́m ɛni, ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ yí ákwày bɛsɔt anchyɛ bɛ́ yi ampɛt ambɔŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛni?
Nɛ́yi nɔkɔ, ɛnɛ́ Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bárɔ Bɛ́tani bápɛtnsɛm, nsay akɛ́m Yesu.
Sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi amɛm bɛkáti ɛbhé Moses bɛ́yɨ̀ŋɨ chi bo abhɛn Mandɛm achyɛ bhɔ ɛbhé ɛyɔ. Ɛ́yɔ ɛ́chòk manyu bo abhɛn báyàŋ bɛtaŋa mmʉɛt bɛ bapu bo bɛbʉ́. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu abhɔŋ bɛte bɛsí Mandɛm ndǔ manyé.
Ɛ́fákári yɛ bɛ bǒnkwɔ Yesu abhɛn bachi atú Judɛ́ya, nɛ abhɛn atú Gálili, nɛ abhɛn atú Samária nkɛm kɛpɛrɛ bhɔŋ ɛsɔŋɔri. Bakoŋo Yesu bábhʉrɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnap ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ nɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ́ bɔ báchyɛ̀ Mandɛm kɛnókó. Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ are chyɛ bhɔ nɛpɔptǐntɨ́, anchyɛ nɔkɔ bhɔ bɛtaŋ. Ɛ́kʉ bɛyǎ bo báchák báre noko Yesu mánchɛm nɔkɔ nɛ bhɔ.
Ɛyɔ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ́ Ábraham abhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm tɛtɛp, aka bɛkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm ághátí yi ánkʉ́. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yí ákʉ́, kɛ ɛ́tɔ́ŋ bɛ́ yi aká nɛ Mandɛm tɛtɛp.
Mbák sɛchi bɛchɨŋtǐ bho mbɔ ɛnyǔ mbɔk bo bárɛ̀m, sɛ́bhák nɔ chí ndu sɛ́nù bɛchyɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó. Kɛ mbák bǎká bɛ sɛ́pú bɛchɨŋtǐ bho, dɨŋí yɛ́ ka bɛ sɛ́kʉ̀ bɛtɨk chi ɛ̌ti yɛka.
Sɨkɨ́ ká ntɨ nɛ mmǔ anɛ áchyɛ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ nɛ́nɛ, ndǔ yi abhʉɛ́t nɛ bhe, bɛ́ mǎmbák bɔ̌ bɛdyɛrɛ.” Yesu árɛ́mɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, arɔk abhɛsɛ ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ bo bápú kwáy bɛghɔ yi.
Aghati yɛ bhɔ́ bɛ, “Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎghɔ̀-nɛ́, chí nkúbhɛ́ barak anɛ mɛ̌ghàti nyaka bhe mpok mbʉɛt nɛ bhe. Mɛ̌ghàti nyaka be bɛ, mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn bɛ́chi amɛm basɨŋɨ́ Moses nɛ amɛn abhɛn bɛchi ndǔ basɨŋɨ́ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ nɛ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chí amɛm Ɛkáti Bakway ɛ̌ti ya, bɛ́bhɔŋ bɛfu tɛtɛp.”
Sɛ́mfú yɛka amɛm ɛtɔk sɛndɔk sɛntɛmɛri yi nɛfí, sɛ́mbɔŋ ntíánwɔ́p anɛ́ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka.
Kɛ dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mmu anɛ ákɔ́ŋ mbi Mandɛm ákʉ̀ kɛ bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnɛ́n nɛ́fú ntá Mandɛm nɛchi tɛtɛp.” 
Yɛ̌ndu mánáŋ báchyɛ́ nyaka bhɛsɛ bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri nɛ ntíánwɔ́p ɛtɔk Fílipi mbɔ ɛnyu bǎrɨŋɨ, Mandɛm ywɛsɛ afyɛ́ bhɛsɛ ntɨ bɛ sɛ́ntwɔ́ sɛ́ngátí bhe Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ áfú ntá yi yɛ̌ndu bɛyǎ bo mánù nyaka tontó bɛchyɛt bhɛsɛ mbi.
Bo Israɛl bakɛm mmu wu báre yáŋ bɛway yi. Ngók nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́ yi abhɔ̌ŋ bɛtaŋ ɛtɔk Rom mbɔ mɔ̌mɨk, nsɔt batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bha ndɔk mfɛ́rɛ́ yi amɔ́ yap.
Nchí niɛ yɛ bhe bɛ mǎntwɔ ntá ya mǎnkú pú anɛ básɔ́ŋɔ́ ango bafɛrɛ mɛ́nyɨ́ŋ mɛnkɛm arɛ́ bɛ́ mǎmbák bǒ bakáp tɛtɛp. Twɔ́ ká ku ndɛn pɛ́pɛ́p mǎmfyɛ́ amʉɛt bɛ́ mǎnkútí bɛbhó bɛwɔ ɛbhɛka ɛbhɛn bɛ́chyɛ bhe ntíánwɔ́p. Twɔ́ ka, mǎnku babhé mǎmfyɛ amík bɛ mǎnkwáy bɛghɔ mbaŋ tɛtɛp.
Mbɔŋ Ɛta akɔŋ be mbɔnyunɛ bǎkɔŋ mɛ, nɛ mǎnókó bɛ mfu chí ntá yi.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ wap anyíɛ́ kpát ajwi.
Mbɔŋ yɛ ɛkwak nɛ́nɛ ncha ɛnyu ɛsɨ́ bɛto yi ampɛtnsɛm antɛmɛri bhe awu bɛ mǎngɔ yi batɨ ámpɔ́p be amɛm nɛ bɛ basɛ́mɛ́ ma nkwɔ ámay.
Símun Píta akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Wɔ kɛ ɔ́chí Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò, wɔ kɛ ɔ́chí Mmɔ Mandɛm anɛ áchí nɛpɛ́m.”
Ghɔ́ ká ndu Ɛtayɛsɛ áre kɔŋ bhɛsɛ. Akɔŋ bhɛsɛ́ tontó kpát ǎbhɨ́ŋɨ́ bhɛsɛ bɛ bɔ̌bhi, nɛ sɛchi bɔ̌bhi tɛtɛp. Ntí anɛ bǒ mmɨk babhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ bɛ sɛchi bɔ̌ Mandɛm chi bɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ Mandɛm.
Mbák mmu abhɨ́kɨ́ ka bɛ ɛchi ɛnyu ɛyɔ, bǎkɛ́ ka yi nkwɔ.
Ɛ́chí mbɔ ɛnyǔ básɨ́ŋɨ́ amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm bɛ, “Agha ákwày bɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chí antɨ Mandɛm Acha? Agha ákwày bɛ́chyɛ́ yí maníɛ́?” Kɛ mbák chí bhɛsɛ́ bo bho Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm áchí nɛ bhɛsɛ́, sɛ́bhɔ́ŋ ɛnyǔ ntɨ ɛnɛ́n Yesu Kristo áchyɛ́ bhɛsɛ́.
Nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ ywɛka abhɔŋ bɛ́fyɛ mkpá nkɔ anɛ Mandɛm aghoko, bɛ ámbák mbɔ yímbɔŋ. Mkpá nkɔ yɔ chi ɛpɨŋ ɛkɔ ɛnɛ ɛchi chak tɛtɛp bɛsí Mandɛm, nɛ ɛchi nyáŋá tɛtɛp.
Nɛ átwɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ fá amɨk mbɔ nkwǎŋwaŋ, arɔk ambɨ bɛ́sɛ́pti mmʉɛt amɨk anchyɛ nɔkɔ Mandɛm kɛnókó, kpatɛ agú nɛwú ntíánwɔ́p ndǔ ɛkotákátí.
Amɨ́k ayɛka achi bɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛbhɛn bɛ́kʉ̀ mǎngɔ mbaŋ. Mpok amɨ́k ayɛka achi arɨ́árɨ́, mmʉɛt ɛyɛka ɛnkɛm ɛ́jwi nɛ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́. Kɛ mbák amɨ́k ayɛka ápú arɨarɨ, mmʉɛt ɛyɛka ɛnkɛm ɛ́jwi nɛ ɛjuri.
Nɛ mamiɛ́ mbɛ́ntí wu acha nyaka bɛsa bɛpay. 
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́chák ɛ́chí bɛ́ mbɔk baghɔrɛ́ ndǔ nkwɔ ywɛsɛ bákʉ batí átaka bhɛsɛ amɛm. Bárɔ́k ndǔ nnɛm běti bheti,
Báré bɨk nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ bɛ, “Mandɛm aywɛsɛ mmu achi ndu ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ nɛ Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n kɛ bápɛ́mɛ́ bhɛsɛ!”
Mbák chi bhɛsɛ, sɛ́pú pányu ɛncha ɛnyu sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ. Sɛ́tɨ bɛwɛnti chi ndǔ ndiɛrɛ anɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ bɛ sɛ́nkʉ sɛ́ngwɛnti arɛ́, nɛ be nkwɔ bǎchí ɛbhe ɛyɛsɛ.
Yesu arɨŋɨ bɛ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bághók bɛ bɛyǎ bo bárɔbhɛ koŋo chi yi nɛ yí anjwiti nɔkɔ bhɔ, nɛ bɛ́ bakoŋo bhi báyá máncha nɔkɔ abhɛn Jɔ̌n.
Amfay ntí Yesu, ɛbhɔ́kɛnɔk ɛbhak babhát ndǔ ɛko ɛnɛ básɨ́ŋɨ́ arɛ bɛ: “Nɛ́ chi Mfɔ bo Israɛl.”
Kɛ Ɛta ǎtò chɔŋ Nkwak ndǔ nnyɛ́n ɛna. Yí wu chi Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ. Ánáŋ ántwɔ́, chɔŋ antɔŋ be yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ, ankwak be mǎntɨk mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn ngáti bhe.
Kɛ Yesu aghati yi bɛ, “Fǎ mɛ bɛsí, wɔ Satan! Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ ‘Mmu abhɔŋ bɛchyɛ kɛnókó chi ntá Mandɛm Acha, antók chí yi aywǐnti.’”
Akʉ bɛtaŋtí mɛnyɨŋ nɛ awɔ́ ywi, aták bo abhɛn báyòŋ mmʉɛ́t nɛ nkaysi anɛ achi amɛm batɨ̌ yap.
Mandɛm kɛ áchyɛ̀ bhɛsɛ nɛ be bɛtaŋ bɛ sɛ́nté kpirí nɛ Kristo. Yi kɛ afyɛ́ bhɛsɛ bɛ́ sɛ́mbák bǒbhi,
Bǒnto bábhó bɛbhɛp batɨ bɛ, “Ntɨkɨ mmǔ ywɛsɛ ákway bɛkʉ anɛ ɛnyǔ ndak ntá yi e?” 
Bɛkoŋo ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ Mandɛm ághókó mɛnyɨŋ, be babhɔŋ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛ́ ɛrɔ́rí ɛmɛnɛ chí ɛnyɨŋ ntíánwɔ́p nta mbakanɛm?
Sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔt mɛnɨkmʉɛt ɛ̌ti yɛka bɛbho nywɔp ɛnɛn sɛ́ghókó nɔ. Sɛ́nɨ̀kmʉɛt bɛ Mandɛm amfʉɛt ntá Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ánkwak mǎndɨŋɨ sayri ɛnyiŋ ɛnɛ yi áyàŋ mǎnkʉ. Sɛ́nɨ̀kmʉɛt bɛ Mandɛm ánkʉ nɔ ndu ákʉ mǎmbak barɨŋɨ́ndak bɛyɨŋɨ baraká Ɛfoŋo nɛ ndu akwak mǎmbɔŋ nɛjwǐmɛm ndu bɔ bɛchi. Achyɛ́ bhe nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak bɛ mǎndɨŋɨ sayri yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi atɨ́ nyaka bɛkʉ nɛ ǎkʉ̀ ntá bǒbhi.
Ɛwak ɛ́mɔt, ɛnɛ́ Yesu átɔ̀ŋ bo amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm angati nɔkɔ bhɔ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́, bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm nɛ bǒbati ɛtɔk bárɔ́k ntá yi,
Ágháká nɔ́kɔ́ kɛ́kwɔ́t bɔ̌bɛtɔk Bɛtfágɛ nɛ Bɛ́tani, ndǔ Njiɛ Mɛnɔk *Ólif, ató baghɔkɔ́ bhi bati apay ambɨ.
Nɛ́nɛ, ɛnɛ́ sɛ́sɨ́kɨ́ ntɨ nɛ Kristo bɛbhé bɛ́pú mbɔ mmu anɛ ábhàbhɛri, anyurɛ nɔkɔ bhɛsɛ.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛtɔŋ. Arɛm bɛ, “Kɛ nchí ghati bhe bho bǎghòk mɛ bɛ, kɔ́ŋ ká bo abhɛn bápábhɛ́ bhe, mǎntɔŋ bɔ́ bɛrɨ.
Akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Ɛchí mɛ nɛpɔp tontó bɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ yi áfú, yɛ̌ndu yi ánɛ́nɛ́ mɛ amɨ́k!
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Chiɛ́ yɛ́ ka nta Mfɔ Rom yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi ɛyi, mǎnchyɛ ntá Mandɛm yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi ɛnɛ Mandɛm.”
Sɔt yɛka yí nɛ bɛyǎ maŋák mbɔ ɛnyǔ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛsyɛpti ntɨ nkoŋo Yesu. Chiɛ̌ ká yi kɛnókó, mǎnchyɛ kɛnókó ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu achák anɛ áchí mbɔ yi.
Bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ɔbhɛ́ ɔpú Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò, ɔbhɛ́ ɔpú Ɛláija, nɛ ɔpú ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ, kɛ ndaká yí ɔ́jwìti bho?”
Chɔŋ Mandɛm antɛmsi yɛ mkpáká bho abhɛn ɛchɔŋ ɛ̌ti manoŋ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ mankɛm abhɛn bɔ báwáy tɛ nɛbhǒmɨk,
Mbɔk bakoŋo Jɔ̌n Njwiti bárɔ́k ntá Yesu bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ndaká yí bɛsɛ́ nɛ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi sɛ́tarɛ nɔkɔ nsay ndu mɛnɨkmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm, kɛ bakoŋo bhɛ bápú kʉ nɔ?”
Abhɛ́p yɛ́ bhɔ bɛ, “Ntɨkɨ mmǔ ywɛka anɛ mɔ́ywi nɛ yɛ̌ mpɔŋ yi ákwɛn amɛm mbokó manyiɛp ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt kɛ yi kɛya yɛ̌ yi, yɛ̌ yɔ tɛ́mté ámfɛ́rɛ́?”
Ǎkʉ bɔ mangɔ bɛ nchí chak bɛsí Mandɛm mbɔnyunɛ mɛ̌rɔ̀ŋ ntá Ɛtaya nɛ bǎpú pɛrɛ ghɔ́ chɔ́ŋ mɛ.
Nkúbhɛ́ ɛwak ɛyɔ, bakoŋo Yesu bati apay báfá Yerúsalɛm bare rɔŋ ndu mɔ́tɔk anɛ bábhìŋɨ bɛ Ɛmayus, nɛkɔ̌ ɛnɛn nɛchi mbɔ bɔkilɔ́mɛta nɛ́nɛnamɔt nɛ ɛbhɔ́k.
Ngɔrɛ́ bɛtok amɔt anɛ achi arɛ, aghɔ́ Píta nkwɔ arɛ́ chɔkɔ ndǔ ngo ághɔ̀ yi amʉɛt. Áyɨ́ŋɨ́ yi dǐǐ, arɛm bɛ, “Mɔ́nkwǎnɛ nkwɔ́ achi mbʉ nɛ Yesu.”
Kaká ká Asínkritɔs nɛ Flɛ́gɔn nɛ Hɛ́mis nɛ Patróbas nɛ Hɛ́mas nɛ batɨ̌ bǒnkwɔ bachak abhɛn bachi nɛ bhɔ.
Kɔ́ŋ ka batɨ nɛ ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ́ tɛtɛp. Pap ka barak abʉ́abʉ. Kɛ́m ká sayri yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛrɨ́tí ɛnyɨŋ.
Ɛkʉ bo abhɛn mánóko ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Píta arɛmɛ bárɔ́k bájwiti bhɔ. Nɛ bo abhɛn bachɛmɛ nɛ bakoŋo Yesu nywɔp ɛnɔ babhak mbɔ nká ɛ́rát.
Mmu ákɛ́ rɔ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛ́nsɔ́ŋɔ́rí ntɨ ɛni amɛm. Yɛ̌yi yɛ̌yi, ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ chí mɛnɨk nɔ́kɔ́ mmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎyàŋ yi ánchyɛ́ bhe. Nɨk nɔ́kɔ́ ká mmʉɛt, mǎnkaka nɔkɔ yí ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ́.
Yesu aya yí batú ansɛmti nɔkɔ
Mpok Yesu achi nɛ bǒnto bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Acha, chɔŋ ɔ́nsɔt kɛfɔ Israɛl ɔ́nkɛmɛ ntá yɛsɛ bo Israɛl kɛ?”
Kɛ bárɨŋɨ nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́ achí mmu Israɛl, bápɛ́t bábho bɛwat mandɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Atɛ́mis, mandɛm anɛ bǒ Ɛ́fɛsɔs, chí mandɛm ngo!” Barɔk ambɨ bɛkʉ ɛnyuyɔ ndǔ maŋɔkɔ́ nywɔp ápáy.
Yɛ̌ nɔ, Píta arɛm nɛ ntɨ ɛni nɛnkɛm bɛ, “Yɛ̌ chí nɛwú, chɔŋ ngu nɛ wɔ. Mpú bʉɛ wɔ.” Baghɔk Yesu báchák mankɛm bárɛ́m ɛnyumɔt. 
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, bakoŋo Yesu bárɔ́k ntá yi babhɛp yi bɛ, “Ndǔ nkwɔ́ bhó abhɛn Mandɛm achi Mfɔ wap, ághá áchɨ́kɨ́ áchá báchák?”
Mpú rɛm chi ɛ̌ti yɛka mankɛm, ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bo abhɛn njábhɛ́. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́ghàti bhɛsɛ ɛ́bhɔŋ bɛ́fú kpoŋoroŋ mbɔ ɛnyu basɨŋɨ bɛ, ‘Anɛ ányíɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ mɛ ǎti chɔŋ mɛ.’
Nɛ́nɛ, bɔ̌ma, bʉrɛ́ ká nkaysi ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́rɨ́, nɛ ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́chyɛ̀ mmu kɛnókó, nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chí chak bɛsí Mandɛm, nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ bakwap, nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bo bághɔ̀ mánkɔŋ, nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bo bábhɔ̀ŋ ɛkwak bɛghɔ, nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́rɨ́ bɛ́chá, nɛ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́kʉ̀ bo mámbɨti bhe.
árɛm bɛ, ‘Kɔnéliɔs, Mandɛm aghok nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt ɛnɛ, nɛ aghɔ nɛkwak ɛnɛ́n ɔ́chyɛ̀ bachɛ́bhɛ́ bho.
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, mbák mmu anɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ syɛp yi ákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɛbhé ɛ́yàŋ, Mandɛm apu sɔt yi mbɔ mmu anɛ basyɛphɛ?
Mɛ kɛ nchí nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn nɛ́chyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛ́fú amfay. Mmu anɛ ányíɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn, ǎbhák nɛpɛ́m mpoknkɛm. Nɛnyiɛ́ ɛnɛ́n mɛ̌chyɛ chɔŋ bɛ́ bǒ mmɨk mámbɔ́ŋ nɛpɛ́m, chi nyamwʉɛ́t ɛya.”
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛtɔk ɛnɛ bǎchwe arɛ́ nɛ básiɛ́pti be nɛ maŋák, nyiɛ́ ká yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn bachyɛ bhe.
Mbǎy-ngɔrɛ kɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ngɔrɛ́. Mmʉɛrɛ mbǎyngɔrɛ́ anɛ áchí téé ánòŋ bɛ́ghok ɛyɔŋ ɛnɛ mbǎyngɔrɛ́,   ǎghok ɛyɔŋ ɛyi, ambɔ́ŋ bɛyǎ maŋák. Ɛnyu yɔ kɛ ɛ́chi nɛ mɛ. Maŋák ama ajwí pɔɔt nɛ́nɛ.
Yɛ̌ndu ɛ́chí nɔ́, mbɨ́kɨ́ rɛm bɛ́ mǎnkwák mɛ nɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Nɛ mpú sɨ́ŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ ndu bɛ́kʉ mǎntó mɛ mɛnyɨŋ. Ɛ́chí sayri bɛ ngú ɛsɔŋɔri ɛ́chá mɛ bɛbhɛp bɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ. Mbɨ́kɨ́ yáŋ yɛ̌ mmu ankʉ nkɛ́pɛrɛ dɛp awɔ́ antɨ bɛ mɛ́ghàti bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ nkɛbhɛ́p bɔ mánkwák mɛ.
Bágháti yi bɛ, “Bábhɔŋ bɛbhe yi ɛtɔk Bɛ́tlɛhɛm, fá atú Judɛ́ya, mbɔnyunɛ ɛchi amɛm ɛkáti ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ bɛ,
Ɛ́rɨ ɛcha ntá bǒ abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛsɛptǐmʉɛt nɛ bápú tɔŋ bɛtaŋ, mbɔnyunɛ chɔŋ yí anchyɛ bhɔ áfɔ́k ankɛm anɛ yi afyɛ́ bariɛp bɛchyɛ bhɔ́!
Bǒnkwɔ Fárisi báfú, bárɔ́k. Bátɛmɛri bo Israɛl abhɛn báté ansɛm Hɛ́rɔd, bákɛ́m ɛchɛmɛ, batɨ bɛway Yesu. 
“Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ mǎnɨkmʉɛt, bǎkɛ́ kʉ mbɔ bǒ abhɛn bákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ chi bɛ mángɔ́ bhɔ́. Bákɔŋ bɛte amɛm bɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt nɛ ndǔ manyé mbi kɛ manɨkmʉɛt bɛ́ mángɔ́ bhɔ. Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ, nɛghɔ́ anɛ bo bághɔ̀ bɛ bɔ mǎnɨkmʉɛt, chi awap akap anɛ mǎnáŋ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́.
Arɛ́, bágháti mbok Yesu amɛm ɛtɔk Pɛga. Báfá Pɛga basɛp bárɔk Atália.
Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Chí ɛ̌ti nɛtaŋántɨ ɛnɛka kɛ Moses áchyɛ́ nyaka bhe ɛbhé ɛnɛ.
Bǒ mankɛm abhɛn baghoko ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bɔ barɛmɛ babhak maknkay.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bakuti, chɔŋ mánɛnɛ. Nɛ ɛnɛ́ ɛchi bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ chɔŋ mánkʉ bo mandɨŋɨ yɔ.
Mbɨ́kɨ́ yaŋ ɛmbak mbɔ bɛ mɛ̌sɔ̀t bɛkáti ɛbhɛn mɛ̌sɨ̀ŋ bɛkʉ mǎmbɔŋ bɛcháy.
Bɛtaŋ abhɛn mpɔŋɔ́ndɨk ɛyɔ bɛ́fù nyaka chi ndǔ manyu yap nɛ ndǔ baghɔ́ yap. Baghɔ́ yap achi nyaka mbɔ nnyɔ́. Ábhɔ́ŋ batí. Nɛ baghɔ́ yɔ kɛ yɔ ɛ́nɛ̀m nyaka bo ɛnchyɛ nɔkɔ bhɔ ɛsɔŋɔri.
Yesu árɛ́mɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, bo Israɛl bápɛt bábho bɛbwɔpti batay ndu bɛtɛmti yi nɛ yɔ́ mángwáy.
Ǎtwɔ̀ awu nɛ Ɔnɛ́simɔs, mmǔ ywɛka amɔt. Ɔnɛ́simɔs achi mmu tɛtɛp nɛ manɔ anɛ sɛ́kɔ́ŋɔ́ tontó. Chɔŋ bɔ mángati bhe yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fákárí fá.
Bǒ mankɛm abhɛn bághókó yi, bábhák maknkay, mámbɛbhɛ nɔkɔ batɨ bɛ, “Pú nkúbhɛ́ mmǔ-nɛ kɛ ákɔ̀ nyaka angʉɛbhɛ nɔkɔ nɛnu nɛ bo abhɛn bábhɨ̀ŋɨ nnyɛ́n Yesu awu Yerúsalɛm nɛ? Atwɔ fá chí bɛ́ ánkɛ́mtí bo Yesu angwɔt, ansɔt ampɛtnsɛm nɛ bhɔ Yerúsalɛm. Atwɔ fá ndu bɛkɛmti bhɔ bɛ ansɔt ampɛtnsɛm nɛ bhɔ́ ntá bǒ batí bachiǎkap Mandɛm.”
Bafɔ̌ mmɨk bátòŋtí mmʉɛt mɛ́nu nɛnu, bǒbatí ɛtɔk báchɛm nɛbhʉɛt amɔt, báte ɛyu mɛnu nɛ Mandɛm Acha nɛ Mpɛmɛ yí afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò.’
Chɔŋ bǒ mmɨk mankɛm mánkɔ ndǔ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ ɛtɔk ɛyɔ. Chɔŋ bafɔ̌ mmɨk mǎnchwe amɛm nɛ kɛnókó ɛkap.
mbɔnyunɛ bǒbhɛn bágwɔt batɨ yap amɛm, nɛ báchók batú, mánɛ́mámɨ́k bɛ́ bákɛ́ ghɔ yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Ɛkʉ amɨ́k ayap ápú kway bɛghɔ mbaŋ, batú yap ápú kway bɛghok mbaŋ nɛ batɨ̌ yap apu kway bɛjwimɛm bɛ mantwɔ ntá ya, mɛ mbú bhɔ.’”
Atɛ́m bakay bɛtɔŋ bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Aisáya árɛ́mɛ́ nyaka bɛ chɔŋ ɛmfakari, ɛ́fákárí. Aisáya arɛm nyaka bɛ, “Chɔŋ ngati bhɔ mɛnyɨŋ chi ndǔ bakay, chɔŋ ntɔŋ bɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm ákʉ́ mɛ́mbák bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́, tɛ ndǔ nɛbhǒmɨk.” 
Mpok sɛ́nyìɛ nɛnyíɛ́ Acha, sɛ́sɔ̀t nkɔ́p mmɛm sɛ́nchyɛ bakak ntá Mandɛm, bɛsɛ́ mankɛm sɛ́nyú. Nɛkʉ anɛ sɛ́kʉ̀ nɔ́, pú sɛ́chɛ̀m mmʉɛt nɛ batɨ ndǔ manoŋ Kristo? Nɛ mpok sɛ́bɔkɔti brɛ́t sɛ́nyìɛ, pú sɛ́chɛ̀m mmʉɛt nɛ batɨ ndǔ mmʉɛt Kristo?
“Nnáŋ nkɔ mbáŋ nɛ mbaŋ, ngáti bhe ɛnyǔ Mandɛm ábhàk nɛ bo mbɔ Mfɔ wap, nɛ nɛ́nɛ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ yɛ̌ mmu ywɛka amɔt apú pɛrɛ ghɔ́ mɛ.
Yí nɛ mamʉɛrɛ bhi bárɔk bagʉɛp bɛyǎ nkáp anyɛ́n, bákɛ́m bɛyǎ nsi. Ɛ́yá kpát bɛyǎ nkáp yap abho bɛrakati.
Bɛsɛ́ babhɔŋ sɛ́ghók ɛyɔŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́fǔ amfay mbɔnyunɛ sɛ́chí nyaka nɛ yi amfǎy njiɛ Mandɛm.
Kɛ wɔ Táytɔs, ɔbhɔŋ bɛtɔŋ bo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́kɔ̀ ndɔŋ amɔt nɛ nɛtɔ́ŋ ɛnɛ́n tɛtɛp.
Bɔ̌ma, kɛ́p yɛ ká ntɨ ndǔ mǎnòŋ mpok anɛ Yesu Acha átwɔ̀. Yɨŋɨ́ ká bakwaŋá bakɨ. Bákɛ̀pntɨ mɛ́noŋ manyiɛp nchyɛ́miɛ nɛ amɛn ákʉ̀ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ́ngó. Nɛ bákɛ̀pntɨ mɛnoŋ mpok anɛ báfɛ̀rɛ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛbhɨ.
Ɛ́rɨ ɛcha ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ bo báchyɛ̀ ɛsɔŋɔri ndǔ ákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi chak bɛsí Mandɛm. Ǎyɛt yi mbɔnyunɛ achí Mfɔ ywi!
Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Mbakanɛm abhɔŋ bɛrɔ máyi nɛ ɛtayi anchɛm mmʉɛt nɛ ngɔrɛ́ ywi, bɔ bati apay mándɔp mmǔ amɔt.”
Abhɔ́ŋ maŋák bɛkʉ mɛndɨ́ŋɨ́ Mɔ́ywi, bɛ mbɔ́ŋ mbi bɛghati bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu ntá bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl. Ákʉ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, mbɨ́kɨ́ rɔŋ ntá yɛ̌ mmu bɛ anchyɛ mɛ maniɛ.
Ntɛnátɛn achí nyaka arɛ́ anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ Dɛmɛ́triyɔs. Ǎsɔt nyaka Silbha ankʉ nɔkɔ bɔ̌bɛkɛrɛ́ mandɛm nsé anɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ Atɛ́mis. Awɔ́-bɛtɨk ɛbhi áre chyɛ̀ yí nɛ bo báchák abhɛn bákʉ̀ bhɔ bɛyǎ nsay.
Bɛyǎ bhó báchɛ́mɛ nɔ́kɔ́ ɛkɛt Páílet betí ɛbhɔ, abhɛ́p bɔ́ bɛ, “Agha bǎyáŋ mɛndɔ́ ándɔ́k, Barábas kɛ chí Yesu, anɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ́ Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò?”
Njɨŋɨ yɛ ngɔ́ ndǔ ɛbhɔkɔ ɛ́rè tɛ amfǎy nɛbu, ɛ́mbɨkɨ nɔkɔ nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ bɛ, “Chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛp ɛncha! Chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛp ɛcha! Chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛp ɛncha ntá bo abhɛn bachi awu amɨk! Bɔangɛl abhɛ́n bárɔ́bhɛ́ bárát báfe ɛyap mmbá!”
bǎkɛ́ rɔ batí ywɛka ángwákárí bɛtaka amɛm. Yɛ̌ mmu andɛm chi bɛ yi achi ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ, yɛ̌ chi bɛ achi ngati Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm, nɛ yɛ̌ chi bɛ ɛkáti ɛ́fú ntá yɛsɛ bɛ nywɔp Yesu Acha átwɔ̀ nɛ́gháká, bǎkɛ fyɛ́ ntí.
Kɛ bo bachak báchí mbɔ mbwɔt anɛ ákwɛ́ntí ndǔ mmɨk ndɨ́ndɨ́. Bághòk Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm, mányu kɛpɛm ndǔ bapɛ́m ayap. Mbuɔt amɔt anchyɛ mbwɔt nkɔ anɛ aya acha anɛ bapɨ ndɔŋ ɛsa nsɛm byo, achák ndɔŋ bɛsa bɛ́rát, anɛfú ndɔŋ bɛsa bɛtay.” 
Yɛ̌ nɔ, bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm bákʉ ngɛ́mtáy bǒbhɔ mándɛm Páílet ámfɛrɛ chi Barábas ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ.
Kaká ká bǒbati bhɛka mankɛm, nɛ bo Mandɛm báchák mankɛm. Bǒnkwɔ abhɛn báfú Itali bátó bhe bakak.
Yesu ánáŋá anɛnɛ ɛkat, achyɛ bhɛsɛ mbǐ akɔ anɛ nɛpɛ́m bɛ́ sɛ́nkwáy bɛ́fʉɛt arɛ́ sɛndɔk tɛ amɛm. Ɛkat ɛnɛ yi ánɛ́nɛ́ chi mmʉɛt yi anɛ yi áchyɛ́, ndu ágú ɛ̌ti yɛsɛ.
Nnɛ́m ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ̌ghàti bhe mbɔ ɛnyǔ bághátí nyaka mɛ nkwɔ chi bɛ: Kristo agú nyaka ɛ̌ti bɛbʉ́ bhɛsɛ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ́mɛ́ nyaka bɛ chɔŋ ɛ́mfakari.
Bɛyǎ bhap báré rɛm bɛ, “Ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri yi! Ǎbhokori! Ndaká yí bǎté, bǎghòk ɛnyɨŋ yi árɛ̀m?”
Moses ǎkùti nyaka bɛsí bhi nɛ ndɛn mpoknkɛm anɛ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ Mandɛm ɛbhɛn bɛ́ghɔ̀ bɛsí bhi bɛ́bhó mɛmay mandú mandú, bɛ bo Israɛl bákɛ́ ghɔ ndǔ mɛ́nɛ̀msi. Sɛ́pú bhɛsɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ.
Bo abhɛn bachi arɛ bátɔŋ bhɛsɛ bɛyǎ bɛrɨ̌ntɨ nɛ básɔt bhɛsɛ mankɛm sayri. Manyiɛp ábhó nɔ́kɔ́ mɛniɛ, nɛ ndǔ mbaŋ ǎkwɛn, bábháyti ngo bɛ sɛ́ngwák.
Kɛ bǎkɛ́ sɔt ɛnyu mmu wu mbɔ mǔmpap. Kɛ ya ká yí batú nɛ ɛkɔŋ mbɔ ntɨ mǔnkwɔ. 
Ɛ̌ti ɛyɔ kɛ̌ básɨ́ŋɨ́ amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm bɛ, “Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yɛ̌ mmu ábhɨ́kɨ́ kaysi bɛ́ chɔŋ mɛ́mfakari wáwák, bɔ́ kɛ̌ Mandɛm átóŋtí ábhʉ́rɛ́ ntá bǒ abhɛn bákɔŋ yi.”
Bě bǎchi nyaka ndǔ ɛjuri. Nɛ̌nɛ, ɛnɛ́ Mandɛm áchɛ́mɛ́ bhe nɛ Yesu Acha, bɔ́ŋ ká ɛkakánɛkɔ ɛnɛ ɛ́kwáy nɛ bo abhɛn bachi amɛm bɛdiɛ́rɛ́.
Yɛ̌ nɔ, bɛyǎ bo bághók, bábho bɛkoŋo yi. Asɔt bhɔ sayri, abho bɛghati bhɔ ɛnyu Mandɛm abhak nɛ bho mbɔ Mfɔ wap ámbu nɔkɔ abhɛn báyàŋ yi ambu bhɔ.
Are yáŋ mɛnyiɛ nɛnyiɛ́ bakók, kɛ yɛ̌ mmu kɛchyɛ yi ɛnyɨŋ mɛnyiɛ.
Bákɔŋ nkwɔ́ bɛchɔkɔ ndǔ bɛbhaká kɛnókó amɛm bɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt nɛ ndǔ bɛpa.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ndǔ ɛká Mandɛm ǎrɛ̀m ɛrɨ́rɨ́ ɛ̌ti Dɛmɛ́triyɔs. Yɛ̌ chi nɛpɛ́m ɛni nɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ akɔŋ tɛtɛp Mandɛm nɛ achi ɛrɨ́tí mmu. Bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ́rɛ̀m ɛchi tɛtɛp. 
Árɛ́mɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, apá batiɛ́ amɨk, anywɔbhɛri ntɔp nɛ sɛnɔŋ awɔ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ yi apá batiɛ́, asɔt ntɔp wu achɔri yi amɨ́k
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nywɔp Yesu are tɔ́ŋ bo amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm. Ɛ́ghaka nɔkɔ běku, ankó andɔk ambʉrɛ amfay njiɛ mɛnɔk Ólif.
Nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́, bǒbati ɛtɔk, bǒ batí bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm bákɛ́m ɛchɛmɛ ɛghǒ yap. Básɔ́t Yesu barɔk arɛ́ nɛ yi.
Dɨŋɨ́ ká tɛtɛp bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ bághàti Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ndǔ mmɨk nkɛm, chɔŋ bo mándɛm ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ mɔ́ngɔrɛ́ anɛ ákʉ́.” Nɛ ndǔ bo bárɛ̀m ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ yi ákʉ́, chɔŋ mántɨ́k nɔkɔ yi. 
Mpú rɔ bɛ́bhɔŋ maŋák mbɔnyunɛ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ be mǎnɨk Mandɛm mmʉɛt ɛ̌ti ya nɛ bɛ́ ndǔ bɛtaŋ Ɛfóŋó Yesu Kristo, chɔŋ mámfɛrɛ mɛ ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ.
Nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́, bo abhɛn bárɔ́bhɛ́ ɛbhěnyɛn ɛnɛ Yesu nɛ bakoŋo bhi báfú arɛ́, bátɨk bɛ ndiɛrɛ áchwí amɔt kɛ áchí nyaka arɛ, nɛ bɛ Yesu abhɨ́kɨ́ chwe amɛm áchwí wu andɔk nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi. Bɔ́ bárɔ́ nyaka yi bárɔ́k.
Nchí nɨkmʉɛt bɛ mǎnkɛpntɨ nɛ mɛ ndu nchí rɛm kɛpɨ mbɔ ɛchɨŋtɨ́mu. Kɛ́p ká ntɨ nɛ mɛ.
Ndɛn akɔ́rɛ́ nyaka mɔ́kɛt anɛ mbɨ nɛ anɛ ansɛm. Bábhɨ̀ŋɨ nyaka mɔ́kɛt wu bɛ Nɛbhʉɛt anɛ achi Nyáŋá Áchá.
Nɛ mbák baghɔrɛ́ bati apay bachi nɛbhʉɛt amɔt bákɔ̀k nchwi, bákway bɛsɔt amɔt mándɔ achák.
Yɛ̌ agha anɛ áyàŋ bɛpɛmɛ mmʉɛt yi ǎnɛm nɛpɛ́m ɛni. Kɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ áká mɛnɛm nɛpɛ́m ɛni ɛ̌ti ya, ǎbhɔŋ nɔ.
Ángɛl wu átwɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ntá yi arɛm bɛ, “Mmá, nkáká! Mandɛm ayɛt wɔ tontó!” Acha achí nɛ wɔ.
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu árɔ́ ɛbhak ɛnɛ yi ábú mbɛ́ntí ákɔ̀, árɔ̀ŋ, aghɔ́ mbɛbhɛ́ nkabhɛ́nti amɔt chɔkɔ amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́bɛtɨk ɛyi. Aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Mátio. Abhɨŋɨ yí, arɛm bɛ, “Twɔ́, bhák nkoŋo wa.” Mátio afate, abho bɛkoŋo Yesu.
Bɔ̌ chi amɔt bati tándrámɔt báchí nyaka. Anɛ mbɨ abháy ngɔrɛ́, agú kɛbhɔ́ŋ yɛ̌ mmɔ́.
Báká ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt, bátó mbɔk bakoŋo bhap nɛ mbɔk bo Israɛl abhɛn báté ansɛm Hɛ́rɔd ntá Yesu bɛ mámbɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ wɔ ɔchí mmu tɛtɛp, nɛ bɛ́ ɔ̌tɔ̀ŋ bho mbi Mandɛm tɛtɛp. Sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ ɔpú yɨŋɨ mmu ndǔ bɛsí ɔ́ncháy yi.
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, mbák ɔsɔt mɛ mbɔ ntɨ nkʉbɛtɨk Kristo, yi ánáŋ ántwɔ́ awu, syɛpti yi nɛ maŋák nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyu ɔ́syɛpti nɔkɔ mɛ.
Mandɛm ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛkʉ yi ankway ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbi, ayibhiri arɔp mmu anɛ áchyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ághòk yi.
Ɛ̌tiyɔ kɛ nkaysi yɛ bɛ ɛrɨ mfyɛ́ bɛtaŋ bɛ bɔ̌mayɛsɛ mánjámbɨ mántwɔ awu mǎntoŋti akap anɛ bǎfyɛ bariɛp bɛchyɛ kɛ mɛ̌ntwɔ. Ɛrɨ bɛkʉ bɛ akap wu ámbák chi anɛ áfù be antɨ, puyɛ̌ chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mányiɛrɛ be nyiɛrɛ mǎnkʉ.
Básɔ́t yɛ Yesu ɛkɛt Káyfas betí beti bárɔk ndǔ sɛnta gɔ́bhanɔ nɛ yi. Gɔ́bhanɔ abhak mmǔ Rom. Babhɔŋɔ́ bo Israɛl kɛchwe ndu áchá gɔ́bhanɔ. Ɛbhé yap ɛ́rɛ̀m nyaka bɛ́ mbák mmu Israɛl ánchwé ɛkɛt mmu anɛ ápú mmu Israɛl, apú bhák pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí Mandɛm. Ndu báyàŋ nyaka mɛnyiɛ Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ, bɔ́ kɛyaŋ bɛ́bhak nɛ bakwap bɛsí Mandɛm.
Bɔ̌bha, nchí sɨŋ ntá yɛka mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm afóŋórí bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛka ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo.
Hɛ́rɔd ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, abhɨŋɨ mankɔ bhɔ, abhɔ́ŋ kɛpɨ nɛ bhɔ ansɛm ansɛm, abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ́ mángátí yi mpok anɛ bɔ baghɔ nɛmbe ɛnɔ atú ɛtɔk yap.
Sɛ́chí yɛ chí awɔ́-bɛtɨk Mandɛm. Aghókó bhɛsɛ, abhat nɛ Yesu Kristo, bɛ́ sɛ́nkʉ́ nɔ́kɔ́ chí bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ. Nɛ Mandɛm anáŋ átóŋtí nyaka bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ ábhʉ́rɛ́ ntá yɛsɛ, bɛ sɛ́nkʉ nɔkɔ bhɔ. 
Mpok ágháká nɔ́kɔ́ kɛ́kwɔ́t anɛ Mandɛm asɔt Yesu amfay, Yesu akʉ ntɨ ɛni bɛrɔŋ Yerúsalɛm nɛ abho bɛrɔŋ.
Nchi ghati yɛ́ wɔ bɛ́ mɔ́ngɔrɛ́-nɛ atɔ̌ŋ bɛyǎ ɛkɔŋ bɛtɔŋ bɛ Mandɛm afóŋórí bɛyǎ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ́. Kɛ mmu anɛ ákáysí bɛ bɛbʉ́ bhi ɛbhɛn Mandɛm ákway bɛfóŋóri bɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ ya, ǎtɔ̀ŋ chi mandú ɛkɔŋ.”
Mák nɛ Arístakɔs nɛ Demas nɛ Lukas, batɨ̌ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk Mandɛm, bátò bhe bakak nkwɔ́.
Abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka nkɨ, atí wú, atwɔ́ nɛ nkáp, abhʉrɛ bɛsí bǒnto Yesu.
Atɔ́ŋ yɛ mmʉɛt ntá mpǎy bakoŋo bhi mpok amɔt. Báyá bácha bati hɔndrɛt ɛtay (). Yɛ̌ndu mbɔk ɛyap mǎnáŋ bágú, bɛyǎ bhap bábhʉɛ́t nɛpɛ́m.
Aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Bǎkɛ́ chɔŋti mmɨk, bǎkɛ́ chɔŋti bɔmanyu nɛ bǎkɛ́ chɔŋti mɛnɔk kpátɛ sɛ̌mfyɛ ɛrɨŋ Mandɛm aywɛsɛ nɛfó yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nkʉbɛtɨk aywi.”
Bǒ mankɛm abhɛn bachi arɛ́ bare di mɔ́wu mámbyaka nɔkɔ amɔ antɨ. Kɛ Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Bɔ́t ká kɛbhɔ. Mɔ́nɛ abhɨkɨ gú. Ǎbhʉ̀rɛ chí kɛnɔ́!”
Dɔ́k yɛ nɛ bhɔ amɛm ɛkɛrákap bɛ mǎnsó bɛsí nɛ Mandɛm, bɛtɔŋ bɛ nku yap amay. Wɔmbɔ̌ŋ chyɛ̌ nkáp anɛ bɔ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛchyɛ kɛ mǎmu bati yap. Chɔŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́nkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu andɨŋɨ bɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bárɛ̀m ɛ̌ti yɛ bɛ́pú tɛtɛp, nɛ bɛ́ ɔ̌bhʉ̀rɛ bɛbhé Moses.
Nɨk nɔ́kɔ́ ká mmʉɛt ɛ̌ti yɛsɛ. Sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ batɨ yɛsɛ achi pɛ́pɛ́p, nɛ sɛ́yaŋ bɛbhak chak ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ sɛ́kʉ̀.
Kɛ yɛ̌ chi mpok Máikɛl mǔnti bɔángɛl ákɛ̀m nyaka ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ Satan ɛ̌ti mmu wap anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛsɔt ɛrɛnɛ Moses, abhɨ́kɨ́ sɔt bɛtaŋ ndǔ mmʉɛt yi bɛ́ ándɛm ɛbɛ́ptí ɛnyɨŋ ntá Satan. Arɛm nyaka chi bɛ, “Mandɛm Acha ánji wɔ!”
Mandɛm Ɛtayɛsɛ nɛ Yesu Kristo Acha mántɔ́ŋ be bɛrɨ̌ndu mánchyɛ be kpák.
Njɨŋɨ yɛ, ngɔ́ ndǔ ngɛ́mtáy bɔángɛl bate bakabhɛ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi nɛpɛ́m, nɛ bǒbati. Ngók bɛyɔŋ ɛbhap.
Ndu mɛ̌ghati bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ nɛ, kɛ nchí ghɔ́ ɛsɔŋɔri, nɛ ngɛm amɔ mbɔ nkʉ bɛbʉ́. Kɛ mmu ápú kwáy bɛ́fe Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ.
Ndu sɛ́ghɔ̀ bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛ̌ti sɛ́bhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Kristo nɔ́ kɛ Mandɛm áfʉɛt ntá Kristo bɛchyɛ bhɛsɛ nɛpɔptǐntɨ́.
Nɛchwe anɛ Yesu achwe amɛm áchwi, mmu anɛ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri nyaka yi, abho mɛnɨk yi mmʉɛt bɛ́ ándɔ́ yí ándɔ́k nɛ yi.
Abɨk nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chí mbɔ ɛnɛ́ nkʉ anɛ ábɨ̀k. Ábɨ́kɨ́ nɔ́kɔ́, nɛfaŋ asáy ndɔŋ tándrámɔt.
Ɛwak ɛ́mɔt, mbɔ nkarɛnka ɛrat nɛ ngósí, aghɔ́ kɛnɔ́ amɨ́k anti fúú. Aghɔ́ sayri ndu ángɛl Mandɛm amɔt átwɔ́ ábhɨ́ŋɨ́ yi bɛ, “Kɔnéliɔs!”
Mpok yɔ, bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ bǒbati ɛtɔk báchɛm amɛm sɛnta Mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm. Mǔngo wu aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Káyfas.
Sɛ́nɨ̀kmʉɛt bɛ Yesu Acha ánkʉ ɛkɔŋ ɛyɛka nɛ batɨ nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu achak ɛ́ngó ɛ́ndɔ́k nɔ́kɔ́ chí ambɨ, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ ntá yɛka.
Bábhɛ́p yɛ yi bɛ, “Ɛtayɛ achí fá?” Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mɛ, nɛ yɛ̌ Ɛtaya, bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ. Mbɔ bǎrɨ́ŋɨ́ mɛ, mbʉ bǎrɨŋɨ Ɛtaya nkwɔ.”
Mandú mpok, bǒ mmɨk bápú pɛrɛ ghɔ́ mɛ kɛ bǎghɔ́ chɔŋ mɛ. Nɛ tɛ̌ndu mpɛt nchi bhak chɔŋ nɛpɛ́m, chɔŋ bě nkwɔ mǎmpɛt mǎmbak nɛpɛ́m.
Dɨŋɨ́ bɛ́ ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ yɛ ɛnyɨŋ ndu bɛtɨk ɛbhɛsɛ́ mbɔnyunɛ ntɨ ɛnɛ nɛ́pú chak bɛsí Mandɛm.
Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bápɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nsɛm anywɔ́p, baghɔkɔ́ bhi bápɛt babhɛp yi mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti nkúbhɛ́ ndaka wu.
Bákɛ́m bǒnto báfyɛ́ ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ.
Ǎchɔ̀kɔ nyaka chí ndǔ manɛm nɛ yɛ̌ mmu kɛpɛrɛ kwáy bɛgwɔt yi yɛ̌ chí nɛ ngɛm.
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ, chɔŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́, ɛ́mfú kpoŋoroŋ, nɛ ɛnɛ́ bábhɛ́sɛ́ ɛ́mfú kpoŋoroŋ.
Táytɔs, ghatí bakoŋo Yesu bɛ mámbɔŋ nɛsɛptǐmʉɛt nta bo bati ɛtɔk nɛ bo abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ amfay yap. Bákɛ́ tɔ́ŋ nɛtaŋántɨ nɛ bɛ́ ɛ́mbák wɨkɨrɨk nta yap bɛ́kʉ bɛtɨk nɛ ntɨ nɛmɔt.
Yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛpu cha Mandɛm.”
Mánaŋ nyaka basɨŋ nnyɛ́n ndǔ nɛfó ɛni. Bǒ kɛrɨŋɨ ntí nnyɛ́n ɛnɔ. Nnyɛ́n ɛ́nɛrɛ nɛ́bhak bɛ, “Nnɛ́m ɛtɔk Bábilɔn chi nnɔ baghɔrɛ́-nɛkɔ nɛ bɛpɔ̌ mɛnyɨŋ ndǔ mmɨk nkɛm.”
Fɛstɔs áyàŋ nyaka bo Israɛl mankɔŋ yi. Ɛ́kʉ́ abhɛp Pɔ̌l bɛ, “Ɔkɔŋ bɛ́ko Yerúsalɛm bɛ́ ntáŋ ndak anɛ arɛ?”
Nɛ bághók ɛtaŋtí ɛyɔŋɔ́ mmba, nɛ bághók Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm nkwɔ. Bɛcháy bɛ́kɛ́m bɔ, bábho mɛnɨkmʉɛt bɛ Mandɛm andɔ bɛrɛm kɛpɨ nɛ bhɔ,
Nɛ ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka basɛ́mɛ́ ákway bɛkʉ nɛpɛ́m ɛni nɛ́nsap, yɛ chi mandú nɨŋɨnɨŋɨ nɛ́nchá ɛnyu nɛbhɔŋɔ bɛbhak?
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Ɛ́chí tɛtɛp bɛ́ Ɛláija abhɔŋ bɛ́yámbɨ antwɔ́, angoko yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ fá amɨk, kɛ Mpɛmɛ antwɔ.
Mandɛm áfɛ́rɛ bhɛsɛ́ ndǔ nɛwú, nɛ chɔŋ andɔk ambɨ bɛpɛmɛ bhɛsɛ. Sɛ́bhàka ntɨ chi nɛ yi bɛ chɔŋ ampɛt ampɛmɛ bhɛsɛ.
Ɛnɛ́ bárɔ̀ŋ, ngɔrɛ́ amɔt afú Yesu ansɛm, arɔk pɛtii, atɔk nkokoŋ nkú yi. Ngɔrɛ́ wu ǎfɛ̀rɛ nyaka manoŋ ndǔ mamiɛ́ byo nɛ apay.
Bǒbati bachiǎkap bárɔ́k ntá Páílet barɛm bɛ, “Ɔ́kɛ́ sɨ́ŋ bɛ, ‘Mfɔ bo Israɛl.’ Sɨ́ŋ chí bɛ, ‘Mmǔ-nɛ arɛm nyaka bɛ achí Mfɔ bo Israɛl.’”
Ɛnɛ́ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi babhʉɛt ɛbhak ɛ́mɔt nɛ Yesu, yi abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ,
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, tɨ́k nsɛm ndǔ nkaysi bɛbʉ́ anɛ achi wɔ antɨ ɔ́nɨkmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm Acha. Ngufú chɔŋ amfoŋori nkaysi anɛ achi wɔ antɨ.
Ngɔrɛ́ abʉɛ́ arɔk amɛm baso, nɛbhʉɛt anɛ Mandɛm atoŋti ntá yi bɛ máne yi arɛ ndǔ manywɔp nka amɔt nɛ.
Mpok Mandɛm ásɔ́rɛ́ Ábraham bɛ achi chak, mánaŋ basyɛp nyaka yi kɛ? Chi mpok bábhɨ́kɨ́ re syɛp yi, puyɛ̌ mpok manaŋ basyɛphɛ yi.
Ángɛl amɔt ndǔ abhɛn tándrámɔt abhɛn bakɛmɛ bɛkwɔp tándrámɔt atwɔ́ arɛm ntá ya bɛ, “Twɔ́, chɔŋ ntɔŋ wɔ ntɛ́msí anɛ Mandɛm áchyɛ chɔŋ nta nnɛ́m ngɔrɛ́-nɛkɔ, nɔ chi, ɛrɛm ɛtɔk ɛnɛ ɛchi kɛkwɔt nɛ bɛyǎ manyɛ́n agho.
Nkáysí bɛ ɛchi chak bɛ ntɨ́k nɔ́kɔ́ bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ndu mbʉɛ́t fá amɨk bɛ bǎkɛ́ bhʉrɛ kɛnɔ́,
BɔPɔ̌l bárɔk báfʉɛ́t bɛtɔk Amfípolis nɛ Apolónia báchwɔp ɛtɔk Tɛsalónika, nɛbhʉɛt anɛ ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí bo Israɛl ɛchi.
Báre dɛpti yi anti nɛ mɛnɔk. Mámpati nɔkɔ yí batiɛ́ amʉɛt nɛ mántɛp nɔkɔ mánɛ́n bɛsí bhi mbɔ́ bɛ báchyɛ̀ nɔ yi chi kɛnókó.
Yesu apɛt arɛm bɛ, “Ɛrɨ́tí ɛnɔk ɛ́pú nyu bɛbɛ́ptí kɛpɛm. Nɛ ɛbɛ́ptí ɛnɔk ɛ́pú nyu bɛrɨ́tí kɛpɛm.
Bě bho bǎpà, mǎndɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Mbák ɛ́pú ɛchɔŋ nɔ́ mbúrɛ́, chɔŋ sɛ́ndɔ́k ɛtɔk ɛgho fú, sɛ́nchɔkɔ arɛ́ ndǔ mmíɛ́ nɛmɔt sɛ́nkɔ ɛsiɛ́, sɛ́mbɔŋ bɛyǎ nkáp,” Ghók ká.
Nɛ́nɛ, nchí twɔ ntá yɛ, nɛ nchí rɛm mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ndǔ mpok mbʉɛ́t fá amɨk, bɛ́ maŋák ama ámbák nɛ bhɔ.
“Bǎrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ ndǔ manywɔp apay ɛchɔŋ, Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ ɛbho. Chɔŋ mánti Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm ntá bǒmpap abha, mánkɛ́m mɛ mango ndǔ ɛkotákátí.”
Batɛmɛ́ nɛnu básɔt yi bárɔk amɛm áchá gɔ́bhanɔ. Bábhɨŋɨ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu báchák mankɛm nɛbhʉɛt amɔt.
Mǔngo bachiǎkap wu ákʉ̀ bɛtɨk ɛbhi amɛm ɛtɛm ɛnɛ ɛchi nyáŋá, ɛnɛ́ mbɔŋ Mandɛm Acha áté, kɛbhak chi nkwǎŋwaŋ.
Nɛ́ chí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Jóɛl arɛmɛ nyaka bɛ chɔŋ ɛmfakari. Joɛl arɛm nyaka bɛ,
Nchí ghati bhe bɛ, mbák nkʉbɛtɨk wu ákʉ nɔ chi-bɛtɨk ywi ǎchyɛ yi bɛtaŋ amfǎy mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhí mɛnkɛm.
Ghɔ́ bɛ bápày Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ntá bho, nɛ ghɔ́ bɛ́ báfyɛ̀ bho ntɨ nɛ bɛ bátɔ̀ŋ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm. Kʉ nɔ, kpátɛ mpok anɛ mɛ̌twɔ̀ awu.
Bákwɛ́n yɛ bɛyɔŋ bɛyɔŋ. Bápɛ́rɛ taka, Pɔ̌l aghati bhɔ ndak achak amɔt bɛ, “Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ arɛm nyaka tɛtɛp mpok yi akʉ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Aisáya angati bachǐmbɨ bhɛka bɛ:
Ɛyɔ ɛ́chyɛ̀ yɛ bɛsɛ nɛpɔptǐntɨ́. Bǎfyɛ́ bhɛsɛ ntɨ, nɛ bɛrɔŋ ambɨ, sɛchi maŋák ɛ̌ti maŋák amɛn Táytɔs ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ndǔ be mankɛm bǎsɔ́rɛ́ yi awu sayri, bǎkʉ́ ntɨ ɛni nɛpɔp amɛm.
Arɔ bhɔ nkáp bɛkoŋo ɛnyǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap ákwày bɛkʉ nɛ aywi nkáp. Achyɛ amɔt bɛbhǎ nkáp bɛtay. Achyɛ achák bɛbhǎ nkáp bɛpay. Achyɛ anɛfu ɛbhǎ nkáp ɛ́mɔt. Afa yɛ arɔk nɛkɔ.
Chɔŋ anja bɛyǎ bo Israɛl, mámpɛtnsɛm ntá Mandɛm Acha wap.
Kɔnéliɔs akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Ɛ́kʉ manywɔp anwi ɛchɔŋ ɛnɛ́ nchí amɛm ɛkɛt ɛya nchí nɨkmʉɛt. Nkúbhɛ́ mpok mbɔ anɛ, mbɔ nkarɛnka ɛ́rát nɛ ngósí, mmu abhesi mɛ bɛsí nɛ nkú anɛ are ghɔɔ,
Bǒnto Yesu nɛ bǒbatí nɛ bǒnkwɔ́ Yesu mankɛm bághɔ́ bɛ́ chí ɛrɨ́tí nkaysi. Báká ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt bɛ mánjáp bo mánto Antiɔk nɛ Pɔ̌l nɛ Banábas. Báyáp yɛ Sáilas nɛ Júdas anɛ nnyɛ́n ɛni nɛ́chák nɛ́chí bɛ Básabas. Bɔ batí apay bábhak bǒbatí nkwɔ Yesu.
Ángɛl ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ̀m, ngók ɛwat mbɔ ɛnɛ ngɛmtay-bǒ amfay ndǔ bábɨ̀k bɛ, “Haleluya! Yí kɛ ápɛ́mɛ́ bhɛsɛ. Kɛnókó nɛ bɛtaŋ bɛchi amɔ́ Mandɛm.
Áchwi arɔk achwe ndu ntó ɛ̌siɛ́p ɛnɛ babhɨkɨ re ghaka angɔkɔnyɛ́n. Ntí áchwí ápaŋ arɛ. Bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn mbʉ́ɛ́p bɛ́kʉ mpɛ́rɛ́nyɛn ɛ́rákáti nnɛt áchwí.
Mbɨ́kɨ́ yáŋ bɛ mǎmbɔ́ŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛsɔŋɔri batɨ yɛka amɛm. Mmǔ anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ bháy ngɔrɛ́, afyɛ́ ntí ndu bɛkʉ bɛtɨk Acha Yesu, nɛ ǎkaysi bɛkʉ́ chí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛkʉ Mandɛm ambɔŋ maŋák nɛ yi.
Yesu apɛt abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Aghǎ bǎyàŋ?” Bárɛ́m bɛ, “Yesu mmu Násárɛt.”
Jɔ̌n árɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, sɛ́ghɔ mmu anɛ apu ndǔ nkwɔ ywɛsɛ ndu ábòk bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ ndǔ nnyɛ́n ɛna. Sɛ́gháti yi bɛ, ákɛ́pɛrɛ kʉ nɔ mbɔnyunɛ apú ndǔ nkwɔ ywɛsɛ.”
Nchí ghati yɛ bǒbati abhɛn bachi ndǔ nkwɔ ywɛka mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́kʉ. Mɛ nkwɔ nchí mǔnti mbɔ bhe. Ngɔ̌ nyaka ɛnyu Kristo ághɔ̀ ɛsɔŋɔri nɛ nchí ndǔ mpǎy bo abhɛn Mandɛm ákʉ̀ chɔŋ mǎngɔ kɛnɛ́m Kristo mpok yi átwɔ̀.
Mbák ámbɛ́p wɔ tansi, ɔ̌chyɛ yi nnyɔ́ kɛ?
Yɛ̌ mmu achí chi mmu Israɛl yɛ ápú, yɛ̌ mmu achí chí nsɛm yɛ mɔ̌mɨk, yɛ chí ngɔrɛ́ yɛ mbakanɛm, be mankɛm abhɛn babhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Kristo bǎrɔp chí ɛnyu ɛ́mɔt.
Nchí ghati bhe bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ básɨ́ŋɨ́ ndǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ̌ti ya, ɛbhɔŋ bɛfu tɛtɛp. Nɔ chi ɛnɛ́ ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Básɔt yi mbɔ nkʉ bɛbʉ́ amɔt.’ Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn básɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛ̌ti ya bɛ́bhɔŋ bɛfu tɛtɛp.”
Mǔngo batɛmɛ́ nɛnu are yáŋ bɛ́rɨŋɨ mbɔ̌ŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bo Israɛl bárɛ̀m bɛ́ Pɔ̌l akʉ. Nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́, arɛm yɛ bɛ mámfɛ́rɛ́ Pɔ̌l ngɛm amɔ. Achyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ́ bǒbatí bachiǎkap nɛ bǒbatí ɛtɔk mankɛm mánchɔ́kɔ́ mánjɨ́ŋɨ́ ndaká Pɔ̌l. Báchɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ achyɛ ɛyɔŋ básɔt Pɔ̌l bakʉ yi ate bɛsí bhap.
“Acha, bo abhɛn báwáy barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ bhɛ nɛ mámokoti bɛbhak ɛbhɛn sɛ́chyɛ̀ wɔ akap. Mɛ awánti kɛ ndɔ́bhɛ́ nɛ báyàŋ bɛway mɛ nkwɔ.”
Ngɔrɛ́ wu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Acha, ɛ́chí tɛtɛp. Kɛ mmú ɛ́nyiɛ nɔkɔ bɛchɔkɔtí ɛbhɛn bɛ́fù ntá mǎmbɔ amfay ɛ́fɛ́mɛ́ nɛnyiɛ mɛ́nkwɛnti amɨk.”
Ɛ́chí mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Acha árɛm bɛ, ‘Nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyu ɛchi tɛtɛp bɛ nchí nɛpɛ́m, ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ ɛchi tɛtɛp bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu abhɔŋ bɛtɛp mánɛ́n bɛsí bha. Nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu abhɔŋ bɛrɛm nɛ nnyu ywi bɛ, Mɛ Nchí Mandɛm.’”
Babhɔ̌ŋ nyaka awɔ́-bɛtɨk ámɔ́t nɛ Pɔ̌l, nɔ́ chí bɛtɨk bɛ́ghóko bɛ́tɛm nɛ ndɛn. Pɔ̌l achɔkɔ nɛ bhɔ mángoko nɔkɔ bɛ́tɛm.
mandɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Amen! Ɛrɨ bǒ mándɛm mpoknkɛm bɛ Mandɛm aywɛsɛ kɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ. Achi ndɨŋɨndak nɛ abhɔ̌ŋ kɛfɔ kɛnkɛm. Sɛnchyɛ́ yi bakak, sɛnchyɛ́ yi kɛnókó, sɛ́mbɨti yi. Abhɔŋ bɛyǎ mɛnwɔp!” Amen.
Mmǔ ntí bo Mandɛm abhɔŋ bɛbhak mmu anɛ ákɛ̀m ɛfo yi sayri, ankʉ bɔ̌bhi mámbak bo abhɛn bághòk yí mánchyɛ nɔkɔ bo kɛnókó ndu yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ndɛ́mɛ́ puyɛ̌ chí nkaysi bǒ mmɨk. Pú ɛnyiŋ ɛ́rɛ́ ɛ́mɔt kɛ ɛbhé Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ́mɛ́?
Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ mmǔ anɛ achi nyaka nkoŋo Kristo. Ɛ́gháká mamiɛ́ byo nɛ anwi ɛchɔŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm ásɔ́rɛ́ yi tɛ amfay.
Bákʉ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, mándɛm nɔkɔ bɛ, “Ndɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm, Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò, ghati bhɛsɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm akʉ wɔ ɔ́rɨ́ŋɨ́. Ghatí bhɛsɛ! Agha ádɛ́bhɛ́ nɔ́ wɔ?” 
Ábraham achí nyaka chi Áisek, Áisek abhak chi Jekɔ́p, Jekɔ́p abhak chi Júda nɛ bɔ̌mayi. Júda achí nyaka chi Pɛ́res nɛ mɔ́mayi Sɛrá. Máyap aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Táma. Pɛ́res abhak chi Hɛ́srɔn, Hɛ́srɔn abhak chi Rám. Rám achí nyaka chi Amínadap, Amínadap abhak chi Náshɔn, Náshɔn abhak chi Sálmɔn. Sálmɔn achí nyaka chi Bóas. Nnɔ Bóas aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Ráhab. Bóas abhak chi Óbɛd. Nnɔ Óbɛd aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Rút. Óbɛd abhak chi Jése,
Baghɔk Yesu bárɔ́k bakʉ ntoŋti mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi aghati bhɔ.
Sɔt ka mpok mbɔnyunɛ bo bákɛ̀m chɔŋ bhe mámfyɛ amɔ bǒ batí ɛtɔk, mándɛp manɛt ayɛka amɛm bɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt ɛbhap.
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, yɛ̌ chí mmɛ kɛ ngátí nyaka bhe Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́, yɛ̌ chi bǒnto báchák, bɛsɛ mankɛm sɛ́ghàti bho chi nkúbhɛ́ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ́rɛ ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo, nɛ yɔ kɛ̌ be mǎnókó. 
Sɛ́bhɔŋ ákɔ́rɛ́ ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu Kristo ákʉ́ nta yɛsɛ mbák sɛ́ndɔ́k ambɨ bɛte kpirí ndǔ nɛsɨkɨ́ntɨ ɛnɛn sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka nɛ yi ndǔ nɛbhǒnɛt. Sɛ́bhɔŋ bɛkʉ nɔ tɛ ndǔ ngwɛnti.
Mpok ɛpa ákwáy nɔ́kɔ́, ató bɔ̌-bɛtok abhi bɛ́ mándɔ́k mángátí bǒ abhɛn yi ánáká bɛ mpok akway. Kɛ yɛ̌ amɔt kɛ twɔ.
Mpok yɔ, bɔ́ bárɔŋ yɛ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt ntɛmsi anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti, kɛ bǒ abhɛn bachi chak bɛsí bhi, mǎnchwe ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.”
Nchí nɨkmʉɛt bɛ́ bɛrɨ̌ndu Yesu Kristo Acha mɛ́mbak amɛm batɨ ayɛka. Amen.
Kɛ mbɔŋɔ́nkɨ akɛmɛ mmu wap amɔt bɛ, “Nkwǎnɛ, mbɨ́kɨ́ nyiɛ́ be yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Sɛ́ká ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt nɛ bhe bɛ mɛ̌chyɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka nkáp bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn nywɔp nɛmɔt. Pú nɔ́?
Bě bǎchi bɔ̌ ɛtayɛka Satan, nɛ bǎkɔŋ bɛkʉ chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ɛtayɛka áyàŋ mǎnkʉ. Achí ngwayti bho tɛ nɛbhǒnɛt. Abhɨ́kɨ́ kɔŋ tɛtɛp Mandɛm mbɔnyunɛ tɛtɛp apu nɛ yi. Mpok yi ásè nsé, ǎkʉ̀ chí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kɔ́ ndɔ́ŋ ámɔt nɛ ɛpɨŋ ɛyi, mbɔnyunɛ achi nsěnse, nɛ nsé ɛnkɛm ɛ́fù chí ntá yi.
Mɛnyɨŋɨ́ nɛnu ɛbhɛsɛ puyɛ̌ chi ɛbhɛn bakwǎŋwaŋ. Mandɛm kɛ áchyɛ̀ bhɛsɛ bhɔ, nɛ bɛ́bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ bɛchɔŋti bɛpok ɛbhɛn bǒmpap abhɛsɛ bábhɛ̀sɛ.
Mɔ́ngɔrɛ́ wu anáŋ árɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́fákárí nɛ yi. Afú angwɛrɛ nɔkɔ gbagbǎgbak nɛ bɛcháy. Atɛp mánɛ́n bɛsí Yesu aghati yi tɛtɛp nkɛm.
Arɛm yɛ ntá yi bɛ, “Báchyɛ́ bɛtaŋ nɛ kɛfɔ̌ mmɨk nkɛm ntá ya, nɛ nchí kway bɛchyɛ kɔ ntá yɛ̌ agha anɛ nkɔ́ŋɔ́. Chɔŋ nchyɛ́ wɔ bǒbhɛn mɛnkɛm nɛ kɛfɔ ɛkap.
Yesu árɛ́m nɔ́, arɔp atú Gálili. 
Páílet ághókó nɔkɔ nɔ, abho bɛyaŋ mbi bɛfɛrɛ Yesu amɔ. Kɛ bo Israɛl bárɔ́k chí ambɨ bɛbɨk bɛ, “Mbák ɔ́ndɔ́ mmǔ-nɛ ándɔ́k, nɔ́ ɔpú mmʉɛ́rɛ Mfɔ Rom! Mmu anɛ ǎrɛ̀m bɛ áchí Mfɔ, chi mmǔ anɛ ánù nɛ Mfɔ Rom bɛ ambak ndǔ mmʉɛt ɛyi!”
Apɛtnsɛm ɛtɔk ɛyi Násárɛt. Ɛnɛ́ yi átɔ̀ŋ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm amɛm ɛkɛt ɛnɛ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt ɛyap, bo bábhak maknkay tontó. Bábhó bɛbhɛp batɨ bɛ, “Aré bhɔŋ ɛnɛn ɛnyǔ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak fá? Aré bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ fá ndu bɛkʉ bɛrɛm mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛnyu ɛnɛ?
Abhɛ́p mmu wu bɛ, ‘Nkwǎnɛ, ɔkʉ́ ná kɛ ɔ̌chwe fá, nkú-nɛbhay wɔ amʉɛt tí?’ Ɛcha mmu wu ɛnyɨŋ bɛrɛm.
Ɛnɛ́ baghɔrɛ́ bhɔ bárɔ̀ŋ, ɛ́fákari bɛ mbɔk bo abhɛn bábhàbhɛri nnɛm bárɔ́k Yerúsalɛm bágháti bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛfakari mpok ángɛl Mandɛm ásɛ́bhɛ́ átwɔ́ ndǔ nnɛm.
Mpok aghaka anɛ bo Israɛl mányìɛ ɛpa ɛnɛ bátɨ̀k ndu mánɨ́kɨ́mʉɛt báfyɛ́ ɛkɛrákap ɛnɛ Yerúsalɛm awɔ Mandɛm.
Ndǔ mamiɛ́ ankɛm anɛ́ bɔ báchɔ́kɔ́ ɛtɔk Íjip nɛ anɛ́ báchí amɛm baso kɛ báchwe Kánǎn ábhák mbɔ mamiɛ́ bɛsa bɛbay nsɛm byo (). Achyɛ yɛ bhɔ bataŋá manyé nɛ bɔ babhak kpátɛ ndǔ mpok Samuɛl anɛ achi nyaka ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm.
Mpok nchí bhak nɛ bǒ abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl nchí kʉ mɛnyɨŋ chí mbɔ mmu anɛ ápú koŋo bɛbhé Moses, ndǔ nchí nu bɛ́kwák bɔ́ mántwɔ ntá Yesu Acha. Ɛnɛ ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tɔ́ŋ bɛ́ mpú bhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé Mandɛm. Ɛbhé Yesu Kristo achyɛ kɛ̌ nchí koŋo.
Bǎbhɔŋ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ mǎnáŋ bǎtɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛka tɛtɛp.
Yesu aghati yi bɛ, “Dɔ́k bhɨŋɨ nnɛ́m aywɛ, twɔ́ nɛ yí.”
Bǒbhɔ bákù nyaka bawɛt amɛn ɛrɨ́tí ɛriɛp mbɔ amɛn bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ sínamɔn, nɛ ínsɛns nɛ mɨ́ɨ nɛ frankinsɛns. Bákù nyaka bɛyé ɛbhɛn bɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛrɨ́tí ɛriɛp nɛ bɛ́kʉ̀ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛmfʉɛt anyu. Bɔ bákù nyaka mmɛ́m nɛ bawɛt nɛ fláwa nchwi, nɛ ɛnyu nchwi anɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ wit. Bákù nyaka nkwɔ mpɔŋ nɛ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n nɛ mpɔŋɔ́ndɨk nɛ bɛ́kárɨk ɛbhɛn mpɔŋɔ́ndɨk ɛ́yà. Bǒbhɔ bákù nyaka bakwǎŋwaŋ nkwɔ mbɔ basɛm.
Mandɛm akɛ́mɛ́ nyaka yi bɛ yi? Akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Mbʉ́rɛ́ bo nka tándrámɔt () abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ nɨkmʉɛt ntá mandɛm nsé anɛ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ Bál.”
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Wáwák! Mbák mmu ántóŋórí bɛkʉ wɔ bɛbʉ́, ɔbhɔŋ bɛ́fóŋóri yi maŋɔk bɛsa bɛrat nsɛm byo, ndɔŋ tándrámɔt.”
Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛnyǔ mɛ̌kwáy bɛbhak mbɔ mmu anɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛ́pú sɔŋɔri yí mpok mɛnyɨŋ bɛ́chɛ́bhɛ́ mɛ́ nɛ yɛ̌ chí mpok mbɔ́ŋɔ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ. Yɛ̌ ɛ́mbak bɛ́ yi, ngɔk bɛbhak mbɔ mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ mpǒknkɛm, yɛ̌ chí mpok nnyiɛ́ njwí, nɛ mpok anɛ nchɔkɔ nsay, nɛ yɛ̌ mbɔ́ŋ, yɛ̌ mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ.
Bǎkɛ́ sɔŋɔri yɛ batɨ̌ yɛka bɛbhɛp ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ mɛ́nyiɛ nɛ ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ mɛnyu.
Ɛ̌ti ɛyɔ kɛ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi fá amɨk ɛbhɛn bɛ́chí ndɨkandi mɛnyɨŋɨ́ mbɔŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi amfay bɛ mɛ́mbák pɛ́pɛ́p ɛnyu ɛyɔ. Kɛ ndu bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ mfay mɛ́mbák pɛ́pɛ́p bábhɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɛsɔt chi manoŋ amɛn acha manǒŋ nnya.
Mbɔk bǒnkwɔ Fárisi abhɛn báchí ndǔ ngɛ́mtáy bo bhɔ, bárɛ́m ntá Yesu bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, sáy bakoŋo bhɛ mánchɔkɔ kpák.”
Sɛ́ghɔ̀ yɛ bɛ Mandɛm ǎsɔt bɛ mmu achi chak chi mbák abhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Yesu. Ɛyɔ ɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛkʉ nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mmu ákʉ̀ bɛkoŋo ɛbhé.
Ábraham abhak fá, yɛ̌ nɔ, Mandɛm kɛchyɛ yí yɛ̌ chí mɔ́nɛbhʉɛ́rɛ́ mmɨk. Afyɛ́ chí bariɛp bɛ́chyɛ mmɨk ntá yi nɛ ntá bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ bhi yɛ̌ndu yi abhɨkɨ bhɔŋ nyaka mmɔ́.
Nchí ghati wɔ bɛ, ɔpú fu wawak kpátɛ ɔnchyɛ ákwɔ́ ywɛ ankɛm, yɛ̌nyɨŋ kɛrɔp.”
“Mbɔ̌ŋ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ bɛghati bhe, kɛ mbák ngátí bhe bɔ mɛnkɛm nɛ́nɛ, bǎpú kway bɛ́jwimɛm.
Ná nɛ anɛ bɛkpok tándrámɔt anɛ nká bho ɛnwi mányíɛ́? Bǎghɔ́kɔ́ntɨk brɛt anɛ árɔ́bhɛ́ mǎnyókóti bǎfyɛ ndǔ bɛkay?
Mɛ̌ghàti nyaka bhe chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi tɛtɛp mpoknkɛm. Nɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ chyɛ mɛ ntíánwɔ́p ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ngátí Táytɔs ndɛbhɛ nɔkɔ awɔ́ antɨ ɛ̌ti yɛka, nɛ ɛ́fú nkwɔ tɛtɛp.
Bě abhɛn bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ basɛm, kɛ́m ká bhɔ ɛrɨ́rɨ́ nɛ ɛnyu ɛnɛ ɛchi chak. Bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ be nkwɔ bǎbhɔŋ mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ be amfay. 
Bǒ bhɔ bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu árɛ́mɛ́, bábhó bɛrɔ amɔt amɔt, bɛbho nɛ baseansi. Yesu arɔp aywǐnti nɛ ngɔrɛ́ wu arɛ́ téé, bɛsí bhi.
Símun ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ atwɔ achi nɛ bhɔ́ ndǔ bǒnto mányáŋá bɔ amɔ antí, afɛrɛ nkáp bɛ́chyɛ bǒnto,
Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ɛ́táka atú ɛtɔk wu ankɛm.
Bɛcháy bɛ́kɛ́m bǒ atú Gɛrása wu mankɛm. Bágháti Yesu bɛ́ amfu ɛtɔk ɛyap ándɔ́k. Arɔk achwe amɛm áchwí ndu bɛrɔŋ.
Nɛ Aisáya arɛm nyaka nkwɔ kɛbhɔ́ŋ bɛcháy bɛ, Mandɛm arɛm bɛ, “Bo abhɛn bápú yaŋ nyaka mɛ bághɔ́ mɛ. Ntɔ̌ŋ mmʉɛt ntá bo abhɛn bápú bhɛp mɛ.”
“Bǎkɛ́ chay yɛ̌ mmu anɛ ápàbhe. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bákútí, chɔŋ mánɛnɛ. Nɛ ɛnɛ́ ɛchi bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́, chɔŋ mánkʉ bɛ bo mándɨŋɨ yɔ.
Ɛkáti bɛbhé Moses ɛ́ghàti bhɛsɛ bɛ bábhɔŋ bɛ́tɛ́mti ɛnyǔ ngɔrɛ́ nɛ nɛ batay mángwáy. Ɔrɛm bɛ́ yí?”
Kɛ Mandɛm Acha aghɔ̌ nyaka bɛ bɛ́kwɛ́nɛ́ bɛchí nɛ bǒbhi. Ɛ̌ti yɔ, arɛm bɛ, “Mpok ǎtwɔ̀ anɛ nchí nyu nku achák nɛ bo Israɛl, nɛ bǒ Júda nkwɔ.
Páílet ásɔ́t yɛ Yesu achyɛ ntá yap bɛ mándɔk mángó yi ndǔ ɛkotákátí. 
Árɛ́mɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, ayibhiri mmʉɛt aghɔ́ Yesu téé, kɛ yi kɛrɨŋɨ bɛ chi yi.
Mbʉ́ɛ́p ataŋataŋ abho mɛnu. Ɛkʉ bɛtaŋtí mpɛ́rɛ́nyɛn ɛya anyɛ́n.
Mpok Yesu áchɔ́kɔ́, ányìɛ nɛnyíɛ́, běku nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi. Satan anáŋ achwe nyaka antí Júdas, mmɔ̌ Símun Iskariɔt, ndu bɛkʉ yi ántí Yesu.
Arɛm ntá ya bɛ, ‘Mandɛm bachǐmbɨ bhɛsɛ́ ayap wɔ bɛ́ ɔ́ndɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi atɨ bɛkʉ. Ayap wɔ bɛ ɔ́ngɔ́ anɛ babhɨŋɨ bɛ Mmu Chak. Ayap wɔ bɛ ɔ́ngɔ́k ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fù yi anyu.
Mandɛm ághàti bhɛsɛ mbɔ ɛnyu ɛ́chí amɛm ɛkáti yi bɛ, yi ǎrɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ̌yáŋ chi bɛ bo mángɔ́ ntínso nɛ batɨ, puyɛ̌ chi akabhɛ́nya. Mbɔ bě bǎrɨŋɨ ntí bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn, mbʉ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ ji bǒ abhɛn bɛ́kwɛ́nɛ́ bɛ́pú nɛ bhɔ.’
Mmǔ wu arɛm bɛ, “Acha, nnókó.” Akwɛ́n Yesu bɛkak, abho bɛ́chyɛ yi kɛnókó.
Ɛ́gháká nɔkɔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt ɛnɛn nɛ́kòŋo, ɛtɔk ɛnkɛm ɛ́twɔ́ bɛ́ghok Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm.
Mmɔ̌ bɛtok arɔk atwɔ́, arɛm ntá yi bɛ, ‘Ɛta, nkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɔ́rɛ́mɛ́ kɛ ɛkɛt ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ re jwi.’
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛyɔ nɔ Mandɛm atɨ bɛkʉ ɛchi nyaka bɛ mpok ánáŋ ánkwáy, yi ǎchɛm mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm, ɛbhɛn amfay nɛ ɛbhɛn fá amɨk, amfyɛ́ amɔ Kristo.
Abhɛ́n ɛkɔŋ, bǎchi mankɔ nɛ bǎfʉɛrɛ fʉɛt fá amɨk. Ndu ɛchi nɔ, nnɨkmʉɛt, fɛrɛ́ ká amɔ́ ndǔ barak abʉ́abʉ anɛ mmʉɛt ɛyɛka ɛ́kʉ̀ mǎŋwaka bɛkʉ mbɔnyunɛ mɛnyǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ mɛ́nù nɛ bɛfóŋó ɛbhɛka.
Nɛ́ chi manyɛ́n bachǐmbɨ Yesu Kristo, ɛbhárɛ́mɔ Mfɔ Debhít nɛ Ábraham.
Jɔ̌n kɛ̌ achi mmu anɛ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m ɛ̌ti yi bɛ, ‘Mandɛm arɛm nyaka bɛ, Yɨŋɨ́, chɔŋ ntó mpɔkɔntó wa wɔ ambɨ, bɛ ángókó mbi ywɛ kɛ ɔ́ntwɔ.’”
Nkúbhɛ́ ɛnyu yɔ kɛ ɛ́chí nyaka nɛ Ráhab, ngɔrɛ́-nɛkɔ. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yí ákʉ́ kɛ̌ Mandɛm ághɔ́, asɔt bɛ́ yí achí chak bɛsí bhi. Nɔ́ chí, Ráhab asɔt baghokotǐ kɛpɨ abhɛn báfú Israɛl abhɛsɛ amɛm ɛkɛt ɛyi, achyɛ bhɔ́ maniɛ́. Báfʉɛ́t yɛ́ mbi áchák bápɛtnsɛm Israɛl kɛbhɔ́ŋ ɛsɔŋɔri.
Yesu are rɔ́ŋ nɛ bhɔ. Mpok bághaka kɛkwɔt nɛ ɛkɛt, mǔnti wu ató mamʉɛrɛ bhi bɛ́ mángátí Yesu bɛ, “Acha, kɛ́sɔŋɔri mmʉɛt bɛ́twɔ ndǔ ɛkɛt ɛya. Mbɨ́kɨ́ kway mmu anɛ ɔ́twɔ́ ɛkɛt ɛyi.
Bǎkɛ́ nyiɛ ɛkɔŋ nɛ nkáp. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu abhɔŋ bɛbhak maŋák nɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm yímbɔŋ arɛm bɛ, “Mpú kway bɛrɔ wɔ, mpú kway bɛfɛrɛ ntí nɛ wɔ.”
Aghátí yɛ bo abhɛn báchí arɛ téé bɛ, ‘Sɔt ka ɛbhǎ nkáp ɛyǐ yɔ mǎnchyɛ ntá mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛbha byo.’
Mpok Mandɛm ákʉ́ bachiǎkap abhɛn bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ Lɛ́vi manchyɛ bɛbhé ɛbhɛn bɛ́kwáy nɛ nkwɔ́ bachiǎkap abhɔ, mbɔ bɛtɨk ɛbhap bɛ́kway nyaka bɛkʉ bɛ bo mámbák chak mbɔ ɛnyǔ Mandɛm áyàŋ, mbʉ́ ntí apu anɛ nchiakap achak átwɔ anɛ achi mbɔ Mɛlkísɛdɛk, nɛ abhak kɛkúrí nɛ bachiǎkap abhɛn nnɛrɛ́kɛt Arɔn.
Bɛyǎ bo abhɛn báchí nyaka arɛ bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu árɛ́mɛ́, manyu áchók bhɔ, bɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ ɛnyǔ nɛtɔ́ŋ ɛnɛn Yesu átɔ̀ŋ. 
Mmɔ̌ bɛtok wu arɔk aghati ɛtayi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǒbhɔ bárɛmɛ. Mbɔŋɔ́kɛt abéntɨ. Aghati mɔ̌bɛtok yi wu bɛ, ‘Fú, dɔ́k áyák ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbay anɛ áchí ɛtɔk nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nɛbhʉɛ́t anɛ bo báchí arɛ sɔt bachɛ́bhɛ́bho twɔ ndǔ ɛpa nɛ bhɔ. Twɔ́ nɛ babák nɛ bakɛm nɛ manɛ́mámɨk.’
Fíɛ́ ká mmu anɛ ákʉ́ awu ndak awɔ́ Satan, bɛ́ ánchɔ́ŋtí mmʉɛt yi. Ánáŋ ambak awɔ́ Satan, chɔŋ Satan anchɔŋti mmʉɛt ɛyi. Kʉ ka ɛnyu ɛyɔ nɛ manɔ ywɛka, bɛ Mandɛm ampɛmɛ ɛfóŋó ɛyi ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɛn Yesu Acha ápɛ̀tnsɛm.
Bɔ̌ma, ndu ɛchí mbɔ ɛnyǔ nchí rɛm nɔkɔ, nɛ ɛ̌ti ntínso Mandɛm nɛ bhɛsɛ, nchí kwɛn be bɛkak bɛrɛm bɛ mǎnchyɛ mmʉɛt ɛyɛka ɛnkɛm ntá yi mbɔ akap anɛ achi nɛpɛ́m, nɛ nyáŋá, nɛ anɛ yi akɔŋɔ. Ɛyɔ kɛ ɛchi ɛsayri mbi bɛchyɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó.
Ndu nchí sɨŋ ɛkáti-nɛ, mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛcháy nɛ wɔ mbɔnyunɛ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ chɔŋ ɔ́nkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ́yàŋ wɔ ɔ́nkʉ, nɛ ɔ́nkʉ mbɔŋ ɛncha ɛnyu ɛnɛ mɛ́yàŋ.
Bakak ámbák nɛ Mandɛm mmu ákʉ̀ nɔ bɛfʉɛt ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu Kristo Acha ywɛsɛ ákʉ́.Ɛchi yɛ bɛ ndǔ nkaysi aya, nchí ndǔ kɛsɛmɛ́ ɛbhé Mandɛm, kɛ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛna mbɔ nkwǎŋwaŋ, nchí ndǔ kɛsɛm ɛbhé bɛbʉ́.
mbɔnyunɛ mmǔ anɛ áyàŋ bɛpɛmɛ mmʉɛt yi ǎnɛ́m nɛpɛ́m ɛni. Kɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ áká mɛnɛm nɛpɛ́m ɛni ɛ̌ti ya, ǎbhɔŋ chɔŋ nɔ.
Kɛ Yesu abhɛp yi bɛ, “Júdas, ɔ̌bhɛ̀nɛ Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm ndu bɛti mɛ ntá bǒmpap abha?”
Mandɛm arɔk ambɨ bɛ́ghati yi bɛ: ‘Chɔŋ bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ bhɛ mámbak mankɔ amɛm ɛtɔk bǒ bachak. Bǒ bhɔ mambʉrɛ bhɔ ndu kɛsɛm, mánchyɛ nɔkɔ bhɔ bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri ndu mamiɛ́ bɛsǎ ɛsa.
Yesu akɛmɛ bɛ, “Ɛ́chí mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɔ́rɛ́mɛ́. Kɛ dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ́ mpok átwɔ̀ anɛ bǎghɔ chɔŋ Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm, chɔkɔ ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ, ɛbhe awɔ́nɛm Mandɛm bɛtaŋ mɛnkɛm. Chɔŋ mǎngɔ ndǔ Mmu anɛ áfú amfay átwɔ̀ amɛm nɛbháŋ.”
Yɛ̌ nɔ, bárɛ́m ntá yi bɛ, “Yɛ̌ mmu apú ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt aywɛka anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nnyɛ́n ɛnɔ!”
Ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛni, anáŋ aghɔ nkwɔ bɛrɨ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fù ndu Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm, aghɔ́ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́bhàk chɔŋ ndǔ nɛŋɔkɔ́ mpok ɛnɛn nɛ́twɔ̀ ansɛm.
Mandɛm abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́rɨ́ bɛ́chá antɨ ntá yap, nɛ bɔ bɛchi ntá yɛsɛ nkwɔ. Nɛ ɛchi bɛ bɛsɛ́ nɛ bhɔ sɛ́chɛm nɛbhʉɛt amɔt kɛ bɛsɛ mankɛm sɛ́nkwáy ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbi bɛsí Mandɛm.
Kɛ Yesu abhak anɛt áchwí. Anyáŋá nyaka ntí ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́nti, ambʉɛrɛ nɔkɔ kɛnɔ́. Kɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bárɔ́k máŋɛ́mɛ yi bárɛm bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ yɨŋɨ wɔ bɛ́ sɛ́twɔ̀ gu anyɛ́n-ɛ́?”
Kɛ yi aghati bhɔ́ bɛ́, “Mbɔŋ bɛ́gháti Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ bɛ Mandɛm achi Mfɔ amɛm bɛtɔk bɛchak nkwɔ, mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm átó mɛ fá amɨk chi ɛ̌ti yɔ.”
Mpok yɔ, mbák mmu ángátí bhe bɛ, ‘Ghɔ́ ká Mpɛmɛ anɛ Mandɛm átó fá’, yɛ̌ chi bɛ, ‘Ghɔ́ yi awu!’ Bǎkɛ́ noko bɛ ɛchi tɛtɛp.
Ntí anɛ bo bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́bhʉrɛ bapɛm ayap ɛnyu ɛyɔ chi bɛ Mandɛm atɔ̌ŋ bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhi ndu áchyɛ́ mbi anɛ bo mankɛm bákway bɛfʉɛt arɛ, yi ampɛmɛ bhɔ.
Kɛ abhɛn kɛ́ŋwáŋ bápɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ɛbhap bɛrɔ́ŋɔ́, bápɔ́kɔ mɛnyɨŋ bawɛt nkwɔ bákɛ́m amʉɛt.
Bǎkɛ́ pɔkɔ́ yɛ̌ mɔ́bha nkáp, yɛ̌ ɛbhǎ nɛkɔ, nɛ yɛ̌ nkwɔbhánya ɛchak. Nɛ bǎkɛ́ kaka yɛ̌ mmu ambi.
Ɛ̌ti yɔ, yɛ̌ndu manyiɛp ákwɛ́nɛ́ tontó, nɛ manyɛ́n ájwí, agboko, babhʉɛ́p ataŋataŋ anu, ɛkɛt ɛyɔ ɛ́kɛ kwɛn. Ɛ́kɛ kwɛn mbɔnyunɛ mbɔŋɔ́kɛt até yɔ́ ndǔ sɛtárɛ́bhɛ́.
Nɛ chɔŋ ɛmbak bɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ apu ghok ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ wu, báfap yi nɛ bǒ Mandɛm, mangway.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Chɔŋ njɛnti mkpáká bho abhɛn ɛchɔŋ nɛ yi? Bachi mbɔ yi?
Mbabhɛri wu ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, asɔt bhɔ́, arɔk afyɛ́ ndu mɔ́kɛt anɛ achi tɛ amɛm. Báfyɛ́ bhɔ́ bɛko bɛkak.
Bábhó bɛ́pa yi batiɛ́ bɛsí, mándɛpti nɔkɔ. Báchák mánchyɛ nɔkɔ yi nsáp.
Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Nɛnyiɛ́ ɛna chi bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mmu anɛ átó mɛ áyàŋ nkʉ́, nɛ mɛnáŋá bɛtɨk ɛbhi.
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ yi ǎkap yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu bɛkoŋo bɛrɨ ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ́, yɛ̌ achi nsɛm, yɛ apu.
Nɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti, chí bɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ wɔ, wɔ mmu ɔ́chí Mandɛm tɛtɛp nɛ achák apu nɛ bɛrɨŋɨ Yesu Kristo mmu ɔ́tó.
Ɛ̌ti yɔ, sɛ́rɨŋɨ mbɔŋ nɛ́nɛ ɛcha ɛnyu ɛsɨ́ bɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ bárɛ́mɛ́ nyaka bɛ́chí tɛtɛp. Fíɛ́ yɛ́ ka ntí ndǔ bɛyɔŋ ɛbhap, mbɔnyunɛ bɛ́chí mbɔ ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛnɛ ɛ́ghɔ̀ amɛm ɛjuri. Dɔ́k ká ambɨ bɛghok bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɔ kpatɛ mpok anɛ nywɔp nɛ́yì. Ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɔ, nɛmbe   ɛnɛn beti nɛ́ghɔ̀ amɛm batɨ yɛka.
Tɛtɛ̌tɛp, mbák bábhɨ́kɨ́ pɨ nyɛ́sɛ́ nchwi amɨk nɛ́mpɔ́, nɛ́bhak chi nyɛ́sɛ́ nchwi nɛmɔt. Kɛ mbák mámpɨ́ nyɛ́sɛ́ nchwi amɨk nɛ́mpɔ, nɛ́nchak, nɛ́chyɛ bɛyǎ nchwi nkɔ.
Mbák chí Táytɔs, chi ntɨ nkʉbɛtɨk awa. Ǎkʉ̀ bɛtɨk nɛ mɛ ndu bɛkwak be. Mbák chí bɔ̌mayɛsɛ bachak abhɔ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap achi mǔnto ndǔ ntí bakwɔ́ bho Kristo abhɛn bátó yi, bɔ bho báchyɛ̀ Kristo kɛnókó.
Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛpɛ́m bɛbhɔŋ mmʉɛt kɛkúrí kɛkúrí. Bakwǎŋwaŋ bábhɔŋ ayap ɛnyǔ mmʉɛt, nnya ɛ́bhɔ́ŋ ɛyap ɛnyǔ mmʉɛt, kɛnɛn kɛbhɔ́ŋ ɛyap ɛnyǔ mmʉɛt, nɛ nsi ɛ́bhɔ̌ŋ ɛyap ɛnyu mmʉɛt.
Kɛ ndu Yesu árɨ́ŋɨ́ nkaysi yap, aghati bhɔ́ bɛ, “Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛtɔk ɛnɛ akɔrɛ achi arɛ bo mánù nɔkɔ nɛ batɨ, ɛ́bhɔŋ chi mɛnɛmɛ. Nɛ nnɛrɛ́kɛt anɛ́ ákɔ́rɛ́ áchí arɛ nɛ bo mánù nɔkɔ nɛ batɨ, ákwɛ́nɛ́ kwɛn.
Ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ ɛ́bhàk chɔŋ mpok mmɨk ámay. Bɔangɛl bátwɔ̀, mámfɛrɛ bakʉ̌ bɛbʉ́ ndǔ nkwɔ bǒ abhɛn bachi chak bɛsí Mandɛm,
Nɛ ndǔ yi ákɔ̀ árɔ̀ŋ, bo báré sɔt ndɛnɛ́ mfǎymʉɛt ɛyap mángay nɔkɔ ambi bɛ mɔ́mpɔŋɔ batu wu ankɔ amfay.
Yesu atɛ́m bo Israɛl nɛkay ɛnɛn, kɛ bɔ́ kɛjwimɛm ndǔ ntí nɛkay. 
Ansɛm mpǎy manywɔp, apɛtnsɛm Kapɛ̌naum nɛ mbok ataka mbǎnkɛm bɛ́ Yesu achí ɛtɔk.
Mbák mmu akáysí bɛ yi achi ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ, nɛ yɛ bɛ́ abhɔŋ akap anɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm achyɛ yi, ándɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ̌sɨ̀ŋ-nɛ ntá yɛka chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu Acha ághátí mɛ nsɨŋ.
Mbɔ ɛnyu Ɛtaya ákɔ́ŋ mɛ, nɔ́ kɛ nkɔ́ŋɔ́ bhe. Bat ka mmʉɛt nɛ mɛ bɛ́ ɛkɔŋ ɛya ɛ́mbák amɛm batɨ yɛka mpoknkɛm.
Bɔ̌ma, bǎrɔp bo abhɛn mǎŋɔkɔ ɛkakánɛkɔ ɛnɛ́ bǒnkwɔ Mandɛm abhɛn atú Judɛ́ya. Bǎbhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Kristo mbɔnyunɛ bǎghɔ̌ ɛsɔŋɔri amɔ batɨ bo ɛtɔk ɛyɛka nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ bo Israɛl báchyɛ́ nyaka bhɔ ɛsɔŋɔri atú Judɛ́ya.
Yɛ̌ agha anɛ ábyak nyaka ɛbhé Moses nɛ bo bati apay, yɛ̌ bati arat, mánte ntísiɛ bɛ akʉ nɔ tɛtɛp, báway yi kɛbhɔŋ ntínso nɛ yi.
Yesu mmu ákʉ̀ bo mambák pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí Mandɛm abhɔŋ chi amɔt nɛ bo abhɛn yi ákʉ́ bɛ mambák pɛ́pɛ́p. Ɛ̌ti yɔ, yi ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ntíánwɔ́p ndu bɛbhɨŋɨ bɔ bɛ, “Bɔ̌ma.”
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu abhʉɛt bɛghati bhɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn, bápɛ́rɛ ghɔ mǔnti bo Israɛl amɔt arɔk akwɛ́n yi bɛkak, abho bɛrɛm bɛ, “Ɛta, mɔ́wa agu nɛ́nɛ. Chí mɔ́ngɔrɛ́. Nnɨkmʉɛt, twɔ́ nyaŋá amɔ yi amʉɛt, nɛ chɔŋ ampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.”
Kɛ mmu anɛ afyɛ́ ntí ndǔ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm, ankʉ nɔkɔ mbɔnyǔ ɛ́ghàti yi, yí kɛghɔkɔntɨk yɔ, ɛ́rɨ ntá yi ɛncha. Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm chí ɛbhé Mandɛm. Ɛ́rɨ ndǔ babhi ankɛm, nɛ ɛ́bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ bɛ́fɛ́rɛ bɛsɛ ndǔ bɛbʉ́.
Mandɛm aghókó mmʉɛt nkwǎŋwaŋ ɛnyu ɛyɔ bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛ́pókómʉɛt ɛmbak sayri nɛ bɛ́pókómʉɛt bɛ́chák.
“Chɔŋ mǎngɔ ‘Ɛrɛm ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm ápábhɛ́’ téé amɛm Ɛkɛrɛ́ Mandɛm ndu ɛ́nyɔ̀p yɔ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Daniɛl ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm árɛ́mɛ́ tɛsáy bɛ chɔŋ ɛ́mfakari.” [Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ápay ɛkáti ɛnɛ́ ámfyɛ anti, anjwimɛm.]
Nchí sɔt ɛrɨŋ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m nɛ ntí bɛ mɛ́yàŋ mǎnjwimɛm ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ́rɛ̀m, mbɔnyunɛ ɛ́bemʉɛt bɛ bakwǎŋwaŋ mámbɔ́ŋ nɛjwǐmɛm ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛ́bhɛn. Nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ bǎchyɛ́ nyaka bɛpókómʉɛt ɛbhɛka ndǔ kɛsɛm ɛkɛn bɛkʉ barak ɛpúsí nɛ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ bɛchak ɛbhɛn bɛyǎ mɛndɔk nɔkɔ chi ambɨ, chyɛ ká bɛpókómʉɛt ɛbhɛka nɛ́nɛ mbɔ basɛm ntá Mandɛm bɛ yi ankʉ mǎmbák chak bɛsí bhi ɛnyu ɛnɛ babhak nyáŋá.
Bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ Yesu ányìɛ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ bhɔ́, bábhó bɛbhɛp bakoŋo Yesu bɛ, “Ndaká yí ntɔŋ ywɛka ányìɛ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ mɛnyǔ bǒbhɛn?”
Píta abho bɛrɛm ntá Yesu bɛ, “Acha, ɛ́rɨ tontó bɛ sɛchi fá. Dɔ̌ sɛ́nté bɛ́tɛ́m barat. Ɛ́mɔt ntá yɛ, ɛ́chák ntá Moses, nɛ ɛnɛ́fú ntá Ɛláija.”
Ɛ́chí yɛ mbɔ ɛnyu Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Chɔŋ bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́re ghati bhɔ ɛ̌ti yi mángɔ yi, nɛ chɔŋ bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́re ghok ɛ̌ti yi, mánjwimɛm.” Pɔ̌l átɨ bɛrɔŋ Rom
Mbɔ bo abhɛn bábhʉ̀rɛ bɛbhé kɛ babhɔ̌ŋ nyaka mɛnyiɛ mmɨk mbʉ nɛka ɛnɛka nɛ Mandɛm nɛchi chi ndɛ́ndɛm, nɛ mbʉ bariɛp ami nkwɔ abhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ntí.
Baghɔk Yesu babho yɛ bɛ́kwɛ́n yi bɛkak, ndu bɛchyɛ yi kɛnókó, mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Tɛtɛp, ɔchí Mmɔ Mandɛm!” 
“Acha, ɔkʉ bariɛp amɛ afǔ tɛtɛp, dɔ yɛ́ mɛ, mmɔ̌bɛtok ywɛ ndɔ́k pɛtii,
Josɛ́f nɛ María manaŋa nɔkɔ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm bɛkoŋo ɛbhé Mandɛm, bápɛtnsɛm nɛ mmɔ́ ɛtɔk ɛyap Násárɛt atú Gálili.
Yɛ̌ nɔ́, Yesu achɔkɔ kpák, akɛ rɛm yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm arɛm bɛ, “Ndǔ nnyɛ́n Mandɛm anɛ achi nɛpɛ́m mpoknkɛm, ghatí bhɛsɛ́ tɛtɛp mbák wɔ kɛ ɔ́chí Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò, Mmɔ Mandɛm.”
Mɛnkɛm bɛ́kwàk ndǔ bɛyǎ babhi. Ɛnyɨŋɨ́ mbɨ ɛnɛ ɛkwak mmu anɛ achi mmu Israɛl chi bɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ ɛyɔŋ ɛyi amɔ ayap.
Arɛ́, aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Nɨk nɔ́kɔ́ ká mmʉɛt bɛ mbák nɛmɔ nɛ́twɔ bǎkɛ́ kwɛn.”
Nɛ dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ mmu anɛ nɛmɔ nɛ́twɔ̀ ntá yí, nɛ ǎyàŋ bɛ́kʉ bɛbʉ́, ákɛ́ rɛm bɛ́ “Mandɛm kɛ̌ átó mɛ́ nɛmɔ ɛnɛn.” Yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛ́pú kway mɛmɔ Mandɛm ɛ́ntɛn yi ndǔ bɛbʉ́. Nɛ yímbɔŋ Mandɛm apú kwáy mɛmɔ yɛ̌ mmu bɛ ánkʉ bɛbʉ́.
Ɛ́tárɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, mbɔk bǒnkwɔ Fárisi nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm báfú Yerúsalɛm bárɔ́k ntá Yesu bábhɛp yi bɛ,
Kɛ nchí ghati bhe bɛ Ɛláija anáŋ átwɔ nɛ bo bákʉ́ yi bɛbʉ́ mbɔ ɛnyu bákɔ́ŋɔ́ mbɔ ɛnyu básɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ̌ti yi.”
