Kɛ arɔk ambɨ arɛm ntá bo mankɛm bɛ, “Sɔt ka mpok! Kɛ́m ká mmʉɛt bɛ bǎkɛ́ fyɛ ngoŋo ndu bɛbhɔŋ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ. Puyɛ̌ chi bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ kɛ bɛ́kɛ̀m nɛpɛ́m nkwǎ.”
Bábho yɛ mɛ́nɨkmʉɛt ntá Yesu bɛ ándɔ́ atú ɛtɔk ɛyap.
Yesu apɛt yɛ nsɛm atú Gálili ndǔ bɛtaŋá Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ. Mbok yi ataka atú Gálili wu ankɛm.
Nɛ bɛfʉɛt ndǔ nɛka ɛni, “Mandɛm asɔt bɛ Ábraham achi chak bɛsí bhi.”
Mǔfú abhak bɛsí Yesu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛmě afɛmntay.
Nsɨŋ be mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ mɛ́nkʉ mǎndɨŋɨ bǒbhɔ nɔ báyàŋ bɛrwɔ bhe.
Arɛ́ amɛm baso, Yesu abhak ndǔ nɛtarɛ́nsay bɛti nɛ ngósí ndǔ manywɔp bɛsa bɛpay. Nsay akɛ́m yi.
Mbák sɛ́bhɔŋ yɛ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ ndɛn sɛ́ndɔ́ ɛbhɔ mɛ́nkwáy nɛ bhɛsɛ.
Yesu árɛ́mɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, abhɨŋɨ bɛyǎ bo abhɛn bachi arɛ́ arɛm bɛ, “Tá ká batú mǎngok ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́rɛ́m, mǎnjwimɛm!
Ngɛ́mtay bo báré koŋo yi mbɔnyunɛ bághɔ̌ nyaka mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ́ ntá bǒmame.
Bɛ́rɔ́ŋ ambɨ Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Mbák mámbók ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ́ndɔ́ mmu, ɛ́rɔp chí bóŋboŋbóŋ amɛm baso, ɛ́njaŋ nɔkɔ ɛbhak ɛnɛ yɔ ɛ́chwe. Mbák ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ ghɔ́ ɛbhak bɛchɔkɔ,
Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ nɛntɨ ɛpa, Yesu arɔk amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm abho bɛtɔŋ bo Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm.
Ɛ́kʉ́ nnyɛ́n Yesu nɛ́táka kpát nɛ́gháka atú Síria ankɛm. Bo báré pɔkɔ́ bǒ abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ mame mɛnyu nɛ mɛnyu mándɔk nɔkɔ ntá Yesu bɛ ámbú bhɔ. Mbɔk yap bábhák bo abhɛn bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri bhɔ, báchák bábhák bǒ abhɛn bákwɛ̀n ntímɛn, abhɛ́nɛ́fú babhak bǒ abhɛn bachi bhʉrɛ́. Yesu abú bhɔ mankɛm.
Ɛ́chí tɛtɛp bɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ́pú kwáy bɛkʉ bɛsɛ́ sɛmbák kɛ́kwɔ́t nɛ Mandɛm. Mbák sɛ́nyìɛ nɛnyíɛ́, ɛyɔ ɛ́pú kwak bhɛsɛ́. Nɛ mbák sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ nyiɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́, ɛyɔ ɛ́pú kʉ bhɛsɛ́ yɛ̌nyɨŋ.
Yesu arɛm yɛ ntá bakoŋo bhi bɛ, “Bǎchay ɛnyunɛ ndaká yí? Bǎbhɨ́kí re bhɔ́ŋ nɛka nɛ mɛ?”
Tɛ́mté wu, bárɔ́ áchwí wap nɛ ɛtayap, bákoŋo yi. 
Báchyɛ́, mánɨk nɔkɔ bhɛsɛ mmʉɛt ndɔŋ nɛ ndɔŋ nɛ ntɨ nɛnkɛm bɛ́ sɛ́nchíɛ bɔ́ mbi mánkwák bo Mandɛm abhɛn bachi Yerúsalɛm.
Átát nɔ́kɔ́ arɛ́ mpǎy manywɔp, afa are kɔ bɛtɔk nɛ bɛtɔk atú Galéshia nɛ Fríjia, amfyɛ nɔkɔ bakoŋo Yesu mankɛm ntɨ ndǔ nɛsɨkɨ́ntɨ ɛnap. 
Bɔ̌ma, ndu bɛrɔŋ ambɨ, sɛ́ghati bhe ɛnyǔ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛbhʉrɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛka nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ bǎkʉ̀ nɔ bɛ Mandɛm ámbɔ́ŋ maŋák nɛ bhe. Sɛ́nɨ̀k yɛ be mmʉɛt sɛ́mkpɛmɛ nɔkɔ ndu nnyɛ́n Yesu Acha bɛ mǎndɔk ambɨ bɛkʉ nɔ.
Bɛbʉ́ ná nɛ mkpáká bho anɛ ɛchɔŋ! Bápú kʉ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Mandɛm áyàŋ. Báyàŋ bɛghɔ chi ɛrɨŋɨ́ maknkay! Kɛ yɛ̌ ɛ́mɔt mpú tɔŋ be, ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ fʉɛt chi ɛnɛ́ Jóna, ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm.” Yesu árɛ́mɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, arɔ bhɔ, arɔk.   
Mbák mmu akaysi bɛ achi mǔngo, ɛnɛ́ yi apú yɛ̌nyɨŋ, ǎrwɔ́ chi mmʉɛt.
Ábraham aghati yɛ yi bɛ, ‘Mbák bɔ̌mayɛ babhɨkɨ ka bɛghok mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi amɛm basɨŋ Moses nɛ amɛn barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ, nɔ bápú kway bɛghok yɛ chi mmu anɛ ánáŋá ágú kɛ ǎpɛtnsɛm ntá yap.’”
Mbɔŋɔ́nkɨ ató mǔbɛtok achak. Bákɛ́m awu nkwɔ́ bádɛn, báchyɛ́ yi ntiánwɔ́p, bábók apɛtnsɛm amɔ́ apay.
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, mpok Mandɛm ákʉ̀ bawú mámpɛ́tnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, ngɔrɛ́ wu ǎbhák anɛ agha? Ndu bɔ́ mankɛm, batí tándrámɔt, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ wap abhǎy nyaka yi.”
Debhít mmɔ̌ Jése, Jése mmɔ̌ Óbɛd, Óbɛd mmɔ̌ Bóas, Bóas mmɔ̌ Sálmɔn, Sálmɔn mmɔ̌ Náshɔn,
Ɛ́chí ɛnyu yɔ mbɔnyunɛ batɨ̌ bǒbhɛn ákʉ bárɔp bɛchɨŋtǐ bho, báchí mbɔ bǒ abhɛn batú ábé bhɔ nɛ bapu pɛrɛ yáŋ bɛghok yɛ̌nyɨŋ, báchí mbɔ bo abhɛn bákútí amɨ́k bɛ bákɛ́ ghɔ́ mbaŋ, nɛ bɛ́ batú yap ákɛ́ ghók yɛ̌nyɨŋ, nɛ bɛ bákɛ́ jwimɛm, mantwɔ ntá ya, mbú bhɔ.’”
Kɛ mbǎyngɔrɛ́ akɛmɛ bhɔ chi bɛ, ‘Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bhe!’”
Baghɛ́p abhɛn bágó ndǔ ɛbhap bɛko mbɔ yí, báré so yí nkwɔ́ nɛ nsɔk ɛnyu ɛ́mɔ́t. 
Arɛm bɛ, “Ghók ká, sɛ́rɔ̀ŋ nɔ chi Yerúsalɛm, nɛ mpok sɛ́gháká arɛ́, chɔŋ mámfyɛ Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm amɔ́ bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ ntá batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses, bɔ́ mándɛm bɛ mángwáy yi.
Bo abhɛn bábhʉ̀rɛ kɛnɔ́, bábhʉ̀rɛ chi nɛ bɛ́ti, nɛ bo bákwɛ̀n mmɛ́m chí nɛ bɛti.
Kristo nkwɔ aghɔ nyaka ɛsɔŋɔri, agú ɛ̌ti bɛbʉ́ bo mankɛm, ndɔŋ amɔt ndak ámáy. Anaŋa bɛtɨk ɛbhɔ, yi mmu achi chak, ɛ̌ti bo abhɛn bapu chak, bɛ́ ánsɔt bɛsɛ ntá Mandɛm. Báwáy yi, agú ndǔ nkwɔmʉɛt, kɛ ndǔ Ɛfóŋó, Mandɛm akʉ yi apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.
Yesu ayɨŋɨ bhɔ dǐǐ arɛm bɛ, “Ntá nkwǎŋwaŋ, mbi ápú, kɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛ́pú cha Mandɛm.”
Yí nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi báfʉɛ́t bárɔk ndu mɔ́tɔk achak. 
Bofú básɔ́t bɔ̌bhap bárɔ́k ntá Yesu nɛ bhɔ bɛ yi anyaŋa bɔ amɔ anti anjɛt bhɔ. Baghɔkɔ́ bhi bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, bábho bɛsáyti bhɔ bɛ bákɛ́ kʉ nɔ.
Árɛ́m nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, asɨ́ŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ́ ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ,
Ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhɛn Mandɛm átɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛ, nchí rɛm ntá yɛka mankɛm bɛ yɛ̌ mmu akɛ sɔt mmʉɛt yi mbɔ bɛ achá ɛnyǔ mmu yi achi. Kɛ ámbɔ́ŋ chi nkaysi anɛ achi chak ɛ̌ti ɛnyu ɛnɛ yi achi, bɛ́kóŋó ɛnǐ nɛka ɛnɛn Mandɛm áchyɛ yi.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ́rɛ̀m nɔ chi bɛ, sɛ́mbɔ́ŋ mbi bɛfyɛ batɨ ntɨ, nɔ chí bɛ, mǎnsɔt nɛka ɛnɛka nɛ Yesu mǎmfyɛ mɛ ntɨ, mɛ nkwɔ nsɔt nɛka ɛná nɛ Yesu mfyɛ́ bhe ntɨ.
Bo mankɛm bábhɔŋ bɛkɛm nɛbhay nɛ kɛnókó. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ngɔrɛ́ abhɔŋ bɛbhak tɛtɛp nɛ nnɛ́m, yí kɛkwɛ́n bɛrwɔp, nnɛ́m nkwɔ abhɔŋ bɛbhak ɛnyumɔt, mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm apú rɔ bɛ́táŋ mmu anɛ ákʉ́ ɛpúsí nɛ nkwɛnɛ́ bɛrwɔp.
Nchí nɨkmʉɛt bɛ́ bɔ́ mankɛm mámbák mbɔ mmu amɔt. Ɛtaya, mɛ̌nɨ̀kmʉɛt bɛ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɔ́bhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ mɛ nɛ mbát mmʉɛt nɛ wɔ, bɔ́ nkwɔ mámbát mmʉɛt nɛ bhɛsɛ bɛ́ mmɨk ánkwáy mɛ́nóko bɛ wɔ kɛ ɔ́tó mɛ tɛtɛp.
Mɛ Jems, mmɔ̌bɛtok Mandɛm nɛ Yesu Kristo Acha kɛ̌ nchí sɨ́ŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ. Nchí sɨ́ŋ ntá yɛká bǒ Mandɛm, bě bho bǎtaka ndǔ bɛtɔkɔ́ mmɨk mɛnkɛm. Nchí tó be mankɛm bakak. 
Ɛ́kʉ bǎrɔ́p ɛrɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bakoŋo Yesu mankɛm atú Masidónia nɛ Akáiya máŋɔ̀kɔ.
Lámɛk mmɔ̌ Mɛtúsɛla, Mɛtúsɛla mmɔ̌ Ɛ́nɔk, Ɛ́nɔk mmɔ̌ Járɛt, Járɛt mmɔ̌ Mahálálɛl, Mahálálɛl mmɔ̌ Kánǎn,
Bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛ́n ngátí bhe bɛ́kʉ bǎchí pɛ́pɛ́p.
Ɛchí amɛm basɨŋɨ́ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ bɛ, ‘Chɔŋ Mandɛm ántɔ́ŋ bɔ́ mankɛm.’ Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ághókó, nɛ aghɔ́k ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛtaya árɛ́mɛ́, ǎtwɔ̀ ntá ya.
Bo mankɛm babhɔŋ akap bɛ́bu bǒmame kɛ? Bo mankɛm bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ akap bɛrɛm bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛbhɛ́n bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ kɛ? Bo mankɛm babhɔŋ akap mɛnɛnɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bárɛ́mɛ́ ndǔ bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛbhɛn babhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ kɛ?
Bě nkwɔ, bɔ́ŋ ká ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ, mǎnte kpirí mbɔnyunɛ mpok anɛ Yesu Acha ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́twɔ arɔp kɛkwɔt.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎyàŋ chi ɛnɛ? Bǎyàŋ ntwɔ́ awu chí nɛ ɛ́kpá awɔ́, kɛ chi nɛ ɛyɔŋ pɛtii bɛtɔŋ bɛ nkɔŋ be tɛtɛp?
Aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Dɔ́k ká ndǔ mɔ́tɔk anɛ achi afɔ ambɨ. Nɛchwe anɛ báchwe arɛ chɔŋ mǎngɔ mɔ́ mpɔŋɔ batu sɛsɛ́t, anɛ yɛ̌ mmu abhɨkɨ re kɔ nɛ yɔ́. Kaŋarí ká twɔ́ mɛ nɛ yɔ́.
kɛ Ɛyɔŋ Acha ɛbhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.” Ɛyɔŋ ɛyɔ chi Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ bághátí nyaka bhe.
Bágháti Yesu bɛ, “Ɛtayɛsɛ chi Ábraham.” Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Mbɔ bǎchí bɔ̌ Ábraham tɛtɛp, mbʉ́ bǎkʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ mbɔ Ábraham ákʉ̀ nyaka.
Mfɔ wu akɛmɛ bɛ, ‘Nchí ghati bhe bɛ, mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́, báchyɛ yi ɛ́chák. Kɛ anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ, básɔ̀t ntá yi yɛ̌ chí mandú anɛ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́.
Mandɛm abhɨ́kɨ́ gʉɛp bǒbhi abhɛn yi áyábhɛ́ tɛ ndǔ nɛbhǒnɛt ɛbhɨ. Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m ɛ̌ti ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Ɛláija ndu yi ághàti nyaka Mandɛm mɛnyɨŋ, anji nɔkɔ bo Israɛl? Yi ǎrɛ̀m nyaka bɛ,
Mpok anɛ mmok ánɛ̀m, bǒ mankɛm abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bǒmame mɛnyu nɛ mɛnyu básɔ́t bhɔ bárɔ́k ntá Yesu. Abho mɛ́nyáŋa amɔ amʉɛt yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap, kpat abú bhɔ mankɛm.
Yesu aghati yɛ bo abhɛn bachi arɛ bɛ, “Bɨŋɨrí ká ntay ɛnɔ fɛrɛ́.” Kɛ Matá, manɔ ngú arɛm bɛ, “Acha, ɛriɛp ɛ́ya chɔŋ ɛncha. Ɛ́kʉ manywɔp anwi ɛchɔŋ ɛnɛ́ bábhɛ́mɛ́ yi!”
Arɛm yɛ bɛ, “Yesu, ghɔ́ mɛ ntínso, mpok ɔ́bhak Mfɔ.”
Mɛnyɨŋ ɛ́bhɛn barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ bárɛ́mɛ́ mɛnkɛm bɛ́yɨŋɨ bhe. Nɛ nku anɛ Mandɛm ányú nyaka nɛ bachǐmbɨ bhɛka, ányu nɛ be nkwɔ́, mbɔnyunɛ arɛm nyaka ntá Ábraham bɛ, ‘Chɔŋ mfʉɛ́t ntá bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ bhɛ ńjɛt manɛrɛ́kɛrɛ́ mmɨk ankɛm.’
Kɛ yɛ̌ nɔ, mbok Yesu ataka mbǎnkɛm. Ngɛ́mtay bo bárɔ́k ntá yi ndu bɛghók Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm nɛ bɛ́ yi ambu mame yap.
Nkʉ bɛtɨk wu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, ‘Ɛta, dɔ̌ ɛ́mpɛ́t ɛmbak ndǔ mmíɛ́ ɛnɛn nkwɔ. Chɔŋ ntɛ́m nnɛt ywi ngabhɛri, mfyɛ́ ntɔbhɛ́-píɔ.
Mɛ Pɔ̌l kɛ nchí sɨŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ. Nchí nkʉbɛtɨk Mandɛm nɛ mǔnto Yesu Kristo. Mandɛm mmú ápɛmɛ bhɛsɛ nɛ Yesu Kristo mmu sɛ́bháká ntɨ nɛ yi ndu nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛ́twɔ̀ ambɨ kɛ bátó mɛ.
Nɛ mbák mmu áfɛ́rɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ndu ɛbhɛn bɛchi amɛm ɛkáti ɛnɛ ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛbhɔŋ bɛfakari, chɔŋ Mandɛm amfɛrɛ aywi ákɔ́rɛ́ ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ nɛpɛ́m nɛ ndǔ ɛtɔkɔ́ Mandɛm.
Kɛ nnɨkmʉɛt ɛ̌ti yɛ bɛ́ ɔ́kɛ́ rɔ bɛ́bhɔŋ nɛka nɛ mɛ. Nɛ ɔ́náŋ ɔ́mpɛ́tnsɛm ntá ya, ɔ́kɛ́ rɔ bɛfyɛ bɔ̌mayɛ ntɨ.”
Pɔ̌l apɛt yɛ nsɛm amfay. Mányiɛ nɔ́kɔ́ Nɛnyiɛ́ Acha, arɛm kɛpɨ nɛ bhɔ ndǔ ɛrɔ́rí mpok tɛ̌ nywɔp nɛ́yí. Arɔ yɛ bɔ́ arɔk.
Yɛ̌ ɛmbak yi, sɛpú kway bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́chɛt tɛtɛp mbi. Sɛ́kʉ̀ chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛkʉ tɛtɛp anɛ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ándɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ambɨ.
Nɛ ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka basɛ́mɛ́ ákway bɛkʉ nɛpɛ́m ɛni nɛ́nsap yɛ̌ chi mandú nɨŋɨnɨŋɨ, nɛncha ɛnyu nɛbhɔŋɔ bɛbhak?
Yesu aghati bhɔ́ bɛ, “Tɛtɛ̌tɛp, mmǔ anɛ árɔ́ yɛ̌ chí ɛkɛt ɛyi, yɛ̌ chí bɔ̌mayi abhɛn babhakanɛm yɛ̌ chí abhɛn baghɔrɛ́, yɛ̌ chí máyi nɛ ɛtayi, yɛ̌ chí bɔ̌bhi, nɛ yɛ̌ chí bakɨ̌ yi ɛ̌ti ya nɛ ɛ̌ti Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́,
Nnyɛ́n nɛmbe ɛnɔ chi Ǎnɛn. Ndu amɔt ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ barǔ nyɛ́n arat árɔ́bhɛ́ nɛnɛnɛ́n. Nɛ bɛyǎ bo bagu ɛ̌ti manyiɛbhɛ́ mɔ mbɔnyunɛ ǎnɛ̀n nyaka tontó.
Akɛmɛ bhɔ́ bɛ, “Ngátí bhé kpoŋoroŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ ɛ̌ti Kɛfɔ Mandɛm, kɛ ntá bo báchák, nchí ghati bhɔ mɛnyɨŋ chi ndǔ bakay,
Bɔ́ bárɨ́ŋɨ́ sayri ndǔ ɛrɔ́rí mpok bɛ́ nchí nyaka ndǔ nkwɔ́ bǒ Farisi abhɛn báfyɛ̀ bɛtaŋ tontó ndǔ baraká Mandɛm. Mbák ɔmbɛ́p bhɔ chɔŋ mángati bhe ɛnyúmɔt mbák báyaŋ bɛrɛm tɛtɛp anɛ bárɨŋɨ.
Kɛ Píta nɛ Jɔ̌n bákɛ́mɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Bě babhɔŋ bɛ́p ká mmʉɛt ɛyɛka ndak anɛ. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́chí chak bɛsí Mandɛm chi ɛnɛ́? Bɛ́ghok bhe kɛ chi bɛghok Mandɛm?
“Bě bo Korasín, chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛ́p ntá yɛka ɛncha! Bě bo Bɛtsáida, chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛ́p ntá yɛka nkwɔ ɛncha! Mbɔ chi amɛm bɛtɔk Táya nɛ Sídɔn kɛ̌ nkʉ́ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛbhɛn-nɛ nkʉ ntá yɛka, mbʉ́ báfyɛ́ ndɛn pyɔ, mánto batwɔ́p anti tɛsáy, bɛtɔŋ bɛ bátɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhap!
Mpok ɛyɔ bo bábhák ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ. Báfyɛ bhɔ́ kɛnɔŋ ndu bápú noko bǒbati ɛtɔk nɛ ndu bágʉ́ɛ́bhɛ́ ɛbyɔk amɛm ɛtɔk kpát báway bho. Mmǔ wap amɔt aka nnyɛ́n bɛ́ Barábas.
Sɛ́chyɛ̀ bakak ntá Mandɛm mpoknkɛm ɛ̌ti yɛka mankɛm nɛ sɛ́fyɛ̀ bhé ndǔ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt ɛnɛsɛ́ mpoknkɛm.
Mbuɔt áchák akwɛnti ndǔ mmɨk sɛtárɛ́bhɛ́ anɛ ntɔp abhɨkɨ ya arɛ. Awakari achak.
Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm kɛ áchyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m. Mmʉɛt nkwǎ apu kʉ yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛ́n ngátí bhe bɛ́twɔ̀ nɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm nɛ bɛ́chyɛ nɛpɛ́m.
Nɛ tɛ̌ndu bǎbhɨ̀ŋɨ Mandɛm bɛ Ɛta mpok mǎnɨ̀kmʉɛt ntá yi mmú átàŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu bɛkoŋo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ̀ kɛtɔ́ŋ kɛ́rɨ́ŋámík, bɔ́ŋ ká kɛnókó nɛ yi ndǔ ɛkakánɛkɔ ɛyɛka fá amɨk mbɔ mankɔ.
Yesu Acha ánáŋá nɔkɔ bɛ́rɛm kɛpɨ nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi, Mandɛm asɔt yi apɛtnsɛm amfay, achɔkɔ ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛnókó ndu ɛbhe awɔ́nɛm Mandɛm.
Ngɛ́mtay ɛ́bhɔ́ŋ ɛnyɨŋ ambeápak mbɔ ndɛ́-nɛnu anɛ bághókó nɛ ɛse, ndu bɛkuti mbeápak nɛ ɛwat ɛnɛ ɛ́fù ndǔ bɛbhap ɛbhap ɛbhak mbɔ bɛrɛmti ɛbhɛn bɛ́fù ndu bɛ́kárɨ́k ɛbhɛn mpɔŋɔ́ndɨk ɛnɛ́ ɛ́rɔ̀ŋ ɛbhɨ̌nɛnu ntiɛ́t ntiɛt.
Sɔt ká mmʉɛt mbɔ bɛ́ bǎpú yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛsí Mandɛm, nɛ chɔŋ yi ankosi bhe. 
Pɔ̌l afa Atɛns arɔk ɛtɔk Kɔrint.
Tɛ́mté wu, afate kpɛrɛp bɛsí bhap, apɔkɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ábhʉ̀rɛ nyaka arɛ́, abho bɛgurɛ, ambɨti nɔkɔ Mandɛm.
Yesu Kristo akʉ nɔ bɛ áfɔ́k anɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛchyɛ Ábraham, ámbák nɛ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl, ndu bábhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ yi, nɛ bɛ́ Mandɛm anchyɛ bɛsɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ nyaka yi afyɛ́ bariɛp bɛ́chyɛ́ ɛ̌ti nɛka ɛnɛsɛ. 
Nɛ bǒbati mánsɔt yi mamfyɛ amɔ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl, bɛ́ mánjɔ́kɔ́ yi, nɛ bɛ mándɛ́n yí nɛ ɛkpa, nɛ bɛ mángó yi ndǔ ɛkotákátí. Kɛ ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ manywɔp arat, ampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.” 
Mbák ɔ̌rɔ̀ŋ yɛ bɛchyɛ akap ntá Mandɛm kɛ ɔ́ntɨk bɛ ntɨ manɔ́ ǎbè ntɨ ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɔ́kʉ́ yi,
Sɛ́bhɔŋ yɛ ntɨ nɛtaŋ nɛtaŋ mpoknkɛm ndu sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ, ɛnɛ́ sɛ́bhʉɛ́t ndǔ mmʉɛt ɛnɛ, sɛ́pú kway bɛbhak amfay nɛ Yesu Acha.
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ ɛnyǔ Mandɛm átàŋ chɔŋ bo ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ ɛchi chak. Chɔŋ ɛyɔ ɛnkʉ mǎnkwáy bɛbhak bo abhɛn Mandɛm ábhàk Mfɔ wap. Tɛ̌ndu ɛ̌ti Kɛfɔ ɛki kɛ bǎbhɔ̀ŋ ɛsɔŋɔri.
Báre noŋ mánkàysi nɔkɔ bɛ chɔŋ Pɔ̌l amwɔt nɛ bɛ mbák abhɨ́kɨ́ mwɔt abhɔŋ bɛkwɛn amɨk angú. Mánóŋ ndǔ ɛrɔ́ri mpok. Kɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ kɛkʉ yi. Báyíbhíri nkaysi yap, bábho bɛrɛm nɛ batɨ bɛ, “Pɔ̌l chí ɛnyǔ mandɛm ɛfú.”
Bɛyǎ bo mánóko yi, mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Mbák Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò ántwɔ́, chɔŋ ankʉ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛbhɛn bɛ́chá ɛbhɛn mmǔ-nɛ ákʉ̀?”
Mámɛ́sɛ yɛ Nɛwú nɛ Ɛtɔkɔ́ Bawú amɛm nɛpǐngó. Arɛ́ kɛ̌ nɛwú ɛnɛn nɛjwi apay nɛchi.
Kɛ Máykɛl nɛ abhi bɔángɛl básɔt awɔ́nɛm amfǎy yap, bɔ́ kɛpɛrɛ bhɔŋ nɛbhʉɛt amfay.
Mpokófu, babhɛbhɛ́ nkábhɛ́nti nɛ bakʉ̌ bɛbʉ́ bachak báré kap Yesu ndu bɛghok mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yí átɔ̀ŋ.
Mɛ Pɔ̌l, mǔnto Yesu Kristo bɛkoŋo nkaysi Mandɛm, kɛ nchí sɨŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ. Nchí fá nɛ Tímɔti, mɔmáyɛsɛ amɔt. Nchí sɨŋ ntá yɛka bǒnkwɔ Mandɛm abhɛn ɛtɔk Kɔrint nɛ bo Mandɛm mankɛm abhɛn báchi atú Akáiya ankɛm.
Bo abhɛn bákʉ̀ chi bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ bɛkoŋo nɛpɛ́m bakwǎŋwaŋ, bábhʉ̀rɛ ntɨ chi ndǔ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nɛpɛ́m bakwǎŋwaŋ nɛ́yàŋ. Kɛ bo abhɛn bákʉ chi bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ bɛkoŋo ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ árɛ̀m, bábhʉ̀rɛ ntɨ chi ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ákɔ́ŋɔ́.
Nikɔdɛ́mɔs mmu árɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka bɛghɔ Yesu nɛ betí ɛwak ɛ́mɔt, abhak nkwɔ nɛ Josɛ́f. Yí, Nikɔdɛ́mɔs arɔk nɛ babhé amɛn bábyɔk amʉɛt ngu bɛ́ ákɛ́ chɔŋɔ. Babhé mɛ́rɛ́ abhak nchɔ́ptí myrrh nɛ álos. Ǎkway nyaka bɛbhak mbɔ kilo bɛsa bɛpay nsɛm byo ndǔ mɛnwɔp ɛbhi.
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Fílip, mpok anɛ nkɛm nchí nɛ bhe, yɛ̌ nɔ, ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mɛ? Mmu ángɔ́ mɛ nɔ́ aghɔ Ɛtaya nkwɔ. Ná ɔ́rɛ̀m yɛ bɛ, ‘Tɔ́ŋ bhɛsɛ́ ɛtayɛ?’
Chɔŋ mándɛ́n yi nɛ ɛkpa, nɛ mángwáy yi. Kɛ ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ manywɔp arat, ampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.”
Nkúbhɛ́ ɛnyu yɔ kɛ ɛ́chi kpátɛ ɛchɔŋ. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ bápày basɨŋ amɛn Moses, bápú jwimɛm, mbɔnyunɛ ɛ́bhak ntá yap chi mbɔ bɛ básɔt ɛnyɨŋ bákuti batɨ̌ ayap.
Tɛ́mté wu, Yesu arɨŋɨ bɛ bɛtaŋ bɛ́fú yi amʉɛt. Ayibhiri mmʉɛt, abhɛ́p bɛyǎ bo abhɛn bachi yi ansɛm bɛ, “Agha átɔ́kɔ́ ndɛn ɛya?”
Mandɛm ákʉ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi átɨ́ nyaka tɛ mpok yi ábhɨ́kɨ́ re fʉɛt ntá Acha ywɛsɛ Yesu Kristo.
Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Tɛtɛ̌tɛp, Mmɛ Mmɔ Mandɛm mpú kwáy bɛkʉ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ndǔ bɛtaŋ ɛbha. Mɛ́kʉ̀ chí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ngɔ́ Ɛtaya ákʉ̀. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ Ɛtaya ákʉ̀, yɔ́ kɛ Mɛ Mɔ́ywi nchí kʉ nkwɔ́.
Nsɨŋ be nɛ bɛyǎ bɛbe antɨ, nɛ basɛ́mɛ́, nɛ babhɛsɛ amík. Mbɨ́kɨ́ sɨŋ bɛ́chɔŋti batɨ ayɛka amɛm. Nsɨŋ chi bɛkʉ mǎndɨŋɨ bɛ nkɔŋ be tontó. 
Are bhaŋari ndu bɛghɔ mmu anɛ átɔ́kɔ́ yi.
Nchí nɨkmʉɛt bɛ Acha ángɔ́ yi ntínso ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ manyé. Ɔ̌rɨŋɨ sayri nɛkwak ɛnɛ́n yi áchyɛ́ mɛ amɛm ɛtɔk Ɛ́fɛsɔs.
Nchí ghati bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ yɛ̌ mmu ákɛ́ sɔt sɛ́rwɔrɛ́nyu ándwɔ bhe ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛyɨŋɨ Kristo, bɛ mǎnɛm ɛbhɨ.
Yesu ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́tɛ́m nɛkay ɛnɛn, abhɛ́p yɛ bǒbati ɛtɔk Israɛl bɛ, “Bě bǎkáysí bɛ́ mpok mbɔŋɔ́nkɨ wu ápɛ́rɛ́nsɛm nɛkɔ ɛnɛn yí árɔ́ŋɔ́, ǎkʉ yi nɛ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk bhɔ?”
Nɛka ɛnɛ́n bo Israɛl nɛ Mandɛm kɛ nɛ́kʉ́ bákɔ́ bághábhɛ́rí ɛtɔk Jɛríko ndǔ manywɔp tándrámɔt, nkok anɛ́ ákábhɛ́ ɛtɔk, ámóko akwɛn.
Báyóŋ nɔ́kɔ́ amɨ́k amfay, bɔ́ kɛpɛrɛ ghɔ yɛ̌ mmu. Ɛrɔp chi Yesu aywǐntí.
mbɔnyunɛ nchí ghok ɛ̌ti ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ bo Mandɛm, nɛ ɛnyu ɔ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛka nɛ Yesu Acha.
Bǎkɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛka. Bák ká ndǔ basɛ́mɛ́ nɛ nɛdǐ kɛbhɔ, babhɛsɛ ansɛbhɛ nɔkɔ amɨ́k byaká byaká byaká. Dɔ̌ ká nɛway-ámɛ́n ɛnɛká mǎmbák ndǔ basɛ́mɛ́. Dɔ̌ ká maŋák amɛká mǎndɔp ndǔ kɛbhɔ.
Mbák mmu ǎkʉ̀ bɛtɨkɨ́ Kristo ɛnyǔ ɛyɔ, Mandɛm ǎbhɔ̀ŋ maŋák nɛ yi, nɛ bo bárɛ̀m bɛ yi ǎkʉ̀ sayri.
Mɛ̌nɨ̀kmʉɛt bɛ mǎndɨŋɨ ɛnyǔ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi bɛyǎ ɛnyǔ ɛnɛ́ sɛpu kway bɛyɛnti bhɔ. Bɛyǎ ndu bɛkwak bhɛsɛ bho sɛ́nókó yi. Bɛtaŋ ɛbhi bhɔ bɛyǎ tontó.
Aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Twɔ́ ká ghɔ.” Bárɔ́k nɛ Yesu baghɔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ yi áchɔ̀kɔ. Mpok yɔ nywɔp nɛ́bhák mbɔ nkárɛ́nká ɛnwi ɛnɛ́ ngósí. Bábhák nɛ yi kpátɛ̌ bɛti bɛgʉ.
Áchwé nɔ́kɔ́ amɛm áchwí, mbʉ́ɛ́p wu ákwɛn. Bɛchay bɛ́kɛ́m bɔ́ tontó.
Ɛwak ɛ́mɔt, Yesu abhɨŋɨ bakoŋo bhi bati byo nɛ apay, achyɛ bhɔ bɛtaŋ bɛ́bók bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ nɛ ndǔ bɛ́bú mame mɛnyu nɛ mɛnyu.
Mbák mǎndɔk ambɨ bɛbhʉrɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛya, mpú rɔ bɛkɔŋ be nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ nchí bhʉɛrɛ Ɛyɔŋ Ɛtaya nɛ yi akɔŋ mɛ mpoknkɛm.
Bákú mmɨk ntá ngoko-bɛte nɛ nkáp ɛ́rɛ, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyu Mandɛm ághátí nyaka mɛ nkʉ.” 
Kɛ chyɛ nɔkɔ ka Kristo kɛnókó mbɔ Acha amɛm batɨ yɛka. Tě ká mpoknkɛm bɛghati yɛ̌ agha anɛ ábhɛ̀p bhe ntí anɛ bǎbháká ntɨ nɛ Yesu. Kʉ nɔ́kɔ́ ka nɔ nɛ ɛrɨ́tí ɛyɔŋɔ́nyu, nɛ kɛnókó.
Nɛ́ chi manoŋ ma. Ǎkʉ nku anɛ Mandɛm ányú nɛ bǒbhi ántéé. Bákʉ manoŋ ma arɔŋ amɨk bɛ́ Mandɛm ámfóŋórí bɛbʉ́ bɛyǎ bho.
Josɛ́f aŋɛmɛ, asɔt nnɔ nɛ mmɔ́ apɛtnsɛm ɛtɔk Israɛl.
Arɔ bhɔ́ atɛ́n mmʉɛt ambɨ mandú. Akwɛn nɛ bɛsí amɨk, abho mɛnɨkmʉɛt, bɛ́ghɔ mbák ǎkway bɛ́fɛrɛ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chi yi ambɨ.
Bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ yɛ̌ndu nku nsɨ́ anɛ átwɔ̀ nɛ nɛwú, ǎkʉ̀ nyaka bo mángɔ bɛtaŋ Mandɛm kpoŋoroŋ. Mandɛm asɨ́ŋ bɛbhé ndǔ bɛ́gbáká batay achyɛ ntá Moses. Ɛnɛ́ Moses ásɛ̀p bɛ́rɔŋ ntá bo Israɛl nɛ batay yɔ, bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ Mamdɛm bɛ́re ghɔ yi bɛsí. Ndu ásɛ̀p bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ Mandɛm ɛbhɔ mɛ́may nɔkɔ. Yɛ̌ nɔ, yɛ̌ mmu wap kɛkwáy bɛyɨŋɨ yi bɛsí tɛbhɛ tɛbhɛ.
Bo abhɛn bárɛ̀m mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fú ntá Mandɛm bǎkway bɛkʉ nɔ amɔt amɔt bɛ bǒ mankɛm mángɔ́k ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ ɛ́mfyɛ́ bhɔ ntɨ.
Kɛ mbák chí bhɛsɛ, ɛyɛsɛ́ ɛtɔk ɛ́chí amfay, ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ Yesu Kristo Acha achi. Nɛ sɛ́bhaka ntɨ bɛ́ yí mmu áchí Mpɛmɛ ywɛsɛ́ ámfú arɛ́ ámpɛtnsɛm.
Ɛsakámu ɛyɔ ɛ́ghati bhɔ́ bɛ, “Bǎkɛ́ cháy! Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ bǎyàŋ Yesu anɛ Násárɛt anɛ bágó ndǔ ɛkotákátí. Apú fá. Mandɛm akʉ yi apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi árɛ́mɛ́ nyaka bɛ ɛbhɔŋ bɛfakari. Twɔ́ ká ghɔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bábhʉ́rɛ́ yi.
Yesu adi.
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ, yɛ̌ agha anɛ árɔ́ ngɔrɛ́ ywi ndǔ nɛbhay, kɛbhák bɛ́ ngɔrɛ́ akwɛn bɛrwɔp, ambáy ngɔrɛ́ achak, akwɛn bɛrwɔp.”
Mánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́ghati bo mbok Yesu nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi akʉ ntá yap, bárɔ́ bare pɛtnsɛm Yerúsalɛm. Báre téé ndǔ bɔ́bɛtɔk Samária mangati nɔkɔ bo Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu. 
Yesu átɛ́m bɔ́ nɛkay bɛ, “Nkɨ mǔnkáp amɔt áchyɛ̀ nyaka yi bɛyǎ mbwɔt.
ɔ́nkʉ bǒbhi mándɨŋɨ bɛ chɔŋ yi amfoŋori bɛbʉ́ bhap, nɛ ampɛmɛ bhɔ.
Mmu anɛ ánù ásɔt awɔ́nɛm, chɔŋ ntɛp yi mbɔ ɛkwap amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm Mmu mɛ̌tòk, yí kɛfú arɛ wáwák. Nɛ chɔŋ nsɨ́ŋ nnyɛ́n Mandɛm nɛ nnyɛ́n ɛtɔk Mandɛm yi amʉɛt. Ɛtɔk ɛyɔ chi Yerúsalɛm anɛ nkɔ anɛ áfù amfay ntá Mandɛm átwɔ̀ fá amɨk. Chɔŋ nsɨŋ nnyɛ́n nɛkɔ ɛna nkwɔ yi amʉɛt.
Chɔŋ nsɔt nɛwú nsak bo abhɛn bákòŋo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi átɔ̀ŋ. Nɛ chɔŋ bɛká bǒnkwɔ mankɛm mándɨŋɨ bɛ́ Mmɛ kɛ̌ nchí chak nkaysi bo nɛ batɨ̌ yap, nɛ chɔŋ ńkap yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ayɛka bɛ́kóŋó ɛbhi bɛtɨk.
Ndu árɔ̀ŋ, ató bapɔkɔ́ ntó ambɨ. Bárɔk bachwe amɛm mɔ́tɔk amɔt atú Samária ndu bɛtoŋti mbaŋ ntá yi.
Fílip arɔk atɛmɛri Natániɛl aghati yi bɛ, “Sɛ́ghɔ̌ mmu anɛ Moses ásɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka ɛ̌ti yi amɛm Ɛkáti Bɛbhé Mandɛm, nkúbhɛ́ yi mmǔ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ nkwɔ básɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛ̌ti yi. Nɔ chi, Yesu mmu Násárɛt, mmɔ̌ Josɛ́f.”
Nkúbhɛ́ Moses-nɛ árɛ́mɛ́ nyaka ntá bo Israɛl bɛ, ‘Chɔŋ Mandɛm anchyɛ bhe ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ achak anɛ áfù ndu nkwɔ yɛka mbɔ ɛnyǔ achyɛ mɛ ntá yɛka.’
Símiɔn ayɛ́t bhɔ, arɛm ntá máyi María bɛ, “Mandɛm ayap mɔ́nɛ bɛ ankʉ bɛyǎ bo Israɛl mankwɛn nɛ bɛ ánjoŋ abhɛnɛfu, nɛ bɛ ámbák ɛrɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bo bárɛ̀m bɛ bápú yaŋ.
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, arɛm bɛ, nɛ́nɛ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ nchí kʉ bɛ́ bo mánsíɛ́ptí mɛ amɛm bɛkɛt ɛbhap mpok báfɛrɛ mɛ ndǔ bɛtɨk.’
Yesu atɛ́m nɛkay nɛ́chák bɛ, “Kɛfɔ Mandɛm kɛchi mbɔ ɛnyɨŋ bɛyǎ nkáp ɛnɛ ɛchi bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ amɛm nkɨ. Mmu amɔt ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ yɔ, apɛt abhɛsɛ yɔ sayri, arɔ, arɔk nɛ bɛyǎ maŋák, ati yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛyi, asɔt nkáp, aku nkɨ wu.” 
Mpok bo abhɛn bábhárɛ́ yi barak amʉɛt báfáté, bɔ́kɛ rɛm yɛ̌ ndak abʉ́abʉ mbɔ anɛ nkaysi bɛ bɔ bakway bɛrɛm bɛ yi akʉ.
Bakoŋo Yesu báchák bati byo bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bɔ̌ Sɛbɛdi barɛmɛ, bábhó bɛběntɨ nɛ mamʉɛrɛ bhap nɔ bachi nnɔ amɔt.
Chɔŋ Mandɛm anchyɛ bhe bɛtaŋ mpok Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ atwɔ́ ntá yɛka, mǎmbak yɛ batísiɛ bha amɛm Yerúsalɛm, nɛ atú Judɛ́ya ankɛm, nɛ atú Samária, nɛ ndǔ mmɨk nkɛm.” 
Bárɔ́k yɛ nɛ yɔ ntá Yesu. Básɔ́t ndɛn ɛnɛ́ mfǎymʉɛt ɛyap basɔbhɛri mɔ́mpɔŋɔ batu wu, bákwák yi achɔkɔ amfay.
Bě bǎsiɛ̀p bo ndǔ nywɔp nɛywěmʉɛt bɛ bǎkɛ kwɛn ɛbhé Moses. Bǎbentɨ nɛ mɛ mbɔnyunɛ́ nkʉ mmǔ nɛme átáŋ ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt?
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu abhʉɛ́t bɛrɛm nɔ nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi, ngɔ̌k aywi amɔt ndǔ abhɛn bati byo nɛ apay anɛ aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Júdas, achwɔp nɛ bɛyǎ bho. Bǒ bhɔ bábhák nɛ bɔakparɛnja nɛ nkɨ́k amɔ. Bǒbati bachiǎkap, nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses, nɛ bǒbati ɛtɔk kɛ̌ bátó nyaka bhɔ.
nɛ Júdas Iskariɔt anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka bɛti Yesu. 
Mpok Yesu achwe anywɔ́p, manɛ́mɛ́ amɨ́k bhɔ bákóŋo yi arɛ́. Abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ́ “Mǎnókó bɛ mɛ̌kwáy bɛkʉ mǎngɔ́ mbaŋ?” Bákɛ́mɛ bɛ, “Acha, sɛ́noko.”
Mfɔ Agripa arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Chɔŋ mɛmbɔŋ nkɔŋ bɛghok nɛ batú ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ̀m.” Fɛstɔs akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Chɔŋ ɔ́ngok yi mbúrɛ́.”
Kokosí nɔ́kɔ́ ká mmʉɛt nɛ Mandɛm nɛ chɔŋ Mandɛm ankokosi mmʉɛt nɛ bhe. Bě bakʉ̌ bɛbʉ́, fɛrɛ́ ká amɔ́ ndǔ bɛbʉ́. Bě bho bǎchí ɛkak nɛfí ɛkak ánywɔp, fɛrɛ́ ká bɛbʉ́ antɨ bɛ́ batɨ yɛka ambak pɛ́pɛ́p.
Báchyɛ bɛbhé ɛ̌ti bo abhɛn bákòŋo baghɔrɛ́ nɛ babhakanɛm nɛfí. Bachyɛ bɛbhé ɛ̌ti babhakanɛm abhɛn bábhʉrɛ nɛ batɨ̌ babhakanɛm nɛ baghɔrɛ́ nkwɔ abhɛn bákʉ̀ nɔ. Bachyɛ bɛbhé ɛ̌ti bo abhɛn bághɛ̀p batɨ̌ bakwǎŋwaŋ ndu bɛti bhɔ mbɔ basɛm. Báfyɛ bɛbhé ɛ̌ti basěnse. Bachyɛ bɛbhé ɛ̌ti bo abhɛn bátè ntísiɛ ákwárɛ́, nɛ Mandɛm achyɛ bɛbhé ɛ̌ti yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ákʉ̀ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́pú ndɔ́ŋ ámɔt nɛ nɛtɔ́ŋ ɛnɛ́n tɛtɛp.
Bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Wɔ ɔchí agha?” Yesu ákɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Nchí mmu anɛ ngáti bhe tɛ nɛbhǒnɛt bɛ nchi.
Ndaká yí bǎpú jwimɛm ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ́rɛ̀m? Chi mbɔnyunɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ntɨ bɛghok bɛyɔŋ ɛbha.
Yí Júdas achí nyaka ndǔ nkwɔ́ ywɛsɛ́ ndu Yesu áyábhɛ́ yi bɛ ankʉ bɛtɨk nɛ bhɛsɛ.
Mɛ kɛ nchí nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛ́n nɛ́chyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m.
Ndaká yí ɔ́yɨ̀ŋɨ mɔ́ɛ̌nyɨŋɨ anɛ achi anyɛsɛ ntɨ, ɛnɛ́ ɔ́pú fyɛ ntí ndǔ nkɔkɔ́nɔk anɛ achi wɔ anyɛsɛ?
Bátát nɔkɔ arɛ́ ndu bárɛ̀m ndaka wu, Píta afate aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Bɔ̌ma, bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ Mandɛm anáŋ ayap mɛ nɛ́ntɨ ɛnɛka tɛ mpok anɛ áfʉɛ́rɛ́ ansɛm bɛ́ ngati Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu ntá bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl bɛ́ bɔ́ nkwɔ́ mangok, mánoko.
Bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ɛ́fákárí ná kɛ ɔbho bɛghɔ mbaŋ?”
Yesu ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Ɛ́rɔp ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mɔt ɛnɛ́ ɔ́bhɨ́kɨ́ re kʉ. Dɔ́k tí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ mɛnkɛm, chyɛ̌ nkáp ntá bachɛ́bhɛ́bho. Mbák ɔ́nkʉ́ nɔ, chɔŋ ɔ́mbɔ́ŋ kɛfɔ̌ mɛnyɨŋ amfay. Ɔ́ntwɔ́ yɛ ɔnkoŋo mɛ. Nɛ chɔŋ ɔ́mbɔ́ŋ kɛfɔ̌ mɛnyɨŋ awǔ amfay.”
Basɛm, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka abhɔŋ bɛ́ghok mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ yi fá amɨk sayri. Chiɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ka bhɔ kɛnókó nɛ bɛchǎy nɛ nɛwɛrɛ́mʉɛt nɛ mǎnkʉ nɔ́kɔ́ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛka nɛ ntɨ nɛmɔt nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ bághòk Kristo.
Bě babhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛ ɛwak ɛ́mɔ́t, chɔŋ bo Mandɛm mántáŋ bǒ mmɨk kɛ? Mbák bǎbhɔŋ bɛtáŋ bǒ mmɨk ɛwak ɛ́mɔ́t, bɔ̌bɛkpɨ́kɨ́ri abhɛn báchí nɛ́ntɨ́ ɛnɛká kɛ̌ bapú kwáy bɛ́táŋ kɛ́?
Mandɛm apɛ́mɛ́ bhɛsɛ ndu áfɛ́rɛ́ bhɛsɛ ndǔ bɛbʉ́. Ayap bhɛsɛ bɛ sɛ́mbák bǒbhi. Akʉ nɔ yɛ̌ndu sɛ́pú bɛrɨ́tí bho. Anáŋ abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka nkaysi bɛ́pɛ́mɛ bhɛsɛ, tɛ mpok mmɨk ábhɨ́kɨ́re bho. Mandɛm anáŋ abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka nkaysi bɛ́fʉɛ́t ntá Yesu Kristo, antɔŋ bhɛsɛ bɛrɨ̌ndu bhi.
Bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎkʉ̀ ndǔ bǎbhɔŋɔ nɛka nɛ Yesu bɛ́chí mbɔ nnya anɛ básɔ́rɛ́ bɛchyɛ akap ntá Mandɛm mbɔ akap. Yɛ̌ ɛmbak chi bɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛna nɛ́rɔ̀ŋ mbɔ mmɛ́m amɛn bátò amfay nnya yɔ, mɛ̌bhák chi maŋák, nɛ nchí ŋák nɛ bhe mankɛm.
Ɛyɔ ɛ́ghàti bhɛsɛ bɛ yi? Chí bɛ́ bo Israɛl bábhɨ́kɨ́ ghɔ nyaka ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bɔ báyàŋ. Bǎru bho abhɛn Mandɛm áyábhɛ́ kɛ bághɔ́ nyaka yɔ. Mbák chí báchák, bágwɔt nyaka batɨ yap amɛm
Ɛ́tárɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, ɛnɛ́ Yesu achi chɔ́kɔ́ ɛbhě Njiɛ Mɛnok Ólif ɛnɛ ɛ́yɨŋɨ ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm, Píta nɛ Jems nɛ Jɔ̌n nɛ Andru bárɔ́k ntá yi ansɛm ansɛm.
abho mɛ́nɨkmʉɛt ntá yi nɛ ntɨ ɛni nɛnkɛm bɛ, “Mɔ́wa anɛ mɔ́ngɔrɛ́ ǎme tontó. Acha, twɔ́ nyaŋá yi amɔ amʉɛt bɛ ántaŋ, ákɛ́ gu.”
Asɨ́ŋ, andɛmɛ nɔkɔ amɛm bɛkáti bhi mɛnkɛm ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn. Mbɔk mɛnyɨŋ bɛchi amɛm bɛkáti ɛ́bhɛn yi asɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛbhɛn bɛ́bèmʉɛt bɛjwimɛm. Nɛ bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ, nɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ te kpirí, báyìbhiri mɛnyɨŋ yi asɨŋɨ́, mángati nɔkɔ bho chi mɛnyɨŋ bɛchak ɛbhɛn bɛpú ndɔ́ŋ amɔt nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛ́bhɛn yi ásɨ́ŋɨ́. Ndu bákʉ̀ nɔ, bábhɨ̀ŋɨ chi mɛ́nɛ́mɛ́ amʉɛt.
Barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ nsé báchi nyaka nɛntɨ bǒ Mandɛm. Nkúbhɛ́ ɛnyu yɔ kɛ ɛchi ɛchɔŋ bɛ batɔŋɔ́ nsé bábhɔŋ bɛbhesi nɛntɨ ɛnɛka mántɔŋ nɔkɔ be baraká nsé ɛ̌ti Mandɛm nɛ bapu ɛnɛ́ ɛyɔ ɛ́twɔ̀ bhɔ chi nɛ mɛ́nɛ́mɛ́. Bátɔ̀ŋ nɛ mánìsi bɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ ɛtayap mmu ákú bhɔ́ áfɛ́rɛ́ ndǔ kɛsɛm. Nɛ ndu bákʉ̀ nɔ, ngwɛnti yap ǎbɛ́p ancha.
Abhɛn ɛkɔŋ, bǎkáysí bɛ ndu mpok anɛ nkɛm sɛ́rɛ̀m mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn chi ndu bɛ́táŋá mmʉɛt ntá yɛka kɛ? Wáwák! Sɛ́rɛ̀m chi ɛnyǔ Kristo áyàŋ bɛ sɛ́ndɛm nɛ bɛsí Mandɛm. Sɛ́kʉ̀ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ chi bɛ mǎnsɛ́nɛ́ ndǔ mbi Mandɛm.
Ndu bǎkʉ̀ nɔ, mbɔŋ bɛcháy mbɔnyunɛ ɛchi mbɔ bɛ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn nkʉ bɛkwak bhe bɛchi chi ndɛ́ndɛm.
Nɨk nɔ́kɔ́ ka mmʉɛt bɛ mpok bɛbʉɛ ákɛ́ kwɛn yɛ̌ chi mpok mbaŋ ǎkwɛn chaɛɛ, nɛ yɛ̌ chi ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt.
Mpok yɔ, mbák bǒ bati apay bachi ɛbhɨ bákʉ̀ bɛtɨk, bákway bɛsɔt amɔt mándɔ achak.
Bǒ mbɨ̌ŋ nkú bápɛtnsɛm baghati bǒbatí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Pɔ̌l arɛmɛ nɛ bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́ Pɔ̌l nɛ Sáilas báchí bǒ Rom, bɛcháy bɛkɛm bɔ.
mbɔnyu básɨŋ nyaka ndǔ Ɛbhé Mandɛm bɛ, “Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mɔ̌mbɨ anɛ achi mbakanɛm, bábhɔŋ bɛchyɛ yi ntá Mandɛm.
Aghati bɔPíta bɛ, “Basɛ́mɛ́ ajwi mɛ antɨ mbɔ bɛ ǎway mɛ way. Chɔkɔ́ ká fá, mǎmbak pě nɛ mɛ.”
Mandɛm atɔŋ mɛ bɛrɨ̌ndu, asɔt mɛ bɛ nkʉ́ bɛtɨk ɛbhi ndu bɛghati bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́-nɛ. Akʉ nɔ ndǔ áchyɛ́ mɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi.
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, mbɔk bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bárɔ́k báté ɛyu, babho bɛyaŋ ɛnyǔ bákway bɛkʉ Yesu ánkwɛ́n anyu, bɛ bɔ mámbɔ́ŋ mbi bɛkɛm yi.
Bě nɛ bhɔ bǎchi bɛkpɔkɔ́ ntɔp ɛbhɛn básɔ́rɛ́ báté ɛkɛt ɛyɔ. Barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ nɛ bǒnto Yesu báchí nɛbhʉɛ́rɛ́kɛt ɛnɛn bághókó báté ɛkɛt ɛyɔ arɛ, nɛ Yesu Kristo yímbɔŋ achi ɛkwap ɛnɛ ɛ́kɛ̀m ɛkɛt.
Arɔk, ate nɛku bɛkɔk ɛbhɛn yi achi arɛ bhʉ́rɛ́. Achyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ mbʉ́ɛ́p wu ándɔ́ yí. Ámay. Afaté akʉ nɛnyíɛ́ abho mɛne bhɔ.
Ɛyɔ ɛ́yàŋ yɛ bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ ámbɔ́ŋ kɛboŋ. Bati tándrámɔt ate ndǔ njiɛ ɛgho tándrámɔt ɛnɛ ngɔrɛ́ wu áchɔ́kɔ́ arɛ. Njiɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́te nkwɔ ndǔ bafɔ tándrámɔt.
Ábraham afa yɛ atú bo Cháldia wu, arɔk achɔkɔ ɛtɔk Háran. Ɛtayi ágú nɔ́kɔ́, Mandɛm akʉ yi afa arɛ́ atwɔ́ ndǔ mmɨk anɛ bǎchí arɛ́ ɛchɔŋ.
Mbɔk batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses abhɛn báchí nyaka arɛ́ chɔkɔ báre bhɛp mmʉɛt ɛyap bɛ,
Ndɔŋ anɛ, Píta arɛm bɛ, “Mandɛm ántɛ́msí mɛ mbák mɛ̌sè chi nsé! Mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mbɔ̌ŋ mmu wu!” Tɛ́mté wu, nnɛ́m nkɔk akók.
Fílip abho ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt ɛkáti Aisáya wu agháti mǔngo Ɛtǒpia Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ Yesu.
Píta asá áwɔ́ akɛm yi akwak yi afate. Abhɨŋɨ yɛ bo Mandɛm nɛ mánkwɛ́sɛ́, asɔt Dɔ́kas atɔ́ŋ bɔ́ bɛ mangɔ bɛ́ yi achí nɛpɛ́m.
Yesu abhɔŋ bɛkɛm kɛfɔ kpátɛ Mandɛm ankʉ bǒmpap abhi mámdɔp mbɔ ɛnɔk ɛnɛ yi anyaŋa bɛkak amfay.
Mmu anɛ ákáysí bɛ́ arɨ́ŋɨ́, ǎtɔ̀ŋ chí bɛ́ abhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áyàŋ yí ándɨ́ŋɨ́.
Pú amɔ́ ya kɛ ághókó mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm-ɛ?’
Ɛka bǒnkwɔ abhɛn bachi fá ɛtɔk Bábilɔn, bátò be bakak. Mandɛm ayap bɔ́ nkwɔ mbɔ bhe. Mɔ́wa Mák nkwɔ ǎtò be bakak.
Bágháká nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ Njiɛ Mɛnɔk Ólif, Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Chɔŋ bě mankɛm mǎmfɛrɛ ntí nɛ mɛ mbɔnyunɛ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Mandɛm ǎdɛp chɔŋ mbabhɛri bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n angʉɛ́p amɨk, nkwɔ́ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n ántaka ɛbhɨ.
Mpú kʉ bɛrɨ ɛbhɛn mbɔ́ŋɔ́ ntɨ bɛkʉ. Kɛ nchí kʉ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mpu yaŋ bɛkʉ.
Mpok Mandɛm anɛ ápɛmɛ bhɛsɛ́ afyɛ́ ákwáy nɔkɔ, akʉ bo mándɨŋɨ ɛ̌ti nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛ́n bɛ́fʉɛ́t ndu Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ Yesu anɛ yi afyɛ́ amɔ́ya bɛ ngati bho.
Chɔŋ mǎnjaŋ mɛ, kɛ bǎpú ghɔ mɛ. Nɛbhʉɛt anɛ mɛ́rɔ̀ŋ bǎpú kwáy bɛ́twɔ arɛ́.”
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ́ bɛ, “Bě babhɔŋ, chyɛ̌ ká bhɔ nɛnyíɛ́ mányíɛ́.” Kɛ bábhɛ́p yí bɛ, “Ɔ̌yáŋ sɛ́ndɔ́k sɛ́nku nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ nkáp anɛ nkʉ bɛ́tɨk ányìɛ ndǔ bataŋ ánɛn sɛ́chíɛ bǒbhɛn?”
Arɔ yɛ are rɔ́ŋ. Kɛ bǒ ɛtɔk yi bápap nyaka yi. Bátó yɛ bo bɛ mándɔ́k mángátí mfɔ ngo bɛ ‘Acha, sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ yaŋ mmǔ-nɛ ambák mfɔ ywɛsɛ.’
Ɛpa ɛ́máy nɔ́kɔ́, bare pɛtnsɛm ɛtɔk ɛyap kɛ Yesu arɔp Yerúsalɛm, chi nɛ nnɔ kɛrɨŋɨ.
Mbɔ bɛ́pókómʉɛt mɛnkɛm bɛ́chí chí ɛ́pókómʉɛt ɛ́mɔ́t, mbʉ́ mmʉɛt nkwǎŋwaŋ ǎfu fá?
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Pɛtnsɛm anywɔ́p, mɔ́ywɛ apú gú.” Mǔngo wu anoko ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Yesu árɛ́mɛ́, afa, are gurɛ.
Júdas anáŋ achyɛ́ nyaka bhɔ ɛrɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kwák bɔ mándɨŋɨ Yesu. Akʉ nɔ́, ndǔ ághátí bhɔ́ bɛ, “Mmǔ anɛ mɛ̌bhɛnɛ chɔŋ chí yi. Kɛ́m ká yi mǎndɔk nɛ yi bɛ ákɛ́ bʉɛ.”
“Ɛ́rɨ ɛcha ntá yɛka mpok bo bápàp bhe, nɛ mánsɔkɔti nɔkɔ bhe nɛ mándɛm bɛbɛ́pti mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti yɛka, nɛ mándɛm nɔkɔ bɛ bǎchí bɛbɛ́ptí bho ɛ̌ti ya, Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm!
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Bádurɛ ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ mánsɔt ɛnyɨŋ mankuti kɛ? Bádurɛ ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ mántɛn antɛnɛ́ bɛkɔk kɛ? Pú bádùrɛ ɛrɔŋɔ mánte chi ndǔ nɛbhʉ́ɛ́t anɛ báte ɛrɔŋɔ?
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ɛchi nɛpɛ́m nɛ ɛbhɔŋ bɛtaŋ. Ɛ́chap ɛcha yɛ̌ntɨkɨ akparɛnja nsɛm ɛpay. Ɛ́chwè tɛ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ nɛpɛ́m nkwǎ nɛ́chɛm nɛ ɛfóŋó ɛyi. Ɛ́chwè mmu antɨ ɛ́ntɔŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi átɨ́ bɛkʉ.
Bɛsí ángɛl Mandɛm wu bɛ́ré ghɔɔ mbɔ miámiaŋ, ndɛn ɛyi ɛ́ndiɛrɛ nɔkɔ pɛ́pɛ̌pɛ́p mbɔ ɛtɔkɔfiɔŋ.
Amɛm ɛkɛt ɛgho puyɛ̌ ndiɛrɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bághókó nɛ pú nɛ ɛbhɛn bághókó nɛ *ɛ́gírí kɛ bɛ́bhak arɛ. Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn baghoko nɛ mɛnɔk nɛ ɛbhɛn bághoko nɛ ntɔp bɛ́bhak arɛ́ nkwɔ. Mbɔk mɛnyɨŋ chí ɛbhɛn básɔt mánkʉ ɛnyɨŋ arɛ nɛ kɛnókó. Bɛ́chák chi ɛbhɛn bápu sɔt mankʉ ɛnyɨŋ arɛ nɛ kɛnókó.
Kɛ bo mankɛm bághók ɛnyǔ bǎghòk Mandɛm, nɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́chyɛ̀ mɛ maŋák ɛ̌ti yɛka. Nchí yaŋ mǎmbák barɨŋɨ́ndak bɛ mǎnkʉ nɔkɔ chi bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ, kɛ bo abhɛn amɨ́k ábhɨ́kɨ́re nɛ́nɛ bhɔ bɛ bákɛ́ kʉ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ.
Ábraham anoko bɛ́ yɛ Áisek agǔ gu, Mandɛm ǎkway bɛkʉ bawú mampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Sɛ́kway yɛ bɛrɛm bɛ Áisek achí nyaka chi mbɔ mmu anɛ ánáŋ ágú kɛ Mandɛm akʉ yi afú ndǔ nɛwú, apɛtnsɛm ntá ɛtayi.
Yesu áte, achyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ mántwɔ́ nɛ yi. Bátwɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ kɛ́kwɔ́t nɛ yi, Yesu abhɛ́p yi bɛ,
Bǎbhɔŋ bɛrɨŋɨ bɛ mpok anɛ yi ánáŋ ákʉ́ nɔ, are yaŋ bɛ ɛtayap ánjɛ́t yi mmu achi nsensi, kɛ ɛtayap anisi mbɔnyunɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ nyaka mbi bɛyibhiri ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ákú yɛ̌ndu mɔ́wu áyàŋ nyaka áfɔ́k nɛ babhɛsɛ amɨ́k.
Mmu anɛ ápɨ̀ mbwɔ́t nɛ mmu anɛ ámyàkati manyiɛp arɛ́ báchí ɛnyu ɛ́mɔ́t, mbɔnyunɛ bákʉ̀ chí ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́rɛ́ ɛ́mɔ́t. Mandɛm ǎkap yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap bɛ́kóŋo ɛbhi bɛtɨk ɛbhɛ́n yí ákʉ́.
Ángɛl arɛm bɛ, “María, ɔ́kɛ́ cháy. Mandɛm atɔŋ wɔ bɛrɨ̌ndu.
Nɛ́nɛ, nsáy ǎnoŋ mɛ. Nsáy yɔ, Yesu Acha mmu achí ntaŋá manyé kɛ áchyɛ̀ mburɛ mɛ yɔ́ ndǔ ɛwak ɛnɛ yi ápɛtnsɛm. Yi achi chak bɛsí Mandɛm. Nɛ nsáy yɔ apu chí ntá ya mɛ awánti. Achí ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ anɛ ánòŋ nɛpɛrɛ́nsɛm Yesu nɛ maŋák. 
Mbɔk ɛyap mánóko, báchɛ́m mmʉɛt nɛ Pɔ̌l. Bɛyǎ bǒ Grik abhɛn mánɨ̀kmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm bo Israɛl nɛ bɛyǎ manɛ́m baghɔrɛ́ ɛtɔk ɛyɔ mánóko nkwɔ, báchɛ́m mmʉɛt nɛ bɔPɔ̌l mbɔ bakoŋo Yesu.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chí arɛ́ chí bɛ mǔbɛtɨk anɛ báfyɛ́ yí ɛnyɨŋ awɔ́ bɛ́ ánkɛ́m sayri, abhɔŋ bɛtɔŋ chi-bɛtɨk aywi bɛ́ yí achí mmǔ tɛtɛp.
Ndu bárɔŋ ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ yi ánchyɛ́ bhɔ ɛyɔŋ, anyabhɛ mmʉɛt téé, aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Mmǔ ywɛka anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ re kʉ bɛbʉ́ ánjámbɨ ámbwɔ́p ntay antɛm yi.”
Yesu aghati yi bɛ, “Mmǔ anɛ ánáŋ ásó mmʉɛt, abhɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ bhɔŋ bɛso mmʉɛt, ɛbhɨkɨ fʉɛt bɛkak ɛbhi, mbɔnyunɛ mmʉɛt nkɛm achi pɛ́pɛ́p. Nɛ bǎchi pɛ́pɛ́p, kɛ puyɛ̌ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka.”
Mpók nchí kɛnkɔ nɛntɨ ɛnɛka, bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ sɔt mɛ mbɔ ntɨ manɔ́; mpok mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ ndɛn, bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ chyɛ mɛ ndɛn; mpok mɛ̌me, bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ kokori mɛ, nɛ mpok nchí ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ, bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ twɔ bɛghɔ mɛ.’
Mbɔk batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm abhɛn báchí nyaka bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ndu Yesu ányìɛ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ bǒ bɛbʉ́ nɛ babhɛbhɛ́ nkábhɛ́nti, bábhɛ́p bakoŋo bhi bɛ, “Ndaká yí yi ányìɛ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ mɛnyǔ bǒbhɛn?”
Hɛ́rɔd are cháy bɛway Jɔ̌n mbɔnyunɛ arɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka bɛ Jɔ̌n achi chak nɛ nyáŋá bɛsí Mandɛm. Yɛ̌ndu ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Jɔ̌n árɛ̀m ɛ́fyɛ̀ nyaka yi ɛbyɔk antɨ abhɔ̌ŋ maŋák bɛghok Jɔ̌n.
Arɛ́, bágháti Galío bɛ, “Mmǔnɛ ánù bɛkʉ bo mánchyɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ Mandɛm kɛnókó ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ ɛbhé yɛsɛ́ ɛ́pú yaŋ mmu ankʉ.”
Njibhiri yɛ mmʉɛt ndu bɛ́ghɔ mmu anɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛyi ɛ́twɔ̀ ntá ya. Ngɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ pú tándrámɔt ɛbhɛn bɛ́pɔ̀kɔ bɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ mkpak.
Abɨk nɛ bɛtaŋ arɛm ntá María bɛ, “Ɔchí anɛ Mandɛm áyɛ́rɛ́ ndǔ nkwɔ baghɔrɛ́, nɛ áfɔ́k ámbák nɛ mmɔ̌ anɛ ɔ́bhe chɔŋ!
Mbɔ̌ŋ yɛ nkaysi bɛtɨk bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm, mpoknkɛm, yɛ̌ndu bǎrɨŋɨ bhɔ nɛ bǎte kpirí ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ tɛtɛp ɛbhɛn bátɔ́ŋɔ́ be.
Bɛ́bhó mpok yɔ, Yesu abho bɛ́gháti bakoŋo bhi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛbhɔŋɔ bɛfakari nɛ yi. Arɛm bɛ yi abhɔŋ bɛrɔŋ Yerúsalɛm, nɛ arɛ́, bǒbati ɛtɔk, nɛ bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses mánchyɛ yi bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri, kpát mángwáy yi, kɛ ɛ́ghaka nɔkɔ manywɔp arat, ampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.
Kɛ mmu anɛ átáŋá bɛsí bho bɛ yi apu mmu wa, chɔŋ mɛnkwɔ́ ntaŋa bɛsí Ɛtaya mmu achi amfay bɛ yi apu mmu wa.” 
Yesu akɛmɛ bɛ, “Chi mɛ, nɛ chɔŋ mǎngɔ Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm chɔkɔ ndǔ ɛnɔk kɛnókó ɛbhe awɔ́nɛm Mandɛm bɛtaŋ mɛnkɛm. Chɔŋ mǎngɔ ndǔ Mmu anɛ áfú amfay átwɔ̀ amɛm nɛbháŋ.”
Bɛyǎ bo bárɔ́k ɛkɛt ɛnɛ́ yi achi arɛ́, ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ ɛpok ɛ́pú nyaka bɛsoŋ ɛkak, yɛ̌ chí nɛfí. Yesu are ghati bhɔ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm.
Mpok nchwɔ́bhɛ́ Troas ndu bɛghati bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo, Acha ánɛ́nɛ́ mbi ntá ya.
Nɛpɛ́m nɛkɔ ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ fu chi ntá bachi nɛ manɔ abhɛka bo bapɛm ayap áfʉɛrɛ fʉɛt. Mandɛm asɔt chi Ɛyɔŋ ɛyi kɛ ǎchyɛ bhe nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn, nɛ nɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti mbɔnyunɛ nɛ́fǔ ndǔ Ɛyɔŋ ɛyi ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m, nɛ ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.
Tɔmás átɛ́mɛ́rí nɔ́kɔ́ bhɔ, báré ghati yi bɛ, “Sɛ́ghɔ Yesu Acha.” Kɛ yi akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Kpátɛ ngɔ́ nɛ amɨ́k bɛbhé-mpi yí amɔ, ntɔk bhɔ́ nɛ sɛnɔŋ awɔ, mbát awɔ́ ndǔ tambe ywi mpú noko.”
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu átɔ̀ŋ arɛm bɛ, “Sɔt ka mpok nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses. Bákɔŋ bɛ́ghap, mǎnkó mansɛp nɛ bɛwubhɛ wubhɛ́ ndɛn amʉɛt nɛfísiɛ bɛ bo mánkaka nɔkɔ bhɔ nɛ kɛnókó.
Tɛ́mté wu, Safíra akwɛ́n bɛkak Píta agú. Bɛsak báchwé nɔ́kɔ́ bághɔ́ bɛ agu, bápɔkɔ bafu barɔk babhɛmɛ kɛkwɔt nɛ nnɛ́m.
Yi kɛ aghoko mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm nɛ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm bɛchi chi ndǔ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi, nɛ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm bɛchi chi ndǔ bɛchyɛ yi kɛnókó. Sɛ́nchíɛ yi kɛnókó mpoknkɛm. Amen.
Bɛyǎ bakoŋo Yesu báfú nyaka Yerúsalɛm ɛ̌ti ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ ɛbho mpok báwáy Stífin bataka mbaŋ nɛ mbaŋ. Mbɔk bárɔk kpatɛ atú Foníshia, báchák tɛ Sáyprɔs nɛ abhɛnɛfu tɛ Ántiɔk. Bárɔŋ nɔkɔ nɔ, mangati nɔkɔ mbok Yesu ntá bo Israɛl bɔ́bhɔ.
Ɛrɨ nyaka mbɔŋ bɛ bákɛ́ rɨŋɨ ɛnyǔ mmu abhak chak ɛ́cha bɔ bɛrɨŋɨ, kɛ mámpɛt mánjibhiri mmʉɛt, mándɔ bɛbhé Mandɛm áchyɛ́, kɛpɛrɛ koŋo bhɔ.
Bárɔ bare rɔŋ, bágháká kɛ́kwɔ́t nɛ ɛtɔk mbɔ nkárɛ́nká byo nɛ ɛpay. Nkúbhɛ́ mpok yɔ, Píta akó amfay ɛkɛt ndu mɛnɨkmʉɛt. Mfay ɛkɛt abhak ransi.
Chɔŋ bo mámfu mbɨ nɛ nsɛm, ɛbhě awɔ́nɛm nɛ awɔ́ghɔ, mánchɔkɔ mányiɛ ɛpǎ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛ́rɛ́ kɛfɔ̌ Mandɛm.
Kɛ Píta arɛm bɛ, “Mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ nkáp, kɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ chɔŋ nchyɛ́ wɔ. Ndǔ nnyɛ́n Yesu Kristo mmu Násárɛt, faté kɔ!”
Yɛ̌ nɛ́nɛ, mbɔk yap báchwè ndǔ manɛrɛ́kɛt mándwɔ nɔ́kɔ́ baghɔrɛ́ abhɛn bápu ka bɛkɛm mmʉɛt bɛ mángwákárí bɛkwɛn ndǔ ntǎ bɛbʉ́.
Nkɛ ghɔ yɛ̌ mǔnto achak arɛ, ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ fʉɛ́t Jems, manɔ Yesu Acha.
Ndǔ nkwɔ bho abhɛn ntó ntá yɛka, yɛ̌ amɔt ábhɨ́kɨ́ sɔt nnyɛ́n ɛna bɛrwɔ bhe. Ɛ́pú nɔ kɛ?
Nchí ghati bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mbɔnyunɛ chɔŋ Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm mpɛtnsɛm fá amɨk nɛ bɛtaŋ Ɛtaya. Mbɔŋ bɛ́twɔ nɛ bɔángɛl Mandɛm, nchyɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu aywi akap, bɛ́kóŋo bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ́.
Bǎkwáy bɛ́rɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́fàkari mbúrɛ́ ná? Bapɛ́m ayɛka achi mbɔ mɔ́ngo. Ɔ̌ghɔ́ mɔ́ngo nɛ́nɛ kɛ mandú mpok anɛmsi.
Yesu asɔt yɛ bɛkpɔkɔ́ brɛt bhɔ. Áchyɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bakak ntá Mandɛm, akɔrɛ ntá bo abhɛn báchɔ́kɔ́ amɨk. Akʉ ɛnyumɔ́t nɛ nsi. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anyiɛ́ kpát ajwi.
Basɨŋ nkwɔ amɛm ɛkáti bɛ, “Ntay ɛnɛ́n nɛ́kʉ̀ chɔŋ bo mántɛm ɛkak mánkwɛ́n, nkúbhɛ́ nɔ́ kɛ nɛchi sɛtárɛ́bhɛ́ ɛsɛn sɛ́kʉ̀ bo mánkwɛn.” Bátɛ̀m ɛkak arɛ́ mbɔnyunɛ bápú bhʉɛrɛ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyu Mandɛm atɨ nyaka bɛ ɛ́mbák.
Kpátɛ̌ ɛchɔŋ, bǎbhɨkɨ re bhɛ́p Ɛtaya yɛ̌nyɨŋ ndǔ nnyɛ́n ɛna. Bɛ́p ká, nɛ chɔŋ anchyɛ be bɛ maŋák amɛka anjwi pɔɔt.” 
Bǒnkwɔ abhɛn Lístra nɛ Ikɔ́niɔm bárɛ̀m nyaka ɛrɨrɨ ɛ̌ti Tímɔti.
“Ɛ̌! Yesu, Mmu Násárɛt, ɔbhɔŋ yí bɛkʉ nɛ bhɛsɛ! Ɔtwɔ fá bɛway bhɛsɛ? Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ mmu wɔ ɔ́chí. Ɔ́chí Mmu Nyáŋá anɛ Mandɛm átó!”
Ɛwak ɛ́mɔt, mǔnti bo Israɛl abhɛ́p Yesu bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, wɔ mmǔ ndɨ́ndɨ́, chɔŋ nkʉ yi kɛ mbɔ̌ŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛ́n nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti?”
Mandɛm áyàŋ nyaka bɛ bǒbhɔ mándɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ ɛnyɨŋ bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ ɛnɛ yi átóŋtí abhʉrɛ chi nnɛ́m ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛbhɔŋɔ bɛkwak bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl. Kristo achí amɛm batɨ yɛka, nɛ bǎkway bɛbhaka ntɨ bɛ chɔŋ mǎnyiɛ kɛnɛ́m ɛki nɛ yi.
Baghɔk Yesu bábhɛ́p yi ntí nɛkay ɛnɛn.
Afɔ̌ kɛ Yesu árɛ́mɛ́ ntá yap bɛ, “Bo báchyɛ̀ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm kɛnókó yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak. Ndiɛrɛ ɛtɔk ɛyi nɛ ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt ywi, kɛ bápú chyɛ yi kɛnókó.”
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kpɨ́k ɛ́kʉ́ bɔ bádí kɛbhɔ tontó chi ndǔ yi ághátí bhɔ bɛ bápú pɛrɛ ghɔ yi.
Sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ mmu anɛ Mandɛm áchyɛ́ yi nɛpɛ́m nɛkɔ apú pɛrɛ kɔŋ bɛkʉ bɛbʉ́ mbɔnyunɛ Mmɔ Mandɛm achi nɛ yi nɛ ákɛ̀m yi ɛnyu ɛnɛ Satan apu kway bɛkʉ yi yɛ̌nyɨŋ.
Sɛ́pú kwáy bɛrɔ bɛrɛm ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn sɛ́ghɔ́ nɛ amɨ́k nɛ sɛ́ghók nɛ batú.”
“Agha nɛ́? Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ̀m chi nsɔk ntá Mandɛm! Mandɛm aywǐnti kɛ ákway bɛfoŋori bɛbʉ́ mmu!”
Kʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛ́bhɛn. Fíɛ́ ntí arɛ́ bɛ́ bo mángɔ́ ndu ɔ́kʉ̀ sayri.
Nchí ghati bhe bɛ báchyɛ mbɔ ɛnyǔ amɔ yap átɔ̀ŋ. Nɛ mpok báchyɛ̀, báchyɛ́ mbɔŋ ɛcha ɛnyǔ amɔ́ ayap átɔ́ŋɔ́, mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɛ́fú bhɔ antɨ.
Mfɔ Hɛ́rɔd apɔp! Ɛ̌ti nɛyɨkɨ anɛ yí áyɨkɨ nyaka bɛsí mankɔ abhi ɛ́chá yi bɛyibhiri ɛyɔŋ ɛyi. Achyɛ yɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ́ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu mankʉ mbɔ ɛnyǔ mmɔ̌ Hɛródias áyàŋ.
Bo abhɛn báté kɛ́kwɔ́t nɛ Pɔ̌l bábhɛp yi bɛ, “Ɔ̌sɔkɔti mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm-ɛ?”
Yesu aghɔ́ bhɔ ntínso. Atɔk amɨ́k ayap. Tɛ́mté wu, babho bɛghɔ mbaŋ nɛ babho bɛkoŋo Yesu.
Nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́, arɔk atɛmɛri ndu bǒbhi, bo Israɛl bati apay mánù. Achwe bɛkʉ bɔ mambak ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt, arɛm bɛ, ‘Ghók ká, bǎchí bǒ mmu amɔt, ndaká yí mánù nɛ batɨ?’
Sɛ́chɛ̀m amɔ ndǔ bɛtɨk Mandɛm. Nɛ bǎchí mbɔ nkɨ Mandɛm, anɛ sɛ́kʉ̀ bɛtɨk amɛm, bǎpɛ́t bǎbhak mbɔ ɛkɛt ɛnɛ Mandɛm átè.
Ndu mpok ɛyɔ, Mandɛm ǎrɛm nyaka kɛpɨ, mmɨk anyɨkɨsi, kɛ nɛ́nɛ afyɛ́ bariɛp bɛ, “Chɔŋ nkʉ mmɨk anyɨkɨsi ndɔŋ achak gbogbǒgbok, nɛ puyɛ̌ mmɨk yɔ́yɔ́, kɛ mfǎy nkwɔ.”
Kɛ Mɛlkísɛdɛk mmu ápú nyaka mbɔ̌ŋ mmǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt Lɛ́vi asɔt nyaka ɛnyǔ akap wu nɔ Ábraham áchyɛ́ yi, ayɛ́t yi mmu Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp nɛ yi.
Kɛ mmu anɛ ngó ásɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛ́n yí ákʉ́ ndǔ nɛbhʉ́ɛ́rɛ́kɛt ɛnɔ, ǎbhɔŋ chí mɛ́nɛ́mɛ́. Mandɛm ǎpɛmɛ ɛnyǔ nte-bɛkɛt wu, kɛ ǎbhák chí mbɔ mmu anɛ árɔ́bhɛ́ chí mandú bɛ́sɔ́ŋɔ amɛm ɛkɛt, kɛ anɔnɛ, afú, ɛkɛt ɛ́sɔ́ŋɔ́ kurukotok.
Tɛ̌ndu Kristo ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ yɛ ɛsɔŋɔri fá amɨk, agú, bǎbhɔŋ bɛgwɔt mmʉɛt nɛ ɛnyǔ nkaysi anɛ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka mbɔnyunɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛsɔŋɔri mbɔ Kristo fá amɨk abhɨkɨ pɛrɛ bhɔŋ ɛnyɨŋ bɛkʉ nɛ bɛbʉ́.
Nɛ mbák sɛ́bhɔŋ nɛbhakántɨ, ɛyɔ ɛ́pú twɔ bhɛsɛ nɛ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́. Sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ Mandɛm akɔŋ bhɛsɛ tontó, mbɔnyunɛ akʉ bɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ mmu yi achyɛ bhɛsɛ ánkʉ ɛkɔŋ ɛyi ɛnjwi bhɛsɛ antɨ.
Bakoŋó Jɔ̌n bárɔ́k, basɔt ɛrɛnɛ́ Jɔ̌n barɔk, babhɛmɛ. Bárɔ́k yɛ baghati Yesu ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́fákárí nɛ Jɔ̌n. 
Kɛ faté. Mbésí wɔ bɛsí ndu bɛyap wɔ ɔ́mbák mǔbɛtok awa. Chɔŋ ɔ́mbak ntísiɛ wa, ɔ́ngati nɔkɔ bo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ɔ́ghɔ́ fá ambi ɛchɔŋ, nɛ ɛbhɛ́n mɛ́tɔ̀ŋ chɔŋ wɔ ansɛm mpok.
Kɛ María ate nɛpaka nnɛm andi nɔkɔ kɛbhɔ, nɛ ɛnɛ́ yí ábhʉɛ́t bɛdi, akuri amɨk, agʉɛ́p amɨ́k awu amɛm nnɛm.
Ɛkɔŋ ɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti. Kɛ mbák chi akap bɛghati bho mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fú nta Mandɛm, chɔŋ wu ámfʉɛt. Chɔŋ akap bɛrɛm bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛbhɛn mmu abhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ ámay nɛ anɛ́ bɛrɨŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ndǔ bɛtaŋ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ áfʉɛrɛ fʉɛt nkwɔ.
Yesu abho yɛ̌ bɛ́tɛm nɛkay ɛnɛn bɛ, “Mmǔ amɔt apwɔ nyaka nkáp ntá bǒ batí apay. Amɔt akɛ́m yi bɛbhǎ nkáp byo. Anɛfú ɛbhǎ nkáp ɛ́mɔt.
Kɛ Mandɛm atɨknsɛm ntá yap akpɨk arɔ bɔ mánchyɛ̀ nɔkɔ kɛnókó ntá mmok, nɛ ntaŋ nɛ mambě mfay mbɔ bɔmandɛm abhap, mbɔ ɛnyu ɛchi amɛm bɛkáti barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ bɛ, ‘Bo Israɛl! Mpok anɛ bǎkɔ̀ amɛm baso ndǔ mamiɛ́ bɛsa bɛ́páy, ntá yá kɛ̌ báwày nyaka nnya mánchyɛ̀ nɔkɔ akap kɛ?
Ansɛm mpok, bachǐmbɨ bhɛsɛ́ bárɔ yɔ́ ntá bɔ̌bhap. Bápɔ́kɔ́ yɔ́ mpok bákɔ̀ nɛ Jóshua. Mandɛm abók bo abhɛn báchí arɛ bɛsí bɔtayɛsɛ, basɔt mmɨk. Ɛ́tɛm ɛyɔ ɛ́bhák arɛ́ tɛ mpok anɛ Debhít achi mfɔ.
Kɛ ndǔ bo Israɛl bábhɨkɨ ka, nkɛbhɔŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛchak bɛkʉ, ɛbhɨkɨ fʉɛt chi bɛrɛm bɛ́ mántɛn nyé ɛna ntá Mfɔ Rom, yɛ̌ndu mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ mbɔ̌ŋ manyé nɛ bǒbha.”
Batɨ ayɛka ájwí nɛ́nɛ nɛ basɛ́mɛ́ mbɔnyunɛ ngátí bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn.
Pú Mandɛm arɛm ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ chí ɛ̌ti yɛsɛ́? Tɛtɛp, básɨŋ yɔ́ amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm chí ɛ̌ti yɛsɛ́ mbɔnyunɛ ɛ́rɨ bɛ́ mmu anɛ ákwáŋá nkɨ nɛ mmu anɛ áfɛ́rɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛbhɨ mámbáká ntɨ bɛ́ báchyɛ̀ bɔ́ ɛnap nɛnyíɛ́, ndǔ ɛnɛn bɔ báfɛ́rɛ́ ɛbhɨ.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ághòk mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ̌rɛ̀m, ankʉ mbɔ ɛnyǔ ndɛ́mɛ́, achí mbɔ ndɨŋɨndak anɛ até ɛkɛt ndǔ sɛtárɛ́bhɛ́.
Ángɛl akɛmɛ Sakaría bɛ, “Dɨŋɨ́ bɛ́ mɛ nchí Gábriɛl. Nchí téé bɛsí Mandɛm, nɛ yímbɔŋ kɛ átó mɛ bɛ ngati wɔ mbok ndɨ́ndɨ́ nɛ.
Ngɔ́ yɛ mfǎy nkɔ nɛ mmɨk nkɔ. Mfǎy anɛ mbɨ nɛ mmɨk anɛ mbɨ mǎnáŋ mánɛmsi nyaka. Manyu nkwɔ́ kɛpɛrɛ bhák.
Ndaká yí bǎpányu? Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛ́ mandú yís anɛ báfyɛ́ ndu fláwa anɛ bábáy ndu bɛ́ghaŋ pɔfpɔ́f, ǎkʉ fláwa amwɔt kɛ?
Tímɔti, nchí sɛmti yɛ wɔ bɛsí Mandɛm nɛ bɛsí Yesu Kristo mmú átaŋ mburɛ bo abhɛn báchi pě nɛ abhɛn bágu ɛwak ɛ́mɔt mpok yi ábhèsi bɛkʉ bo mángɔ bɛ yi achi Mfɔ.
Ɔnókó bɛ́ Mandɛm amɔt kɛ áchí, achák ápú? Ɛrɨ! Kɛ ɔ́kɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk bɛ́ yɛ̌ chí bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ mɛ́nókó nkwɔ́ bɛ́ Mandɛm amɔt kɛ áchí nɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́chyɛ̀ bhɔ́ bɛcháy, mángwɛrɛ nɔkɔ gbagbǎgbak.
Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm kɛ̌ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ yɛ bɛrɛm ɛnyǔ mmu abhɔŋɔ bɛkʉ nɛ ɛbhé ɛnɛ ɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ́ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt.”
Ɛkáti ɛnɛ ɛ́rɛ̀m ɛ̌ti Ɛyɔŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi tɛ mpok anɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́re ghoko mmɨk. Sɛ́ghók ɛ̌ti yi, sɛ́ghɔ́ yi nɛ amɨ́k, sɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ yi, nɛ sɛ́tɔk yi nɛ amɔ. Ɛyɔŋ ǎchyɛ Nɛpɛ́m.
Kɛ ɛ̌ti yɛká, ɛ́rɨ bɛ́ mbák nɛpɛ́m.
Kɛ nchí bhɛp bɛ, bo Israɛl bábhɨ́kɨ́ jwi nyaka mmɛm kɛ? Bájwimɛm mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm árɛ̀m mbɔ ɛnyǔ Moses ásɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ, “Chɔŋ nkʉ mǎmbɔŋ mpabhamɨ́k nɛ bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ɛtɔk. Chɔŋ nkʉ batɨ ámbe be amɛm ɛ̌ti bǒ bɛtɔk bɛchak abhɛn bachi bɛchɨŋtǐ bho.”
Chɔŋ bɔ́ nɛ nnya mbʉmbʉ mánte nɛnu nɛ Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n nɛ yi ansɔt awɔ́nɛm amfay yap mbɔnyunɛ yi kɛ achi Acha Mfɔ nɛ Mfɔ bafɔ. Bakoŋo bhi chí bo abhɛn Mandɛm ábhɨ́ŋɨ́, ayap, nɛ bákòŋo yi nɛ ntɨ nɛmɔt.”
Mbák ɔ́ntɔ́ŋ bǒnkwɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn, chɔŋ ɔ́mbak ɛrɨ́tí nkʉbɛtɨk Yesu Kristo anɛ máné nɛ bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chyɛ nɛka nɛ nɛtɔ́ŋ ɛnɛ́n tɛtɛp ɛnɛn ɔ́kóŋó.
Kɛ ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, mbʉ́ɛ́p ataŋataŋ anɛ átwɔ̀ nɛ bɛyǎ mpɛ́rɛ́nyɛn abho mɛnu, bɛ́fú atú ɛtɔk anɛ mmok, áfù arɛ. Bábhɨŋɨ nyaka mbʉ́ɛ́p wu bɛ Mbʉ́ɛ́p Nɔt-Is bɛkoŋo atú anɛ wu áfù.
Bakʉ̌-bɛtɨk amɛm áchwí báré yáŋ mbi bɛpɛmɛ mmʉɛt ɛyap. Básɔt áchwí nɨŋɨnɨŋɨ anɛ́ básɛ́rɛ́ amfay básɛ́bhɛ anyɛ́n bɛ manok manko abhɨ kɛ bákɔt ngɛpti mbɔ bɛ bárɔ̀ŋ bɛfɛrɛ chi baro áchák ambɨ áchwí mánsɛbhɛ anyɛ́n.
Bǒfú bátwɔ́ nɛ mbɛ́ntí amɔt anɛ bápɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ bɛkpaka. Báré yaŋ mbi bɛchwe anywɔ́p bɛ mambʉrɛ yi bɛsí Yesu.
mbɔnyunɛ mɔ́wa-nɛ agǔ nyaka, kɛ nɛ̌nɛ apɛt achi nɛpɛ́m. Anɛm nyaka kɛ mpɛt ngɔ yí.’ Afɔ̌ kɛ̌ ɛpa ɛ́bhó.
Mbák mmu adɛp wɔ atá ndǔ ɛbhe awɔ́nɛm, tɔ́ŋ yi ɛbhe ɛ́chák nkwɔ. Nɛ mbák mmu ásɔt ndɛ́ yɛ, dɔ̌ yi ansɔt yɛ̌ chí nkú yɛ nkwɔ.
Bágháti bhɔ bɛ, “Ghatí nɔ́kɔ́ ká bho chi bɛ bakoŋo bhi bátwɔ́ nɛ bɛti, mpok sɛ́kwɛ́nɛ́ kɛnɔ́, bághɛ́p yi, bápɔ́kɔ bárɔk.
Bǎkaysi bɛ yi? Mbák mmu abhɔŋ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n bɛsa bɛtay, amɔt anɛm ɛbhɨ, yí ǎkʉ yi? Pú ǎrɔ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n anɛ achi ndǔ nkwɔ́ bɛsa mɛnwi nsɛm nɛku nɛ anwi ambɨ̌-njiɛ, andɔk bɛyaŋ awu amɔt anɛ ánɛ́mɛ́?
Yɛ̌ mmu apú anɛ ásɔ̀t nɛpɛ́m ɛna ntá ya. Mɛmbɔ̌ŋ kɛ nchí chyɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛna. Mbɔ̌ŋ bɛtaŋ bɛ́chyɛ nɔ, nɛ mbɔ̌ŋ bɛtaŋ bɛ́pɛ́t bɛbhɔŋ nɔ. Ɛnɛ, chí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ Ɛtaya ághátí mɛ nkʉ.”
Kɛ mpok ɔ́bhak ndǔ nɛtarɛ́nsay, sǒ bɛsí bhɛ watí, ɔ́mpák ntí.
Mpok ngɔ́ yi, nkwɛ́n bɛkak ɛbhi nkáy mbɔ ngú. Kɛ yi anyaŋa awɔ́nɛm aywi mɛ amʉɛt arɛm bɛ, “Ɔ́kɛ́ chay, Mmɛ kɛ̌ nchí Ambɨ nɛ Ansɛm.”
Kɛ́m ká mmʉɛt sayri, mǎnkɛm bǒnkwɔ Mandɛm ankɛm nkwɔ sayri. Bǎkɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk bɛ Mandɛm asɔt manoŋ Mɔ́ywi akʉ bɔ mámbák bǒbhi. Nɛ ɛ̌ti yap kɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ákʉ́ mǎmbak bǒ batí bhap.
Kɛ nywɔp ɛnɛn Yesu Acha ápɛ̀tnsɛm nɛ́twɔ chɔŋ mbɔ ngɛ́p. Mpok yɔ, chɔŋ nɛbu nɛ́ngwat wɔ́ɔ́ɔ́ nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ, nɛ́nɛ́msi. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛchi amfay ɛ́nsayri amɛm ngó, ɛnɛmsi. Nɛ mmɨk ansɔŋɔ nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi arɛ́.
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Dɔ̌ yí! Ɛ́rɨ yi ambʉrɛ bawɛt amɛn bɛ ámbák ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɛn bábhɛmɛ mɛ.
Nchyɛ́ bhɔ́ nkúbhɛ́ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn ɔ́chyɛ́ mɛ, bɛ́ bɔ́ mámbák mmu amɔt, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ wɔ nɛ mɛ sɛchi.
Bɛdiɛrɛ́ bɛ́kʉ̀ bo mǎmbɔŋ ɛrɨ́tí ɛpɨŋ, mámbak chak, nɛ mámbak bo abhɛn bachi tɛtɛp.
Árɨ́ŋɨ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́fákárí ntá yi, afʉɛ́t arɔk ɛkɛrɛ́ Maria, nnɔ Jɔ̌n Mák. Bɛyǎ bo báchɛmti nyaka arɛ mánɨk nɔkɔ mmʉɛt.
Tɛ́mté wu, afaté achɔkɔ chɔ́kɔ́, abho bɛrɛm kɛpɨ. Yesu asɔt yi achyɛ ntá máyi.
Kɛ Yesu asɛmti bhɔ́ bɛ́, “Bǎkɛ́ ghati yɛ̌ mmu ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fákárí.” Achyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ mánchyɛ́ Tabíta nɛnyíɛ́ ányíɛ́.
Ɛbhɔŋ bɛbhak nɔ mbɔnyunɛ puyɛ̌ ngɔrɛ́ kɛ̌ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ mmʉɛt ɛyi, chí nnɛ́m. Nɛ puyɛ̌ nnɛ́m kɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ mmʉɛt ɛyi, chí ngɔrɛ́.
Mbák yɛ batɨ yɛka ankɛm ajwi nɛ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́, nɛ yɛ̌ mandú ɛjuri apu arɛ, chɔŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛka nɛnkɛm nɛmbak pɛ́pɛ́p, mbɔ mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ ɛ́ghɔ̀, ɛntɔŋ nɔkɔ yi mbi.” 
Batɛmɛ́ nɛnu Páílet básɔ́t Yesu bárɔ́k amɛm áchá ywi nɛ yí, batɛmɛ́ nɛnu báchák mankɛm ndǔ ɛká batɛmɛ́ nɛnu ɛyap bátwɔ́ nkwɔ́ bákáp Yesu.
Kɛ abhɛ́nɛ́fú báré rɛm bɛ, “Dɔ̌ yi sɛ́ngɔ́ mbák Ɛláija ǎtwɔ̀ bɛpɛmɛ yi!”
Mankɛm bátɨknsɛm ntá Mandɛm, bɔ mankɛm barɔp bǒ bɛkwɛnɛ, yɛ̌ amɔt apú kʉ bɛrɨ, wáwák! Yɛ̌ amɔt apu.”
Arɔk ntá mmu anɛ áchí ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ asɔt ɛkáti nɛ́nɛ́p ɛyɔ nɔ́ ɛchi ndǔ awɔ́nɛm ayi.
Ɛchi ɛnyu ɛyɔ bɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́ghàti bhɛsɛ ɛmfu tɛtɛp, nɔ chi bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ ‘Bápap mɛ ntí tí.’
Mpok anɛ bo bárɛ̀m bɛ, “Mbǎŋ achi kpák, yɛ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛ́pu.” Mpok ɛyɔ kɛ̌ ɛrɛ̌m ɛsɔŋɔri ɛ́kwɛn bɔ amʉɛt tɛ́mchok mbɔ bɛbe ngɔrɛ́ anɛ ánòŋsi. Nɛ mbi bɛ́bʉ́ɛ kɛbhák.
Ɔ́kɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk bɛ Mandɛm arɛm nyaka bɛ ɛtayɛsɛ Ábraham achi chak bɛsí bhi ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ákʉ́. Nɔ́ chí ndǔ ásɔ́rɛ́ mɔ́ywi Áisek arɔk bɛchyɛ mbɔ akap ndǔ mpok anɛ Mandɛm aghati yi ánkʉ ɛnyuyɔ.
Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ Mandɛm árɛm nyaka ntá Mfɔ Íjip bɛ, “Nkʉ wɔ ɔ́mbák Mfɔ bɛ ntɔ́ŋ bɛtaŋ ɛbha wɔ amʉɛt ɛnyu ɛnɛ mmɨk nkɛm ághok chɔŋ ɛ̌ti ya.”
Mbák chí nnya anɛ achi nyaka nɛpɛ́m kɛ apɛt apú, yɔ́ achi mfɔ anɛ ajwí mánɛn. Achí nyaka amɔt ndǔ abhɛn tándrámɔt. Chɔŋ mángwáy yɔ ndak amay.
Mpu rɛm nɔ chí bɛ bǎbhɔŋ bɛkʉ mbɔ ɛnyǔ ngátí bhe. Nchí kʉ chi bɛ mǎndɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛnyǔ bǒ báchák bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛkɔŋ ndu bɛ́kwák. Nkʉ chi bɛ mǎmbɔ́ŋ mbi bɛtɔŋ bɛ bǎkɔŋ bo bachak tɛtɛp.
“Chɔŋ yi ambak ɛrɛmɛ́mu nɛ chɔŋ nnyɛ́n ɛni nɛmbak bɛ Mmɔ Mandɛm Acha. Chɔŋ Ɛta Mandɛm anchyɛ yí ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ ɛnɛ́ Debhít mmu yi achi ɛbhárɛ́mɔ ywi.
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Mmu anɛ ákɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛ, ǎbhʉ̀rɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛya. Ɛtaya ǎkɔ̀ŋ yi. Nɛ mɛ, nɛ Ɛtaya sɛ́ntwɔ sɛnchɔkɔ nɛ yi.
Mbɔk bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bátwɔ́ mɛmɔ yi. Bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ɛbhé yɛsɛ ɛ́ká bɛ mmu ándɔ́ ngɔrɛ́ ywi ndǔ nɛbhay?”
Páílet ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́ yí ǎchɔŋti chí mpok nɛ bɛ́ ɛbyɔk ɛ́bho bɛ́kwɛ́n, arɛm mántwɔ́ yí nɛ manyiɛp ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ. Asɔt manyiɛp amɔ aso amɔ amɛm bɛsí bɛyǎ bǒbhɔ andɛm nɔkɔ bɛ, “Mɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ amɔ ndǔ nɛwú mmu nɛ. Nɛwú ɛni nɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ́ chí bhé!”
“Mfɔ Agripa, ndǔ Yesu áfú amfay atwɔ ntá ya ndu kɛnɔ́ amɨ́k antifú, mbɔ̌ŋ yɛ nyaka bɛ́kóŋo ɛyɔŋ ɛyi.
Abhɛn ɛchɨŋti bápɔ́kɔ bɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ bhap, kɛ bɔ́ kɛpɔkɔ bawɛt mánkɛ́m amʉɛt.
Nnɛ́m abhɔŋ bɛ́chyɛ mmʉɛt nta ngɔrɛ́ ywi, nɛ ngɔrɛ́ abhɔŋ bɛchyɛ mmʉɛt nta nnɛ́m, mbɔ ɛnyu ɛ́yàŋ.
Bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Wɔ nkwɔ́ ɔchí mmǔ Gálili? Yɨŋɨ́ Ɛkáti Mandɛm, chɔŋ ɔ́ngɔ́ bɛ́ yɛ̌ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ amɔt apú kway bɛfu atú Gálili.” Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu árɔ́ yɛ, agurɛ ɛkɛt ɛyi.
Yesu asáy ɛfóŋó yɔ bɛ, “Kusí! Fú yi amʉɛt!” Ɛfóŋó yɔ ɛ́gʉɛp mmǔ wu amɨk bɛsí bhap. Kɛ ɛ́fú yi amʉɛt kɛkʉ yi yɛ̌nyɨŋ.
Mɛ̌nɨ̀kmʉɛt ntá yɛka bɛ́ mǎnkóŋó ɛpɨŋ ɛyá mbɔ ɛnyǔ mmɔ́ ákòŋo ɛpɨŋɨ́ ɛ́táyi.
‘Mfay chí ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ ɛya, nɛ mmɨk chi ɛrwɔ ɛnɛ mɛ́sɨ̀kɨ bɛkak arɛ. Ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ ɛkɛt ɔ́kway bɛte ntá ya? nɛbhʉɛ́t anɛ mɛ̌kwáy bɛywemʉɛt achí nɛ fá?
Bárɛ̀m nyaka ɛnyuyɔ mbɔnyunɛ mǎnáŋ nyaka bághɔ̌ Pɔ̌l nɛ Trofimɔs mmu Ɛ́fɛsɔs, amɛm ɛtɔk. Ɛkʉ basɔt bɛ Pɔ̌l achwe amɛm ɛkɛrákap nɛ yi.
Kɛ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ yi? Ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Bók ngɔrɛ́ anɛ achi nsɛm nɛ mɔ́ywi, mbɔnyunɛ mmɔ̌ nsɛm ápú kwáy mɛnyiɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛ́táyi nɛ mmɔ̌ ngɔrɛ́ anɛ ápú nsɛm.”
Báre yaŋ bɛkɛm yi, kɛ báchày nyaka bɛyǎ bo abhɛn báchi arɛ, mbɔnyunɛ bárɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka bɛ bǒbhɔ básɔt Yesu mbɔ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm.
Ɛ́bhɨ́kí tat, Yesu afú atú Gálili arɔk ndǔ Nnyɛ́n Jɔ́dan bɛ Jɔ̌n anjwiti yi.
Nɛ chɔŋ nchyɛ́ wɔ bɛtaŋ amɛm Kɛfɔ Mandɛm. Nɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɔ́gwɔ́rɛ́ fá amɨk, chɔŋ Mandɛm angwɔt yɔ awu amfay. Ɛnɛ́ ɔ́káŋárí, Mandɛm ǎkaŋari awu amfay.”
Yesu achyɛ bhɔ mbi. Bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bhɔ bɛ́fú mmǔ wu amʉɛt, bɛrɔk bɛchwe ndǔ nkwɔ́ bakók. Nkwɔ́ bakók ankɛm abhak mbɔ nká ɛpay. Bárókóri básɛp ndǔ nkókónjiɛ dúgúdúgúdúgú kpát bágúrɛ anyɛ́n.
Bákway mbʉ bɛti mɔ ndǔ bɛyǎ nkáp, mánsɔt nkáp wu mánchyɛ ntá bachɛ́bhɛ́bho”.
Yesu abhɛ́p batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm nɛ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi abhɛn bachi arɛ bɛ, “Ɛbhé ɛyɛsɛ ɛ́ká bɛ mámbú mmu ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt kɛ?”
Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛ́pú kway bɛfɛrɛ bhɛsɛ ndǔ ɛkɔŋ ɛyi. Nɛwú nɛpu kway bɛkʉ nɔ. Sɛ́chí chi nɛpɛ́m, nɛ nɛpɛ́m nɛ́pú kway bɛkʉ nɔ. Bɔángɛl Mandɛm bápú kway bɛkʉ nɔ. Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ amfay bɛ́pú kway bɛkʉ nɔ. Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi nɛ́nɛ, nɛ ɛbhɛn bɛ́twɔ̀ ambɨ bɛ́pú kway bɛkʉ nɔ.
Júdas Iskariɔt, nkoŋo Yesu amɔt anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka bɛti yi arɛm bɛ,
Kɛ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, babho bɛrɛm bɛ, “Chí Bɛlsɛbul, mfɔ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ kɛ áchyɛ́ Yesu bɛtaŋ bɛ́bók bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ mɛ́mfú, mɛ́ndɔ́, bho.” Mmǔ achák apú!
Mpok anɛ Ɛlísabɛt ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́bhé ákwáy nɔkɔ, abhé mɔ́mbakanɛm.
Mpok mánaŋ bǎbhɛbhɛ mɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ nkʉ, bághɔ́ bɛ́ mbɨ́kɨ́ kʉ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́yàŋ bɛ mángwáy mɛ. Bátɨ bɛrɔ mɛ.
Mǔnti babhabhɛri ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm nɛ bǒ batí bachiǎkap baghoko nɔkɔ nɔ, batí átáka bhɔ amɛm, bare bhɛp mmʉɛt ɛyap ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛfakari nɛ bǒnto Yesu.
Pɔ̌l anyaŋa yɛ bɔ́ amɔ anti. Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ abhak nɛ bhɔ, bábho bɛrɛm bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk nyáŋá nyáŋá ɛbhɛ́n bɔ́ babhɨkɨ ghɔ́k, mándɛm nɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n Mandɛm afyɛ́ bhɔ́ antɨ.
Bǎbhɔŋ yɛ bɛte kpirí bɛ mǎnkwáy bɛkoŋo nkaysi Mandɛm, mǎmbɔŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yí afyɛ́ bariɛp bɛchyɛ be.
Bɔ̌ma, mpok ntwɔ́ awu ntá yɛka, mbɨ́kɨ́ twɔ́ bɛ́gháti bhe Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm mbɔ mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ sɛ́rwɔrɛ́nyu, nɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ twɔ́ mbɔ mmǔ anɛ achí ndɨŋɨndak.
Ntwɔ fá amɨk mbɔ ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́ yɛ̌ agha anɛ ánókó mɛ, ákɛ́ rɔp amɛm ɛjuri.
Sɛ́tárɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ Malta ndu bataŋ árát, sɛ́sɔ́t áchwí achak anɛ́ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ, Bɔmandɛm Bɛfak. Áfǔ nyaka Aleksándriya kɛ átat Malta ndu mbaŋ akwɛn tontó.
Awu áfʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, ngɔ́ bɔángɛl manwi téé ndǔ amɔ́-mmɨk anwi, mánchɛrɛ nɔkɔ babhʉ́ɛ́p anwi bɛ akɛ fok antwɔ yɛ̌ chi amɨk, nɛ yɛ̌ chi ndǔ manyu, nɛ yɛ̌ chi ndǔ mɛnɔk.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́fakari nɛ mɛnyǔ bo bhɔ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ bakay anɛ́ árɛ̀m bɛ, “Mmú ǎgwɔ ɛnyɨŋ ampɛtnsɛm anyiɛ yɔ”, nɛ bɛ, “Báso akók ampɛtsnɛm anyɔ́p mmʉɛt ndǔ batɔp”, achi tɛtɛp.
Ntɨ nywɔp, Jɔ̌n aghɔ Yesu ndu átwɔ̀ ntá yi, arɛm bɛ, “Yɨŋɨ́ Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n Mandɛm anɛ ápɔ̀kɔ bɛbʉ́ bo mankɛm fá amɨk!
Nɛ ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ́ tɛtɛp chi bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm ághátí bhɛsɛ sɛnkʉ. Ɛbhé Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ sɛ́nkɔŋ batɨ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ bǎghókó tɛ nɛbhǒnɛt.
Josɛ́f abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka nnɛm nɛkɔ ɛnɛ́n yi átɛ́mɛ́ ndǔ sɛtárɛ́bhɛ́. Arɔk abhɛmɛ Yesu ndǔ nnɛm ɛni nɔ. Abɨŋɨri yɛ ɛrɛm ntay áchók nnyǔ nnɛm, agurɛ.
Bě baghɔrɛ́ nkwɔ bǎbhɔŋ bɛsɛptimʉɛt ntá manɛ́m abhɛka. Mbák mǎnkʉ nɔ, bǎkway bɛkʉ manɛ́m abhɛka abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ noko Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm mánoko yɛ̌ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɛm chí ɛnyɨŋ ntá yap.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ́ bɛ, “Sɔt ka mpok bɛ bákɛ́ rwɔ bhe mǎnjíbhírí batɨ yɛka. Bɛyǎ bo bátwɔ̀ chɔŋ mánsɔt nnyɛ́n ɛna mántɛn ambɨ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap andɛm nɔkɔ bɛ, ‘Mɛ kɛ nchi Mpɛmɛ anɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtó!’ Nɛ bɛ, ‘Mpok akway anɛ Mandɛm ápɛ̀mɛ mmɨk!’ Mbák mǎngók nɔ́ bǎkɛ́ koŋo bhɔ́.
Ɛ́nɛ́ bákàŋari mɔ́mpɔŋɔ batu wu, bǒ abhɛn babhɔŋɔ yɔ, bábhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Ndaká yí bǎkàŋari mɔ́mpɔŋɔ batu wu?”
Ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛkʉ nɔ, akó amfǎy njiɛ aywǐntí ndu mɛnɨkmʉɛt. Bɛti bɛgʉ́ bɛ́tɛ́mɛri yi arɛ.
Bɛ́fú afɔ, Satan asɔt Yesu ndǔ njiɛ anɛ áré sáp amfay, atɔ́ŋ yi bɛtɔkɔ́ mmɨk mɛnkɛm nɛ kɛfɔ ɛkɛn kɛ́chí arɛ́.
Yesu átɛ́mɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɛkay ɛnɛn, aghati yɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Mmʉɛrɛ ywɛsɛ Lásárɔs akwɛn kɛnɔ́, kɛ nchí rɔŋ mɛ́ŋɛ́mɛ yi ndǔ kɛnɔ́.”
Ngɔrɛ́ amɔt abhak arɛ́, anɛ áfɛ̀rɛ manoŋ ndǔ mamiɛ́ byo nɛ apay. Anáŋ achɔ́ŋtí nyaka nkáp anɛ́ yí ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ankɛm kɛ yɛ̌ mmu kɛkwáy bɛbu yi.
Mmǔ anɛ ápábhɛ́ mmʉɛt yi apú. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu áyɨ̀ŋɨ mmʉɛt yi sayri ankɛ́m yɔ ɛrɨrɨ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Kristo áyɨ̀ŋɨ bǒnkwɔ,
Bɔ̌ma, dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ ngátí bhe abhɨki fu ndǔ nkaysi bakwǎŋwaŋ,
Ɛ̌ti ɛyɔ kɛ sɛ́nɨ̀k Mandɛm mmʉɛt mpoknkɛm ɛ̌ti yɛka bɛ yi ánkʉ mǎmbak bo abhɛn bákwáy bɛ́bhak bǒbhi. Sɛ́nɨ̀kmʉɛt bɛ́ yi anchyɛ bhe bɛtaŋ mǎnáŋá bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎyaŋ bɛkʉ nɛ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn bákʉ̀ ɛ̌ti nɛka ɛnɛka nɛ Yesu Kristo.
Yesu akɛmɛ Píta bɛ, “Sɛp twɔ́.” Píta afú amɛm áchwí asɛp anyɛ́n abho bɛkɔ andɔkɔ nɔkɔ bɛtɛmɛri Yesu.
Bɛsɛ́ bǒnto sɛ́chí bɛchɨŋtǐ bho ndǔ sɛ́chíɛ bapɛ́m yɛsɛ́ ntá Kristo, kɛ be bachí barɨŋɨ́ndak ndǔ babhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu. Sɛ́chí mbɔ bǒ abhɛn Mandɛm ábhɨ́kɨ́ chyɛ bhɔ́ bɛtaŋ, kɛ be bǎbhɔŋ bɛtaŋ. Bo báchyɛ̀ be kɛnókó, kɛ báwày bhɛsɛ́ wáy.
Ndu ɛchi nɔ, dɔ́k ká ambɨ bɛte kpɨrí. Tɛtɛp anɛ bǎrɨ́ŋɨ́ ámbák mbɔ mgbat anɛ ákɛ̀m mɛnyɨŋí nɛnu ɛbhɛka. Kʉ nɔ́kɔ́ ká chi ndiɛrɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi chak mbɔnyunɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ bɛchi mbɔ nkú bɛsé anɛ ntɛmɛ́ nɛnu afyɛ́ ndu bɛkuti mbeápak ɛyi.
Ɛchi mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Mmu Mandɛm achi awɔ́ fúú. Ǎchyɛ bo abhɛn ɛyap ɛpu kɛyɨŋɨ nsɛm. Bɛrɨ́tí bɛtɨk ɛbhi bɛ́pú nɛm.”
Bǒnkwɔ mankɛm abhɛn báchí fá bátò nkwɔ bhe bakak.
Sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ nyiɛ nyaka nɛnyíɛ́ mmu ywɛka kɛchyɛ nkáp. Kɛ sɛ́kʉ̀ nyaka bɛtɨk bɛti nɛ ngósí, sɛ́mkpɔt nɔkɔ nsɔ́ŋti bɛ́ sɛ́kɛ́ chyɛ bhe ɛsɔŋɔri.
arɛm bɛ, “Wɔ mmɔ̌ Satan! Wɔ mmu ɔ́pábhɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi chak bɛsí Mandɛm. Wɔ mmu bapu ájwí wɔ́ mɛniɛ. Ɔpú rɔ bɛkʉ mbi Mandɛm anɛ achí chak ambak ŋɔ́tíŋɔ́tí?”
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Nchí ghati bhe bɛ, bápú ka ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ amɛm ɛtɔk yi.
Yesu arɛm yɛ bɛ, “Pú bǒ bati byo kɛ mbúú? Abhɛ́nɛ́fú bati nɛ́nɛ́namɔt báchí fá?
Bɛrɨ̌ndu Yesu Kristo Acha mɛ́mbak nɛ bhe.
Mǔfu anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ Jáyrɔs arɔk ntá Yesu. Achí nyaka mǔnti ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí bo Israɛl ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ yi achí arɛ. Akwɛ́n Yesu bɛkak anɨkmʉɛt bɛ Yesu andɔk ɛkɛt ɛyi.
Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi báré kɔ mámfʉɛt nɔkɔ amɛm nkɨ̌ nchwifú ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt bo Israɛl. Baghɔkɔ́ bhi bábho bɛkʉɛp ɛnyǔ nchwi yɔ, mámfɨkɨri mányiɛ nɔkɔ.
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Ntwɔ fá amɨk bɛ mámkpɔ́t manyé bho. Ntwɔ bɛ́ bo abhɛn bachi amɨ́k nɛ́mɛ́nɛ́mɛ́ mangɔ mbaŋ, nɛ bɛ́ amɨ́k ánɛ́mɛ́ abhɛn bághɔ̀ mbaŋ.”
Nɛka Moses nɛ Mandɛm kɛ̌ nɛ́kʉ́ yi ághátí bo Israɛl bɛ mámbʉ́rɛ́ Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ. Arɛm bɛ bɔ mámyákátì manoŋ mɔ́mɛn amfay ndǔ bɛchɨ́kɨ́ mfay ɛbhɛn babhǐnywɔp ayap, bɛ ángɛl Mandɛm anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka bɛway yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mɔ̌mbɨ bo Íjip, ánáŋ ángáká ndǔ ɛkɛt ɛnɛ́ mmu Israɛl, ankɨŋɨ, kɛtɔk yɛ̌ mmɔ́ wap.
Bakoŋo Yesu báchák kɛrɨŋɨ ntí anɛ Yesu árɛ́mɛ́ nɔ ntá Júdas.
Apú fá. Mandɛm akʉ yi apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi árɛ́mɛ́ nyaka bɛ ɛbhɔŋ bɛfakari. Twɔ́ ká ghɔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bábhʉ́rɛ́ yi. Tɨ́k ka ndǔ yi ágháti bhe mpok ábhʉɛ́t atú Gálili nɛ bhe.
“Yɛ̌ mmu apú durɛ ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ ansɔt ɛnyɨŋ ankuti. Bádʉrɛ ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́, mánte chi ɛbhak ɛnɛ babhɔŋɔ bɛte yɔ bɛ mbaŋ angɔ́ɔ́ ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ achwe anywɔ́p.
Ndu ákʉ̀ nɔ, are rɛm bɛ, “Manoŋ amɛn ákɛm nku anɛ Mandɛm anyu nɛ bhe nɛ ǎghati bhe bɛ mǎmbʉ́rɛ́ yɔ.”
Nɛ nnáŋ, ndɔ́k, ngókó ɛbhak mbʉrɛ́, ntá yɛka chɔŋ mpɛtnsɛm, nsɔt be, bɛ́ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ nchí, bě nkwɔ mambák arɛ.
Ngɔ́ Yerúsalɛm nkɔ, ɛtɔk Mandɛm, ndu ɛ́fú amfay ntá yi ɛ́twɔ̀ amɨk. Bághóko yɔ ɛ́rɨ́ mbɔ ngɔsɔ́ŋ anɛ basɔbhɛri, achɔkɔ anoŋ nɔkɔ mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛbhay yi.
Ntɨ nkʉbɛtɨk wu akwɛ́n yi bɛkak abho mɛnɨkmʉɛt bɛ, ‘Chiɛ́ mɛ́ mpok, chɔŋ nchyɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ̌kɛ̀m wɔ.’
Aghati mɛ bɛ, “Ndak ámay! Mmɛ kɛ̌ nchí Alfa nɛ Ɔmɛga, Mmɛ kɛ nchí kʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mbɔ́ŋ nɛbhǒnɛt nɛ ngwɛnti. Ntá mmu anɛ manyiɛp ákwak, mɛ̌chyɛ manyiɛp ndɛ́ndɛm. Manyiɛp mɔ ǎnyay ndǔ mbokó manyiɛp amɛn áchyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m.
Aghók bɛ́ chí ɛyɔŋ Píta. Nɛ bɛyǎ maŋák, arɔ mbǐnyɔ́p kɛnɛnɛ apɛtnsɛm aghati bǒ mankɛm bɛ́, “Píta achí ambǐnywɔp téé!”
“Ndak yí bě babhɔŋ bapú kway bɛrɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi chak bɛ mmu ankʉ?
Mbɨ́kɨ́ ghɔkɔntɨk babhɛsɛ mɛ nɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ mbɔŋ ɛkwak bɛti nɛ ngósí bɛ́ghɔ wɔ bɛ́ maŋák ánjwí mɛ antɨ.
Mbɔ mǎnókó ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Moses ásɨ́ŋɨ́ tɛtɛp, mbʉ́ mǎnókó ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ̌ghàti bhe. Moses asɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka chí ɛ̌ti ya.
Mandɛm ato bhe batɔŋ mbɔ mɛ Pɔ̌l, nɛ Apólos nɛ Píta bɛ́ sɛ́nkwák bhe. Mandɛm aghókó mmɨk bɛ ánkwák bhe. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́fàkari nɛ bhe ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn, nɛ yɛ̌ chi ndǔ mpok anɛ mmu ágú ɛ́kwàk be. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛchi nɛ́nɛ nɛ yɛ̌ chi ɛnɛ ɛ́twɔ̀ ambɨ ɛ̌twɔ́ be chi nɛ bɛrɨ. Mɛnkɛm chi ɛbhɛka.
Kɛ Yesu akɛrɛm yɛ̌nyɨŋ. Ɛ́kʉ́ gɔbhánɔ abhak maknkay tontó. 
Yesu asɔt yɛ bhɔ́ amɔt amɔt, nɛ yɛntɨkɨ anɛ yi ásɔ́rɛ́ ambat amʉɛt, anyaŋa yi awɔ anti, anjɛt yi. 
Kɛ bɔ́ kɛbhɔ́ŋ mbi anɛ báfʉɛt manchwe amɛm ɛ̌ti bɛyǎ bó. Bákó amfǎy ɛkɛt, manɛnɛ mbok arɛ́, basɛbhɛ yi bhʉrɛ ndǔ bɛkpaka bhi, nɛ́ntɨ́ bhó, bɛsí Yesu.
Mɔ́ngɔrɛ́ wu arɛm bɛ, “Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò, yi mmu bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ Kristo átwɔ̀. Ánáŋ ántwɔ́, chɔŋ angati bhɛsɛ barak ankɛm.”
Achák arɛm bɛ, ‘Nku mpɔŋ byó ɛnɛ ɛ́kwàŋ bakɨ. Nchí yaŋ ndɔ́k ngɔ́ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn yɔ ɛ́kwày bɛkʉ. Nɨkmʉɛ́t. Ghatí Ɛtayɛ bɛ́ ákɛ́ bentɨ.’
Jɔ̌n anáŋ ayambɨ aghátí nyaka bo Israɛl mankɛm bɛ mántɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhap mámpɛtnsɛm ntá Mandɛm bɛ yi anjwiti bhɔ́, kɛ Yesu antwɔ.
mbɔnyunɛ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm nɛ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt bɛ́kʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛmbak nyáŋá bɛsí Mandɛm. 
Nɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ̀ sɛ́ndɨŋɨ bɛ sɛrɔp chi bo abhɛn bárɨŋɨ Mandɛm chi nɛkʉ anɛ sɛ́kʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi áyàŋ sɛ́nkʉ́.
Dɨŋɨ́ bɛ awɔ Mandɛm ákwɛn wɔ amʉɛt nɛ́nɛ. Nɛ chɔŋ amɨ́k ánɛmɛ wɔ, ɔ́kɛ́pɛrɛ kwáy bɛghɔ mbaŋ ndǔ mbɨŋɨ́ mpok. Tɛ́mté wu, nɛbháŋ nɛ́kúti yi amɨ́k ɛjuri ɛ́kwɛ́n yi bɛsí arɔbhɛ nɛmɛri nɛ́mɛ́ri ambɛbhɛ nɔkɔ mbák mmu achí anɛ ákway bɛkɛm yi awɔ ánjá yi mbi.
Bápɛ́rɛ ghɔ, mbɛ́ntí wu afáté kpɛrɛp, apɔkɔ bɛkpaka bhi, afa amɨk. Bɔ́ mankɛm bábhak maknkay tontó bábho bɛbɨti Mandɛm mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ re ghɔ ɛnɛ́ ɛnyu!” 
Kɛ Yesu ayibhiri mmʉɛt ayɨŋɨ Píta, arɛm bɛ, “Satan, fá mɛ́ bɛsí! Ɔchí ɛrɛm ntá, ntá ya. Nkaysi yɛ chí nkaysi nkwǎŋwaŋ, abhɨ́kɨ́ fu ntá Mandɛm!” 
Mandu mpok, chɔŋ Mandɛm mmu áchyɛ̀ kpák anchyɛ bhe awɔ́nɛm amfay Satan mpok bǎyátí yi amɨk. Nchí nɨkmʉɛt bɛ bɛrɨ̌ndu Yesu Kristo Acha mɛ́mbak nɛ bhe.
Sɛ́ghɔ bɛ́ mmǔ-nɛ chí nchyɛ ɛsɔŋɔri anɛ tɔ́ŋ sɛ́ngɔ́ nɛ nyɔŋ-ndak ndǔ nkwɔ bo Israɛl mbaŋ ɛnkɛm. Achí nkwɔ́ mǔnti ndǔ ɛká bho abhɛn bábhɨŋɨ bɛ bo Násárɛt.
Ghók yɛ́ ka, nchí to be baghatǐ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ áchí ndɨŋɨndak ndu ákòŋo Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm. Chɔŋ ntó be bátɔ̀ŋ-Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm nkwɔ́. Chɔŋ mǎngwáy mbɔk ɛyap, mǎngo báchák ndǔ bɛkotakati, nɛ mǎndɛn abhɛ́nɛ́fú nɛ bɛkpa amɛm bɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt ɛbhɛka, mǎnkoŋo nɔkɔ bɔ́ bɛtɔk nɛ bɛtɔk ndu bɛkɛm bhɔ bɛway.
Aghati yɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Dɔ́k ká Bɛ́tlɛhɛm, mǎmbɛp sayri nɛbhʉɛt anɛ mɔ́wu achi. Mǎnáŋ mǎngɔ́ yi, pɛt ká nsɛm mǎngati mɛ, bɛ́ mɛ nkwɔ́ ndɔ́k nchyɛ́ yi kɛnókó.”
Ndiɛrɛ Lukas kɛ áchi nɛ mɛ. Mpok ɔ́yaŋ bɛ́twɔ, sɔt Mák twɔ́ nɛ yi mbɔnyunɛ ǎkwak chɔŋ mɛ fá.
María arɛm bɛ, “Mɛnchí chí mǔbɛtok Mandɛm, ɛ́mfákárí nɛ mɛ mbɔ ɛnyu ɔ́rɛ́mɛ́.” Ángɛl arɔ yɛ yi arɔk. 
Nɛ ndǔ kɛnɔ́ amɨ́k ántí fúú, aghɔ́ mmu anɛ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ́ Ananías, ndu áchwé anywɔ́p. Anyaŋa amɔ anti ywi bɛ́ ámpɛt ankway bɛghɔ mbaŋ.”
“Ɛwak ɛ́mɔ́t, nde rɔ́ŋ Damáskɔs nɛ bɛkáti ɛbhɛ́n nsɔ́rɛ́ nta bǒ batí bachiǎkap bɛchyɛ mɛ bɛtaŋ bɛ ndɔ́k nkɛ́mtí bhɔ.
Mbák mbɨ́kɨ́ wakari bɛ́twɔ, ɔ̌kwáy bɛ́rɨŋɨ ɛnyǔ bǒ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛbhak ndu nnɛrɛ́kɛt Mandɛm, nɔ chí Nkwɔ Yesu. Mandɛm ywɛsɛ́ achí nɛpɛ́m, nɛ Nkwɔ Yesu bachi mbɔ bɛkwap ɛbhɛn bɛ́kɛ̀m nɛtɔŋ ɛnɛn tɛtɛp.
Mbɔŋɔ́kɛt ánáŋ chɔŋ amfate antiɛp mbǐnywɔp, bǎte nɛfí mǎndɛp nɔkɔ nɛkok nɛ mǎnɨk nɔkɔ mmʉɛt bɛ, ‘Acha, nɛnɛ́ bhɛsɛ mbǐnywɔp.’ Kɛ mbɔŋɔ́kɛt ankɛmɛ chí bɛ, ‘Mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bhe nɛ yɛ̌ chí ɛbhak ɛnɛ bǎfú.’
Tɛ́mté wu Sakaría apɛt abho bɛrɛm kɛpɨ ankaka nɔkɔ Mandɛm.
Ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ yɔ ɛ́ghɔ̀ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ ɛjuri ɛchi, nɛ ɛjuri ɛ́pú kway mɛnɛmɛ yɔ.
Bě bo bǎrɛ̀m bɛ, “Mmu abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛkwɛn bɛrwɔp,” Bě babhɔŋ bǎpú kwɛn bɛrwɔbhɛ? Bě bo bǎre pap baraká bɔmandɛm nsé, bǎpú ghɛp mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi amɛm bɛkɛrɛ́ bɔmandɛm nsé?
Yɛ̌ mmu, Ɛta apu taŋ manyé yi. Áchyɛ́ bɛtaŋ mɛnkɛm ntá ya, Mmɛ Mɔ́ywi, bɛ ntáŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu.
Pɔ̌l atɛp bɔ́ amɨ́k amʉɛt arɛm bɛ, “Bɔ̌ma, mpoknkɛm anɛ nchí bɛsí Mandɛm nɛ kpatɛ̌ ɛchɔŋ ntɨ ɛna nɛchi amɛm pɛ́pɛ́p.”
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛtɔk ɛnɛ́ bǎchuɔ́bhɛ́ arɛ́, yáŋ ká ɛsáyrí mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛkɔŋ bɛsyɛpti bhe ɛkɛt ɛyi, mǎnchɔkɔ nɛ yi kpátɛ mpok anɛ bǎrɔ ɛtɔk ɛyɔ.
Kɛ bǎghàti bho bɛ, ‘Mbák mmu ándɛ́m ntá ɛtayi, yɛ̌ máyi bɛ, “Nsɔt ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ mbʉ́ bɛkwak wɔ nɛ yɔ, nchyɛ́ ntá Mandɛm”, nɛ bɛ́ yi abhɨkɨ bhɔŋ bɛchyɛ máyi, yɛ̌ ɛtayi kɛnókó,’
Arɛ́ sɛ́ghɔ́ áchwi áchák anɛ́ árɔ̀ŋ atú Foníshia. Sɛ́chwé sɛ́ré rɔ́ŋ.
Bě manɛ́mámɨk! Bɛsí Mandɛm, ɛ́fɛ́mɛ́ akap Mandɛm kɛ̌ ɛcha mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bábhʉrɛ arɛ́ ndu bɛchyɛ akap, kɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ kɛ bɛcha ɛ́fɛ́mɛ́ akap Mandɛm? Pú ɛ́fɛ́mɛ́ yɔ kɛ̌ ɛ́kʉ̀ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bábhʉ́rɛ́ arɛ ɛmbak nyáŋá?
Kɛ be, puyɛ̌ ɛnyǔ ɛyɔ kɛ bátɔ́ŋ bhe ɛ̌ti Kristo.
Ntǐ ɛna nɛ́jwi yɛ nɛ maŋák, nɛ nchí rɛm kɛpɨ nɛ maŋák. Nɛ mbákántɨ chí nɛ Mandɛm,
Mmu anɛ ápɨ̀ mbwɔ́t nɛ mmu anɛ ámyàkati manyiɛp arɛ́ bápú yɛ̌nyɨŋ, Mandɛm mmu ákʉ̀ mbwɔ́t ángó kɛ̌ ákʉ̀ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ.
Ɛ́fákárí nyaka ɛnyu yɔ mbɔnyunɛ bǒnkwɔ Sádusi bárɛ̀m bɛ bawú bápú kway bɛpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, nɛ bɛ bɔángɛl bápú, nɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛpu ɛnɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ bɛfoŋɔ. Kɛ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi mánoko bɛ chɔŋ bawú mámpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, nɛ bɛ bɔángɛl bachi nɛ bɛfóŋó nkwɔ bɛchi.
Mbákántɨ nɛ Mandɛm ɛnyumɔ́t mbɔ bhɔ́, bɛ́ ɛwak ɛ́mɔt chɔŋ yí ankʉ bawú mankɛm abhɛn báchí chak bɛsí bhi nɛ abhɛn bapu mámpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.
Mbɔ bo abhɛn Jóshua ásɔ́rɛ́ achwe ɛtɔk Kánǎn nɛ bhɔ bábhɔ̌ŋ nyaka nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt tɛtɛp, mbʉ Mandɛm abhɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ rɛm ɛ̌ti mpok nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt achak.
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Nɛ́nɛ, ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ ntí anɛ mɛ̌kʉ̀ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ̌kʉ̀, kɛ ansɛmpok chɔŋ ɔ́njwimɛm.”
Bě bǒ bɛtábhá! Ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Aisáya arɛm nyaka ndak aywi tɛtɛp ɛ̌ti yɛka! Aghátí nyaka bho bɛ Mandɛm arɛm bɛ,
Kɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎbhɔŋɔ bɛkʉ chi bɛsɔt mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi amɛm bɛkpʉrɛ ɛbhɛka mánchyɛ ntá bachɛ́bhɛ́bho nɛ chɔŋ bɛpɨŋ ɛbhɛka mɛnkɛm mɛ́mbak nkwɔ pɛ́pɛ́p.
Nɛ sɛ́kɛ́ bhak bǒ ɛnywíntí mbɔ ɛnyǔ mbɔk ɛyap báchí nyaka, ɛ́kʉ́ ángɛl nɛwú anaŋa bho.
Kɛ bɛ́bhó ɛchɔŋ, chɔŋ Mandɛm Bɛtaŋ Mɛnkɛm amfyɛ́ Mɛ Mmu mfú amfay nchɔkɔ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt bɛyǎ kɛnókó, ɛbhě awɔ́nɛm ɛyi.”
Tɛ̌ndu bǎchi bo abhɛn bǎghòk Mandɛm, bǎkɛ́ yibhiri mmʉɛt mǎnkóŋó bɛpɔ̌ bɛpɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka mpok bǎbhʉɛ́t amɛm ɛjuri.
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu áyɨ̀ŋɨ, aghɔ́ ndǔ bǒ abhɛn mánáká ndǔ ɛpa báre yap bɛbhaká kɛnókó. Achyɛ bhɔ maniɛ bɛ,
Yesu ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ ngɛ́mtay bho bátwɔ̀ ntá yi, aghɔ́ bhɔ ntínso mbɔnyunɛ báchi ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri, kɛbhɔ́ŋ nkwak, mbɔ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ mbabhɛri.
Ngɔrɛ́ wu asɔbhɛri mmʉɛt nɛ ndɛn ɛnɛ ɛchi chuu, ɛnyǔ ndɛn ɛnɛ bafɔ báfyɛ, nɛ mɛnyɨŋ pú, nɛ mɛnyɨŋ nkáp, nɛ mɛnyɨŋ bɛfyɛ ɛmɨ ɛbhɛn bághókó nɛ bɔ̌batay bɛyǎ nkáp abhɛn bábhɨŋɨ bɛ pɛ́l.
Mpok mánáká wɔ ndǔ ɛpa, yap chi ɛnɔk ɛnɛ ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ yɛ̌ kɛnókó, bɛ mmu anɛ ánáká ɛpa ántwɔ́, ankwáy bɛrɛm ntá yɛ bɛ, ‘Nkwǎnɛ, twɔ́ chɔkɔ ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛnókó.’ Bǒ ɛpa bachak mángɔ bɛ mmu anɛ ánáká ɛpa ǎchyɛ̀ wɔ kɛnókó.
“Mɛ kɛ nchí ɛrɨ́tí mbabhɛri bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n. Ɛrɨ́tí mbabhɛri bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n ǎchyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m ɛni ɛ̌ti bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n ayi.
Mbák chi bhe, bǎbhʉ́rɛ́ ɛyɔŋ ɛya, bǎrɔ́k ambɨ bɛte kpirí ndǔ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ. Ɛ̌ti yɔ, chɔŋ mbak nɛ bhe bɛ bǎkɛ́ chwe ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ́ ɛ́twɔ̀ mɛmɔ bo abhɛn báchi fá amɨk mankɛm.
Páílet aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Sɔt ka yi bɛ bě babhɔŋ mǎntáŋ manyé yi bɛ́kóŋo ɛbhé ɛyɛka.” Bákɛ́mɛ Páílet bɛ, “Ɛbhé ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ chyɛ bhɛsɛ bɛtaŋ bɛ́táŋ manyé mmu, kpát sɛ́nchyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ mangway yi.”
Sǒ yɛ́ ka amɔ́ mǎmfɛ́rɛ́ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́yɨ̀ŋɨ nɛpɛ́m nɛsɨ́ ɛnɛka. Nɔ chi ɛpúsí, nɛ yɛ̌ chí bɛpɔ̌ baraká kɛbhʉrɛ, nɛ mɛ́ŋwáka ndǔ baraká kɛbhʉrɛ, nɛ nkaysi bɛkʉ bɛbʉ́, nɛ yɛ̌chi bɛfyɛ amɨ́k ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ bo bachak mbɔnyunɛ bɛfyɛ amɨ́k ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ chi bɛsɔt bhɔ mbɔ bɔmandɛm mmɨk.
Bák ká maŋák mpoknkɛm bɛ bǎchí bǒ Yesu Acha. Mbʉɛ́t bɛ́sɛ́mti bhe, bák ká maŋák mpoknkɛm.
Píta ataŋa, arɛm bɛ, “Mma, mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ yi.”
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛká ándɔ́p ɛnyǔ yí áchí nyaka mpok Mandɛm ábhɨ́ŋɨ́ yí ámbák nkoŋo Yesu.
Yesu ághók ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bárɛ̀m, akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Bo abhɛn bapu me, bápú yaŋ ngaŋ. Bǒ mame kɛ báyàŋ ngaŋ. Mbɨ́kɨ́ twɔ bɛbhɨŋɨ bǒ abhɛn bákáysí bɛ bachi chak bɛsí Mandɛm bɛ mámbák bakoŋo bha, ntwɔ bɛbhɨŋɨ chi bǒ bɛbʉ́.” 
Ábraham akɔrɛ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn yi áfú ɛbhɨ̌nɛnu nɛ bhɔ ndu baru byo, achyɛ yi ndu amɔt. Nnyɛ́n Mɛlkísɛdɛk ɛnɔ nɛ́te ndǔ “Mfɔ anɛ ákʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi chak.” Achi nkwɔ Mfɔ Salɛm, nɔ chi “Mfɔ anɛ áchyɛ kpák.”
Nchí chyɛ nyaka nɛnyok ntá bo abhɛn bákòŋo Mbi Yesu wu kpát mbɔk mángu nɔkɔ, nɛ ńkɛ́mti nɔkɔ baghɔrɛ́ nɛ babhakanɛm mámfyɛ nɔkɔ bhɔ́ ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ.
Ndu sɛbharɛ mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Kristo Acha, dɨŋɨ́ ká sayri bɛ bǎbhɔŋ bɛkoŋo chí nkaysi aya, puyɛ̌ achak. Mmu anɛ afyɛ́ be ɛbyɔk antɨ, ntɛmsi Mandɛm ǎbhák nɛ yi, yɛ yi achi agha!
Mbák mmu ámbɛ́p nɔ́, nɔ achí ɛchɨŋtɨ́mu! Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛ, mmu ámpɨ́ mbwɔt, mbák yɔ abhɨ́kɨ́ yambɨ angu, apú chak ángó?
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́pɛt ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Kɛ́mɔ Mandɛm Acha ywɛ.’”
“Bɔta, ngɔ bɛ́ mbák sɛ́ndɔ́k ambɨ nɛ nɛkɔ ɛnɛn chɔŋ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛ́mfú, bɛyǎ mɛ́nɛ́mɛ́ mɛ́mbak, puyɛ́ ndiɛrɛ nɛ áchwí nɛ batu, kɛ nɛ bapɛ́m ayɛsɛ nkwɔ.”
Puyɛ̌ ntá bɔángɛl kɛ Mandɛm áchyɛ́ bɛtaŋ amfay mmɨk anɛ sɛ́rɛ̀m nɛ́ bɛ ǎtwɔ̀ ansɛm.
Mpok sɛ́chwɔ́bhɛ́ Yerúsalɛm batɨ bǒnkwɔ abhɛn bachi árɛ́ básɔ́t bhɛsɛ nɛ maŋák.
Kɛ mbák mmɨk ǎgò chi bɔ̌mɛnɔk nɛ tákɔ nsěnse, nɔ yɔ abhɨ́kɨ́ rɨ́, ǎrɔp chi mmɨk anɛ báchɔ̀ŋti chɔŋti, nɛ ndu ngwɛnti, mánsɔŋ yɔ sɔŋ.
Kɛ yí abhɔŋ bɛyambɨ angɔ́ bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri nɛ mkpáká bho abhɛn ɛchɔŋ mámbyak yí, kɛ antwɔ́.
Yesu arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Ɛchɔŋ, Mandɛm apɛ́mɛ́ wɔ́ nɛ ɛfo ɛyɛ ɛnkɛm mbɔnyunɛ wɔ nkwɔ́ ɔchí ɛbhárɛ́mɔ Ábraham anɛ Mandɛm ábhɔ́ŋ bɛ́pɛ́mɛ.
Mbák ákɔ́rɛ́ ánkwɛ́n ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt, bo mánu nɔkɔ nɛ batɨ, nnɛrɛ́kɛt wu ákwɛ̀n.
Mandɛm afyɛ́ yi ambak ɛnyǔ mǔngo bachiǎkap anɛ Mɛlkísɛdɛk achi nyaka. 
Bǎkɛ́ cháy bǒ abhɛn bápábhɛ́ bhe. Mánáŋ mángɔ́ bɛ bǎpú chay bhɔ bárɛ̀m bɛ, “Ɔ́e! Bácha bhɛsɛ. Mandɛm ǎtɛmsi chɔŋ bhɛsɛ.” Ɛyɔ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ Mandɛm ǎpɛmɛ chɔŋ bhe.
Mandɛm ǎkʉ̀ bo mámbák chak mpok babhɔŋɔ nɛka nɛ Yesu Kristo. Ǎkʉ̀ nɔ nɛ yɛ agha anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛka nɛ Yesu Kristo. Mandɛm apu tɔŋ kɛ́rɨ́ŋámík.
Amfǎy ntí Yesu, ndǔ ɛkotákátí, ɛbhɔk ɛnɔk ɛbhak babhát. Básɨŋ arɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́kʉ kɛ báway yi. Básɨŋ bɛ, “Mfɔ bo Israɛl.”
Mbák mmu anɨ́ŋɨ́ wɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́, chyɛ̌ yi. Nɛ mbák mmu asɔt ɛnyɨŋ ɛyɛ, kɛ́ghati yi bɛ ákɛ́mɛ́ yɔ ntá yɛ.
Mpú nɨkmʉɛt bɛ́ ɔ́mfɛ́rɛ́ bhɔ fá amɨk, kɛ chí bɛ́ ɔ́nkɛ́m bɔ́ bɛ mbʉ́mbʉ ákɛ́ kʉ bhɔ yɛ̌nyɨŋ.
Mbák mmu abhɨ́kɨ́ ka bɛ́kóŋo ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ sɛ́sɨ́ŋɨ́ amɛm ɛkáti ɛnɛ, fyɛ́ ká yi amɨ́k amʉɛt nɛ bǎkɛ́ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛkʉ nɛ yí. Kʉ́ ká yí ɛnyu yɔ bɛ ntíánwɔ́p ánkɛ́m yi.
Ndiɛrɛ bɛsɛ bho sɛ́nókó kɛ sɛ́chwè ndǔ nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt ɛnɔ, puyɛ̌ bǒ abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ noko. Kɛ Mandɛm árɛ́m nyaka ɛ̌ti yap bɛ, “Njɨ́kɨ́ ndǔ bɛběntɨ ɛbha bɛ, ‘Bápú kway bɛchwe ndǔ nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt ɛna wáwák.’” Mandɛm arɛm nɔ yɛ̌ndu ánáŋ ánáŋá nyaka bɛghoko nɛbhʉɛt nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt ɛnɔ nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi atɨ bɛkʉ tɛ mpok anɛ yí ághókó mmɨk.
Mbɔnyunɛ wɔ Mandɛm ɔpú chɛn chɔŋ mɛ ɔ́ndɔ́ amɛm ɛtɔkɔ́ bawú, ɔpú rɔ chɔŋ Mmu anɛ áchyɛ́ nɛpɛ́m ɛni ntá yɛ ámpɔ́ amɛm nnɛm.
Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Bǎkɛ́ cháy. Dɔ́k ká ghati bakoŋo bha. Ghatí ká bhɔ bɛ, mándɔ́k atú Gálili. Chɔŋ mángɔ́ mɛ arɛ́.” 
Ɛnyu yɔ kɛ ɛ́chí nɛ ɛrɨ́tí ɛnɔk. Ɛ́nyu chi bɛrɨ́tí kɛpɛm, ɛpu kway mɛnyu bɛbɛ́ptí kɛpɛm.
Nɛ́nɛ, nchí fyɛ́ bhé amɔ Mandɛm nɛ nchí rɔ bhe Ɛyɔŋ ɛyi ɛnɛ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ be bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhi. Ɛyɔŋ ɛyi ɛ́kwày bɛkʉ mǎngó mǎnsɛ́nɛ́, nɛ ɛkway bɛchyɛ bhe áfɔ́k anɛ́ Mandɛm ábhʉ́rɛ́ ntá bǒ abhɛn yí ákʉ́ mámbák abhi.
Nɛbhʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ mmɨk anɛ nkók áte amfay abhɔ́ŋ batay byo nɛ apay. Básɨ́ŋ byo nɛ apay ndǔ batay yɔ. Manyɛ́n yɔ abhak anɛ́ bǒnto Mɔ́nkwɔmɛn byo nɛ apay.
Nɛyí nɔ́kɔ́, Yesu afate kpaŋwák, arɔk nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bo bápú arɛ, are nɨkmʉɛt.
Kɛ mmu anɛ ághàti bo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fú nta Mandɛm ǎchyɛ̀ bhɔ bɛtaŋ, afyɛ́ bho ntɨ, nɛ ǎchyɛ̀ bhɔ nɛpɔptǐntɨ.
Mɛ kɛ nchí nnɛrɛ́nɔk. Bǎchí batáp. Mmu anɛ achí babhat nɛ mɛ mpoknkɛm, mɛnkwɔ́ mbak babhát nɛ yi, yí wu kɛ ányù bɛyǎ kɛpɛm. Mbák mpú nɛ bhe, bǎpú kway bɛkʉ yɛ̌nyɨŋ.
Kɛ ngɔrɛ́ wu arɔk akwɛ́n bɛkak Yesu are nɨk yi mmʉɛt andɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Acha, kwak mɛ.”
Nnya mbémbé anɛ ɔ́ghɔ́ achi nyaka nɛpɛ́m, kɛ nɛ́nɛ apɛt apú, nɛ abhɔŋ bɛfu ndǔ nɛpi ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti, bɛ andɔk ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ babhɔŋɔ báway yɔ, ndak amay. Bo abhɛn babhɨkɨ sɨŋ manyɛ́n ayap tɛ nɛbhǒmɨk, bághɔ chɔŋ yɔ mámbak maknkay bɛ́ achi nyaka kɛ nɛ́nɛ apɛt apú nɛ chɔŋ ampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.
Nkáp chi awa. Mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ ɛnyǔ nkɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ wú? Mpabhamɨ́k akʉ ɔ̌béntɨ ndǔ ntɔ́ŋɔ́ bǒbhɛn bɛrɨ̌ntɨ?”
Kɛ nnɔ nɛ chi kɛjwimɛm ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ yi arɛmɛ ntá yap.
Apɛt atɛp ntí amɨk ánsɨ́ŋɨ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ amɨk nɛ sɛnɔŋ awɔ.
Ǎgu mbɔnyunɛ mpok mmok áfú, átíɛ́ nɛ bɛtaŋ, ánku tákɔ ansɔŋɔ, bɔchuchu mánkuri, bɛrɨ̌ bhap mɛ́may mɛnkɛm. Ɛ́chí ɛnyumɔt nɛ mǔnkáp. Yɛ̌ chí mpok anɛ yi áyàŋ nkáp, ɛyi ɛ́kwáy mɛ́máy. 
abhɛ́nɛ́fú bákɛ́mti bɔ̌-bɛtok abhɛn mfɔ wu átó, bádɛn mbɔ nnya baway.
Arɛ́, sɛ́tɛ́mɛ́ri mbɔk bǒnkwɔ Yesu. Barɛm bɛ́ sɛnchɔkɔ nɛ bhɔ́ ndu manywɔp tándrámɔt. Sɛ́chɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɛ bhɔ, sɛfǎ yɛ sɛrɔk Rom.
Bákʉ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, bápáti yí batiɛ́ amʉɛt, báfɔ́ŋɔ ɛnɔk ɛyɔ yi awɔ bákɛ́bhɛ bɛdɛpti yi anti nɛ yɔ.
Bǎkɛ́ fyɛ ntí ndǔ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn nɛ́chɔ̀ŋti. Fíɛ́ ká ntí chí ndǔ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn nɛpu chɔŋti, nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn nɛ́chyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti, ɛnɛn Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm nchí chyɛ chɔŋ be. Ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ Ɛtaya achyɛ ɛrɨŋ bɛtɔŋ bɛ yi kɛ átó mɛ.”
Sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ atwɔ nyaka bɛkwak chi bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ Ábraham, puyɛ̌ bɔángɛl.
Báchwɔ́bhɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ arɛ́, bákó amfay ndu mɔ́kɛt amɔt amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́mfáy anɛ bɔ báchɔ̀kɔ nyaka arɛ. Bǒnto bhɔ babhak Píta, nɛ Jɔ̌n, nɛ Jems, nɛ Andru, nɛ Fílip, nɛ Tɔmás, nɛ Batolómio, nɛ Mátio, nɛ Jems mmɔ́ Alfeyɔs, nɛ Símun anɛ achi nyaka ndǔ nkwɔ bo abhɛn mánù ɛ̌ti ɛtɔk ɛyap, nɛ Júdas mmɔ́ Jems.
Ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ́ bɛ mɛ nkwáy bɛ́twɔ bɛghɔ bhe nɛ maŋák mbák Mandɛm aká, nɛ bɛ́ nkwáy bɛbhɔŋ nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt nɛntɨ ɛnɛka.
Bábhó bɛrɛm nɛ batɨ bɛ, “Ǎrɛ̀m nɔ mbɔnyunɛ sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ brɛt.”
Yesu ayɨŋɨ yi nɛ bɛyǎ ɛkɔŋ arɛm bɛ, “Ɛ́rɔp chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mɔt ɛnɛ́ ɔbhɔŋɔ bɛkʉ. Dɔ́k tí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ mɛnkɛm chyɛ̌ nkáp ntá bachɛ́bhɛ́bho. Mbák ɔ́nkʉ́ nɔ, chɔŋ ɔ́mbɔŋ kɛfɔ̌ mɛnyɨŋ amfay. Ɔ́ntwɔ́ yɛ ɔnkoŋo mɛ.”
Kɛ yɛ̌ chi bɔ̌mayi kɛnoko yí.
Bǒbati bachiǎkap nɛ babhahɛrǐ ɛkɛrákap bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ yí, bábho bɛbɨk mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Dɛm mángó yi ndǔ ɛkotákátí! Mángó yi ndǔ ɛkotákátí!” Páílet arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Bě babhɔŋ mǎnsɔt yi mǎngó ndǔ ɛkotákátí, mbɨ́kɨ́ ghɔ ɛbɛ́ptí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ákʉ́ ɛnɛ ɛ́yàŋ mángwáy yi.”
Ángɛl arɛm ntá ya bɛ, “Manyɛ́n anɛ ɔ́ghɔ́ ngɔrɛ́-nɛkɔ arɛ chɔ́kɔ́ áte ndǔ ngɛ́mtáy bho, nɛ manɛrɛ́kɛrɛ bho ankɛm, nɛ bǒ bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk mɛnkɛm.
nɛ bɛsɛ mankɛm sɛchi bɛpókómʉɛt ɛbhi.
Ngɔrɛ́ wu arɛm bɛ, “Ɛta, ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ɛnyɨŋ ndu bɛ́yǎ manyiɛp nɛ yɔ, nɛ mbokó manyiɛp áchwe, ɔ̌bhɔŋ manyiɛp amɛn áchyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m fá?
“Bě manɛ́mámɨk abhɛn bǎyà bho mbi, chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛ́p ntá yɛka ɛncha! Bě bǎrɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Mbák mmu ámfyɛ́ bariɛp nɛ Mandɛm bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ, anjɨkɨ ndǔ nnyɛ́n ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm bɛtɔŋ bɛ yi abhɔŋ bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛyɔ, kɛ yi kɛkʉ yɔ, yɛ̌ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛpu bhak.’ Nɛ bɛ, ‘Mbák mmu ánjɨ́kɨ́ ambɨŋɨ bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm, abhɔŋ bɛ́bhʉrɛ bariɛp ami.’
Nɛ ɛ́rɨ ɛcha ntá mmǔ anɛ ápú kwɛ́n ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛ̌kʉ̀.”
Awu áfʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, ángɛl achak afú ndǔ ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm ɛnɛ ɛchi amfay. Yi nkwɔ abhɔ́ŋ ngak anɛ ácháp ndǔ bɛkpɔt mbwɔt.
Bǒbati bo Judeya bábhák maknkay ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi átɔ̀ŋ mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Ná mmǔ-nɛ áré rɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnyu ɛnɛ, ɛnɛ́ yi ábhɨ́kɨ́ ghɔk ɛkáti?”
Bɛrɨ̌ndu Yesu Kristo Acha mɛ́mbák nɛ bhe.
árɛ́m bɛ, ‘Pɔ̌l, kɛbhɔ́ŋ bɛcháy. Ɔ́bhɔŋ bɛ́té bɛsí Mfɔ Rom. Nɛ ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm nɛ wɔ, ǎpɛ́mɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ɔ́kɔ̀ nɛ yi.’
Nɛ mbwɔt anɛ ákwɛ́ntí ndǔ mmɨk tákɔ nsěnse, até ndǔ mmu anɛ ághòk Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm, kɛ bakáysí ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ mmɨk, nɛ bakáp, nɛ nɛpɛ́m mɛ́nyiɛ, akʉ bɔ́ kɛsɛnɛ ndǔ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm.
Ɛtɔk ɛnkɛm ɛ́rɔk ɛ́chɛm ambǐnywɔp.
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ ákwáká mmu bɛbʉ́ wu bɛ ántɨ́knsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhi ámpɛ́tnsɛm ntá Mandɛm, mmǔ wu afɛ́rɛ́ yí ndǔ nɛwú, nɛ Mandɛm ǎfoŋori bɛyǎ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhi.
Árɛ́mɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, arɔ bhɔ, atɛ́n mmʉɛt ambɨ mandú, mbɔ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ ɔ́tɛ́m ntay nɛngaka. Atɛp mánɛ́n amɨk, abho mɛnɨkmʉɛt bɛ,
Mandɛm Acha arɛm yɛ ntá yi bɛ, ‘Fɛrɛ́ nkwɔbhánya ɛyɛ bɛkak, mbɔnyunɛ nɛbhʉɛ́rɛ́mɨk anɛ ɛ́té nɔ arɛ achi nyáŋá.
Nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́, sɛ́tɛ́mɛ ndǔ nɛchyɛ Sídɔn. Júliɔs atɔ́ŋ Pɔ̌l bɛrɨ̌ntɨ. Arɔ Pɔ̌l ánkó ɛtɔk, ángɔ́ mamʉɛrɛ bhi bɛ mánkwák yí nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛkway bɛ́kwák yi.
Tɛ̌ndu bɛbʉ́ bo Israɛl bɛ́kʉ́ Mandɛm áyɛ́rɛ́ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl, nɛ tɛ̌ndu bo Israɛl bákwɛ́nɛ́ bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm áyàŋ nyaka bɛ mánkʉ, ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ́ Mandɛm ayɛt bo bachak tontó. Chɔŋ Mandɛm apú chyɛ mbɔ̌ŋ bɛyǎ áfɔ́k anɛ áyá áchá ntá bo bachak mpok anɛ bo Israɛl mankɛm bápɛtnsɛm ntá yi kɛ? 
Sɛ́nú yɛ bɛchwe ndǔ nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt ɛnɔ bɛ ɛnyǔ nɛtaŋa ntɨ bo Israɛl nɛ́kɛ́ kʉ yɛ̌ mmu ywɛsɛ ankwɛn.
Báre bok bɛyǎ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ, nɛ mángwati nɔkɔ bɛyǎ bǒmame nɛ bawɛt ólif mámbu nɔkɔ bhɔ. 
Bǎkɛ́ byák ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ákʉ́ ntɨ mǔnkwɔ ándɛm.
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, mandú mbʉ́ɛ́p abho bɛ́fók bɛ́fú ɛbhe manyu nɛ bo bakaysi bɛ chɔŋ mɛnyɨŋ mɛ́mbak sayri. Báya yɛ ndo báfɛ́rɛ anyɛ́n, babho mɛnok bɛrɔŋ ambɨ mámfʉɛrɛ nɔkɔ nɛkʉ nnyɛ́n.
Bo bábhɔŋ bɛ́fyɛ kpɨk amɨ́k bɔ amʉɛt. Mbák mángɔ́ yɛ bɛ́ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bɛ́pú nɛ bhɔ́, mánsɔt bhɔ́ mbɔ bo abhɛn bákwàk bɛ́kʉ bɛtɨk Mandɛm.
Ángɛl Mandɛm abhesi tɛ́mchók, bɛdiɛrɛ bɛ́kwɛ́n amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ. Ángɛl akɛ́m Píta ndǔ nɛnkɨ anyɨkɨsi, áŋɛ́mɛ́ yí arɛm bɛ, “Faté áyák!” Tɛ́mté wu ngɛm ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chí amɔ́ Píta ɛ́yóko ɛ́kwɛ́n amɨk.
Ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt achak amɛm ɛkáti ɛyi, Mandɛm apɛt ǎrɛm nyaka bɛ, “Bɔ́ bápú kway bɛchwe ndǔ nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt ɛna wáwák.”
Mankɔ̌ bhɔ bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mfɔ Hɛ́rɔd árɛ́mɛ́, báfá bare rɔŋ. Ndǔ bárɔ̀ŋ, bághɔ́ nkúbhɛ́ nɛmbe ɛnɛ́n báyámbɨ baghɔ atú ɛtɔk ɛyap nɛ nɔ́ nɛ́rɔ́ŋ nɔ́kɔ́ ambɨ, bɔ́ mánkoŋo nɔkɔ ansɛm. Báchwɔ́bhɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ Bɛ́tlɛhɛm, nɛmbe ɛnɔ nɛ́te amfay nɛbu, tɛ́bhɛ́ tɛ́bhɛ́ nɛ ɛkɛt ɛnɛ́ mɔ́wu áchí arɛ́. Nɛghɔ́ bághɔ́ nɛmbe ɛnɔ, maŋák amap aya acha.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Mpok anɛ nkɛm, ngátí bhe barak anɛ chí ndǔ bakay. Kɛ mpok ǎtwɔ̀ anɛ mpú pɛrɛ ghati be mɛnyɨŋ ndǔ bakay. Mpok yɔ ánkwáy, ndɔbhɛ ghati bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti Ɛtaya chi kpoŋoroŋ.
Nkoŋo anɛ Yesu ákɔ́ŋɔ́ tontó abhak chɔ́kɔ́ kɛkwɔt nɛ yi.
Barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ bhɔ bati apay bághók yɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fú amfay ɛ́rɛ̀m ntá yap bɛ, “Twɔ́ ká wɛn amfay!” Báré rɔŋ amfay amɛm ɛkpɔkɔ́ nɛbhaŋ, bǒmpap abhap bate mámpɔkɔ nɔkɔ bhɔ́.
Bě babhɔŋ bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ bǎbhɔŋ bɛkoŋo bayarɛ́kak ayɛsɛ. Sɛ́pú bhɔt nyaka abhɔ́t mpok sɛchi nɛ bhe.
Batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bákʉ mbɔ ɛnyu mǔngo wap ághátí bhɔ́. Básɔ́t Pɔ̌l bɛtǐ bhɔ bárɔk nɛ yi kpát bágháka Antipatris.
Bo ɛtɔk ɛyɔ bákù nyaka batu pú, nɛ anɛ silbha, nɛ batǔ mɛnyɨŋ bɛsɔbhɛri mmʉɛt ɛbhɛn bɛ́kɔ̀t ŋwaŋwǎŋwaŋ, nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ŋwaŋwaŋ bɛ́chák. Bákù nyaka bɛyǎ ndɛn chu ɛnɛ nkáp mɛnyu nɛ mɛnyu ɛnɛ babhɨŋɨ bɛ silk nkwɔ. Bákù nyaka mɛnɔk bɛyǎ nkáp nɛ ɛbhɛn bɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛrɨ́tí ɛriɛp nkwɔ. Bákù nyaka nkwɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn baghoko nɛ babhaŋá nsɔk, nɛ ɛbhɛn bághókó nɛ brɔ́ns, nɛ ɛbhɛn ɛsé nɛ ɛbhɛn bághókó nɛ ɛnyǔ ntay ɛnɛn bábhɨŋɨ bɛ mábɨl.
Batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bágó nɔ́kɔ́ Yesu ndǔ ɛkotákátí, básɔ́t ndɛn ɛyi bákɔ́rɛ ndǔ baru anwi, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap asɔt ndu amɔt. Kɛ ɛ́rɔp nkú amɔt. Nkú yɔ abhak ntěndɛn nɛmɔt ɛnɛn báyɛ́mɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nɛku ɛni bɛ́fú amfay bɛ́gháka amɨk, kɛkpɔti yɔ́ yɛ̌ ɛbhak.
Bɛghori ɛbhɔ bɛrat, nɔ chi, ngó, nɛ mɔ́ngo, nɛ ɛriɛbhɛ́ sɔ́lfɔ, bɛ́fú anyǔ mpɔŋɔ́ndɨk bɛ́wáy mmu amɔt ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ bǒ bati arat.
Mmǔ anɛ árɔ́bhɛ́ chi mmɔ́ Mandɛm, apú pɛrɛ kʉ bɛbʉ́ mbɔnyunɛ nɛpɛ́m Mandɛm nɛchi nɛ yi. Nɛ apú kwáy bɛrɔŋ ambɨ bɛkʉ bɛbʉ́ mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm ákʉ́ yi abhɔŋ nɛbhě nɛkɔ.
Pɔ̌l nɛ Banábas bárɔp Antiɔk. Arɛ́, báre tɔ́ŋ, mángati nɔkɔ bo ɛyɔŋ Acha nɛ bɛyǎ bo báchák nkwɔ. 
Nɛ nkwɔ sɛ́kàka Mandɛm mpoknkɛm mbɔnyunɛ mpok sɛ́gháti bhe Ɛyɔŋ ɛyi, bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ sɔt yɔ́ mbɔ ɛyɔŋ ɛnɛ nkwǎ. Bǎsɔ́t bɛ tɛtɛp chi Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ɛnɛ́ ɛ́kʉ̀ bɛtɨk amɛm batɨ yɛka, be bho mánóko.
Bɔ̌ma, ɛ́rɨ yɛ bɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛká ándɔ́k ambɨ bɛbhak ndu nte anɛ yí áchí nyaka mpok Mandɛm ábhɨ́ŋɨ́ yí.
Ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ mbɨ ɛnɛ́n nchwé amɛm áchá manyé bɛ ntáŋá mmʉɛt, yɛ̌ mmu apú nyaka nɛ mɛ. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu abʉɛ́ mɛ. Mandɛm ámfóŋóri bhɔ́.
Kwae! Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ɛ́bho chi ntá yɛka kɛ? Kɛ chí bɛ ndiɛrɛ ntá yɛka kɛ yɔ ɛ́chwɔ́bhɛ́?
Bɛ́kóŋo bɛpɨŋ ɛbhɛsɛ bo Israɛl, básyɛp mɛ mpok bábhe mɛ. Nchí mmǔ ɛtɔk Israɛl, ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt Bɛnjamin. Bachǐmbɨ bha chí bo Israɛl. Bárɨ́ŋɨ bɛpɨŋ bo Israɛl nɛ ɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk bo Israɛl nkwɔ́. Nɛ nchí mmu nkwɔ Fárisi, bɔ bho báte kpirí bɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu abhɔŋ bɛbhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé bɔtayɛsɛ.
Yesu arɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bɔ́ bárɛ̀m, abhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Ndaká yí bǎrɛ̀m ɛ̌ti brɛt anɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ? Nɛka ɛnɛka nɛ́gʉpsi nɛcha!
Bǎkɛ́ rɛm yɛ̌ bɛpɔ̌-kɛpɨ nɛ bɛbhokori kɛpɨ, nɛ bǎkɛ́ kʉ bɛchoŋó ntok. Kɛ chyɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ká bakak ntá Mandɛm.
María arɔk nɛbhʉɛt anɛ Yesu achi. Nɛghɔ́ yí ághɔ́ Yesu, akwɛ́n yi bɛkak abho bɛrɛm bɛ, “Acha, mbɔ ɔchí fá, mbʉ́ mɔ́maya abhɨ́kɨ́ gú!”
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎghókó tɛ nɛbhǒnɛt chi bɛ sɛ́bhɔŋ bɛkɔŋ batɨ.
Bo bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛ́n Yesu árɛ́mɛ́, mbɔk bo bábho bɛrɛm bɛ, “Nɛ́, chí ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka bɛ́twɔ.”
Mbák Nkwɔ Kristo ankɛm achɛm ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt amɔt nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ achi amɛm ǎrɛ̀m ɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛnɛ yi ábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ, kɛ ɛ́mfakari bɛ bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ akap wu nɛ bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ noko manchwe amɛm, bɔ́ bhɔ bapu rɛm bɛ ɛbhokori ɛ́kɛm be?
Nɛ yɛ̌ chí mpok Mandɛm átó Mmɔ̌ mbɨ ywi fá amɨk, arɛm chí bɛ́ bɔángɛl abhi mankɛm mánchyɛ́ Mɔ́ywi kɛnókó.
Bǎkɛ́ bhɔŋ ɛnyɨŋ bɛkʉ nɛ barak abʉ́abʉ.
Ɛ́kʉ́ Páílet apɛt abhɛ́p bɔ́ bɛ, “Ndǔ bǒbhɛn bati apay, anɛ bǎyáŋ ndɔ́ ándɔ́k chí agha?” Bábɨ́k bɛ, “Barábas!”
Mandɛm akʉ ɛbhárɛ́mɔ Debhít ambák Mpɛmɛ bo Israɛl bɛ́kóŋo bariɛp ami ntá bachǐmbɨ bhap. Mpɛmɛ wu chí Yesu.
Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ ɔ̌ghok mɛ mpoknkɛm, kɛ ndɛm ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ chí ɛ̌ti bo abhɛn bachi fá téé bɛ́ mánkwáy mɛnoko bɛ wɔ kɛ ɔ́tó mɛ fá amɨk.”
Nɛtɔ́ŋ ɛnɛn tɛtɛp nɛ́kɔ̀ ndɔ́ŋ amɔt nɛ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ mɛ amɔ́ bɛ ngati bho. Yí kɛ̌ bo báchyɛ̀ bakak nɛ áfɔ́k ankɛm áfù chi ntá yi. 
Ɛ́fákárí nkwɔ́ bɛ, ɛnɛ́ Páílet áchɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́táŋ Yesu, ngɔrɛ́ ywi ató mmu ntá yi nɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ, “Dɔ̌ mmu wu ándɔ́k. Achi chak. Ngɔ kɛnɔ́ ɛkɛ́n kɛ́re sɔŋɔri mɛ ɛ̌ti yi ndǔ bɛti ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́.”
Kɛ mbák chí bhe, bǎchyɛ bachɛ́bhɛ́bho ntíánwɔ́p! Ntɨkɨ bo báchyɛ̀ bhe ɛsɔŋɔri mánja nɔkɔ bhe ndǔ báchá manyé? Pú bǒ bakábhɛ?
