Nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt bo Israɛl nɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, María mmɔ̌ ɛtɔk Mágdala nɛ María achák, báfú ntɨnywɔp, ɛnɛ́ mbaŋ ábhɨ́kɨ́ re kaŋari ndu bɛrɔŋ bɛyɨŋɨ nnɛm Yesu.
abho bɛ́bɨk nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ andɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Ɛ̌ Yesu, Mmɔ Mandɛm mfay! Ɔ́bhɔ̌ŋ ntɨkɨ ndak nɛ bhɛsɛ́? Yɨkɨ́ Mandɛm bɛ́ ɔpú chyɛ chɔŋ mɛ ɛsɔŋɔrí.”
nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka anɛ áyàŋ bɛbhak mmǔ mbɨ abhɔŋ bɛbhak nsɛm ywɛka, abhɔŋ bɛbhak nsɛm ntá abhɛnɛfu mankɛm.
Yí kɛ ánɛ̀nɛ mbi bɛ sɛ́mbák barɨŋɨ́ndak nɛ bɛ sɛ́ndɨ́ŋɨ́ mɛnyɨŋ. Nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnɛn nɛ́rɨ nɛcha.
Ndaká yí bǎpú kway bɛghɔ bɛ mpú rɛm mbʉ chi ɛ̌ti brɛt? Sɔt ka mpok nɛ yís anɛ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi, nɛ anɛ bǒnkwɔ Sádusi.”
Básɨŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chí amɛm ɛkáti ɛnɛ bɛ mɛnkwak be mǎnókó bɛ Yesu kɛ achi Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò, Mmɔ Mandɛm. Nɛ bɛ́ ndǔ mǎnókó yí, mǎmbɔ́ŋ nɛpɛ́m ndǔ nnyɛ́n ɛni.
Bafɔ̌ mmɨk bákʉ ɛpúsí nɛ yi, nɛ bǒ mmɨk mányú mmɛ́m ami kpát bákwɛn, bákʉ ɛpúsí nɛ yi.”
Wɔ kɛ ɔ́chyɛ́ mɛ́ bɛtaŋ amfay bǒ mankɛm bɛ́ nkʉ mankɛm abhɛn ɔ́chɛ́ mɛ mambɔŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.
Kɛ mbák chí nkaysi Mandɛm, chɔŋ ntwɔ́ awu mandú mpok. Nɛ nnáŋ nchwɔ́p awu, chɔŋ mɛmbɔŋ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ mbák bǒ abhɛn bápà nɔ́ nyu báchí chí bǒ nyu wúwú, nɛ mbák bɛtaŋ Mandɛm bɛ́chí nɛ bhɔ́ tɛtɛp. chɔŋ ndɨ́ŋɨ́.
Afʉɛ́t ndǔ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛbhɛn báchyɛ́ yi mbi bɛ ánkʉ bɛsí nnya anɛ mbɨ arwɔ́ bǒ mmɨk. Aghati bhɔ́ bɛ́ mángókó ntíako anɛ bɔ básɔ̀t manchyɛ nɔkɔ kɛnókó ntá nnya anɛ achi nɛpɛ́m yɛ̌ndu mǎnáŋ báchyɛ́ nyaka yɔ ɛfʉɛt ɛnɛ ɛkway bɛway yɔ nɛ akparɛnja.
Yɛ̌ nɔ, nɛrɔŋ yi arɔŋɔ bákʉ́ yí mfɔ. Ápɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nsɛm ɛtɔk yi, abhɨŋɨ bǒ bɛtɨk abhɛn yi achyɛ nyaka nkáp bɛ mántwɔ́ yi angɔ nsay anɛ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́.
Arɨ́ŋɨ́ nyaka bɛ Mandɛm abhɔŋ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi afyɛ́ bariɛp bɛkʉ.
Kɛ mbʉ́ɛ́p ábhɔŋ bɛ́pɔ́kɔ chɔŋ bhɛsɛ kpát áchwí andɔk ántu mmʉɛt ndǔ ɛtɔkɔfú ɛnɛ́ nnyɛ́n nɛ́kábhɛ́.”
Moses achí nyaka mmǔ tɛtɛp ndu bɛtɨk ɛbhi mbɔ mǔbɛtok amɛm ɛkɛrɛ Mandɛm. Bɛtɨk ɛbhi bɛ́te ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka bɛkʉ bo mándɨ́ŋɨ́ ansɛmpok.
Mandɛm akʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛpay ndu bɛ́fyɛ bhɛsɛ ntɨ, bɛsɛ bho sɛ́bʉɛ́ sɛ́rɔ́ŋɔ́ ntá yi bɛ yi ampɛmɛ bhɛsɛ. Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ bɛpay bɛpu wupsi mbɔnyunɛ yí apú kway bɛsense. Afyɛ́ bɛsɛ ntɨ bɛ sɛkɛ rɔ bɛbhaka ntɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi afyɛ́ bariɛp bɛchyɛ bhɛsɛ.
Nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ báfɛ́rɛ́ nchaŋ, mányokoti nɛbhʉɛt amɔt básɔ́ŋ, ɛnyu yɔ kɛ ɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́fákari mpok mmɨk ámay.
Ɛ́chí wɨkɨrɨk bɛ mpɔŋɔ baso ámfʉɛ́t ndǔ mbok mbíábhan ɛ́cha mǔnkáp bɛka Mandɛm ambak Mfɔ ywi.”
Kɛ Yesu abhɨŋɨ bǒbhɔ nɛ bɔ̌bhap. Nɛ ntá baghɔkɔ́ bhi arɛm bɛ, “Dɔ̌ ká mǎmbɔ mántwɔ ntá ya, bǎkɛ́ chyɛt bɔ mbi mbɔnyunɛ bǒ abhɛn bachi mbɔ bhɔ́ kɛ̌ Mandɛm abhak Mfɔ wap.”
Kristo árɛ́m nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, apɛt arɛm bɛ, “Ɛta Mandɛm, ghɔ́ mɛ́ nɛ́. Ntwɔ bɛ́kʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́yàŋ mɛnkʉ.” Kristo ǎtɔ̀ŋ ndǔ nɛrɛm anɛ yi árɛ́mɛ́ nɔ bɛ Mandɛm afɛ́rɛ́ ɛsɨ́ akap, afyɛ́ anɛ akɔ.
Mmu anɛ ákʉ̀ nɔ, abhɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛchak ɛnɛ yi ánoŋ, ɛbhɨkɨ fʉɛt chi mɛnoŋ nɛ bɛcháy manyé anɛ átwɔ̀ ambɨ nɛ ngó anɛ́ ádù gum gum gum anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛ́mɛn bǒmpap Mandɛm.
Ngók ɛnyɨŋ mbɔ ɛyɔŋ ndu ɛ́fù nɛ́ntɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi nɛpɛ́m mɛnwi. Ɛyɔŋ ɛyɔ ɛre rɛm bɛ, “Nkáp bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn nywɔp nɛmɔt ákway bɛku nkɔ́bhɛ́ nchwi ɛnwi. Nɛ nkúbhɛ́ nkáp wu ánkway bɛ́ku chi nkɔ́p ɛnyǔ nchwi anɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ taŋ ɛsiɛ byo nɛ ɛpay. Kɛ bǎkɛ́ chɔŋti bawɛt nɛ mmɛm.”
Nɛka nɛ́kʉ́ mbɔk baghɔrɛ́ bághɔ́ ndǔ bǒbhap abhɛn bágú bápɛ́rɛ́nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Bádɛ́n mbɔk kpát bágú, yɛ̌ nɔ, bɔ kɛka bɛ́fɛ́rɛ ntɨ nɛ Mandɛm bɛ mamfɛrɛ bhɔ amɔ́. Báká bɛ ɛ́rɨ tontó bɛ bɔ mángú bɛ́ Mandɛm ankʉ bɔ mampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛ́rɨ nɛcha.
Bápɛ́t babɨk bɛ, “Puyɛ̌ mmǔ-nɛ, fɛrɛ́ chí Barábas. Barábas achí nyaka ngɛ́bhɛ́ ntantaŋ.”
“Ápɛ̀mɛ nyaka bo báchák, kɛ apú kway bɛpɛmɛ mmʉɛt yi! Pú yí achi Mfɔ bo Israɛl? Ámfá ndǔ ɛkotákátí ansɛp amɨk, chɔŋ sɛ́noko yi.
Ɛ́kʉ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ataka mbaŋ nɛ mbaŋ, ɛndɔk nɔkɔ chi ambɨ nɛ bɛtaŋ. 
bárɛm bɛ, “Yí wu arɛm bɛ ǎkwáy mɛmokoti ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm ampɛt ante yɔ́ ndǔ manywɔp arat.”
Bák ká mbɔ bo abhɛn bábhɔŋɔ ngǎngaŋ bɛbhak ndǔ mmʉɛt ɛyap. Kɛ bǎkɛ́ rɛm bɛ ɛ̌ti bǎbhɔŋ ngǎngaŋ, bǎkway bɛkʉ bɛbʉ́. Bák ká mbɔ bǒ bɛtok Mandɛm.
Bǒnkwɔ Fárisi kɛ bátó nyaka bǒbhɔ ntá Jɔ̌n.
Mbák chí bo abhɛn báyábhɛ́ bɛ́ mámbák bǒbati ntá bǒnkwɔ, bɛtaŋ ɛbhap bɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛkʉ nɛ mɛ. Mandɛm ápú tɔŋ kɛ́rɨ́ŋámík. Bɔ́ bábhɨ́kɨ́ tɔ́ŋ mɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛkɔ mɛ́máka ndǔ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ mɛ̌ghàti bho.
Atɔ́ŋ yɛ mmʉɛt ntá Píta nɛ, ansɛm mpok, ntá bǒnto bhi batí byo nɛ apay.
Kristo abhɨ́kɨ́ tó mɛ́ bɛjwiti bho. Ató mɛ́ chí bɛ́ ngátí nɔ́kɔ́ bo Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́. Nɛ mpú sɔt chí nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnɛn bǒ mmɨk nɛ sɛ́rwɔrɛ́nyu bɛ́gháti bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ mbɔnyunɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ yáŋ bɛ́ bɛtaŋá nɛwú ɛnɛ́n Yesu ndǔ ɛkotákátí mɛ́mbák ndɛ́ndɛm.
Arɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fù mmu antɨ kɛ ɛ́kʉ̀ yi akɛ bhak pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí Mandɛm.
Yesu ayɨŋɨ mfay asɔ́k nsɔk arɛm bɛ, “Ɛfáta” nɔ chi, “Nɛnɛ́.”
Bábhɨ́ŋɨ yɛ bhɔ bápɛtnsɛm amɛm áchá. Básɛ́mti bhɔ́ bɛ bakɛpɛrɛ rɛm nɛ bakɛpɛrɛ tɔ́ŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ndǔ nnyɛ́n Yesu.
Sɛmtí nɔ́kɔ́ ka batɨ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nywɔp bɛ bɛbʉ́ bɛkɛ rwɔ mmǔ ywɛka ántáŋntɨ nɛ Mandɛm. Kʉ ka nɔ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok, ɛnɛ́ nywɔp nɛ́chák nɛ́bhʉɛ́t ɛnɛ́n bábhɨŋɨ bɛ, “Ɛchɔŋ.”
Bǎtò nyaka bo ntá Jɔ̌n bɛ mámbɛp yi ángati bhe ɛ̌ti ya, nɛ aghati bhe ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛchi tɛtɛp.
Yesu Acha ángɔ́ nnɛrɛ́kɛt Ɔnɛsifórɔs ntínso. Akwɛ́nɛ́ mɛ ntɨ bɛyǎ mpok, kɛbhɔ́ŋ ntíánwɔ́p bɛ nchí mǔkɛnɔŋ nɛ ngɛm amɔ.
Kɛ Yesu Acha aghati yi bɛ, “Dɔ́k mbɔnyunɛ njap yí ámbák mʉ̌bɛtɨk awa, bɛ́ ándɔk ángati bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl, nɛ bafɔ bhap, nɛ bo Israɛl ɛ̌ti ɛya.
mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Bǒ abhɛn bákʉ́ bɛtɨk chi ndǔ nɛŋɔkɔ́ nywɔp nɛmɔt, ɔchyɛ́ bhɔ nkáp ɛnyumɔt nɛ bhɛsɛ́ bhó sɛ́kʉ́ bɛtɨk ndǔ nywɔp nɛnkɛm amɛm ɛsɔ́ŋtí mmok.”
Kɛ mpok ǎtwɔ̀ anɛ báfɛrɛ chɔŋ mbǎyngɔrɛ́ ntá yap. Nɛ chɔŋ mántarɛ nɔkɔ nsay ndǔ mpok yɔ.”
Nɛ mbák ndǔ bɛtaŋ Satan kɛ̌ mɛ̌bòk bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ, bakoŋo bhɛka bábòk bhɔ ndǔ bɛtaŋ agha? Chɔŋ bakoŋo bhɛka mántaŋ be!
Yesu arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Kɛ́ ghati yɛ̌ mmu ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fákárí, kɛ dɔ́k ntá nchiakap Mandɛm bɛ yi angɔ bɛ ɛbhaŋákwa yɛ ɛ́may. Ánáŋ ámbyó wɔ, ɔ́ndɔk, ɔnchyɛ yɛ akap ntá Mandɛm bɛ́kóŋo ɛbhé Moses. Chɔŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́mbak ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bo bɛ ɛbhaŋákwa yɛ ɛmay.” 
Bě bɛfé, nɔ́ kɛ ɛ́chí nɛ bhe. Ná bɛrɨ́tí kɛpɨ kɛkwáy yɛ bɛ́fú be anyu ɛnɛ́ bǎchí bǒ bɛbʉ́? Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́jwí mmu antɨ, yɔ́ kɛ ɛ́fù yi anyu.
Yɛ̌ mmu wap abhɨkɨ chɛ́p nyaka ɛnyɨŋ mbɔnyunɛ abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bakɨ nɛ yɛ̌ chi bɛkɛt, bátì nyaka mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ mántwɔ nɛ nkáp
Ábhó nɔ́kɔ́ bɛbhɛp barɛm ami, bátwɔ́ ntá yi nɛ mmu amɔt anɛ ákɛ̀m yi nkáp anɛ aya acha.
Mandɛm amɔt kɛ achi nɛ ǎkʉ̀ bo abhɛn básiɛ̀p bo nɛ abhɛn bapú syɛp bo mámbák chak chi mbák bábhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Yesu.
Bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ yɛ̌ mandú ntíánwɔ́p. Báchyɛ́ yɛ mmʉɛt ndǔ bɛkʉ baraká ntianwɔp anɛ mmʉɛt ɛyap ɛ́yàŋ bɔ mankʉ. Bákʉ̀ barak ɛ́pusi ankɛm, nɛ bápú rɔ bɛkʉ yɔ.
Yesu arɛm bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn ndu bɛtɔŋ ɛnyǔ nɛwú ɛnɛn yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́gu.
Nɛ́nɛ, Acha anɛ sɛ́rɛ̀m nɔ ɛ̌ti yi ǎkʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ chi nɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm, nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ Ɛfóŋó Acha achi nɛ bho, bábhɔŋ ngangaŋ.
kɛ bákɛ ghɔ Yesu. Bápɛtnsɛm barɛm bɛ bághɔ̌ bo mbɔ bɔángɛl Mandɛm ndǔ kɛnɔ́ amɨ́k antifú abhɛn bághátí bhɔ bɛ Yesu achi nɛpɛ́m.
Bo bábhák maknkay, mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Yɨŋɨ́, ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yí ákʉ́ ɛ́rɨ ɛcha. Ǎkʉ yɛ̌ chí bo abhɛn batú áchókó mángók mbaŋ, babhók mándɛm kɛpɨ.”
Bɔ̌ma, nchí ghati bhe bɛ ɛnyǔ mmʉɛt ɛnɛ sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛpú kway bɛbhak ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ Mandɛm achi Mfɔ arɛ, nɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́gugu ɛ́pú kway bɛchɔkɔ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt amɔt nɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛpu kway bɛgu wáwák.
Nchí ghati bhe bɛ, bɛyǎ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ nɛ bǒ abhɛn báchí chak bɛsí Mandɛm bábhɔ́ŋ nyaka ɛkwak bɛghɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎghɔ̀ kɛ bɔ kɛghɔ bhɔ. Bábhɔ́ŋ ɛkwak bɛghok mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎghòk, kɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ ghok bhɔ.” 
Ɔ́kɛ́ chɔŋti bɛtɨk Mandɛm ɛ̌ti nɛnyíɛ́. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nɛnyíɛ́ chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bo bákway mɛnyiɛ. Kɛ ɛpu chak mbák ɔ́nyìɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́kʉ̀ batɨ bǒnkwɔ mǎnkwɛn ndǔ bɛbʉ́.
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Ngáŋ áchí ɛrɨ́tí ɛnyɨŋ. Kɛ mbák ngáŋ ábhɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ bhɔŋ manyɨŋti mi, ná bákway bɛkʉ wu ampɛt ambak ɛrɨ́tí ngáŋ?
Faté ká sɛ́ndɔ́k, ghɔ́ ká, mmǔ anɛ áti mɛ ndǔ átwɔ̀.” 
Nɛ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ mpok ntwɔ́ awu, chɔŋ Kristo anjɛt bhɛsɛ tontó.
Bǎkɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk bɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ sɛ́gháti bhe ɛ́chí tɛtɛp nɛ yɛ̌ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bɛpu arɛ́. Sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ nkaysi bɛ́rwɔ́ yɛ̌ mmu.
Kɛ́m ká mmʉɛt. Bák ká pě. Satan mǔmpap ywɛka ǎghàp, amkpe nɔkɔ mbɔ nkʉ, ndu áyàŋ mmu anɛ yi akɛm anyiɛ.
Bɔ agha bákʉ́ nyaka Mandɛm ambe ntɨ ndǔ mamiɛ́ bɛsa bɛpay? Pú bo abhɛn bákʉ́ bɛbʉ́, nɛ bágú amɛm baso?
Nɛ mbɔ ɛnyu Aisáya arɛmɛ nyaka bɛ chɔŋ ɛmfakari, “Mbɔ Mandɛm Acha bɛtaŋ mɛnkɛm abhɨ́kɨ́ naŋa rɔ̌ nyaka mbɔk bho amɛm manɛrɛ́kɛt ayɛsɛ mbʉ sɛ́may mankɛm mbɔ bǒ Sódom nɛ abhɛn Gomóra.” 
‑ “Ɛ́rɨ yɛ bɛ́ mmu áchák ánchɛ́m nɛ bhɛsɛ bɛ sɛ́ngátí nɔ́kɔ́ bo mbɔ batísiɛ bɛ Yesu apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Mmu wu abhɔŋ bɛ́bhak chi mmu anɛ achi nyaka ndǔ nkwɔ ywɛsɛ mpok Yesu Acha achi nɛ bhɛsɛ, bɛ́bho mpok Jɔ̌n ájwítí yí bɛghaka nywɔp ɛnɛn yi arɔŋɔ amfay.”
Nkɔŋ yɛ bɛ́ mánkwɛ́sɛ́ abhɛn bábhʉɛ́t nɛ manoŋ amʉɛt mámbáy manɛ́m, mámbe bɔ, mánkɛm bɛkɛt ɛbhap sayri, bɛ bákɛ́ chyɛ mǔmpap ywɛsɛ mbi bɛrɛm ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti yɛsɛ.
Yesu aghati mǔngo wu bɛ, “Bǎpú ka mɛnoko mɛ mbák bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ ghɔ́ bɛrɨŋɨ́ maknkay.”
Mbʉ́ɛ́p ataŋataŋ ándɔkɔ nɔkɔ chí ambɨ ndǔ bɛyǎ manywɔp. Nɛ ngósí mmok kɛtyɛ́, nɛ bɛti bɔ́ kɛghɔ́ mambe. Ɛnyuyɔ̌ ɛnyuyɔ, kpátɛ sɛ́fɛ́rɛ ntɨ sɛ́rɛ́m bɛ́ ndak ywɛsɛ ámay.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anyíɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́ ajwi, báfɛ́rɛ yɛ batǔ amɛm nchwi ankɛm mamɛsɛ anyɛ́n bɛ áchwí amfʉɛp. 
Bǎkɛ́ bhak ndǔ nsoŋ amɔt nɛ mɛnyǔ bǒbhɔ.
Mpok ápɛ́rɛ́nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, ákó amfay, achɔkɔ ndu ɛbhe awɔ́nɛm Mandɛm. Arɛ́, bɔángɛl, bɛfóŋó, nɛ bɛtaŋtí bɛfóŋó, nɛ mɛnyǔ bɛtaŋ mɛnkɛm bɛ́chí antɛnɛ yi.
Bo Israɛl bárɔ́k, bákáp yi, bábhó bɛbhɛp yi bɛ, “Chɔŋ ɔ́ndɔ sɛ́noŋ ɛntat ná kɛ ɔ́ngati bhɛsɛ mbák wɔ kɛ ɔ́chí Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò. Mbák wɔ kɛ ɔchí Mpɛmɛ, ghatí bhɛsɛ́ kpoŋoroŋ.”
Kɛ Yesu arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Dɔ̌ sɛ́nchíɛ kpɨ́k mǎmbɔ nɛnyíɛ́. Ɛ́pú chak bɛsɔt nɛnyíɛ́ mǎmbɔ mánchyɛ́ ntá mmú.”
Yesu atɛ́m bhɔ nɛkay nɛ́chák bɛ, “Kɛfɔ Mandɛm fá amɨk kɛchi mbɔ yís anɛ ngɔrɛ́ ásɔ́rɛ́ achɛmti nɛ nchán fláwa ɛ́rát. Mandu yís wu akʉ fláwa nkɛm amwɔt, kpát ajwi ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi achi arɛ.” 
Mpok ntwɔ́ awu ndǔ nɛkɔ ɛnɛn nɛ́jwí ndɔŋ ɛpay, njɛp batú bo abhɛn bákʉ̀ bɛbʉ́ nɛ bǒnkwɔ bachak mankɛm. Nɛ́nɛ, mpɛt nchí sɛmti bhɔ ɛnɛ́ mpú awu nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ nkʉ nyaka mpok ntwɔ́ awu bɛ, mbák mpɛ́t ntwɔ, mpú rɔ bhɔ ɛnyu ɛyɔ.
Mpɛt nchí rɛm bɛ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ Mandɛm asɔt nyaka mmu wu árɔk Paradays* nɛ yi, kɛ chí ndu ɛfóŋó kɛ chí ndu nkwɔmʉɛt a, mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ. Mbɔŋ Mandɛm kɛ árɨ́ŋɨ́.
Bě bǎrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ mbakanɛm abhɨ́kɨ́ fú ntá ngɔrɛ́, ngɔrɛ́ kɛ̌ áfú ntá mbakanɛm.
Yesu achyɛ yɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ bɔ́ mankɛm mánchɔ́kɔ́ amɨk.
Nɛ ghati ká Akípɔs bɛ, “Ghɔ bɛ ɔnáŋá bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn Yesu Acha achyɛ wɔ.”
Pɔ̌l arɛm nɔkɔ nɔ, apɛt arɛm bɛ, “Dɨŋɨ́ yɛ ka bɛ́ bápɔ́kɔ́ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ árɛ̀m ɛnyǔ Mandɛm ápɛ̀mɛ bho bárɔŋ ntá bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl nkwɔ nɛ yɔ. Nɛ chɔŋ mǎntá batú mangok!” [Pɔ̌l arɛm nɔkɔ nɔ bo Israɛl bátáka nɛ bágúrɛ mankɛm nɔkɔ bɛyǎ ɛpʉítí nɛ batɨ.]
Ɛchi nɔ mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm ákʉ́ bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi aghoko mɛ́mbák chí ndɛ́ndɛm. Puyɛ̌ bhɔ kɛ bɛ́yàŋ bɛbhak ɛnyu yɔ. Mandɛm mmu ághókó bhɔ kɛ ákʉ́ bɛ ɛ́mbák nɔ. Kɛ bɛrɨ bɛ́chí ambɨ.
Kɛ bǎbhɔŋ bɛrɔŋ ambɨ bɛbhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́, mǎnte sɛnɛ́ nɛ kpirí. Bǎkɛ́ rɔ nɛbhakántɨ ɛnɛn Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ákʉ́ bǎbhɔŋɔ mpok bǎghókó yɔ. Bághati Mbok anɛ ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu fá amɨk. Mɛ Pɔ̌l nchí mǔbɛtok anɛ nchí kʉ bo mándɨŋɨ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́-nɛ. 
Mfɔ árɨ́ŋɨ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm, ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ̌ nchí ghati wɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nkɛbhɔ́ŋ bɛcháy. Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ ndu mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm ɛnɛ́ ɛ́bhɛ́sɛ́ wɔ ɛ́pú, mbɔnyunɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛ́bhɨkɨ fakari bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́.
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, baghɔsɔ́ŋ abhɛn báfú bɛku bawɛt bápɛtnsɛm, báte nɛfí, babho bɛdɛp nɛkok, mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, ‘Ɛta, Ɛta, dɛm mánɛ́nɛ́ bhɛsɛ mbǐnywɔp’.
“Ghɔ́ ka mɔ̌bɛtok wa anɛ njábhɛ́. Chi Mɔ̌ntɨ wa nɛ mbɔ̌ŋ maŋák nɛ yi tontó. Chɔŋ nkʉ Ɛfóŋó ya ɛ́mbák nɛ yi. Nɛ chɔŋ yí ankʉ mǎngati manɛrɛ́kɛt bǒ mmɨk ankɛm bɛ chɔŋ yí ampɛmɛ bhɔ.
Ntó yɛ bo tɛ́mté bɛ́ mámbɨ́ŋɨ́ wɔ, nɛ ɛ́rɨ ndu ɔ́twɔ́. Bɛsɛ́ mankɛm sɛ́chí fá bɛsí Mandɛm ndu bɛghok yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ Acha ágháti wɔ ɔ́ngátí bhɛsɛ́.” 
Kɛ ɛbhé ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ́ nyaka mfyɛ́ ngoŋo ndǔ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ bho mɛnyu nɛ mɛnyu. Mbák ɛbhé ɛ́pú, bɛbʉ́ bɛ́bhàk chi mbɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́gú.
Dɔ̌ ká kpák anɛ Kristo áchyɛ̀ ántɔ́ŋ be ɛnyǔ bǎbhɔŋɔ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ tɛ̌ndu Mandɛm ábhɨ́ŋɨ́ be bɛ mǎmbak ndu mmʉɛt amɔt, nɛ bɛ kpák ambak nɛ bhe. Nɛ bǎbhɔŋ bɛkaka Mandɛm ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ̀.
Mbuɔt anɛ áchí amɨk ǎchak ndǔ mmʉɛt yi ango nɔkɔ, kpát anchyɛ anɛ nkɔ.
Mmǔ abhɔŋ bɛ́bhɔŋ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak. Mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ kɛboŋ ǎrɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mpǎy anɛ achi amʉɛt nnya yɔ átɔ̀ŋ. Mpǎy yɔ chi mpǎy bakwǎŋwaŋ nɛ mpǎy yɔ chi bɔhundrɛt batándat nɛ bɛsa bɛrat nsɛm bɛtandat ().
Afú Yesu ansɛm, atɔti amɛm bɛyǎ bhó kpát arɔk atɔk nkokoŋ nkú yi. Tɛ́mté wu, manǒŋ mɔ asiɛ́p.
Dɔ́k ká chi ntá bo Israɛl abhɛn bachi mbɔ ághɔ́ŋɔmɛn anɛ́ ánɛ́mɛ́ ɛbhɨ.
Ɛ́nɛ́ bákàŋari mɔ́mpɔŋɔ batu wu, bo abhɛn báchí arɛ téé bábhɛ́p bhɔ bɛ, “Ndaká yí bǎkàŋari mɔ́mpɔŋɔ batu wu?”
Píta afa yɛ are rɔŋ nɛ bhɔ. Ágháká nɔ́kɔ́ arɛ́, basɔt yi bako ndu mɔ́kɛrɛ́mfay. Bɛyǎ mánkwɛ́sɛ́ bábhak arɛ. Bɔ́ mankɛm bakap Píta. Báre di, mántɔŋ nɔkɔ ndɛn ɛnɛ Tabita áyɛ́mɛ́ ntá yap mpok yi achi nɛpɛ́m.
Matá arɛm bɛ, “Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ chɔŋ ampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛwak ɛnɛ bawú mankɛm bápɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, ndǔ ngwɛnti mmɨk.”
Tɛ́mte wu, Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ atwɔ́ abhak nɛ mɛ. Ngɔ́ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ amfay. Mmǔ abhak arɛ́ chɔkɔ.
Bǒnkwɔ Fárisi nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm bábho mɛ́nywínti bɛ, “Mɔ́nkwǎnɛ ǎsyɛpti bǒ bɛbʉ́, nɛ ǎnyiɛ tɛ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ bhɔ.”
Wɔ mmu ɔ́pànyu, agha ághátí wɔ́ bɛ́ ɔchá bo báchák? Mmu ywɛká anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ puyɛ̌ Mandɛm kɛ̌ áchyɛ́ yí yɔ́, chí agha? Mbák Mandɛm kɛ áchyɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛká ábhɔ́ŋɔ́, ndáká yí bǎpányu mbɔ bɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́, bǎbhɔŋ bɔ chí ndǔ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛka?
Amɛm nɛpǐngo ɛnɔ, kɛ́nyɔrɛ ɛkɛn kɛ́nyiɛ bho kɛ́pú gú, nɛ ngó apu nɛmɛ.
Bɛ́táŋá bɛ́yá bɛ́chá, ɛrɔp chi bɛ́kɛm batɨ nɛ amɔ. Ɛkʉ mǔngo batɛmɛ́ nɛnu abhɔ́ŋ bɛcháy bɛ bákway bɛdakati Pɔ̌l. Achyɛ yɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bhi mánsɛp mámfɔ́ŋɔ́ Pɔ̌l ntá bǒbhɔ mándɔk amɛm ɛbhá batɛmɛ́ nɛnu nɛ yi.
Ndɔk mbɔ ɛnyǔ Mandɛm akʉ nyaka mɛndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ mbɔŋ bɛ́rɔŋ arɛ́. Ngáká nɔ́kɔ́ arɛ, mɛ nɛ bǒbati sɛ́chɔ́kɔ́ ansɛm ansɛm, nkʉ bɔ mándɨ́ŋɨ́ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ mɛ́ghàti bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl. Nkʉ nɔ bɛ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn mɛ̌kʉ̀ nɛ ɛbhɛn mbʉ́ɛ́t bɛkʉ bɛkɛ bhak ndɛ́ndɛm.
Nɛjwiti Jɔ̌n ájwítí yi, Yesu afú anyɛ́n. Nɛbu nɛ́nɛ́nɛ, aghɔ ndǔ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm áfú amfay, asɔt mkpá ɛbhóŋó are sɛp kpát ate yi amʉɛt.
Kɛ Yesu aghati bɔ bɛ, “Bě babhɔŋ, chyɛ̌ ká bhɔ nɛnyíɛ́ mányíɛ́.” Bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Sɛ́bhɔŋ chi bɔ̌bɛkpɔkɔ́ brɛt batay nɛ nsi ɛpay. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛchak ɛpu. Ɔ̌yáŋ sɛ́ndɔ́k sɛ́nku nɛnyíɛ́ ntá ngɛ́mtáy bǒbhɛn mankɛm kɛ?”
Yesu árɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ baghɔkɔ́ bhi mánywìnti ɛ̌ti ndak anɛ. Abhɛ́p bɔ bɛ, “Batɨ ábé bhe ɛ̌ti ndak anɛ ndɛ́mɛ́?
Yesu arɨŋɨ nkaysi yap. Arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛtɔk ɛnɛ ákɔ́rɛ́ áchí arɛ nɛ bǒbati mánu nɔkɔ nɛ batɨ, ɛ́bhɔ́ŋ chi mɛ́nɛ́mɛ́. Nnɛrɛ́kɛt anɛ ákɔ́rɛ́ achi arɛ ákwɛnɛ kwɛn.
Ananías akɛmɛ bɛ, “Acha, bɛyǎ bo bághátí mɛ mbok Sɔ̌l wu nɛ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ákú ntá bǒbhɛ awu Yerúsalɛm.
Kɛ mbák mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ ɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛnɛ mmu árɛ̀m, nchí bhak chi kɛnkɔ ntá yi, yí nkwɔ ambak chí kɛnkɔ ntá ya.
Bǒ Rom bákʉ́ nɔ́kɔ́ Galío gɔ́bhanɔ atú Gris, bo Israɛl abhɛn bachi arɛ bágwɔ́t nnɛt nɛ bákɛ́m Pɔ̌l bárɔk ndu acha manyɛ́ nɛ yi.
Ngɛ́mtáy bhó báre koŋo Yesu ansɛm. Mbɔk yap bábhák baghɔrɛ́ abhɛn básɛ̀mɛ nyaka, mándi nɔkɔ yi.
“Babhaŋá nya yɔ byo anɛ ɔghɔ áte ndǔ bafɔ byo abhɛn bábhɨkɨ re chyɛ bhɔ bɛtaŋ bɛkɛm kɛfɔ. Kɛ chɔŋ mánchyɛ bhɔ nɛ nnya mbʉ́mbʉ bɛtaŋ mbɔ bafɔ ndǔ nɛŋɔkɔ́ nywɔp nɛmɔt.
Ángɛl achak afú kɛ́kwɔ́t ɛ́fɛ́mɛ́ akap. Awú abhɔ́ŋ bɛtaŋ amfǎy ngó. Arɛm ntá anɛ akɛmɛ ngak bɛkpɔt mbwɔt anɛ ácháp nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ bɛ, “Kpɔ́t kɛpɛm ɛ́nɔk ɛkɛ́n bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ grep amɨk nyokoti mbɔnyunɛ kɛ́náŋ kɛ́pe.”
Kɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ ghɔ́ nyaka ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ yi ákʉ́ bɛ mangway yi, nɛ tɛ̌ndu yímbɔŋ árɛ́mɛ́ bɛ manyé ayi abhɔŋ bɛ́rɔŋ ntá Mfɔ Rom, nka nɛ yí.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Dɔ́k ká ghatí Hɛ́rɔd ɛsɔp ɛyɔ bɛ, ‘Chɔŋ ndɔk ambɨ bɛ́bok bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ nɛ mbú bho ɛchɔŋ nɛ mbúrɛ́, nɛ ɛ́gháká nɔkɔ manywɔp arat, nnaŋa bɛtɨk ɛbha.
Nɛ́ chi Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò. Atwɔ́ fá amɨk, bájwíti yi nɛ manyiɛp. Ɛ́tárɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ manoŋ mi arɔk amɨk. Nɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ achí ntísiɛ bɛ Yesu Kristo ǎrɛ̀m chi tɛtɛp.
Nɛ tɛtɛp, bǎkɔŋ batɨ̌ bǒnkwɔ atú Masidónia ankɛm. Kɛ bɔmá, sɛ́ghàti bhe bɛ́ ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ́ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ batɨ ɛ́ndɔ́k nɔ́kɔ́ chi ambɨ.
Kɛ mbák nkʉ nɔ, ná ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́fú tɛtɛp?”
Bɛyǎ bo abhɛn bachi arɛ bachɛm nɛ bǒ ngɔsɔ́ŋ wu bɛbhat bɔPɔ̌l barak amʉɛt. Bataŋá manyé báchyɛ́ ɛyɔŋ, báyók bɔ́ ndɛn amʉɛt nɛ bádɛ́n bɔ́ nɛ bɛkpa.
Bǎkɛ́ chyɛ yi mbi. Tě ka kpirí ndǔ nɛka ɛnɛka. Bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ batɨ bǒnkwɔ mbaŋ nkɛm fá amɨk, bághɔ̀ nkúbhɛ́ mɛnyu bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛn bǎghɔ̀.
Ngɔ́ ywi áyá ndǔ mambe amɔt ndǔ baru arat ámɛ́sɛ amɨk. Ate bɛsí ngɔrɛ́ wu nɔ ánòŋsi, ánoŋ nɔkɔ mɛnyiɛ mmɔ̌ anɛ yi ánòŋsi bɛbhe.
Bě babhɔŋ mǎndɔ́k ndǔ ɛpa. Mpú rɔŋ. Mpok aya abhɨ́kɨ́ re kwáy.”
Bǎkɛ́ fyɛ́ mmʉɛt ndǔ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bo abhɛn bachi amɛm ɛjuri bákʉ̀. Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ bɛ́chí ndɛ́ndɛm. Bǎbhɔŋ bɛkʉ bo mandɨŋɨ kpoŋoroŋ bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ bɛ́bɛp.
Páílet ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn, bɛcháy bɛ́pɛ́t bɛkɛm yi bɛcha.
Bǎbhɔŋ bɛ́chyɛ bhɔ ɛsɔŋɔri mbɔnyunɛ bɔ báchyɛ̀ bo bachak ɛsɔŋɔri. Bo abhɛn báyàŋ mɛnyiɛ nɛpɛ́m, Maŋák amap chi bɛkʉ nɔ yɛ̌ chi nɛ ngósí chuuu. Bɛpɨŋ ɛbhap bɛ́twɔ̀ nɛ ntíánwɔ́p ntá yɛka. Báchɔ̀kɔ nɛ bhe manyíɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́ kɛ bákʉ̀ chi bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chyɛ bɔ maŋák.
Akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, ‘Mǔmpap kɛ̌ ápɨ́ nɔ nchaŋ ɛyɔ.’ Bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, ‘Sɛ́ndɔ́k sɛ́mfɛ́rɛ́ yɔ́ ɛ́ndɔp chi nchwi yɔyɔ kɛ?’
Mpok Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n ánɛ́nɛ́ ɛtabhɛ́ sɛrwɔ ɛnɛ ɛjwi ɛtandat, njɨŋɨ, ngɔ́ ɛrɛmɛ́ nɛnyɨkɨsi mmɨk. Mmok arɔp pyɔɔ mbɔ ndɛn nɛkwɛsɛ́. Ntaŋ arɔp mbɔ manoŋ.
Fiɛ́ ká ntí ndǔ bɛ́bhɔŋ ɛkɔŋ nɛ bho, mǎmbɔŋ bɛyǎ ɛkwak bɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ánchyɛ́ be akap, sayri sayri, akap bɛ́gháti bho mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fú ntá Mandɛm.
Mmu ákɛ́ táŋ ntɨ mbɔnyunɛ, ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ ɔ́tàŋ ntɨ ɛnyu yɔ kɛ Mandɛm átàŋ wɔ. Ɛnyǔ ɔ́yɛ̀nti ɔ́nchyɛ ntɨ, nkúbhɛ́ ɛnyu yɔ kɛ báyɛ̀nti mánchyɛ wɔ.
Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm bɛ́fʉɛ̀rɛ fʉɛt, kɛ wɔ ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti. Chɔŋ bɔ́ mɛnkɛm mɛ́nkɔk mɛndɔp mbɔ bɛsɨ ndɛn.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Ngátí bhe bɛ chi mɛ. Mbák yɛ mɛ kɛ bǎyàŋ, dɔ̌ ká bakoŋo bha abhɛn mandɔk.”
Nti achi bɛ ɛbhé yɔ ɛ́pú kway bɛkwak mmu ankway ndu yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbi bɛsí Mandɛm. Nɛ́nɛ, bátwɔ́ nɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛchak ɛnɛ ɛcha bɛbhé. Yɔ́ kɛ sɛ́bháká ntɨ arɛ́ nɛ ɛ́yà bhɛsɛ kɛkwɔt nɛ Mandɛm.
Chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛ́p ntá yɛka ɛncha! Bachǐmbɨ bhɛka báwày nyaka barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ. Bǎtè manɛm ayap nɛ́nɛ, mǎngwati mbɨ arɛ́ bɛkʉ yɔ ándɨ́ amɨk.
Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mmu ákway bɛrɨŋɨ ɛ̌ti Mandɛm bɛ́chí kpoŋoroŋ ntá bǒ abhɛn bákʉ̀ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm atɔŋ bɔ́ ntá yap bɛ mandɨŋɨ bhɔ.
Yesu ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛtɛm nɛkay ɛnɛn, arɛm bɛ, “Mandɛm ǎnak bɛyǎ bho, kɛ ǎyap chí bǎrú.” 
Sɛ́kɛ́ bhak mbɔ Ken mmu achi nyaka mmɔ̌ Satan, mbʉ́mbʉ, ɛ́kʉ awáy mɔ́mayi Ábɛl. Awáy manɔ ndaká yí? Awáy manɔ mbɔnyunɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi akʉ bɛbɛp nyaka, kɛ ɛbhɛn manɔ bɛbhak chak bɛsí Mandɛm.
Jekɔ́p ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ yɛ bɛ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛchi Íjip, ató bachi bhɛsɛ arɛ́. Ɛbhak ndɔŋ anɛ mbɨ anɛ bɔ́ bárɔ́ŋɔ́ Íjip.
Arɔk ambɨ bɛ́go ndǔ nkwɔmʉɛt nɛ ndǔ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak. Mandɛm abhɔ́ŋ maŋák nɛ yi andɔk nɔkɔ chí ambɨ. Ɛbhak ɛnyumɔt nɛ bo.
Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛ́ nkwɔ́ Kristo mankɛm chí mmʉɛt Kristo? Ɛ́rɨ yɛ́ bɛ́ mmu ánsɔ́t mmʉɛt anɛ áchí ɛpókómʉɛt Kristo anchyɛ ntá ngɔrɛ́-nɛkɔ? Wáwák!
Mfú chí ntá Ɛta kɛ nchí twɔ fá amɨk. Nɛ́nɛ, nchí rɔ mmɨk, nchí pɛtnsɛm ntá Ɛta.”
Kɛ mpok mɔ́ywɛ-nɛ mmu árɔ́ŋɔ́ ányíɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ nɛ baghɔrɛ́-nɛkɔ ápɛ́rɛ́nsɛm, ɔwǎy yi ɛsɛnɛ́mpɔŋ!’
Yí ánáŋ ántwɔ́, ǎsɔt nkúbhɛ́ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mbák antɛn yi, anjibhiri mmʉɛ́rɛ́ ntɔp ɛyɛsɛ-nɛ, ankʉ yɔ́ ɛ́ndɔp chí mbɔ mmʉɛt anɛ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka mpok Mandɛm ákʉ́ yí apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.
Arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Bǎtwɔ̀ fá ntá ya nɛ mmǔ-nɛ bɛ ǎkʉ̀ bo bákɛ́ bhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé ɛtɔk. Mbɛ̌p yi mɛnyɨŋ bɛsí bhɛka, nɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ ghɔ́ yɛ̌ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ ɛbhě yi.
Bǒnto Yesu báré ghati bo nɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhap mɛnkɛm bɛ Yesu Acha apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, nɛ bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm bɛbhak nɛ bɔ mankɛm tontó.
Ɛnɛ́ Hɛ́rɔd árɔ̀ŋ ambɨ bɛbhɛp yi bɛbhɛp, bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm báte kɛkwɔt, mámbat nɔkɔ yi barak amʉɛt nɛ bɛyǎ ɛ̌yu.
Ɛnɛ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ́ kpatɛ mpok anɛ Acha ápɛ̀tnsɛm, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ mǎnyìɛ brɛt anɛ, mǎnyú mmɛ̌m amɛn, bǎghati bo bɛ́ yi agu nyaka ndu bɛ́pɛ́mɛ bhɛsɛ́.
Achwe nyaka amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́ Mandɛm, yi nɛ bǒbhi, mányíɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn báchyɛ́ ntá Mandɛm. Bɛ́kóŋo ɛbhé, ɛpú nyaka chak bɛ yi nɛ bǒbhi mányiɛ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɔ. Ndiɛrɛ bachiǎkap Mandɛm kɛ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka ngǎngaŋ mɛnyiɛ nɔ.
Bě bɛsakábho nɛ baghɔsɔ́ŋ, bɔ́ŋ ká nɛsɛptímʉɛt ntá bǒ batɨ́ bhɛka. Bɔ́ŋ ká nɛsɛptímʉɛt nɛ batɨ. Nɛsɛptǐmʉɛt nɛ́mbák ntá yɛka mbɔ nkú anɛ mmu afyɛ́ amʉɛt. Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Mandɛm apú chyɛ mbi ntá mmu anɛ áyòŋmʉɛt, kɛ ǎtɔ̀ŋ bɛrɨ̌ndu ntá bo abhɛn básɛptimʉɛt amɨk.”
Bǎbhɔŋ bɛchyɛ bhɔ bɛyǎ kɛnókó, mǎnkɔŋ bɔ́ ɛ̌ti bɛtɨk ɛbhɛ́n bɔ bákʉ̀. Nɛ mǎmbák sayri nɛ batɨ.
Bǎghok ɛnyǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛna nɛchi nyaka mpok mɛ́kòŋo bɛpɨŋɨ́ bo Israɛl, bǎghók ndu nchí chyɛ nyaka bǒnkwɔ Mandɛm bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri, nnu nɔkɔ bɛ nnáŋá nkwɔ wap.
Yesu anáŋ ayámbɨ arɔŋ arɛ ndǔ ntí ayɛsɛ mpok yi árɔ́bhɛ́ chi mǔnti bachiǎkap anɛ mpoknkɛm mbɔ ɛnyǔ bárɛ́mɛ́ nyaka ɛ̌ti Mɛlkísɛdɛk.
Ɛnɛ́ bɔ bachi Bɛ́tlɛhɛm, mpok nɛbhe ayi akway.
Ɛrɨ mɛ́nɨkmʉɛt ɛnyu ɛyɔ mbɔnyunɛ ɛ́chyɛ̀ Mandɛm mmú ápɛ́mɛ́ bhɛsɛ maŋák.
Bǎkɛ́ chay yɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bo bakway bɛkʉ bhe. Bɛsí Mandɛm, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka abhɔŋ mɛnwɔp tontó achá ngɛ́mtáy kɛnɛn.” 
Yɛ̌ nɔ, chɔŋ Mandɛm ampɛmɛ baghɔrɛ́ bɛfʉɛt ndǔ nɛbhé anɛ bɔ́ bábhè bɔ, nɛ mbák bapu tɔŋ mmʉɛt, nɛ mbák bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɔ bɛsɨkɨ ntɨ nɛ Kristo, nɛ mbák bárɔ̀ŋ ambɨ bɛkɔŋ bɛtɨ̌ bakwaŋwaŋ, nɛ mbák báchi nyáŋá ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnap, kɛbhɔŋ bɛkwɛnɛ.
Nchí rɛm nɔ́ nɛ ntí bɛ bǎrɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ́ Mandɛm achí nɛ mmu mbɔ Mfɔ aywi chí mbák bɛtaŋ Mandɛm bɛ́chí nɛ yí ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛni. Ɛ́pú wɛnti chí ndǔ ɛrɨ́tí ɛyɔŋɔ́nyu yɔ́yɔ́.
Ndu ɛ́chí nɔ, sɛ́kwáy bɛrɛm nɛ ntɨ̌ nɛnkɛm bɛ, “Mandɛm Acha achi nkwak wa, mpú chay yɛ̌nyɨŋ, mmu ǎkway bɛkʉ mɛ yi?”
Bǎghók Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ nɛ ntá Ɛpafras. Yi achi ntɨ mǔbɛtok Mandɛm anɛ sɛ́kɔ́ŋɔ́ tontó. Achi nkʉbɛtɨk Kristo anɛ ábhʉ̀ɛrɛ bariɛp ami. Achi awu ndǔ nnyɛ́n ɛnɛsɛ.
“Mpok mfɛ́rɛ́ bɛbʉ́ bhap, chɔŋ ɛnɛ ɛmbak mbɔ ɛnyǔ nyú nyaka nku nɛ bhɔ.”
Kɛ mbák ngɔrɛ́ arɔ́ nnɛ́m, abhɔŋ bɛ́chɔ́kɔ ndǔ mmʉɛt ɛyi, kɛbháy mmu achák. Mbák ɛ́pú nɔ́, ámpɛ́tnsɛm ntá nnɛ́m aywi. Mbakanɛm nkwɔ abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ bɛ́rɔ́ ngɔrɛ́ ywi ndǔ nɛbhay.
Mɔ́ngɔrɛ́ wu ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́ Yesu arɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛfakari, arɔk angwɛrɛ nɔkɔ gbagbǎgbak, ákwɛ́n bɛkak Yesu arɛm bɛsí bo mankɛm ntí anɛ yi átɔ́kɔ́ Yesu nɛ ɛnyǔ yi átáŋ tɛ́mté.
ndɔ́k ngáti yi mbok anɛ ákʉ̀ yi andɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛnyu Mandɛm akway bɛpɛmɛ yi nɛ ɛfo ɛyi ɛnkɛm.
bɛ́ bě mankɛm mǎnchyɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ kɛnókó nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt ntá Mandɛm mmu áchí chi Yesu Kristo Acha ywɛsɛ. 
Arɔk ntá yi, achɨti babhe ndǔ bɛfʉɛt bhi, agwɔ́t. Apɔkɔ yɛ yi anyaŋa amfǎy mpɔŋɔ batu yi, arɔk nɛ yí ndǔ ɛkɛt ɛnɛ́ mankɔ bachyɛ nkáp kɛ mabʉrɛ arɛ́. Akwak yí.
Ɛ́rɨ ɛcha ntá yɛka bǒ nsay ánù nɛ́nɛ, mbɔnyunɛ chɔŋ yi anchyɛ bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛkwak bɛbhɔŋ. Ɛ́rɨ ɛcha ntá yɛka bǒ bǎdì kɛbhɔ nɛ́nɛ, mbɔnyunɛ chɔŋ mǎngway ámɛn!
Chiɛ́ ntá ntɨ, nɛ chɔŋ Mandɛm anchyɛ wɔ nkwɔ́. Yi apɛrɛ́ chyɛ, ǎyɛnti sayri, angoko kpát ɛ́njwi ɛntakati nɔkɔ amɨk. Ɛnyǔ ɛnɛ́ ɔ́yɛ̀nti ɔnchyɛ ntɨ, nkúbhɛ́ ɛnyuyɔ̌ kɛ báyɛ̀nti manchyɛ wɔ.”
Tɛ̌ndu sɛ́nókó bɛ́ Yesu ágú nyaka, apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, sɛ́noko nkwɔ bɛ chɔŋ Mandɛm ankʉ bakoŋo Yesu abhɛn bágú mámpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m mpok Yesu átwɔ.
Nkúbhɛ́ mpok yɔ, bo batí arat bachwɔp ambǐnywɔp ɛkɛt ɛnɛ́ nchí arɛ́. Báfú Seséria nɛ ntó bɛ́ mánsɔt mɛ.
Ndǔ bǎbhɔŋ nɛka nɛ Mandɛm ǎbhàbhɛri bhe. Ǎkʉ̀ nɔ bɛ ámpɛ́mɛ́ bhe ndǔ ngwɛnti mpok. Mandú mpok yi ǎkʉ̀ be mǎndɨŋɨ ndǔ yi ápɛ̀mɛ bho.
Nɛ Mandɛm mmu arɨŋɨ batɨ bo mankɛm, atɔŋ kpóŋóróŋ bɛ́ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl bákway mɛ́nóko nkwɔ. Akʉ nɔ́ ndu áchyɛ́ bhɔ́ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyu yi achyɛ nyaka bhɛsɛ.
Bě babhɔŋ bǎrɨŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn sɛ́ghátí nyaka bhe ndǔ nnyɛ́n Yesu Acha bɛ bǎbhɔŋ bɛ́kʉ.
Ɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́ nɔkɔ mbɔ nɛŋɔkɔ́ nywɔp nɛmɔt, mmǔ achak arɛm bɛ, “Tɛtɛp, mmǔ-nɛ nkwɔ́ achi mbʉ nɛ Yesu. Yi nkwɔ chi mmu Gálili.”
Kɛ Píta akɛmɛ bɛ, “Cháá! Acha mbɨ́kɨ́ re nyiɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛpu pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí Mandɛm wáwák.”
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛbhɛp be chi bɛ, “Agha áchyɛ́ nyaka Jɔ̌n Njwiti bɛtaŋ bɛjwiti bho? Mandɛm, kɛ chí bǒ mmɨk?” Báre kɛm ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ batɨ bɛ, “Chɔŋ sɛ́ndɛm bɛ yi? Mbák sɛ́ndɛm bɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn Jɔ̌n bɛ́fú nyaka ntá Mandɛm, ǎbhɛ́p bhɛsɛ bɛ, ‘Kɛ ndaká yi bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ noko ɛyɔŋ ɛyi?’
Nɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ ghɔkɔntɨk ɛnyu ɔ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛka nɛ Yesu tɛtɛp nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ nnɔ máyɛ Lóis nɛ máyɛ Yúnis bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka. Nnókó tɛtɛp bɛ ɛnyǔ nɛka ɛnɔ nɛbhʉɛt nɛ wɔ.
Mpok bághoko ndu Pɔ̌l árɛ̀mɛ ɛ̌ti nɛpɛrɛ́nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, mbɔk ɛyap bare yɔkɔ yi, kɛ bachak barɛm bɛ, “Sɛ́kɔŋ bɛ ɔ́mpɛt ɔ́mfʉɛ́t ɔngati bhɛsɛ ɛ̌ti nɛpɛrɛ́nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.”
Ɛ́rɨ ɛcha ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ághɔ̀ bho ntínso, mbɔnyunɛ chɔŋ Mandɛm angɔ́ yi ntínso!
Nyɛ́sɛ́ mmu nɛ́pú kwáy bɛ́gháti awɔ́ bɛ, “Mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ɛnyɨŋ bɛ́kʉ nɛ wɔ?” Nɛ ntí apu kway bɛ́gháti bɛkak bɛ, “Mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛ́kʉ nɛ wɔ.”
Bák yɛ ka pě mpoknkɛm, mǎnɨk nɔkɔ mmʉɛt bɛ mǎmbɔ́ŋ bɛtaŋ bɛ́bʉɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛbhɔŋɔ bɛfakari, mǎnte bɛsí Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm.”
Mǔnti wu asɔt yí arɔk ntá mǔngo wap arɛm bɛ, “Pɔ̌l mǔkɛnɔŋ abhɨ́ŋɨ́ mɛ arɛm bɛ́ nsɔt ɛsakámu anɛ́ ntwɔ́ ntá yɛ nɛ yí mbɔnyunɛ abhɔŋ ɛnyɨŋ bɛ́gháti wɔ.”
Kɛ chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛp ntá yɛka bafɔ̌nkáp ɛncha mbɔnyunɛ, mǎnaŋ bǎbhɔŋ ɛbhɛka bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ, nɛ mǎnyiɛ̌ nɛpɛ́m, ndak ámay.
Nɛ bɛ́te kpirí ǎkwak bhɛsɛ sɛ́mbɔ́ŋ ɛpɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ sɛ́fʉɛt nɛmɔ. Nɛ ɛpɨŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ̀ sɛmbaka ntɨ bɛ chɔŋ Mandɛm ankʉ mbɔnyu yi arɛmɛ.
Kɛ mbák chi bhe, Mandɛm ayap bhe bɛ mǎmbak nnɛrɛ́kɛt anɛ bachiǎkap ntá Mfɔ ywɛsɛ. Bǎchi nyáŋá bɛsí Mandɛm. Ayap be bɛ mǎmbák bǒbhi mǎngátí nɔ́kɔ́ bho bɛtɨkɨ́ maknkay ɛbhi, yi mmu áfɛ́rɛ́ bhe ndǔ ɛjuri abhʉrɛ amɛm ɛrɛmɛ́ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́.
Nɛbho mpok yɔ, bɛyǎ bakoŋo bhi báya mmʉɛt ansɛm, bɔ́ kɛpɛrɛ koŋo yi.
Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́-nɛ kɛ Mandɛm ásɔt bɛpɛmɛ bhe, mbák mǎndɔ́k ambɨ bɛkɛm yɔ nɛ bɛtaŋ. Mbák ɛ́pú ɛnyu ɛyɔ, nɔ mǎnókó chi ndɛ́ndɛm.
Tɛtɛp, be kɛ bǎkʉ sɛ́dɛ̀p awɔ́ antɨ, nɛ be kɛ báchyɛ̀ bhɛsɛ bɛyǎ maŋák.
Abhɛ́n bachi bhap mánókó Yesu bákɛ́ rɔ bɛ́chyɛ bhɔ kɛnókó ɛkɛ́n kɛ́kwáy nɛ bhɔ nɛ bákɛ rɔ bɛghok bhɔ yɛ̌ndu bárɔ́bhɛ́ chí bǒ mmu amɔt. Ɛrɨ́ bɛ́ mántók bachi bhap sayri ɛ́ncha mbɔ̌ŋ ɛnyu ɛsɨ, mbɔnyunɛ bachi abhɛ́n bɔ́ bákwàk mánoko Yesu Kristo nɛ Mandɛm akɔŋ bhɔ́.  Tɔ́ŋ bo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn, ɔ́ngati bɔ́ mánkʉ bhɔ́.
Mpok básɔ́rɛ́ bhe ambɨ ndu bɛtaŋ be amɛm bɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt ɛbhap nɛ bɛsí bǒbati ɛtɔk nɛ bɔgɔ́bhanɔ, bǎkɛ́ sɛmɛ ɛnyǔ bǎkwày bɛtaŋa mmʉɛt nɛ ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ bɛrɛm.
Kɛ ángɛl Acha atwɔ́ arɛm ntá Fílip bɛ, “Faté sɛp ndǔ ɛsɨ́ mbi anɛ áfù Yerúsalɛm árɔ̀ŋ Gása”.
Mǎnyìɛ nɛpɛ́m fá amɨk, mǎnkʉ nɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chyɛ bhe maŋák. Mǎnyiɛ, bǎchɨkɨti bǎrɔp muri múrí mbɔ ɛsɛnɛ́ mpɔŋ ɛnɛ́ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛrɔŋ bɛway.
Mmɔ ágháká nɔ́kɔ́ manywɔp ánɛn, bo bárɔ́k bɛ́siɛ́p yi. Báre yàŋ bɛdu yi nnyɛ́n bɛ Sakaría mbɔnyunɛ chi nnyɛ́n Ɛtayi.
Mánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ mɛ́nyiɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́, asɔt nkɔ́p nɛ mmɛ́m amɛm, achyɛ bakak ntá Mandɛm nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yí ákʉ́ nɛ nɛnyíɛ́. Arɛm bɛ, “Nɛ́ chí Nku Nkɔ anɛ Mandɛm ányú nɛ bǒ mmɨk ɛ̌ti nɛwú ɛna ndu bɛtɔŋ bɛ chɔŋ ankʉ *Nku Nkɔ anɛ yi ányú nɛ bo ante.
Kɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu abhɔŋ ayi njɛnti akap kɛkúrí anɛ Kristo áchyɛ́ yi ndu bɛkʉ bɛtɨk nɛ wu.
Ɛyɔŋ ɛ́fú amfay ɛ́ré rɛm bɛ, “Wɔ ɔchí Mɔ́wa. Nkɔŋ wɔ tontó. Ɔ̌chyɛ̀ mɛ bɛyǎ maŋák.”
Mpok yɔ kɛ̌ bakoŋo Yesu bárɨ̀ŋɨ sayri sayri bɛ Yesu ǎrɛ̀m chi ɛ̌ti Jɔ̌n Njwiti. 
Nɛ́nɛ, ɛchí kpoŋoroŋ bɛ yɛ̌ mmu apú kway bɛbhak chak bɛsí Mandɛm ɛ̌ti yi ábhʉ̀rɛ bɛbhé. Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Mmu anɛ achi chak bɛsí Mandɛm ɛ̌ti yí ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛka nɛ Kristo, ǎbhɔ̀ŋ nɛpɛ́m.”
Chiɛ́ yɛ́ ka yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mǔnti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛchyɛ yi. Mbák chi nkábhɛ́nti kɛ mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛchyɛ, ánchyɛ́. Mbák chí nkáp anɛ mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛchyɛ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́, ánkʉ̌ nɔ. Mbák mmu abhɔŋ bɛsɛpti mmʉɛt ntá achak, ánsɛ́ptí mmʉɛt ntá yi. Nɛ mbák mmu abhɔŋ bɛchyɛ kɛnókó ntá achak, ánchyɛ́ yi kɛnókó. 
Josɛ́f arɔk, achɔkɔ amɛm ɛtɔk Gálili ɛnɛ́ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ Násárɛt, mbɔnyunɛ ɛ́chí amɛm ɛkáti ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ bɛ Mandɛm arɛm ɛ̌ti Kristo bɛ, “Chɔŋ bo mámbɨŋɨ yi bɛ ‘Mmu Násárɛt’”.
Báchwɔ́bhɛ́ nɔkɔ arɛ ndu mɔ́tɔk anɛ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ́ Salamis, bárɔ áchwi nɛkunyɛ́n bákó ɛtɔk mángati nɔkɔ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm amɛm bɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt bo Israɛl. Jɔ̌n Mák abhak nɛ bhɔ́, ankwak nɔkɔ bhɔ.
Ngɔrɛ́ amɔt abhak arɛ́ anɛ áfɛ̀rɛ manoŋ ndǔ mamiɛ́ byo nɛ apay.
Yesu ághókó nɔkɔ nɔ, ate arɛm bɛ, “Bɨŋɨ́ ká yi antwɔ́.” Bárɔk babhɨŋɨ yi bárɛm bɛ, “Faté twɔ́, ɔ́kɛ́ chay, ǎbhɨ̀ŋɨ wɔ.”
“Mbák manywɔp anɛ bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri yɔ ámay, mmok ánɛm tɛ́mté, ntaŋ kɛpɛrɛ ghɔɔ,
Sakaría nɛ ngɔrɛ́ ywi babhak chak bɛsí Mandɛm. Bábhɔŋ kɛnókó nɛ Mandɛm, mámbʉrɛ nɔkɔ bɛbhé bhi mɛnkɛm bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ ti.
Bakoŋo bhi bábhó bɛyɨŋɨ batɨ, kɛrɨŋɨ mmu anɛ Yesu árɛ̀m nɔ ɛ̌ti yi.
Dɔ̌ ká Mandɛm ankʉ mǎmbak bǒ bakɔ ndǔ batɨ yɛka bɛ nkaysi ywɛka ámbák nkɔ.
Mmu anɛ ákɛpntɨ ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ báchyɛ̀ yi ndɛ́ndɛm ndu yi árɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ Mandɛm achi nɛ yi, Mandɛm ǎbhɔŋ maŋák nɛ yi.
Kpátɛ̌ ɛchɔŋ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́re jwimɛm-ɛ? Bǎghɔ́kɔ́ntɨk ndu ndɨ́kɨ́ nka bho ɛtay nɛ bɛkpɔkɔ́ brɛt bɛtay? Bǎghɔ́kɔ́ntɨk bɛkǎy brɛt anɛ árɔ́bhɛ́?
Yɛ̌ ákʉ́ wɔ chi ɛnyɨŋ, yɛ̌ ǎkɛ̀m wɔ chi barɛm, fyɛ́ mɔ́ ndǔ nnyɛ́n ɛna.
kɛ ndu mɔ́ngɔrɛ́-nɛ árɔ̀ŋ chi ambɨ bɛchyɛ mɛ ɛsɔŋɔri, chɔŋ ntáŋ manyé yi sayri nchyɛ́ yi. Mbák ɛ́pú nɔ́, apú sɛbhɛ mɛ ante amɨk.’”
Pú sɛ́bháká ntɨ chi nɛ bhe? Pú be kɛ̌ báchyɛ̀ bhɛsɛ maŋák-á? Pú be kɛ̌ bǎkʉ̀ sɛ́ndɛp chɔŋ awɔ́ antɨ bɛsí Yesu Acha ywɛsɛ ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɛn yi apɛtnsɛm, bɛ sɛ́kʉ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛsɛ́ sayri?
Píta arɔk ambɨ bɛchɔkɔ Jopa ndǔ bɛyǎ manywɔp nɛ ngoko nkwɔbhɛ́nya ɛnɛ bághárɛ́ amʉɛt nnya ɛnɛ baway. Nnyɛ́n ɛni nɛ́bhak bɛ Símun.
Nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́, bɛyǎ bo abhɛn bátwɔ́ ndǔ Ɛpǎ Nɛkɨŋɨ bághók bɛ́ Yesu ǎtwɔ̀ Yerúsalɛm.
“Bachǐmbɨ bhɔ bábhɔ́ŋ mpabhamɨ́k nɛ mɔ́máyap Josɛ́f. Bátǐ yi mbɔ nsɛm ntá bakɔ̌siɛ, Bɔ́ bárɔ́k ɛtɔk Íjip nɛ yi. Kɛ Mandɛm abhak nɛ yi,
Mfɔ wú achyɛ bǒ bhɛsɛ bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri, akʉ bɔtayɛsɛ mándɔ́ bɔ̌bhap nɛfí mángú.
Ɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ manywɔp atandat, Yesu asɔt Píta, asɔt Jems nkwɔ́ nɛ manɔ ywi Jɔ̌n, akó amfay njiɛ ngo nɛ bhɔ, bábhak arɛ́ bɔ́bhɔ́.
Nɛ mbɔ Acha abhɨ́kɨ́ kpɔt manywɔp yɔ bɛ akɛ ya, mbʉ yɛ̌ nkwǎŋwaŋ amɔt apu rɔp nɛpɛ́m. Kɛ Mandɛm akpɔt mpok ɛsɔŋɔri yɔ mbɨŋ ɛ̌ti bo abhɛn yi áyábhɛ́ bɛ mambak abhi.
Mǔmpap anɛ ápɨ́ nchaŋ chi Satan. Mpok anɛ báfɛ̀rɛ mbwɔt ɛbhɨ chi nɛmǎy mmɨk, nɛ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk abhɛn báfɛ̀rɛ mbwɔt ɛbhɨ chi bɔángɛl Mandɛm.
kɛ bɛsɛ́ bho sɛchi nɛpɛ́m nɛ sɛ́bhʉɛ́t ansɛm, sɛ́nko ndǔ nɛbháŋ tɛ́mté nɛ bhɔ, sɛ́ntɛmɛri Yesu Acha ndǔ yi ásɛ̀p. Nɛ bɛbho mpok ɛyɔ, sɛ́mbak nɛ yi mpoknkɛm.
Ndǔ árɔ̀ŋ, aghɔ́ ɛnɔk fig nɛ́kú mbi. Arɔk arɛ́, kɛ yɛ̌ mɔ́sɛpɛmɛ́nɔk akɛ ghɔ́ amfay. Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ fʉɛ́t chí bɛyé bɔbhɔ. Yesu arɛm ntá ɛnɔk ɛyɔ bɛ, “Tɛ̌ mmɨk ámáy, ɔpú pɛrɛ kway mɛnyu kɛpɛm.” Ɛnɔk fig ɛyɔ ɛgu tɛ́mté.
Dɔ̌ ká bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛka mɛnkɛm ntá yi. Yí kɛ áyɨ̀ŋɨ bhe.
Nkúbhɛ́ mpok yɔ, ɛkát ɛnɛ ɛchi amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm ɛ́ghárɛ bɛbhɔk bɛpay bɛfu amfay bɛghaka amɨk. Mmɨk anyɨkɨsi, kɛtárábhɛ́ kɛ́rákáti.
Mfɔ wu arɛm ntá yi bɛ, ‘Ɔkʉ sayri, ɔchí ɛrɨ́tí nkʉbɛtɨk! Tɛ̌ndu ɔ́tɔ́ŋɔ́ ndǔ mandú ɛnyɨŋ bɛ ɔ̌bhʉ̀rɛ bariɛp, mɛ̌chyɛ̀ wɔ bɛtaŋ bɛkɛm bɛtɔk byo.’
Básɔt ɛsakámu wu bápɛtnsɛm anywɔ́p nɛ yí mbɨk nɛ bɛyǎ maŋák antɨ.
Ŋák ká nɛ mǎmbɔ́ŋ maŋák mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm abhʉ́rɛ́ bhe ɛrɛm akap awu amfay. Nɛ bǎkɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk bɛ báchyɛ̀ nyaka barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ abhɛn tɛsáy ɛsɔŋɔri nkwɔ.” 
Bɔ̌ma, tě yɛka kpirí, mǎndɔk ambɨ mɛnoko mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn sɛ́tɔ́ŋ be mpok sɛchi nɛ bhe nɛ ɛbhɛn sɛ́sɨ́ŋɨ́ amɛm bɛkáti ɛbhɛn sɛ́tó ntá yɛka.
Ndiɛrɛ yí kɛ ákway bɛpɛmɛ bhɛsɛ. Mmu achak apú fá amɨk anɛ Mandɛm achyɛ bɛ ampɛmɛ bhɛsɛ.”
Mpok yɔ, apɛ́mɛ́ Lɔt mmu achí chak, yi mmu bɛpɔ̌ barak ɛpúsí anɛ bǒ bɛbʉ́ bhɔ bákʉ̀, áchyɛ nyaka yi ɛsɔŋɔri antɨ.
Ngátí bhɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ɔ́chyɛ́ mɛ bɛ ngati bhɔ. Báká nɛ mɛ, nɛ bárɨŋɨ yɛ tɛtɛp bɛ mfu chí ntá yɛ. Mánoko nkwɔ bɛ wɔ kɛ ɔ́tó mɛ.
Bǎkway bɛ́fyɛ́ nnyɛ́n kɛ́nkwɛ́sɛ́ ndu nkwɔ́ mánkwɛ́sɛ́ abhɛn báyàŋ nɛkwak mbák arɛm agháká mamiɛ́ bɛsa bɛ́rát. Ɛnyu kɛ́nkwɛ́sɛ́ wu abhɔŋ bɛbhak chí ngɔrɛ́ anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka ndiɛrɛ nnɛ́m amɔt.
Puyɛ̌ bo abhɛn bághòk ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛbhé ɛ́ghàti bhɔ kɛ bábhàk chak bɛsí Mandɛm, chi bo abhɛn bákʉ̀ mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɛbhé ɛ́rɛ̀m kɛ bábhàk chak bɛsí bhi.
Mandɛm atǒ nyaka mmu amɔt anɛ aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Jɔ̌n.
Chi bɛbhak sayri nɛ batɨ kɛ ákʉ̀ bo abhɛn bákʉ̀ kpák ambak nɛntɨ bho mámpɨ́ mbwɔt, nɛ chɔŋ mángɔ mbwɔt mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bo bákʉ̀ ɛbhɛn bɛchi chak bɛsí Mandɛm.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Pɛt ka nsɛm ghatí Jɔ̌n mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎghókó bo bárɛ̀m, nɛ ɛbhɛn be babhɔŋ bǎghɔ.
“Stífin arɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ, nkúbhɛ́ Moses anɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ ka nyaka bɛghok yi, nɛ babhɛp yi bɛ, ‘Agha ákʉ́ wɔ mfɔ nɛ ntaŋá manyé ntá yɛsɛ?’ Mandɛm afʉɛt ntá ángɛl anɛ abhesi ntá yi ndu mɔ́nɔk bɛghati yi bɛ ándɔ́k ámbák mǔnti wap nɛ mmu anɛ áfɛrɛ bhɔ ndu ɛsɔŋɔri.
Tɛ́mté wu, bɛyǎ bo bho mankɛm bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ Yesu, bábhák maknkay tontó. Báre rɔŋ ntiɛ́t ntiɛt bɛkaka yi.
Ansɛm mpok, nsay akwɛ́n ɛtɔk Íjip ɛnkɛm nɛ ɛtɔk Kánǎn. Ɛkʉ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛya ɛcha. Bachǐmbɨ bhɛsɛ kɛkwáy bɛbhɔŋ nɛnyiɛ.
Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ běku, mpok bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk bápɛtnsɛm anywɔ́p, mbɔŋɔ́nkɨ abhɨŋɨ mmu anɛ áyɨ̀ŋɨ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk aghati yi bɛ, “Bɨŋɨ́ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk chyɛ bhɔ bakáp ayap, bɛ́bhó nɛ abhɛn bárɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛbhɨ ndɔbhɛnsɛm, bɛwɛnti nɛ abhɛn báyámbɨ.”
Nɛ yi kɛ ákɔ́rɛ́ akap ntá bho. Ntá mbɔk, achyɛ́ akap bɛbhak bǒnto. Ntá bachak, achyɛ́ akap bɛbhak barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ. Nɛ ntá abhɛnɛfu, anɛ bɛghati bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́, nɛ achyɛ́ mbɔk akap bɛbhak babhabhɛri.
“Bɔ̌ma, nɛ́nɛ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ ká bɛ́ be nɛ bǒ batí bhɛka bǎchí nyaka chi amɛm ɛjuri bɛyɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎkʉ́ ntá Yesu.
Ɛ́fákárí bɛ́ ángɛl Mandɛm áfú amfay ásɛ̀p amɨk, abɨŋɨri ntay afɛrɛ anyǔnnɛm, achɔkɔ arɛ́.
Ndǔ bɛyǎ bakap kɛ̌ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap áfɛ́rɛ́ mandú achyɛ mbɔ akap, kɛ nchɛ́bhɛ́ ngɔrɛ́ nɛ, achyɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́.” 
Kristo abhɨ́kɨ́ rɔŋ ndǔ ɛkɛrɛ́ Mandɛm ɛnɛ bághókó nɛ amɔ, ɛnɛ́ ɛ́chí ndɨ́kándi ɛkɛrákap ɛnɛ mbɔŋ awu amfay. Achwe chi amɛm mbɔŋ ɛtɛm ɛnɛ́ amfay nɛ achí arɛ nɛ́nɛ bɛsí Mandɛm, ɛ̌ti yɛsɛ.
Ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt bo Israɛl nɛmɔt, Yesu arɔk mɛ́nyiɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́ amɛm ɛkɛt ɛnɛ mǔnti amɔt anɛ achi mǔnkwɔ Fárisi. Bo Fárisi bhɔ bátɛp yi amɨ́k amʉɛt bɛghɔ ndǔ yi ákʉ̀.
Bátɛ́mti mbɔk nɛ batay baway, bákpɔ́t abhɛ́nɛ́fú mbɨŋ ɛpay nɛ nsɔ̌. Báwáy báchák nɛ bɔ akparɛnja. Mbɔk yap báré kɔ nɛ nkwɔbhɛ́mɛ́n amʉɛt mbɔ ɛyap ndɛn, nɛ babhak ndu kɛchɛp. Bo báré chyɛ bhɔ nɛnyok nɛ bɛsɔŋɔri mɛnyu nɛ mɛnyu.
Ɛwak ɛ́mɔ́t, ɛnɛ́ sɛ́rɔ̀ŋ ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt, sɛ́tɛ́mɛri mɔ́ngɔsɔ́ŋ anɛ áchi nsɛm. Ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́ɛbʉ ɛbhak nɛ yi ɛ́kʉ́ are rɛ́m mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́bhɔŋɔ bɛfakari. Ɛyɔ ɛ́chyɛ̀ nyaka bo abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ yí bɛyǎ nkáp.
Mbák ntwɔ́ awu nɛ mbɔk bǒnkwɔ Masidónia ɛnɛ́ bǎbhɨkɨ re toŋti mmʉɛt sayri, chɔŋ mbɔ̌ŋ bɛyǎ ntíánwɔ́p mbɔnyunɛ ngátí bhɔ́ ɛnyǔ nsɨkɨ ntɨ nɛ bhe. Mbák ɛ́mfákárí nɔ, ntíánwɔ́p ɛnɛka nɛ́ya mbɔŋ nɛ́ncha.
Mfɔ wu aghati yi bɛ ‘Wɔ nkʉbɛtɨk mbʉ́mbʉ, ɛyɔŋɔ́nyu yɛ ɛ́way wɔ! Ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ nchí mmu mbeápak. Ɔrɨŋɨ bɛ́ nchí sɔt ɛnɛ́ ɛ́pú ɛya, nɛ nchí ghɛm ɛnɛ́ mbɨ́kɨ́ pɨ, pú nɔ́?
Bárɔ́k yɛ ambɨ bɛyaŋ mbi bɛkɛm yi. Bátó baghokotǐ kɛpɨ ntá yi bɛ mánkɔt ngɛpti bɛ bachi bǒ tɛtɛp. Kɛ bárɔ̌ŋ nyaka chi bɛ mámbɛ́bhɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ yi mɛnyɨŋ kpát ankwɛ́n anyu, ankwɛ́n ndǔ ntǎ yap bɛ mansɔt yi manto ntá Gɔ́bhanɔ Rom mmǔ bɛtaŋ mɛnkɛm bɛchi yi amɔ.
Tɔ́ŋ yɛ̌ nɛŋɔkɔ́ baghɔrɛ́ abhɛn bákòŋo bhɔ́ ansɛm bɛ mánkɔŋ manɛ́m abhap nɛ bɔ̌bhap.
Jɔ̌n arɛm ntá Yesu bɛ, “Ɛta, sɛ́ghɔ mmu anɛ apu ndǔ nkwɔ ywɛsɛ ndu ábòk bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ ndǔ nnyɛ́n ɛna, sɛ́gháti yi bɛ, ákɛ́pɛrɛ kʉ nɔ mbɔnyunɛ apú ndǔ nkwɔ ywɛsɛ.”
Akuri amɨk. Asá nɔ́kɔ́ amɨ́k awu amɛm, aghɔ́ bɛbhɔ́k ɛ́síɛndɛn arɛ kɛ akɛ chwe amɛm.
Batɔŋɔ́ nse bhɔ́ báchi chi babhok manyiɛp anɛ manyiɛp ápú nyáy arɛ. Báchí mbɔ nɛbháŋ ɛnɛn mbʉ́ɛ́p ápɔ̀kɔ nɛ manyiɛp kɛfú arɛ ánkwɛ́n. Mandɛm aghókó ɛbhak ɛnɛ ɛ́giri pyɔɔ abhʉrɛ ntá yap.
‘Mmɛ kɛ nchí Mandɛm bachǐmbɨ bhɛka, Mandɛm Ábraham, Mandɛm Áisek, nɛ Mandɛm Jekɔ́p.’ Nɛ́kóŋó nɛ́kɛ́m Moses, afɛrɛ amɨ́k arɛ.
Bǎkɛ́ nyiɛ ɛkɔŋ nɛ mmɨk, nɛ yɛ̌ chí mɛnyɨŋɨ́ mmɨk. Ɛkɔŋ Ɛta ɛpu amɛm ntɨ mmu anɛ ányìɛ ɛkɔŋ nɛ mmɨk.
“Mpok yɔ, bǒ abhɛn bachi atú Judɛ́ya mámbʉ́ɛ́, mámbɛ́sɛ́ amfǎy njiɛ.
Sɛ́ghɔ̌ nɛ amɨ́k, nɛ sɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ Ɛta ato Mɔ́ywi Yesu fá amɨk mbɔ Mpɛmɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎbhɛ́bhɛ́ ndǔ nnyɛ́n ɛna, chɔŋ nkʉ yɔ́ bɛ́ bo mángɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mmɔ́ ákʉ̀ nɛ mánchyɛ Ɛta kɛnókó ɛ̌ti Mɔ́ywi.
Ngátí bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ mǎmbát mmʉɛt nɛ mɛ mǎmbɔ́ŋ kpák amɛm batɨ ayɛka. Chɔŋ mǎmbɔŋ bɛsɔŋɔri fá amɨk, kɛ bɔ́ŋ ká nɛtaŋántɨ́, nnáŋ mfɔ́kɔ́rí mmɨk.”
Barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ mankɛm bárɛ̀m nyaka ɛ̌ti yi bɛ, yɛ̌ agha anɛ asɨkɨ ntɨ nɛ Yesu, Mandɛm ǎfoŋori bɛbʉ́ ɛbhi ɛ̌ti yi Yesu.” 
Mmǔ anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ ka bɛ Mmɔ achi Mpɛmɛ anɛ Mandɛm átó apú kway bɛbhak mmu Ɛta. Kɛ mmǔ anɛ árɛ̀m kpoŋoroŋ bɛ Yesu achi Mmɔ̌ Ɛta, abhɔŋ nɛbharɛ́mʉɛt nɛ Ɛta.
Bábhó bɛsɔkɔti yi mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Wɔ kɛ ɔ́chí nkoŋo ywi, bɛsɛ sɛ́chí chí bakoŋo Moses.
Kɛ Pɔ̌l ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, aghati mǔnti batɛmɛ́ nɛnu nɛ bǒbhi bɛ, “Mbák bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk abhɛn áchwí mámfú, yɛ̌ mmú ywɛka apú pɛ́m.”
Páílet abhɛ́p bɔ́ bɛ, “Bǎyaŋ mfɛ́rɛ́ Mfɔ bo Israɛl amɔ bɛ yi andɔkɔ?”
Mpok Moses ánáŋá ághátí bho bɛbhé Mandɛm mɛnkɛm, asɔt ntábhɛ́nɔk hysɔp, anɛp babyɔk mmɛ́n amɛn achi chu arɛ. Asɔt manoŋ mɔ́mpɔŋ nɛ amɛn mmɛ́n, achɔpti nɛ manyiɛp. Asɔt yɛ ntábhɛ́nɔk hysɔp wu, atap amɛm manoŋ mɔ, amyakati ndǔ ɛkáti bɛbhé nɛ amʉɛt bo mankɛm.
Kaká ká Hɛródion ntɨ mmu Israɛl wa. Kaká ká nkwɔ bo ɛfo Nasísɔs abhɛn bábhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Acha.
Bǎbhɔŋ bɛrɨŋɨ bɛ mbák mbɔŋɔ́kɛt arɨ́ŋɨ́ mpok anɛ ngɛ́p átwɔ̀ ɛkɛt ɛyi, apú bhʉɛrɛ kɛnɔ́. Ǎbhak pě, bɛ ngɛ́p akɛ twɔ andak ɛkɛt.
Mfɔ Hɛ́rɔd aghók ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm, mbɔnyunɛ bo mánáŋ bárɨŋɨ nyaka nnyɛ́n Yesu mbǎnkɛm. Mbɔk bárɛ̀m nyaka bɛ, “Jɔ̌n Njwiti kɛ ápɛ́rɛ́nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ̌ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay.”
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ, chɔŋ mbɔk bho abhɛn báchí ansɛm nɛ́nɛ mándɔp bǒmbɨ, nɛ abhɛn báchí bǒmbɨ mandɔp ansɛm.” 
Yesu apɛt aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Tá ká batú ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎghòk! Ɛnyu ɔ́yɛ̀nti ɔnchyɛ ntɨ, nkúbhɛ́ ɛnyu yɔ̌ kɛ báyɛ̀nti mánchyɛ wɔ. Bápɛrɛ́ chyɛ wɔ, mámaka ɛ́chák arɛ́,
Bě nkwɔ bǎbhɔŋ bɛtoŋti mmʉɛt Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm átwɔ̀ chɔŋ chi ndǔ mpok anɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ kaysi bɛ yi ǎtwɔ̀.” 
Jɔ̌n Njwiti atwɔ nyaka antarɛ nɔkɔ nsay ndu mɛnɨkmʉɛt nɛ mmɛm yi kɛ nyu. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu are rɛm bɛ, ‘Ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛchi nɛ yi!’
Mpok achi anɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ nyaka ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛbhé ɛ́yàŋ bo mankʉ. Kɛ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ɛbhé, ngɔ́ bɛ nnáŋ nkwɛn nyaka ɛbhé, nɛ ngú.
Nɛ mbɔ̌ŋ bɛghɔ bɛ mpok nnáŋ ndɔ́ mmɨk, mǎntɨk nɔ́kɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mpoknkɛm. 
Sɛ́pú yɨŋɨ yɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bo bághɔ̀ nɛ amɨ́k. Sɛ́yɨ̀ŋɨ chi ɛbhɛn bápú ghɔ, mbɔnyunɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bo baghɔ bɛ́fʉɛrɛ fʉɛt. Ɛbhɛn bápú ghɔ kɛ bɛbhak mpoknkɛm.
Nɛ tɛ̌ndu sɛ́bhɔŋɔ Nnɛ́m Nchiakap nɛ yi kɛ ákɛ́mɛ́ ɛkɛrɛ́ Mandɛm,
Mpok ɛyɔ nkɛm, Sɔ̌l arɔk ambɨ bɛpa bɛ yi abhɔŋ bɛway bakoŋo Yesu. Arɔk ntá mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm,
Yɛ̌ agha anɛ áyàŋ bɛghok ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ́rɛ̀m, ántá batú ángók sayri.
Akap anɛ bǒ Mandɛm bábhɔ̀ŋ áchí mɛnyu nɛ mɛnyu, kɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ́ amɔt kɛ̌ áchyɛ̀ akap ankɛm.
Nɛ chɔŋ ɔ́mbɔ́ŋ bɛyǎ maŋák; nɛ bɛyǎ bo mámbɔŋ maŋák mpok bábhé yi.
Natániɛl ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Fílip árɛ́mɛ́ abhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ntɨkɨ ɛrɨ́tí ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́kway bɛfu Násárɛt?” Fílip aghati yi bɛ, “Wɔmbɔŋ twɔ́ ghɔ́.”
Mbakanɛm anɛ yɛ̌ ǎnɨ̀k chí mmʉɛt yɛ̌ ǎghati chí bho mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fú ntá Mandɛm, mbák ǎkʉ̀ nɔ ntí kútí, nɔ apú chyɛ Kristo mǔnti ywi kɛnókó.
Nchí kʉ nyaka mbɔ bǒ mmɨk kɛ? Mmǔ mmɨk kɛ árɛ̀m ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mɔt ankʉ chi ɛ́chák.
“Nɛ chɔŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́nkʉ bɛ nkaysi anɛ achi bo ántɨ ambo bɛfú kpoŋoroŋ, nɛ wɔ ɔ́mbɔŋ bɛyǎ basɛ́mɛ́ ɛ̌ti mɔ́nɛ mbɔ mmu anɛ ɛɛkak ɛ́yɛ́mɛ́ yi antɨ.”
Mpok yɔ, bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɔ ntínso Mandɛm nɛmbak nɛ bhe kɛ nɛ́nɛ, bǎrɔ ntínso Mandɛm nɛmbak nɛ bhe. 
Nɛ chɔŋ Mandɛm amfoŋori yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ árɛ̀m ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm, kɛ apú foŋori mmu anɛ árɛ̀m ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ.
Mbɔ bǎchí bǒ mmɨk, mbʉ́ mmɨk akɔŋ be nɛ ntí bɛ́ bǎchí bo bhi. Kɛ ndǔ njábhɛ́ bhe mfɛ́rɛ́ nɛ́ntɨ bǒ mmɨk, ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ̌ bápábhɛ́ be.
Ɛnɛ́ mányìɛ nɛnyíɛ́, Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Dɨŋɨ́ ká tɛtɛp bɛ mmu ywɛka amɔt ǎti chɔŋ mɛ. Yí wu achi fá nɛ mɛ ǎnyiɛ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnɛn.”
Mpok Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm ntwɔ́, nde nyiɛ, nnyú nɔkɔ. Běka bǎre rɛm bɛ, ‘Ghɔ́ ká yi awu, nyiɛ̌ mɛnyɨŋɨ́nyíɛ́ nɛ nyǔmɛm. Mamʉɛrɛ bhi chi babhɛbhɛ́ nkábhɛ́nti nɛ bakʉ̌ bɛbʉ́ bachak!’
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ápàp ntɨ achí ngwayti bho. Nɛ bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti nɛ́pú bhak nɛ ngwayti bho.
Batɨ bǒ-nsé nɛ bǒ bapu bhɔ ájwi nɛ ɛjuri nɛ básɔ̀t mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fú ntá bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛtɔŋ bo.
Bǒbati bo Judeya báré yaŋ yi arɛ́ mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Yi achí fá?”
Bátwɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́, aghati bhɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ángɛl Mandɛm árɛ́mɛ́. Ató yɛ bɔ́ ɛtɔk Jopa.
Nywɔp nɛmɔt Yesu arɛm ntá baghɔkɔ́ bhi bɛ, “Sɛ́mpé sɛ́ndɔ́k ɛbhě manyu ɛ́nɛ awu.” Báchwe amɛm áchwí nɛ yi bábhó mɛnok mandɔkɔ nɔkɔ.
Mfá nɔ́kɔ́ Yerúsalɛm, ndɔk nkó atú Síria nɛ atú Silísha nkwɔ.
Nɛ mpok nchí awu nɛ bhe nkɛ bhɔŋ nkáp mbɨ́kɨ́ chyɛ yɛ̌ mmu ywɛka ɛsɔŋɔri mbɔnyunɛ batɨ bɔ̌mayɛsɛ abhɛn báfú atú Masidónia kɛ báchyɛ̀ nyaka mɛ nɛkwak. Mbɨ́kɨ́ chyɛ bhe ntu wa bɛ mǎmpɔkɔ wáwák. Nɛ ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ nchí bhak.
Mpú rɛm chi bɛ mmu achi anɛ anaŋ aghɔ Ɛtaya. Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm kɛ ánáŋ ághɔ́ yi.
Nkɔŋ bě mankɛm. Sɛ́rɔp chi ndǔ nsoŋ amɔt ndu sɛ́bhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Kristo.
Mmǔ anɛ árɛ̀m bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛbhɛn yi ábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ, ǎchyɛ̀ chi mmʉɛt yi bɛtaŋ. Kɛ mmu anɛ ághàti bho Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ǎchyɛ̀ batɨ bǒnkwɔ bɛtaŋ Mandɛm.
Mbák be bǒ bɛbʉ́, bǎbhɔŋ ntɨ bɛchyɛ bɛrɨ́tɨ́ mɛnyɨŋ ntá bɔ̌bhɛka, bǎkáysí bɛ Ɛtayɛka mmu achi amfay kɛ anɔk bɛbhɔŋ bɛyǎ ɛkɔŋ ndu bɛchyɛ bɛrɨ́tɨ́ mɛnyɨŋ ntá bǒ abhɛn mǎnɨ̀kmʉɛt kɛ?
Bɛyǎ bo abhɛn bachi arɛ́ téé bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ ɛyɔŋ ɛyɔ, bare rɛm bɛ, “Nɛfaŋ kɛ ásáy!” Báchák bɛ, “Ángɛl Mandɛm árɛ̀m kɛpɨ nɛ yi.”
Wɔ, ɔchí sɛtárɛ́bhɛ́,   nɛ ndǔ sɛtárɛ́bhɛ́ ɛsɛ́n kɛ nchí te ɛkɛt ɛya.   Nɛ yɛ̌ chí bɛtaŋá nɛwú bɛ́pú kway bɛtaŋ mɛncha nkwɔ bo Mandɛm.
Achák akwɛnti ndǔ mmɨk sɛtárɛ́bhɛ́ nɛ mpok ácháká, anɨŋti, awɔsi, mbɔnyunɛ nɛbhʉɛ́rɛ́mɨk wu apu kɛm manyiɛp.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ mɛ̌yaŋ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛna nɛ ntɨ ɛna nɛnkɛm nɛ ɛnɛ́ mbákántɨ arɛ́ chi bɛ nkɛ́ kʉ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ̀ ntíánwɔ́p ánkɛm mɛ. Mɛ̌yàŋ chi bɛ mbɔ́ŋ nɛtaŋántɨ mpoknkɛm bɛ nɛ́nɛ, nɛ yɛ̌ chi ndǔ mpok anɛ átwɔ̀ ambɨ, nɛtaŋántɨ ɛna nɛ́nchyɛ́ Kristo kɛnókó, yɛ̌ ngǔgú, yɛ̌ nchí chí nɛpɛ́m.
Sɛ́mbɨ́tí Mandɛm. Yi ǎkway bɛkʉ be mǎntáŋ ndǔ nɛka ɛnɛka bɛkoŋo Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ mɛ̌ghàti bo ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo nɛ bɛkoŋo tɛtɛp anɛ nchí ghati bho. Yɔ́ achí nyaka bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ ndǔ ɛrɔri mpok kɛ Mandɛm ákʉ́ sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ yɔ.
“Bě bo Korasín, chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛ́p ntá yɛka ɛncha! Bě bo Bɛtsáida, chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛ́p ntá yɛka nkwɔ ɛncha! Mbɔ chí amɛm bɛtɔk Táya nɛ Sídɔn kɛ nkʉ́ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛbhɛn-nɛ nkʉ ntá yɛka, mbʉ́ báfyɛ́ ndɛn pyɔ, mánto batwɔ́p anti tɛsáy, bɛtɔŋ bɛ bátɨ̀knsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhap!
Bápú bǒ mmɨk nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ mpú mmǔ mmɨk.
Ɛ́kʉ, akɔ aghaka ɛtɔk Samária ɛnɛ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ́ Síka, kɛ́kwɔ́t nɛ nɛbhʉɛ́rɛ́mɨk anɛ Jekɔ́p áchyɛ tɛntɛp ntá mɔ́ywi Josɛ́f.
Bǒbhɔ bábho bɛbɨk mandɛm nɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋ kɛkuri kɛkuri ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ mbɔk bárɛ̀m ɛyap ɛnyu, báchák mándɛm nɔkɔ ɛyap. Ɛbyɔk ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ mǔngo batɛmɛ́ nɛnu kɛ́kɛm ntí nɛ nnɛt ndǔ ndak anɛ áfákárí. Aghati bǒbhi bɛ́ mansɔt Pɔ̌l mandɔk mamfyɛ amɛm ɛbhǎ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu.
Nɛ yɛ̌ mmú apú kwáy bɛrɛm yɛ̌ bɛ, ‘Ghɔ́ ká Mandɛm fa nɛ bho mbɔ Mfɔ wap!’ Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ Mandɛm anáŋ achi Mfɔ ndǔ nkwɔ ywɛka.”
Mbák ɛ́pú nɔ, mbák mmu ywɛka ǎnɨ̀kmʉɛt bɛchyɛ bakak ntá Mandɛm ndu ɛfóŋó, ná mmu anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ ɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛnɛ yi árɛ̀m ǎkway bɛka bɛ, “Amen” ɛnɛ́ yi ábhɨ́kɨ́ jwimɛm?
Mbák chi bakoŋo Yesu abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl, sɛ́to bɔ bɛkáti ndu bɛ́gháti bhɔ́ bɛ́ bákɛ́ nyiɛ́ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛnɛ báchyɛ́ ntá mandɛm nsé mbɔ akap. Nɛ bɛ́ bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ mɛ́nyiɛ́ manoŋ nɛ nnya anɛ manoŋ ami ábhɨ́kɨ́ rɔŋ amɨk, nɛ bɛ́ bǎkɛ́ fyɛ amɔ ndǔ barak ɛpúsí.”
Bɔ̌ma, mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nɛ́ mɛ̌ghati bhe bɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ mɛ nɛ Apólos. Ntí achí bɛ mǎngɔ́k ɛnyɨŋ arɛ́, ndu bɛ́kóŋó chí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ básɨ́ŋɨ́ amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm. Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ rɨ́ bɛ́ mǎmpányu ɛ̌ti mbɔk bǒbatí, mǎmbyaka nɔkɔ báchák.
Ngɔ́ ɛrɛm ɛrɨŋ nɛ ɛrɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛchak amfay. Ngɔ́ bɔángɛl tándrámɔt, nɛ bɛghori tándrámɔt ɛbhɛn bɛchi bɛghori ɛbhɛn ngwɛnti mbɔnyunɛ bɔ kɛ bɛtɔŋ bɛběntɨ Mandɛm ɛbhɛn bɛ́twɔ̀ ndǔ ngwɛnti.
Nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ sɛ́chí mbɔ mmu anɛ bághókó nɛ ntɔp nɛ́nɛ, mpok ǎtwɔ̀ anɛ sɛ́bhak mbɔ mmu anɛ áfú amfay.
chi-bɛtɨk ywi ǎtwɔ̀ ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɛn mǔbɛtok abhɨkɨ kaysi bɛ yí ǎtwɔ̀ nɛ ndǔ nɛŋɔkɔ́ nywɔp ɛnɛn mǔbɛtok wu abhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ. Antɛmsi yi, amfyɛ yi nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ noko Mandɛm bachi.
Bo abhɛn báyàŋ bɛbhɔŋ bɛyǎ nkáp báwakari bɛkwɛn ndǔ nɛmɔ, mánkwɛn ndu ntá nɛ nkaysi anɛ átwɔ̀ bhɔ́ nɛ mɛ́nɛ́mɛ́ nɛ nɛwú.
Yɛ̌ nɔ́, Píta arɛm bɛ, “Yɛ̌ chí nɛwú, chɔŋ ngu nɛ wɔ. Mpú bʉɛ wɔ.” Baghɔk Yesu báchák mankɛm bárɛ́m chí ɛnyumɔt. 
Kɛ nchí rɔŋ kpɨk Yerúsalɛm bɛ nchyɛ́ nɛkɛp ɛnɛ́n batɨ̌ bǒnkwɔ bátó ntá bo Mandɛm abhɛn bachi arɛ.
Bǒbhɔ kɛ bachi pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí Mandɛm mbɔnyunɛ babhɨkɨ nyɔ́p mmʉɛt ndǔ baraká kɛbhʉrɛ nɛ baghɔrɛ́. Bɔ́ kɛ bákòŋo Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ yi árɔ̀ŋ. Bɔ́bhɔ kɛ Mandɛm ápɛmɛ ndǔ nkwɔ bǒ mmɨk bɛ mámbak ntá yi nɛ ntá Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n.
Abhɛn ɛkɔŋ, bǎkɛ́ rɔ yɛ̌ mmu ándwɔ́ bhé bɛ́ Mandɛm kɛ̌ átò mmu nɛmɔ.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bábhɛ́bhɛ́ ndǔ nnyɛ́n ɛna, chɔŋ nkʉ yɔ nta yɛka.” 
Arɛm yɛ ntá Yesu bɛ, “Chɔŋ nchyɛ́ wɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm mbák ɔ́ntɛ́p mánɛ́n bɛsí bha, ɔnchyɛ mɛ kɛnókó.”
Bafɔ̌ mmɨk nɛ manɛ́m bho, nɛ bǒbatí batɛmɛ́ nɛnu, nɛ bǒ bakáp, nɛ bɛtaŋtí bho, nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu achák, yɛ̌ chí abhɛn bachí basɛm, nɛ yɛ̌ chi abhɛn bapu basɛm, bábʉ́ɛ́ bábhɛ́sɛ amɛm bɔbasɛm,   kɛtárábhɛ́ ndǔ njiɛ ɛgho.
Bě manɛ́m nkwɔ, mǎnkɛ́m nɔ́kɔ́ baghɔrɛ́ bhɛka sayri, mǎnchyɛ nɔkɔ bɔ́ kɛnókó mbɔ bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ mbɔ bhe. Bě nɛ bhɔ bǎbhɔŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn Mandɛm achyɛ ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhi. Kʉ nɔ́kɔ́ ká nɔ bɛ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛkɛ chyɛt nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt ɛnɛka. 
Básɔt Yesu bárɔ́k ntá mǔngo bachiǎkap Mandɛm. Bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ bo batí ɛtɔk nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses báchɛm arɛ́.
Yesu mmu ákʉ́ bo mandɨŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn árɛ̀m bɛ, “Nchí twɔ́ mandú mpok!” Amen. Yesu Acha, twɔ́!
Ɛwak ɛ́mɔt, nkwɔ́ bachiǎkap anɛ́ Sakaría bábhák ndǔ bɛtɨk. Ɛkʉ Sakaría are kʉ bɛtɨk mbɔ nchiakap bɛsí Mandɛm.
Yi arɛm nyaka bɛ, chɔŋ mámfyɛ Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm amɔ́ bǒ bɛbʉ́, mángó yi ndǔ ɛkotákátí, nɛ ɛ́ghaka nɔkɔ manywɔp arat, ampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.”
Mpǎy bo abhɛn mányú nku yɔ báchá bɛsa bɛ́pay.
Kɛ mbɔk ɛyap báchók batú kɛnoko ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Pɔ̌l árɛ̀m. Báré rɛm chí bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti mbi Acha bɛsí bo mankɛm. Ndu bákʉ̀ nɔ Pɔ̌l asɔt bo abhɛn mánókó arɔk nɛ bhɔ́, ankɛm nɔkɔ ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ bhɔ ɛ̌ti Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm amɛm áchá Tiránɔs yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nywɔp.
Mmɔ̌ bɛtok wu aghati yí bɛ ‘Mɔmáyɛ apɛtnsɛm, kɛ ɛtayɛ áway mɔ́sɛnɛ́ mpɔŋ mbɔnyunɛ́ apɛtnsɛm dok.’
Arɛm ɛnyu ɛyɔ mbɔnyunɛ Yesu asay nyaka ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛnɛ ɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri yi bɛ ɛ́ndɔ́ yi. Bɛyǎ mpok, ɛfóŋó yɔ ɛ́fate nyaka yi amʉɛt, nɛ yɛ̌ bákɛm yi báfyɛ ngɛm amɔ nɛ bɛkak, mámbabhɛri nɔkɔ yi, ǎkɨti ngɛm ɛyɔ, ɛfóŋó ɛyɔ ɛ́nkʉ yi ambʉ́ɛ́ anchwe amɛm baso.
Báchwɔ́bhɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ Antiɔk, babhɨŋɨ Bǒ nkwɔ́ Yesu báchɛm nɛbhʉɛt amɔt. Bágháti bhɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn bɔ bákʉ́ ndu bɛtaŋ Mandɛm, nɛ ɛnyu Mandɛm ánɛ́nɛ́ mbi bɛ́ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl mánsɨ́kɨ́ ntɨ nɛ Yesu.
Yesu ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyǔ nɛka ɛnɛ́n bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ yi, aghati mbɛ́ntí wu bɛ, “Mɔ́wa, mfóŋórí bɛbʉ́ bhɛ.”
Sɛ́ghok nkwɔ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ bo abhɛn tɛntɛp bághókó nyaka. Kɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bɔ bághòk ɛ́kɛ kwak bhɔ mbɔnyunɛ batɨ yap apu nyaka arɛ.
Ɛchí tɛtɛp mbɔ ɛnyu bárɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Mmu bɛ́pɨ ǎpɨ, anɛ bɛghɛm angɛm.’
Mandɛm achi Mandɛm chi ndiɛrɛ ntá bo Israɛl? Apu Mandɛm bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl? Achi Mandɛm bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl nkwɔ.
Sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m ɛ́pú kway bɛwupsi ɛnyu. Mbák Mandɛm abhɨŋɨ nyaka bo abhɛn bághòk ɛyɔŋ ɛyi bɛ bɔmandɛm,
Ɛta Tiófilɔs, ndǔ ɛkáti ɛya ɛnɛ mbɨ, nsɨŋ ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛ́n Yesu ákʉ́ nɛ ɛbhɛn yi atɔŋɔ bɛbho mpok yi ábhó bɛtɨk ɛbhi fá amɨk,
Bábhɨ́ŋɨ́ nɔ́kɔ́ yɛ bǒnto Yesu, badɛn bɔ, básɛ́mti bhɔ bɛ bákɛ́pɛrɛ rɛm yɛ̌nyɨŋ ndu nnyɛ́n Yesu, barɔ bɔ mándɔ́k.
Ɛ́tárɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, bǒfú básɔt mbók bárɔ́k ntá Yesu nɛ yi. Ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ kɛ ɛ́kʉ́ nyaka amɨ́k anɛ́mɛ́ yi nɛ akwɛ́n kɛbhok. Yesu abú yí, abho bɛrɛm kɛpɨ, nɛ abho bɛghɔ mbaŋ.
Kɛmɛ́ ká ntá bǒ ɛtɔk Bábilɔn yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbɛ́ptí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bɔ bákʉ́ ntá bo bachak. Kɛmɛ́ ká ntá yap ndɔŋ ɛpay yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bɔ bákʉ́ bǒ bachak. Chyɛ ká bhɔ mmɛ́m amɛn bátáŋá ndɔŋ ɛpay ndǔ nkɔ́p anɛ bɔ́ báfyɛ́ mmɛ́m bataŋbataŋ amɛm báchyɛ́ bhe.
Bɛyǎ bó abhɛn bághókó bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn, mánóko yi. 
Fílip átwɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɛ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti ɛnyu Mandɛm abhak nɛ bǒbhi mbɔ Mfɔ wap nɛ ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo, baghɔrɛ́ nɛ babhakanɛm bábho mɛ́nóko mándɔkɔ nɔkɔ bɛ mánjwiti bhɔ́.
Ɛ́nɔk mmu achi nyaka ndǔ mkpák bachǐmbɨ bhɛsɛ tándrámɔt bɛbho amʉɛt Adam anáŋ arɛm nyaka tɛmbɨ ɛ̌ti bǒbhɛn bɛ, “Acha ǎtwɔ̀ nɛ ngɛ́mtáy bɔángɛl Mandɛm.
Nchí ghati bhe bɛ, bɛyǎ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ nɛ bafɔ babhɔ̌ŋ nyaka ɛkwak bɛghɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎghɔ̀, kɛ bɔ kɛghɔ bhɔ. Bábhɔ́ŋ ɛkwak bɛghok mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎghòk, kɛ bábhɨkɨ ghok bhɔ.” 
Ɛyɔ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bhɛsɛ bɛ bɛrɛm kɛpɨ ndǔ bɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛbhɛn bo bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ, chí ɛrɨŋ ntá bo abhɛn babhɨkɨ noko Yesu Kristo, puyɛ̌ ntá bo abhɛn mánóko. Kɛ akap bɛghati bho mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fú ntá Mandɛm, chí ɛrɨŋ ntá bo abhɛn mánóko.
Mfɔ wu achyɛ ɛyɔŋ nɛ bɛyǎ bɛběntɨ́, bɛ mánsɔt yi mǎmɛ́sɛ ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ bɛ́ mbák abhɨ́kɨ́ kɛmɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ákɛ́mɛ́, apu fú arɛ.”
Yɛ̌ mɔbɛtok apu kwáy bɛtok bachi batí apay ndɔŋ amɔt. Mbák ámbɔ́ŋ bachi bapay, ǎkɔŋ amɔt ancha anɛfú, mbák ɛ́pú nɔ́, ǎchyɛ kɛnókó ntá amɔt, ambyak anɛfu. Mmu apu kwáy bɛtok Mandɛm antok nɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋ mmɨk.” 
Kɛ mmu anɛ ányù manyiɛp amɛn mɛ̌chyɛ̀, apú pɛrɛ bhɔŋ ɛkwaká manyiɛp wáwák. Manyiɛp amɛn mɛ̌chyɛ̀ yi, ǎbhák ntá yi mbɔ ntí mɔ́nyɛn anɛ́ manyiɛp ányày arɛ, anchyɛ nɔkɔ yi nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.”
Bǒ abhɛn bábhàbhɛri bakók, bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, bábʉɛ́, bárɔk ndǔ ɛtɔk ɛnɛ ɛchi kɛkwɔt, baghati bho yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ nɛ ɛnyǔ ɛ́fákárí nɛ bǒ abhɛn bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri nyaka bhɔ.
Kɛ nchí ghati bhe bɛ, kɔŋ ka bǒmpap abhɛka, mǎnɨk nɔkɔ mmʉɛt bɛ Mandɛm ankwak bǒ abhɛn báchyɛ̀ bhe ɛsɔŋɔri.
Bɛ́kóŋo ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mbɔŋ Yesu Acha árɛ́mɛ́, sɛ́ghàti bhe bɛ mpok Yesu Acha átwɔ́, bɛsɛ́ bho sɛchi nɛpɛ́m sɛ́pú yambɨ bɛ́tɛ́mɛri yi kɛ abhɛn bágú mántɛmɛri yi.
Ndɛm yɛ bɛ, “Ɛta Mandɛm, ghɔ́ mɛ́ nɛ. Ntwɔ bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ wɔ ɔ́yàŋ mɛnkʉ́ nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ basɨŋɨ ɛ̌ti ya amɛm ɛkáti ɛyɛ.”
Nchí nɨkmʉɛt bɛ Mandɛm ántɔ́ŋ bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhi ntá bǒ mankɛm abhɛn bákɔ́ŋɔ́ Yesu Kristo Acha nɛ ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ ɛpu gu manyiɛp.
Nnɛ́m ɛnyɨŋ ntá bo abhɛn Mandɛm achi Mfɔ wap puyɛ̌ chi nɛnyíɛ́ mɛnyiɛ nɛ mmɛm mɛnyu. Nnɛ́m ɛnyɨŋ chi bɛbhak chak bɛsí Mandɛm, nɛ bɛbhak kpák nɛ batɨ, nɛ bɛbhɔŋ maŋák amɛn Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ áchyɛ̀.
Ɛ́kʉ bábho bɛbwɔpti batay bɛtɛmti yi nɛ yɔ́ mángwáy, kɛ Yesu abhɛsɛ, tɛ áfú amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm.
Mandɛm ághátí Rɛbɛ́ka bɛ, “Chɔŋ mɔ̌mbɨ ántók anɛ mɔ́nkwɛn.”
Bǒ nnɛrɛ́kɛt ywi bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, bábho bɛrɔŋ ndu bɛsɔt yi mbɔnyunɛ bárɛ̀m nyaka bɛ, “Nti átáká yi amɛm!”
Bɛsɛ́ nɛ Pɔ̌l sɛ́rɔ́ bǒbatí nkwɔ́ Ɛ́fɛsɔs. Achwi ápɔ́kɔ bhɛsɛ́ sɛ́pé sɛrɔk téé sɛ́gháká ndǔ ɛtɔk ɛnɛ nnyɛ́n nɛkabhɛ ɛnɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ Kós. Nɛ́yí nɔkɔ sɛ́rɔ́k sɛ́chwɔ́p Ródes. Sɛ́fú nɔ́kɔ́ árɛ́ sɛ́rɔ́k sɛ́gháka Patara.
Ayɨkɨ arɛm bɛ, “Mpú nɔ́k bɛ́yɛt wɔ, nɛ chɔŋ nchyɛ́ wɔ bɛyǎ bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ.”
Nchí nɨk yɛ be mmʉɛt bɛ mǎmpɛt mǎnkʉ yi angɔ bɛ bǎkɔŋ yi tɛtɛp.
Kɛ ndǔ bábhɨkɨ ghɔ bɔPɔ̌l, báyá Jáson nɛ bǒnkwɔ́ Yesu báchák gbaka gbaka gbaka bárɔ́k ntá bǒbatí ɛtɔk nɛ bhɔ, mambɨkɨ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Bǒ abhɛn bákɔ̀ mbǎnkɛm mánchyɛ nɔkɔ ɛsɔŋɔri bátwɔ fá nkwɔ́
Ndǔ bǎbhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ yi, bǎjwi pɔɔt. Yi kɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ amfǎy mɛnyǔ bɛfóŋó mɛnkɛm.
Bákɔ bábhʉrɛ ambi, kɛ nɛ́yí nɔ́kɔ́ báchwɔp Seséria. Kɔnéliɔs anáŋ arɨŋɨ nyaka bɛ́ Píta ǎtwɔ̀. Ató bábhɨŋɨ bǒ nnɛrɛ́kɛt nɛ mamʉɛrɛ bhi. Bɔ́ mankɛm bachɔkɔ mánoŋ nɔkɔ bɔPíta.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ákʉ̀ bɛbʉ́, chi mmu anɛ ápú bhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé Mandɛm, nɛ bɛ́kʉ bɛbʉ́ chí bɛkwɛn bɛbhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé Mandɛm.
Ɛ́rɨ ɛcha ntá yɛ́ mbɔnyunɛ ɔnókó bɛ́ chɔŋ Mandɛm ankʉ ntá yɛ mbɔ ɛnyu yí árɛ́mɛ́.” 
bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ámbák ndǔ mmʉɛt ɛyi kɛbhɔ́ŋ ngɔrɛ́ mbɔ mɛ, kɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu abhɔŋ aywi akap anɛ́ Mandɛm áchyɛ́ yi. Achyɛ́ mbɔk akap bɛ́bhɔŋ nɛbhay, achyɛ báchák chí akap bɛ́chɔ́kɔ ndǔ mmʉɛt ɛyap kɛbháy nɛbhay.
Twɔ́ ká mǎnyiɛ nyamwʉɛ́t bafɔ nɛ nyamwʉɛ́t bǒbati nɛ anɛ manɛ́m bho nɛ nyamwʉɛ́t batɛmɛ́ nɛnu nɛ nyamwʉɛ́t mpɔŋɔ́ndɨk nɛ bo abhɛn bákɔ̀ nyaka yɔ. Twɔ́ ká mǎnyiɛ nyamwʉɛ́t bǒ mankɛm ɛnɛ́ bo abhɛn bapu basɛm, nɛ ɛnɛ́ bo abhɛn bachi basɛm, ɛnɛ́ ndɛ́ndɛmɛ bho nɛ ɛnɛ́ manɛ́m bho.”
Yɛ̌ ɛmbak chi bɛ ɛkáti ɛnɛ́ nsɨ́ŋɨ́ bhe ɛ́kʉ́ bǎbhɔ́ŋ basɛ́mɛ́, áyɔ́mɛ apú nɛ mɛ bɛ nsɨŋ yɔ́. Ndǔ nɛbhǒnɛt mbɔ́ŋ áyɔ́mɛ mbɔnyunɛ ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ yɔ́ ɛ́chyɛ́ bhe basɛ́mɛ́, yɛ̌ndu basɛ́mɛ́ mɔ áchí chí ndǔ mɔ́mbɨŋɨ mpok.
Ngɔrɛ́ amɔt abhak arɛ́ anɛ ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ́kʉ́ yi ápɛ́nɛ́ ndǔ mamiɛ́ nɛku-nɛ-arat, yí kɛpɛrɛ kway bɛkɔ chak.
Chɔŋ bɛtɔk mɛ́nu nɛ bɛtɔk bɛ́chák, bafɔ̌ ɛtɔk mánu nɛ batɨ̌ bafɔ̌ ɛtɔk. Chɔŋ nsay ankwɛ́n mbaŋ nɛ mbaŋ, mmɨk anyɨkɨsi ndǔ bɛtɔk nɛ bɛtɔk.
Batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bábhɔ́ŋ nkaysi bɛway bǒkɛnɔŋ mankɛm bɛ yɛ̌ amɔt ákɛ́ bhɔ́ŋ mbi bɛghɔk nnyɛ́n ámbwɛ́.
Nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Jóna achi nyaka ɛrɨŋ ntá bo Ninivɛ, ɛnyu yɔ kɛ̌ Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm nchí bhak chɔŋ ɛrɨŋ ntá mkpáká bho abhɛn ɛchɔŋ.
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu abhʉɛ́t bɛrɛm nɔ nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi, ngɔ̌k aywi amɔt ndǔ abhɛn bati byo nɛ apay anɛ aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Júdas, achwɔp nɛ bɛyǎ bho. Bǒ bhɔ bábhák nɛ bɔ akparɛnja nɛ nkɨ́k amɔ. Bǒbati bachiǎkap nɛ bǒbati ɛtɔk kɛ̌ bátó nyaka bhɔ.
Mɛlkísɛdɛk-nɛ achi nyaka mfɔ ɛtɔk Salɛm nɛ nchiakap Mandɛm Acha. Ábraham anu nyaka nɛ bɛyǎ bafɔ awáy bhɔ. Mpok yi áfú ɛbhɨ̌nɛnu ápɛ̀tnsɛm, Mɛlkísɛdɛk atɛmɛri yi, ayɛ́t yi.
Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ɛ́kwàk bo mámbɔ́ŋ nɛpɛ́m. Ghatí nɔ́kɔ́ ká yɔ ntá bho. Bǎbhɔŋ bɛkʉ nɔ bɛ mbɔ́ŋ maŋák ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɛn Kristo ápɛ̀tnsɛm, nɛ bɛ ntiɛt anɛ́ njɛ́rɛ́ nɛ́ntɨ́ ɛnɛka nɛ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn nkʉ́, bɛ́kɛ́ bhak ndɛ́ndɛm.
Mbabhɛri wu arɛm bɛ́ mántwɔ́ yí nɛ ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́. Bátwɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɛ yɔ́, arɔk ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ ntiɛ́t ntiɛt akwɛ́n ndǔ bɛkak Pɔ̌l nɛ Sáilas angwɛrɛ nɔkɔ nɛ bɛcháy.
Nɛ ndǔ Mandɛm áchɛ́mɛ́ bhe nɛ Kristo, yí ákʉ́ bǎbhàt mmʉɛt nɛ bǒnkwɔ bachak mankɛm bɛ be nɛ bhɔ mǎmbák ɛkɛt ɛnɛ Mandɛm áchɔ̀kɔ arɛ bɛfʉɛt ntá bɛtaŋ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ.
Kɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm bɛ́pɛrɛ́ fákári, chɔŋ mánkɛm be, mánchyɛ ɛsɔŋɔri, mánsɔt be mandɔk amɛm bɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt ɛbhap mántaŋ be arɛ, mamfyɛ́ bhe amɛm bɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ. Nɛ chɔŋ mámfyɛ be amɔ́ bafɔ nɛ bɔgɔ́bhanɔ bɛ mántáŋ be ɛ̌ti ya.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ánókó bɛ Yesu chi Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò achi mmɔ́ Mandɛm. Nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ákɔ́ŋ chi ǎkɔ̀ŋ mɔ́ywi nkwɔ́.
Yesu afʉɛ́t yɛ are rɔŋ ndǔ ɛkɛt ɛnɛ mǔnti bo Israɛl wu. Ágháká nɔ́kɔ́ arɛ́, achwe anywɔ́p, aghɔ́ bafě babhaŋ nɛ ngɛ́mtay bho ndǔ bádì kɛbhɔ nɛ bɛyǎ ɛwat.
Bɛrɛm tɛtɛp, ǎme nyaka, kpát ɛ́rɔ́p chí nɛwú, kɛ Mandɛm aghɔ́ yi ntínso. Nɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ ghɔ chí yi aywǐnti ntínso, aghɔ mɛ nkwɔ ntínso. Mbɔ abhɨ́kɨ́ kʉ nɔ, mbʉ basɛ́mɛ́ ma aya acha.
Yesu afa yɛ atú Gálili nɛ bakoŋo bhi, bárɔk ndǔ atú ɛtɔk anɛ achi kɛkwɔt Táya nɛ Sídɔn.
Ndǔ mpok anɛ bǎchí ndu kɛsɛmɛ́ bɛbʉ́, bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ nyaka yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛkʉ nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi chak.
Bɔ̌ma, be bho Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ achi nɛ bhe, mbák mǎngɔ́ ndǔ mmu ákʉ̀ bɛbʉ́, kwák ká yí pɛtii bɛ ampɛtnsɛm ndǔ mbi Mandɛm. Nɛ ndǔ bǎkʉ̀ nɔ, sɔt ká mpok bɛ be babhɔŋ bǎkɛ kwɛn ndǔ nɛmɔ.
Bɔ bátɔ̀ŋ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bákʉ̀ bɛ Mandɛm asɨŋ bɛbhé amɛm batɨ yap. Batɨ yap átè ntísiɛ bɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́chí tɛtɛp, tɛ̌ndu mpokófu batɨ yap ághàti bhɔ bɛ babhɔŋ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ nɛ mpok achak bɛ báchí chak.
Nywɔp nɛmɔt, Yesu ǎtɔ̀ŋ nyaka bho Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm, Mandɛm Acha achyɛ yi bɛtaŋ, are bú bǒmame. Bǒnkwɔ Fárisi nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm babhak arɛ́. Báfú ndǔ bɔ̌bɛtɔk mankɛm atú Gálili, nɛ bachak báfú atú Judɛ́ya, nɛ abhɛnɛfu báfú Yerúsalɛm.
Píta ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ yi, abhɛp Yesu bɛ, “Acha, ná nɛ anɛ?”
Nchí ghati bhe mankɛm, bɛ Mandɛm akɔŋ be tontó nɛ abhɨ́ŋɨ́ be bɛ mǎmbak bǒbhi. Mandɛm Ɛtayɛsɛ nɛ Yesu Kristo Acha mántɔ́ŋ be bɛrɨ̌ndu, mánchyɛ bɛ kpák. 
Nchí ghati bhe bɛ mpok ǎtwɔ̀ anɛ bo bárɛ̀m chɔŋ bɛ, ‘Ɛ́rɨ ntá yɛntɨkɨ nkongɔrɛ́ nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ngɔrɛ́ anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ re bhé!’
Sɛ́fú nɔkɔ arɛ́, sɛkɔ amɨk sɛ́gháka Fílipi. Fílipi abhak ɛtɔk ɛgho atú Masidónia, nɛ abhak antɛn Mfɔ Rom. Sɛ́bhak Fílipi ndu mpǎy manywɔp.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Ghók yɛ́ ka ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ nɛkǎy mmu anɛ ataka mbwɔt nɛ́tɔ̀ŋ.
Sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ sɛchi bɔ̌ Mandɛm kɛ bǒ mmɨk mankɛm báchí amɔ mbʉ́mbʉ.
Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ akʉ Símiɔn arɔk ndǔ ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm. Nnɔ nɛ chi Yesu báchwe arɛ́ nɛ yi ndu bɛtɔŋ yi ntá Mandɛm bɛkoŋo ɛbhé Moses.
Mbák mmu wu ántáŋ ntí nɛ Kristo, bápú kway bɛkʉ yi ampɛt antɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhi, tɛ̌ndu yi achi mbɔ mmu anɛ apɛt ágò Mmɔ Mandɛm ndǔ ɛkotákátí, anchyɛ nɔkɔ yi ntíánwɔ́p bɛsí bho, ɛnɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́twɔ̀ yi chi nɛ mɛ́nɛ́mɛ́.
mámfɛrɛ ntí ndu bakǎy bapu amɛn bo Israɛl nɛ ndǔ bɛbhé ɛbhɛ́n bo abhɛn bápú koŋo Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ Yesu báfyɛ́.
Fílip abhak mmǔ Bɛtsáida, nkúbhɛ́ ɛtɔk ɛnɛ Andru nɛ Píta báfú arɛ́.
Ntí achi bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu abhɔŋ bɛ́te bɛsí Kristo mmu átàŋ bo mankɛm. Chɔŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ambɔ́ŋ nsáy anɛ ákwáy nɛ yi bɛ́kóŋo nɛpɛ́m ɛni fá amɨk. Mbák sɛ́kʉ bɛrɨ, chɔŋ sɛ́mbɔ́ŋ ɛrɨ́tí akap, nɛ mbák sɛ́kʉ bɛbʉ́, sɛ́mbɔŋ ntɛ́msi.
Nchí rɛm nɔ́ mbɔnyunɛ mpok bǎchɛm ɛbhak ɛ́mɔ́t, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ǎwɛnɛ chi mɛ́nyiɛ ɛni nɛnyíɛ́, kɛnoŋ batɨ̌ bǒnkwɔ. Ɛyɔ ɛ́nkʉ bɛ mbɔk yɛka manchɔkɔ nsay, ɛnɛ́ báchák mányìɛ, mányu, mánkwɛn.
Bo abhɛn báyàŋ bɛkʉ bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ambɔŋ maŋák nɛ bhɔ kɛ báfyɛ̀ bɛtaŋ bɛ mansyɛp bhe. Bákʉ̀ nɔ ndu bápú yaŋ bɛ bo Israɛl mánchyɛ bhɔ ɛsɔŋɔri bɛ́ bághàti bo bɛ́ nɛwú Kristo ndǔ ɛkotákátí kɛ nɛ́pɛmɛ mmu.
Kɛ nɛ́nɛ, bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn Kristo bɛ́chá ɛbhɛn bachiǎkap abhɛn Nku Nsɨ́, nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ nku anɛ ákʉ́ Yesu ate nɛntɨ Mandɛm nɛ bho áchá anɛ nsɨ́, mbɔnyunɛ akɔ nɛ nku anɛ árɨ́ áchá.
Sɛ́sɔt achwǐnyɛ́n ɛtɔk Fílipi, sɛ́ré koŋo bhɔ, mpok ɛpǎ bo Israɛl ɛnɛ́ brɛt anɛ kɛbhɔŋ yís ɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́. Sɛ́kɔ́ anyɛ́n anyɛn ndǔ manywɔp átáy sɛ́tɛ́mɛri bhɔ Troas, nɛ sɛ́bhák arɛ́ ndu manywɔp tándrámɔt. 
Ɛnɛ chí ɛrɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bhɛsɛ ndǔ mkpáká mmɨk anɛ ɛchɔŋ bɛ akap nɛ akabhɛ́nya anɛ báchyɛ̀ Mandɛm apu kway bɛkʉ ntɨ mmu nɛ́nkwáy ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbi bɛsí Mandɛm.
Bǒ bhɔ bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́ bábhɛp Jɔ̌n bɛ, “Yi sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ yɛ bɛkʉ?”
Ɛ̌ti ɛyɔ kɛ̌ bɛyǎ bhɛka mámè, báchák kɛpɛrɛ bhɔ́ŋ bɛtaŋ, nɛ abhɛ́nɛ́fú bágu.
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Mmá, ndaká yí ɔ́sɔŋɔri mɛ ɛ̌ti mmɛ́m? Mpok aya abhɨ́kɨ́ re kway.”
Ŋák ka nɛ bo abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ maŋák. Dí ká nɛ abhɛ́n bachi ndǔ nɛdǐ kɛbhɔ.
Nɛka Ábraham kɛ nɛ́kʉ́ yi ákʉ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm aghati yi. Mpok Mandɛm ábhɨ́ŋɨ́ yi bɛ́ ámfá, ándɔ́k nɛbhʉɛt anɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ bariɛp bɛchyɛ yi, arɔ ɛtɔk ɛyi, are kɔ andɔk nɔkɔ, kɛrɨŋɨ atú anɛ́ yi árɔŋ.
Dɔ̌ ka bapɛ́m ayɛka ambak nɛ Yesu mbɔ ɛnɔk ɛnɛ ɛ́mʉ́rɛ́ bakaŋ amɨk, mǎnsɛnɛ ndǔ nɛka ɛnɛka nɛ yi nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ bátɔ́ŋ be, mǎnchyɛ nɔ́kɔ́ Mandɛm bɛyǎ kɛnókó.
Mandɛm achyɛ yí bɛyǎ kɛnókó ndu akʉ yi achɔkɔ ɛbhe awɔ́nɛm ɛyi ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ. Ɛta abhʉrɛ bariɛp ami ndu achyɛ yí Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ. Nɛ chí Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ mmu Yesu achyɛ bhɛsɛ kɛ ákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́fàkari nɛ mbɔ ɛnyǔ bǎghɔ̀ nɛ bǎghòk.
Kɛ Páílet abhɛ́p bɔ́ bɛ, “Ntɨkɨ ɛbɛ́ptí ndak yi ákʉ́?” Kɛ ngɛ́mtáy bǒbhɔ bápɛt báre bɨk nɛ bɛtaŋ bɛ, “Dɛm mángó yi ndǔ ɛkotákátí!”
Nɛ́rɨ́ nkwǎ nɛ́chí mbɔ ngó. Ɛyɔŋɔ́nyu ɛnɛ mmu ɛ́kwày bɛ́twɔ nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ bɛbʉ́ fá amɨk. Bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛn nɛ́rɨ́ nɛ́twɔ̀ nɛ bhɔ bɛ́chɔ̀ŋti nɛpɛ́m nkwǎŋwaŋ nɛnkɛm. Nɛ́kʉ̀ ngó ánkɛ́m anɛ́ ásɔ̀ŋ nɛpɛ́m nkwǎŋwaŋ nɛnkɛm. Nɛ ngó wu áfù chí ndǔ nɛpǐngo anɛ́ ápú nɛmɛ.
Nɛghɔ́ Yesu aghɔ bhɔ, abhɨŋɨ bhɔ bɛ mankoŋo yi. Bárɔ́ ɛtayap Sɛbɛdi amɛm áchwí nɛ bǒ bɛtɨk, bákóŋo yi. 
Kɛ mmu amɔt amɛm nkwɔ bǒbhɔ akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, ntwɔ̌ nɛ mɔ́wa ntá yɛ. Ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛpú ka yi andɛm kɛpɨ,
Bácháyti, nɛ bɛcháy bɛ́kɛ́m bhɔ. Bákáysi bɛ bághɔ̀ nɔ chi ɛfóŋó ngu.
Kpátɛ̌ ɛchɔŋ Mandɛm kɛ ákwàk mɛ, nɛ ákʉ́ bɛ́ nté fá ndɛ́m ntá bǒ mankɛm, manɛ́m bho nɛ ndɛ́ndɛ́mɛ́ bho, nkúbhɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ bárɛ́mɛ́ nyaka nɛ Moses árɛ̀m bɛ́ chɔŋ ɛ́mfakari.
Bɛtaŋ mɛnkɛm chi ɛbhi mpoknkɛm. Amen. 
Ɛnyu ɛnɛ kɛ̌ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛnɨkmʉɛt: ‘Ɛtayɛsɛ, wɔ mmu ɔ́chí amfay: Kʉ bo mánchyɛ́ nnyɛ́n ɛna kɛnókó;
Mbɔ̌ŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ mɛ̌yáŋ bɛkʉ mǎndɨ́ŋɨ́ chí yí? Chí bɛ́ mandɛm nsé anɛ́ bǒ abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ Mandɛm báchyɛ̀ akap nta yi abhɔŋ bɛtaŋ kɛ? Kɛ chí bɛ́ nnya ɛnɛ́ báchyɛ̀ mbɔ akap ntá mandɛm nsé ɛcha nnya ɛ́chák?
Akɛmɛ baghɔkɔ́ Jɔ̌n bɛ, “Pɛt ka nsɛm ghati Jɔ̌n mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎghɔ́ nɛ ɛbhɛn bághókó bo bárɛ̀m: Bǎghók nɛ bǎghɔ́ bɛ manɛ́mámɨk bághɔ̀ mbaŋ nɛ́nɛ, nɛ bakɛm báfáté bákɔ̀. Bǒ ɛbhaŋákwa bátáŋ nɛ babhók bághòk mbaŋ. Bawú bápɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m nɛ bághàti bachɛ́bhɛ́bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́.
Akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nkú ɛpay ánchyɛ́ amɔt ntá anɛ abhɨkɨ bhɔŋ, nɛ mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛnyíɛ́ ánkɔ́rɛ́ nɛ anɛ abhɨkɨ bhɔŋ.”
Bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn Jɔ̌n ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka ndu bɛjwiti bho, bɛ́fú chi ntá Mandɛm kɛ ntá nkwǎ?”
Nti anɛ nchí sɨŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ ntá yɛka ambɨ ambɨ chi bɛ mpok anɛ mɛ̌twɔ chɔŋ awu, nkɛ́sɔt bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áchyɛ́ mɛ mbak bɛběbɛbe nɛ bhe. Mandɛm achyɛ́ mɛ bhɔ chi bɛkʉ mǎnte ndǔ nɛka ɛnɛka, puyɛ̌ chi bɛkʉ mǎnkwɛn.
Yesu ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, abhak maknkay tontó. Ayibhiri mmʉɛt arɛm ntá bɛyǎ bo abhɛn bákòŋo yi bɛ, “Dɨŋɨ́ ká tɛtɛp bɛ, mbɨ́kɨ́ re ghɔ mmǔ Israɛl amɔt anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛka nɛ mɛ mbɔ kɛnkɔ̌-nɛ.”
Júdas abhɨkɨ rɛm nyaka ɛnyu ɛyɔ chi bɛ ǎghɔ báchɛ́bɛ́ bho ntínso. Arɛm nɔ chi ndu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka ntɨ ngɛ́p. Nɛ ndǔ nkwɔ bakoŋo Yesu, yi kɛ áchí nyaka mbʉrɛ nkáp, nɛ ǎsɔ̀t nyaka aywi arɛ́ ansɛm ansɛm anyiɛ nɔkɔ.
Yesu atɛ́m yɛ bhɔ nɛkay ɛnɛn bɛ, “Mmu amɔt apɨ nyaka ɛnɔk ɛnɛ babhɨŋɨ bɛ́ *fig amɛm nkɨ ywi. Ɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ mɛ́nyu kɛpɛm, are kɔ ambyo nɔkɔ mbák ɛ́nyu kɛpɛm, kɛ akɛ ghɔ́ yɛ̌nyɨŋ.
Yesu aghati yi bɛ, “Tɛtɛ̌tɛp, chɔŋ mǎngɔ ndǔ nɛbu nɛ́nɛnɛ gbee, bɔángɛl Mandɛm mánkó amfay mánsɛbhɛ nɔkɔ amɨk bɛtɛmɛri Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm.”
Báfʉɛ́t nɛbhʉɛt anɛ babhabhɛri abhɛn mbɨ nɛ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ abhɛn bákòŋo báchwɔp ndu nyǔbha anɛ́ mmu ǎfʉɛt anchwe ɛtɔk. Nnyǔbha wu ánɛ́nɛ ndu mmʉɛt ɛyi. Báfú bárɔ́k nɛfí, bákɔ baghaka ndʉ́ nkɔngɔ ɛtɔk amɔt. Píta ápɛ́rɛ́ yɨŋɨ ángɛl ánáŋ árɔ́ yi arɔŋ.
Mandɛm akʉ yɛ be bǎpɛt bǎpu basɛm, bǎrɔp chi bɔ́. Nɛ tɛ̌ndu yi asɔrɛ bhe bɛ mǎmbák bɔ̌bhi, chɔŋ anchyɛ bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛchyɛ bɔ̌bhi. 
Ntɨkɨ mpok ɔ́mè, mbák ɛ́pú nɔ, ɔbhak ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ, kɛ sɛ́ré twɔ́ bɛghɔ wɔ?’
tɛ̌ndu Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ sɛ́ghàti bho abhɨkɨ twɔ nyaka ntá yɛka chí ndǔ ɛyɔŋɔ́nyu yɔyɔ, kɛ ndǔ bɛtaŋ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ nkwɔ. Nɛ bǎrɨŋɨ nyaka bɛ yɔ achi tɛtɛp. Mpok sɛ́chí awu nɛ bhe, bǎrɨŋɨ nyaka ɛnyǔ ɛkakánɛkɔ ɛyɛsɛ ɛchi. Sɛ́bhʉ̀rɛ nyaka mmʉɛt ɛyɛsɛ ɛnyu ɛyɔ ndu bɛkwak bhe!
Yesu akɛ́m yi ndu awɔ, aya bárɔk antí ɛtɔk. Apá yi batíɛ́ amɨ́k, anyaŋa amɔ́ anti ywi abhɛp yi bɛ, “Ɔ̌ghɔ̀ nɔ yɛ̌nyɨŋ?”
Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bápɛtnsɛm Yerúsalɛm. Ɛnɛ́ Yesu ákɔ̀ amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm, bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses nɛ bǒbati ɛtɔk bárɔ́k,
Ndu bákʉ̀ ɛnyu yɔ kɛ Mandɛm afɛ́rɛ́ amɔ nɛ bhɔ bɛ máŋwáká nɔ́kɔ́ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chyɛ̀ bhɔ ntíánwɔ́p. Baghɔrɛ́ bhap bárɔ babhakanɛm bárɔbhɛ bhʉrɛ chi nɛ batɨ baghɔrɛ́, ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛbhɨkɨ kway wawak.
Mmu amɔt abhak arɛ́ anɛ ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri. Are bɨk nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ andɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ́,
Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Kʉ ka bo mánchɔ́kɔ́ amɨk.” Tákɔ ayá nɛbhʉɛt ɛ́rɛ. Ɛ́kʉ bo báchɔ́kɔ amɨk. Babhakanɛm bábhák mbɔ nká ɛtay.
Símun Píta mmu ákòŋo yi ansɛm áchwɔ́bhɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ nnɛm, afʉɛ́t, arɔk amɛm, aghɔ́ bɛbhɔ́k ɛ́síɛndɛn ɛbhɔ arɛ bhʉ́rɛ́.
Ɛchi nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ mmʉɛt nkwǎ anɛ achi amɔt, yɛ̌ nɔ, abhɔ́ŋ bɛyǎ bɛpókómʉɛt nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛpókómʉɛt ɛbhɔŋ ɛbhi bɛtɨk.
Chɔŋ antwɔ́ angway bhɔ, anchyɛ nkɨ wu ntá bo bachak.” Bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, babho bɛrɛm bɛ, “Mandɛm akɛ ka!”
Aghati batǐ bɛbhóŋó bɛ, “Fɛrɛ́ ká mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn fá! Bǎkɛ́ sɔt ɛkɛt Ɛtaya mǎnjibhiri ndǔ ɛkɛrɛ́siɛ!”
Bǎkɛ́ bhak mbɔ bhɔ́. Bǎpɛrɛ nɨkmʉɛt, Mandɛm Ɛtayɛka anaŋ arɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎyaŋ.
Ɔ́kɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk Yesu Kristo, ɛbhárɛ́mɔ Mfɔ Debhít mmu Mandɛm ákú nyaka yi apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m mbɔ ɛnyu ɛchi amɛm Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ mɛ̌ghati bho.
Nchí kway bɛte bhɔ ntísiɛ bɛ bɔ báfyɛ̀ bɛtaŋ bɛkoŋo Mandɛm, kɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mbɔ̌ŋ mbi anɛ tɛtɛp.
Yesu asɛmti bhɔ bɛ bákɛ́ ghati yɛ̌ mmu. 
Yɛ̌ nɔ, abhɨkɨ rɔ nyaka bɛtɔŋ kpoŋoroŋ bɛ́ yí áchí. Ǎkʉ bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ. Yí kɛ ákʉ̀ manyiɛp ámfú amfay nɛ ǎchyɛ̀ mbwɔt ndǔ ayi mpok, anchyɛ bhe nɛnyíɛ́, anchyɛ maŋák.”
Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi mánók yɛ, bápe nnyɛ́n, báchwɔ́p ɛtɔk Gɛrása. Gɛrása abhak ɛbhěnyɛn ɛnɛ ɛ́yɨ̀ŋɨ Gálili.
Baghɔrɛ́ abhɛn tɛsáy abhɛn bachi nyáŋá nɛ básɨ́kɨ́ ntɨ nɛ Mandɛm bághòk nyaka manɛ́m abhap nɛ ɛnyu ɛyɔ, báre fyɛ́ bɛrɨ amʉɛt.
Kɛ baghɔk Yesu bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, batɨ ábé bhɔ amɛm, bábho bɛrɛm nɛ batɨ bɛ, “Ndaká yí ngɔrɛ́ nɛ áré chɔŋti bawɛrɛ́riɛp amɛn ɛnyunɛ́?
Ɛnɛ́ nchí kɔ ɛtɔk mfyɛ́ nɔkɔ amɨ́k ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎchyɛ kɛnókó mbɔ bɔmandɛm, ndɔk ngaka nɛbhʉɛ́t amɔt anɛ ɛfɛmɛ akap ɛchi, ngɔ́ ndu básɨŋ arɛ́ bɛ, ‘Ntá mandɛm anɛ bo bábhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ.’ Mandɛm anɛ nɔ bé bǎchyɛ̀ kɛnókó yɛ̌ndu bǎbhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ yí kɛ mɛ́ghàti bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti yi.
Nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ mɛ̌nɨ̀kmʉɛt ɛ̌ti yɛka mankɛm, nchí kʉ nɔ chí nɛ bɛyǎ maŋák.
Yesu aghati bhɔ nɔ kpoŋoroŋ. Píta asɔt yi nɛpak arɛm bɛ, “Ɛta kɛrɛm awǔ ndak.”
Kɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛpu ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛni achí nnɛ́mámɨ́k. Mbák ɛ́pú nɔ́, apú ghɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ, nɛ ághɔ́kɔ́ntɨk bɛ Mandɛm asó bɛbʉ́ bhɛsɛ afɛrɛ.
Yesu asɔ́k nsɔk arɛm bɛ, “Ndaká yí mkpáká bho anɛ́ ɛchɔŋ áyàŋ ɛrɨŋɨ́ maknkay? Tɛtɛp, nchí ghati bhe bɛ yɛ̌ mmu apú tɔŋ bhɔ ɛnyǔ ɛrɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛnɛ́ bɔ báyàŋ.”
Bǎyɨ̀ŋɨ bho chí nɛ amɨ́k kɛ mǎmkpɔt manyé yap. Mɛmbɔŋ mpú kpɔ́t manyé mmu.
Yesu akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Kɛfɔ ɛka kɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ fu fá amɨk. Mbɔ kɛfɔ ɛka kɛ́fu chi fá amɨk, mbʉ bǒbha mánú bɛ bákɛ́ kɛm mɛ manchyɛ ntá bo Israɛl. Kɛ, kɛfɔ ɛka kɛbhɨkɨ fu ndǔ mmɨkɨ nɛ.”
Bǎkɛ́ bhɔ́ŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛkʉ nɛ barak ɛpúsí! Bɛbʉ́ bɛ́chák mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛ́n mmu ákʉ̀ bɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔ́ŋ ndak nɛ mmʉɛt mmu. Kɛ mmu anɛ ákʉ̀ barak ɛpúsí, ǎchɔŋti chí mmʉɛt ɛyi yímbɔŋ.
Nchí rɛm nɔ mbɔnyunɛ ɛchi mbɔ bhɛ mbák mmu atwɔ ntá yɛka aghati bhe ɛnyɨŋ, yɛ̌ yi árɛ̀m chi ɛ̌ti Yesu achak anɛ achi kɛkúrí nɛ anɛ sɛ́ghàti bhe mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti yi, mǎnoko nóko. Nɛ yɛ̌ árɛ̀m chi ɛ̌ti ɛfóŋó ɛnɛ ɛchi kɛkúrí nɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm mmu mǎnɛnɛ batɨ ntá yi bǎkaka, nɛ yɛ̌ árɛ̀m chi ɛ̌ti Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ achi kɛkúrí nɛ anɛ mǎnókó, mǎnsɔrɛ sɔt amɔ apay.
Ángɛl apɔkɔ mɛ ndǔ Ɛfóŋó akó amfay ɛrɛmɛ́ njiɛ ngo. Atɔ́ŋ mɛ Yerúsalɛm, ɛtɔk Mandɛm, ndu ɛ́fú amfay ntá yi ɛ́sɛ̀p amɨk.
Bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛn Aleksánda ntɛnátɛn ákʉ́ mɛ bɛ́yǎ bɛcha. Kɛ chɔŋ Acha Yesu anchyɛ yi nsáy ndu bɛbʉ́ ɛbhi.
Bɔ̌ma, bǎkɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk barɛmɛ́ kɛpǐntɨ Mandɛm, bo bárɛ̀m nyaka mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm afyɛ́ bɔ́ antɨ bɛ mándɛm. Báchí bɛrɨ́tí bɛrɨŋ ntá yɛsɛ́. Bɔ́ bábhɔ̀ŋ nyaka bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri, yɛ̌ nɔ́, mánkɛbhɛ nɔkɔ chí ntɨ.
- Mpok ɛyɔ, ngɔrɛ́ anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ Ána abhak Yerúsalɛm. Abhak ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm. Abhak mmɔ̌ Fanuɛl, ɛbhárɛ́mɔ anɛ nnɛrɛ́kɛt Ásha. Akɔk nyaka tontó nɛ anáŋ achi nyaka ɛkɛrɛ́nɛbhay ndǔ mamiɛ́ tándrámɔt kɛ nnɛ́m aywi ǎgu. Arɔp kɛ́nkwɛ́sɛ́, tɛ mpok anɛ yi aghaka mamiɛ́ bɛsa mɛnwi nsɛm anwi. Yí kɛrɔ bɛrɔŋ ndǔ ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm ndu bɛchyɛ yi kɛnókó, nɛ are nɨkmʉɛt ambak nɔkɔ ndǔ nɛtarɛ́nsay, bɛti nɛ ngósí.
Mbɔ mmǔ nɛ abhɨ́kɨ́ fú chi ntá Mandɛm, mbʉ abhɨkɨ kway bɛ́kʉ ɛnɛ ɛnyɨŋ.”
Yɛ̌ nɔ, mpok yi ághókó bɛ́ Lásárɔs ǎme, achɔkɔ ɛbhak ɛnɛ yi achi ndǔ manywɔp apay.
Mbák ndɛm ɛ̌ti mmʉɛ́t ɛya, mbɔ̌ŋ bo abhɛn bakway bɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ̌rɛ̀m ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ mɛnwɔp.
Tɛtúlɔs árɛ́m nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, bo Israɛl báchɛ́m nɛ yí báká bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ́mɛ́ bɛ́ Pɔ̌l ákʉ́ ɛchi tɛtɛp. 
‑ Mpok Jɔ̌n mmɔ̌ Sakaría achi amɛm baso, Mandɛm achyɛ yi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛghati bho. Mpok Tibériɔs achi mfɔ ngo anɛ ɛtɔk Rom ndǔ mamiɛ́ nɛku, Pɔ́ntiɔs Páílet abhak gɔ́bhanɔ atú Judɛ́ya, Hɛ́rɔd abhak mǔnti atú Gálili, mɔmáyi Fílip abhak mǔnti atú Itúria nɛ Trakonítis, nɛ Lisánias abhak mǔnti atú Abilene. Káyfas nɛ Ánas babhak bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm. Mandɛm aghati Jɔ̌n mmɔ̌ Sakaría ɛnyɨŋ mpok yi achi amɛm baso,
Yɛ̌ndu bǎchi bo abhɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛbhak batɔŋ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm nɛ́nɛ, nté yɛka ǎtɔ̀ŋ bɛ bǎbhʉɛt chi bo abhɛn mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtɔŋ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ mbɨ ɛbhɛn mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛghɔk ɛ̌ti Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm. Bǎchí mbɔ mǎmbɔ abhɛn bábhʉɛt mɛnyu chi nɛ́bhɨ. Bǎpú mbɔ bǒ abhɛn bákwáy mɛnyiɛ nɛnyíɛ́ mbɔŋ.
Nkúbhɛ́ mpok yɔ, mbɔk bho abhɛn bachi arɛ́, bátɛ́mɛ Yesu ɛ̌ti bo Galili abhɛn Páílet akʉ baway mpok báchyɛ̀ akap ntá Mandɛm.
Abhɛn ɛkɔŋ, sɛ́ndɔ́k ambɨ bɛkɔŋ batɨ mbɔnyunɛ ɛkɔŋ ɛ́fù chi ntá Mandɛm. Nɛ mmu anɛ akɔŋ bo achí mmɔ́ Mandɛm nɛ arɨŋɨ Mandɛm.
Kʉ nɔ, mbɔnyunɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ánɨ̀kmʉɛt ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi áyàŋ, Mandɛm ǎchyɛ yɔ ntá yi. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ áyàŋ ɛnyɨŋ, ǎghɔ yɔ. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ádɛ́bhɛ́ nɛkok, mánɛnɛ ntá yi.
Bɛ́bhó ndǔ mpok anɛ Jɔ̌n Njwiti ághàti nyaka bho Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm bɛghaka ɛchɔŋ, Kɛfɔ̌ mfáy kɛ́gò nɛ bɛtaŋ nɛ mbɔk bho mánù bɛ́chwe arɛ nɛ bɛtaŋ.
Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Nchí ghati bhe bɛ ndǔ mmɨk nkɔ, mpok Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm áchɔ̀kɔ ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ yi nɛ kɛnɛ́m kɛnkɛm, be bakoŋo bha bǎchɔ̀k nkwɔ́ ndǔ mɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ, bɛkɛm manɛrɛ́kɛt Israɛl byo nɛ apay.
Ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ nkwɔ́ ndǔ bo báre nyok mɛ. Ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛn nde bhɔ́ŋ. Ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ ndu báre nyok mɛ amɛm bɛtɔk Antiɔk, nɛ Ikɔ́niɔm nɛ Lístra. Ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ ndé bhɔ́ŋ kɛ Acha Yesu ǎfɛrɛ mɛ ndu bɔ́ mɛnkɛm.
Mandɛm atɔ́ŋ Debhít bɛrɨ̌ndu. Anɨkmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm Jekɔ́p bɛ andɔ yi anté ɛkɛt ntá yi.
Nɛ Mandɛm ápú rɔ mɛ́nɛ́nɛ mbǐnywɔp fúú, bɛ mǎnchwe ndǔ kɛfɔ ɛkɛn Acha nɛ Mpɛmɛ ywɛsɛ Yesu Kristo. Kɛfɔ ɛkɔ kɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti. 
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Ngɔ̌ ndu Satan áfú amfay akwɛnɛ amɨk mbɔ miámiaŋ.
mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm ayɛsɛ achí ngó anɛ ásɔ́ŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ.
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Ɛ̌ti bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛ ɛbhɛn, pɛtnsɛm anywɔ́p, ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛyɔ ɛ́naŋ ɛ́rɔ mɔ́ywɛ.”
Tɛ́mté wu ɛbhak ntá Sɔ̌l mbɔ bɛ mɛnyɨŋ mbɔ bɛfabhɛ́ nsi bɛfu yí amɨ́k bɛkwɛnti. Apɛt abho bɛghɔ mbaŋ. Afate yɛ arɔk bájwíti yi.
Nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka ánkʉ́ yɛ nɛ batɨ mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi ákway bɛyaŋ bɛ bo mánkʉ ntá yi.
Sɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ sɛ́ghɔ̀ Sáyprɔs, sɛ́rɔ́ yɛ Sáyprɔs ɛbhe awɔ́ghɔ, sɛ́fʉɛ́t bɛ́rɔ́ŋ ndǔ mmɨk Síria. Sɛ́rɔ́k sɛ́chwɔ́p Táya, nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka bɛ́fɛ́rɛ batu.
Mǔngo bachiǎkap abhɛ́p Yesu ɛ̌ti bakoŋo bhi nɛ ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi átɔ̀ŋ bho.
Nsáy bɛbʉ́ chi nɛwú, kɛ akap anɛ Mandɛm áchyɛ̀ ndɛ́ndɛm chi nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ abhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Kristo Acha ywɛsɛ.
Kɛ mbák bághátí wɔ́ bɛ, “Nɛnyiɛ́ ɛnɛn chí nɛnyíɛ́ mandɛm nsé”, kɛ́nyiɛ́ nɔ́. Nɛ́kwày bɛ́chɔ́ŋti ntɨ mmu wu amɛm.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛka. Bǎchí mbɔ manyiɛp amɛn ásɔ́tí, sɔ́ŋ be kɛsɔŋ, kwɛn be kɛkwɛ́n! Ɛrɨ bɛ mǎmbák mbɔ manyiɛp bakwɛn, mbák ɛ́pú nɔ, mbɔ manyiɛp basɔŋ.
Mpú rɛm nɔ́ chí bɛ́fyɛ́ bé ɛbhé bɛ́ bǎbhɔŋ bɛkʉ nɔ́, nchí chyɛ be chí maníɛ́,
Aghati yɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Bák ká pě, mǎnɨk nɔkɔ mmʉɛt, bɛ́ nɛmɔ nɛ́kɛ́ dɛp be amɨk. Bǎbhɔŋ ntɨ, kɛ mmʉɛt apu bhe.”
Ɛ̌ti yɔ, ‘Mbakanɛm abhɔŋ bɛ́rɔ́ ɛtayi nɛ máyi, ambat mmʉɛt nɛ ngɔrɛ́ ywi,
Yesu apɛt asɛp arɔk Kapɛ̌naum, ɛtɔk ɛgho, atú Gálili. Arɛ́, are tɔ́ŋ bo amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí bo Israɛl ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt ɛnap.
Ángɛl anɛ ájwí tándrámɔt apɨkɨri ɛyǐ ɛkwɔp ndǔ mbʉ́ɛ́p. Ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ ɛ́fú ndǔ ɛkɛrɛ́ Mandɛm nɛbhʉɛt anɛ yi achi ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ ɛyi bɛ, “Ndak ámay!”
Bachɛ́bhɛ́bho bachi nɛ bhe mpoknkɛm, kɛ mpú bhak nɛ bhe mpoknkɛm.” 
Nɔ́ bhɔ! Dɔ̌ ngati be bɛ, mbák bǎbhɨkɨ tɨ́knsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛka, chɔŋ be mankɛm mǎngu mbɔ bhɔ.
Ndǔ mkpáká bho anɛ ɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́ ansɛm, Mandɛm abhɨ́kɨ́ kʉ bho mándɨŋɨ nkaysi yɔ, mbɔ ɛnyǔ yi ákʉ́ nɛ́nɛ bɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ántɔ́ŋ yɔ ntá bǒnto nɛ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ bhi, bɔ́ bho báchi nyáŋá ntá yi.
Mɛ́mbák chí bɛrɨ̌ ɛpɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fù amɛm ntɨ, nɛ bɛbhak kpák, nɛ nɛsɛptímʉɛt mbɔnyunɛ ɛnyǔ bɛrɨ ɛbhɔ bɛpu gu manyiɛp, nɛ ɛbhɔ kɛ Mandɛm ákɔŋ tontó.
Bǎsɔt bǒbhɛn bǎtwɔ fá nɛ bhɔ ɛnɛ́ bábhɨ́kɨ́ ghɛp yɛ̌nyɨŋ amɛm ɛkɛrákap ɛyɛsɛ nɛ yɛ̌ ɛbɛ́ptí ɛnyɨŋ bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɛm ɛ̌ti Mandɛm aywɛsɛ
Mbák yɛ̌ mmu abhɛp be ntí anɛ bǎkàŋari yɔ, ghatí ká yi bɛ, ‘Acha, áyàŋ yɔ.’ Tɛ́mté wu, chɔŋ yi andɔ mǎnsɔt yɔ.”
Bǎrɨŋɨ sayri bɛ báyà bo abhɛn bachi mbɔ manɛ́mámɨk mbi nɛ bɛ bǎchi mbɔ ɛrɔŋɔ ntá bo abhɛn bachi amɛm ɛjuri.
Sɛbhɔŋ ɛkɔŋ amɛm batɨ mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm ayambɨ akɔŋ bɛsɛ.
Nsyɛ́p anɛ básiɛ́bhɛ́ Abraham kɛ achi nyaka ɛrɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ yi amʉɛt bɛtɔŋ bɛ yi abhɔŋ nɛka nɛ yi tɛ mpok anɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ re syɛp yi. Mandɛm ákʉ́ nyaka nɔ bɛ Ábraham ambak chi-mbɨ ntá bo mankɛm abhɛn mánóko Mandɛm mpok bábhɨ́kɨ́ re syɛp bhɔ, nɛ nta abhɛn nɛka ɛnap nɛ Mandɛm nɛ́kʉ́ yi ásɔ́rɛ́ bɛ bɔ bachi chak bɛsí bhi.
Bo Israɛl bhɔ bárɛm bɛ, “Bɛ́kóŋo bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛ, sɛ́ghɔ nɛ́nɛ bɛ ɔbhɔŋ ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ. Ábraham agǔ nyaka, barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm mankɛm bágú nkwɔ, kɛ wɔ, ɔ̌rɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Mbák mmu ámbʉ́rɛ́ bɛyɔŋ ɛbha apú gú wáwák.’
“Kɛ bě babhɔŋ bǎrɛ̀m bɛ mɛ nchí agha?” Símun Píta akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Wɔ kɛ ɔ́chí Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎto.”
Nɛ ǎchyɛ̀ bhɛsɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ sɛ́nɨkmʉɛt bɛ yi anchyɛ bhɛsɛ mbɔnyunɛ sɛ́bhʉ̀rɛ bɛbhé bhi nɛ sɛ́kʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chyɛ̀ yi maŋák.
Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Tɛtɛ̌tɛp, mbák bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ nyiɛ́ nyamwʉɛ́t Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm, mǎnyú manoŋ ami, bǎpú bhɔŋ nɛpɛ́m.
Kɛ Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Bǎkɛ́ chay. Chi mɛ!”
Mmu anɛ bárɛ̀m mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ɛ̌ti yi afu chí ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt anɛ́ achí kɛkúrí nɛ anɛ́ yɛ̌ mmu abhɨ́kɨ́ re fu arɛ, nɛ anɛ́ ákʉ̀ bɛtɨkɨ́ Mandɛm mbɔ nchiakap.
Chɔŋ yí antɛmsi bǒ abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ yaŋ bɛrɨŋɨ Mandɛm nɛ abhɛn bápú ka bɛkoŋo Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo Acha ywɛsɛ.
Mpǎy bo Israɛl babhak arɛ abhɛn bákɔ̀ mánkʉ nɔkɔ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ mɛ́mfú mɛ́ndɔ́ bo abhɛn bɔ bɛsɔŋɔri. Báre mɔ bɛ́bok bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ ndu nnyɛ́n Yesu Acha nkwɔ́. Babho yɛ bɛrɛm ntá bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ, “Ndu nnyɛ́n Yesu mmu Pɔ̌l ághàti bo ɛ̌ti yi, fú ka yi amʉɛt.”
mbɔnyunɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ághátí bhɔ chi ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛcha bɛtaŋ ɛbhap. Ǎghàti nyaka bhɔ bɛ “Mbák mmu antɔk njiɛ-nɛ, tɛmtí ká yi nɛ batay mǎngwáy, yɛ̌ chi nnya, tɛmtí ká wáy mbák atɔk njiɛ nɛ.”
“Nyǔbhá anɛ́ mmu áfʉɛ̀t arɛ́ bɛchwe ndǔ Kɛfɔ Mandɛm áchí mábhɛ́rí. Nyǔbhá anɛ́ mmu áfʉɛt arɛ andɔk anchwe ndǔ mbǐ nɛwú ánɛ́nɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ mbi wu áchɨk, nɛ ɛ́chí wɨkɨrɨk bɛfʉɛt arɛ. Ɛ́kʉ bo abhɛn báfʉɛ̀t arɛ baya. Fʉɛ́t yɛ́ ka chi ndǔ nyǔbhá anɛ achi mábhɛ́rí.
Pɔ̌l anyokoti mɔ́nɛkɔkɔ́ kɛbhe. Ɛnɛ́ yi afyɛ́ kɔ ango, bɛsɔŋɔ́ ngó bɛkʉ ɛfé ɛ́fú ndǔ kɛbhe ɛkɔ ɛ́nɛ́m yi ndu awɔ́ ɛ́rɔ́p arɛ́.
Ɛnyuyɔ kɛ ɛbhak mpok Mandɛm ákʉ bawú mámpɛ́tnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Mmʉɛ́t ngú anɛ bábhɛ́mɛ́, ǎpɔpɔ́ɔ. Kɛ mpok yi ákʉ̀ bawú mámpɛ́tnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, mmʉɛt nkwǎ ǎbhák chi anɛ ápú gu wáwák.
Ɛ́kʉ́ bo babho bɛ́kpɔ́ti bɛ́wɔ̌amáŋ mandɔkɔ nɔkɔ bɛtɛmɛri yi, mámbɨk mandɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Sɛ́mbɨ́tí Mandɛm mfay! Mandɛm ánjɛ́t mmu anɛ átwɔ̀ ndǔ nnyɛ́n Acha! Sɛ́mbɨ́tɨ́ Mfɔ bo Israɛl!”
bábhɛp yi bɛ, “Ntɨkɨ bɛtaŋ ɔ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn nɛ ɔ́kʉ̀? Agha áchyɛ́ wɔ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɔ?”
Yesu arɔk achwe amɛm áchwí amɔt. Abhak anɛ Símun. Aghati yi bɛ ánók áchwí antɛn anyɛ́n mandú. Yesu achɔkɔ yɛ amɛm áchwí wu, antɔŋ nɔkɔ bo abhɛn bachi angɔkɔnyɛ́n Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm.
mbɔnyunɛ nnáŋ ngɔ nɛ amɨ́k mmu anɛ ɔ́tó bɛ ampɛmɛ bhɛsɛ.
Kɛ tɛ̌ndu bɛyǎ bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ nɛbhay bábhɔ̀ŋ mamɔ bɛkʉ ɛpúsí, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbakanɛm abhɔŋ bɛbhay ngɔrɛ́ anchɔkɔ nɛ yí, nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ngɔrɛ́ ámbɔ́ŋ aywi nnɛ́m anchɔkɔ nɛ yi.
Kɛ mmǔ anɛ ápábhɛ́ mɔ́mayi, achí amɛm ɛjuri nɛ ǎkɔ̀ amɛm ɛjuri, kɛrɨŋɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ yi árɔ̀ŋ mbɔnyunɛ ɛjuri ɛnɛ yi achi amɛm ɛ́kʉ́ yi achi mbɔ nnɛ́mámɨ́k 
Kɛ mmu anɛ ákɔ̀ nɛ bɛti ǎchɨ̀ŋti ankwɛn mbɔnyunɛ mbaŋ apu ghɔ.”
Běku bɛ́gháká nɔ́kɔ́, bakoŋo Yesu basɛp, barɔk angɔkɔ manyu,
Mbák mmu ywɛka aběntɨ, ákɛ́ rɔ bɛběntɨ bhi mɛnto yi ndǔ bɛbʉ́, nɛ ákɛ́ bhʉɛrɛ bɛběntɨ antɨ ndǔ nywɔp nɛnkɛm.
Nɛ́yí nɔkɔ Pɔ̌l asɔt bhɛsɛ́ sɛ́rɔk bɛghɔ Jems. Bǒbati bǒnkwɔ bachak abhɛn Yerúsalɛm mankɛm bábhák arɛ.
Mpok ɛyɔ chɔŋ bo mánde kɔt ngɛpti bɛ báchi bo Mandɛm yɛ̌ndu bábhɨkɨ noko bɛ́ Mandɛm abhɔŋ bɛtaŋ bɛ́kʉ bɔ́ mámbak bǒbhi. Kɛ́chɛm ɛkak nɛ mɛnyǔ bo bhɔ.
Nɛ nkúbhɛ́ ɛyɔŋɔ́nyu kɛ Mandɛm abhʉrɛ mfay nɛ mmɨk anɛ ɛchɔŋ mɛnoŋ ngó ansɔŋ mfay nɛ mmɨk, kɛ anaŋa bo abhɛn bapú mbɔ ɛnyǔ bo Mandɛm bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́bhak, ndǔ nywɔp manyé.
Ndǔ mpok anɛ áfʉɛ́rɛ́ ansɛm, Mandɛm ǎfʉ̀ɛt nyaka ntá barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ bhi ndu bɛrɛm kɛpɨ ntá bachǐmbɨ bhɛsɛ. Akʉ́ nɔ ndɔŋ nɛ ndɔŋ nɛ ndǔ bɛyǎ babhi.
Mandɛm afɛ́rɛ́ amɔ nɛ bhɔ mbɔnyunɛ barɔ mɛnoko mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi tɛtɛp ɛ̌ti yi bárɔbhɛ koŋo chi nsé. Nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm ághókó kɛ bɔ bárɔ́bhɛ́ chyɛ kɛnókó, puyɛ̌ mmu anɛ ághókó yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ. Yi kɛ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛchyɛ bakak mpoknkɛm. Amen.
Píta afate yɛ nɛ bǒnto báchák batí byó nɛ amɔt, abho bɛrɛm nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ ntá bɛyǎ bǒbhɔ bɛ, “Bǒ Judɛ́ya nɛ be mankɛm abhɛn bǎchi Yerúsalɛm, tá ká batú mǎngók ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ̌rɛ̀m.
Bɔ̌ma, ɛnyɨŋ ɛchi ɛnɛ sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛkʉ, kɛ puyɛ̌ bɛ sɛbhɔŋ bɛkoŋo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bakwǎŋwaŋ báyàŋ bɛkʉ.
Sɛ́pú kʉ nyaka nɔ chi bɛ sɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ bɛ́gháti bhe bɛ mǎnchyɛ bhɛsɛ nɛkwak. Sɛ́yàŋ nyaka chí bɛ sɛ́ntɔ́ŋ be ɛpɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́kóŋo.
Mpok bɛkɔk kɛpɛmɛ́nɔk ákwáy nɔ́kɔ́, mbɔŋɔ́nkɨ ató bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk bhi bachak bɛ mándɔ́k mánsɔ́t aywi ákɔ́rɛ́ mbwɔt.
Bo abhɛn básɔ̀t mbɔk manywɔp bɛ acha achak bákʉ̀ nɔ chi bɛchyɛ Acha kɛnókó. Mmǔ anɛ ányìɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ákʉ̀ nɔ chi bɛchyɛ Acha kɛnókó, tɛ̌ndu áchyɛ̀ Mandɛm bakak kɛ anyiɛ yɔ. Nɛ mmu anɛ apu nyiɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ǎkʉ̀ nɔ chi ndu áyàŋ bɛchyɛ Acha kɛnókó nkwɔ nɛ ǎchyɛ̀ bakak ntá Mandɛm.
“Bě batɔŋ ɛbhé Moses, nɛ be bǒnkwɔ Fárisi, bǒ bɛtábhá! Chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛ́p ntá yɛka ɛncha mbɔnyunɛ, bǎchí mbɔ manɛm anɛ bághókó sayri, bawati nɛ mbɨ pɛ́pɛ́p, ɛnyu ɛnɛ mmu ághɔ̀, ankɔŋ, yɛ̌ndu bɛrɛnɛ́ bawú ɛbhɛn mɛ́náŋ bɛ́chɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ bɛghɛp kɛ bɛchi amɛm.
Fǎ ká mɛ bɛsí. Mpǒk nsay ánù mɛ, bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ chyɛ mɛ nɛnyíɛ́; mpǒk manyiɛp ákwàk mɛ, bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ chyɛ mɛ manyiɛp mɛnyú.
Bě batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm, chɔŋ ɛ́mbɛp ntá yɛka ɛncha! Bǎbhɛsɛ ɛfɨŋɨ́ ɛnɛ mánɛ̀nɛ mbǐnywɔp anɛ mmu áfʉɛ̀t arɛ́ kɛ ambɔ́ŋ nɛjwǐmɛm ndǔ barak Mandɛm. Bǎbhɨkɨ chwe arɛ, nɛ bǎchyɛt mbi ntá abhɛn báyàŋ nyaka bɛchwe arɛ!”
Píta abho bɛ́dɛp nɛkok ɛnɛn mbɨ. Ngɔsɔ́ŋ anɛ aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Róda áchí nyaka mmɔ̌ bɛtok anywɔ́p. Arɔk bɛrɨŋɨ mmu anɛ ádɛ̀p nɛkok.
Nɛfú báfú amɛm áchwi, bo bárɨ́ŋɨ bɛ́ Yesu achi arɛ.
