Mbák bǒ abhɛn bákwàk bɛkʉ bɛtɨk Mandɛm bákʉ̀ bhɔ sayri, bo báchyɛ bhɔ kɛnókó nɛ bákway bɛ́rɛm mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo kɛbhɔŋ bɛcháy. 
Chɔŋ mfay amfʉɛt, mmɨk amfʉ́ɛ́t, kɛ Ɛyɔŋ ɛya ɛ́pú fʉɛt. 
Nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ bǎchuɔ́bhɛ́ kɛ bo kɛ syɛpti bhe, dɔ̌ ká ɛtɔk ɛyɔ nɛ bǎpɛrɛ́ fá arɛ́, kwɛt ka mfok anɛ áchí be bɛkak. Chɔŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́mbak mbɔ ntísiɛ ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bɔ́ bákʉ́.”
Bo abhɛn bábhɔ̀ŋ ɛsɔŋɔri mbɔnyunɛ ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ nkaysi Mandɛm achi, bábhɔŋ bɛrɔ́ŋ ambɨ bɛ́kʉ bɛrɨ, mándɔ bapɛm ayap ntá Mandɛm mmu aghoko bhɔ. Yi apú rɔ bɛbhʉrɛ bariɛp ami.
Bǎtwɔ́ ndǔ ɛchɛmɛ bɔ̌mbɨ Mandɛm abhɛn yi ásɨ́ŋɨ́ manyɛ́n ayap amɛm ɛkáti ɛyi amfay. Bǎtwɔ́ ntá Mandɛm mmu átàŋ bho mankɛm. Bǎtwɔ́ bǎchɛm nɛ bɛfóŋó bo abhɛn bayambɨ bátwɔ́. Chí bɛfóŋó bo abhɛn bachi chak, abhɛn Mandɛm ákʉ̀ bákwáy ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbi bɛsí bhi.
Ɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ manywɔp árát, Pɔ̌l abhɨŋɨ bǒ batí bo Israɛl abhɛn bachi arɛ́. Bátwɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Bɔ̌ma, mbɨ́kɨ́ kʉ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ntá bo bhɛsɛ́ nɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ kʉ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛ́byak bɛpɨŋɨ́ ɛtɔk ɛbhɛ́n bachǐmbɨ barɔ ntá yɛsɛ. Yɛ̌ nɔ, bǒ bhɛsɛ́ bákɛ́m mɛ Yerúsalɛm báfyɛ́ amɔ bǒ Rom.
Bɔ̌ma, bɛrɨ̌ndu Yesu Kristo Acha mɛ́mbak amɛm batɨ ayɛka. Amen.
Tɛ̌ndu sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛbhakántɨ́, sɛ́bhɔŋ ngǎngaŋ nɛ sɛ́kʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ nɛ nɛtaŋántɨ.
Bǎchí bo abhɛn bǎkɔ̀ nɛ ngósí, mpok mbaŋ ághɔ̀. Sɛ́pú bo ɛjuri, sɛ́pú bo bɛti.
Chɔŋ manɔ́ anchyɛ ntɨ manɔ́ ntá bǒbati bɛ mángwáy. Chɔŋ mbɔk bachi mánkʉ ɛnyumɔt nɛ bɔ̌bhap. Chɔŋ mbɔk bhɔ mánte nɛnu nɛ bachi nɛ manɔ, mánkʉ bɛ mángwáy bhɔ.
Kɛ ɔbhɨkɨ bhɔ́ŋ bɛ́kɛm kɛfě nɛ bo ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́bhɨkɨ bhɔ́ŋ ntí nɛ nnɛt, nɛ ɛ̌ti manyɛ́n bachǐmbɨ. Kɛ́ táŋ nɛ bho ɛ̌ti bɛbhé ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áchyɛ nyaka Moses. Bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ apú kwak yɛ̌ mmu, nɛ bɛ́bɛp tontó.
Mpok anɛ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl bákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn ɛbhé ɛ́rɛ̀m mbɔ ɛnyǔ batɨ yap aghati bhɔ, yɛ̌ndu babhɨkɨ bhɔŋ bɛbhé ɛbhɛn bɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́ ntá Moses, bátɔ̀ŋ ndu mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ bákʉ̀, bɛ bárɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ babhɔŋɔ bɛkʉ nɛ ɛnɛ babhɨkɨ bhɔŋ bɛkʉ.
Fá chí Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo Mmɔ Mandɛm.
Bákʉ́ ɛnyu ɛyɔ, bátó Banábas nɛ Sɔ̌l Yerúsalɛm bɛ mándɔk mánchyɛ nkáp wu ntá bǒbati bǒnkwɔ Yesu.
Ɛ́tárɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, bɔ́ bárɔ́ bhɛsɛ́   bárɔ́k ambɨ mɛnoŋ bhɛsɛ́ ɛtɔk Troas.
nɛ chɔŋ nchyɛ́ bhe bɛtaŋ ndu bɛ́bók bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ ɛbhɛn bɛ́sɔŋɔri bho.”
Ɛrɨ mǎmbɔ́ŋ ɛkwak ɛnyu yɔ mbɔnyunɛ mǎnaŋ bǎrɨŋɨ nɛ́nɛ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛka ɛnyǔ bɛrɨ̌ntɨ ɛbhɛn Acha Yesu Kristo átɔ̀ŋ bhɛsɛ.
Mpǎy babhakanɛm abhɛn bachi arɛ abhak mbɔ nká ɛtay. Yesu aghati baghɔkɔ́ bhi bɛ, “Kʉ ka bo mánchɔ́kɔ́ amɨk ndǔ bakwɔ́, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nkwɔ́ ámbɔ́ŋ bǒbati bɛsa bɛpay nsɛm byo.”
Bɛti bɛ́gʉ, ambʉrɛ kɛnɔ́. Nɛ́yi nɔ́kɔ́, amfate, ankɔ, ankʉ nɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋ. Mbuɔt anchak, ango nɔkɔ, kɛ yi kɛrɨŋɨ ndu ɛ́fákári.
‘Anɛ abho bɛte ɛkɛt kɛ ɛcha yi mɛnaŋa.’
Ɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ manywɔp apay, ɛpǎ nɛbhay ɛ́bhák amɛm ɛtɔk Kána, atú Gálili. Nnɔ Yesu abhak arɛ́.
Nɛ nkʉ́ nɔ amɛm ɛtɔk Yerúsalɛm. Bǒ-batí bachiǎkap báchyɛ́ mɛ bɛtaŋ bɛ́fyɛ́ bo Mandɛm amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ. Nɛ mpok anɛ bárɛ́mɛ́ bɛ mángwáy bhɔ́, nka bɛ mángwáy.
Dɔ́k yɛ́ ká ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbay, mǎnák yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ bǎghɔ́, bɛ́ ántwɔ́ ndǔ ɛpǎ nɛbhay.’
Pɔ̌l nɛ Banábas bákwɛ́t mfok ɛtɔk ɛyɔ anɛ áchí bhɔ́ bɛkak bɛtɔŋ bɛ́ chɔŋ Mandɛm antáŋ bǒbhɔ ndu ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bɔ́ bákʉ́. Báfa báré rɔ́ŋ Ikɔ́niɔm.
Bǎkʉ́ báwáy yi mmu áchyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m. Kɛ Mandɛm akʉ yí apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Bɛsɛ́ sɛ́ghɔ́ nɛ amɨ́k ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛfakari.
Báfyɛ̀ bho bariɛp bɛkʉ mánkáysí bɛ chɔŋ bɔ́ mámbɔŋ ngǎngaŋ bɛkoŋo nɛtɔŋ ɛnɛsɛ, ɛnɛ́ bɔ́ babhɔŋ bachi basɛ́mɛ́ bɛbʉ́. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛbhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ amfay mmu, mmu wu ǎbhák chi nsɛm ntá ɛnyɨŋ ɛyɔ.
Bǎrɨŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛyɨŋɨ mɛ chi amfay amfay. Mbák yɛ mmu arɨŋɨ sayri bɛ yi achi nkoŋo Kristo, ándɨŋɨ bɛ bɛsɛ nkwɔ sɛchi bakoŋo Kristo mbɔ yi.
Ngɔrɛ́ wu arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Ɛta, ngɔ nɛ́nɛ bɛ ɔchí ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm.
Bǎbhɔŋ bɛchak yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ sayri, mǎnkɛm ɛ́nɛ ɛ́rɨ́.
Mpok nchí nɛ bo Israɛl, nchí bhák mbɔ mmu Israɛl ndǔ nchí nu bɛ́kwák bhɔ́ mánsɨ́kɨ́ntɨ nɛ Yesu. Mpok nchí bhák nɛ bǒ abhɛn bákòŋo bɛbhé Moses, nchí bhák mbɔ bhɔ yɛ̌ndu mpú antɛn bɛbhé Moses, ndǔ nchí nu bɛkʉ bɔ́ mántwɔ ntá Yesu Acha.
Nywɔp Mfɔ Hɛ́rɔd afyɛ́ ndu bɛrɛm kɛpɨ nɛ bhɔ nɛkwáy nɔ́kɔ́, afyɛ́ ndɛn kɛfɔ yi, achɔkɔ ndu ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ arɛm kɛpɨ bɛsi bǒbhɔ.
Ɛrɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́tɔŋ chɔŋ be mmɔ̌rɛ chi bɛ bǎghɔ̀ chɔŋ ndǔ mánɛ́bhɛ́ yi nɛ ndɛn, bábhʉrɛ amɛm ɛkwɔbhɛ́ nɛnyiɛ nnya.”
Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ yɛ bɛ yɛ̌ ɛrɨ́tí ɛnyɨŋ ɛpu ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛna mbɔ nkwǎŋwaŋ. Yɛ̌ bɛrɨ bɛpu fu mɛ antɨ. Yɛ̌ndu mbɔ́ŋɔ́ ntɨ bɛkʉ bɛrɨ, mmʉɛt apu mɛ.
Awu áfʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, ngɔ́ ɛtaŋtí ángɛl achak ndu áfú amfay ásɛ̀p amɨk. Nɛbháŋ nɛ́káp yi. Mbaŋ táfoŋ abhak amfǎy ntí ywi. Bɛsí ɛbhi mɛ́ngɔ nɔkɔ mbɔ mmok, nɛ bɛkak ɛbhi mbɔ bɛkwabhɛ́ ngó.
“Ndǔ nkaysi yɛka, Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò abhɔŋ bɛbhak mmɔ̌ agha?” Bákɛ́mɛ Yesu bɛ, “Abhɔŋ bɛbhak ɛbhárɛ́mɔ Debhít.”
Ɛ̌ti yɔ kɛ sɛ́chɔ́kɔ́, sɛkǎ ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt bɛ́ sɛ́njap bo sɛ́nto ntá yɛka nɛ abhɛn ɛkɔŋ abhɛsɛ, Pɔ̌l nɛ Banábas,
Ndɔŋ ayɔ abhak anɛ ajwi ɛrat ɛnɛ́ Yesu átɔ́ŋɔ́ mmʉɛt ntá bakoŋo bhi, bɛbho ndǔ mpok anɛ yi ápɛ́rɛ́nsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. 
“Hɛ́rɔd nɛ Pɔ́ntiɔs Páílet báchɛm nɛ bo Israɛl nɛ mbɔk bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl fá amɛm Yerúsalɛm, báte ɛyu antí Yesu mmǔ bɛtok ywɛ anɛ achi nyáŋá.
Bɔ̌ma, sɛ́bhɔŋ bɛ́chyɛ́ bakak ntá Mandɛm mpoknkɛm ɛ̌ti yɛka. Ɛ́kway bɛ sɛ́nkʉ́ nɔ mbɔnyunɛ bǎbhɔ̀ŋ nɛka nɛ Yesu Kristo mǎndɔk nɔkɔ chí ambɨ, nɛ ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ batɨ ɛ́rɔ̀ŋ chí ambɨ.
Ágháká nɔ́kɔ́ bɛsí ɛbhap arɛm bɛ, “Nkʉ-bɛbʉ́ ndu ntí mmu anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ kʉ yɛ̌nyɨŋ, kpatɛ bátwɔ̀ way yi.” Bákɛ́mɛ yí bɛ, “Ɛyɔ ɛ́yɨ́ŋɨ́ bhɛsɛ́ ná? Ɛsɔŋɔri ɛyɛ kɛ ɛ́chí.”
Yɛ̌ nɔ, Mandɛm Acha apu chɔkɔ ndǔ bɛkɛt ɛbhɛ́n bo bate nɛ amɔ. Ɛ́chí mbɔ ɛnyǔ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ árɛ́mɛ́ bɛ Mandɛm arɛm bɛ,
‑ Fílip afate abho bɛ́rɔŋ. Ɛ́fákari bɛ́ mmǔ Ɛtǒpia amɔt anɛ afú Yerúsalɛm ndǔ mɛnɨkmʉɛt ápɛtnsɛm ɛtɔk ɛyi amɛm ɛ́kárɨk ɛnɛ mpɔŋɔ́ndɨ́k ɛ́yà. Abhak mǔngo Ɛtǒpia anɛ baghaka nɛ yi kɛ akɛmɛ nyaka ɛfɨŋɨ́ ɛkɛrɛ́ nkáp mbɔ mmu anɛ baghaka yi apu kway nyaka bɛchɛm nɛ bo abhɛn mfɔ ngɔrɛ́   Mfɔ Ɛtǒpia wu aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Kándas. Ɛnɛ́ yí áchi amɛm ɛkarɨk ɛyi árɔ̀ŋ, are pay ɛkáti ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Aisáya.
Nsɨŋɨ́-bɛkati anɛ ɛtɔk Ɛ́fɛsɔs anu kpát akʉ mbaŋ akwɛn. Abho yɛ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Bo Ɛ́fɛsɔs! Agha abhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ bɛ ɛtɔk Ɛ́fɛsɔs kɛ ɛ́bhàbhɛri ɛkɛrákap ɛnɛ Atɛ́mis nɛ ntay mandɛm ɛnɛn nɛ́fú amfay nɛ́kwɛ́nɛ́ fá amɨk ntá yɛsɛ?
Mɛ́tò wɔ ɔndɔk ɔ́nɛ́nɛ́ bɔ́ amɨ́k bɛ mándɔ́ ɛjuri mankoŋo bɛdiɛ́rɛ́, nɛ bɛ mamfu ndu bɛtaŋ Satan, mánkoŋo Mandɛm ɛnyu ɛnɛ Mandɛm áfoŋori bhɔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhap, ankʉ mámbak ndu nkwɔ bo abhɛn yi ákʉ́ bachi nyáŋá mbɔnyunɛ babhɔŋ nɛka nɛ mɛ.’ 
Yesu nɛ bakoŋo bhi bárɔ bárɔk angɔkɔ Manyu Gálili. Ngɛ́mtay bho báre koŋo yi. Bo báfú atú Gálili, mbɔk atú Judɛ́ya,
Báré kɛ́m chi ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ yí ɛ̌ti baraká Mandɛm ayap nɛ ɛ̌ti mmu anɛ ákà nnyɛ́n bɛ́ Yesu anɛ ánáŋ ágú, kɛ Pɔ̌l ǎrɛ̀m bɛ́ achi nɛpɛ́m.
Mpok ɛyɔ, mmu abhak Yerúsalɛm anɛ aka nnyɛ́n bɛ Símiɔn. Abhak chak anchyɛ nɔkɔ Mandɛm kɛnókó. Ǎnòŋ nyaka mpok anɛ Mandɛm átwɔ ankwɛnɛ batɨ bo Israɛl. Nɛ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ abhak nɛ yi.
afɛrɛ yí ndǔ bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhi mɛnkɛm, atɔ́ŋ yi bɛrɨ̌ndu, nɛ achyɛ́ yi nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak bɛsí Mfɔ Íjip. Mfɔ Íjip achyɛ yi bɛtaŋ amfǎy ɛtɔk Íjip ɛnkɛm, nɛ ɛkɛt ɛyi ɛnkɛm.
Yesu asá awɔ ntá bakoŋo bhi, arɛm bɛ, “Máya chí bǒbhɛn, nɛ bɔ̌maya chí bǒbhɛn.
Mǔnti babhabhɛri ɛkɛrákap nɛ bǒbhi bárɔk basɔt bǒnto, kɛ bákɛ tɔk bɔ́ awɔ amʉɛt ndǔ báchày bɛ bo bákɛ́ tɛmti bɔ́ nɛ batay mangway.
Dɔ́k yɛ́ ka, mǎnkʉ́ bɛ bǒ bɛtɔk mɛnkɛm mámbak bakoŋo bha, mǎnjwiti bhɔ ndǔ nnyɛ́n Ɛta, nɛ nnyɛ́n Mmɔ, nɛ nnyɛ́n Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ,
Chi Mandɛm Acha kɛ akʉ ɛ́mbak nɔ, nɛ chí ɛrɛmɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ntá yɛsɛ́.’”
Sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛ́tɨ́ŋɨ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ. Chɔŋ sɛ́ndɔ́k chi ambɨ mbák ɛ́chí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm áyaŋ.
Josɛ́f mmɔ̌ Matátias, Matátias mmɔ̌ Ɛ́mɔs, Ɛ́mɔs mmɔ̌ Náhum, Náhum mmɔ̌ Ɛ́sli, Ɛ́sli mmɔ̌ Nágai,
Pɔ̌l afate yɛ ate nɛ́ntɨ́ bǒ ɛchɛmɛ́ Areopagɔs yɔ abho bɛ́rɛm bɛ, “Bǒ Atɛns, ngɔ bɛ́ bǎfyɛ́ ntí ndǔ baraká bɔmandɛm tontó.
Yesu arɛm nɔ́ bɛtɔŋ ɛnyǔ nɛwú ɛnɛn Píta ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́gu ndu bɛchyɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó. Yesu arɛm yɛ ntá Píta bɛ, “Koŋó mɛ́.” 
Bábhɨ́ŋɨ́ Pɔ̌l, achwe anywɔ́p. Tɛtúlɔs abho bɛ́rɛ́m ɛ̌ti yi ntá gɔ́bhanɔ bɛ, “Ɛta! Ɛ̌ti yɛ kpák achi fá ɛtɔk ɛyɛsɛ ndǔ ɛrɔ́ri mpok, nɛ ɛ̌ti nɛkʉ ywɛ anɛ ndɨ́ndɨ́, ɛgúpsí ɛ́chí ɛtɔk.
Mmǔ amɔt achi nyaka ɛtɔk Bɛ́tani, anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ Lásárɔs. Akwɛ́n nɛme. Bɛ́tani abhak ɛtɔk ɛnɛ María nɛ mɔ́mayi Matá báchɔ̀kɔ.
- Banábas nɛ mɛ sɛ́twɔ fá bɛ́gháti beka Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ bɛ bariɛp amɛn Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka nɛ bachǐmbɨ bhɛsɛ́, akʉ mɔ́ afǔ tɛtɛp ntá yɛsɛ́ bɛbhárɛ́ bhɔ́ bhap, ndu ákʉ́ Yesu apɛrɛnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m. Mandɛm akʉ bariɛp ɛmɔ afǔ tɛtɛp mbɔ ɛnyu ɛchi amɛm Ɛkáti Bakway, bɛbhɔ́k bɛpay bɛ Mandɛm arɛm bɛ: ‘Wɔ ɔchí Mɔ́wa, nɛ ɛchɔŋ nchí rɛm kpoŋoroŋ bɛ Nchí Ɛtayɛ.’
Bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Mmǔrɛ́ ághátí wɔ ɔmpɛt ɛ̌sák ɛyɛ ɔnkɔ chí agha?”
Ásɔ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ɛkáti, mɛnyɨŋ mɛnwi nɛ bǒbati ɛsǎ nsɛm anwi, bákwɛ́n bɛsí Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap akɛ́m nɛkɨ́ŋ nɛ bɛkwɔp ɛbhɛn baghoko nɛ pú. Bɛkwɔbhɛ ɛbhɔ bɛ́jwí nɛ insɛns. Insɛns wu atee ndǔ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt bo Mandɛm.
Nɛ mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Mbák tɛtɛp ɔchí Mfɔ bo Israɛl, pɛmɛ́ mmʉɛt ɛyɛ!”
Ntá Yesu kɛ yi áyɨ́kɨ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́ghàti bɛsí bɛ, “Ɛta Mandɛm ayɨkɨ, nɛ ápú kway bɛyibhiri nkaysi yi. Ayɨ́kɨ́, arɛm bɛ, ‘Ɔchí nchiakap ngwɛnti ti.’”
Sɛ́rɨŋɨ nkwɔ bɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ fyɛ́ bɛbhé ɛbhɛn ntá bo abhɛn báchi chak bɛsí Mandɛm, nɔ chi bo abhɛn bábhʉ̀ɛrɛ bɛbhé. Báfyɛ bɛbhé chi ntá bo abhɛn bápu bhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé, nɛ abhɛn bátáŋntí, nɛ ntá bo abhɛn bábhɨkɨ bhɔŋ mpok nɛ Mandɛm, nɛ bo abhɛn bákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm ápú yáŋ sɛ́nkʉ. Bɛbhé bɛ́chí ntá bo abhɛn bákáysi bɛ ntí apu anɛ mánɨkmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm nɛ abhɛn bábyàk Mandɛm. Bɛbhé ɛbhɛn bɛ́chi nkwɔ ntá bo abhɛn báway bachi nɛ manɔ bhap nɛ bo bachak.
Ndu Mandɛm ábhárɛ́ bhɛsɛ nɛ Kristo nɛ sɛ́sɨkɨ ntɨ nɛ yi, sɛ́kwáy bɛrɔŋ ntá Mandɛm ndu bɛrɛm kɛpɨ nɛ yi, kɛbhɔŋ bɛcháy nɛ kɛmakati bɛ yi ǎghòk bhɛsɛ.
Mbɔk baghɔrɛ́ bhɔ bábhák María mmɔ̌ ɛtɔk Mágdala, nɛ María nnɔ Jems nɛ Josɛ́f, nɛ María ngɔrɛ́ Sɛbɛdi, nnɔ Jems nɛ Jɔ̌n. 
Ɛrɛm ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ́ ɛ́jwí bɛ́pay ɛ́fʉɛt. Ghɔ́ ká, ɛnɛ́ ɛjwi bɛrat ɛ́twɔ̀ mandú mpok. 
“Mpok yɔ, chɔŋ bɛrɨŋɨ́ maknkay mɛ́mbak amfay ndǔ mmok, nɛ ndǔ ntaŋ nɛ ndǔ mambe. Nɛ fá amɨk, chɔŋ bɛtɔk mɛ́mbɔ́ŋ basɛ́mɛ́ nɛ bɛcháy ɛ̌ti bɛrɛmti ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́fù ndǔ mpɛ́rɛ́nyɛn ɛnɛ bɔmanyu.
Sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ Mandɛm arɛm nyaka kɛpɨ nɛ Moses, kɛ mmǔ-nɛ, sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ yi áfú.”
Mandɛm ápɛ́mɛ́ bhe ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ̌ndu bhi nɛ ndǔ bǎbhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛka nɛ yi. Abhɨ́kɨ́ pɛmɛ bhe ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǎkʉ̀, chi akap anɛ yi áchyɛ́ bhe ndɛ́ndɛm.
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu abhʉɛ́t bɛrɛm nɔ nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi, ɛká bho ɛ́chwɔ́p. Júdas, mmu amɔt ndǔ nkwɔ baghɔk Yesu batí byó nɛ apay, abhak bɔ ambɨ. Arɔk kɛkwɔt nɛ Yesu ndu bɛ́bhɛ́nɛ yi.
Ɛ́chi ɛnyumɔt mbɔ mmǔ anɛ árɔ̀ŋ nɛkɔ, kɛ ápɛ́rɛ́ rɔ ɛkɛt ɛyi, arɔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ amɔ bǒ bɛtɨk abhi, achyɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap ayi ntí bɛtɨk. Aghati yɛ mbabhɛri nyǔbha bɛ́ ámbák pě.
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat, María afa, arɔk áyák, ndǔ ɛtɔk njiɛ ɛmɔ́t atú Júda.
Nti achi bɛ, ɛbhé Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm mmu áchyɛ mɛ nɛpɛ́m ndu nchɛmɛ mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Kristo, ɛ́fɛ́rɛ́ mɛ ndǔ ɛbhé ɛnɛ́ ɛchyɛ bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛn bɛ́twɔ chi nɛ nɛwú.
Ghók ká, nchí ambǐnywɔp téé nchí dɛp. Mbák mmú aghok ɛyɔŋ ɛya ánɛ́nɛ mbǐnywɔp chɔŋ nchwe anywɔ́p, nnyiɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́ nɛ yi.
Ɛ́rɨ ɛcha ntá bǒ abhɛn báchí ndǔ nɛdǐ kɛbhɔ nɛ́nɛ; mbɔnyunɛ chɔŋ mánchyɛ bhɔ́ nɛpɔptí ntɨ!
Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛ́ mmu anɛ áchɛ́mɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ ngɔrɛ́-nɛkɔ, arɔp chí mmʉɛt amɔt nɛ yi? Ɛ́chí ɛnyu ɛyɔ mbɔnyunɛ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛghati bhɛsɛ bɛ, “Bǒ bati apay, bárɔp chí mmǔ amɔt.”
Nchí ghati bhe bɛ, chɔŋ Mandɛm antɛmsi be bho mkpák anɛ ɛchɔŋ mankɛm ɛ̌ti bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bě nɛ bachǐmbɨ bhɛka bǎkʉ́.” 
Jɔ̌n akɛmɛ bhɔ́ bɛ, “Mɛ̌jwìti bho nɛ manyiɛp, kɛ mmu áchí fá téé nɛntɨ ɛnɛka anɛ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ.
Sɛ́chwɔ́bhɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ nɛchyɛ̌nyɛ́n ɛnɛn ɛtɔk Sírakɔs, sɛ́tát arɛ ndu manywɔp árát.
Ɛnɛ́ ɛ́jwí bɛpay ɛ́chí mbɔ ɛyɔ nɛ ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Kɔ́ŋ ntɨ nkwǎ mbɔ ɛnyu ɔ́kɔ́ŋɔ́ mmʉɛt ɛyɛ.’ Ɛbhé ɛnɛ ɛ́cha ɛbhɛn bɛpay ɛpu.”
Tɛtɛ̌tɛp, “Mmǔ anɛ ásɔ̀t yɛ̌ agha anɛ ntó sayri, ǎsɔt mɛ. Nɛ mmǔ anɛ ásɔ́rɛ́ mɛ́ sayri, ǎsɔt mmǔ anɛ átó mɛ.” 
Mɔ́kati nɛ́nɛ́p anɛ mánɛ́nɛ́ abhak yi awɔ. Atee ɛkak awɔ́nɛm ɛyi ndǔ manyu, atee ɛnɛ́ awɔ́ghɔ ɛbhɨ.
Tɛ̌ndu nywɔp ɛnɔ nɛ́chí nyaka chí nywɔp ɛnɛn bo Israɛl bákʉ̀ ntoŋti bɛ́chwe ndǔ nywɔp nɛywěmʉɛt ɛnap, nɛ mbɔnyunɛ nnɛm ɛnɔ nɛ́bhɨkɨ sap nyaka nɛkɔ, Josɛ́f nɛ Nikɔdɛ́mɔs bárɔ́k bábhɛ́mɛ Yesu arɛ.
Ndiɛrɛ kɛnkɔ̌ nɛ aywǐntí kɛ ápɛ́rɛ́nsɛm bɛbɨti Mandɛm-ɛ́?”
Nchí ghati yɛ bhe nɛ nchí sɛmti bhe ndǔ nnyɛ́n Acha bɛ bǎbhɨkɨ pɛrɛ bhɔŋ bɛ́bhak mbɔ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl. Bɔ bákɔŋ chi bɛpɔ̌ nkaysi yap.
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ mmu Mandɛm achi, ɛnyuyɔ kɛ Kristo achi.
Dɔ́k yɛ́ ka áyák mǎngátí bakoŋo bhi bɛ apɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m nɛ achi be ambɨ ǎrɔ̀ŋ atú Gálili. Chɔŋ mǎngɔ́ yi arɛ! Nnáŋ ngati nɔ bhe.”
Píta abho yɛ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Ngɔ sayri bɛ́ Mandɛm apú tɔŋ kɛ́rɨ́ŋámík.
María asɔt ɛsáyrí ɛ́kpɛ́mɛ́ bawɛrɛ́riɛp amɛn áyá nkáp apɨkɨri bɛkak Yesu, antɛsɛ nɔkɔ nɛ ɛmɛnɛ́ntí yi. Ɛkɛt ɛnkɛm ɛ́jwi nɛ ɛrɨ́tí ɛriɛbhɛ́ bawɛrɛ mɔ.
Debhít abhɨ́kɨ́ rɔ nyaka ɛtɔkɔ́ bawú ándɔ́k amfay. Kɛ yímbɔŋ arɛm bɛ, ‘Ɛta Mandɛm arɛm nyaka ntá Acha wa bɛ́: “Chɔkɔ́ fá ɛbhe awɔ́nɛm ɛya ndu ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ,
Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Mɛ kɛ nchí kʉ bawú mampɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m, mámbak nɛpɛ́m. Mmu anɛ ánókó mɛ, yɛ̌ angú gú, chɔŋ ampɛt ambak nɛpɛ́m.
Nɛ puyɛ̌ bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ Ábraham mankɛm kɛ bachi bǒbhi tɛtɛp. Mandɛm arɛm nyaka bɛ, “Bɛfʉɛt ntá Áisek kɛ̌ ɔ́bhɔŋ chɔŋ bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ abhɛn mfyɛ́ bariɛp bɛchyɛ wɔ.”
Bábhó bɛrɛm nɛ batɨ bɛ, “Ǎrɛ̀m nɔ chi ndǔ sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ twɔ nɛ brɛt.”
Mbák ngó ábhɨ́kɨ́ sɔŋ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛ́n mmu ákʉ́ ndǔ nɛbhʉ́ɛ́rɛ́kɛt ɛnɔ, chɔŋ Mandɛm ankap yí ndǔ bɛtɨk ɛbhi.
Yesu achwe ɛtɔk Jɛríko are kɔ bɛfʉɛt.
Bágháká nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ Njiɛ Mɛnɔk Ólif, Yesu aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Nkúbhɛ́ bɛti ɛbhɛn ɛchɔŋ, chɔŋ bě mankɛm mǎmfɛrɛ ntí nɛ mɛ mbɔnyunɛ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, ‘Mandɛm ǎdɛp chɔŋ mbabhɛri bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n angʉɛp amɨk, nkwɔ́ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n ántaka ɛbhɨ.
Mmu anɛ achi chɔkɔ ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ arɛm bɛ, “Ghɔ́ ka, mɛ́kʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm mɛ́mbák bɛkɔ.” Arɛm nkwɔ ntá ya bɛ, “Sɨ́ŋ bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn amɨk mbɔnyunɛ bɛ́chí tɛtɛp nɛ chí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛ́noko.”
Ná ɔ́ghàti ntɨ bɛ, ‘Manɔ́, dɔ̌ mɛ mfɛ́rɛ́ mɔ́ɛ̌nyɨ́ŋɨ́ anɛ achi wɔ anyɛ́sɛ́,’ ɛnɛ́ nkɔkɔ́nɔk achi wɔmbɔŋ anyɛsɛ?
Yesu arɔk yɛ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ Gɛtsɛ́mani nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi. Arɛ́, aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Chɔkɔ́ ká fa, mɛ̌tɛn mmʉɛt ambɨ ndu mɛnɨkmʉɛt.”
Yɛ̌ mmǔ ywɛka ákɛ́ pá yɛ́ nnyu ɛ̌ti bǒ abhɛn Mandɛm átó mankwák yi. Bǎbhɔŋ bɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ bɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ Mandɛm áchyɛ́ bhe, achyɛ́ ntá yɛká mankɛm, nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ Mandɛm áchyɛ́ bhe, ɛ́chí chí ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ ywɛka.
Kɛ mbák mbɔ̌ŋ mbakanɛm akʉ ntɨ ɛni bɛ́ yí apú pɛrɛ bháy ngɔrɛ́ anɛ yí átɨ́, nɛ ǎkwáy bɛ́kɛ́m mmʉɛt, nɔ́ akʉ sayri ndǔ ábhɨ́kɨ́ bháy ngɔrɛ́.
Mmu wu ayɨŋɨ mfay arɛm bɛ, “Nchí ghɔ́ bo kɛ bachi chi mbɔ bɛ mɛnɔk kɛ bɛ́kɔ̀.”
Nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛta áchyɛ̀ nɛpɛ́m, nɔ kɛ̌ yi áchyɛ́ Mmɛ Mɔ́ywi nkwɔ bɛtaŋ bɛ́chyɛ bo nɛpɛ́m.
Ɛnɛ́ mpok ánáŋ árɔ́ŋɔ́ beku bhɔ, áchwí ábhak nɛntɨ manyu, Yesu abhak ɛbhɨ aywǐnti.
Nɛchwe yí áchwé Yerúsalɛm, arɔk amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm, abyo yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ. Ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́ mpok ǎfʉɛt, asɔt baghɔkɔ́ bhi bati byo nɛ ápay bárɔk ndu mɔ́tɔk Bɛ́tani. 
Bárɛm bɛ, “Ɛta, sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ re ghɔkɔntɨk bɛ mmǔ nsé wu arɛm nyaka bɛ ndǔ manywɔp arat yi ǎpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.
Mɔ́nkwɔmɛ́n anɛnɛ ɛ́bhánɛ́ ɛnɛ́ ɛjwi bɛtay, ngɔ́ antɛn ɛ́fɛ́mɛ́ akap Mandɛm bɛfóŋó bo abhɛn baway nyaka. Báwáy bhɔ mbɔnyunɛ bághàti bho Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm nɛ ntɨ nɛmɔt.
Sɔ̌l akwɛ́n amɨk, aghók ɛyɔŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́bhɛ̀p yi bɛ, “Sɔ̌l, Sɔ̌l, ndaká yí ɔ́chyɛ̀ mɛ nɛnyok?”
Nɛ ndu bǎrɔbhɛ chi bɔ̌bhi, Mandɛm ató Ɛfóŋó Mɔ́ywi bɛ ambak amɛm batɨ yɛsɛ, nɛ yi Ǎkwàk bhɛsɛ sɛmbɨ́ŋɨ́ nɔ́kɔ́ Mandɛm bɛ, “Ɛta, Ɛtaya!”
Sɛ́sɨ̀ŋ ntá yɛká bǒ nkwɔ Mandɛm awu ɛtɔk Kɔrint. Sɛ́sɨ̀ŋ ntá yɛká bo Mandɛm ábhɨ́ŋɨ́, akʉ mǎmbák nyáŋá bɛ́ mǎmbak bǒbhi. Akʉ mǎmbák bǒbhi mpoknkɛm ndǔ bǎbhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu Kristo. Nɛ nkúbhɛ́ ɛnyu ɛyɔ kɛ̌ yí ákʉ́ nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ábhárɛ́ mmʉɛt nɛ Yesu mbǎnkɛm. Nɔ́ chí yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ápú rɔ mɛ́nɨ̀kmʉɛt ntá Yesu Kristo anchyɛ nɔkɔ yí kɛnókó. Yí Yesu kɛ̌ achí Acha ywɛsɛ nɛ abhak Acha ntá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ mmu wu anɛ ághòk chí nɛ yí.
Nɛtɔk yí átɔ́kɔ́ nkokoŋ nkú Yesu, manoŋ amɛn yi áfɛ̀rɛ nyaka asíɛ́p. Aghók ndǔ mmʉɛt yi bɛ́ nɛme ɛni nɛ́may.
Ǎchɔkɔ nyaka nɛ bɛbɛ́ptí bǒbhɔ, angɔ nɔkɔ bɛbɛ́ptí barak anɛ bɔ bákʉ̀ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nywɔp nɛ angok nɔkɔ bɛpɔ̌ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ bárɛ̀m. Bɛbɛpti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ bɛ́chɔ̀ŋti nyaka ntɨ ɛni amɛm tontó mbɔnyunɛ yímbɔŋ achi nyaka mmu chak.
Ɛnɛ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ́ batísiɛ́ abhɛn bárɛ̀m bɛ́ Yesu chi Kristo báchí bárát.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Kɛfɔ Mandɛm kɛ́chí mbɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fákárí ndǔ mpok anɛ nkwaŋankɨ átìɛ̀ mbwɔt ɛbhɨ.
Kɛ chɔŋ nkʉ mǎndɨŋɨ bɛ, Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm mbɔ̌ŋ bɛtaŋ fá amɨk ndu bɛfoŋori bɛbʉ́ bho.” Arɛm ntá mbɛ́ntí wu bɛ,
Yesu asɔ́k mmɛ́m mɔ, arɛm bɛ, “Bɛtɨk ɛbha mɛ́may.” Akʉ́ɛ́p ɛmɨ, arɔ nɛpɛ́m ɛni nɛndɔk. 
Mbɔŋ Mandɛm kɛ ákʉ̀ bɔ mambak bǒbhi. Bábhɨ́kɨ́ fu nyaka yɛ chi amʉɛt nkwǎ, nɛ yɛ̌ chi ndǔ nkaysi nkwǎŋwaŋ.
Chɔŋ Ɛta Mandɛm ankʉ bɛ́ mǎnte kpirí tɛ ndǔ ngwɛnti, kɛbhɔ́ŋ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɛn Yesu Kristo Acha ápɛ̀tnsɛm.
Bǒnto Yesu bábho bɛkʉ bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay nɛ bɛrɨŋɨ́ maknkay. Bɛcháy bɛ́kɛ́m bo mankɛm abhɛn bághɔ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ.
Ntǒ be bɛ mǎndɔk mǎmfɛrɛ mbwɔt anɛ bǎbhɨkɨ pɨ. Bo bachak bápɨ, be bǎghɛ̀m mbwɔt anɛ bɔ bapɨ.”
Kɛ Jɔ̌n ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ bɛyǎ bǒnkwɔ Fárisi nɛ bǒnkwɔ Sádusi bátwɔ̀ bɛ yi anjwiti bhɔ, abho bɛ́rɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Bě bɛfé! Agha áyɛ́bhɛ́ be batú bɛ mǎnjaŋ mbi bɛbʉɛ ntɛmsi Mandɛm anɛ átwɔ̀?
Ɛkʉ bɛyǎ maŋák abhak nɛ bǒ ɛtɔk ɛgho Samária ɛyɔ.
Mpok nchí nɛ bhe, mbɨ́kɨ́ fyɛ́ amɨ́k ndǔ nkáp anɛ mmu nɛ yɛ̌ chi ndɛn ɛnɛ mmú.
Yesu Acha akʉ sɛ́sɨ́kɨ́ ntɨ nɛ bhe bɛ bǎkʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn sɛ́ghátí bhe mǎnkʉ nɛ bɛ chɔŋ mǎndɔk ambɨ bɛkʉ bhɔ.
Hɛ́rɔd ǎbentɨ tontó nɛ bǒ-Taya nɛ abhɛn Sídɔn. Ɛkʉ bɛtɔk ɛbhɔ bɛ́pay bɛyap nkwɔ bho. Bátó bhɔ́ mándɔ́k mángɔ́ Hɛ́rɔd. Báyámbɨ bághɔ́ chí Blastɔs, nkɛ́mfɔ anɛ Hɛ́rɔd. Aka bɛkwak bhɔ mánsókórí nɛ Mfɔ Hɛ́rɔd bɛ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛ́máy nɛ́ntɨ́ bɛtɔk Táya nɛ Sídɔn nɛ ɛyi. Báyàŋ nyaka bɛbhak ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt nɛ Mfɔ Hɛ́rɔd mbɔnyunɛ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛnap nɛ́fù nyaka chi atú ɛtɔk ɛnɛ achi antɛn yi.
Bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ yi, bárɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ǎyàŋ wɔ.”
Nnáŋ ngáká yɛ arɛ́ nchyɛ́ bhɔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎto ntá yap, chɔŋ ndɔk Spen. Kɛ chɔŋ njambɨ ntee awu ngɔ bhe.
Kɛ mbák mɛ̌kʉ̀ chí bɛtɨk Ɛtaya, yɛ̌ndu bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ noko mɛ, nokó ká ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ bɛtɨk ɛbhɛ́n mɛ́kʉ̀ bɛ́ghàti bhe. Chɔŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́nkwak mǎndɨŋɨ, nɛ mǎnjwimɛm bɛ́ Ɛtaya achi babhat nɛ mɛ, nɛ mɛ nchí babhat nɛ Ɛtaya.”
Kɛ bɔ́ kɛjwimɛm ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛmɛ nɛ báre chay bɛbhɛp yi. 
Chi nɛ nnɔ bákɛ́mɛ ɛnyu ɛyɔ mbɔnyunɛ báchày nyaka bǒbati bo Israɛl nɛ ntí bɛ báká nyaka ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt bɛ mbák mmu ándɛm bɛ Yesu chi Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò, bábòk yi ndǔ ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí ɛyap.
Bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bhɔ mɛ́ník Yesu mmʉɛt bɛ andɔ bɔ mándɔk mǎnchwe amʉɛt bakók bhɔ.
Bɔ̌ma, sɛ́yàŋ mǎndɨŋɨ bɛyǎ bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛn sɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ awu atú Esia. Báchyɛ bhɛsɛ nɛnyok ɛnɛn nɛ́yá nɛcha. Ɛkʉ sɛ́fɛ́rɛ ntí ndǔ sɛ́kàysi bɛ ndak ywɛsɛ ámay.
Mǔnkáp wu arɛm bɛ, ‘Ɛta Ábraham, nɨkmʉɛt tó yɛ Lásárɔs ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt ɛtaya.
Mpok yɔ, chɔŋ bo mánjaŋ nɛwú, kɛ bápú ghɔ́ nɔ́. Mámbɨŋɨ nɛwú, kɛ nɛwú nɛ́mbʉɛ bhɔ.
Bábhák maknkay tontó ɛ̌ti ɛnyu ɛnɛ yí átɔ̀ŋ mbɔnyunɛ ǎtɔ̀ŋ nyaka mbɔ mmǔ anɛ árɛ̀m ɛ́may.
Yesu ayibhiri yɛ mmʉɛt arɛm ntá mǔnti batɛmɛ́ nɛnu bɛ, “Pɛtnsɛm anywɔ́p, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛchi mbɔ ɛnyu ɔ́nókó.” Nkúbhɛ́ mpok anɛ Yesu árɛ̀m nɔ, mmɔ̌bɛtok wu ataŋ. 
Manɔ́, ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ ɔ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛkɔŋ nɛ batǐ bǒnkwɔ ɛ́chyɛ̀ mɛ bɛyǎ maŋák nɛ nɛpɔptǐntɨ́ tontó mbɔnyunɛ ɔ́kʉ́ batɨ̌ bo Mandɛm mankɛm ataŋ amɛm.
Nɛ ndu bɛyǎ manywɔp are bhesi bɛsí bo abhɛn bákɔ̀ nyaka nɛ yi bɛbho Gálili kpatɛ Yerúsalɛm. Bɔ́bhɔ kɛ báchí batísiɛ́ bhi ntá bo Israɛl.
Píta akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmǔ yɛka abhɔŋ bɛ́tɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhi nɛ mánjwiti yi ndǔ nnyɛ́n Yesu Kristo bɛ Mandɛm amfoŋori bɛbʉ́ bhi. Mmǔ anɛ ákʉ́ nɔ Mandɛm ǎchyɛ yi Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ mbɔ akap.
Njɨŋɨ sayri bɛghɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛchi arɛ. Ngɔ́ nnya mɛnyu nɛ mɛnyu. Nnya ɛnɛ anywɔ́p nɛ nnya ɛbebe nɛ nnya ɛnɛ́ ɛ́sù mɛniɛ amɨk nɛ kɛnɛn.
Nnya mbʉ́mbʉ ábé yɛ́ ntɨ nɛ ngɔrɛ́ wu. Arɔk mɛnu nɛ bɔ̌bhi nɛ bɛbhárɛ́ bɔ̌bhi. Bɔ̌bhi bhɔ chi bo abhɛn bábhʉ̀rɛ bɛbhé Mandɛm, nɛ báte batísiɛ ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Yesu ákʉ́ bo barɨŋɨ. Nnyɔ́ áte yɛ ndǔ ɛ̌siɛ́p, angɔkɔ manyu ánoŋ nɔkɔ arɛ́.
“Nɛ́nɛ, mɛ́rɔ̀ŋ Yerúsalɛm nkúbhɛ́ mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ányìɛrɛ mɛ, yɛ̌ndu mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́fákari chɔŋ nɛ mɛ arɛ́.
Pɔ̌l akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Puyɛ̌ mɛ. Nchí mmu Israɛl, mmɔ̌ ɛtɔk Tásɔs, ɛtɔk ɛgho ɛnɛ ɛbhɔŋɔ mɛnwɔp atú Silísha. Nnɨkmʉɛt, chyɛ mɛ ɛpok ndɛm kɛpɨ ntá bo abhɛn.”
Yesu atɛ́m bɔ nɛkay ɛnɛ́n nkwɔ bɛ, “Yɛ̌ mmu apú kway bɛdak ɛbhɔ́kɔ́ndɛn ndǔ nkú anɛ nkɔ anchók mbok ndǔ ɛsɨ́ nku. Mbák mmu ánkʉ́ nɔ́, ǎchɔŋti nkú nkɔ, mbɔnyunɛ ɛbhɔ́kɔ́ndɛn ɛnɛ́ ɛ́fú ndǔ nkú nkɔ ɛ́pú kɔ nɛ ɛsɨ́ ndɛn.
Bákó nɔ́kɔ́ ɛbhɨ baghɔ ngo anɛ bábháytí nɛ bakiri. Nsi ɛbhak arɛ. Brɛt nkwɔ abhak arɛ.
Chi-bɛtɨk akaka yi tontó arɛm bɛ, ‘Ɔkʉ sayri! Ɔchí ɛrɨ́tí mǔbɛtɨk nɛ ɔchí mmu tɛtɛp. Ɔtɔ̌ŋ ndǔ mandú nkáp bɛ ɔchí mmu tɛtɛp. Nɛ́nɛ, chɔŋ nchyɛ́ wɔ bɛtaŋ amfay bɛyǎ mɛnyɨŋ. Twɔ́ sɛ́nkʉ́ maŋák!’
Báré fyɛ́ bakoŋo Yesu ntɨ mbaŋ ɛyɔ ɛnkɛm mánchyɛ nɔkɔ bhɔ́ maníɛ́ bɛ́ mándɔ́k ambɨ bɛ́te kpirí ndʉ̌ nɛsɨkɨ́ntɨ ɛnap nɛ Yesu. BɔPɔ̌l bágháti bhɔ́ bɛ bábhɔŋ bɛghɔ bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri kɛ mǎnchwe ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛ́n Mandɛm ǎbhák Mfɔ wap.
Ɛsakámu amɔt abhak arɛ́ anɛ áchi nɛ ndɛn amʉɛt nɛ́nɛ́p. Are koŋo Yesu. Báyaŋ nyaka bɛkɛm yi,
Abhɨŋɨ yɛ bɔ̌-bɛtok abhi arɛm bɛ, ‘Mpok ɛpa akway. Kɛ bǒ abhɛn nnáká bátɔŋ bɛ babhɨkɨ kway bǒ abhɛn bátwɔ̀ ndǔ ɛpǎ ɛya.
Básɔt yɔ bárɔ́k ntá Yesu. Básɔ́t ndɛn mfǎmʉɛt yap básɔbhɛri mɔ́mpɔŋɔ batu wu, Yesu achɔkɔ amfay.
Páílet apɛt achwe amɛm áchá ywi. Abhɨŋɨ Yesu abhɛp yi bɛ, “Wɔ kɛ ɔ́chí Mfɔ bo Israɛl?”
Mbɔk batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm báká nɛ yi, barɛm bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, ɔrɛm sayri!”
Kɛ ndu bɛkʉ bɛ mbok anɛ ákɛ́pɛrɛ taka ɛtɔk, sɛ́bhɔŋ bɛya bǒbhɛn batú bɛ bákɛ́pɛrɛ rɛm yɛ̌nyɨŋ ntá mmu ndǔ nnyɛ́n Yesu.”
Mmɛ́m ámáy nɔ́kɔ́, nnɔ Yesu arɔk aghati yi bɛ, “Mmɛ́m ɛpǎ amay.”
Nɛ Jísɔs anɛ bábhɨŋɨ bɛ Jɔ́stɔs ǎtò bhe bakak nkwɔ. Ndiɛrɛ bo Israɛl abhɛn bati arat kɛ bachi batɨ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk nɛ mɛ ndú bɛkʉ bo mándɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛnyu Mandɛm abhak nɛ bho mbɔ Mfɔ wap. Bɔ́ mankɛm báchyɛ̀ mɛ nɛpɔptǐntɨ́ tontó.
Dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ, yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ bo bághàti Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ fá amɨk, chɔŋ mángati ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ngɔrɛ́ nɛ ákʉ́ nkwɔ, nɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́nkʉ bɛ́ bákɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk yi.” 
Ató baghɔkɔ́ bhi bati apay nɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ, “Dɔ́k ká afɔ ndǔ ɛtɔk ɛgho. Arɛ́, chɔŋ mǎngɔ́ mmu anɛ ápɔ́kɔ́ ɛjɔ̌ manyiɛp. Koŋó ká yi.
Bǎkɛ́ ghɔkɔntɨk ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bárɛ́mɛ́ nyaka bɛ, “Ɛchɔŋ, mbák mǎngok Ɛyɔŋ ɛyi bǎkɛ́ gwɔt batɨ amɛm mbɔ ɛnyǔ bachǐmbɨ bhɛka bátàŋ nyaka ntí nɛ Mandɛm.”
Nɛ nsɨkɨ ntɨ bɛ́ chɔŋ Yesu Acha ankʉ bɛ mɛ nkwɔ ntwɔ awu mandú mpok.
Jɔ̌n arɛm ntá bɛyǎ bo abhɛn bárɔ̀ŋ ntá yi bɛ́ yi anjwiti bhɔ́ bɛ, “Bě bɛfé! Agha áyɛ́bhɛ́ be batú bɛ mǎnjaŋ mbi ndu bɛbʉɛ ntɛmsi Mandɛm anɛ átwɔ̀?
Nnɔ nɛ chi bákɛmɛ bɛ, “Sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ nɛ chi mmɔ́ ywɛsɛ, nɛ bɛ́ amɨ́k anɛmɛ yi tɛ̌ndu nɛbhe ɛni.
Yesu ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ máyi nɛ nkoŋo anɛ yi ákɔ́ŋɔ́ téé kɛ́kwɔ́t, arɛm ntá máyi bɛ, “Mmá, ghɔ́ mɔ́ywɛ nɔ!”
Nchí sɔt ɛrɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ngɔrɛ́ nɛbhay. Mpoknkɛm anɛ nnɛ́m achi nɛpɛ́m ɛbhé ɛ́gwɔ̀t yi nɛ nnɛ́m ɛyi. Kɛ mbák nnɛ́m agu, ɛbhé yɔ ɛ́pu pɛrɛ gwɔt yi.
mbɔnyunɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ fú amfay ntwɔ́ fá amɨk bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mɛ̌yáŋ. Ntwɔ bɛkʉ chí ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mmu anɛ átó mɛ áyàŋ mɛ̌nkʉ.
Mandɛm achi chak mpoknkɛm nɛ apu kway bɛghɔkɔntɨk bɛtɨk ɛbhɛka nɛ ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ bǎtɔ́ŋɔ́ yi ndǔ bǎkwàk batɨ bǒnkwɔ nɛ bǎrɔ̀ŋ ambɨ bɛkʉ nɔ.
Kɛ ndǔ yi áyàŋ bɛtaŋa mmʉɛt, arɛm bɛ, “Kɛ mbɔ̌ŋ nkokosi wa chi agha?”
Akʉ nɔ bɛ́ yɛ̌ mmu ákɛ́ bhɔŋ mbi bɛku nɛ yɛ̌ chi bɛti ɛnyɨŋ kpátɛ ɛrɨ̌ŋ ɛnɛ nnya mbɨ ɛmbak yi amʉɛt. Ɛrɨŋ ɛyɔ chí nnyɛ́n nnya yɔ, mbák ɛpu nɔ, mpǎy anɛ áté ndǔ nnyɛ́n ɛni.
Pɛmɛ́ mmʉɛt, nɛ fǎ ndǔ ɛkotákátí sɛp amɨk!”
Nkʉ bɛtɨk wu kɛkway bɛkɛmɛ bɛyǎ nkáp wu. Chi-bɛtɨk ywi achyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ mántí yi nɛ ngɔrɛ́ ywi nɛ bɔ̌bhi, nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́chák ɛnɛ yi ábhɔ́ŋɔ́, bɛ́ nkáp ywi ámfú.
Bákpɔ́ti manɨk anɛ́ baro bárɔ́ yɔ ankɛm anyɛ́n. Bákáŋari manɨk anɛ bagwɔ́rɛ mɛnyǔ nsɔm nɛ yɔ, básɛ́bhɛ nsɔm anyɛ́n bɛ mánók áchwí. Bátɛ́n ndɛn ɛnɛ ɛ́kɛ̀m mbʉ́ɛ́p amfay bɛ ampɔkɔ áchwí ankɔ, babho bɛrɔŋ angɔkɔnyɛ́n.
Abhɛ́p bɛ, “Ntɨkɨ mɛnyɨŋ?” Bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́fákárí nɛ Yesu anɛ Násárɛt. Achi nyaka ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm, nɛ atɔ́ŋ bɛsí bho nɛ bɛsí Mandɛm bɛ bɛtaŋ Mandɛm bɛchi nɛ yi ndǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi árɛ̀m nɛ ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ̀.
Yɛ̌ mmu amɔt ábhɨ́kɨ́ re ko amfay ɛbhak ɛnɛ Mandɛm achi, ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ fʉɛt Mmu anɛ áfú ntá Mandɛm, yi mmu áfú amfay atwɔ amɨk.
Yesu árɛ́m nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, asɔt bɔ̌bhɔ anyaŋa bhɔ amɔ anti, ayɛt bhɔ. Ákʉ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ́, arɔ nɛbhʉɛt wu arɔk ɛbhak ɛ́chak. 
Ndǔ Yesu ákʉ̀ nɔ, aghati bhɔ bɛ, Mandɛm arɛm bɛ, “Ɛkɛt ɛya ɛ́bhɔŋ bɛbhak chi ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt, kɛ bǎyibhiri yɔ ɛ́rɔp nɛbhʉɛt anɛ baghɛ́p bábhɛ̀sɛ arɛ.” Nɔ́ kɛ̌ básɨ́ŋɨ́ amɛm Ɛkáti Mandɛm.
Bɔ̌ma, sɛ́yàŋ mǎndɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm ɛbhɛn bakwɔ́ bho Kristo abhɛn atú Masidónia bátɔ́ŋɔ́.
Nɛ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛpɛt ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Aisáya arɛm nyaka bɛ, “Chɔŋ ɛbhárɛ́mɔ Jése antwɔ́. Ǎtwɔ̀ bɛbhak Mfɔ ntá bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl, nɛ chɔŋ mámbaka ntɨ bɛ yi ampɛmɛ bhɔ.”
Mpɛt nchí sɛmti be bɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ aka bɛ mansyɛp yi abhɔŋ bɛbhʉɛrɛ bɛbhé mɛnkɛm.
Matá ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ Yesu, arɛm bɛ, “Acha, mbɔ ɔchí fá, mbʉ mɔ́maya abhɨkɨ gu!
Ɛyɔ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ yɛ bɛ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt nɛchak nɛbhʉɛt ambɨ ntá bo Mandɛm.
Kaká ká bo Mandɛm báchák abhɛn báchí bakoŋo Yesu Kristo awu mankɛm ntá ya. Batɨ̌ bakoŋo Yesu abhɛn báchí fá Rom nɛ mɛ bátó nkwɔ bhe bakak.
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka ankɛ́m mmʉɛt ɛyi,   ɛnyu ɛnɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛni nɛ́bhak pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí Mandɛm, nɛ bo mámbɔŋ kɛnókó nɛ yi.
Ngɔrɛ́ wu apú nyaka mmu Israɛl. Bábhe yi chi atú Síria ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt agho anɛ́ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ Fonísia. Anɨk Yesu mmʉɛt bɛ ambok ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ yɔ ɛ́mfu mɔ́ywi amʉɛt.
Mpok yɔ, mbák ɛ́fákárí bɛ́ mmu ǎkʉ bɛtɨk amfǎy ɛkɛt ɛyi, ákɛ́ sɔŋɔri mmʉɛt bɛsɛp kpɨk bɛ andɔk amfɛrɛ mɛnyɨŋ anywɔ́p kɛ ambʉɛ.
Satan arɔk arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Mbák ɔchí Mmɔ Mandɛm, chyɛ̌ ɛyɔŋ bɛ ntǎy ɛnɛn nɛ́njíbhírí nɛ́ndɔp ɛkpɔkɔ́ brɛd.”
Yesu apɛt arɛm bɛ, “Ɛtaya achyɛ́ mɛ mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm. Yɛ̌ mmu abhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mmu anɛ Mmɔ áchí ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ fʉɛt chí Ɛtayi. Nɛ yɛ̌ mmu abhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ mmu Ɛta áchí ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ fʉɛt chí Mɔ́ywi nɛ bǒ abhɛn yi áyábhɛ́ ndu bɛkʉ bɔ mándɨ́ŋɨ́ Ɛtayi.”
Ágháká nɔ́kɔ́ arɛ́, mbɔk bǒnkwɔ Fárisi bárɔ́k mɛmɔ yi, bábhɛp yi bɛ, “Yɛ̌ yí, yɛ̌ yi, ɛbhé ɛyɛsɛ ɛka bɛ mmu ándɔ́ ngɔrɛ́ ywi ndǔ nɛbhay kɛ ɛbhɨkɨ ka?”
Básɔt yɛ ɛtaŋtí nnya mbʉ́mbʉ nɛ bɔángɛl abhɛn bachi antɛn yi báfɛmɛri amɨk. Bábhɨ̀ŋɨ nnyɔ́ anɛ tɛ nyaka yɔ bɛ Mfɔ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ, nɛ nnyɛ́n ɛni nɛchak bɛ Satan, ndu yi achi mmu árwɔ̀ bǒ mmɨk.
Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ chɔŋ Ábraham nɛ bɛbhárɛ́bhɔ bhi mányiɛ mmɨk. Ɛpú nyaka chi ɛ̌ti Ábraham abhʉrɛ bɛbhé. Bɛfʉɛt ndǔ nɛka Ábraham kɛ Mandɛm ásɔ́rɛ́ yi bɛ achi chak.
Mbʉ́ nkɔŋ bɛ yi andɔp fá ánkwáká nɔ́kɔ́ mɛ ndǔ kɛnɔŋ ɛkɛ́nɛ nchí arɛ ɛ̌ti Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́. Mbʉ yi arɔp fá bɛkwak mɛ ndǔ ntí ywɛ.
Arɛm yɛ ntá Tɔmás bɛ, “Tɔ́k bɛrɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛchi ndu amɔ́ ya nɛ kɛnɔŋámɔ ɛkɛ ghɔ. Sá awɔ́ fá ndǔ tambe wa. Kɛ́pɛrɛ makati. Bák mmu anɛ ánòko!”
Nɔ́ kɛ ɛ́chí nɛ mmu batɨ ápáy mbɔnyunɛ apú te kákáti ndǔ yɛ̌nyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ yí ákʉ̀. 
Ndǔ ngwɛnti, Yesu nɛ baghɔkɔ́ bhi bákwáy nɛkwáy báchyɛ́ Mandɛm bakak. Báfú yɛ bákó amfay Njiɛ Mɛnɔk Ólif. 
Kɛ nkɛmɛ bɛ ‘Acha wáwák! Mbɨ́kɨ́ re nyiɛ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́pú pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí ɛbhɛ.’
Kɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛ́mɔt ɛchi nɛ bhe ɛnɛ́ mbɨ́kɨ́ kɔŋ. Ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ́ mbɨ ɛnɛ́ bǎbhɔŋɔ nyaka nɛ mɛ ɛpɛt ɛpu.
Nchí rɛm nɔ mbɔnyunɛ mbɔk bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ Mandɛm mánɔ́nɛ bachwe ndǔ nkwɔ yɛka. Bɔ mánù bɛyibhiri Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhi nɛ bhɛsɛ. Bákʉ̀ nɔ ndu bárɛ̀m bɛ Mandɛm áchyɛ́ bhɛsɛ ngǎngaŋ bɛ sɛnchwe ndǔ barak ɛpúsí. Bábyàk Yesu Kristo ɛnɛ́ yi kɛ achi Ɛta ntá yɛsɛ nɛ yi aywǐnti kɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bhɛsɛ. Mǎnaŋ basɨŋ nyaka tɛntɛp bɛ chɔŋ Mandɛm antɛmsi mɛnyǔ bǒbhɔ.
Yesu nɛ bakoŋo bhi básɛ́bhɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ antɛn njiɛ, bátɛ́mɛri bɛyǎ bo abhɛn báchɛ́mɛ́ arɛ́ mánòŋ bhɔ. Mmu amɔt afú ndǔ ɛka yɔ, arɔk, atɛp mánɛ́n bɛsí Yesu,
[Nnyɛ́n Ba-Jesus nɛchak nɛchi nyaka bɛ́ Ɛ́límas nɔ chi mǔnjɔ ndu ɛyɔŋ Grik.] Ɛ́límas mǔnjɔ abho bɛ́kɛm ɛpʉ́ítí nɛ bhɔ ndu yi áyàŋ bɛ́kʉ gɔ́bhanɔ ákɛ́ koŋo mbi Yesu.
Fílip afa, arɔk aghati Andru. Bɔ́ bati apay bárɔ́k baghati Yesu.
Yesu apɛt arɛm bɛ, “Chɔŋ mpɛt njɛnti Kɛfɔ Mandɛm nɛ yi?
Sɛ́nkáká nɔ́kɔ́ Mandɛm ndǔ akap anɛ yi áchyɛ́ anɛ mmu apú kway bɛrɛm ɛnyǔ wu achí.
Yesu arɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ ɛtayi achyɛ yi bɛtaŋ amfay mɛnyɨŋ mɛnkɛm, nɛ bɛ́ yí afú chí ntá Mandɛm nɛ ǎpɛ̀tnsɛm ntá Mandɛm.
Bǎchí nyaka mbɔ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n anɛ́ ánɛ́mɛ́ ɛbhɨ, kɛ nɛ́nɛ bápɛtnsɛm ntá Mbabhɛri bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n, mmu achi Mbabhɛri bapɛ́m ayɛka.
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ rɨ bɛ yi ántwɔ́ tɛ́mchok antɛmɛri bhe ndǔ bǎbhʉ̀rɛ kɛŋɔ.
Abhɛn ɛkɔŋ, bǎkɛ́ noko yɛ̌ntɨkɨ Ɛfóŋó, kɛ bǎbhɔŋ bɛchak ɛnɛ́ ɛchi ansɛm ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mmu árɛ̀m ndu bɛghɔ mbák chi Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm mbɔnyunɛ, barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ nsé báya fá amɨk.
Bágó yi ndǔ ɛkotákátí mpok nywɔp nɛ́ghaka nkárɛnka nɛ́nɛnamɔt.
Báchyɛ̀ chɔŋ be bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm ɛ̌ti bǎkoŋo mɛ, mbɔnyunɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ mmu anɛ átó mɛ fá amɨk.
Sɔ̌l akɛmɛ bɛ, “Acha, chí wɔ agha?” Ɛyɔŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́kɛ́mɛ yí bɛ, “Mmɛ Yesu kɛ ɔ́kòŋo gbɔkɔ́gbɔkɔ ɔnchyɛ nɔkɔ nɛnyok.
Ndǔ mpok anɛ áfʉɛ́rɛ́ ansɛm, bǎkʉ nyaka mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mpok bachi ndǔ ɛsɨ́ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛka.
Chɔŋ ntwɔ́ bɛghɔ bhe mpok nnáŋ mfʉɛ́rɛ́ atú Masidónia mbɔnyunɛ mbɔ̌ŋ ntɨ bɛfʉɛt arɛ.
Mɔ́wu akɛmɛ bɛ, “Mpú rɔ́ŋ.” Kɛ ansɛm mpok, awupsi ntɨ arɔk.
Nɛghɔ́ anɛ bághɔ́ Yesu, babho bɛbɨk mándɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ, “Mmɔ Mandɛm, ɔbhɔ̌ŋ ntɨkɨ ndak nɛ bhɛsɛ́? Ɔ́twɔ́ bɛchyɛ bhɛsɛ ntɛmsi ɛnɛ́ mpok abhɨkɨ re kway?”
Mbák ɛ́pókómʉɛt ɛ́mɔ́t ɛ́ghòk bɛbe, bɛ́chák mɛnkɛm bɛ́ghòk bɛbe, nɛ mbák báchyɛ̀ ɛpókómʉɛt ɛ́mɔ́t kɛnókó, bɛ́chák bɛ́bhɔŋ maŋák nɛ yɔ́.
bɛ yɛ̌ mmu ywɛka amɔt ákɛ́ kwɛn ansɛm ɛ̌ti bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛn. Bě babhɔŋ bǎrɨŋɨ bɛ, bɛkoŋo nkaysi Mandɛm, bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛn bɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́tɛ́mɛ́ri bhɛsɛ.
Stífin akɛmɛ bɛ, “Bɔmá nɛ bɔta, ghók ka mɛ! Mandɛm bɛtaŋ mɛnkɛm abhesi nyaka ntá chi-mbɨ aywɛsɛ́ Ábraham mpok yi achi atú Mɛsopotemia kɛ árɔ̀ŋ ɛtɔk Haran,
Ndak anɛ ákʉ́ batɨ ábé baghɔkɔ́ bhi amɛm, bábho bɛbhɛp Yesu amɔt amɔt bɛ, “Puyɛ̌ mɛ, pú nɔ?”
mbák bábhɛ̀p bhɛsɛ ɛchɔŋ ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ̌ ɛbhɛn sɛ́kʉ́ ntá mbɛ́ntí-nɛ, nɛ ɛnyǔ ɛ́fákárí kɛ yi ǎtaŋ,
Nɛ mmɨkɨ nɛ ǎfʉɛ̀rɛ fʉɛt nɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhi ɛbhɛn bo máŋwaka bɛbhɔŋ. Kɛ mmu anɛ ákʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áyàŋ bo mánkʉ, ǎbhak nɛpɛ́m mpoknkɛm. 
Mmu amɔt abhak amɛm ɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛtí ɛyɔ anɛ awɔ ywi ágú. Mbɔk bo bábhák arɛ́ abhɛn báyàŋ mbi bɛ́rɛ́m bɛ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bɛ́chí nɛ Yesu. Bábhɛ́p Yesu bɛ, “Ɛbhé yɛsɛ ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ ɛ́pu chak bɛbu mmu ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywěmʉɛt kɛ?”
Nɛ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛnaŋ ɛrɛm nyaka tɛsáy bɛ́ chɔŋ Mandɛm ankʉ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl mámbak chak bɛsí ɛbhi mbɔnyunɛ bábhɔ̌ŋ nɛka nɛ yi. Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́pɛt ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ Mandɛm aghati nyaka Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ntá Ábraham bɛ, “Ɛ̌ti yɛ, chɔŋ njɛt manɛrɛ́kɛrɛ bhǒ mmɨk ankɛm.”
Kɛ báchwɔ́bhɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ amɛm nkɨ, bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk ndǔ nkɨ bákɛ́m bhɔ. Bádɛ́n amɔt, báwáy áchák, bátɛ́mtí anɛfú nɛ batay.
Fɛstɔs abhak nɛ bhɔ́ mbɔ manywɔp ánɛ̀n nɛ byó. Apɛt yɛ nsɛm Seséria. Nɛ́yi nɔ́kɔ́, achɔkɔ ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ manyé ɛyi, achyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ́ mánsɔ́t Pɔ̌l mántwɔ́ nɛ yí.
Mpok Mandɛm mmu achi Ɛta átɔ́ŋɔ́ kɛnɛ́m ɛki nɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi, sɛbhak arɛ nɛ Yesu. Sɛ́ghók ndu Mandɛm mmu acha mankɛm árɛ̀m bɛ, “Nɛ́ chi Mɔ́wa. Nkɔŋ yi tontó. Ǎchyɛ̀ mɛ bɛyǎ kɛnókó.”
Mmǔfú anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ́ Símun achí nyaka ɛtɔk ɛyɔ nkwɔ. Abhak mǔnjɔ. Anaŋ ákʉ̀ nyaka mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ ndu ɛrɔri mpok, andɛmɛ nɔkɔ bɛ́ yí achí ɛtaŋtí mmu. Bǒ Samária babhak maknkay bɛ́ghɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ̀.
Kɛ kɛ́nkwɛ́sɛ́ anɛ árɔ́ mmʉ́ɛt myáká myáká ndu ɛpɔ̌ nɛpɛ́m, achí ngú ndǔ ɛfóŋó, yɛ̌ndu abhʉɛ́t nɛpɛ́m ndǔ nkwɔmʉɛt.
Chiɛ́ ká yi kɛnókó mbɔnyunɛ ntí ywi áyaŋá rɔŋ ɛ̌ti bɛtɨk Kristo. Chiɛ̌ ká yi kɛnókó nɛ ntí bɛ́ be kɛ bǎtó yi antwɔ tɛ fá ankwak mɛ tɛ̌ndu be babhɔŋ bǎpú kway nyaka bɛ́twɔ.
Bɔ̌ma, mbák chi bhe, Mandɛm abhɨ́ŋɨ́ be bɛ bǎkɛ́pɛrɛ bhak basɛm antɛn bɛbhé, kɛ nɛfɛrɛ anɛ bafɛrɛ bhe ndǔ kɛsɛm ákɛ́ bhak ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ̀ mǎnkáysí bɛ bǎkway bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mmʉɛt nkwǎ áyàŋ mmu ankʉ. Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎbhɔŋɔ bɛkʉ chi bɛkwak batɨ ndǔ ɛkɔŋ.
Bɛrɨ̌ndu Yesu Kristo Acha mɛ́mbák nɛ bhe mankɛm.
Nsɛm apú bhak ndǔ nnɛrɛ́kɛt mpoknkɛm. Mmɔ̌ nnɛrɛ́kɛt kɛ ábhák arɛ mpoknkɛm.
Mpok yɔ, mbɔk barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ báfú Yerúsalɛm barɔk Antiɔk.
Yesu arɛm ntá bakoŋo bhi bɛ, “Bě mkpáká bho anɛ́ ábhɨkɨ bhɔŋ nɛka nɛ mɛ, bě bhó bǎyìbhiri tɛtɛp ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛchak, chɔŋ mpɛt ntat nɛ bhe ná? Chɔŋ nkɛ́pntɨ nɛ bhe ngaka fá? Twɔ́ ká nɛ mɔ́wu ntá ya.”
Bo bárɛ́m ntá Yesu bɛ, “Bakoŋó Jɔ̌n Njwiti bátat nɔkɔ nsay ndu mɛnɨkmʉɛt. Bakoŋó nkwɔ Fárisi bákʉ̀ ɛnyumɔt. Kɛ abhɛ mányiɛ, mányu nɛ bapu tat nsay?”
Mandɛm mmu ághókó mmɨk nkɛm nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́chí arɛ́, yí kɛ áchí Acha anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ mɛnkɛm amfay nɛ fá amɨk. Apú chɔkɔ amɛm bɛkɛt ɛbhɛ́n bakwǎŋwaŋ bághókó.
Ɛnɛ́ Yesu árɔ̀ŋ nɛkɔ, mmǔfú ajiɛt, arɔk, atɛp mánɛ́n bɛsí bhi, abhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, wɔ mmǔ ndɨ́ndɨ́, chɔŋ nkʉ yi kɛ mbɔ̌ŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛ́n nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti?”
Júda mmɔ̌ Jekɔ́p, Jekɔ́p mmɔ̌ Áisek, Áisek mmɔ̌ Ábraham, Ábraham mmɔ̌ Tɛ́ra, Tɛ́ra mmɔ̌ Náhɔ,
Chɔŋ mǎngók nsóŋó nɛnu, mǎngok mbok ɛ̌ti manu anɛ achi nɛkɔ nɛsiɛ nɛ anɛ átwɔ̀ ansɛm. Kɛ bǎkɛ́ chay. Mɛnyǔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ bɛ́bhɔŋ bɛfakari, kɛ ɛyɔ ɛpu tɔŋ bɛ ngwɛnti mmɨk aghaka.
Yesu apɛt aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Nchí rɔ bhe, bɛ́rɔŋ. Nnáŋ ndɔ́k, chɔŋ mǎnjaŋ mɛ. Kɛ bǎgu chɔŋ ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛka. Bǎpú kwáy bɛ́twɔ ɛbhak ɛnɛ mɛ́rɔ̀ŋ.”
Yesu arɛm yɛ ntá yi bɛ, “Ghɔ́ mbaŋ. Nɛka ɛnɛ́n ɔbhɔŋɔ nɛ mɛ nɛ́kʉ ɔtaŋ.”
Nɛ́yí nɔkɔ, Yesu afa ɛtɔk, arɔk ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bo bápú arɛ́. Bǒ babho bɛyaŋ yi. Bághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ yí, babho mɛnɨkmʉɛt bɛ́ ákɛ́ rɔ ɛtɔk ɛyap.
Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ akʉ nyaka mbɔ̌ŋ Mfɔ Debhít arɛm bɛ Mandɛm Acha arɛm nyaka ntá Acha wa bɛ, ‘Chɔkɔ́ fá ɛbhě awɔ́nɛm ɛya ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛnókó, kpatɛ nkʉ bǒmpap abhɛ mámbak mbɔ ɛnɔk ɛnɛ ɔ́nyàŋa bɛkak arɛ́.’
Mmu anɛ árɛ̀m ɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛnɛ yi ábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ, anɨ́kmʉɛt bɛ Mandɛm ánchyɛ́ yi akap mɛ́nɛ́nɛ́ nta bho ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ̀m ndǔ ɛyɔŋɔ́tɔk ɛnɛ yi abhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ.
Mmǔ anɛ ɛfóŋó ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛsɔŋɔri yí akwɛ́n bɔ́ amʉɛt arakati ndɛn ɛyap nɛ aták bɔ́ mankɛm kpát bábʉɛ́ báfú bɛbho bɛwɔ nɛ bɛfʉɛt amʉɛt.
Bachǐ-bhɔ, bǎkɛ́ kʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́kʉ̀ bɔ̌bhɛka mambe ntɨ. Mbák mǎnkʉ nɔ, bákway bɛfɛrɛ amɔ.
Tɛ́mté wu, chimɔ arɛm nɛ ɛyɔŋ amfay bɛ, “Nnókó kɛ nɛka ɛná nɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ taŋ. Kwak mɛ nnókó sayri.”
Nɛ wɔ mɔ́wa, chɔŋ mámbɨŋɨ wɔ bɛ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ anɛ Mandɛm Acha, mbɔnyunɛ́ chɔŋ ɔ́njambɨ kɛ Acha antwɔ, bɛ ɔntoŋti mbi ntá yi,
Ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛsɛ fá amɨk sɛ́bhɔ̌ŋ nɛka nɛ yi. Sɛ́pú ghɔ yi nɛ amɨ́k.
Ná nɛ mmu anɛ ábyak Mmɔ Mandɛm? Bǎkaysi bɛ ntɨkɨ ntɛ́msí anɛ ábɛ́bhɛ́ áchá ákwáy nɛ yi? Ɛnyǔ mmu wu ǎsɔ̀t manoŋ nku anɛ ákʉ́ yi ambak pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí Mandɛm mbɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛpú nyáŋá, nɛ ǎrɛm ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ mmu ákʉ̀ bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm mɛ́mbak nɛ bǒbhi.
Nɛ Ɛta, yímbɔŋ, mmu átó mɛ áté mɛ ntísiɛ. Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ re ghok ɛyɔŋ ɛyi, bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ re ghɔ́ ɛnyǔ yi achi.
Nku mbɨ anɛ Mandɛm ányú nɛ bo Israɛl abhɔ̌ŋ nyaka bɛbhé ɛbhɛn bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ ɛnyǔ bo babhɔŋɔ bɛchyɛ Mandɛm kɛnókó, nɛ ɛtɛm ɛbhak fá amɨk ɛnɛ́ bǒ báchyɛ̀ yi kɛnókó arɛ́.
Nɛ́nɛ, mbɔŋ maŋák ndu bɛsɔŋɔri ɛbhɛn mɛ́bhɔ̀ŋ mbɔnyunɛ bɛ́kwàk bhe. Nchí bhɔŋ bɛsɔŋɔri ndǔ nkwɔmʉɛt mbɔnyunɛ nchí naŋa bɛbhɔŋ bɛsɔŋɔri mɛnkɛm ɛbhɛn bɛrɔbhɛ nyaka bɛ Kristo ámbɔ́ŋ, ɛ̌ti bǒnkwɔ. Bǒnkwɔ Kristo bhɔ chi mmʉɛt ɛyi.
Nɛ bɛyǎ bo báchák mánóko ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Yesu aghati bhɔ.
Nɛpɛ́m nkwǎ nɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ cha nɛnyíɛ́? Nɛpɛ́m nkwǎ nɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ cha ndɛnɛ́?
Yɛ̌ agha anɛ ánókó Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ nɛ bǎjwíti yi, Mandɛm ǎpɛmɛ yi ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bɛ ámbák mmǔ ywi mpoknkɛm. Kɛ mmu anɛ abhɨkɨ ka mɛnoko, Mandɛm ǎchyɛ yi ntɛmsi ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhi bɛbhʉɛt nɛ yi.
Mbɔk bo abhɛn báté kɛ́kwɔ́t báyɨ̀ŋɨ, bághók nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ Yesu ábɨ́kɨ́ ɛnyu ɛyɔ, báré rɛm nɛ batɨ bɛ, “Ghók ka, ǎbhɨŋɨ Ɛláija!”
Ɛfʉɛrɛ nɔkɔ bɛyǎ manywɔp, bǒbati bo Israɛl báté ɛyu bɛway Sɔ̌l.
Ɛkaká nɛkɔ ɛyɛka ɛbhɔŋ bɛtɔŋ bɛ bǎchi barɨŋɨ́ndak bɛsí bo abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ Mandɛm, nɛ bǎkɛ́ chɔŋti yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mpok anɛ bǎbhɔŋɔ mbi bɛghati bɔ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́.
Satan asɔt yi akó ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ achi tɛ amfay atɔ́ŋ yí bɛtɔkɔ́ mmɨk mɛnkɛm nɛ kɛfɔ ɛkɛn kɛ́chí arɛ́ ndu mɔ́mbɨŋɨ́ mpok.
Yesu ayibhiri mmʉɛ́t ayɨŋɨ bɔ́ mankɛm, arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Nyabhɛ́ awɔ́ ywɛ.” Akʉ nɔ, awɔ́ ywi apɛt ataŋ, ábhák mbɔ ɛnyu ɛsɨ́.
Bǒ ɛchɛmɛ bǒbatí ɛtɔk bághókó nɔ́kɔ́ nɔ, batɨ ábe bhɔ tontó. Bábho bɛyaŋ mbi ndu bɛ́way bǒnto Yesu.
Bɛcháy bɛ́pú ndǔ ɛkɔŋ. Ɛkɔŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́jwí pɔɔt ɛ́fɛ̀rɛ mmu bɛcháy antɨ. Mmu anɛ bɛcháy bɛchi yi antɨ ǎchày chí ntɛmsi. Nɛ mmu anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛcháy chí anɛ ɛkɔŋ Mandɛm ɛbhɨ́kɨ́ jwi yi antɨ pɔɔt.
Mmu anɛ áfɛ̀rɛ mbwɔt ɛbhɨ, ǎbhɔŋ akap ndǔ bɛtɨk ɛbhi. Nɛ ǎnyokoti mbwɔt anɛ áchí chí bo abhɛn bábhɔ̀ŋ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti, bɛ mmu anɛ ápɨ̀ mbwɔt nɛ anɛ áfɛ̀rɛ yɔ ɛbhɨ, bɔ́ mankɛm mámbɔ́ŋ maŋák.
Ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ́ ɔrɔp chi mame mame, kɛ́pɛrɛ nyú yɛ̌ chí ndiɛrɛ manyiɛp. Sɔt nɔ́kɔ́ nkwɔ mandú mmɛ́m bɛ ánkwák bɛkʉ mɛniɛ ɛbhɛ mɛ́mpɔp.
Nchí ghati bhe bɛ, ɛwak ɛnɛ Mandɛm átàŋ bǒ mmɨk, chɔŋ angɔ́ ntínso nɛ bǒ ɛtɔk Sódom nɛ abhɛn Gomóra ɛncha bǒ ɛtɔk ɛnɛ́ bábhɨ́kɨ́ sɔt bhe nɛ ɛkɔŋ.”   
Arɨ́ŋɨ́ nkwɔ báráká ntianywɔp anɛ mmʉɛt ɛyap ɛ́ŋwaka bɛ mánkʉ nɛ bo abhɛn bábyak bɛfóŋó ɛbhɛn bɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ.
Bě bachǐbhɔ, mmǔ ywɛka anɛ mbák mɔ́ywi abhɛp yi tansi, ansɔt chi nnyɔ́ anchyɛ yi, chi agha?
Kɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mɛnkɛm bɛchi chi mbɔ nɛbhǒnɛt ɛnɛn bɛbe ntá ngɔrɛ́ anɛ ánòŋsi.
Yesu afa yɛ arɔk amfay Njiɛ Mɛnok Ólif mbɔ ɛnyu ɛsɨ́. Baghɔkɔ́ bhi barɔk nɛ yi.
Nɛfaŋ asay nɔkɔ ndɔŋ tándrámɔt, nde yaŋ bɛsɨŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ nɛfaŋ árɛ́mɛ́. Kɛ ngók ɛyɔŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fú amfay ndu ɛ́ghàti mɛ bɛ, “Ɔ́kɛ́ kʉ yɛ̌ mmu ándɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ nɛfaŋ ásáy ndɔŋ tándrámɔt arɛm. Kɛ́sɨŋ yɔ.”
Mbɔ̌ŋ yɛ̌ bɛcháy bɛ́kɔ́ ɛsiɛ́ nɛ nkáp aywɛ kɛ́ka ánɛ́m mbɔŋ ɛsɔŋɔri nɛ wɔ. Ɛ́kʉ́ ndɔk ntɛ́m mbok amɨk mbɛmɛ wú arɛ́. Yɨŋɨ́ ɛbhǎ nkáp ɛyɛ.
Kɛ sɛ́kɔŋ bɛghok ayɛ nkaysi mbɔnyunɛ sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak bo mankɛm bárɛ̀m chi ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti nkwɔ bho abhɛn wɔ ɔchí mmǔ wap.”
Ndu ɔ́nù, kɛ́m nɛka ɛnɛn ɔ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛ Yesu sayri. Mbɔk bho bábyàk ɛnyǔ ntɨ ɛnɛn nɛpu twɔ mmu nɛ áyɔ́mɛ, nɛ ɛyɔ ɛ́kʉ nɛka ɛnɛn bábhɔŋɔ nɛ Yesu nɛ́rɔp mbɔ áchwi anɛ́ árákátí anyɛ́n ndǔ batay. Kɛ́m yɛ̌ ntɨ ɛnɛ bɛ ɔ́kɛ́ kʉ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́twɔ̀ nɛ áyɔ́mɛ.
Ǎbʉɛ́ mbɔnyunɛ achí chí mǔbɛtɨk, nɛ ápú fyɛ́ ntí nɛ bághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n.
Sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fákárí nɛ bhɛsɛ, Mandɛm ǎsɔt yɔ ankʉ bɛ́ ɛ́ntwɔ́ nɛ bɛrɨ ntá bo abhɛn bákɔŋ yi, bo abhɛn yi ábhɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛkoŋo nkaysi yi.
Sɛ́nsɔ́t mpɔŋɔndɨ́k. Mmu ǎsɔt mɔ́mbɨŋɨ́ sɛnɔŋ amfyɛ́ yɔ́ anyu ndu bɛkʉ yɔ angok yi, andɔk yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ́ yi áyàŋ yɔ́ ándɔ́k.
Yesu arɔk amfay Njiɛ Mɛnɔk Ólif.
Achí nchiakap, puyɛ̌ chi bɛkoŋo ɛbhé ɛnɛ ɛ́rɛ̀m ɛ̌ti nnɛrɛ́kɛt anɛ nchiakap ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛfu arɛ, kɛ chi bɛkoŋo bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛn nɛpɛ́m ɛni ɛnɛn yɛ̌ mmu apu kway bɛchɔŋti.
Chɔŋ mámfyɛ́ mɛ ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri mbɔ mmǔ anɛ báfyɛ́ yi anyɛ́n ndǔ mpok anɛ bájwìti yi. Ntɨ nɛ́pú pɔp mɛ amɛm tɛ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛnɛ ɛ́ntwɔ ɛmfʉɛt!
Bájwiti yi nɛ *ɛfo ɛyi. Anɨk bhɛsɛ mmʉɛt arɛm bɛ, “Mbák bǎsɔt mɛ mbɔ mmǔ anɛ ánókó Yesu tɛtɛp, twɔ́ ká chɔkɔ́ ɛkɛt ɛyá.” Anyiɛrɛ bhɛsɛ́ ɛnyu ɛyɔ kpát sɛrɔk. 
Aghɔ́ ndɛn anɛ mánɛ́bhɛ́ nyaka ntí Yesu nɛ yɔ nkwɔ. Nɛ ndɛn ɛyɔ ɛbhak aywi nɛbhʉɛt kɛkúrí nɛnɛp.
Tɛ̌ndu Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm mmu ákʉ́ Yesu Kristo áfú ndǔ nɛwú achi nɛ bhe, chɔŋ Mandɛm ankʉ mmʉɛt ɛyɛka ɛnɛ ɛ́gù nkwɔ ɛ́mpɛt ɛ́mbak nɛpɛ́m ndǔ bɛtaŋ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ mmu achi nɛ bhe.
“Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛka abhɔŋ bɛtɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhi mbɔnyunɛ mpok Mandɛm ábhák nɛ bo mbɔ Mfɔ wap arɔp chi kɛkwɔt.”
Bati atay bábhɔ́ŋ kɛ́ŋwáŋ, báchák bati atay bábhák ɛchɨŋti.
Kɛ ná bo bákway mɛnɨkmʉɛt ntá mmu anɛ bɔ́ bábhɨ́kɨ́ noko? Nɛ ná bákway mɛnoko mmǔ anɛ babhɨkɨre ghók ɛ̌ti yi? Nɛ ná bɔ bákway bɛghok ɛ̌ti mmu wu mbák yɛ̌ mmu abhɨ́kɨ́ ghati bhɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti yi?
Bɛyǎ bo abhɛn mánókó babho bɛfu kpoŋoroŋ mánsu nɔkɔ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ bákʉ̀.
Aghati bhɔ bɛ, “Tɔ́ŋ ká mɛ nkáp kpokorok anɛ básɔ̀t bɛchyɛ ndǔ nkábhɛ́nti.” Bátwɔ́ yi nɛ ɛbhɔkɔ nkáp.
María aghoko nɔkɔ nɔ, ntí átáka yi amɛm, are bhɛp mmʉɛt ɛyi bɛ́, “Ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ bakak nɛ!”
Sɔ̌l apɛtnsɛm Yerúsalɛm are mɔ bɛ́chɛm mmʉɛt nɛ bakoŋo Yesu arɛ́, kɛ bɔ́ kɛnoko bɛ yi achi nkoŋo Yesu. Báre chay mámbʉɛ nɔkɔ yí.
Mbɨ́kɨ́ twɔ bɛbhɨŋɨ bo abhɛn bakaysi bɛ bachi chak bɛsí Mandɛm bɛ mántɨ́knsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhap, ntwɔ bɛ́bhɨ́ŋɨ chi bo babʉ́babʉ́.” 
María afa yɛ arɔk ntiɛ́t ntiɛt ntá Símun Píta nɛ nkoŋo Yesu áchák anɛ Yesu ákɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka, arɛm bɛ, “Báfɛ́rɛ́ Yesu Acha ndǔ nnɛm nɛ sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bárɔ́ŋ bábhʉ́rɛ́ yi.”
Chók ká yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛ́yɛ́mɛ́, mánkʉ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ njiɛ ngo nɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mɔ́njiɛ andɔp mmɨk nɛbhʉɛt. Nyabhɛ́ ká babhi anɛ achi ŋɔ́tí ŋɔ́tí, mǎndansi anɛ́ achi gbokotí gbókótí,
Dɨŋɨ́ yɛ́ ka bɛ, Mandɛm ǎfoŋori bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛn bo bákʉ̀ nɛ bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɔ bárɛ̀m. Kɛ apú foŋori mmu anɛ árɛ̀m bɛbɛ́ptí mɛnyɨŋ ɛ̌ti Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ.
“Ɛchi mbɔ ɛnyǔ Mfɔ Debhít asɨŋɨ amɛm Ɛkáti Bakway bɛ́: ‘Ɛkɛt ɛyi ɛ́ndɔ́p ɛwɔ́, yɛ̌ mmu kɛ́chɔkɔ amɛm.’ Nɛ Debhít apɛt asɨŋ bɛ, ‘Mmu áchák ánsɔ́t ɛ́pɔ́kɔ́ bɛtɨk ɛyi.’
Bágháká kɛkwɔt ɛtɔk ɛnɛ bárɔ̀ŋ, Yesu akʉ mbɔ bɛ ǎrɔ̀ bhɔ bɛrɔŋ ambɨ.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛfakari nyaka ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bhɛsɛ bɛ baghɔrɛ́ abhɔ bati apay bate ndǔ nku ɛpay. Amɔt afú amfay njiɛ Sináy. Nku yɔ ate ndu ntí Hága, mmu abhé bɔ abhɛn báchí ndǔ kɛsɛm.
Ɛmɛnɛ́nti yap ɛ́bhák mbɔ ɛnɛ baghɔrɛ́, nɛ ámɛ́n ayap abhak mbɔ anɛ nkʉ.
Mbák mmú achi anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ kɔŋ Yesu Kristo Acha, ɛyak ɛ́mbák nɛ yi. Acha ywɛsɛ, twɔ́!
Yesu asɔt yɛ bɛkpɔkɔ́ brɛt bhɔ bɛtay nɛ nsi ɛpay. Ayoŋ amɨ́k amfay. Achyɛ bakak ntá Mandɛm, abho bɛ́bɔ́kɔ́ti brɛt wu anchyɛ nɔkɔ ntá baghɔkɔ́ bhi bɛ mánkɔ́rɛ́ nɛ nsi ntá bɛyǎ bǒbhɔ.
Kaysí nɔ́kɔ́ ka bo abhɛn báchí ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ mbɔ bɛ bǎchi arɛ nɛ bhɔ. Kaysí nɔ́kɔ́ ka bo abhɛn batɨ̌ bakwǎŋwaŋ báchyɛ bhɔ ɛsɔŋɔri, tɛ̌ndu be nkwɔ bǎkwáy bɛbhɔŋ ɛsɔŋɔri bɔ bhɔ.
Nɛpɛ́m abhésí nyaka nɛ sɛ́ghɔ yi, nɛ sɛ́rɛ̀m ɛ̌ti yi. Sɛ́ghàti bhe ɛ̌ti Nɛpɛ́m. Abhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti nɛ achi nyaka nɛ Ɛta kɛ ǎbhesi ntá yɛsɛ́.
Tɛ̌ndu yímbɔŋ ánáŋ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ nyaka ɛsɔŋɔri nɛ mamɔ, abhɔŋ mbi bɛkwak abhɛn mamɔ átwɔ̀ ntá yap.
Ɔ́bhɔ̌ŋ bɛkʉ bǒbhɔ́ mánchók manyu yap. Bátɔ̀ŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bábhɨkɨ bhɔ́ŋ bɛtɔŋ, mánchɔŋti nɔkɔ batí bo mankɛm ndǔ mbɔk manɛrɛ́kɛt bɛ mándɔ́ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu. Bákʉ̀ nɔ, chi bɛsɔt bakáp ntá bho, ɛnɛ́ ɛyɔ chí ɛnyɨŋɨ́ ntíánwɔ́p.
Yesu arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Bɔ̌bha, bǎkɛm nsi?” Bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Ǎe.”
Nɛ́ri mmɔ̌ Mɛ́lki, Mɛ́lki mmɔ̌ Ádi, Ádi mmɔ̌ Kósam, Kósam mmɔ̌ Ɛlmádam, Ɛlmádam mmɔ̌ Ɛ́r,
Yesu kɛka yɛ̌ mmu amɔt ánkóŋó yi, ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́fʉɛt Píta nɛ Jems nɛ mɔ́mayi Jɔ̌n.
Bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm báchɔ́kɔ nɛ bǒbati ɛtɔk, báká ɛyɔŋ ɛ́mɔt, báchyɛ́ bhɔ bɛyǎ nkáp ndǔ bɛsɔŋ.
Baghɔrɛ́ bati ápay bákway bɛbhak ndǔ ntay nɛmɔt mánkɔk nɔkɔ nchwi, mánsɔt amɔt mándɔk nɛ yi, mándɔ anɛfú.” [Bǒ bati apay bákwày bɛbhak ɛbhɨ, mánsɔt amɔt, mándɔ anɛfú.]
Símun Píta akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Ɛta, ntá agha? Wɔ kɛ ɔ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́chyɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.
Nɛfú Yesu áfú amɛm áchwí, mǔfu afú ɛtɔk Gɛrása ɛyɔ akwɛsɛ yi. Bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri nyaka yi. Ndǔ ɛrɔri mpok, mmǔ wu ǎkɔ̀ nyaka chi ɛbhowɔ, yi kɛ chɔkɔ anywɔ́p. Ǎchɔkɔ nyaka ndǔ nɛbhʉ́ɛ́rɛ́ manɛm.
Nɛ ndu báyàŋ bɛway Pɔ̌l, ɛyɔŋ ɛ́rɔ́k ntá mǔngo batɛmɛ́ nɛnu Rom bɛ, ɛbyɔk ɛ́kwɛn amɛm ɛtɔk Yerúsalɛm ɛnkɛm.
Ɛnɛ́ bárɔ̀ŋ, bátɛmɛri mmǔ ɛtɔk Sírene amɔt anɛ aka nnyɛ́n bɛ́ Símun ndu áfú ɛbhɨ árɔ̀ŋ ɛtɔk. Mányiɛrɛ yi ámpɔ́kɔ́ ɛkotákátí Yesu. Símun achi nyaka chi Aleksánda nɛ Rúfɔs.
Fílip ajɛt arɔk kɛkwɔt nɛ yɔ́, aghók ndǔ mmu wu ápày ɛkáti ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ Aisáya. Abhɛ́p yí bɛ, “Ɔ̌bhɔŋ nɔ nɛjwǐmɛm ndǔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɔ́pày?”
Ɛta Tiófilɔs: Ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ bɛyǎ mámɔ bɛsɨŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛfakari ndǔ nkwɔ ywɛsɛ.
Yesu aghati baghɔkɔ́ bhi bɛ, “Bǎkɛ́ rɔ batɨ ánsɔ́ŋɔ́rí be amɛm. Sɨkɨ́ ká ntɨ nɛ Mandɛm, mǎnsɨkɨ ntɨ nɛ mɛnkwɔ.
Mpok yɔ kɛ̌ ɛrɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ Mɛ Mmǔ mfú ntá Mandɛm nchí twɔ ɛ́bhesi yɛ amfay, nɛ bǒ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nnɛrɛ́kɛt fá amɨk mámbo mɛ́miak nɛ amɔ mámbɨkɨ nɔkɔ ndǔ kɛbhɔ áyɔ́mɛ. Nɛ mángɔ nɔkɔ ndǔ Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm nchí sɛp nchí twɔ amɛm nɛbháŋ ɛnɛn mfay nɛ bɛtaŋ, mbaŋ ɛ́nkɛm ɛ́ngɔ nɔkɔ nɛ bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ Mandɛm.
Mfɔ achyɛ ɛyɔŋ bɛ́ mándɔ́k mántwɔ́ nɛ yi. Bátwɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɛ yí, arɛm ntá yi bɛ, ‘Wɔ ɛbɛ́ptí nkʉbɛtɨk nɛ! Ɔ́nɨ́kmʉɛt ndɔ́ wɔ́ ɔrɔ̌ŋ nɛ bɛyǎ nkáp anɛ ɔ́kɛ́mɛ́ mɛ.
Kánǎn mmɔ̌ Ɛ́nɔs, Ɛ́nɔs mmɔ̌ Sét, Sét mmɔ̌ Ádam, Ádam mmɔ̌ Mandɛm.
Ndǔ Pɔ̌l ákɛ̀m ɛpʉ́ítí andɛmɛ nɔkɔ ɛnyǔ mmu ákwày bɛbhak chak bɛsí Mandɛm nɛ ɛnyǔ mmu ákwày bɛ́kɛ́m mmʉɛt bɛ ákɛ́ kʉ bɛbʉ́, nɛ ɛ̌ti nywɔp ɛnɛn Mandɛm ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu, bɛcháy bɛ́kɛ́m Fɛ́liks, arɛm bɛ, “Dɔ́k kpɨ́k, nnaŋ mbɔ̌ŋ ɛ́pók chɔŋ mpɛt mbɨŋɨ wɔ.”
Ɛ́chí ɛnyu ɛyɔ mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm ákʉ́ mǎmbák bakoŋo Yesu Kristo puyɛ̌ chí ndiɛrɛ ndu mɛnoko yí, kɛ ndu bɛghɔ ɛsɔŋɔri ɛ̌ti yi nkwɔ.
Yesu ǎrɛ̀m nyaka nɔ ɛ̌ti Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ɛnɛ́ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛchyɛ ntá bo abhɛn mánóko yi. Bábhɨ́kɨ́ re chyɛ nyaka Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ ntá bo abhɛn mánóko mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm ábhɨ́kɨ́ re sɔt nyaka Yesu amfay, ánchyɛ́ yi kɛnókó.
Bǎchi nyaka chi bawú ɛ̌ti bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛka mbɔnyunɛ bábhɨ́kɨ́re fyɛ nyaka be ɛrɨŋ amʉɛt bɛtɔŋ bɛ bǎchi bo Mandɛm. Kɛ achyɛ́ bhe nɛpɛ́m nɛkɔ nɛ Kristo ndu áfóŋórí bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛsɛ mɛnkɛm.
Nɛ bápu nyiɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́fu ɛsiɛ kpátɛ mánso yɔ mbɔ ɛnyǔ ɛpɨŋ ɛyap ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ. Bábhɔŋ bɛpɨŋ bɛ́chak tontó ɛbhɛn bábhʉ̀rɛ mbɔ bɛ́so nkɔ́p, bɛkpʉrɛ, nɛ bɛte árɨk.
Ndu bǎre chɨŋti nɔ? Bǎbho bɛkoŋo Kristo ndu bɛtaŋ Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ, nɛ́nɛ, barɔbhɛ yaŋ bɛ́wɛ́nti chi ndǔ bɛtaŋ ɛbhɛka babhɔŋɔ́
Kɛ ntá yɛsɛ, sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ Mandɛm amɔt kɛ áchí. Yí chí Ɛta nɛ yi kɛ ághókó yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ. Aghókó bhɛsɛ bɛ sɛ́mbák bǒbhi. Yesu Kristo Acha achí nkwɔ chi amɔt. Mandɛm afʉɛrɛ́ ntá yi kɛ ǎghoko yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ, nɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛsɛ nɛ́fù chi ntá yi.
Ndǔ nɛpɛ́m nɛkɔ ɛnɛn, yɛ̌ mmu achi chi mmu Israɛl yɛ̌ mmu ɛtɔk ɛchak, yɛ̌ básyɛp mmu yɛ̌ bábhɨ́kɨ́ syɛp, yɛ̌ chi mmu anɛ amɨ́k ánɛ́nɛ́ yi yɛ̌ chi anɛ achi nyabhɨ, yɛ̌ chi nsɛm yɛ chi mɔ̌mɨk, mankɛm báchí ɛnyumɔt. Nnɛ́m ɛnyɨŋ chi Kristo nɛ yi achi amɛm batɨ bǒbhi mankɛm.
Nkaysi bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ yɔ achi bɛ bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl bábhɔ̀ŋ nkwɔ áfɔ́k anɛ bo Israɛl bábhɔ̀ŋ, bɛ bɔ bárɔp chi mmu amɔt nɛ bo Israɛl nɛ bɛ chɔŋ mámbɔŋ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm afyɛ́ bariɛp bɛ ǎkʉ ntá bɔ̌bhi ndǔ yi ábhárɛ́ bhɔ nɛ Kristo. Bɛfʉɛt ndǔ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu Kristo kɛ bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɔ.
Ɔ́mfoŋori bɛbʉ́ bhɛsɛ, mbɔ ɛnyu sɛ́fóŋórí bo abhɛn bákʉ́ bhɛsɛ bɛbʉ́.
Ɛwak ɛ́mɔ́t, bǒnkwɔ Fárisi nɛ bǒnkwɔ Sádusi bárɔ́k ntá Yesu bárè yaŋ mbi mɛmɔ yi. Bábhɛ́p yi ankʉ ɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛnɛ́ ɛ́bhak mbɔ ɛrɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛ́tɔŋ bɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi bɛ́fú chi ntá Mandɛm.
Ɛ́kʉ́ bátɛ́n kpɨ́k bɔ́ nɛfí. Bábho bɛsokori mámbɛbhɛ nɔkɔ batɨ bɛ,
Ná mmu ákway bɛchwe amɛm ɛkɛt ɛnɛ́ ntantaŋ angɛ́p mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhi mbák abhɨkɨ yambɨ ánkɛ́m yi angwɔt? Ǎnaŋa kɛ́m yi angwɔ́t, kɛ ánkwáy bɛghɛp mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhi.
Pú mmu akway bɛku bɔ̌kɛnɛn batay nɛ nkáp anɛ apu yɛ̌nyɨŋ? Yɛ̌ nɔ, Mandɛm apú ghɔkɔntɨk yɛ̌ amɔt.
Puyɛ̌ bɛ́gháti bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́, kɛ ákʉ̀ mɛ mpányu, mbɔnyunɛ ɛyɔ chí bɛtɨk ɛbhɛ́n Mandɛm arɛmɛ bɛ mɛmbɔŋ bɛkʉ. Nɛ mbák mbɨ́kɨ́ ghati bho Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́, ɛ́bɛ̀p ntá ya ɛ́ncha!
Ɛrɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛnɛ tɛtɛp, ɛnɛ́ ɛ́kʉ̀ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu angɔ mbaŋ ɛ́twɔ́ ntá bǒ mmɨk.
Bɛyǎ bo báre sayti yi bɛ ánchɔ́kɔ́ kpák. Kɛ akpɨk are bɨk nɛ ɛyɔŋ amfay bɛ, “Mmɔ̌ Mfɔ Debhít, ghɔ́ mɛ ntínso!”
Nkú Jɔ̌n abhak ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ baghoko nɛ babyɔk mpɔŋɔ baso. Mgbat anɛ yi ágwɔ̀t ɛbho abhak nkwɔbhɛ́nya nɛ nɛnyíɛ́ ɛni nɛ́bhak ngɛ́mtáy nɛ bawɛrɛ́ bɛtu amɛn yi ághɔ̀ amɛm baso.
Bǎkáysí bɛ́ ntwɔ fá amɨk chi bɛkʉ bo mámbák ndu kpák nɛ batɨ kɛ? Ǎe, ntwɔ chí nɛ akɔrɛ.
Mɛ̌ghati wɔ bɛsí Mandɛm mú áchyɛ̀ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ nɛpɛ́m, nɛ bɛsí Yesu Kristo mu áté ntísiɛ ndǔ tɛtɛp Mandɛm bɛsí Pɔ́ntiɔs Páílet,
Kɛ Yesu arɛm ntá yap bɛ, “Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǎyàŋ nkʉ ntá yɛka. Bǎkwáy bɛka mɛnyu nkɔ́p ɛsɔŋɔri anɛ mbɔ́ŋɔ́ mɛ́nyú? Chɔŋ mǎnkwáy bɛká bɛ́gu ɛnyu nɛwú ɛnɛn mbɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛgu?”
Ntɨkɨ ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ bachǐmbɨ bhɛka bábhɨ́kɨ́ chyɛ ɛsɔŋɔri? Nɛ báwày nyaka barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ Mandɛm abhɛn bárɛ́mɛ́ mbɨ mbɨ bɛ, Mmɔ̌ bɛtok anɛ achí chak bɛsí Mandɛm ǎtwɔ̀. Yí wu kɛ bǎtí nɛ bǎwáy.
Mbák ɔbhɔ̌ŋ ndak nɛ mmu nɛ yi ákʉ́ manyé nɛ wɔ, ɔ̌kʉ yi? Ɔ́bhɔ̌ŋ bɛ́ghɔ bɛ ndaka wu ámay ansɛm ɛnɛ́ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɔŋ ndu acha manyé. Mbák ɔ́nká yi ansɔt wɔ ambɨ ndǔ manyé, ntaŋá manyé ǎchyɛ̀ wɔ ntá bo mbɨ̌ŋ nkú nɛ bɔ mámfe wɔ.
Mbákántɨ nɛ bhe tontó. Mɛ̌dɛ̀p awɔ́ antɨ tontó ɛ̌ti yɛka. Bǎchyɛ̀ mɛ nɛpɔptǐntɨ́ tontó, nɛ yɛ̌ndu sɛ́bhɔ̀ŋ bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri, maŋák ama aya acha.
Sayri sayri, mbɔ yi ǎrɔ̀ŋ nyaka amfay ndɔŋ nɛ ndɔŋ ndu bɛchyɛ akap, mbʉ́ yi abhɔŋ bɛbhɔŋ ɛsɔŋɔri tɛ ndǔ ngwɛnti mmɨk. Kɛ abhésí ndɔŋ amɔt ndak ámáy ndǔ ngwɛnti mpok achyɛ mmʉɛt mbɔ akap anɛ ápɔ́kɔ́ bɛbʉ́ bo.
Yesu abho bɛghati bhɔ bɛ, “Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm mbɔ̌ŋ bɛghɔ bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri. Bǒbati ɛtɔk, nɛ bǒbati bachiǎkap Mandɛm, nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm bábyak chɔŋ mɛ nɛ mángwáy mɛ, kɛ ɛ́gháká nɔkɔ manywɔp arat, mpɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m.”
Ánáŋá nɔ́kɔ́ bɛtɔŋ bo arɛm ntá Símun bɛ, “Tɛ́n áchwí ndǔ ɛɛntɛm mǎngʉɛp basɨ yɛka anyɛ́n bɛ mǎnkɛm nsi.”
Chɔŋ sɛ́mbɔŋ mmʉɛt ɛkɔ tɛ́mchók, ndǔ mɔ́mbɨŋɨ mpok anɛ mmu ákiɛp amɨ́k, ndǔ mpok anɛ mmbá anɛ ngwɛnti ákwɛ́nɛ́. Mpok ɛyɔ, bawú bápɛtnsɛm ndǔ nɛpɛ́m nɛ mmʉɛt ɛnɛ ɛ́pú gu wawak; kɛ mánjibhiri bhɛsɛ abhɛn sɛchi pě tɛ́mté, sɛ́mbɔŋ mmʉɛt ɛkɔ.
Bárɛ́m ntá María bɛ, “Mmá, ɔ̌di yi?” María akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Chi ɛ̌ti báfɛ́rɛ́ Acha bárɔŋ nɛ yi, nɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ ɛbhak ɛnɛ bábhʉ́rɛ́ yi.”
Yesu arɛm yɛ bɛ, “Nchí ghati bhe bɛ nkúbhɛ́ ɛnyu yɔ kɛ̌ maŋák ǎbhák amfay ntá Mandɛm nɛ bɔángɛl ɛ̌ti mmǔ bɛbʉ́ amɔt anɛ átɨ́kɨ́nsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhi ɛncha bo bɛsa mɛnwi nsɛm nɛku nɛ anwi abhɛn bákáysi bɛ bachi chak bɛsí Mandɛm nɛ ntí apú anɛ bɔ́ bátɨ̀k nsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhap.” 
Mbák mɛ̌chyɛ̀ Mandɛm bakak kɛ nnyiɛ́ nɛnyíɛ́ ndaká yí mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́chɔ́ŋti nnyɛ́n ɛna?
Mpáy baghɔrɛ́ bákɔ̀ nyaka nkwɔ nɛ bhɔ. Bábhák baghɔrɛ́ abhɛn Yesu ábú mame yap nɛ mbɔk bábhák abhɛn Yesu ábókó bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ ɛbhɛn bɛ́sɔŋɔri nyaka bhɔ. Ngɔrɛ́ amɔt abhak arɛ́ anɛ áká nnyɛ́n bɛ María mmɔ̌ ɛtɔk Mágdala. Yesu anáŋ abok nyaka bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ tándrámɔt ɛbhɛn bɛ́sɔ̀ŋɔri yí.
Bǒ batí bachiǎkap Mandɛm nɛ batɔŋ ɛbhé Mandɛm báré yaŋ mbi bɛway Yesu bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ mbɔnyunɛ báchày nyaka ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bo bakway bɛkʉ. 
Ŋɔkɔ́ ká ɛpɨŋ ɛya, mbɔ ɛnyǔ mɛ̌ŋɔ̀kɔ ɛpɨŋɨ́ Kristo. 
Chɔŋ Mandɛm ankap yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu bɛkoŋo mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi ákʉ́.
Mɔ́nkɨ áchi nyaka ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ bágó Yesu ndǔ ɛkotákátí. Nnɛm nɛkɔ nɛ́bhák arɛ ɛnɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ re bhɛmɛ yɛ̌ ngú amɔt amɛm.
Jɔ̌n abho bɛghati bho ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi ághɔ́ nɛ amɨ́k ɛ̌ti Yesu. Yí bɛ, “Ngɔ ndǔ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm áfú amfay asɔt mkpá ɛbhóŋó are sɛp kpát ate yi amʉɛt.
Bághɔ́ŋɔ́mɛn aya ághòk ɛyɔŋ ɛya. Ndɨ́ŋɨ́ yɔ́, nɛ yɔ ákòŋo mɛ.
Arɛm nyaka bɛ chɔŋ angɔ́ bachǐmbɨ bhɛsɛ ntínso, nɛ ántɨk nku anɛ yi anyu nɛ bǒbhi.
Bágháká nɔ́kɔ́ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ Yesu achi, bághɔ mmu anɛ bɛfóŋó bɛbʉ́bɛbʉ bɛ́fú yi amʉɛt arɛ́ chɔkɔ. Abhak sayri ndǔ nkaysi yi, nɛ ndɛn amʉɛt. Bɛcháy bɛ́kɛ́m bo mankɛm.
Mpú rɛm nɔ́ chi ɛ̌ti nchɛ́bhɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ. Yɛ̌ mbɔ̌ŋ ɛnyɨŋ, yɛ̌ mbɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ, ngɔk bɛbhak mbɔ mmu anɛ ábhɨ́kɨ́ chɛp yɛ̌nyɨŋ.
Mhm, njwítí nyaka nkwɔ Stɛfánas nɛ ɛkɛt ɛyi ɛnkɛm. Mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛ́ njwítí yɛ̌ mmu achák.
Bě Nkwɔ Fárisi, manɛ́mámɨk! Ya ká mbɨ sǒ mmɛm ámók nɛ mmɛm nchán. Mbák mǎnkʉ nɔ, chɔŋ nsɛm-ámok nɛ nsɛmɛ́ nchán ɛ́ndyɛrɛ pɛ́pɛ̌pɛ́p nkwɔ.
Nɛ mbák chí bǒmpap abha bhɛn, abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ yaŋ nyaka bɛ mbák mfɔ wap, twɔ́ ká nɛ bhɔ fá, mǎngwáy bhɔ́ bɛsí bha.’” 
Kɛ ndu yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛtɔk, yɛ agha anɛ áchày Mandɛm ankʉ nɔkɔ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n bɛ́chi chak bɛsí bhi, Mandɛm ǎsɔt yi ambak mmǔ ywi.
Mbák sɛ́pu bhʉrɛ bariɛp amɛsɛ, yí ǎbhʉrɛ bariɛp ami mpoknkɛm. Kristo apú kwáy bɛ́táŋa bɛ yí apú mmu anɛ yi achi.”
Kɛ nkaysi mmu anɛ ábháy ngɔrɛ́ ǎbhák chí ndǔ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ mmɨk. Ǎyaŋ bɛkʉ chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛkʉ ngɔrɛ́ ywi ámbɔ́ŋ maŋák nɛ yi.
Mɛnyǔ bǒbhɔ bábhɔŋ bɛrɨŋɨ bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn sɛ́sɨ̀ŋ ndǔ bɛkáti mpok sɛ́pú awu, bɔ́ kɛ sɛ́kʉ chɔŋ mpok sɛ́bhak awu nɛ bhe.
Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm ɛ́re go ɛndɔk nɔkɔ chi ambɨ, nɛ mpǎy bakoŋo Yesu ayá tontó amɛm ɛtɔk Yerúsalɛm. Bɛyǎ bachiǎkap Mandɛm nkwɔ́ báre noko Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́. 
Mpɨ ɛrɨ́tí mbwɔ́t amɛm batɨ yɛka, Apólos amíákátí manyiɛp arɛ́. Kɛ Mandɛm kɛ̌ ákʉ̀ mbwɔ́t ángó.
Bɛbhak mmu Israɛl ǎkʉ̀ mmu ánchá bo abhɛn bapu bo Israɛl kɛ? Nɛ nsyɛ́p ǎkwak mmu ndǔ ntɨkɨ mbi?
Baghaka nɔkɔ Yerúsalɛm, Yesu arɔk achwe amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm. Abók bakɔ̌siɛ nɛ bo abhɛn bákù mɛnyɨŋ. Atakati bɛ́fɛ́mɛ́ bo abhɛn bákɔ̀ ɛsiɛ bakáp bɛwupsi. Atakati nkwɔ́ mɛnɔk bo abhɛn bátì bɛbhóŋó,
Chiɛ́ bhɛsɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nywɔp, ɛnǐ nɛnyíɛ́.
“Ndaká yí baghɔkɔ́ bhɛ bápú koŋo bɛpɨŋ ɛbhɛn bachǐmbɨ bhɛsɛ? Bápú so amɔ kɛ manyíɛ́ nɛnyiɛ.”
Mmɨk amay yɛ, Yesu Kristo ansɔt awɔ́nɛm amfǎy bɛfóŋó ɛbhɛn bɛ́bhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛtaŋ amfǎy bho, ansɔt kɛfɔ ɛki anchyɛ ntá Mandɛm mmu achi Ɛtayi.
Kristo ákʉ bɛ bɛbhé ɛbhɛn Mandɛm áchyɛ́ nyaka ntá Moses bɛkɛpɛrɛ bhɔŋ bɛtaŋ, bɛ́ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu anɛ ánókó ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Kristo akʉ ntá yi ámbák chak bɛsí Mandɛm. 
Chɔŋ bǒ mándɔk arɛ nɛ bɛrɨ́tí mɛnyɨŋ nɛ kɛnɛ́m ɛkɛn bɛtɔkɔ́ mmɨk.
Kɛ chi bɛ ɔ̌sɔ̀t bɛyǎ bɛrɨ̌ntɨ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm átɔ̀ŋ bhɛsɛ, nɛ nɛghɔ́ anɛ yi ághɔ̀ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn sɛ́kʉ̀ mbɔ bɛ apú ghɔ, nɛ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ́ ɛyi mbɔ ɛráká ndak? Ɔ́bhɨ́kɨ́ ghɔ bɛ ntí anɛ Mandɛm átɔ̀ŋ bhɛsɛ bɛrɨ̌ntɨ chi bɛkwak bhɛsɛ sɛntɨknsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ ɛbhɛsɛ?
Ɛbhé Moses ɛ́kʉ̀ nyaka bo abhɛn bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bɛ́chí nɛ bhɔ mámbák bǒ bagho bachiǎkap, kɛ Mandɛm anyu nku akʉ Mɔ́ywi mmu ákwáy ndǔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mbi mpoknkɛm ámbák mǔngo bachiǎkap.
Apólos achí kpɨ́k agha? Mɛ Pɔ̌l nchí agha? Bɛsɛ́ sɛ́chí chí bǒ bɛtok abhɛn Mandɛm átó bɛ sɛ́nkʉ́ mǎnókó Yesu. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu ywɛsɛ́ ǎkʉ́ chí ɛbhi bɛtɨk ɛbhɛ́n Mandɛm áchyɛ́ yí ánkʉ́.
Kɛ ɛ̌ti bɛrɨ̌ndu Mandɛm, nchí mmu anɛ nchí ɛchɔŋ, nɛ bɛrɨ̌ndu bhi nɛ mɛ bɛ́pú nyaka ndɛ́ndɛm. Bɛ́pú nyaka ndɛ́ndɛm mbɔnyunɛ nkʉ́ bɛtɨk nchá yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mǔnto achak, yɛ̌ndu ɛpu chi nɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbha kɛ ndǔ bɛtaŋ Mandɛm ndǔ bɛrɨ̌ndu ɛbhi bɛchi nɛ mɛ.
Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ tat Yesu arɛm bɛ, “Agha yɛ́ áchí mmɔ̌bɛtok tɛtɛp anɛ ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ kɛboŋ nɛ mbɔŋɔ́kɛt ásɨ́kɨ́ntɨ nɛ yí? Chí mmɔ̌bɛtok anɛ mbɔŋɔ́kɛt ákway bɛrɔ ɛkɛt ntá yi, angati yí bɛ ánchyɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nɛnyíɛ́ ntá batɨ̌ bɔ̌-bɛtok ndǔ mpok.
Mɛ Pɔ̌l kɛ nchí sɨŋ ɛkáti ɛnɛ. Nchí mɔ̌bɛtok Yesu Kristo.   Mandɛm abhɨ́ŋɨ́ mɛ bɛ mbak mǔnto, abhʉrɛ mɛ nyáŋá bɛ ngati bhó Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́.
Bakoŋo Yesu bápé barɔk ebhě manyu ɛchak, baghɔ bɛ baghɔkɔntɨk bɛpɔkɔ brɛt.
Mpok Mɛ Mmu mfú ntá Mandɛm ntwɔ́, nde nyiɛ, nnyú nɔkɔ nɛ bhe. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu arɛm bɛ, ‘Yɨŋɨ́ nyiɛ̌ mɛnyɨŋɨ́nyíɛ́ nɛ nyǔmɛ́m wu. Mamʉrɛ bhi chi babhɛbhɛ́ nkábhɛ́nti nɛ bakʉ̌ bɛbʉ́ bachak!’ Kɛ dɨŋɨ́ ká bɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mmu anɛ ákòŋo mbi Mandɛm ákʉ̀ kɛ bɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ nɛrɨŋɨ́ndak ɛnɛn nɛ́fú ntá Mandɛm nɛchi tɛtɛp.” 
Bapɔkɔ́ ntó Jɔ̌n bhɔ bápɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́ nsɛm, Yesu abho bɛrɛm ntá bɛyǎ bo abhɛn bárɔ́ŋɔ́ nɛbhʉɛt anɛ yi achi ɛ̌ti Jɔ̌n bɛ, “Mpok bǎrɔ̀ŋ nyaka awu amɛm baso, bǎrɔ́k bɛghɔ ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ mmʉ? Bǎrɔk bɛghɔ mmu anɛ achi mbɔ ɛ̌nsɔ́manyiɛp ɛnɛ babhʉ́ɛ́p áfòk ɛ́nkwɛ́n ɛnɛ ɛbhe, ámfok ɛnkwɛn ɛbhe ɛ́chák kɛ?
“Bǎkɛ́ kaysi bɛ́ ntwɔ bɛ́fɛ́rɛ bɛbhé Moses. Bǎkɛ́ kaysi bɛ́ ntwɔ chí bɛfɛrɛ basɨŋɨ́ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ. Mbɨ́kɨ́ twɔ́ bɛ́fɛ́rɛ mɔ́, ntwɔ chí bɛkʉ bɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bɔ básɨ́ŋɨ́ ɛ́mfú tɛtɛp.
Yesu abho bɛkɔ atú Gálili ankɛm antɔŋ nɔkɔ bho Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm amɛm bɛkɛrɛ́ nɛnɨkɨ́mʉɛt bo Israɛl, angati nɔkɔ bhɔ nkwɔ Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ anɛ árɛ̀m ɛnyǔ Mandɛm ábhák nɛ bhɔ mbɔ Mfɔ wap. Nɛ ambu nɔkɔ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyǔ nɛme ɛnɛn bo babhɔŋɔ.
Ɛbhé ɛnɛ ɛchi mɛ antɨ ɛ́rɔ́bhɛ twɔ́ mɛ chi nɛ nɛwú.
“Bǒ ɛtɔk Síɔn,   bǎkɛ́ cháy. Ghɔ́ ká, Mfɔ ywɛka ǎtwɔ̀, chɔ́kɔ́, amfay mɔ́mpɔŋɔ batu.”
Chɔŋ amfɛrɛ bhɔ́ bɛsí bhi nɛ ndǔ bɛdíɛ́rɛ́ bhi nɛ bɛtaŋ ɛbhi, anchyɛ bhɔ ntɛmsi anɛ abhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ nchí ghati yɛ bhe chi bɛ dɔ̌ ká Ɛfóŋó Bɛdyɛrɛ anja nɔkɔ bhe mbi, nɛ bǎkɛ́ kʉ chi mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn mmʉɛt nkwǎ áŋwaka bɛ yi ankʉ.
Démas achɛn mɛ arɔ́, arɔŋ ɛtɔk Tɛsalónika mbɔnyunɛ akɔŋ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ mmɨk. Krésens arɔŋ Galéshia, arɔŋ Táytɔs, nɛ Damátia.
Sɛ́bʉ́ɛ nɔ́kɔ́ sɛ́kó ɛbhɨ. Bákʉ́ yɛ sɛ́rɨŋɨ bɛ ɛkpɔkɔ́ mmɨk ɛnɛ́ nnyɛ́n nɛ́kábhɛ chi ɛnɛ bábhɨ̀ŋɨ bɛ Málta.
Nchí rɛm nɔ mbɔnyunɛ Mandɛm achi nɛ bhe mpoknkɛm nɛ ǎkwàk bhe bɛ mǎmbɔ́ŋ ntɨ bɛ́ghok yi, anchyɛ nɔkɔ be bɛtaŋ bɛkʉ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn yi áyàŋ mǎnkʉ.
Yesu arɛm ntá yi bɛ, “Chi ɛnyu yɔ. Kʉ nɔ́, nɛ chɔŋ ɔ́mbɔ́ŋ nɛpɛ́m.”
Kɛ ntá mmu anɛ ákʉ́ ɛbɛ́ptí ɛnyɨŋ, mbák mándɛ́n wɔ ɔ́nkɛpntɨ, nsáy anɛ ɔ́bhɔ̀ŋ ǎbhák bɛ yi? Kɛ mbák ɔ́kʉ̀ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ ɛchi chak kɛ ɔ́mbɔŋ ɛsɔŋɔri nɛ ɔ́nkɛpntɨ ndǔ ɛsɔŋɔri yɔ, Mandɛm ǎbhɔ́ŋ maŋák nɛ wɔ.
Yesu ágháká nɔ́kɔ́ arɛ, ayoŋ amɨ́k amfay aghati Sakio bɛ, “Sakio, sɛp twɔ́ áyák. Mbɔŋ bɛ́bhak ɛkɛt ɛyɛ ɛchɔŋ.”
Ɛnyɨŋ bhɛ́sɛ́ bhɛ́sɛ́ ɛnɛ Mandɛm ákʉ́ sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ nɛ sɛ́nóko ɛ́chí ɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay. Agha ákway mɛ́mákáti yɔ? Ɛnyɨŋ ɛyɔ ɛ́chí bɛ yi? Ɛ́chí bɛ: Yí, Yesu Kristo akʉ mmʉɛt bɛ ámbák nkwǎ, Atwɔ́ fá amɨk, Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm átɔ́ŋ bo bɛ yí achi chak bɛsí Mandɛm. Bɔangɛl Mandɛm bághɔ́ yi. Bo bágháti bachak ɛ̌ti yi amɛm bɛtɔkɔ́ mmɨk, bǒ mmɨk mánoko yi, Mandɛm asɔt yɛ yi amfay ndǔ ɛnɔkɔ́ kɛfɔ ɛyi.
Tɛ̌ndu bǎte kpirí ndu mbi Yesu Acha, sɛ́chí sayri.
Yesu arɛm ntá mmu anɛ awɔ ágú bɛ, “Nyabhɛ́ awɔ́ ywɛ.” Anyabhɛ, awɔ́ wu ápɛt ataŋ, abhak mbɔ áchák.
Gɔ́bhanɔ ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛ́fákári, anoko Mbok Ndɨ́ndɨ́ ɛ̌ti Yesu. Ɛ́bhak yi maknkay bɛ́ghok mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bátɔ̀ŋ ɛ̌ti Yesu Acha. 
Yɛ̌ mmu apú nɛpɛ́m bɛ achi ndǔ mmʉɛt yi. Nɛ yɛ̌ mmu apú gu bɛ achi ndǔ mmʉɛt yi.
Sɛ́tò nkwɔ mɔ́mayɛsɛ achák nɛ bhɔ. Sɛ́naŋ sɛmɔ yi ndɔŋ nɛ ndɔŋ, ndu bɛyǎ babhi, nɛ sɛ́ghɔ́ bɛ abhɔŋ ntɨ bɛ́kʉ bɛtɨkɨ́ Mandɛm. Nɛ́nɛ, áchyɛ́ mmʉɛt ndu bɛkʉ bhɔ achá mbɔ̌ŋ ɛnyu ɛsɨ́ mbɔnyunɛ abháká ntɨ nɛ be tontó.
Yesu arɔk achwe amɛm ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm abho bɛbok bǒ abhɛn bákɔ̀ ɛsiɛ́ amɛm,
Bǒ Yerusalɛm nɛ bǒbatí bhap bábhɨ́kɨ́ sɔt nyaka Yesu mbɔ Mpɛmɛ anɛ Mandɛm átó. Ɛkʉ bátáŋ yi, bakpɔt manyé yi bɛ babhɔŋ bɛway yi. Nɛ ndu bákʉ́ nɔ, ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ bárɛ́mɛ́ nyaka ɛ̌ti yi ɛ́fú tɛtɛp. Nɛ yɔ kɛ bɔ bápày nyaka yɛ̌ntɨkɨ nywɔbhɛ́ nɛywɛ̌mʉɛt ɛnap.
Mɛmbɔŋ Pɔ̌l kɛ nchí nɨk be mmʉɛt ndǔ nnyɛ́n Kristo mmu ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ ɛkɛ́bhɛ́ntɨ nɛ nɛsɛptǐmʉɛt. Chi mɛ mmu mbɔk bho bárɛ̀m bɛ mpok nchí nɛ bhe bɛsí nɛ bɛsi nchí rɛm kɛpɨ nɛ bɛcháy, kɛ mpok mpu nɛ bhe nchí sɨŋ be bɛkáti nɛ bɛtaŋtí bɛyɔŋ.
Mǔngo wu abhɛ́p Fílip bɛ, “Ɛ̌tá, ghati mɛ́, ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ asɨ̌ŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi árɛ̀m nɔ́ ɛ̌ti agha? Arɛm nɔ chí ɛ̌ti mmu áchák kɛ ɛ̌ti mmʉɛt ɛyi?”
Nɨk yɛ ka mmʉɛt ntá Mandɛm mmu achi mbɔŋɔ́nkɨ bɛ́ ántó bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk mamfɛrɛ mbwɔt ɛbhɨ.”
Ɛ́chí mbɔ ɛnyǔ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Ɛ̌ti yɛ, bo báyàŋ bɛway bhɛsɛ mpoknkɛm. Básɔ̀t bhɛsɛ chi mbɔ ághɔ́ŋɔmɛ́n anɛ báyà bɛrɔŋ bɛway.”
Kɛ yí aghati mɛ bɛ, “Kɛ́chyɛ mɛ kɛnókó wáwák! Nchí chí mɔ̌bɛtok mbɔ wɔ nɛ bɔ̌mayɛ abhɛn bachi barɛmɛ́ kɛpɨ̌ntɨ, nɛ mbɔ bo abhɛn bábhʉ̀rɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn básɨ́ŋɨ́ amɛm ɛkáti ɛnɛ. Chiɛ́ kɛnókó chi ntá Mandɛm.”
Nɛ Yesu Kristo mmu achi ntísiɛ Mandɛm anɛ tɛtɛp ántɔ́ŋ be bɛrɨ̌ndu, anchyɛ bhe kpák. Yi chí mmǔ mbɨ anɛ áfú ndǔ nɛwú, nɛ Mfɔ bafɔ̌ mmɨk. Akɔŋ bhɛsɛ́ nɛ afɛ́rɛ́ bhɛsɛ ndǔ bɛbʉ́ nɛ manoŋ ami.
Píta akɛmɛ yi bɛ, “Acha, yɛ̌ báfyɛ̀ wɔ chi ɛkɛrɛ́kɛnɔŋ, yɛ báwày wɔ wáy, mɛ̌gú chi nɛ wɔ.”
Mpok ntwɔ́ awu chɔŋ mbʉrɛ ndak anɛ nɛ ɛnyǔ yi áchɔ̀ŋti nnyɛ́n ɛna bɛsí bǒnkwɔ. Ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ ɛ́may nɔ. Yímbɔŋ apú ka bɛsyɛpti batɨ̌ bǒnkwɔ nɛ ǎkàŋ tɛ bo abhɛn báyàŋ bɛkʉ nɔ, nɛ abók bhɔ bɛ mándɔ Nkwɔ Kristo.
Kɛ chi-bɛtɨk akɛmɛ yi bɛ, ‘Wɔ ɛbɛ́ptí nkʉbɛtɨk! Wɔ mbɔ́t! Ɔrɨ́ŋɨ́ sayri bɛ́ nkɔŋ bɛghɛm nɛbhʉɛt anɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ pɨ, nnyokoti nɛbhʉɛt anɛ mbɨ́kɨ́ ták mbwɔt arɛ, pú nɔ?
Bágó yi ndǔ ɛkotákátí. Básɔt ndɛn ɛyi bɛkɔ́rɛ. Bágʉɛp ɛbháŋá bɛ́rɨŋɨ anɛ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu wap ábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛ́sɔt.
Ɛnɛ Yesu árɛ́m nɔ, bo báre twɔ, kpát báyá báchá, mánjati nɔkɔ batɨ. Yesu ayambɨ arɛm ntá baghɔkɔ́ bhi bɛ, “Sɔt ka mpok nɛ yís bǒnkwɔ Fárisi. Báchi chi bǒ bɛtábhá.
Abhɛn ɛkɔŋ, ndǔ ɛ́chí nɔ́, bǎkɛ́ fyɛ́ yɛ́ amɔ ndǔ barak mandɛm nsé.
Chɔŋ mánkɛ́m yi mámfyɛ amɔ́ bǒbati abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl, mánjɔ́kɔ́ yi, nɛ mánsɔkɔti yí, nɛ mámpati yi batiɛ́ amʉɛt.
Bákɛ́mɛ yi bɛ, “Mbɔ mmǔ nɛ apú nkʉ bɛbʉ́, mbʉ́ sɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ twɔ fá ntá yɛ nɛ yi.”
Mandɛm arɔ́ bo mankɛm mǎnchwe ndǔ kɛnɔŋ ɛ̌ti nɛtaŋántɨ ɛnap bɛ yi angɔ bhɔ mankɛm ntínso. 
Chɔŋ nkʉ nɔ bɛ bǒbhɔ mankɛm mámbo bɛyaŋ mbi bɛ́twɔ ntá ya, yɛ̌ chi bo abhɛn bápú bo Israɛl, mankɛm abhɛn mbɨ́ŋɨ́ bɛ mámbák bǒbha nkwɔ.
Bák ká pě, mǎnɨk nɔkɔ mmʉɛt, bɛ́ nɛmɔ nɛ́kɛ́ dɛp be amɨk. Bǎbhɔŋ ntɨ, kɛ mmʉɛt apu bhe.”
Báfyɛ̀ yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mǔngo bachiǎkap chi bɛ anchyɛ nɔkɔ akap nɛ akabhɛ́nya ntá Mandɛm. Ndu ɛchi nɔ, nchiakap ywɛsɛ nkwɔ abhɔŋ bɛ́bhɔŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ yi áchyɛ ntá Mandɛm mbɔ akap.
Kɛ Ɛkáti Mandɛm ɛ́rɛ̀m bɛ, “Yɛ̌ agha anɛ áyaŋ bɛ́panyu, ámpányu ɛ̌ti ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Mandɛm Acha ákʉ́.”
Mbák ɔ́nká bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ, dɛm bɛ, ‘Ɛɛ’. Mbák ɔbhɨ́kɨ́ ka bɛkʉ ɛnyɨŋ, dɛm bɛ, ‘Ǎe’. Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɛcha ɛyɔ, ɛ́fù chi ntá mbʉ́mbʉ.” 
Bábhɛ́p Yesu bɛ, “Ntɔŋ, Moses asɨŋ ndǔ ɛbhé ɛyɛsɛ bɛ, mbák mmu ángú ándɔ́ ngɔrɛ́ kɛ bɔ́ kɛbhɔŋ yɛ̌ mmɔ́, mɔ́mayi abhɔŋ bɛsɔt ngɔrɛ́ wu bɛ́ ámbé bɔ nɛ yi ndǔ nnyɛ́n manɔ anɛ ágú.
Ndǔ Pɔ̌l átɔ̀ŋ Ɛyɔŋ Mandɛm, Mandɛm achyɛ yí bɛtaŋ bɛ́kʉ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay ɛbhɛ́n bo bábhɨkɨre ghɔ́.
Dɔ́k ká ambɨ bɛbhʉɛrɛ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛka ɛnyu ɛnɛ́ ɛ́tɔ̀ŋ bɛ Mandɛm akɔŋ bhe, mǎndɔk ambɨ mɛnoŋ bɛ́ Acha ywɛsɛ Yesu Kristo ánchyɛ́ bhe nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛn nɛbhɨkɨ bhɔŋ ngwɛnti ɛ̌ti ntínso ɛni.
Ndǔ nywɔbhɛ́ manyé, chɔŋ bǒ Ninivɛ mángati be bho mkpáká mmɨk anɛ ɛchɔŋ bɛ́ bɛkwɛ́nɛ́ bɛchi nɛ bhe mbɔnyunɛ mpok bɔ bághókó ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ Jóna aghati bhɔ, bátɨ́knsɛm ndǔ bɛbʉ́ bhap. Nchí ghati bhe bɛ mmu achi fá nɛ́nɛ anɛ áchá Jóna, yɛ̌ nɔ, bǎpú ghok yi! 
Ndǔ Pɔ̌l árɛ̀m mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛyǎ bo abhɛn bachi arɛ́ bátá batú mángoko nɔkɔ sayri. Kɛ nɛtaka yí átáká bo Israɛl bɛyǎ bǒbhɔ bábho bɛbɨk nɛ ɛyɔŋ ɛtaŋataŋ bɛ, “Naŋá ká yí, apú mmú ábhák nɛpɛ́m.”
Kɛ mbɔk bǒ bábhʉɛt ndǔ nkwɔ yɛka awu ɛtɔk Sádis abhɛn bábhɨ́kɨ́ nyɔp nkú ɛyap nɛ bakwap. Chɔŋ bɔ mánkɔ nɛ mɛ nɛ ndɛn pɛ́pɛ́p amʉɛt, mbɔnyunɛ bákway bo abhɛn bákɔ̀ nɛ mɛ.
Afɔ̌ kɛ̌ bakoŋo Yesu bájwimɛm bɛ Yesu abhɨkɨ sɛmti bhɔ chi ɛ̌ti yís anɛ báfyɛ̀ ndǔ flawa, kɛ ɛ̌ti mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bǒnkwɔ Fárisi nɛ ɛbhɛn bǒnkwɔ Sádusi bátɔ̀ŋ. 
- Gáyɔs mmu mɛ́chɔ̀kɔ ɛkɛt ɛyi, nɛ nkúbhɛ́ arɛ́ kɛ̌ bǒnkwɔ báchɛ̀m, ǎtò be bakak. Ɛrástɔs, mbʉrɛ nkáp ɛtɔk nɛ máyɛsɛ Kwátɔs bátò bhe bakak. Áfɔ́k Yesu Kristo Acha ambak nɛ bhe mankɛm. Amen.
Arɛ́, ǎnoŋ Mandɛm ankʉ bǒmpap abhi mámbák mbɔ ɛnɔk ɛnɛ yi ányaŋa bɛkak arɛ.
Báyók nkú yi amʉɛt, básɔ́t nkú chu báfyɛ́ yí amʉɛt.
Kɛ bo abhɛn babhɨkɨ bhɔŋ mpok nɛ batɨ ndu báyɨ̀ŋɨ chi mmʉɛt ɛyap, nɛ bápu koŋo tɛtɛp ndu nɛpɛ́m ɛnap kɛ bákoŋo chi bɛbʉ́, chɔŋ Mandɛm antɔŋ bɔ bɛběntɨ ɛbhi, anchyɛ bhɔ ntɛmsi.
Nɛrɛm Yesu árɛ́mɛ́ nɔ, ntíánwɔ́p akɛm bǒmpap abhi mankɛm. Kɛ bɛyǎ bo bábhɔ́ŋ maŋák bɛ yi ǎkʉ̀ mɛnyɨŋɨ́ maknkay bhɔ mɛnkɛm. 
Ngɔ́ batɛmɛ́ nɛnu abhɛn bákɔ̀ nɛ mpɔŋɔ́ndɨk. Mmǔfu aghati mɛ mpǎy yap. Bábhak bɔ miliɔ́n bɛsa byó (,,).
Mbɔk baghɔkɔ́ bhi báré rɛm nɛ batɨ bɛ, “Ɛnɛ́ yí árɛ̀m nɔ chí yí. Yí bhɛ mandú mpok, sɛ́pú pɛrɛ ghɔ́ yí, nɛ mandú mpok chɔŋ sɛ́mpɛt sɛ́ngɔ́ yi. Apɛt arɛm bɛ chi mbɔnyunɛ yí ǎrɔŋ ntá ɛtayi. Nɔ́ bɛ́ yí?”
Bǒ bhɔ bápɛt bábhɛ́p yi bɛ, “Wɔ ɔchí yɛ́ agha? Ɛláija kɛ?” Jɔ̌n yi bɛ, “Mpú Ɛláija.” Bápɛ́t babhɛp yi bɛ, “Ɔchí ndɛmɛkɛpɨ̌ntɨ anɛ Moses árɛ́mɛ́ nyaka bɛ ǎtwɔ̀?” Akɛmɛ bɛ, “Ǎe.”
Kɛ́m ká ɛrɨ́tɨ́ ɛkakánɛkɔ yɛka nɛntɨ bo abhɛn babhɨkɨ rɨŋɨ Mandɛm bɛ yɛ̌ bárɛ̀m chi ɛbʉ́bʉ ɛ̌ti yɛka, mánáŋ mángɔ́ bɛrɨ́ ɛbhɛn bǎkʉ̀, mánchyɛ kɛnókó ntá Mandɛm ndǔ nywɔp ɛnɛn yi átwɔ bɛtaŋ bo.
Bághɔ́ ɛkɛt ɛnɛ nɔ́ nɛ́té arɛ tɛbhɛ tɛbhɛ, barɔk bachwe amɛm, baghɔ mmɔ́ nɛ máyi María. Bátɛ́p mánɛ́n amɨk bare chyɛ yi kɛnókó. Mánɛ́nɛ bɛbha bhap bafɛrɛ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́yá nkáp báchyɛ́ mbɔ awap akap ntá yi. Ɛ́mɔt ɛbhak pú, ɛ́chák ɛ́bhák ɛnyǔ sɛrwɔ́ ɛsɛn bádùrɛ sɛ́nchyɛ nɔkɔ ɛrɨ́tí ɛriɛp.   Ɛnɛ́fú ɛ́bhák ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ básɔ̀t bɛghoko ngú bɛ ákɛ́ chɔŋti.
Nkʉ bɛtɨk achák atwɔ arɛm bɛ, ‘Acha, ghɔ́ ɛbhǎ nkáp ɛyɛ. Nnɛp nyaka wu ndǔ ɛbhɔ́kɔ́ndɛn mbɛsɛ. Mbɨ́kɨ́ kʉ ɛnyɨŋ nɛ wu.
Kɛ Yesu aghoko nɔkɔ nɔ arɛm ntá Jairɔs bɛ, “Ɔ́kɛ́ cháy. Dɔ́kɔ́ rɔŋ ambɨ mɛnóko, chɔŋ mɔ́ywɛ antaŋ.”
Báchák bɛ, “Chi Mpɛmɛ Mandɛm afyɛ́ nyaka bariɛp bɛ ǎtò.” Kɛ abhɛ́nɛ́fú bárɛm bɛ, “Yi abhɔŋ bɛfu chi atú Gálili kɛ?
Ɛnɛ́ Pɔ̌l ábhʉɛ́t bɛ́táŋa mmʉɛt ɛnyu yɔ, Fɛstɔs abɨk arɛm bɛ, “Pɔ̌l, ɛbhókórí ɛ́kɛm wɔ! Bɛyǎ ɛkáti bɛ́kʉ ɛbhókórí ɛ́kɛm wɔ!”
Bɔ̌ma, ɛkʉ yɛ bɛ yɛ̌ndu báchyɛ̀ bhɛsɛ́ nɛnyok nɛ bɛyǎ ɛsɔŋɔri, batɨ apɔp bhɛsɛ amɛm mbɔnyunɛ bǎte kpirí ndu nɛsɨkɨ́ntɨ ɛnɛka nɛ Kristo.
Anɛ bɛbhǎ nkáp bɛ́páy akʉ ɛnyumɔt, abhɔ́ŋ nsáy bɛbha bɛpay.
Nɛ́nɛ, sɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ́ mɛnyɨŋ chí mbɔk mbɔk. Nɛ sɛ́ghàti bho mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn Mandɛm afyɛ́ bhɛsɛ antɨ chí mbɔk mbɔk.
Yesu ághɔ́ nɔ́kɔ́ ndǔ María ádì nɛ bo Israɛl abhɛn bátwɔ́ bɛ́wáka nɛ yi bádì nkwɔ, ɛ́tɔ́k yi tɛ antɨ, ntínso nɛ́kɛ́m yi.
Bǒ abhɛn bákɔ̀ nyaka nɛ Sɔ̌l, bághók ɛyɔŋ ɛyɔ, kɛ bɔ kɛghɔ yɛ̌ mmú. Báte manyu chochok.
Sɛ́tò yɛ Júdas nɛ Sáilas ntá yɛka. Mǎnaŋ mǎngáká awu chɔŋ mángati bhe bɛsí nɛ bɛsi nkúbhɛ́ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn sɛ́nsɨ́ŋɨ́ amɛm ɛkáti.
Yesu arɔk ambɨ bɛrɛm bɛ, “Kɛ mbák chí bhe, ɛ́rɨ ntá yɛka ɛcha, mbɔnyunɛ amɨ́k ayɛka ághɔ̀ mbaŋ, nɛ batú yɛká ághòk mbaŋ.
Báfɛ́rɛ́ nɔkɔ Píta nɛ Jɔ̌n amɔ, bápɛtnsɛm ntá batɨ̌ bǒnkwɔ Yesu, baghati bhɔ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ bǒbatí ɛkɛrákap Mandɛm nɛ bǒbati ɛtɔk bárɛ́mɛ́ ntá yap.
Kɛ nɛ́nɛ, ɛbhé ɛ́bhɨ́kɨ́ pɛrɛ bhɔŋ yɛ̌nyɨŋ bɛkʉ nɛ bhɛsɛ mbɔnyunɛ, bɛyɨŋɨ mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛn bɛ́gwɔ́rɛ́ nyaka bhɛsɛ, sɛ́rɔp chi mbɔ bawú. Nɛ́nɛ, sɛ́pɛt sɛ́pú ndǔ kɛsɛm bɛkoŋo mbi bɛbhé ɛbhɛn basɨŋɨ mbɔnyunɛ sɛ́rɔbhɛ koŋo chi mbi akɔ anɛ Ɛfóŋó Mandɛm átɔ̀ŋ bhɛsɛ. 
Nkwɔ́ bho Masidónia bákʉ́ bacha ɛnyu ɛnɛ sɛ́kàysi nyaka bɛ bákway bɛkʉ. Nnɛ́m ɛnyɨŋ anɛ bɔ báyámbɨ bákʉ́ chí bɛ báchyɛ́ nɛpɛ́m ɛnap nɛnkɛm ntá Mandɛm Acha. Báchyɛ́ yɛ mmʉɛt ntá yɛsɛ nkwɔ ndu bɛkoŋo nkaysi Mandɛm.
Bɔ́ kɛkwáy bɛ́kɛmɛ Yesu yɛ̌nyɨŋ.
Ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ́ sɛbhaka ntɨ arɛ ɛ́kɛ̀m bɛsɛ ɛrɨ́rɨ́ ndǔ nɛpɛ́m ɛnɛsɛ mbɔ ɛnyǔ ndo ákɛ̀m áchwí nɛbhʉɛt amɔt kpɛmm bɛ nnyɛ́n nɛ́kɛ pɔkɔ́ wu. Nɛbhakántɨ́ ɛnɛsɛ nɛ Yesu nɛ́kʉ́ sɛ́fʉɛ́t ɛkat sɛ́chwe tɛ amɛm mɔ́kɛrɛ kóŋ, ndǔ nɛbhʉɛt bɛdiɛ́rɛ́ Mandɛm.
Yesu arɛm ntá bakoŋo bhi bɛ, “Mbuɔt bɛ́fɛ́rɛ ɛbhɨ aya, kɛ bakʉ̌ bɛtɨk bábhɨkɨ ya.
baghɔrɛ́ bábhɔŋ bɛchɛkɔ kpák amɛm bɛchɛmɛ bǒnkwɔ. Bábhɨ́kɨ́ bhɔŋ bɛrɛm kɛpɨ. Bábhɔŋ bɛsɛptimʉɛt mbɔ ɛnyu ɛbhé Moses ɛ́rɛ̀m.
Ɛpǎ nɛbhay ɛ́fʉɛ́rɛ́ nɔ́kɔ́, Yesu asɛp arɔk Kapɛ̌naum nɛ máyi nɛ bɔ̌mayi nɛ bakoŋo bhi. Bábhak arɛ́ ndǔ mpay manywɔp. 
Mɛnyɨŋ ɛbhɛ́n ɔ́rɛ̀m bɛchi maknkay ntá yɛsɛ́ nɛ sɛ́yàŋ bɛ́rɨ́ŋɨ mbɔ̌ŋ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ ɔ́rɛ̀m.”
Nɛ mbák bǎkʉ̀ bɛrɨ chi ntá bo abhɛn bákʉ̀ bhe bɛrɨ bakak amɛn bábhɔ́ŋɔ́ bɛchyɛ bhe ǎbhák bɛ yi? Yɛ̌ chí bakʉ̌ bɛbʉ́ bákʉ̀ nɔ!
Ntɨkɨ mmǔ ákwày bɛtɔŋ bɛ nkʉ bɛbʉ́? Mɛ̌rɛ̀m chi tɛtɛp, ndaká yí bǎpú noko mɛ?
Yɛ̌ntɨkɨ mmu abhɔŋ bɛ́kʉ chi ɛbhi bɛtɨk ɛbhɛn Mandɛm achyɛ yi ankʉ.
Kɛ ákɛmɛ bhe chi bɛ, ‘Mbɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bhe nɛ yɛ̌ chi ɛbhak ɛnɛ bǎfú. Fǎ ká mɛ bɛsí, bě bakʉ̌ bɛbʉ́ mankɛm!’
Sɛ́yàŋ nyaka bɛ́twɔ awu ntá yɛka. Mɛmbɔŋ Pɔ̌l, mmɔ́ bɛ́twɔ awu ndɔŋ nɛ ndɔŋ, kɛ Satan achɛ́t bhɛsɛ mbi.
Nɛ yɛ̌ agha anɛ áchí nɛpɛ́m, anoko mɛ, apú gú wáwák. Matá, ɔnókó bɛyɔŋ ɛbhɛn?”
Nɛ ɛbhé ɛnɛ Mandɛm achyɛ bhɛsɛ ɛchi bɛ mmu anɛ akɔŋɔ Mandɛm abhɔŋ bɛkɔŋ ntɨ nkwǎ nkwɔ.
Yesu akɛmɛ bhɔ bɛ, “Bě nkwɔ bǎbhɨ́kɨ́re jwimɛm-ɛ? Bǎbhɨ́kɨ́ rɨŋɨ bɛ ɛnyɨŋ ɛnɛ mmu ányìɛ ɛnchwe yi mɛniɛ ɛ́pú kway bɛkʉ bɛ yi akɛ bhak pɛ́pɛ́p bɛsí Mandɛm?
Ághókó nɔ́kɔ́ bɛ́ Yesu anɛ Násárɛt kɛ áfʉɛ̀t, abho bɛbɨk bɛ, “Yesu! Mmɔ̌ Mfɔ Debhít! Ghɔ́ mɛ ntínso!”
Bě nkwɔ́ bǎchí batísiɛ́ bha mbɔnyunɛ bachí nɛ mɛ tɛ̌ndu nɛbhǒnɛt.”
